+++
title = "आचारः"
unicode_script = "devanagari"
+++





**tatra brahmacāriprakaraṇam**

**(atha ṭīkārambhaḥ)**

	saṃsiddhyarthamilatsurāsuranamanmaulisthitaprollasat

		sadratnaprabhavaprakṛṣṭavividhapreṅkhanmayūkhojjvalam |

	śreyovighnamahābhayapraśamane divyaṃ yad ekauṣadhaṃ

		bhūyān no dviradānanāṅghrikamaladvaṃdvaṃ tad iṣṭāptaye || 1 ||

	viśānubhūtisaṃbūtisthitisaṃhṛtimuktayaḥ |

	prabhavanti yatas tasmai parasmai brahmaṇe namaḥ || 2 ||

	yo viśvasargaparipālanasaṃhṛtīho

		brahmā haris trinayanaś ca bhavaty ameyaḥ |

	taṃ śuddhabodham abhayaṃ sukhasatsvabhāvam

		ātmānam advayam anantam upāsmahe 'jam || 3 ||

	siśvātmanaḥ śuklayajūṃṣi bhānor avāpya yo yogigaṇāgravaryaḥ |

	taṃ yājñavalkyaṃ munivṛndavandyaṃ namāmi tatkīrtitadharmabuddhyai || 4 ||

	bhaktyā yasya savismayaḥ smararipur buddhyā ca vācaspatir 

		vikrāntyā dviṣatāṃ gaṇaḥ śucitayā bhāsvān kṣamitvena bhūḥ |

	jīmūtānvayabhūṣaṇaṃ sa vipulāṃ yogīśvareṇodite 

		śāstre vākyanayānugāṃ vitanute vyākhyāṃ satāṃ saṃmatām || 5 ||

dharmasaṃhitām ārabhamāṇas tasyāḥ pauruṣeyatvasāmānyāj jāyamānām aprāmāṇyaśaṅkāṃ mahājanasya tadadhyayanadhāraṇādiviṣaye paripanthinīm apanetum āha |

	**oṃ yogīśvaraṃ yājñavalkyaṃ saṃpūjya munayo 'bruvan |**

**	varṇāśrametarāṇāṃ no brūhi dharmān aśeṣataḥ || 1 ||**

**yogī** saṃyamavān | tatrāpi **ceśvaro** 'ṇimādiguṇaśālī | eṣāṃ ca guṇānām īśvaraśabdapravṛttinimittatvaṃ gamyate mārkaṇḍeyapurāṇe |

	aṇimā laghimā caiva mahimā prāptir eva ca |

	prākāmyaṃ ca tatheśitvaṃ vaśitvaṃ ca tathā param ||

	yatra kāmāvasāyitvaṃ guṇān etān athaiśvarān |

	prāpnoty aṣṭau naravyāghra paranirvāṇasūcakān ||

	sūkṣmāt sūkṣmatarato 'ṇīyāñ śīghratvāl laghimā guṇaḥ |

	mahimāśeṣapūjyatvāt prāptir nāprāpyam asya yat ||

	prākāmyam asya vyāpyatvād īśitvaṃ ceśvaro yataḥ |

	vaśitvād vaśitā nāma yoginaḥ saptamo guṇaḥ ||

	yatrecchāsthānam apy uktaṃ yatra kāmāvasāyitā |

	aiśvaryaṃ kāraṇair ebhir yoginaḥ proktam aṣṭadhā ||

	muktisaṃsūcakaṃ rūpaṃ paranirvāṇacetasaḥ || iti |

evaṃ cāṇimādiguṇapara evāyam īśvaraśabdaḥ | tataś ca yogī cāsāv īśvaraś ca **yogīśvara** iti mukhyārthobhayaśabdaḥ karmadhārayaḥ | na tu yoginām īśvara iti ṣaṣṭhītatpuruṣaḥ, ṣaṣṭhyarthalakṣaṇāprasaṅgāt, yogīśvaraśabdaprayogavaiyarthyaprasaṅgāc ca | na hi tadā yoginām aṇimādilakṣaṇm aiśvaryaṃ yājñavalkyasyoktaṃ bhavati | kiṃ tu yoginaḥ sanakādīn prati svāmitvam | tac ca prakṛtānupayogi | karmadhārayapakṣe tu yoganimittam aṇimādyāiśvaryaṃ granthakārasya gamyate | tataś ca yogavirodhino 'jñānarāgadveṣā yogipadenārthān nirastāḥ | uktaṃ ca yogasya tannirāsakatvaṃ purāṇe |

	prāṇāyāmair dahed deṣān dhāraṇābhiś ca kilbiṣam |

	pratyāhāreṇa saṃsargān dhyānenānīśvarān guṇān || iti |

īśvarapadena ca yathāvasthitavedavedāntaboddhṛtvaṃ paramakāruṇikatvaṃ ca sūcyata iti tatpraṇītagranthasy prāmāṇye niścite katham aprāmāṇyaśaṅkociyāt | yajñavalkyasāpatyaṃ **yājñavalkyaḥ** | **saṃpūjya** saṃmānya | **munayo** maharṣayo **varṇādidharmān aśeṣato** niravaśeṣato **no** 'smān **brūhi** bodhayety **abruvan** | varṇā brāhmaṇādayaḥ | **āśramaśabdo** yady api brahmacārigṛhasthadikarsu vartate tathāpi tatsaṃbandhināṃ dharmāṇām abhāvād āśraśabdenāśramiṇo lakṣyante | ata evāha vasiṣṭhaḥ: "catvāra āśramā brahmacārigṛhasthavānaprasthaparivrājakāḥ" iti | kevalād varṇatvāt kevalāc cāśramitvād vyatiriktāni viśeṣarūpāṇi tadviśeṣasthā ye vakṣyamāṇadharmādhikāriṇas te ih**etare** | tāni ca viśeṣā(ṣarūpā)ṇi — yathā tāvad bhavatpūrvabhikṣācaryāvidhau brāhmaṇatvasahitaṃ brahmacaryam, evaṃ bhavanmadhyādito bhaiṣavaryāvidhau tad eva kṣatriyādyapekṣam, vivāhavidhau vanitārāgaḥ snātakatvaṃ ca, jāyopagamanavidhāv ṛtumaddāratvaṃ saṃyogadāratvaṃ vā, strīdharmeṣu strītvaṃ kvacij jāyātvaṃ kvacit proṣitabhartṛkātvaṃ kvacid vidhavātvam, dravaśuddhividhau śodhyadravyavattvam, pratiṣedhe tu pratiṣedhyakriyāpravartakapauṣkalyakriyāvattvam, śrāddhavidhau śrāddhakālāvicchinnajīvanavataḥ pramītapitṛkatvam, vināyakasnapanavidhau vināyakopasṛṣṭatvam, grahayajñavidhau śriyā(śryā)dikāmitvam, rājadharmavidhau kṣatriyasyābhiṣiktatvam, nirharaṇādividhau mṛtasapiṇḍatvam, āpaddharmavidhau durgatatvam, vasthavidhau valīpalitatvaṃ jātapautratvam, parivrājakavidhau vedādhyayanaputrotpādanayāgānuṣṭhānavataḥ saṃsāravairāgyavattvam, prāyaścittavidhau pāpavattvam ityādīni | etadviśiṣṭā ye te **itare** | varṇāś cāśramāś cetare ca te varṇāśrametarāḥ | teṣāṃ **varṇāśrametarāṇām** | atretaraśabdasya "dvandve ca" iti sarvanāmasaṃjñāpratiṣedhaḥ | śāstraprameyo niḥśreyasakaro dharmaḥ | kratvaṅgapratiṣedhanam adharmaḥ | vakṣyamāṇaśāstrārthaniravadyaniravaśeṣodīraṇakriyāṃ prati aśeṣata iti dharmasāmānyābhiprāyasākalyavacanam | niravaśeṣābhiprāye hy asminn upanayanādau gṛhyoktahomādi na kāryaṃ syāt | varṇāśrametarasaṃbandhopādhikāni trīṇi dharmasāmānyāni | dharmān brūhīti prārthitasya ca dharmasaṃhitākaraṇe tanmadhye 'dhyetṛsamavāyidharmajñānam eva prāyeṇa prayojakam | tataś cādhyetṝṇam adhyayanaprayojakaṃ tad eva | na hi teṣām aprayojakam adhyayanaṃ bhavitum arhati | tasmād dharmaśāstrādhyayanaṃ dharmaśāstratvajñānaprayuktam eva | yājñavalkyapraṇīte py atra śloke "**yājñavalkyaṃ saṃpūjya**" it vacanam, tathottaraśloke "**yogīndro 'bravīt**" iti prathamapuruaṣaprayogaś ca nāhuktaḥ | dṛśyate hi mānave granthe "manur abravīt" iti prayogaḥ, baudhāyane ca "sa ha smāha baudhāyanaḥ" iti | na ca "manur abravīt" iti bhṛgor vacanam idaṃ na manor iti vācyam | yata etad uttarakālam eva manur āha |

	etad vo 'yaṃ bhṛguḥ śāstraṃ śrāvayiṣyaty aśeṣataḥ |

	etad dhi matto 'dhijage sarvam eṣo 'khilaṃ muniḥ || iti |

adhijage 'dhītavān | asyāś ca saṃhitāyā yājñavalkyaḥ preṇeteti vyākhyātṝṇāṃ smṛtir eva pramāṇam | na cārtham eva yājñavalīyatayā te smarantīti vācyam | granthe hi praṇetṛtayā tasyāsādhāraṇyaṃ saṃbhavati na cārthe draṣṭṛtayā, munyantarair api tasya dṛṣṭatvāt | asādhāraṇyena ca vyapadeśo na sādhāraṇye ghaṭate | asādhāraṇyena hi vyapadeśā bhavanti || 1 ||

	**mithilāsthaḥ sa yogīndraḥ kṣaṇaṃ dhyātvābravīn munīn |**

sa munir dharmān brūhīti prārthito **mithilāstha**tvena viśeṣataḥ praśāntaḥ **kṣaṇa**mātraṃ vakṣyamāṇaṃ śāstrārthaṃ munīnāṃ tacchravaṇayogyatāṃ [ca] **dhyātvā** cintayitvā vakṣyamāṇān dharmān **abravīt** | yājñavalkyapraṇītatāṃ śāstre vaktuṃ sa ity uktam | na punar aham iti | na punar ahaṃśabdād yājñavalkyasaṃpratyayaḥ | sa iti śabdāt tu prakṛtavācino yājñavalkya eva prakṛte buddhir upaitīti tam eva prayuktavān | tatsāmānādhikarṇyāc **cābravīd** iti prathamapuruṣa eva yujyate | na punar abravam ity uttamaḥ | 

_tatra dharmānuṣṭhānasya deśaparigrahapūrvakatvād dharmakathanāt prāg eva deśam āha |_

	**yasmin deśe mṛgaḥ kṛṣṇas tasmin dharmān nibodhata || 2||**

**kṛṣṇa**śabdo hariṇavacanaḥ | kṛṣṇājinaṃ kṛṣṇaviṣāṇo yāvat kṛṣṇamṛgo vicaratīti prayogadarśanāt | sa **yasmin deśe** svabhāvād vicaret | tatra **dharmān** śrautasmārtān anuṣṭheyatayā he munayo **nibodhata** nibudhyadhvam | **kṛṣṇa**śabdād arthāntarāvabodho mā bhūd ity uktaṃ **mṛga** iti | kṛṣṇamṛgopalakṣitaś ca deśo brahmāvartādideśāsaṃbhave dharmānuṣṭhānāṅgam iti mantavyam | tathāha **manuḥ** |

	sarasvatīdṛṣadvatyor vyomanadyor yad antaram |

	taṃ devanirmitaṃ deśaṃ brahmāvartaṃ pracakṣate ||

	kurukṣetraṃ ca matsyāś ca pañcālāḥ śūrasenajāḥ |

	eṣa brahmarṣideśo vai brahmāvartād anantaraḥ ||

	himavadvindhyayor madhyaṃ yat prāg vinaśanād api |

	pratyag eva prayāgāc ca madhadeśaḥ prakīrtitaḥ ||

	ā samudrāt tu vai pūrvād ā samudrāt tu paścimāt |

	tayor evāntaraṃ giryor āryāvartaḥ prakīrtitaḥ ||

	kṛṣṇasāras tu carati mṛgo yatra svabhāvataḥ |

	sa deśo yajñiyo jñeyo mlecchadeśas tv ataḥ paraḥ ||

atra ca pūrvaḥ pūrva uttarata uttarataḥ śreṣṭhaḥ | yad āha purāṇam |

	brahmāvartaḥ paro deśa ṛṣideśas tv anantaraḥ |

	madhyadeśas tato nyūna āryāvartas tv anantaraḥ ||

viṣṇuś ca,

	cāturvarṇyavyavasthānaṃ yasmin deśe na vidyate |

	taṃ mlecchadeśaṃ jānīyād āryāvartam ataḥ param ||

ity āryāvartasya lakṣaṇāntaram āha | tataś ca yatra cāturvarṇyavyavasthā kṛṣṇamṛgaś ca nāsti sa mlecchadeśaḥ | tadanyo dharmadeśaḥ | tataś ca brahmāvartādideśacatuṣṭayālābhe tatra cāturvarṇyaṃ vyavatiṣṭhate kṛṣṇamṛgaś ca vicarati tatra dharmecchubhiḥ sthātavyam | tadasaṃbhave cāturvarṇyavyavasthāvati kṛṣṇamṛgayukte vā deśe | dharmān nibodhateti dharmagrahaṇād adharmaparihāre deśe viśeṣaniyamo nastīti mantavyam | śūdrasya vṛttāv anugraham āha manuḥ |

	etān dvijāyato deśān saṃśrayeran prayatnataḥ |

	śūdras tu yasmiś tasmin vā nivased vṛttikarśitaḥ || iti |

_jñānapūrvam anuṣṭhānaṃ dharmasyeti dharmajñānopāyāṃs tāvad āha |_

	**purāṇanyāyamīmāṃsādharmaśāstrāṅgamiśritāḥ |**

**	vedāḥ sthānāni vidyānāṃ dharmasya ca caturdaśa || 3 ||**

**purāṇaṃ** bra(brā)hmādi | **nyāyaḥ** satarkaḥ | **mīmāṃsā** vedavākyavicāraḥ | **dharmaśāstraṃ** manvādismṛtiḥ | **aṅgaiḥ **ṣaḍbhir vyākaraṇādibhiḥ sahitāś catvāro **vedā** ṛgvedadayaḥ | sthānāni (?) **caturdaśa** jñānānāṃ nimittāni, dharmasya ca jñānadvāreṇa, etad utpannasyaiva jñānasya dharmahetutvāt | tataś ca prayogapaddhatyādisamutthitaṃ jñānaṃ na dharmahetur iti siddham |

	evaṃ caturdaśaitāni vidyāsthānāni santy atha |

	vedāntaḥ pañcadaśakaṃ vidyā ṣoḍaśikā bhavet ||

iti brahmapurāṇe yad vedānavidyayor grahaṇaṃ tan mokṣasādhanavidyāsthānābhiprāyam itīhānupayogitvān noktam | vedāntaḥ śārīrakam | vidyā bṛhadāraṇyakādirahasyam | yat tu viṣṇupurāṇam,

	aṅgāni vedāś catvāro mīmāṃsā nyāyavistaraḥ |

	purāṇaṃ dharmaśāstraṃ ca vidyā etāś caturdaśa ||

	āyurvedo dhanurvedo gāndharvaś ceti te trayaḥ |

	arthaśāstraṃ caturthaṃ ca vidyā aṣṭādaśaiva tāḥ ||

tat kevalaṃ vidyāsthānatvābhprāyam, na dharmasthānatvābhiprāyam, āyurvedādīnāṃ ca dharmasthānatvābhāvāt | caturdaśagrahaṇād ṛte 'tharvavedasaṃgraho na syāt || 3 ||

_idānīṃ dharmaśāstrāṇāṃ tadābhāsebhyo vivekāya tatpraṇetṝn āha |_

	**manvatriviṣṇuhārītayājñavalkyośanoṅgiraḥ |**

**	yamāpastambasaṃvartāḥ kātyāyanabṛhaspatī || 4 ||**

**	parāśaravyāsaśaṅkhalikhitā dakṣagautamau |**

**	śātātapo vasiṣṭhaś ca dharmaśāstraprayojakāḥ || 5 ||**

**prayojakāḥ** praṇetāraḥ | atirohitam anyat | atra gautamaḥ: "smṛtir dharmaśāstrāṇi | teṣāṃ praṇetāraḥ: manuviṣṇudakṣāṅgirotribṛhaspatyuśanaāpastambagautamasaṃvartātreyakātyāyana-śaṅkhalikhitaparāśaravyāsaśātātapapracetoyājñavalkyādayaḥ" ityādiśabdaṃ prayuktavān | vedamūlagranthapraṇetāra ādiśabdenātra pragṛhyante | tathā ca manuḥ:

	vedo 'khilo dharmamūlaṃ smrtiśīle ca tadvidām | iti |

ata evāvaśiṣṭaḥ śrauto vākyaikaśeṣaḥ | **aṅgiraḥ**śabdaparyantaḥ samāhāradvandvo napaṃsakaliṅga ekavacanāntaḥ | ata eva bhaviṣyatpurāṇe guhyeśvaravākye smṛtayaḥ ṣaṭtriṃśad evābhihitāḥ |

	manvādismrtayo yas tu ṣaṭtriṃśat parikīrtitāḥ |

	tāsāṃ vākyāni kramaśaḥ samāsena bravīmi te ||

tāś ca manuviṣnuyamadakṣāṅgirotribṛhaspatyuśanāpastambavasiṣṭhakātyāyanaparāśaravyāsa-śaṅkhalikhitasaṃvartagautamaśātātapahārītayājñavalkyapracetobudhadevalasomajamadagni-viśvāmitraprajāpatināradapaiṭhīnasipitāmahabaudhāyanacchāgaleyajābālicyavanamarīcikaśyapā iti ṣaṭtriṃśad eva smṛtyantare paṭhitāḥ | evaṃ vṛddhamanvādayaś ca vayovasthādibhedena manvādipraṇetāra eva draṣṭavyāḥ, avirodhitvāc chrutismṛtyupabṛṃhakatvāc chiṣṭaparigṛhītatvād āptoktatvāc ca | caturviṃśatimatapariśiṣṭādayo 'pi dharmaśāstratvenaiv jñeyāḥ || 4 – 5 ||

_saṃprati yac chāstraṃ śāstrāntaranirapekṣaṃ samagram arthaṃ na śaknoty avagamayituṃ tac chāstrāntarasāpekṣam eva dharme pramāṇam iti dānam udāhṛtvāha |_

	**deśe kāla upāyena dravyaṃ śraddhāsamanvitam |**

**	pātre pradīyate yat tat sakalaṃ dharmalakṣaṇam || 6 ||**

**deśe** kurukṣetrādau, **kāla** uparāgādau, **upāyeneti** kartavyatayā, **dravyaṃ** gavādi, **śraddhayā** tatheti pratyayena **samanvitam**, **pātre** vakṣyamāṇalakṣaṇe, **pradīyate **khyātyādyanapekṣitvarūpeṇa prakarṣeṇa pātrasvīkāraparyantatayā tyajyata ity etatpratipādakaṃ vākyaṃ **sakalaṃ** sarvasādhanopetasyedaṃparyantaviśeṣavato dharmasya bodhakaṃ sarvaṃ **dharmalakṣaṇaṃ** dharme pramāṇaṃ veditavyam | na punaḥ sarvaprakārayuktasya dharmasya bodhakaṃ dharmalakṣaṇam | tathā ca śaṅkhaḥ: "deśaḥ kāla upāyo dravyaṃ śraddhā pātraṃ tyāga iti samasteṣu dharmodayaḥ sādhāraṇo nyāyyo 'nyathā viparītaḥ" iti | sādhāraṇo dānena samānaḥ | nyāyyo 'nyeṣāṃ yāgādidharmāṇām | anyathā sāmastyābhāve | viparīto dharmasyānudaya ity arthaḥ | sati sāmarthye sarvāṅgānuṣṭhānam | asati tu kāmyaṃ heyam | āvaśyakaṃ tu yathāśakti kāryam | yat tu kātyāyanavākyam,

	bahv alpaṃ vā svagṛhyoktaṃ yasya karma prakīrtitam |

	tasya tāvati śāstrārthe kṛte sarvaḥ kṛto bhavet ||

iti, tan nirapekṣārthābhidhāyakasvaśāstraviṣayam | sāpekṣe tu svaśāstre śāstrāntaroktaṃ grāhyam iti sa evāha |

	yan nāmnātaṃ svaśākhāyāṃ pārakyam avirodhi yat |

	vidvadbhis tad anuṣṭheyam agnihotrādikarmavat || iti |

_saṃprati dharmapramāṇāny āha |_

	**śrutismṛtisadācārāḥ svasya ca priyam ātmanaḥ |**

**	samyaksaṃkalpajaḥ kāmo dharmamūlam idaṃ smṛtam || 7 ||**

śrutyadikaṃ pratyekaṃ **dharmamūlaṃ** dharmaniścayasya kāraṇam | purāṇanyāyety atra śrutismṛtyoḥ sāmānyato dharmamūlatvam uktam | atra tu nivārya tanmūlatvam ucyate | arthād anyeṣāṃ vidyāsthānānāṃ vidyānurohakatvam | smṛter na vyākaraṇādivad vedānurohakatvam, kiṃ tu tadanumāpakatvam iti prthaguktiḥ | ācārādeḥ. punar atraiva dharmamūlatvoktir iti na punaruktatā | **śrutir** vedaḥ | **smṛtir** dharmato **vedamūlaṃ** śāstram, **sadācāraḥ** śiṣṭācāraḥ | **svasya** svakīyasy**ātmano** manasaḥ **priyaṃ** tuṣṭikaram | ātmaśabdenātra mano lakṣyate | priyaśabdena tuṣṭiḥ | tena manastuṣṭir atra cikīrṣoparamo nirdiśyate | samīcīnaḥ śāstrārthaviṣayo 'nenedaṃ sādhayāmīti manaḥkarma **saṃkalpaḥ** | tajjaḥ **kāmo** dharmacikīrṣā | etat sarvaṃ dharmaniścaye mūlaṃ kāraṇam ity arthaḥ | dharmeṇa tanniścayo lakṣyate | tatrāgnihotrāder niścayamūlaṃ śrutiḥ, varṇāśramadharmāderḥ smṛtiḥ, holākādeḥ sadācāraḥ, yat karma manasas tuṣṭiparicchinnatayā vidhīyate tasya manastuṣṭiḥ | yathā,

	yasmin karmaṇy asya kṛte manasaḥ syād alāghavam |

	tasmiṃs tāvat tapaḥ kuryād yāvat tuṣṭikaraṃ bhavet || iti |

kālaviśeṣe saṃkalpajaḥ kāmaḥ, yathā: "yadaivainaṃ śraddhayopanayet tadaivādadhīta" iti | atha vā "śrāddhaṃ prati ruciś caiva" iti | vyāsaḥ |

	dharmaśuddhim abhīpsadbhir na devād anyad iṣyate |

	dharmasya kāraṇaṃ śuddhaṃ miśram anyat prakīrtitam ||

śuddhir asaṃkīrṇatā | dharmasya dharmaniścayasyety arthaḥ | śuddham aduṣṭam | miśraṃ saṃbhāvitadoṣam |

	ataḥ sa paramo dharmo yo vedād adhigamyate |

	avaraḥ sa tu vijñeyo yaḥ purāṇādiṣu smṛtaḥ ||

	vedārthavittamaiḥ karma yat smṛtaṃ munibhiḥ purā |

	tad yatnena samātiṣṭhet tanniṣiddhaṃ tu varjayet ||

	te hi vedārthavattvajñā lokānāṃ hitakāmyayā |

	pradiṣṭavanto yaṃ dharmaṃ taṃ dharmaṃ na vicārayet ||

	vedārtho yaḥ svayaṃ jñātas tatrājñānaṃ bhaved api |

	ṛṣibhir niścite tasmin kā śaṅkā syān manīṣiṇām ||

	etebhyo 'pi yad anyat syāt kiṃcid dharmābhidhāyakam |

	tad dūratarato viddhi mohas tasyāśrayo mataḥ ||

na vicārayet, nāpramāṇatayā sāṅketa | etebhyo dharmaśāstrādibhyo yad anyat pauruṣeyaṃ tad dheyam |

	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">nanu</span> ca śaivapāśupatapāñcarātraśātrādyapauruṣeyam eva, tataś ca tadanuṣṭhānācaraṇe 'bhyudaya eva na doṣaḥ kaścit, tasya niḥśreyasahetutvāt | 

	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">maivam</span>,

	ācamya ca purā brāhmīṃ bhajet saṃdhyām dvirāśramī |

	itaras tu virakātmā laukikārthaparṅmukhaḥ ||

	brāhmīṃ kuryān na vā kuryāc chaivīm eva niyogataḥ |

	antaḥ śaivaṃ bahiḥ kaulaṃ lokācāre tu vaidikam ||

	sāram ādāya tiṣṭhet tu nārikelaphalaṃ yathā ||

iti svāyaṃbhyvādivacanenānavakḷptalokānurañcanāpādakatvena pratipāditavaidikakarmavaiphalyadoṣatvāt sarvātmanā śrutismṛtivihitadharmānuṣṭhānaikaparamārthāṃs traividyavṛddhān prati śaivādyāmnāyasyānuṣṭhāne niḥśreyasanimittatvāsiddheḥ | nāpi teṣāṃ śaivādiśāstrānanuṣṭhāne kācit kṣatiḥ | "yāvajjīvam agnihotraṃ juhuyāt," "agnihotraṃ ca juhuyād ādyante dyuniśoḥ sadā," iti śrutismṛtyuktair hi teṣām āśramakarmabhiḥ prayojanaṃ nānyaiḥ, śrutismṛtyarthātikrame pratyāvāyāpatteḥ | tathā ca śrutiḥ: "vīrahā vā eṣa devānāṃ yo 'gnim utsādayate" | smṛtir api |

	agnihotry apavidhyāgnīn brāhmaṇaḥ kāmakārataḥ |

	cāndrāyaṇaṃ caren māsaṃ vīrahatyāsamaṃ hi tat || iti |

na cānanuṣṭhānamātreṇaivārthasiddhaṃ dūaṇam iti vācyam,

	drutena trapuṇā pūrṇavaktrās tiṣṭhanti duḥkhitāḥ |

	dveṣṭāraḥ śivaśāstrāṇāṃ ye ca vedavidūṣakāḥ ||

	sāṃkhyaṃ yogaḥ pāñcarātraṃ vedāḥ pāśupataṃ tathā |

	atipramāṇāny etāni hetubhir na vicārayet ||

iti adūṣyatvena hetvavicāraṇīyatvena ca devīpurāṇayogayājñavalkyayor adūṣyatvena tasya smaraṇāt | na caitāvatā tadanuṣṭhāne ca doṣaḥ kaścid iti vācyam, "yāvad vacanam vācanikam" iti nyāyena nyūnasyādhikasya vā parigrahasya svotprekṣāmātreṇa kartum anarhatvāt sakalādūṣyāgamānuṣṭhānasya ca kartum aśakyatvāt,

	dīkṣitasya ca devoktaṃ śrāddhakarmātigarhitam |

	ity evaṃ vaidikaśrāddhakriyā nādīkṣitair api |

	dīkṣitān prati kartavyā dvayor niryadāyinī ||

ityādinā śaivaśāstrapratipannasya vaidikakarmakaraṇena narakadānādidoṣaprāpteḥ,

	śreyān svadharmo viguṇaḥ paradharmāt svanuṣṭhitāt |

	svadharme nidhanaṃ śreyaḥ paradharmodayād api ||

ityādinā bhāratādau vikalasyāpi svānuṣṭhānasyotkarṣadarśane saty api sakalādūṣyāgamānuṣṭhānasya ca parasparaviruddhārthatve jñānaniṣṭhāprāptyabhāvāc ca | tathā ca śaivāḥ: pradhānapuruṣayor adhiṣṭhātā kevalaṃ nimittakāraṇam īśvara itaretaravilakṣaṇāḥ pradhānapuruṣeśvarā iti bhedeśvaravādinaḥ | sāṃkhyāḥ: nirīśvaravādinaḥ | yogāḥ pātañjalās tu: jagatām kartā kleśakarmavipākāśayair aparāmṛṣṭaḥ sarvaśāstravettṛtvāt sarvajñaḥ puruṣaviśeṣa īśvara iti seśvarāḥ | pāñcarātrāḥ punaḥ: śāntoditavivṛttāvyapadeśyabhinnatayā cāturātmyenāvasthitaḥ paramā prakṛtir bhagavān vāsudeva ity advaitabhāveneśvaraṃ manyante | pāśupatāḥ punaḥ: kāryakāraṇayogavidhiduḥkhāntāḥ pañca padārthāḥ paśupatineśvareṇa paśupāśavimocanārtham uddiṣṭā iti bhedeśvaravādam evāṅgīkurvanti | tad evam anavasthitatvāt sarvāgamajñānasya sarvasvīkāre saṃśayānivṛtter jñānalābho durghaṭa eva | vaikalpikāṅgīkāre conmattatulyatā prasajyeta | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">nanu</span> yathā śaivādyāmnāyasyaivādūṣyatvamātreṇa prāmāṇyam, tathaivādūṣyatvasmaraṇāviśeṣād vedasyāpīti | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">satyam</span>, "drutena trapuṇā" ityādinā vedasya śaivādyāgamasadṛśam evādūṣyatvamātreṇa prāmāṇyam |

	pitṛdevamanuṣyāṇāṃ dedaś cakṣuḥ sanātanam |

	atarkyaṃ cāprameyaṃ ca vedaśāstram iti sthitiḥ ||

ityādinā manvādibhir aihikāmutrikārthaprakṛṣṭasādhakatvaṃ tu vedasyoktam, na śaivādiśāstrasya | pratyuta,

	ye vedamārganirmuktās teṣāṃ mohārtham eva ca |

	siddhāntasaṃjñakaṃ pūrvaṃ mayā śāstraṃ pradarśitam ||

	paśur yo 'paśubhāvasthaḥ sa yadā patito bhavet |

	tadā pāśupataṃ śāstraṃ jñāyate viśvamohakam ||

	mayaiva mohitās te hi bhaviṣyanto janā dvija |

	laulyārthinas tu śāstrāṇi kariṣyanti kalau narāḥ ||

	niḥśvāsasaṃhitā yā hi lakṣamātraṃ pramāṇataḥ |

	saiva pāśupato yogo bhedāḥ pāśupatās tataḥ ||

	etayā vedamārgāder yad anyad iha jāyate |

	tat kṣudrakarma vijñeyaṃ raudraṃ śaucavivarjitam ||

ityādināgastyaṃ prati rudravacanena varāhapurāṇe tasya vimohakatvena vipralambhakatvam eva pratipāditam | sarvajanavimohakatvād vipralambhakam eva śaivādīti | bhūyaś ca tatraiva śrīrudraṃ prati janārdanavākyam |

	eṣa mohaṃ sṛjāmy āśu yo janaṃ mohayiṣyati |

	tvaṃ ca rudra mahābāho mohaśāstrāṇi kāraya ||

	alpāyāsaṃ darśayitvā phalaṃ dīrghaṃ pradarśaya |

	kuhakāś cendrajālāni viruddhacaraṇāni ca ||

	darśayitvā janaṃ sarvaṃ mohayāśu maheśvara || iti |

ata eva ca manuḥ |

	utpadyante vyayante ca yāny ato yāni kānicit |

	tāny arvākkālikatayā niṣphalāny anṛtāni ca || iti |

ata eva ca śaivādiśāstroktasyāprāmāṇyam ācārasyāhā āpastambaḥ: "vedāḥ pramāṇam iti niṣṭhā | tatra yāni śrūyante vrīhiyavapaśvājyapayaḥkapālapātrīsaṃbandhāny uccair nīcaiḥ kāryāṇīti | tair viruddha ācāro 'pramāṇam iti manyante" iti | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">nanu</span> ca |

	alābhe vedamantrāṇāṃ pañcarātroditena hi |

	ācāreṇa pravartante te māṃ prāpsyanti mānavāḥ ||

	brāhmaṇakṣatriyaviśāṃ pañcarātraṃ vidhīyate |

	śūdrādīnām na tacchrotrapadavīm upayāsyati ||

ityādinā varāhapurāṇe bhagavadvākena pāñcarātrasya vedapratinidhitvena smaraṇād vedenāviśeṣaḥ pāṇcarātrasya | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">satyam</span> aviśeṣaḥ | kiṃ tu viṣayaviśeṣād viśeṣaḥ | tathā hi, asya vākyasya kutaścid daivayogād akṛtaprayaścittavrātyaviṣayatvād aviplutabāhmaṇādyanāśrayatvam, evaṃ hi saty atrālābhapadam upapattimat syāt | tādṛśānāṃ vrātyānāṃ vedapariprāpter abhāvāt | tathā ca mānavam |

	naitair apūtair vidhivad āpady api hi karhicit |

	brāhmān yaunāṃś ca saṃbandhān ācared brāhmaṇaḥ saha || iti |

evaṃ ca pāñcarātre dvijātyadhikāro 'pi vicālita eva syāt | tasmād vidhivaśād akṛtaprāyaścittavrātyaviṣayatvād asya vākyasyāsti viśeṣo vedapañcarātrayoḥ | ata eva ca yogayājñavalkye pañcarātrasya pāśupatādisamānaṃ siddhāntatvenābhidhānaṃ vedabāhyatvapratītikṛd eva |

	ekam eva tu vijñeyaṃ praṇavaṃ yogasādhanam |

	gṛhītasaptasiddhāntair anyair brahmavidais tathā ||

	hairaṇyagarbhaiḥ kapilair apāntaratamais tathā |

	sānatkumārair brahmiṣṭhais tathā pāśupatair api ||

	pāñcarātrair apīty etaiḥ siddhāntaiś caiva saptabhiḥ || iti |

evaṃ hi pañcarātrasyādūṣyatvenaiva prāmāṇyaṃ nānuṣṭheyatveneti |

	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">nanu</span> ca yathaiva niyatān kāṃścid adhikṛtya vedādiśāstraṃ pravṛttam, tathaiva jātimataḥ śaivādīn prati śaivādiśāstram astu |

	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">na</span>,

	niṣekādiḥ śmaśānānto mantrair yasyodito vidhiḥ |

	tasya śāstre 'dhikāro 'smiñ jñeyo nānyasya kasyacit ||

ityādinā manvādibhiḥ svaśāstreṣv adhikārasya dvijānām eva pradarśitatvān na śaivādiśāstre śaivabrāhmaṇādīnām | 

	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">astu tarhi</span> śaivādiśāstre śūdro 'dhikṛtaḥ | 

	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">na</span>, smṛtyādiśāstreṣu tathānabhyupagamāt | api ca śaivo nāma jātyā na kaścid apy asti yaṃ prati śaivādiśāstraṃ syāt | api tu "tena proktam" (Pāṇ 4.3.101) ityāṇi kṛte śivena proktaṃ śāstraṃ śaivam | punaś ca śaivaśabdātr "tadadhīte tad veda" (Pāṇ 4.2.59) ity utpannasyāṇaḥ "proktāl luk" (Pāṇ 4.2.64) iti luki kṛte śaivaṃ vetty adhīte vā śaivaḥ | evaṃ pāśupatādiḥ | yasmād evaṃ svabhāvato niyatān kāṃścid anāśrityaiva śaivādiśāstraṃ pravṛttaṃ tasmāt tad ākāśacitram iva prāptam | tathā ca saty anuṣṭhāne tad dheyam eva | na cādūṣyāgamaprasiddher evāśramiṇāṃ tadanuṣṭḥānaṃ syād iti vācyam | na hy adūṣyatvamātreṇa teṣāṃ śrutivat svārthānuṣṭhāpakatvasāmarthayam,

	yā vedabāhyāḥ śrutayo yāś ca kāścit kudṛṣṭayaḥ |

	sarvās tā niṣphalāḥ proktās tamobhūtā hi tāḥ smṛtāḥ ||

ityādinā manvādibhis tadanuṣṭhānasyāmutra vaiphalyāpadakatvādinā niṣiddhatvāt | tataś ca devapūjādau narasiṃhapurāṇādiprasiddhaivetikartavyatā grāhyā nānyā | evaṃ dīkṣāyām apy avagantavyam | na hi purāṇaprasiddhāyāṃ dīkṣāyāṃ jātiśodhanam asti | śaivādyāgameṣu tu,

	prathamaṃ sthāvarā jātis tataḥ sārīsṛpī matā |

	pakṣijātis tṛtīyā tu caturthī mṛgajātikā ||

	pañcamī paśujātis tu ṣaṣṭhī caivāntyajā smrtā |

	saptamī śūdrajātis tu vaiśyajātis tathāṣṭamī ||

	navamī kṣatrajātis tu daśamī viprasaṃjñitā |

	etās tu jātayaḥ śodhyā jātīśena śivena vā ||

ityādinā tacchodanadarśanāc chrautakarmānadhikāritvaprasaktiḥ | "brāhmaṇo 'gnīn ādadhīta," "rājā rājasūyena yajeta," "vaiśyo vaiśyastomena yajeta" ityādinā jātimantam eva prakṛtya vaidikaṃ karma pravṛttam | tat kathaṃ jātinivṛttau syāt | evaṃ pratiṣṭhāyām api purāṇādyuktaivetikartavyatā grāhyā nānyā | teṣām eva vyāmiśradharmapramāṇatvena bhaviṣyatpurāṇe parijñātatvāt | tathā ca bhaviṣyatpurāṇam |

	aṣṭādaśa purāṇāni rāmasya caritaṃ tathā |

	viṣṇudharmādiśāstrāṇi śivadharmāś ca bhārata ||

	kārṣṇaś ca pañcamo vedo yan mahābharataṃ smṛtam |

	saurāś ca dharmajārendra mānavoktā mahīpate |

	jayeti nāma caiteṣāṃ pravadanti manīṣiṇaḥ || iti |

tatrāpi "madyavaarjaṃ surāṃ bhūpa ninayet" ityādi smṛtaṃ kaliyugād anyatra mantavyam,

	dīrghakālaṃ brahmacaryaṃ dhāraṇaṃ ca kamaṇḍaloḥ |

	sagotrād vā sapiṇḍād vā vivāho govadhas tathā ||

	narāśvamedho madyaṃ ca kalau varjyā dvijātibhiḥ ||

ityādinā madyāder brahmapurāṇādau sāmānyato varjyatvenābhihitatvāt | etena caṇḍikādyupahārā vyākhyātāḥ | yad apy añjanavidhau kālikāpurāṇe,

	kapālasaṃpuṭe kṛtvā mahātaighṛte tathā |

	candrasūryoparāge ca kajjalaṃ gṛhya buddhimān ||

	añjayed akṣiṇī tena vaśī kuryāt purandaram ||

ityādi tat "atha śatruṃ mārayitukāmaḥ śmaśānakāṣṭhair agniṃ prajvālya viṣarudhiramiśrāṇ āhitisahasraṃ juhjyāt sadyaḥ śatruṃ mārayati" iti vat "śeyenenābhicaran yajeta" itivad vādharma eva | hiṃsādivad vaśīkaraṇāder api tatra tatra niṣiddhatvāt | tathā ca 

	hiṃśauṣadhīnāṃ stryājīvo 'bhicāro mūlakarma ca |

iti manunā vaśīkaraṇam upapātakamadhye parigaṇitam | yad api devīpurāṇe,

	vāmadakṣiṇavettā yo mātṛvedārthapāragaḥ |

	sa bhavet sthāpakaḥ śreṣṭho devīnāṃ mātarā(tṛkā)su ca ||

	pāñcarātrārthakusalo mātṛtantraviśāradaḥ |

	viṣṇor gṛhī sadā śasto brahmacārī ca śāntidaḥ ||

	śivaśāsanavettā yo grahamātṛgaṇārthavit |

	gṛhastho brahmacārī vā sthāpakaḥ kīrtitaḥ śive |

	saurārthavedakaḥ sūrye sthāpakaḥ pūjakaḥ śubhaḥ ||

iti, etad api na brāhmāgamānuṣṭhānaliṅgam | tadanuṣṭhānasya ca matsyapurāṇe niṣiddhatvāt | tathā ca matsyapurāṇam |

	sthāpakasya samāsena lakṣaṇaṃ śṛṇuta dvijāḥ |

	sarvāvayavasaṃpanno vedamantraviśāradaḥ ||

	purāṇavettā dharmajño dambhalobhavivarjitaḥ |

	kṛṣṇasāracare deśe ya utpannaḥ śubhākṛtiḥ ||

	śaucācāraparo nityaṃ pāṣā(ṣ)ṇḍakulaniḥspṛhaḥ |

	samaḥ śatrau ca mitre ca brahmopendraharapriyaḥ ||

	ūhāpohārthatattvajño vāstuśāstrasya pāragaḥ |

	ācāryas tu bhaven nityaṃ sarvadoṣavivarjitaḥ ||

	mūrtipās tadvidhāś caiva kulīnā ṛjavas tathā || iti |

yathā pāñcarātrasaṃhitāyām: "caturdaśa vidyāsthānāni veditavyāni bhavanti, tad yathā — ṛgvedo yajurvedaḥ śamavedo 'tharvaveda itihāsapurāṇaṃ nyāyo mīmāṃsā śikṣā kalpo vyākaraṇaṃ niruktaṃ jyotiṣāmayanaṃ chandovicitir ity atrāpy anadhikāraḥ kiṃ tu bhavaty evādhikāraḥ" iti trayyādijñānam evopādeyam, tathātrāpi vāmadakṣiṇāmnāyādijñānamātram evopādeyam | tathā ca yogayājñavalkyaḥ |

	ātmajñānanimittaṃ hi siddhāntāni vicintayet |

	kevalāni yadādhīte vedabāhyo bhaved dvijaḥ ||

kevalādhyayanaṃ svadharmaparityāgena paradharmasevanam | tādṛśasyānuṣṭhānasya,

	svadharmaṃ yāh samutsṛjya paradharmarucir bhavet |

	cakoranayane cauraḥ sa śūdraś candrasaṃnibhe ||

ityādinā skandapurāṇādau ninditatvāt | vāmadakṣinādijñānaṃ ca svaśātrāpekṣitasya tacchāstroktasyāviruddhasyāṅgasya kasyacit svīkārārtham | tac cāha manuḥ |

	sāpekṣatve 'py apekṣaiva mānaṃ yāvad apekṣate |

	tāvad evānyataḥ kāryam anyan naivānavasthiteḥ ||

viruddhasya tu tyāga eveti | ata eva ca dharmasaṃkaraparihārābhiprāyeṇa rājadharmeṣu mahābhāratam |

	cāturvarṇyasya dharmāś ca rakṣitavyā mahīkṣitā |

	dharmasaṃkararakṣā hi dharmaḥ sanātanaḥ || iti |

na ca vāvyam: svadharmapratiṣṭhāditantropaskārakartuḥ sthāpakāder vāmadakṣiṇāmnāyajñānaṃ taduktadīkṣāgrahaṇapūrvakam eva, smṛtyadiśāstre tathānaṅgīkārāt, [vāmadakṣiṇādiśāstraṃ (strasya) ca yathoktaṃ sthāpakatvādipratiniyamakatvāsiddheḥ] vāmadakṣiṇādiśastrasya tadvivaraṇadarśanādipūrvaṃ svātmanā nirīkṣaṇenānekavidyāsthānopaskāropaskṛtamatitvād asya niḥśeṣāvabodhena helāmātreṇa svapratiṣṭhātantrādyupaskāramātranivahaṇāc ca | yad api bhāratādau dakṣaṃ pratīśvaravākyam,

	bhūyaś ca te varaṃ dadmi khyātaṃ gṛhṇīṣva suvrata |

	prasannavadano bhūtvā tad ihaikamanāḥ śṛṇu ||

	vedāt ṣaḍaṅgād uddhṛtya sāṃkhyād yogāc ca śaktitaḥ |

	tapaḥ sutaptaṃ vipulaṃ duścaraṃ devadānavaiḥ ||

	apūrvaṃ sarvatobhadraṃ viśvatomukham avyayam |

	arthair daśārdhaiḥ saṃyuktaṃ gūḍham aprājñaninditam ||

	varṇāśramakṛtair dharmair viparītaṃ kvacit samam |

	śatāntair adhyavasitam anyāśramam idaṃ smṛtam ||

	mayā pāśupataṃ pūrvaṃ yogam utpāditaṃ purā |

	asya cīrṇasya samyag yat phalaṃ bhavati puṣkalam ||

	tac cāstu te mahābhāga tyajyatāṃ mānaso jvaraḥ ||

iti, tan nāśramiṇāṃ pāśupataśāstrānuṣṭhāpakatve liṅgaṃ tatphalasāmyamātrasyātra vivakṣitatvāt | santi hi pāśupatādyāgameṣu "agniṣṭomaphalaṃ labhet" ity evamādīni vākyāni | na caitāvatā teṣāṃ tadadhikāraḥ sidhyati | nāpi "tad etad vrataṃ bhasmanāṅgāni saṃspṛśet tasmād vratam etat pāśupataṃ paśupāśavimokṣaṇāya" iti atharvaśiraupaniṣatpāśupataśāstrārthānuṣṭhāpakatve liṅgam, bhasmanāṅgasaṃsparśamātrasya niyamasyātra śravaṇāt | na ca smṛtau pāśupatādisparśe sacailsnānaśravaṇāt tacchāśtrasya dūṣyatvam āśramiṇām abhipretam ity āśaṅkanīyam | kṛte so mayāgādāv anekamantrasaṃskṛteṣṭakācityasaṃsparśane 'pi snānadarśanāt | na ca cityasya kiṃ duṣṭatvād uta rudranirmālyavad abhyarhitatvād aspṛśyatvam ity etāvatīṃ vicārapadavīm avagāhituṃ śāstraikagocare 'rthe 'smādṛśāṃ matiḥ kramat iti <span style="text-decoration:underline;">kecit</span> | vastutas tu yathā,

	cāturvedo 'pi yo vipro dīkṣito na śivādhvare |

	sa tu śūdraḥ pramantavyo na deyaṃ tasya śāsanam ||

ityādinā śaivādayo dīkṣāvihīnānāṃ traividyavṛddhānām avaravarṇavad vijugupsāṃ kurvanti, tathā,

	kāpālikāḥ pāśupatāḥ śaivāś ca saha kārukaiḥ |

	dṛṣṭāś ced ravim īkṣeta spṛṣṭāś cet snānam ācaret ||

iti smṛtyantaradarśanād antyāvasāyivad darśanasparśanayor duṣṭāḥ śaivādiśāstrapratipannāḥ śaivādayas traividyavṛddhair manyante | etad evopapannam | śāstraṃ hi tathā | tasmāt purāṇādiyuktiparyālocanenaivānuṣṭhānam ādartavyam | na ca kvacit kvacid bāhyāgamānuṣṭheyasāmānyena bāhyāgamair ekārthatvam āśaṅkanīyam | yatrāpi bāhyāgamānuṣṭheyasādṛśyam iva,

	arūpām anurūpāṃ vā subhagāṃ durbhagāṃ tathā |

	satīṃ vā asatīṃ vāpi aṅgānāṃ na jugupsayet(?) ||

ityādi, tatrāpi devīpurāṇādyuktadṛśā dīkṣitasyaivaite niyamā ity anusaṃdheyam | tasmād adūṣyatvenaiva śauvādi pramāṇam anuṣṭheyatve tv aṅgatvena kenacit kvacid aṃśenādeyaṃ sākalyena nānuṣṭheyam iti sthitam | tatrāpi yat pauruṣeyaṃ na kevalam ananuṣṭheyaṃ tad yāvad apramāṇam apīti heyam apīti siddham | ata evāhur ācāryāḥ |

	anuṣṭheyaṃ na bhavati yac chāstraṃ puruṣaiḥ kṛtam |

	tad apramāṇaṃ vijñeyaṃ puṃbuddhiprabhavaṃ hi tat ||

alam atiprasaṅgena |

	**sadācāraḥ** śiṣṭācāra ity uktam | tatra hi śiṣṭasvarūpam āha baudhāyanaḥ: "śiṣṭāḥ khalu vigatamatsarā nirahaṃkārāḥ kumbhīdhānyāḥ |

	alolupā daṃbhalobhamohakopavivarjitāḥ |

	dharmeṇādhigato yaiś ca vedaḥ saparibṛṃhaṇaḥ ||

	śiṣṭās tadanumānajñāḥ śrutipratyakṣahetavaḥ || iti |

kumbhīdhānyā iti vṛttisaṃkocopalakṣaṇaparam |

	itihāsapurāṇābhyāṃ vedaṃ samupabṛṃhayet |

iti manuvacanād itihāsapurāṇādi vedasya paribṛṃhaṇāni, avinābhāvāc ca vyākaraṇādīni | tadanumānajñāḥ smṛtijñāḥ | smṛtir hi tasya vedasyānumānaṃ liṅgam | śrutipratyakṣahetavaḥ śrutiḥ pratyakṣahetur yeṣāṃ saṃmatas te tathoktāḥ | smṛtivacanam ācāraś ca pratyakṣagāmitvāt pratyakṣam | brahmāvartādiṣu bāhulyena vedamūla ācāra iti matvā manur āha |

	yasmin deśe ya ācāraḥ pāramparyāt samāgataḥ |

	varṇānāṃ sāntarālānāṃ sa sadācāra ucyate || iti |

na tu brahmāvarta eva sadācāra iti matvā | tathā sati lobhādimūlo 'pi brahmāvarācāro dharme pramāṇaṃ syāt | vedamūlako 'pi ca deśāntaravartī na syāt | vasiṣṭho 'pi: "āryāvarte prāg ādarśāt parvatāt pratyak kālakād vanād udak pāriyātrād dakṣinena himavantam uttareṇa vindhyaṃ ye dharmā ya ācārās te sarve pratyetavyāḥ | na tv anye pratilomadharmāṇaḥ" ity āha | atrāpi sarvaśabdo bāhulyābhiprāyeṇa | na tv anye pratilometi, atrāpi deśāntarīyāḥ sarve dharmā ācārāś ca na pratyetavyāḥ | yatas teṣu bāhulyena lobhādipūrvakā ācārāḥ, kecid eva śrutipūrvakā iti tasyārthe 'nusaṃdheyāḥ | anyathā deśāntarāvartyasaṃbhavāl lobhādimūla ācāro nirmūlaḥ syāt | manuḥ |

	śrutismṛtivirodhe tu śrutir eva garīyasī |

	avirādhaṃ tu kartavyaṃ smārtaṃ vaikavat sadā ||

vasiṣṭhaḥ: "śrutismṛtivihito dharmas tadalābhe śiṭācāraḥ pramāṇam" iti | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">nanu</span> yadi śrutismṛtyor dharma eva prāmāṇyaṃ kathaṃ tarhy ātmajñānapradhānayoḥ śrutismṛtyor dharmaprāmāṇyanirvāha iti | na hy ātmajñānaṃ dharmaḥ, ananuṣṭheyatvāt | tattvam asītyādivākyārthāvadhāraṇatas taj jñāyate, na tu vākyārtham avadhārya yāgādivad anuṣṭhīyata ity āśaṅkyāha 

	**ijyācāradamāhiṃsādānasvādhyāyakarmaṇām |**

**	ayaṃ tu paramo dharmo yad yogenātmadarśanam || 8 ||**

ijyādidharmāṇām itikartavyatātmanāṃ saṃbandhī paramaḥ pradhānabūto 'yaṃ dharmo yad yogena samādhinātmadarśanaṃ nāma | ātmaśabdo 'yaṃ paramātmani vartate na jīvātmani, tasyejyādikam antareṇa samādhiṃ vinaiva ca prāptatvāt | "ātmā vā are draṣṭavyaḥ" iti tatrotpattividhiḥ | "brahmavid āpnoti param" ity adhikāravidhiḥ | atra hi paraśabdena parmātmābhidhīyate | tadāptiś ca tadātmanaiva kṣetrajñasyāvasthānam | tatra brahmavid itipadopāttā brahmavidyā karaṇam "vividiṣanti yajñena dānena tapasānāśakena" ity atra yajñenetyādiśrutiḥ sakalanityanaimittikavarṇāśramadharmopalakṣaṇārtham | ata eva viṣṇupurāṇam |

	ārādhyate svavarṇoktadharmānuṣṭhānakāriṇā |

	tasmāt tatprāptaye yatnaḥ kartavyaḥ paṇḍitair naraiḥ ||

	tatprāptihetur jñānaṃ ca karma coktaṃ mahāmune ||

tathā ca vasiṣṭhaḥ |

	yathānnaṃ madhusaṃpṛktaṃ madhu cāpy annasaṃyutam |

	evaṃ tapaś ca vidh¥āṃ ca saṃyuktaṃ bheṣajaṃ hi tat ||

iti evamādi matvoktavān: "**ijyācāradamāhiṃsā**" iti | rāgaprāptaṃ karmāśritya śāstreṇa puruṣābhyudayāya vidhīyamāno 'rtha ācāraḥ | yathā "prāṅmukho 'nnāni bhuñjīta tūṣṇīm" ityādi | manaso damanām **damaḥ** | rāgaprāptahiṃsānivṛttir **ahiṃsā** | svasvatvanivṛttiḥ parasvatvāpattir **dānam** | **svādhyāyo** 'dhyayanam | **karma**śabdaḥ kāmyavyatiriktānām anyeṣām api coditakarmaṇāṃ parigrahārthaḥ || 8||

_yad yogenātmadarśanam, na ca tadvākyārthāvadhāraṇād eva sidhyati | kiṃ tu śravaṇamanananididhyāsanebhya iti karmādhikāriṇo viduṣo 'pi kutascit kāraṇād dharmasaṃśaye parṣadadhīno nirṇaya iti tāṃ tāvad āha |_

	**catvāro vedadharmajñāḥ parṣat traividyam eva vā |**

**	sā brūte yaṃ sa dharmaḥ syād eko vādhyātmavittamaḥ || 9 ||**

**vedaḥ** prasiddhaḥ | **dharmo** dharmaśāstram | tadartha**jñāś** **catvāro** dharmanirṇayarūpakāthakarāḥ **parṣad** ity ucyate | ṛgyajuḥsāmavedās **traividyam** | tena cātra tadadhyetāras trayo brāhmaṇā lakṣyante | saiṣā tryavarā parṣad ity āha manuḥ |

	ṛgvedavid yajurvic ca sāmavedavid eva ca |

	avarā pariṣaj jñeyā dharmasaṃśayanirṇaye ||

atha vādhyātmavidāṃ śreṣṭha eko 'pi yam arthaṃ dharmatayā brūte sa eva dharmaḥ | ātmānam adhikṛtya pravṛttaṃ śāstram adhyātmam | bahūnāṃ tadvidāṃ madhye sātiśayajñāno **'dhyātmavittamaḥ** | pariṣattvaṃ brāhmaṇānām eva prāthamakalpikam | yad āha manuḥ |

	anāmnāteṣu dharmeṣu kathaṃ syād iti ced bhavet |

	yaṃ śiṣṭā brāhmaṇā brūyuḥ sa dharmaḥ syād aśaṅkitaḥ || iti |

anāmnāteṣu vākyapāṭhād evānirṇīyamāneṣv ity arthaḥ | aṅgirāḥ |

	cāturvidyo vitarkī ca aṅgavid dharmapāṭhakaḥ |

	trayaś cāśramiṇo vṛddhāḥ parṣad eṣā daśāvarā ||

	caturṇām api varṇānāṃ pāragā ye dvijottamāḥ |

	yathākramaṃ vinopāṅgaiś cāturvidyam iti smṛtam ||

	dharmasya parṣadaś caiva prāyaścittakarmasya ca |

	trayāṇāṃ yaḥ pramāṇajñaḥ sa vitarkī bhaved dvijaḥ ||

	śabde chandasi kalpe ca śikṣāyāṃ ca suniṣṭhitaḥ |

	jyotiḥśāstre ca kuśalaḥ sa nirukto 'aṅgavid bhavet ||

	vedavidyāvratasnātaḥ satyasaṃdho jitendriyaḥ |

	anekadharmaśāstrajñaḥ procyate dharmapāṭhakaḥ ||

	brahmacaryāśramād ūrdhvaṃ vṛddhā āśramiṇas trayaḥ |

	vadeyus tasya te dharmaṃ te mayā parikīrtitāḥ ||

manus tu,

	traividyo hetukas tarkī nairukto dharmapāṭhakaḥ |

	trayaś cāśramiṇaḥ pūrve parṣad eṣā daśāvarā ||

ity āha | hetuko 'numānajñaḥ | tarko 'syāstīti tarkī | saṃśayakoṭau prāmāṇikatvārope kṛte bādhakadarśanād bhavitavyam atra pramāṇeneti pratyayas tarkaḥ | sa ca vedāvirodhī grāhya ity uktaṃ tenaiva |

	ārṣa dharmopadeśaṃ ca vedaśāstrāvirodhinā |

	yas tarkeṇānusaṃdhatte sa dharmaṃ veda netaraḥ || iti |

ārṣaṃ smṛtipurāṇādi | upadeśo vedaḥ | tadvirodhinā vedādi(vi)varjitena tarkeṇa pūrvoktasvarūpeṇa | anusaṃdhānam upapādanā | pūrve gṛhasthādayaḥ | vṛddhā vṛddhatvopetā hi, daśāvareti, daśabhyo na nyūnā | aṅgirāḥ |

	catvāro vā trayo vāpi vedavanto 'gnihotriṇaḥ |

	brāhmaṇāḥ samavāyasthāḥ parṣad ity abhidhīyate ||

	anāhitāgnayo ye ca kevalaṃ vedapāragāḥ |

	pañcaite vedaśāstrajñāḥ parṣatsaṃjñā hy udāhṛtāḥ ||

	ye tu dharmavido viprāḥ kāryākāryavicakṣaṇāḥ |

	prāyaścittapraṇetāraḥ saptaite parikīrtitāḥ ||

	ekaviṃśatisaṃkhyākaiḥ śrutisannyāyapāragaiḥ |

	vedāṅgakuśalaiś caiva parṣattvaṃ tu parkalpayet ||

	yatīnāṃ satyatapasāṃ jñānavijñānacetasām |

	śirovratena snātānām eko 'pi pariṣad bhavet ||

	ye tu pūrvaṃ mayā proktāḥ sthitā yāyāvare pathi |

	trayo 'pi pariṣaj jñeyāḥ sarvapāpāpahārakāḥ ||

	eṣā tu laghukāryeṣu madhyameṣu tu madhyamā |

	mahāpātakiśodhyeṣu śataśo bhūva eva ca || iti |

yatiśāstraprasiddhaṃ sirovratam | eko 'pi pariṣat kāryakara ity arthaḥ | yāyāvaro gṛhasthaviśeṣaḥ | mahāpātakinaś ca te śodhyāś ca mahāpātakiśodhyāḥ || 9 ||

_dharmān vaktuṃ tadadhikāriṇo varṇān dvijāṃś cāha |_

	**brahmakṣatriyaviṭśūdrā varṇās tv ādyās trayo dvijāḥ |**

brāhmaṇakṣatriyavaiśyaśūdrāḥ pratyekaṃ varṇasaṃjñā bhavanti | brāhmaṇakṣatriyavaiśyās tu pratyekaṃ dvijasaṃñā jñeyāḥ ||

	**niṣekādyāḥ śmaśānāntās teṣāṃ vai mantrataḥ kriyāḥ || 10 ||**

**teṣāṃ** dvijānāṃ garbhādhānādyāḥ pretakarmaparyantāḥ **kriyā** mantraiḥ kāryāḥ | śūdrasya tu yāvad uktam upanayanāntasaṃskārānuvṛttau yamaḥ |

	śūdro 'py evaṃvidhaḥ kāryo vinā mantreṇa saṃskṛtaḥ |

	na kenacit samasṛjac chandasā taṃ prajāpatiḥ ||

sṛṣṭvānupanītavān | ato nopaneya ity arthaḥ | yac chrutiḥ: "gāyatryā brāhmaṇam asṛjata | triṣṭubhā rājanyam | jagatyā vaiśyam | na kenacic chandasā śūdram | asaṃskāryo vijñāyate" | asaṃskāryo 'nupaneyaḥ | brahmapurāṇam |

	vivāhamātrasaṃskāraṃ śūdro 'pi labhatāṃ sadā |

mātraśabdān mantrāṇāṃ vyāvṛttiḥ pūrvasaṃskārāṇāṃ vā | tadā ca vikalpaḥ | vihitatvād api teṣām | jātūkarṇyaḥ:

	iṣṭāpūrtau dvijātīnāṃ dharmau sāmāsikau matau |

	adhikārī bhavec chūdraḥ pūrtadharmeṇa vaidike ||

mahābhāratam |

	ekāgnikarma havanaṃ tretāyāṃ yaś ca hūyate |

	antarvedyāṃ ca yad dānam itṣṭam ity abhidhīyate ||

	vāpīkūpataḍāgādi devatāyatanāni ca |

	annapradānam ārāmaḥ pūrtam ity abhidhīyate ||

annadānagrahaṇam ayajñāṅgopalakṣaṇam | tathā ca jātūkarṇyaḥ |

	grahoparāge yad dānaṃ sūryasaṃkramaṇeṣu ca |

	dvādaśyādau ca yad dānaṃ pūrtam ity abhidhīyate || 10 ||

_garbhādānādīn saṃskārān gṛhyavihitasvarūpān api kālaviśeṣasaṃbandhitayā sārdhaślokadvayenādhunā vidhatte |_

	**garbhādhānam ṛtau puṃsaḥ savanaṃ spandhāt purā |**

**	ṣaṣṭhe 'ṣṭame vā sīmanto māsy ete jātakarma ca || 11 ||**

**	ahany ekādaśe nāma caturthe māsi niṣkramaḥ |**

**	ṣaṣṭhe 'nnaprāśanaṃ māsi cūḍā kāryā yathākulam || 12 ||**

**	evam enaḥ śamaṃ yāti bījagarbhasamudbhavam |**

garbha ādhīyate 'nena karmaṇeti **garbhādhānam**, tad **ṛtau** kāyam ity anyataḥ siddham | evaṃ prāg garbhacananāt **puṃsaḥ savanaṃ** puṃsavanākhyaṃ karma | **ṣaṣṭhe 'ṣṭame vā** garbhamāse **sīmantaḥ** sīmantonnayanam | **ete** āgate **jātakarma** | **ahany ekādaśe nāma** dheyam iti śeṣaḥ | ekādaśādisaṃkhyā janmanaḥ, tasya prakṛtatvāt | **caturthe māsi** niṣkramaṇam, sūryācandramasau draṣṭuṃ bahiḥ prasaraṇam | **ṣaṣṭhe** māsy **annaprāśanam** | **cūḍā** śikhā sā yeṣāṃ kule yasmin varṣe tathā yatsaṃkhyā kāryatayā smaryate tadanatikrameṇa kartavyā, yathākuladharmaṃ keśaveśān kārayed iti gṛhyaprasiddhā | evaṃ kṛteṣu saṃskāreṣu **enaḥ** pāpaṃ **bījagarbho**tthaṃ śāmyati | bījaṃ śukraśoṇitam | garbho jaṭharāntarasthito dehaḥ | tena jaṭharavāso lakṣyate | eno 'trāprāyatyam, mātuḥ pītāśanāder utpannam ity arthaḥ | etac ca cāturvarṇyābhiprāyam, na dvijātimātraviṣayam | tathā saty upanayanaṃ vidhāya vācyaṃ syāt | devalaḥ |

	citrakarma yathānekair aṅgair unmīlyate śanaiḥ |

	brāhmaṇyam api tadvat syāt saṃskārair vidhipūrvakaiḥ ||

ata eva manur dvijātyabhiprāyeṇopanayanaṃ vidhāyāha |

	gārbhair homair jātakarmacauḍamauñjīnibandhanaiḥ |

	baijikaṃ gārbhikaṃ caino dvijānām apamṛjyate ||

evam enaḥśāntyā prayujyamānā ete saṃskārāḥ puṃsavanāt pare pitrabhāve pitṛsthānīyena pitrvyādinā kāryā iti siddham | atra gharbhādhādivad ṛtvādayaḥ kālaviśeṣā ay anūdyante iti śāstravihitānāṃ kālāntarāṇāṃ na nivartakāḥ kiṃ tu tadupalakṣakāḥ | tatra śāstrāntarāṇi viśeṣābhidhāyakāni lakṣyante | tatra hārītaḥ |

	sakṛt saṃskṛtasaṃskārāḥ sīmantena dvijastriyaḥ |

	yaṃ yaṃ garbhaṃ prasūyante sa sarvaḥ saṃskṛto bhavet ||

sīmantonnayane baijavāpagṛhyam: "āpūryamāṇapakṣe yadā puṃsā nakṣatreṇa candramā yuktaḥ syāt" | devalaḥ |

	sakṛc ca saṃskṛtā nārī sarvagarbheṣu saṃskṛtā |

ata eva pāraskaraḥ: "atha puṃsavanavat sīmantonnayanaṃ prathamagarbhe" iti | sīmantonnayanaṃ prathamagarbhe 'bhidhatte | puṃsavanaṃ tu pratigarbham āvarteta | atha puṃsavanānavalobhanam, tatra āśvalāyanagṛhyam: "upaniṣadi garbhalambhane puṃsavanam anavalobhanaṃ ca | yadi nādhīyāt tṛtīye garbhe māse tiṣyeṇopoṣitāyāḥ svarūpavatsāyā gor dadhati dvau dvau māṣau yavaṃ ca dadhiprasṛtena prāśayet | kiṃ pibasi kiṃ pibasīti pṛṣṭvā puṃsavanam iti triḥ pratijānīyāt | evaṃ trīn prasṛtān | athāsya maṇḍalāgāracchāyāyāṃ dakṣiṇasyāṃ nāsikāyām ajitām oṣadhiṃ nastaḥ karoti | prajāvaj jīvaputrābhyāṃ vai hetukaprājāpatyasya sthālīpākasya hutvā hṛdayadeśam asyā ālabheta | yat te susīme hṛdaye hitam antaḥ prajāpatau | manye 'ham antar vidvāṃsam āha pautram aghaṃ niyām" iti | "apaśyaṃ tvā manasā dīdhyānaḥ" ityādi prajāvān mantraḥ | "agnir aitu prathamaḥ" ityādi jīvaputrā mantrāḥ | "tṛtīye māsi sīmantaṃ tiṣye vā śravaṇena" iti sāṃkyāyanam | jātakarmaṇi brahmapurāṇokto viśeṣaḥ |

	devāś ca pitaraś caiva putre jāte dvijanmanām |

	āyānti yasmāt tad ahaḥ pūjyaṃ puṇyaṃ ca sarvadā ||

	tatra dadyāt suvarṇaṃ ca bhūmiṃ gāṃ turagaṃ ratham |

	chatraṃ chāgaṃ ca mālyaṃ ca tilān veśma dhanaṃ bahu ||

	jātaśrāddhe pradadyāc ca pakvānnaṃ brāhmaṇeṣv api || iti |

etac ca nābhicchedāt prāk, nordhvam | tathā ca hārītaḥ: "jāte kumāre pitṝṇām āmodāt puṇyaṃ tad ahas tasmāt tilapūrṇāni pātrāṇi sahiraṇyāni brāhmaṇān āhūya pitṛbhyaḥ svadhāṃ kuryāt | prajāpataye ca prāṅ nābhicchedāt saṃskārapuṇyārthān kurvanti | chinnāyām aśaucam" iti | jyotiḥśāstrāt |

	mṛdudhruvacarakṣiprabheṣu vāratraye śubhe |

	gurau śukre 'tha vā kendre jātaṃ karma ca nāma ca ||

bhāni nakṣatrāṇi | bhaviṣyatpurāṇam |

	nāmadheyaṃ daśamyāṃ ca kecid icchanti pārthiva |

	dvādaśyām apare rātryāṃ māse pūrṇe tathā pare ||

	aṣṭādaśe 'hani tathā vadanty anye manīṣiṇaḥ |

	puṇye tithau muhūrte ca nakṣatre ca guṇānvite || iti |

gṛhyapariśiṣṭam: "jananād daśarātre vyuṣṭe śatarātre saṃvatsare vā nāmadhyakaraṇam, aśauce tu vyatikrānte nāmakarma vidhīyate" | nāyaṃ niyamaḥ, "nāmadheyaṃ daśamyām" ityādivacanavirodhāt | ato vikalpa **[27]** eva | svagṛhyāpekṣayā caitad vyavasthā | evaṃ ca "ahany ekādaśe dvādaśyāṃ vāsya kārayet" ityādi vivakṣitārtham eva, nāśaucāntopalakṣaṇārtham | tenāśauce 'pi tatkāryam | śaṅkhalikhitau: "daśamyām utthāpya piṇḍavardhanaṃ pitṝṇāṃ tatra sāṃnidhyam iti śruter brāhmaṇo 'gnāv āhutiṃ datvā pitṛn anumānya brāhmaṇān bhojayitvā tad ahar eva nāmakaraṇaṃ kuryāt | anyo vā kulavṛddhaś caturakṣaraṃ dvyakṣaraṃ vā ghoṣavad ādyantaratnasthaṃ puṃsām īkārāntaṃ strīṇām evaṃ kṛte nāmni śuci tat kulaṃ bhavati" | sūtikāṃ pūrvaṃ śayyāta utthāpya daśamyāṃ tithau daśame 'hanīty arthaḥ | piṇḍavardhanaṃ pūjā, tatsvarūpaṃ ca — brāhmaṇaḥ pūrvam āhutiṃ hutvā pitṝn anumānyābhyudayaśrāddhena pūjayitvā, kavargādīnāṃ tṛtīyādayo varṇā yaralavahāś ca ghoṣavantaḥ | teṣāṃ madhye yakārādayaś catasro 'ntasthāḥ | te nāmno 'ntarmadhe kāryāḥ | śeṣās tu ghoṣavanto nāmādau | baijavāpaḥ: "pitā nāma karoty ekākṣaraṃ vyakṣaraṃ tryakṣaraṃ caturakṣaram aparimitaṃ vā kṛtaṃ kuryān na taddhitam | īkārāntaṃ striyai" | yamaḥ |

	śarmā devaś ca viprasya varmā trātā ca bhūbhujaḥ |

	bhūtir dattaś ca vaiśyasya dāsaḥ śūdrasya kārayet ||

etāny uttarapadāni samāsarūpasya nāmnaḥ kāryāṇi | pūrvapadaniyamam āha manuḥ |

	māṅgalyaṃ brāhmaṇasy syāt kṣatriyasya balānvitam |

	vaiśyasya dhanasaṃyuktaṃ śūdrasya tu jugupsitam ||

tathā |

	strīṇāṃ sukhodyam akrūraṃ (?) vispaṣṭārthaṃ manoharam |

	māṅgalyaṃ dīrghavarṇāntam āśīrvādābhidhānavat ||

niṣkramaṇe yamokto viśeṣaḥ |

	tatas tṛtīye kartavyaṃ māsi sūryasya sūryasya darśanam |

vṛddhaśātātapaḥ |

	prākcūḍākaraṇād bālaḥ prāg annaprāśanāc chiśuḥ |

**[28]**	kumāras tu sa vijñeyo yāvan mauñjīnibandhanam ||

	śiśor abhyukṣaṇaṃ proktaṃ bālasyācamanaṃ smṛtam |

	rajasvalādisaṃsparśe snātavyaṃ tu kumārakaiḥ ||

brahmapurāṇe |

	mātāpitror athocchiṣṭaṃ bālo bhuñjan bhavet sukhī | iti |

dakṣaḥ |

	jātamātraḥ śiśus tāvad yāvad aṣṭau samā gataḥ |

	sa hi garbhasamo jñeyo vyaktimātraprakāśitaḥ ||

	bhakṣyābhakṣye tathāpeye vācyāvācye tathānṛte |

	asmin kāle na doṣaḥ syāt sa yāvan nopanīyate ||

etad abhakṣyabhakṣaṇāpeyapānānumananaṃ mātāpitror ucchiṣṭamātraviṣayaṃ na tu jatibhraṃśakarādyabhakṣāpeyānnapānaviṣayam, saṃskārādyanarhatvaprasaṅgāt | dṛśyate hi smṛtiṣu prācuryeṇa "vasante brāhmaṇam upanayīta grīṣme rājanyaṃ śaradi vaiśyam" ityādinānupahatajātyādyāśrayaṇenaivopanayanādīti | purāṇam |

	caturthe māsi kartavyaṃ śiśoś candrasya darśanam |

	dvādaśe 'hanit rājendra śiśor niṣkarmaṇaṃ gṛhāt ||

	caturthe māsi kartavyaṃ tathānyeṣāṃ mataṃ vibho ||

annaprāśane viśeṣam āha yamaḥ |

	tato 'nnaprāśanaṃ ṣaṣṭhe māsi kāryaṃ yathāvidhi |

	aṣṭame vāpi kartavyaṃ yad veṣṭaṃ maṅgalaṃ kule ||

śaṅkhaḥ: "saṃvatsare 'nnaprāśanam ardharsaṃvatsara ity eke" | laugākṣiḥ: "ṣaṣṭhe māsy annaprāśanaṃ danteṣu jāteṣu" | mārkaṇḍeyaḥ |

	devatāpuratas tasya dhātry utsaṅgagatasya ca |

	alaṃkṛtasya dātavyam annaṃ pātre 'tha kāñcane ||

	madhvājyakanakopetaṃ prāṅmukhaṃ prāśayec chiśum |

	kṛtaprāśam athotsaṅgād dhātrī bālaṃ samutsṛjet ||

	devāgrato 'tha vinyasya śilpabhāṇḍāni sarvaśaḥ |

	śāstrāṇi caiva śastrāṇi tataḥ paśyet tu lakṣaṇam ||

	prathamaṃ yat spṛśed bālas tato bhāṇḍaṃ svayaṃ tadā |

	jīvikā tasya bālasya tenaiva tu bhaviṣyati ||

**[29]**	sarvaiḥ svajanmadivase snātair maṅgalavāribhiḥ |

	gurudevāgniviprāś ca pūjanīyā viśeṣataḥ ||

	svanakṣatraṃ ca pitaras tathā devaḥ prajāpatiḥ |

	pratisaṃvatsaraṃ yatnāt kartavyaś ca mahotsavaḥ ||

pitṛpūjā śrāddham | viṣṇudharmottare |

	janmanakṣatrage some śiraḥsnātena yatnataḥ |

	pūjā somasya kartavyā nakṣatrasya tathātmanaḥ ||

	śrāddhaṃ kuryāt prayatnena vahnibrāhmaṇatarpaṇam |

	surāṇām arcanaṃ keśavasya viśeṣataḥ |

	sarvasv ālaṃkṛtis tiṣṭhed dhautavsāś ca mānavaḥ |

	nirmalāni ca dhāryāṇi dantakeśanakhāni ca ||

caule yamo viśeṣam āha |

	tathā saṃvatsare pūrṇe cūḍākarma vidhīyate |

	dvitīye vā tṛtīye vā kartavyaṃ śruticodanāt ||

śaṅkhalikhitau: "tṛtīye varṣe cūḍākarma pañcame vā" | laugākṣiḥ: "tṛtīyasya varṣasya bhūyiṣṭhe gate cūḍāḥ kārayet | dakṣiṇataḥ kapūjā vasiṣṭhānām ubhayato 'trikaśyapānāṃ muṇḍā bhṛgavaḥ pañcacūḍā aṅgiraso vājim ekamaṅgalārtham | śikhino 'nye yathākuladharmaṃ vā | śuddhapakṣasya puṇyāhe parvaṇi vā" | kapūjā cūḍā | vājiḥ keśapaṅktiḥ | vyāsaḥ |

	nakṣatre 'pi na kartavyaṃ yasmiñ jāto bhaven naraḥ |

	na bhadrapadayoḥ kāryaṃ naivāgneyeṣu bhārata ||

	dāruṇeṣu ca sarveṣu dūṣṭatārāṃ tu varjayet |

	jyotiṣe yāni coktāni tāni sarvāṇi kārayet ||

	vāraṃ śanaiścarādityasomānāṃ rātrim eva ca |

	tithiṃ pratipadaṃ riktāṃ viṣṭiṃ caiva vivarjayet ||

**[30]**	aśvinīśravaṇasvāticitrātiṣyāḥ punarvasuḥ |

	dhaniṣṭhārevatījyeṣṭhā mṛgahasteṣu kārayet ||

	śubheṣv aṃśakakendreṣu śubheṣu karaṇeṣu ca |

	kṣauraṃ prātaḥ prakurvīta āyurbalavivardhanam ||

	hastān trayaṃ mṛgaśiraḥ śravaṇān trayaṃ ca 

		pūṣāśviśakragurubhāni punarvasū ca |

	kṣaure tu karmaṇi hitāny udayekṣaṇe vā 

		yuktāni coḍupatinā yadi śastatārā || 11–12 ||

	**tūṣṇīm etāḥ kriyāḥ strīṇāṃ vivāhas tu samantrakaḥ || 13 ||**

**etā** hi jātakarmādyāḥ **kriyāḥ strīṇām** amantrakāḥ **vivāhaḥ** punaḥ **samantrakāḥ** | gṛhyavihitānāṃ saṃskārāṇām iha parāmarśāt tatra ca tadaṅgānām apy upadeśāt sāṅgānāṃ tūṣṇīṃbhāvo veditavyaḥ | ata eva manuḥ |

	amantrikā tu kāryeyaṃ strīṇām āvṛd aśeṣataḥ |

	saṃskārārthaṃ śarīrasya yathākālaṃ yathākramam ||

āvṛt kriyā | aśeṣataḥ sāṅgā | yathākramam iti vacanāt saṃskāreṣu kramānatikramo vidheya iti darśayati | tadatikrame sarvaprāyaścittaṃ kārayet | kālātikrame kātyāyana āha |

	devatānāṃ viparyāse juhotiṣu kathaṃ bhavet |

	sarvaṃ prāyaścittaṃ hutvā kramaśo juhuyāt punaḥ ||

	saṃskārāś ca viyujyeran svakālaś ca kathaṃcana |

	hutvā tad eva kartavyaṃ tad bhūpa pātayed adhaḥ ||

sarvaprāyaścittaṃ laugākṣir āha: "sarvāṇi prāyaścittāni manojyotir iti saptabhiḥ" | gobhilaś caulādhikāre: "etayaivāvṛtā striyās tūṣṇīṃ mantreṇa tu homaḥ" | mārkaṇḍeyaḥ |

	prāpte 'tha pañcame varṣe apragupte janārdane |

	ṣaṣṭhīṃ pratipadaṃ caiva varjayitvā tathāṣṭamīm ||

	riktāṃ pañcadaśīṃ caiva saurabhaumadinaṃ tathā |

	evaṃ suniścite kāle vidyārambhaṃ tu kārayet ||

**[31\**	pūjayitvā hariṃ lakṣmīṃ devīṃ caiva sarasvatīm |

	svavidyāsūtrakārāṃś ca svāṃ vidyāṃ ca viśeṣataḥ ||

	eteṣām eva devānāṃ nāmnā tu juhuyād dhṛtam |

	dakṣiṇābhir dvijendrāṇāṃ kartavyaṃ catra pūjanam ||

	prāṅmukho gurur āsīno vāruṇāśāmukhaṃ śiśum |

	adhyāpayeta prathamaṃ dvijāśīrbhiḥ supūjitam ||

	tataḥ prabhṛty anadhyāyān varjanīyān vivarjayet |

	aṣṭamīdvitayaṃ caiva pakṣānte ca dinadvayam ||

	aśauca indrayātrāyāṃ bhūkampe rāhudarśane |

	vyatīpāte cāhorātram ulkāpāte tathaiva ca ||

smṛtyantaram |

	mātṛkānyāsaṃ gaṇitaṃ ca kumāraṃ śikṣāpayet || 13 ||

	**garbhāṣṭame 'ṣṭame vābde brāhmaṇasyopanāyanam |**

**	rājñām ekādaśe saike viśām eke yathākulam || 14 ||**

upanetāraṃ pratyupaneyasya prayojakavyāpāra **upanāyanam** | tac copanayanād anyad eva | ata evāha budhaḥ |

	garbhāṣṭame varṣe vasante brāhmaṇa ātmānam upanāyayet | iti |

imam eva ca vidhim āśritya śaunako mantraṃ vidhatta: "jānv anvācyopasaṃgṛhyādhīhi bhoḥ sāvitrīṃ bho anubrūhi" iti | garbhād aṣṭamo **garbhāṣṭamaḥ**, garbhasahacarito 'bdo garbhas tad(ma)pekṣyāṣṭama iti lyablope pañcamī | upanayanasyāpy ayam eva kālaḥ śaunakenoktaḥ: "aṣṭame varṣe brāhmaṇam upanayed garbhāṣṭame caikādaśe kṣatriyaṃ dvādaśe vaiśyam" iti | 

	atha kāmyā upanayanakālāḥ | tatra manuḥ |

	brahmacarcasakāmasya kāryaṃ viprasya pañcame |

	rājño balārthinaḥ ṣaṣṭhe vaiśyasyehārthino 'ṣṭame ||

īhā ceṣṭā | **[32]** gautamaḥ: "upanayanam aṣṭame pañcame navame vā | kāmyaṃ garbhādisaṃkhyāvarṣāṇām upanayanasyāṣṭamaṃ varṣaṃ nityaḥ kālo navamaṃ pañcamaṃ ca kāmyaḥ" | āpastambaḥ: "saptame brahmavarcasakāmam aṣṭama āyuṣkāmaṃ navame tejaskāmaṃ daśame 'nnādikāmam ekādaśa indriyakāmaṃ dvādaśe paśukāmam" | atropanayītety anuṣaṅgaḥ | purāṇāt |

	naṣṭe candre 'stage śukre niraṃśe caiva bhāskare |

	kartavyaṃ nopanayanaṃ nānadhyāye galagrahe ||

rāśeḥ prathamabhāgasthitasūryo niraṃśaḥ | caturthī saptamī navamī trayodaśī galagrahaḥ |

	hastān traye puṣyadhaniṣṭhayoś ca pauṣṇāśvisaumyād iti viṣṇum eṣu |

	śaste tithau candrabalopayukte kāryo dvijānām upanāyano vidhiḥ ||

gobhilaḥ: "yad ahar upoṣyan māṇavako bhavati praga evainaṃ tadahan bhojayanti | kuśalīkārayanti | āplāvaganty alaṃ kurvanti | ahatena vāsasācchadayanti" | prage prātar ity arthaḥ | śaṅkhaḥ: "payoyavāgvāmikṣāhāraḥ kramaśastrayāṇām upanayanāhni garbhādhānādiṣu saṃskāreṣu daśa daśa viprā bhojyāḥ" | yad āha kātyāyanaḥ |

	garbhādhādisarveṣu brāhmaṇān bhojayed daśa || 14 ||

	**upanīya guruḥ śiṣyaṃ mahāvyāhṛtipūrvakam |**

**	vedam adhyāpayed enaṃ śaucācārāṃś ca śikṣayet || 15 ||**

yathāvidhy upanayanakarmaṇā **śiṣyam** anuśāsanīyaṃ pratyāsannaṃ kṛtvā **gurur** ācāryo **vyāhṛtipūrvakaṃ** **vedam adhyāpayec chaucācārāṃś ca** grāhayet | gurugrahaṇāt pitaivopanayanādi **[33]** kuryād iti gamayati | tasya yogyatāvirahe cānya ācāryaḥ syāt | upanayanena ca śiṣyasyācāryaṃ prati saṃbandhaviśeṣātmikā pratyāsattiḥ kriyate | na tu deśasaṃnikarṣātmikaiva | upanetṛguṇān āha āpastambaḥ: "tamaso vā eṣa tamaḥ praviśati yad avidvān upanayate yac cāvidvān iti brāhmaṇānām | tasmād abhijanavidyāsamupetaṃ samāhitaṃ saṃskartāram īpseta" | yaiś cāvidvān upanayate so 'pi tamaḥ praviśatīty arthaḥ | gāyatryadipradhānaṃ copanayanam | yad āha kātyāyanaḥ: "gātryā brāhmaṇam upanayīta triṣṭubhā rājanyam | jagatyā vaiśyaṃ sarveṣāṃ vā gāyatrīm" | anubrūyād iti śeṣaḥ | laugākṣiḥ: "tat savitur vareṇyam iti brāhmaṇasya | tāṃ savitur iti rājanyasya | viśvā rūpāṇīti vaiśyasya | oṃ bhūr bhuvaḥ svar ity uktvā tat savitur vareṇyam iti sāvitrīṃ trir āha paccho'rdharcaśaḥ sarvām antataḥ" | mahāvyāhṛtisaṃkhyām āha manuḥ |

	oṃkārapūrvikās tisro mahāvyāhṛtayo 'vyayāḥ |

	tripadā caiva sāvitrī vijñeyaṃ brahmaṇo mukham ||

mukham ārambhaḥ | tataś ca na mahāvyāhṛtaya evādhyāpanārambhe prayoktavyāḥ | kiṃ tu praṇavo gāyatrī ca | etac ca prathamādhyāpanaprārambhe na tv ahar ahaḥ, mukham iti vyapadeśāt | praṇavamahāvyāhṛtitrikaṃ ca svarūpato manur āha |

	akāraṃ cāpy ukāraṃ ca makāraṃ ca prajāpatiḥ |

	vedatrayān niravahad bhūr bhuvaḥ svar itīti ca ||

gāyatrīm api viśeṣata āha |

**[34]**	tribhya eva tu vedebhyaḥ pādaṃ pādam adūduhat |

	tad ity ṛco 'syāḥ sāvitryāḥ parameṣṭhī prajāpatiḥ ||

tathā |

	adhyeṣyamāṇaṃ tu gurur nityakālam atandritaḥ |

	adhīṣva bhor iti brūyād virāmo 'stv iti cāramet ||

	adhyeṣyamāṇas tv ācānto yathāśāstram atandritaḥ |

	brahmāñjalikṛto 'dhyāpyo laghuvāsā jitendriyaḥ ||

brahmāñjaliṃ sa evāha |

	saṃhatya hastāv adhyeyaṃ sa hi brahmāñjaliḥ smṛtaḥ || 15 ||

_śaucāt prācīnam ācāraṃ tāvad āha |_

	**divāsaṃdhyāsu karṇasthabrahmasūtra udaṅmukhaḥ |**

**	kuryān mūtrapurīṣe tu rātrau ced dakṣiṇāmukhaḥ || 16 ||**

ahani saṃdhyayoś codaṅmukho rātrau dakṣiṇāmukho vāma(dakṣiṇa)karṇāropitayajñopavīto mūtrapurīṣāv utsṛjet | manuḥ |

	tiraskṛtyoccaret kāṣṭhaṃ patraṃ loṣṭaṃ tṛṇāni vā |

	niyamya prayato vācaṃ saṃvītāṅgo 'vaguṇṭhitaḥ ||

kāṣṭhādibhir bhūmim antardhāya malam utsṛjed ity arthaḥ | saṃvītāṅgaḥ prāvṛtāṅgaḥ | avaguṇṭhitaḥ prāvṛtaśirāḥ | yamaḥ |

	śiraḥ prāvṛtya kurvīta śakṛnmūtravisarjanam |

	ayajñiyair anārdraiś ca tṛṇair ācchādya medinīm ||

	pratyaṅmukhas tu pūrvāhṇe 'parāhṇe prāṅmukhas tathā |

	udaṅmukhas tu madhyāhne niśāyāṃ dakṣiṇāmukhaḥ ||

manuḥ |

	chāyāyām andhakāre vā rātrāv ahani vā dvijaḥ |

	yathāsukhamukhaḥ kuryāt prāṇabādhamayeṣu ca ||

aṅgirāḥ |

	utthāya paścime yāme rātrer ācamya codakam |

	antardhāya tṛṇair bhūmiṃ śiraḥ prāvṛtya vasasā ||

	vācaṃ niyamya yatnena ṣṭhīvanocchvāsavarjitaḥ |

	kuryān mūtrapurīṣe ca śucau deśe samāhitaḥ || 16 ||

**[35]** _śaucam āha |_

	**gṛhītaśiśnaś cotthāya mṛdbhir abhyuddhṛtair jalaiḥ |**

**	gandhalepakṣayakaraṃ śaucaṃ kuryād atandritaḥ || 17 ||**

yathā malasaṃsargo na bhavati tathā vāmahastena śiśnaṃ gṛhītvotthāya deśāntara upaviśya kamaṇḍalvādin**oddhṛtajalair** **mṛdbhiś** ca **gandhalepakṣayakaraṃ** malagandhaharaṃ **śaucam** analasaḥ kuryāt | bhāradvājaḥ |

	athāpakṛṣya viṇmūtraṃ kāṣṭhaloṣṭatṛṇādinā |

	śaucaṃ yathārthavat kuryād dṛḍhaṃ vidhṛtamehanaḥ ||

mehanaṃ liṅgam | purāṇāt |

	mārjanaṃ vāmahastena vīraṇādyair ayajñiyaiḥ |

devalaḥ |

	ā śaucān notsṛjec chiśnaṃ prasrāvoccārayoḥ svayam |

vivasvān |

	ratnimātraṃ jalaṃ tyaktvā kuryāc chaucam anuddhṛte |

	paścāt tu śodhayet tīrtham anyathā na śucir bhavet ||

yamaḥ |

	nāharen mṛttikāṃ vipraḥ kūlāt sasikatāt tathā |

	tathā vāpītaḍāgeṣu nāhared bāhyato mṛdam ||

	āharej jalamadhyāt tu parato maṇibandhanāt ||

purāṇāt |

	valmīkān mūṣikotkhātān mṛdam antarjalāt tathā |

	śaucāvaśiṣṭāṃ gehāc ca nādadyāl lepasaṃbhavām ||

	[antaḥ prānyavapannāṃ ca halotkhātāṃ na kardamāt | ]

[vāpīkūpādivyatiriktaviṣayo 'antrajalamṛttikāpratiṣedhaḥ ] | bhāradvājaḥ |

	noṣarān na śmaśānāc ca na mṛdaṃ mūṣakasthalāt |

	na mārgān na jalāj jātu nādadyāt kuḍyataḥ kvacit ||

devalaḥ |

	dharmavid dakṣiṇaṃ hastaṃ nādhaḥśauce niyojayet |

	tathaiva vāmahastena nābher ūrdhvaṃ na śodhayet ||

śātātapaḥ |

	ārdrāmalakamātrās tu grāsā indukṣaye smṛtāḥ |

	tathaivāhutayaḥ sarvāḥ śaucārthe caiva mṛttikāḥ ||

**[36]**	ekā liṅge kare savye tisro dve hastayor dvayoḥ |

	mūtraśaucaṃ samākhyātaṃ śukre tu dviguṇaṃ bhavet ||

manuḥ |

	ekā liṅge gude tisras tathā vāmakare daśa |

	ubhayoḥ sapta dātavyā mṛdaḥ śuddhim abhīpsatā ||

	etac chaucaṃ gṛhasthānāṃ dviguṇaṃ brahmacāriṇām |

	triguṇaṃ syād vanasthānāṃ yatīnāṃ ca caturguṇam ||

dakṣaḥ |

	ardhaprasṛtimātrā tu prathamā mṛttikā smṛtā |

	dvitīyā ca tṛtīyā ca tadardhena prakīrtitā ||

evam api gandhalepakṣayo yadi na bhavet tadā mṛdo 'dhikā grāhyāḥ parimāṇataḥ saṃkhyāto vā | tatra aṅgirāḥ |

	prathamā prasṛtir jñeyā dvitīyā tu tadardhikā |

	tṛtīyā mṛttikā jñeyā tribhāgakarapūraṇī ||

vasiṣṭhaḥ |

	pañcāpāne daśaikasminn ubhayoḥ sapta mṛttikāḥ ||

śaṅkhaḥ |

	mehane mṛttikāḥ sapta liṅge dve parikīrtite |

	ekasmin viṃśatir haste dvayor jñeyāś caturdaśa ||

mehaṇaḥ(naṃ) pāyuḥ | brahmacāriviṣayam etat | hārītaḥ: "daśa savye ṣaṭ pṛṣṭhe saptobhābhyāṃ tisṛbhiḥ pādau parkṣālayet" | vṛddhapārāśaraḥ |

	upaviṣṭas tu viṇmūtraṃ kartuṃ yas tan na vindati |

	sa kuryād ardhaśaucaṃ tu svasya śaucasya sarvadā || 

[gandhalepakṣaye saty apy ardhamitā saṃkhyā pūraṇīyā] | yad āha dakṣaḥ |

	nyūnādhikaṃ na kartavyaṃ śaucaśuddhim abhīpsatā |

	prāyaścittena yujyeta vihitātikrame kṛte ||

	yathāvidhikṛte śauce gandhaś cen nāpagacchati |

tatrāha manuḥ |

	yāvan nāpaity amedhyākto gandho lepaś ca tatkṛtaḥ |

	tāvan mṛd vāri cādeyaṃ sarvāsu dravyaśuddhiṣu ||

manasas tuṣṭyabhāve tu devala āha |

	yāvan na śuddhiṃ manyeta tāvac chaucaṃ vidhīyate | **[37]**

brahmapurāṇāt |

	ādyantayos tu śaucānām adbhiḥ prakṣālanaṃ smṛtam |

	aśeṣalepanāśāya bhāvaśuddhaya eva ca ||

ādipurāṇāt |

	strīśūdrayor ardhamānaṃ proktaṃ śaucaṃ manīṣibhiḥ |

	divāśaucasya niśy ardhaṃ pathi pādo vidhīyate ||

	ārtaḥ kuryād yathāśakti śaktaḥ kuryād yathoditam || 17 ||

	**antarjānu śucau deśa upaviṣṭa udaṅmukhaḥ |**

**	prāg vā brāhmeṇa tīrthena dvijo nityam upaspṛśet || 18 ||**

anupahate deśe prāṅmukha udaṅmukho vopaviśyāntarjānu pāṇinā brāhmeṇa tīrthena dvijanmā sarvadāvācet | gautamaḥ: "śucau deśa āsīno dakṣiṇaṃ bāhuṃ jānvantarā kṛtvā yajñopavīty ā maṇibandhanāt pāṇī prakṣālya vāgyato hṛdaye spṛśaṃs tricaturthā apa ācāmet | pādau cābhyukṣet | khāni copaspṛśet | śīrṣaṇyāni mūdhani ca dadyāt" | āca(cā)med ity anuvṛttau smṛtyantaram |

	kūrparāntaḥ karau kṛtvā prāṅmukho vāpy udaṅmukhaḥ |

	pārṣṇī cāsaṃspṛśann adbhiḥ prakṛtisthābhir eva ca ||

kūrpare jānunī | vṛddhapārāśaraḥ |

	kṛtvātha śaucaṃ prakṣālya pādau hastau ca mṛjjalaiḥ |

	nibaddhaśikha āsīno dvija ācāmam ācaret ||

	kṛtvopavītaṃ savye 'ṃse vāṅmanaḥkāyasaṃyataḥ ||

devalaḥ |

	prathamaṃ prāṅmukhaṃ sthitvā pādau prakṣālayec chanaiḥ |

	udaṅmukho vā daivatye paitṛke dakṣiṇāmukhaḥ ||

	śikhāṃ baddhvā vasitvā dve nirṇikte vāsasī śubhe |

	tūṣṇīṃ bhūtvā samādhāya na krudhyan na vilokayan ||

	na gacchan na śayānaś ca na hvalan na prāmṛśan |

	na hasan naiva jalpaṃś ca nātmānaṃ caiva vīkṣayan ||

**[38]**	keśān nīvīm adhaḥkāyam aspṛśan dharaṇīm api |

	yadi spṛśati caitāni bhūyaḥ prakṣālayet karam ||

	ity evam adbhir ājānu prakṣālya caraṇau pṛthak |

	hastāv ā maṇibandhābhyāṃ paścād āsīta saṃyataḥ ||

	athāmbu prathamāt tīrthād dakṣiṇāt triḥ pibet samam |

	aśabdam anavasrāvam abahirjāv abudbudam ||

na halan na calan | maṇibandhaḥ brahmatīrthamūlam | prathamaṃ tīrthaṃ brāhmatīrtham, dakṣinād dakṣiṇakarād ity arthaḥ | bhāradvājaḥ |

	saṃhatāṅgulinā toyaṃ gṛhītvā pāṇinā dvijaḥ |

	muktāṅguṣṭhakaniṣṭhe tu śeṣeṇācamanaṃ caret ||

	māṣamajjanamātrās tu saṃgṛhya triḥ pibed apaḥ |

	āyataṃ pūrvataḥ kṛtvā gokarṇākṛtivat karam ||

hārītaḥ |

	ārdravāsāḥ sthalasthas tu yady ācāmen narādhamaḥ |

	vastraniścotanaṃ tasya dehāt pretāḥ pibanti hi ||

	kuryād ācamanaṃ nityaṃ prāṅmukho vāpy udaṅmukhaḥ |

	jalastho vā sthastho vā dvayor vā samavasthitaḥ ||

	jalastho jalakāryeṣu sthalasthaḥ sthalakarmasu |

	ubhayos tūbhayasthas tu karmasv adhikṛto bhavet ||

gobhilaḥ |

	jānubhyām ūrdhvam ācamya jale tiṣṭhan na duṣyati |

	tābhyām adhas tathā tiṣṭhan nāca(cā)men na vicakṣaṇaḥ ||

likhitaḥ: "uddhṛtya parīkṣitābhir akṣārābhir aśṛtābhir abudbudābhir aśūdrāśuddhyekapāṇyāvarjitābhir āca(cā)met" | adbhir iti śeṣaḥ | āpastambaḥ: "bhūmigatāsv apsv ācamya prayato bhavati | yaṃ vā pūyate śucācamayet | na varṣadārāsv āca(cā)met | na pradarodake" | **[39]** apa āca(cā)med ity anuvṛttau vasiṣṭhaḥ: "pradarād api yā gos tarpaṇasamarthāḥ | na gandharasaduṣṭābhir yāś ca syur aśubhāgamāḥ" | pradaro gartaḥ | pracetāḥ | 

	anuṣṇahīnaśītābhiḥ pūtābhir vastracakṣuṣā |

	hṛdgābhir aphenābhis triś catur vādbhir ācamet || 1.18 ||

_brahmatīrthasya lakṣaṇam āha prasaṅgāt tīrthāntarāṇāṃ ca |_

	**kaniṣṭādeśinyaṅguṣṭhamūlāny agraṃ karasya ca |**

**	prajapatipitṛbrahmadevatīrthāny anukramāt || 1.19 ||**

kaniṣṭhāmūlaṃ prajāpatitīrtham, pradeśinīmūlaṃ pitṛtīrtham. aṅguṣṭhamūlaṃ brahmatīrtham, hastāgraṃ devatīrtham ca jānīyāt | kaniṣṭhā hrasvāṅguliḥ | deśiṇī tarjanī | aṅguṣṭhaḥ prasiddhaḥ | hārītaḥ: "brāhmeṇa tīrthena cāca(cā)met | āvapanahomatarpaṇāni prājāpatyena kuryāt | mārjanācamanabalikarmabhojanāni daivena | pitrarthāni pitryeṇa | pratigraham āgneyena" | āgneyaṃ pāṇimadhye | āvapanaṃ nirvāpaḥ | keśānāṃ mārjanam, na prokṣaṇam | mārkaṇḍeyapurāṇāt |

	nāndīmukhānāṃ kurvīta prājñaḥ piṇḍodakakriyām |

	prājāpatyena tīrthena yac ca kiṃcit prajāpateḥ ||

bhaviṣyapurāṇe |

	kamaṇḍalūpasparśanaṃ dadhiprāśanam eva ca |

	somatīrthena rājendra sadā kuryād vicakṣaṇaḥ ||

	lājahomaṃ tathā dohaṃ prājāpatyena kārayet ||

yogayājñavalkyaḥ |

	aṅguṣṭhamūle brāhmaṃ syād daivaṃ tv aṅgulimūrdhani |

	prājāpatyaṃ tu mūle syān madhye saumyaṃ pratiṣṭhitam ||

madhye talamadhya ity arthaḥ || 1.19 ||

	**triḥ prāśyāpo dvir unmṛjya kāny adbhiḥ samupaspṛśet |**

trīn vārān apaḥ pītvā vāradvayaṃ mukhaṃ saṃmṛjya chidrāṇy adbhiḥ saṃspṛśet | **[40]** devalaḥ |

	dvis tathāṅguṣṭhamūlena parimṛjyāt tato mukham |

	nāgrāṅgulyā na pṛṣṭhair vā parimṛjyāt kathaṃcana ||

	**adbhis tu prakṛtisthābhir hīnābhiḥ phenabudbudaiḥ || 1.20 ||**

**	hrtkaṇṭhatālugābhis tu yathāsaṃkhyaṃ dvijātayaḥ |**

**	śudhyeran strī ca śūdraś ca sakṛt spṛṣṭābhir antataḥ || 1.21 ||**

adbhir avikṛtābhiḥ phenabudbudarahitābhir hṛdayakaṇṭhatālugāminībhir yathāsaṃkhyaṃ brāhmaṇakṣatriyavaiśyāḥ śudhyanti | strīśūdrau tu mukhasyāntenauṣṭhadvayenaikavāraṃ spṛṣṭābhiḥ | tathā cācamanīyaṃ yathā hṛdayaṃgamā bhavanti | dakṣaḥ |

	prakṣālya hastau pādau ca triḥ pibed ambu vīkṣitam |

	saṃvṛtyāṅguṣṭhamūlena dviḥ pramṛjyāt tato mukham ||

alomakau cauṣṭhau saṃvṛtyety arthaḥ | yamaḥ |

	rātrāv anīkṣitenaiva śuddhir uktā manīṣiṇām |

	udakenāturāṇāṃ ca tathoṣṇenoṣṇapāyinām ||

uṣṇapāyino dīkṣitāḥ | purāṇam |

	dakṣiṇaṃ tu karaṃ kṛtvā gokarākṛtivat punaḥ |

	triḥ pibed īkṣitaṃ toyam āsyaṃ dviḥ parimārjayet ||

	ādau śiras tathābhyukṣya tisṛbhir mukham ālabhet |

	yathoktavidhinā khāni tataḥ spṛṣṭvā tu śudhyati ||

tisṛbhir aṅgulibhir ity arthaḥ | manuḥ |

	trir ācāmed apaḥ pūrvaṃ dviḥ pramṛjyāt tato mukham |

	khāni copaspṛśed adbhir ātmānaṃ śira eva ca ||

dakṣaḥ |

	madhyamābhir mukhaṃ pūrvaṃ tisṛbhiḥ samupaspṛśet |

	aṅguṣṭhadeśinībhyāṃ ca nāsike tadanantaram ||

	aṅguṣṭhānāmikābhyāṃ ca cakṣuṣī samupaspṛśet | **[41]**

	kaniṣṭhāṅguṣṭhayoḥ śrotraṃ nābhim aṅguṣṭhakena ca |

	talena hṛdayaṃ spṛṣṭvā sarvābhiḥ śira eva tu |

	bāhū cāgreṇa saṃspṛśya tataḥ śuddho bhaven naraḥ ||

aṅguṣṭhānantrā deśinī | anāmikā, upakaniṣṭhikā | talaṃ pāṇimadhyam | vaiyāghrapadyaḥ |

	srotaḥsthānāni sarvāṇi spṛṣṭvā spṛṣṭvā viśudhyati |

	ācāman brāhmaṇo nityam ity āha bhagavā bhṛguḥ ||

	aṅguṣṭhena spṛśen nābhiṃ saṃyuktena kaniṣṭhayā |

	urastalenāṅgulibhiḥ śiraḥ paścāt tu pañcabhiḥ ||

	aṃsau spṛṣṭvā karāgreṇa toyaṃ spṛṣṭvā samāhitaḥ |

	saṃsmṛtya padmanābhaṃ ca vipraḥ samyag viśudhyat ||

bhaviṣyatpurāṇe |

	aṅguṣṭho 'gnir mahābāho prokto vāyuḥ pradeśinī |

	anāmikā tathā sūryaḥ kaniṣṭhā candramāḥ smṛtaḥ ||

	prajāpatir madhyamā tu jñeyā bharatasattama ||

yamaḥ |

	tāvan nopaspṛśed vidvān yāvad vāmena saṃspṛśet |

jalam iti śeṣaḥ |

	vāme hi dvādaśādityā varuṇas tridaśeśvaraḥ ||

vyāsaḥ |

	anuddhṛtābhir ācāmet kāmaṃ tiṣṭhann api dvijaḥ |

	āturaś cec chayāno 'pi paśyan bhīto diśas tathā ||

smṛtyantaram |

	tāmrāśmanārikelābjaveṇukālābucarmabhiḥ |

	svastenāpi cācāmet sarvadā śucir eva saḥ ||

na kevalam aninditahastenety apiśabdārthaḥ | baudhāyanaḥ: "pādaprakṣālanāc cheṣeṇa na cācāmed yady ācāmed bhūmau srāvayitvācāmet | na sabudbudābhir na saphenābhir noṣṇābhir na kṣārābhir na vivarṇābhir na kaluṣābhiḥ | na hasan na jalpan na tiṣṭhan na vilokayan na prahvo na praṇato na muktaśikho nābaddhakaccho **[42]** na bahirjānur na veṣṭitaśirā na baddhakakṣo na tvaramāṇo nāyajñopavīto na prasāritapādaḥ śabdam akurvan trir apo hṛdayaṃgamāḥ pibet" | devalaḥ |

	sopānatko jalastho vā muktakeśo 'pi vā dvijaḥ |

	uṣṇīṣī vāpi nācāmed vastreṇāveṣṭya vā śiraḥ ||

āpastambaḥ: "na varṣadhārāsv ācāmet" | yamaḥ |

	apaḥ karanakhaspṛṣṭā ya ācāmati vai dvijaḥ |

	surāṃ pibati sa vyaktaṃ yamasya vacanaṃ yathā ||

tathā ca brahmāṇḍapurāṇāt |

	kaṇṭhaṃ śiro vā prāvṛtya rathyāpaṇagato 'pi vā |

	akṛtvā pādayoḥ śaucam ācānto 'py aśucir bhavet ||

marīciḥ |

	na pādukāstho nācittaḥ śuciḥ prayatamānasaḥ |

	upaspṛśya dvijā śuddha eva bhavaet tu saḥ ||

	bhuktvāsanastho 'py ācāmen nānyakāle kadācana ||

pracetāḥ: "nāntarvāsā na nirvāsā nāśru kurvan nācāmet" | āpastambaḥ: "nāgnyudakaśeṣeṇa vṛthā karmāṇi kurvīta | ācāmed vā bhūmau svāvayitvā vācāmet" | viṣṇuḥ | 

	na spṛśan na hasañ jalpan na śvacāṇḍāladarśane |

	nāpavitrakaraḥ kaścid brāhmaṇo 'pa upaspṛśet ||

	apūtaṃ tasya tat sarvaṃ bhavaty ācamane tathā ||

yamaḥ |

	vāmahastasthite darbhe dakṣiṇenācamed yadi |

	raktaṃ tu tad bhavet toyaṃ pītvā cāndrāyaṇaṃ caret || 1.20–21 ||

_upanītasya kramaprāptāṃ madhyaṃdinasaṃdhyāṃ snānādisahitām āha |_

	**snānam abdaivatair mantrair mārjanaṃ prāṇasaṃyamaḥ |**

**	sūryasya cāpy upasthānaṃ gāyatryāḥ pratyahaṃ japaḥ || 1.22 ||**

snānam āplāvanam, abdeivataiḥ, āpo hi ṣṭhety evamādibhir mantraiḥ | mārjanaṃ svaśiraḥprokṣaṇam, prāṇāyāmaḥ, sūryopasthānaṃ gāyatrījapaś ceti pratyahaṃ madhaṃdine **[43]** kāryam | brahmacāriprakaraṇe viṣṇuḥ: "apsu daṇḍavan majjanam" | kātyāyanaḥ |

	rakṣārthaṃ vāriṇātmānaṃ parikṣipya samantataḥ |

	śiroso mārjanaṃ kuryāt kuśaiḥ sodakabindubhiḥ ||

tatrāpohiṣṭhīyānām ārṣādikam āha yogayājñavalkyaḥ |

	sindhudvīpo bhaved ārṣaṃ gāyatraṃ chanda eva ca |

	āpaś ca daivataṃ proktaṃ viniyogaś ca mārjane ||

vyāsaḥ |

	vipruṣo 'ṣṭau kṣiped ūrdhvam adho yasya kṣayāya jit |

āpo hi ṣṭheti tṛ(tryṛ)cena pratipādaṃ mārjanaṃ kāryam | tatra yasya kṣayāya jinvathety adho bhuvi kṣipet | tathā,

	mārjanaṃ jalamadhye tu prāṇāyāmo yatas tataḥ |

jale va sthale vety arthaḥ | atha pavitrakaraṇam | tatra kātyāyanaḥ |

	anantargarbhiṇaṃ sāgraṃ kauśaṃ dvidalam eva ca |

	prādeśamātraṃ vijñeyaṃ pavitraṃ yatra kutracit ||

	etad eva kapiñjalyā lakṣaṇaṃ samudāhṛtam |

	ājyasyotpavanārthe yat tad apy etāvad eva tu ||

	etat pramāṇām evaike kauśīm evārdramañjarīm |

	śuṣkāṃ vā śīrṇakusumāṃ piñjalīṃ paricakṣate ||

mārkaṇḍeyaḥ |

	caturbhir darbhapiñjūlair brāhmaṇasya pavitrakam |

	ekaikanyūnam uddiṣṭaṃ varṇe varṇe yathakramam ||

	tribhir darbhaiḥ śāntikarma pañcabhiḥ pauṣṭikaṃ tathā |

	piñjalaiḥ saptabhiḥ sarvaṃ daivaṃ pitryaṃ vidhīyate ||

	nīvīmadhye tu ye dharbhā brahmasūtre ca ye kṛtāḥ |

	pavitrāṃs tān vijānīyād yathā kāyas tathā kuśaḥ ||

	jape home tathā dāne svādhyāye pitṛtarpaṇe |

	aśūnyaṃ tu karaṃ kuryāt suvarṇarajataiḥ kuśaiḥ ||

**[44]**	jape home tathā dāne svādhyāye pitṛkarmaṇi |

	savyāpasavyau kurvīta sapavitrau karau budhaḥ ||

	granthir yasya pavitrasya na tenācamanaṃ caret |

	ārṣaṃ chando daivataṃ ca viniyogavidhiṃ smaret ||

	smṛtvoṃkāraṃ ca gayatrīṃ nibadhnīyāc chikhāṃ tataḥ |

	punar ācamya hṛdayaṃ nābhiṃ skandhau ca saṃspṛśet ||

tathā,

	praṇavādyā vyāhṛtīś ca sāvitrīṃ ca japet tataḥ |

	tathābhimantrya salilaṃ saṃdhyopāsanam ācaret || 1.22 ||

_prāṇāyāmasvarūpam āha |_

	**gāyatrīṃ śirasā sārdhaṃ japed vyāhṛtipūrvikām |**

**	pratipraṇavasaṃyuktāṃ trir ayaṃ prāṇasaṃyamaḥ || 1.23 ||**

tat savitur iti **gāyatrī**, asyā eva taittirīyakāraṇyake prāṇāyāmamantratvenāmnānāt | oṃ āpo jyotir ityādikena **śirasā sārdhaṃ vyāhṛtipūrvikāṃ pratipraṇavasaṃyuktām trir japet** | eṣa **prāṇasaṃyamaḥ** prāṇāyāma ity arthaḥ | bhūrādyā vyāhṛtayaḥ sapta satyāntāḥ pūrvā yasyāḥ sā tatpūrvikā | pratimantraṃ praṇavaḥ **pratipraṇavaḥ** | mantrāś ca vyāhṛtayaḥ sāvitrī śiraś ca | śiraso 'nto yaḥ praṇavaḥ sa śirontarmantrāntargata eva | saṃvartaḥ |

	praṇavena tu saṃyuktā vyāhṛtīḥ sapta nityaśaḥ |

	sāvitrīṃ śirasā sārdhaṃ manasā triḥ paṭhed dvijaḥ ||

manuḥ |

	savyāhṛtiṃ sapraṇavāṃ gāyatrīṃ śirasā saha |

	triḥ paṭhed āyataprāṇaḥ prāṇāyāmaḥ sa ucyate ||

bṛhaspatiḥ |

	baddhvāsanaṃ niyamya svaṃ smṛtvā cārṣādikaṃ tathā |

	saṃnimīlitadṛṅ maunī prāṇāyāmaṃ samabhyaset ||

yogayājñavalkyaḥ |

	oṃkāraḥ paramaṃ brahma sarvamantreṣu nāyakaḥ |

	prajāpater mukhotpannas tapaḥsiddhasya vai purā ||

**[45]**	tenopattam atas tasya brahmārṣaṃ ca svayaṃbhuvaḥ |

	gāyatrī ca bhavec chandaś cāgnir daivatam ucyate ||

	ādau sarvatra yuñjīta vividheṣv ekakarmasu |

	viniyogaḥ samuddhiṣṭaḥ śvetavarṇa udāhṛtaḥ ||

	vyāhṛtīnāṃ ca sarvāsām ṛṣir brahmā prakīrtitaḥ |

	tataś chandāṃsi yāny āsāṃ tāni samyak pradarśayet ||

	gāyatry uṣṇig anuṣṭup ca bṛhatī paṅktir eva ca |

	indraś ca viśve devāś ca devatāḥ samudāhṛtāḥ ||

	prāṇāyāmaprayoge ca viniyoga udāhṛtaḥ ||

tathā,

	savitā devatā yasyā mukham agnis tripāt tathā |

	viśvāmitra ṛṣiś chando gāyatrī sā viśiṣyate ||

	viniyoga upanaye prāṇāyāme tathaiva ca |

	gāyatrī vā idaṃ sarvaṃ brāhmaṇaṃ brāhmaṇāni tu ||

	vedeṣv anyāny anekāni gāyatryāḥ kīrtitāni tu |

	om āpo jyotir ity eṣa mantro yas tu prakīrtyate ||

	tasya prajāpater ārṣaṃ yajuśchandovivarjitam |

	brahmāgnir vāyuḥ sūryaś ca devatāḥ samudāhṛtāḥ ||

	prāṇasyāmane caiva viniyoga udāhṛtaḥ ||

pūrakakumbhakarecakaiḥ prāṇāyāmas trilakṣaṇo jñeyaḥ | yathā,

	nāsikākṛṣṭa ucchvāso hy antaḥ pūraka ucyate |

	kumbhako niścalaśvāso mucyamānas tu recakaḥ ||

	nīlotpalaśyāmanibhaṃ nābhideśe pratiṣṭhitam |

	caturbhujaṃ mahātmānaṃ pūrakeṇaiva cintayet ||

	kumbhakena hṛdi sthāne dhyāyec ca kamalāsanam |

	brahmāṇaṃ gaurasarvāṅgaṃ caturvaktraṃ pitāmaham ||

	recakeneśvaraṃ vidyāl lalāṭasthaṃ maheśvaram |

	śuddhasphaṭikasaṃkāśaṃ nirmalaṃ pāpanāśanam ||

**[46]** tathā,

	prāṇāyāmatrayaṃ kāryaṃ saṃdhyāsv atha tisṛṣv api |

	prāṇasyāyamanaṃ kṛtvā ācāmet prayato 'pi san ||

	āntaraṃ svi(khi)dyate yasmāt tasmād ācamanaṃ smṛtam |

	sāyam agniś ca mety uktvā prātaḥ sūryaś ca mā pibet ||

	āpaḥ punantu madhyāgne tataś cācamanaṃ caret ||

āpaḥ punantv iti sindhudvīpa ṛṣiḥ, brahmanaspatir devatā, anuṣṭup chandaḥ | sūryaś ca meti agnir ṛṣiḥ, sūryamanyupatayo devatāḥ | agniś ceti viṣṇur ṛṣiḥ, agnir devatā |

	spṛṣṭvā cābhiṣṭutaṃ toyaṃ mūrdhni brahmamukhena tu |

	āpo hi ṣṭhet sūktena darbhair mārjanam ācaret ||

praṇavo vyāhṛtiḥ sāvitrīti brahmamukham | tena toyaṃ spṛṣṭvā tena toyena mūrdhni darbhair mārjanaṃ cāpo hi ṣṭheti sūktena kuryād ity arthaḥ | āpo hi ṣṭhety asya sūktasyāmbarīṣaḥ sindhudvīpa ṛṣiḥ, āpo devatā | navamyā uttarāva(rdha)rcasyagniḥ | ādyānāṃ saptānāṃ gāyatrī chandaḥ, uttarayor anuṣṭup, mārjane viniyogaḥ | kātyāyanaḥ |

	utthāyārkaṃ prati kṣipet trikeṇāñjalim ambhasaḥ |

praṇavo vyāhṛtayaḥ sāvitrīti trikam | atha svaśākhādhītaiḥ sūryadevatyair mantrair ādityam upatiṣṭheta | tataḥ sāvitrīṃ japet | tatra vyāsaḥ |

	āvāhayet tu gāyatrīṃ sarvapāpapraṇāśinīm |

	āgaccha varade devi japye me saṃnidhau bhava ||

	gāyantaṃ trāyase yasmād gayatrī tvaṃ tataḥ smṛtā ||

yogayājñavalkyaḥ |

	śvetavarṇā samuddiṣṭā kauśeyavasanā tathā |

	śvetair vilepanaiḥ puṇyair alaṃkāraiś ca bhūṣitā ||

	ādityamaṇḍalāntaḥsthā brahmalokanivāsinī |

	akṣasūtradharā devī padmāsanagatā śubhā ||

	āvāhya yajamāno hi ojo 'sīti vidhānataḥ |

	āvāhya pūjayitvā tu namaskṛtya nisarjayet ||

**[47]** 	oṃkāraṃ pūrvam uccārya bhūr bhuvaḥ svas tathaiva ca |

	gāyatrī praṇavaś cānte japo hy evam udāhṛtaḥ ||

yamaḥ |

	sahasraparamāṃ devīṃ śatamadhyāṃ daśāvarām |

	gāyatrīṃ tu japen nityaṃ sarvapāpapraṇāśinīm ||

kuryād ity anuvṛttau yogayājñavalkyaḥ |

	gṛhe tv ekaguṇaṃ japyaṃ nadyāṃ tu triguṇaṃ smṛtam |

	gavāṃ goṣṭhe śataguṇam agnyagāre śatādhikam ||

	siddhakṣetreṣu sarveṣu devatāyāś ca saṃnidhau |

	sahasraśatakoṭīnām anantaṃ śivasaṃnidhau ||

tathā,

	tiṣṭhaṃś ced vīkṣy(kṣa)māṇo 'rkaṃ japaṃ kuryāt samāhitaḥ |

	anyathā prāṅmukho kuryād vakṣyamāṇakrameṇa tu ||

	prākkūleṣu kuśeṣv evam āsīnaś cāsane śubhe |

	nātyucchrite nātinīce darbhapāṇiḥ susaṃyataiḥ ||

	sphoṭikendrākṣarudrākṣaputrajīvasamudbhavaiḥ |

	akṣamālā hi kartavyā uttamā hy uttarottarā ||

	koṭyādhikā bhaved vṛddhir akṣamālā viśeṣataḥ |

	japasya kriyamāṇasya tasmāc chreṣṭhā parā parā ||

	abhāve tv akṣamālāyāḥ kuśagranthyātha pāṇinā |

	japa eva hi kartavya ekāgramanasā sadā ||

śaṅkhaḥ: "kuśabṛsyāṃ samāsīnaḥ kuśottarāyāṃ vā hastopayāmair vā kuśapavitrapāṇir udaṅmukhaḥ sūryābhimukho vākṣamālām ādāya devatāṃ dhyāyañ japaṃ kuryāt" | bṛsī, āsanam | kuśottarā kuśacchannā | suvarṇamaṇimuktāphalasphaṭikapadmākṣendrākṣaputrajīvakānām anyatamām akṣamālāṃ kuryāt | kuśagranthikṛtāṃ vā hastopayāmair vā |

	na tathānyena japyena pāpaṃ nirdahati dvijaḥ |

	yathā sāvitrījapyena sarvapapaiḥ pramucyate || **[48]**

yogayājñavalkyaḥ |

	dhyāyena manasā mantraṃ jihvoṣṭhau na ca calayet |

	na kampayec chirogrīvaṃ dantān naiva prakāśayet ||

	na caṅkraman na ca hasan na pārśvam avalokayan |

	nāpāśrito na jalpaṃś ca na prāvṛtaśirās tathā ||

	na padā padam ākramya na caiva hi tathāsanam |

	na cāsamahitamanā na ca saṃśrāvayañ japet ||

	na klinnavāsāḥ sthalago japādīn ācared budhaḥ |

	vratād ṛte nārdravāsā naikavāsāḥ samācaret ||

	na jīrṇena na nīlena praikliṣṭena vā japet |

	yakṣarākṣasabhūtāni siddhavidyādharā gaṇāḥ ||

	haranti prasabhaṃ yasmātr tasmād guptaṃ tu kārayet |

	japakāle na bhāṣeta vratahomadike tathā ||

	eteṣv evāvasaktas tu yady āgacched dvijottamaḥ |

	abhivādya tato vipraṃ yogakṣemaṃ ca kīrtayet ||

avasakto 'vahitaḥ |

	tūṣṇīm āsīta ca japaṃś caṇḍālapatitādikān |

	dṛṣṭvā tān vāry upaspṛśyābhāṣya snātvā punar japet ||

upaspṛśyācamya | ābhāṣya saṃbhāṣyety arthaḥ |

	ācamya prayato nityaṃ japed aśucidarśane |

	saurān mantrān yathotsāhaṃ pāvamānīś ca śaktitaḥ ||

	upaṃśujapayuktasya saṃsyāc chataguṇo bhavet |

	sāhasro mānasaḥ prokto yasmād dhyānasamo hi saḥ ||

śaṃsya uccair japaḥ |

	oṣṭhaspandanamātraṃ tu yatropāṃśu tathādhvani |

	kṛtvā jihvāṃ nirvikalpāṃ cintayet tad dhi mānasam |

	noccair japaṃ budhaḥ kuryāt sāvitryās tu viśeṣataḥ || iti || 1.23 ||

_sāyaṃsaṃdhyopāstim āha |_

	**prāṇān āyamya saṃprokṣya tṛcenābdaivatena tu |**

**	japann āsīta sāvitrīṃ pratyag ā tarakodayāt || 1.24 ||**

**[49]**

yathāvidhi **prāṇān āyamya** vidhivad āho hi ṣṭheti tryṛcenātmānaṃ **saṃprokṣya** pratyaṅmukhaḥ **sāvitrīṃ** purvavaj **japaṃs** **tārakodayaṃ** yāvan nadyādāv **āsīta** | udayo darśanayogyatā, upāsītety anuvṛttau śaunakaḥ: "ardhāstamite maṇḍala ā nakṣatradarśanāt" iti | atrāgniś ca mā manyuś cety asya, agnir ṛṣiḥ | agnimanyumanyupatayo devatāḥ | prakṛtiś chandaḥ | apām ūrdhvakṣepe viśeṣo vyāsenoktaḥ |

	karābhyāṃ toyam ādāya gāyatryā cābhimantritam |

	ādityābhimukhas tiṣthet trir ūrdhvaṃ saṃdhyayoḥ kṣipet ||

madhyaṃdinasaṃdhyāyāḥ samānam anyat | sāyaṃsaṃdhyājapānte rātryupasthānam | baudhāyana āha: "imaṃ ma iti vāruṇībhyāṃ rātrim upatiṣṭhate iti | imaṃ me varuṇa śrudhī havamadyā ca mṛḍaya | tvām avasyurācake | tat tvā yāmi brāhmaṇā vandamānas tad āśāste yajamāno havirbhiḥ | aheṣamāno varuṇeha bodhyur uśaṃsa mā na āyuḥ pra moṣīḥ" iti | śunaḥśepa ṛṣiḥ | rātrir devatā | pūrvā gāyatrī, uttarā triṣṭup || 1.24 ||

_prātaḥsaṃdhyopāstividhim āha_ |

	**saṃdhyāṃ prāk prātar evaṃ hi tiṣṭhed ā sūryadarśanāt |**

prāṇāyāmaprokṣaṇagāyatrījapā evaṃśabdena gṛhītāḥ | prāṅmukhaḥ sāvitrīṃ japan prātaḥsaṃdhyāṃ sūryadarśanakālaṃ yāvat tiṣṭhet | saṃdhyām iti "kālādhvanor atyantasaṃyoge" (Pāṇ 2.3.5) iti dvitīyā | tena sakalasaṃdhyākālo japena vyapaneyaḥ | atra ca "oṃpūrvāṃ gāyatrīṃ japet" itiśrutivirodhaparihārārthaṃ japa eva prādhānyena vidheyaḥ | snānāsane tu tadaṅgatayā | tena japann āsītety āsīno japed ity arthaḥ | saṃvartaḥ |

	prātaḥsaṃdhyāṃ sanakṣatrām upāsīta yathāvidhi |

	sādityāṃ paścimāṃ saṃdhyām ardhāstamitabhāskarāt ||

yogayājñavalkyaḥ |

	hrāsavṛddhī tu satataṃ divasānāṃ yathākramam |

	saṃdhyā muhūrtamātraṃ tu hrāse vṛddhau tu sā smṛtā ||

	yā bhavet paścimā saṃdhyā sā vijñeyā sarasvatī |

	raktā bhavati gāyatrī sāvitrī śvetaparṇikā ||

**[50]**	kṛṣṇā sarasvatī jñeyā saṃdhyātrayam udāhṛtam |

	saṃdhau saṃdhyām upāsīta nāstaṃge nodgate ravau ||

	saṃdhyātrayaṃ tu kartavyaṃ dvijenātmavidā sadā |

	ubhe saṃdhye ca kartavye brāhmaṇaiś ca gṛheṣv api ||

ataś ca vākyān madhyāhnasaṃdhyā gṛhe na kāryeti gamyate | vasiṣṭhaḥ |

	gṛhe tv ekaguṇā saṃdhyā goṣṭhe daśaguṇā smṛtā |

	śatasāhasrikā nadyām anantaṃ viṣṇusaṃnidhau ||

śātātapaḥ |

	anṛtaṃ madyagandhaṃ ca divāmaithunam eva ca |

	punāti vṛṣalasyānnaṃ bahiḥ saṃdhyā hy upāsitā ||

	bahiḥ saṃdhyā daśaguṇā gartaprasravaṇādiṣu |

	khyātatīrthe śataguṇā sāhasrā jāhnavījale ||

manuḥ |

	etad akṣaram etāṃ ca japan vyāhṛtipūrvakam |

	saṃdhyayor ubhayor vipro vedapuṇyena yujyate ||

etad akṣaraṃ praṇavaḥ | yamaḥ |

	yad ahnā kriyate pāpaṃ karmaṇā manasā girā |

	āsīnaḥ paścimāṃ saṃdhyāṃ prāṇāyāmaiś ca hanti tat ||

	yad rātryā kriyate pāpaṃ karmaṇā manasā girā |

	purvāṃ saṃdhyām upāsīnaḥ prāṇāyāmair vyapohati ||

	saṃdhyām upāsate ye tu satataṃ saṃśitavratāḥ |

	vidhūtapāpās te yānti brahmalokaṃ sanātanam ||

	ṛṣayo dīrghasaṃdhyatvād dīrgham āyur avāpnuvan |

	pūjāṃ yaśaś ca kīrtiś ca brahmavarcasam eva ca ||

viṣṇupurāṇāt |

	sarvakālam upasthānaṃ saṃdhyayoḥ pārthiveṣyate |

	anyatra sūtakāśaucavibhramāturabhītitaḥ ||

pulastyaḥ |

	saṃdhyām iṣṭiṃ caruṃ homaṃ yāvajjīvaṃ samācaret |

	sūtake mṛtake caiva saṃdhyākarma na saṃtyajet ||

	manasoccārayen mantrān prāṇāyāmam ṛte dvijaḥ || **[51]**

yamaḥ |

	anāgatāṃ tu ye pūrvām atītāṃ ye ca paścimām |

	viprāḥ saṃdhyāṃ na tiṣṭhanti vṛṣalās ta udāhṛtāḥ ||

dakṣaḥ |

	upāsate na yaḥ saṃdhyāṃ brāhmaṇo hi viśeṣataḥ |

	sa jīvann eva śūdratvaṃ mṛtaḥ śvā caiva jāyate ||

	saṃdhyāhīno 'śucir nityam anarhaḥ sarvakarmasu |

	yad anyat kurute karma na tasya phalabhāg bhavet ||

	**agnikāryaṃ tataḥ kuryāt saṃdhyayor ubhayor api || 1.25 ||**

tārakodayāt sūryadarśanāc cordhvaṃ saṃdhyākāle pratyāsanna eva kāle svagṛhyoktavidhinā samiddhomaṃ kuryāt | bhaviṣyatpurāṇāt |

	dūrād āhṛtya samidhaḥ saṃnidadhyād gṛhopari |

	sāyaṃ prātaś ca juhuyāt tābhir agnim atandritaḥ ||

dūrād ity aparigṛhītadeśopalakṣaṇārtham | māntravarṇikī cātra devatā | juhuyād iti vacanād agnikāryaṃ homādikaṃ pratīyate | sāyaṃprātaś ca śabdābhyāṃ rātryahanī upalakṣyete | baijavāpaḥ: "purāstamayāt prāg udīcīṃ diśaṃ gatvāhiṃsann araṇyāt samidha āharet | śuṣkā brahmavarcasakāmaḥ | ārdrā annādyakāma ubhayor ubhayakāmaḥ" | kātyāyanaḥ |

	nāṅguṣṭhād adhikā kāryā samitsthūlatayā kvacit |

	na viyuktā tvacā caiva na sakīṭā na pāṭitā ||

	prādeśān nādhikā nonā tathā ca syād dviśākhikā |

	na saparṇā na nirvīryā homeṣu ca vijānatā ||

	viśīrṇā vidalā hrasvā vakrāḥ sasuśi(ṣi)rās tathā |

	na grāhyāś ca guṇair juṣṭāḥ karmasiddhivināśikāḥ ||

vāyupurāṇāt |

	pālāśyaḥ samidhaḥ kāryāḥ khādiryas tadalābhataḥ |

	śamīrohitakāśvatthās tadalābhe 'rkavetasāḥ || **[52]**

kātyāyanaḥ |

	yatropadiśyate karma kartur aṅgaṃ na cocyate |

	dakṣiṇas tatra vijñeyaḥ karmaṇāṃ pāragaḥ karaḥ ||

	yatra diṅniyamo nāsti japahomādikarmasu |

	tisras tatra diśaḥ proktā aindrī saumyāparājitā ||

	āsīna ūrdhvaḥ prahvo vā niyamo yatra nedṛśaḥ |

	tad āsīnena kartavyaṃ na prahveṇa na tiṣṭhatā ||

śātāpataḥ |

	nābhivādyās tu vipreṇa kṣatriyādyāḥ kathaṃcana |

	jñānakarmaguṇopetā yady apy ete bahuśrutāḥ ||

	brāhmaṇaḥ sarvavarṇānāṃ svasti kuryād iti śrutiḥ |

	savarṇais tu savarṇānāṃ kāryam evābhivādanam ||

aṅgirāḥ |

	apraṇamaṃ gate śūdre svasti kurvanti ye dvijāḥ |

	śūdro 'pi narakaṃ yāti brāhmaṇas tadanantaram ||

yamah |

	yat sukhaṃ triṣu lokeṣu vyādhivyasanavarjitam |

	yasmin sarve sthitāḥ kāmāḥ sā svastīty abhisaṃjñitā ||

tathā,

	kṣatriyas triyugaṃ hanti vaiśyo hanti caturyugam |

	hanty ekaviṃśatiyugaṃ śūdro brāhmaṇam abruvan ||

bhaviṣyatpurāṇāt |

	abhīti gadito viṣṇur vādayāmīti śaṃkaraḥ |

	dvāv eva pūjitau tena yaḥ karoty abhivādanam ||

	savyāpasavyādividhir yatra no vidyate kvacit |

	yajñopavītinā tatra bhāvyaṃ sarveṣu karmasu || 1.25 ||

_abhivādanavidhim āha |_

	**tato 'bhivādayed vṛddhān asāv aham iti bruvan |**

agnikāryaṃ kṛtvāsāv aham iti bruvañ jyāyaso 'bhivādayet | asāv ity asya sthāne prathamāntaṃ nāma kīrtayet | tathābhivādaya ity uktvā vā | manuḥ |

	abhivādāt paraṃ vipro jyāyāṃsam abhivādayan |

	asau nāmāham asmīti svanāma parikīrtayet ||

	bhoḥśabdaṃ kārayed ante svasya nāmno 'bhivādane || **[53]**

ataś caivaṃ prayogo bhavati | abhivādaye caitranāmāham asmi bho iti | abhivāditena ca pratyabhivādanaṃ yathā kāryaṃ tathāha sa eva |

	āyuṣmān bhava saumyeti vācyo vipro 'bhivādane |

	akāraś cāsya nāmno 'ntar vācyaḥ pūrvākṣaraḥ plutaḥ ||
