atra cābhivādakanāmasaṃniviṣṭāntimasvaropalakṣaṇārtham akāragrahaṇam | tataś ca ya evāsti svaro 'ntyaḥ sa plutaḥ kāryaḥ pūrvākṣara iti vacanāt | pūrvam akṣaraṃ yasya sa pūrvākṣaraḥ, pūrvam abhivādakanāmāntarvartinaḥ | tac ca sāmarthyād vyañjanam, svarasya hi vyañjanam eva pūrvam | ataś ca pūrvākṣara iti viśeṣaṇopadānād vyañjanasahita eva svaraḥ plāvanīyaḥ | na punar apūrvo 'kāro nāmānte vidhīyata iti niścīyate | tathā ca vasiṣṭhaḥ: "āmantrite svaro 'ntyasya plavate saṃdhyakṣaram apragṛhyam āyāya(u)bhāvaṃ ca" iti | āmantritavibhaktyantasya nāmno 'nte yaḥ svaraḥ sa plavate trimātro bhavati | tathā pragṛhyasaṃjñāvarjitaṃ yat saṃdhyakṣaram ekākāraikārarūpam āibhāvas tasya kāryaḥ | okāraukārarūpaṃ cet tadā tasyāubhāvaḥ karyaḥ | atrodāharaṇāni: āyuṣmān bhava saumya yajñadatta3 bhadraśramā3 [na] yajñabhūtā3i citragā3u | "jyāyāṃsam abhivādayan" ity uktam | tatra kyatā kālena jyāyān bhavatīty apekṣite manur āha |

	daśābdākhyaṃ paurasakhyaṃ pañcābdākhyaṃ kalābhrtām |

	tryabdapūrvaṃ śrotriyāṇām alpenāpi svayoniṣu ||

puravāsino daśabhir varṣaiḥ pūrvaḥ sakhaiva bhavati, tato 'dhikavarṣas tu jyāyān | kalābhṛtāṃ śilpināṃ gāyanādīnāṃ pañcābdapūrvaḥ sakhā, tato 'dhiko jyāyān | tyabdāpekṣam alpatvam | śrotriyāṇāṃ tryabdapūrvaḥ sakhā, tato 'dhiko jyāyān | tasya ca tāratamyaṃ guṇatāratamyāpekṣam | apiśabda evakārārthaḥ | striyaḥ kartavyapratyabhivādanān abhijñāṃś ca puruṣān prati tathāha manuḥ |

**[54]**	nāmadheyasya ye kecic abhivādaṃ na jānate |

	tān prājño 'ham iti brūyāt striyaḥ sarvās tathaiva ca ||

āpastambaḥ: "trivarṣapūrvaḥ śrotriyo 'bhivādanam arhati | jñāyamāne ca vā yoniviśeṣe vṛddhatarāyābhivādyam" | tathā: "samānagrāme ca vasatām anyeṣām api vṛddhatarāṇāṃ prāk prātarāśād abhivādayīta svargam āyuś cepsan | dakṣiṇaṃ bāhuṃ śrotrasamaṃ prasārya brāhmaṇo 'bhivādayīta | uraḥsamaṃ rājanyaḥ | madhyasamaṃ vaiśyaḥ | nīcaiḥ śūdraḥ prāñjalis tathā | viṣamagatāya gurave nābhivādyam anvāruhyābhivādayīta | sarvatra tu pratyutthāyābhivādanam | aprayatena nābhivādyam" | tathā: "aprayataś ca prayatāya na pratyabhivādayet | pativayasaḥ striyo 'vahitaśirā avahitapāṇir vābhivādayīta | sarvā nāmnā striyo rājanyavaiśyau ca na nāmnā māta ramārthadārāṃś cety eke" | sāṃkhyāyanaḥ: "ahar ahar ācāryāyābhivādayet | gurubhyaś ca sametya śrotriyasya" | manuḥ |

	laukikaṃ vaidikaṃ vāpi tathādhyātmikam eva vā |

	ādadīta yato jñānaṃ taṃ pūrvam abhivādayet ||

	guror gurau saṃnihite guruvad vṛttim ācaret |

	na cānisṛṣṭo guruṇā svān gurūn abhivadayet ||

anisṛṣṭo 'nanujñāpitaḥ | svān mātulādīn |

	**guruṃ caivāpy upāsīta svādhyāyārthaṃ samāhitaḥ || 1.26 ||**

guruṃ caivābhivādayet | vṛddhatvād eva guror abhivādane siddhe pṛthagvacanaṃ śāstrāntarokenopasaṃgrahaṇena vikalpārtham | upasaṃgrahaṇam āha manuḥ |

**[55]**	vyatyastapāṇinā kāryam upasaṃgrahaṇaṃ guroḥ |

	savyena savyaḥ spraṣṭavyo dakṣiṇena tu dakṣiṇaḥ ||

savyadakṣiṇābhyāṃ pāṇibhyāṃ savyadakṣiṇau pādau guroḥ spṛśed ity arthaḥ | śrotre saṃspṛśya manaḥsamādhānārtham adhas tajjānvor ā padbhyām | gautamaḥ: "guroḥ pādopasaṃgrahaṇaṃ prātar brāhmānuvacane cādhyantayoḥ" | brahma vedaḥ | anuvacanam adhyāpanam | ādyantayor upakramāvasānayoḥ | āpastambaḥ: "udite tv āditya ācāryeṇa sametyopasaṃgrahaṇaṃ sadaivābhivādanam upasaṃgrāhyācārya ity eke" | gurur atrācāryaḥ pitā vā | atriḥ |

	dakṣiṇaṃ pāṇim uddhṛtya prakāmam abhivādayet |

	śrotriye tv añjaliḥ kāryo guroḥ pādopasaṃgraham ||

atha prakṛtam ucyate: apy upāsīta svādhyāyaprāptyarthaṃ paricaret | gurum ity anuvartate | samāhito 'nanyamanāḥ || 1.26 ||

	**āhūtaś cāpy adhīyīta labdhaṃ cāsmai nivedayet |**

guruṇāhūtaḥ paṭhet | labdhaṃ ca gurave nivedayet | upasaṃgrahaṇānantaraṃ gautamaḥ: "anujñāta upaviśet prāṅmukho dakṣiṇataḥ śiṣya udaṅmukho vā | etat pratyaham adhyayanārambhe kāryam | prathamādhyayane tu pāṇinā savyam upasaṃgṛhyānaṅguṣṭham adhīhi bho iti brūyāt | tatra cakṣurmanaḥprāṇopasparśanaṃ darbhaiḥ prāṇāyāmās trayaḥ pañcadaśa mātrāḥ prākkūleṣv āsanaṃ ca, oṃpūrvā vyāhrtayaḥ sapta satyāntāḥ" | prāṇāḥ śīrṣaṇyāni khāni | hrasvam akṣaraṃ mātrā, tayā kālo lakṣyate | kūlam agram ||

	**hitaṃ cāsyācaren nityaṃ manovacanakarmabhiḥ || 1.27 ||**

**hitam** āyatāv anukūlam **asya** guror **ācaret** | sarvadā mānasavācikakāyikavyāpārair atihitakārī guror apratilomayan vāceti | **ca**kāraḥ śāstrāntaroktavacanasamuccayārthaḥ | tatra manuḥ |

	śārīraṃ caiva vācaṃ ca buddhīndriyamanāṃsi ca |

	niyamya prāṅmukhas tiṣṭhed vīkṣamāṇo guror mukham ||

**[56]**	nityam uddhṛtapāṇiḥ syāt sādhvācāraḥ susaṃyataḥ |

	āsyatām iti coktaḥ sann āsītābhimukhaṃ guroḥ ||

	hīnānnavastraveṣaḥ syāt sarvadā caiva saṃviśet |

	pratiśravaṇasaṃbhāṣe śayāno na samācaret ||

pratiśravaṇam aṅgīkāraḥ |

	nāsīno na ca bhuñjāno na tiṣṭhan na parāṅmukhaḥ |

	āsīnasya sthitaḥ kuryād abhigacchec ca gacchataḥ ||

	pratyudgamya tv āvrajataḥ paścād dhāvaṃs tu dhāvataḥ |

	prāṅmukhasyābhimukho dūrasthasyaitya cāntikam ||

	praṇamya tu śayānasya nideśe caiva tiṣṭhataḥ |

	nīcaṃ śayyāsanaṃ cāsya sarvadā gurusaṃnidhau ||

	guroś ca cakṣurviṣaye na yatheṣṭāsano bhavet |

	nodāhared asya nāma parokṣam api kevalam ||

	na caivāsyānukurvīta gatibhāṣitaceṣṭitam |

	guror yatra parīvādo nindā vāpi pravartate ||

	karṇau tatra pidhātavyau gantavyaṃ vā tato 'nyataḥ |

	dūrastho nārcayed enaṃ na kruddho nāntike striyāḥ ||

	yānāsanasthaś caivainam avaruhyābhivādayet || 1.27 ||

_prasaṅgād guruṃ praty adhyāpyān āha |_

	**kṛtajñādrohimedhāviśucikalyāṇasūcakāḥ |**

**	adhyāpyāḥ sādhuśaktāptasvārthadā dharmatas tv ime || 1.28 ||**

kṛtajña upakartuḥ smartā | adohy anaparādhī | medhāvī dhāraṇāvān | śuciḥ prayataḥ | kalyāṇasūcakaḥ śubhalakṣaṇaḥ | kalyānasūyakā iti tu pāṭhe kalyo nīrogaḥ | anasūyako 'sūyārahitaḥ | āpto 'pratārakaḥ | svo jñātiḥ | arthado 'gurvarthapradātā | jñānavittadā iti tu pāṭhe jñānado jñānahetugranthapradaḥ | ete dharmato **[57]** dharmānatikrameṇa guror adhyāpyā bhavanti | arthapradaṃ praty anenādhyāpanaṃ nādharmaḥ, tasya vṛttitvena vihitatvā | bhṛtisaṃpratipattipūrvakam adhyāpanaṃ pratiṣiddham | manus tv ācāryaputram apy āha |

	ācāryaputraḥ śuśrūṣur jñānado dhārmikaḥ śuciḥ |

	śaktārthadāptāḥ svaḥ sādhur adhyāpyā daśa dharmataḥ || iti |

yat tu tenaivoktam,

	dharmārthau yatra na syātāṃ śuśrūṣā nāpi tadvidhā |

	tatra vidyā na dātavyā guptaṃ bījam ivoṣare ||

iti, tad dharmānuṣṭhānārthadānaśuśrūṣaṇāni sati sāmarthye yo na karoty adhyāpyaguṇāntaravirahe tadviṣayam || 1.28 ||

_upanītaṃ praty āha |_

	**daṇḍājinopavītāni mekhalāṃ caiva dhārayet |**

daṇḍādīni svakāryadhāraṇīyāni | tatra daṇḍasya kāryam avalambanaṃ gavādinivāraṇaṃ tamovagāhanam apsu praveśanam ityādi | ajinopavītamekhalānām adṛṣṭam | atas tāni nityaṃ dhāryāṇi | upavītaṃ brahmasūtram | manuḥ |

	brāhmaṇo bailvapālāśau kṣatriyo vaṭakhādirau |

	paippalaudumbarau vaiśyo daṇḍān arhati dharmataḥ ||

yamaḥ |

	eteṣām apy alābhe tu sarveṣāṃ sarvayajñiyāḥ |

manuḥ |

	ṛjavas te tu sarve syur avraṇāḥ saumyadarśanāḥ |

	anudvegakarā nṝṇāṃ satvaco 'nagnidūṣitāḥ ||

	keśāntiko brāhmaṇasya daṇḍaḥ kāryaḥ pramāṇataḥ |

	lalāṭasaṃmito rājñaḥ syāt tu nāsāntiko viśaḥ ||

tathā,

	kārṣṇarauravabāstāni carmāṇi brahmacāriṇaḥ |

	vasīrann ānupūrvyeṇa śāṇakṣaumāvikāni ca ||

kṛṣṇamṛgarurucchāgānām ajināni brāhmaṇādayo yathākramaṃ vasīrann ācchādayeyur uttarīyāṇi kuryur ity arthaḥ | tathā ca pāraskaraḥ: **[58]** "aiṇeyam ajinam uttarīyaṃ brāhmaṇasya rauravaṃ rājanyasyājaṃ gavyaṃ vā vaiśyasya sarveṣāṃ vā gavyam" | yamaḥ: "sarveṣāṃ rauravaśāṇakṣaumāvikāni sāmarthyād adhovastrāṇītarāṇi na" | gautamas tu sarveṣāṃ brahmacāriṇāṃ śāṇādibhir vikalpitaṃ śuklakārpāsaṃ vastram āha: "sarveṣāṃ kārpāsaṃ vāso 'vikṛtam" iti | avikṛtaṃ śuklam | vasiṣṭhaḥ: "śuklam ahataṃ vāso brāhmaṇasya kārpāsaṃ māñjiṣṭhaṃ kṣaumaṃ kṣatriyasya pītaṃ kauśeyaṃ vaiśyasya sarveṣāṃ vā tāntavam araktam | śuklaṃ kārpāsam evāhataṃ kṣaumādy api" | manuḥ |

	kārpāsam upavītaṃ syād viprasyordhvavṛtaṃ trivṛt |

	śaṇasūtramayaṃ rājño vaiśyasyāvikasūtrikam ||

bhṛguḥ |

	ūrdhvaṃ tu trivṛtaṃ kāryaṃ tantutrayam adhovṛtam |

	trivṛtaṃ copavītaṃ syāt tasyaiko granthir iṣyate ||

trivṛt navasūram ity arthaḥ |

	pṛṣṭhadeśe ca nabhyāṃ ca yad vṛtaṃ vindate kaṭim |

	tad dhāryam upavītaṃ syān nātilambaṃ na cocchritam ||

	sadopavītinā bhāvyaṃ sadā baddhaśikhena ca |

	viśikho vyupavītaś ca yat karoti na tat kṛtam ||

	upavītaṃ baṭor ekaṃ dve tathetarayoḥ smṛte ||

baudhāyanaḥ: "kauśaṃ sautraṃ vā tristrivṛd yajñopavītam" | manuḥ |

	kauśaṃ trivṛt samā ślakṣṇā kāryā viprasya mekhalā |

	kṣatriyasya tu maurvī jyā vaiśyasya śaṇatāntavī ||

	muñjālābhe tu kartavyā kuśāśmantakabalvajaiḥ |

	trivṛtā granthinaikena tribhiḥ pañcabhir eva vā ||

yathārṣeyaṃ granthayaḥ kāryā ity abhiprāyaḥ | paiṭhīnasiḥ: "mauñjī mekhalāśmantakī brāhmaṇasya" | baudhāyanaḥ: "athainaṃ mauñjīṃ mekhalāṃ trivṛtaṃ triḥ pradakṣiṇaṃ parivyayati" | manuḥ |

	yad yasya vihitaṃ carma yat sūtraṃ yā ca mekhalā |

	yo daṇḍo yac ca vasanaṃ tat tad asya vrateṣv api || **[59]**

vratāni sāvitryādīni |

	mekhalājinaṃ daṇḍam upavītaṃ kamaṇḍalum |

	apsu prāpya vinaṣṭāni gṛhṇītānyāni mantrataḥ || iti |

	**brāhmaṇeṣu cared bhaikṣam anindyeṣv ātmavṛttaye || 1.29 ||**

**brāhmaṇeṣv anindyeṣv** anibhiśastādiṣu **bhaikṣaṃ** prāptaṃ caret | bhikṣitam annaṃ bhikṣā, tāsāṃ samūho **baikṣam** | **ātmavṛttaya** ātmana eva vṛttyarthaṃ na parasya guruvyatiriktasya | gurus tu śiṣyaniveditaṃ bhaikṣaṃ samaśnīyād eva | yad āha āpastambaḥ: "bhaikṣaṃ haviṣā saṃstutam | tatrācāryo devatārtha āhavanīyārthe ca taṃ bhojayitvā yad ucchiṣṭaṃ prāśnāti havir ucciṣṭam eva tat" iti | manuḥ |

	udakumbhaṃ sumanaso gośakṛn mṛttikāṃ kuśān |

	āhared yāvad arthāni bhaikṣaṃ cāhar ahaś caret ||

	vedayajñaira ahīnānāṃ praśastānāṃ svakarmasu |

	brahmacāry āhared bhaikṣaṃ gṛhebhyaḥ prayato 'nvaham ||

	guroḥ kule na bhikṣeta na jñātikulabandhuṣu ||

yat tu,

	mātaraṃ vā svasāraṃ vā mātur vā bhaginīṃ nijām |

	bhikṣeta bhikṣāṃ prathamaṃ yā cainaṃ na vimānayet ||

iti, tad upanayanāṅgabhikāviṣayam iti guroḥ kula na bhikṣetety anenāviruddham, nityabhikṣāviṣayatvād asya |

	alābhe tv anyagehānāṃ pūrvaṃ pūrvaṃ vivarjayet |

	sarvaṃ vāpi cared grāmaṃ pūrvoktānām asaṃbhave ||

	antyavarjaṃ mahābāho ity āha bhagavān vibhuḥ ||

antyaḥ śūdraḥ |

	vācaṃ niyamya prayata āmiṣaṃ cāpi varjayet |

	caturvarṇyaṃ cared bhaikṣam alābhe kurunandana ||

alābhe trivarṇikānām iti śeṣaḥ || 1.29 ||

	**ādimadhyāvasāneṣu bhavacchabdopalakṣitāḥ |**

**	brāhmaṇakṣatriyaviśāṃ bhaikṣacaryā yathākramam || 1.30 ||**

**[60]** baikṣaprāktanavākyaṃ **bhaikṣacaryā**śabdena lakṣyate | tad ādau madhye 'vasāne ca strīliṅgasaṃbuddhyantaṃ(nta)bhavacchabdayuktaṃ brāhmaṇasya kṣatriyasa vaiśyasya yathākramaṃ prayoktavyaṃ bhavati | bhavati bhikṣā dehīti brāhmaṇasya, bhikṣāṃ bhavati dehīti kṣatriyasa, bhikṣāṃ bhavatīti vaiśyasyeti siddham | prathamabhikṣām adhikṛtya bhaviṣyatpurāṇam |

	mātaraṃ vā svasāraṃ vā mātur vā bhaginīṃ nijām |

	bhikṣeta prathamaṃ bhikṣāṃ yā cainaṃ na vimānayet ||

	suvarṇaṃ rajataṃ ratnaṃ sā pātre 'sya vinikṣipet ||

smṛtyantaraṃ ca |

	bhikṣārthaṃ kāñcanaṃ vāpi pātraṃ savyena rājatam |

	pitrā kṛtopanītejyo madhuparkakaras tataḥ ||

yamaḥ |

	hastadattā tu yā bhikṣā lavaṇaṃ vyañjanāni ca |

	bhoktā tv aśucitāṃ yāti dātā svargaṃ na gacchati ||

manuḥ |

	parigṛhyepsitaṃ daṇḍam upasthāya ca bhāskaram |

	pradakṣiṇaṃ parītyāgniṃ cared bhaikṣaṃ yathāvidhi || 1.30 ||

	**kṛtāgnikāryo bhuñjīta vāgyato gurvanujñayā |**

**	āpośānakriyāpūrvaṃ satkṛtyānnam akutsayan || 1.39 ||**

kṛtam agnikāryaṃ yena sa **kṛtāgnikāryaḥ** | **vāgyato** maunī | **āpośānakriyāṃ** kṛtvā **satkṛtya** pūjayann **annam akutsayann** anindayan **gurvanujñā** bhuṅkṣveti gurvanumatyā **bhuñjīta** | upanayanakāla āpośānapraiṣoktā kriyāpośānakriyā | bhaikṣād ekadeśahomo 'trāgnikāryam | tad āha paiṭhīnasiḥ: "haviṣo hutvā saṃtarpyāgniṃ samidhaṃ dattvānnaṃ yad annam admy amṛtena devā yad annam admi bahudhā virūpam iti coktvānumantrayet triḥ | sviṣṭakṛtam agnikāryaṃ kṛtvānujñāto bhuñjīta vāgyataḥ" | tathā ca āpastambaḥ: "prokṣitād bhaikṣād agnau hutvā bhuñjīta" | **[61]** ataś cārtha(rthā)saṃnidhāv etad agnikāryaṃ saṃnihite tv ācārye 'gnikāryasthāne bhaikṣam ācāryo bhojayitavya iti tenaivoktaṃ haviṣā saṃstutam ityādinā | atra manuḥ |

	samāhṛtya tu tad bhakṣaṃ yāvad artham amāyayā |

	nivedya gurave 'śnīyād ācamya prāṅmukho śuciḥ ||

	āyuṣyaṃ prāṅmukho bhuṅkte yaśasyaṃ dakṣiṇāmukhaḥ |

	śriyaṃ pratyaṅmukho bhuṅkte ṛtaṃ bhukta udaṅmukhaḥ ||

asyārthaḥ: yat prāṅmukho bhuṅkte tad āyuṣyam | āyuṣe hitam | evaṃ yaśasyam | yaḥ pratyaṅmukho bhuṅkte sa śriyaṃ prāpnoti | yas tūdaṅmukhaḥ sa ṛtaṃ satyaṃ yajñaṃ vāpnoti | evaṃ bhoktuḥ prākmukhatā nityā kāmyā ca |

	nocchiṣṭaṃ kasyacid dadyān nādyād enam athāntarā |

	na caivātyaśanaṃ kuryān na cocchiṣṭaḥ kvacid vrajet ||

saṃvartaḥ |

	sāyaṃ prātar manuṣyāṇām aśanaṃ daivacoditam |

	nāntarā bhojanaṃ kuryād agnihotrasamo vidhiḥ ||

vasiṣṭhaḥ |

	aṣṭau grāsā muher bhakṣyaṃ ṣoḍaśāraṇyavāsinaḥ |

	dvāviṃśatir gṛhasthasya amitaṃ brahmacāriṇaḥ ||

āpastambaḥ: "bhuktvā svayam amantraṃ prakṣālayen na cocchiṣṭaṃ kuryād aśakto bhūmau nikhaned apsu vā prāveśayed āryāya vā paryavadadhyād antarhitena vā śūdrāya" || 1.31 ||

	**brahmacarye sthito naikam annam adyād anāpadi |**

brahmacāry anāpady ekasyānnaṃ nāśnīyāt |

	**brāhmaṇaḥ kāmam aśnīyāc chrāddhe vratam apīḍayan || 1.32 || ||**

brahmacārī brāhmaṇaś cet tadābhyarthitaḥ sann ekānnam anāpady api bhuñjīta | sa cec chrāddhe bhuñjīta tadā vratapīḍākaraṃ madhumāṃsādi varjayitvāśnīyāt || 1.32 ||

_brahmacāriniyamān āha |_

	**madhumāṃsāñjanocchiṣṭaṃ śuktastrīprāṇihiṃsanam |**

**	bhāskarālokanāślīlaparivādāṃś ca varjayet || 1.33 ||**

brahmacārī madhvādikaṃ varjayet | madhu māṃsaṃ śiṣṭabhojanīyam api | añjanaṃ kajjalam | ucchiṣṭaṃ svasya parasya ca guruvyatiriktasya | tathā ca vasiṣṭhaḥ **[62]** : "ucchiṣṭam aguror abhojyaṃ svam ucchiṣṭam ucchiṣṭopahataṃ ca" iti | śuktaṃ paruṣaṃ vaco 'nnaṃ vā yat kālavaśād alaṃ bhavati | strīśabdena strīviṣaye prekṣaṇālambane lakṣyete | tad āha gautamaḥ: "strīprekṣaṇālambane maithunaśaṅkāyām" iti | prāṇihiṃsanaṃ prāṇivadhaḥ | bhāskarālokanaṃ prasiddham | aślīlaṃ sabhānarhaṃ vacaḥ | parivādaḥ paranindāvarjanenātra varjanaviṣayaḥ | saṃkalpo vrataniyamādiśabdavācyo lakṣyate | ata evāha: "śrāddhe vratam apīḍayan" iti | manus tu |

	sevetemāṃś tu niyamān brahmacārī gurau vasan |

	saṃniyamyendriyagrāmaṃ tapovṛddhyartham ātmanaḥ ||

cakāraḥ smṛtyantaropāttānām anyeṣāṃ brahmacāridharmāṇām upasaṃhārārthaḥ | tatra manuḥ |

	nityaṃ snātvā śuciḥ kuryād devarṣipitṛtarpaṇam |

	devatābhyarcanaṃ caiva samidādhānam eva ca ||

	varjayen madhumāṃsāni gandhamālyarasān striyaḥ |

	abhyaṅgam añjanaṃ cākṣṇor upānacchatradhāraṇam ||

	kāmaṃ krodhaṃ ca lobhaṃ ca nartanaṃ gītavāditam |

	dyūtaṃ ca janavādaṃ ca parivādaṃ tathānṛtam ||

	strīṇāṃ ca prekṣaṇālambam upaghātaṃ parasya ca |

	ekaḥ śayīta sarvatra na retaḥ skandayet kvacit ||

	kāmād dhi skandayan reto hinasti vratam eva tu ||

vraṃ brahmacaryam | yamaḥ |

	jitendriyo jitālasyo jitakrodho jitātmavān |

tathā,

	khaṭvāsanaṃ ca śayanaṃ varjayed dantadhavanam |

	svaped ekaḥ kuśeṣv eva na retaḥ skandayet kvacit ||

gautamaḥ: "varjayen madhumāṃsaṃ gandhamālyaṃ divāsvapnāñjanābhyājjanopānacchatra-kāmakrodha**[63]**lobhamohavādyavādanasnānadantadhāvanaharṣanṛttagītaparivādabhayāni | gurudarśane kaṇṭhaprāvṛtāvasaktikāpādaprasāraṇāni | niṣṭhyutahasitavijṛmbhitāvasphoṭanāni ca | strīprekṣaṇālambane maithunaśaṅkāyāṃ dyūtahīnasevām adattādānaṃ hiṃsām ācāryatatputratadīkṣitāni ca | śuktā vāco madyaṃ nityām brāhmaṇaḥ" iti | atra snānaṃ bhogārtham | bhayaṃ paraṃ prati | kaṇṭhaprāvṛtaṃ kaṇṭhaprāvaraṇāni | avasaktikā jānunor upari karabandhaḥ | avasphoṭanam aṅgulyādyaṅgasphoṭanam | hīnasevā mūtrapurīṣāvamārjanādikā | tāṃ guror api varjayet, "aṅgāni prakṣālayītāśuciliptāni guror api" iti darśanāt | śuktā vācaḥ parodvegakarāṇi vakyāni | madyaṃ prasiddham | etāni brahmacārī varjayed iti saṃbandhaḥ | madyaṃ nityaṃ brāhmaṇaḥ | nityam iti vacanān madyaṃ kṛtayuādāv api brāhmaṇena varjyam | kṣatriyavaiśyābhyāṃ tu kalāv eva | yad brahmapurāṇam |

	dīrghakālaṃ brahmacaryaṃ dhāraṇaṃ ca kamaṇḍaloḥ |

	sagotrād vā sapiṇḍād vā vivāho govadhas tathā ||

	narāśvamedhau madyaṃ ca kalau varjyaṃ dvijātibhiḥ || iti |

nityaṃ sarvakālam | abrahmacāry api brāhmaṇo madyaṃ varjayed ity arthaḥ | tathā,

	adhaḥśayyāsanī pūrvotthāyī jaghanyasaṃveśī |

	sarvatrāpraihatavākyo 'nyatra pātakāt ||

adhaḥśayyādi gurvapekṣayā | āpastambaḥ: "ātampraśaṃsāṃ paragarhāṃ ca varjayet" iti | tathā, "utsannaślāgho 'ṅgāni prakṣālayītāśuciliptāni | guror asaṃsarśane" | utsannaślāgha utsannaśobho bhaved iti śeṣaḥ | yathā gurur na paśyati tathā prakṣālayītety arthaḥ | āpastambaḥ: "na prekṣeta nagnāṃ striyam | oṣadhivanaspatīnām ācchidya no jighret | na smayeta yadi smayetāparigṛhya smayeta, iti brāhmaṇam" | aparigṛhya mikhaṃ pidhāya smayeteti brāhmaṇam | **[64]** hārītaḥ: "hayagajarathacaityavṛkṣaviśeṣam ārohaṇaphalacayanasaṃdhisarpaṇakūpāvarohaṇamahānadyarṇavaprataraṇamahāsāhasāni varjayet" | manuḥ |

	muṇḍo vā jaṭilo vā syād atha vā syāc chikājaṭaḥ |

	nainaṃ grāme 'bhinimnocet sūryo nābhyudiyāt kvacit ||

	codito guruṇā nityaṃ apracodita eva vā |

	kuryād adhyayane yogam ācāryasya hiteṣu ca || iti || 1.33 ||

_mānyamānanaṃ brahmacāridharmaṃ vaktuṃ mānyānāṃ lakṣaṇāni tāvad āha |_

	**sa gurur yaḥ kriyāḥ kṛtvā vedam asmai prayacchati |**

garbhādhānādyā upanayanāntāḥ kriyāḥ saṃskārikā yo yasya karoti sa tasya **guruḥ** | etāvad eva gurulakṣaṇam | tatprasaṅgād brāhmaṇaṃ prati **vedad asmai prayacchatīti** vidhyantaram | niṣekādikriyānuṣṭhānasya vedadanasya cārthaprāptapaurvāparyānuvādakaḥ ktvāpratyayaḥ | paramārthatas tu dve evaite vākye | anyathā kṣatriyādeḥ svasutaṃ prati gurutvaṃ na syāt, vedadātṛtvābhāvāt | iṣyate ca kṣatriyāder api svasutaṃ prati gurutvam | anyathā kṣatriyādisutasya pitṛbhāryāṃ gacchato gurutalpagatvaṃ na syāt | ata eva manur garbhādhānādikriyākartṛtvaṃ vedadānanirapekṣaṃ gurulakṣaṇam āha |

	niṣekādīni karmāṇi yaḥ karoti yathāvidhi |

	saṃbhāvayati cānnena sa vipro gurur ucyate ||

atrāpy annasaṃbhāvanam aucityaprāptam anūdyate na gurulakṣaṇatayā vidhīyate | vipragrahaṇaṃ ca pradarśanārthaṃna niyamārtham | tathā sati kṣatriyādir na hi guruḥ syāt | yathāvidhigrahaṇena ca śūdrāder niṣekamātrakāriṇo 'pi gurutvaṃ darśayati, tasya tāvan mātravidhānāt | evaṃ kṣatriyavaiśyāyor api | puṃsavanādiṣu karmasu kṛteṣu prayacchatīti vacanād brāhmaṇaḥ pitaiva saṃbhave saty ācāryo bhaved iti gamyate | ata eva bṛhaspatiḥ |

	evaṃ daṇḍādibhir yuktaṃ saṃskṛtya vidhivat pitā |

	vedam adhyāpayed yatnāc chāstraṃ manvādikaṃ tathā ||

iti pitur evādhikāram āha | pitṛvyatiriktānāṃ gurutvaṃ tv aupacārikam iti darśayitum lakṣaṇābhdhānam | **[65]** devalaḥ |

	upādhyāyaḥ pitā jyeṣṭho bhrātā caiva mahīpatiḥ |

	mātulaḥ śvaśuraś trātā mātāmahapitāmahau ||

	varṇajyeṣṭhaḥ pitṛvyaś ca puṃsy ete guravaḥ smṛtāḥ |

	mātā mātāmahī gurvī pitur mātuś ca sodarā ||

	śvaśrūḥ pitāmahī jyeṣṭhā dhātrī ca guravaḥ striyaḥ |

	ity ukto guruvargo 'yaṃ mātṛtaḥ pitṛto dvidhā ||

iti, tad upacāra iti mantavyam | atra ca guruvat teṣu vartitavyam iti phalam | ata evānuvartanam āha |

	anuvartanam eteṣāṃ manovākkāyakarmabhiḥ || iti |

guror bhāryā gurvī | mātṛtaḥ pitṛta iti bāhulyābhiprāyam | mahīpatiprabhṛtīnāṃ tadabhāvāt | manur api pūjyamātrābhiprāyeṇāha |

	alpaṃ vā bahu vā yasya śrutasyopakaroti yaḥ |

	tam apīha guruṃ vidyāc chrutopakriyayā tayā ||

	**upanīya dadad vedam ācāryaḥ sa udāhrtaḥ || 1.34 ||**

yas tu śiṣyam **upanīya vedam** adhyāpayati **sa ācārya** uktaḥ | vedaśabdenātra vidyāntarāṇy api saṃgṛhyante | tathā ca manuḥ |

	upanīya guruḥ śiṣyaṃ vedam adhyāpayed dvijaḥ |

	sakalaṃ sarahasyaṃ ca tam ācāryaṃ pracakṣate ||

kalpaśabdeneha vyākaraṇādīny aṅgāni mīmāṃsānyāyavistarāś ca pratipādyante | kalpo vedārthaṃ kalpayati | tathā ca vyāsaḥ |

	na vedapāṭhamātreṇa saṃtoṣaṃ kārayed dvijaḥ |

	pāṭhamātrāvasānas tu paṅke gaur iva sīdati ||

pāṭhamātrāvasāno 'rthānabhijña ity arthaḥ || 1.34 ||

	**ekadeśam upādhyayaḥ**

yas tu vedārthaikadeśam adhyāpayati sa tasyopādhyāyaḥ | manuḥ |

	ekadeśaṃ tu vedasya vedāṅgāny api vā punaḥ |

	yo 'dhyāpayati vṛttyartham upādhyāya sa ucyate ||

		**ṛtvig yajñakṛd ucyate |**

**[66]**

yo yajñādhikāriṇā svayajñasiddhyarthaṃ parikrītaḥ san yajñakṛd bhavati sa tasya ṛtvig ity ucyate | manuḥ |

	agnyādheyaṃ pākayajñān agniṣṭomadikān makhān |

	yaḥ karoti vṛto yasya sa tasyartvig ihocyate ||

sa ca trividhaḥ | yathāha hārītaḥ: "kṣīrahotāhāryavṛto viśeṣavṛtaḥ" iti | lakṣaṇāny āha: "yo yasyāgnīn ādatte sa tasya kṣīrahotā" | asyārthaḥ: agnyādheyasaṃbandhinām ṛtvijāṃ madhye yaḥ kaścid agnihotra ṛtvig bhavati sa kṣīrahoteti | tadāha āśvalāyanaḥ: "svayaṃ parvaṇi juhuyād ṛtvijām eka itaraṃ kālam" iti | "tasyālābhe yam anyaṃ nityārthaṃ vṛṇīte sa āhāryavṛtaḥ | atha yam anyam uttarottareṣu kratuṣu vṛṇīte sa viśeṣavṛtaḥ" | ṛtviglakṣaṇam iha prāsaṅgikam, brahmacāriṇaṃ prati tasyānupayogāt ||

	**ete mānyā yathāpūrvam**

ete gurvādayo mānyāḥ pūjyāḥ, yathāpūrvaṃ pūrvam anatikramya, uttarottare 'bhivādanopasaṃgrahaṇādibhir mānyā ity arthaḥ ||

		**ebhyo mātā garīyasī || 1.35 ||**

ebhyo gurvādibhyo 'tyarthaṃ gauravaṃ mātaivārhatīty arthaḥ | gautamas tu mātur ācāryasya gauravam āha: "ācāryaḥ śreṣṭho gurūṇāṃ mātety eke" | atra ca guruśabda aupacārikaḥ | purāṇāt |

	dvau gurū puruṣasyeha pitā mātā ca dharmataḥ |

	tayor api pitā śreyān bījaprādhānyadarśanāt ||

	abhāva etayoḥ śreyān guruḥ samyag vicakṣaṇaḥ |

	svatantrāḥ sarva evaite paratantreṣu sarvadā ||

	anuśiṣṭau visarge vā vikraye ceśvarā matāḥ ||

evaṃ ca sati pitur mātur ācāryasya ca vipratiṣiddhārthaviṣayāyām ājñāyāṃ pitur ājñā garīyasī | tadabhāve mātus tadabhāva ācāryasya | **[67]** ācāryasya punar ājñā pitrājñāto 'pi garīyasīty āha manuḥ |

	utpādakabrahmadātror garīyān brahmadaḥ pitā |

	brahmajanma hi viprasya pretya ceha ca śāśvatam ||

brahmada ācāryaḥ || 1.35 ||

_brahmacaryakālasya parimāṇam āha |_

	**prativedaṃ brahmacaryaṃ dvādaśābdāni pañca vā |**

**	grahaṇāntikam ity eke**

uktaṃ brahmacaryaṃ tat prativedaṃ pratiśākhaṃ dvādaś varṣāṇi pañca vā varṣāṇi vedasvīkārāntaṃ vā kartavyam | manuḥ |

	ṣaṭtriṃśadābdikaṃ caryaṃ gurau traividyakaṃ vratam |

	tadardhikaṃ pādikaṃ vā grahaṇāntikam eva vā ||

ārdhikapakṣe ṣaḍvarṣāṇi, pādikapakṣe trīṇi varṣāṇi, ekavedabrahmacaryam | yamaḥ |

	guror apy avaliptasya kāryākāryam ajānataḥ |

	utpathaṃ pratipannasya parityāgo vidhīyate ||

		**keśāntaś caiva ṣoḍaśe || 1.36 ||**

ṣoḍaśe varṣe brāhmaṇasya keśānto nāma saṃskāraḥ kartavyaḥ | kṣatriyavaiśyayos tu manūktaḥ |

	keśāntaḥ ṣoḍaśe varṣe brāhmaṇasya vidhīyate |

	rājanyabandhor dvāviṃśe vaiśyasya dvyadhike tataḥ || iti |

janmādir eṣā varṣasaṃkhyā, garbhādiś ced vivakṣitā syād garbhaṣoḍaś ity avakṣyat, yathā garbhāṣṭama iti | kevalasaṃkhyopādāne tu janmaivāvadhiḥ, yathāṣṭame cābda iti || 1.36 ||

	**ā ṣoḍaśāc cādvāviṃśāc caturviṃśāc ca vatsarāt |**

**	brahmakṣatraviśāṃ kāla aupanāyanikaḥ paraḥ || 1.37 ||**

janmata ā ṣoḍaśād varṣād brāhmaṇasyopanayanakālaḥ, ata ūrdhvaṃ tatkālo nāstīty arthaḥ | evam ā dvāviṃśād varṣāt kṣatriyasyācaturviṃśād vaiśyasya | abhividhau cāyam ākāraḥ | yata āha vyāsaḥ |

**[68]**	aupanāyanikaḥ kālaḥ paraḥ ṣoḍaśavārṣikaḥ |

	dvāviṃśatiḥ paro 'nyasya syāc caturviṃśatiḥ paraḥ ||

	brāhmaṇakṣatriyaviśāṃ kālaś ced atyagād ayam |

	sāvitrīpatitā vrātyā bhavanty ārthavigarhitāḥ || 1.37 ||

_atikrāntopanayanakālānāṃ yad bhavati tad āha |_

	**ata ūrdhvaṃ trayo 'py ete yathākālam asaṃskṛtāḥ |**

**	sāvitrīpatitā vrātyā vrātyastomād ṛte kratoḥ || 1.38 ||**

dvijātayo 'nupanītā yathāsaṃkhyaṃ ṣoḍaśadvāviṃśaticaturviṃśativarṣebhya **ūrdhvaṃ** vrātyastomākhyaṃ kratuṃ vihāya sarvadharmānadhikāriṇo bhavanti | **sāvitrīpatitā vrātyā** iti teṣāṃ saṃjñā | vrātyastomo nāma vrātyānāṃ prāyaścittakratuḥ | tena cohālakavratādinā kṛtaprāyaścittā upanītā dharmādhikāriṇo bhavanti, saṃvyavahāryāś cānyeṣām | yad āha manuḥ |

	naitair apūtair vidhivad āpady api hi karhicit |

	brāhman yaunāṃś ca saṃbandhān ācared brāhmaṇa saha ||

apūtair iti vacanāt kṛtaprāyaścittaiḥ saha saṃvyavahāro na doṣāyeti gamyate | atra "sarvadharmabahiṣkṛtāḥ" iti tu pāṭhe dharmaśabdo dvijātidharmābhiprāyaḥ, na varṇadharmaviṣayaḥ, vrātyānāṃ varṇatvānapāyāt || 1.38 ||

_atra divjātidharmabahiṣkṛtatve ketum āha |_

	**mātur yad agre jāyante dvitīyaṃ mauñjibandhanāt |**

**	brāhmaṇakṣatriyaviśas tasmād ete dvijāḥ smṛtāḥ || 1.39 ||**

mātṛto brāhmaṇādayaḥ prathamaṃ **jāyante** | **dvitīyaṃ mauñjibandhanāt** | **tasmād dvijā ete** manvādibhiḥ **smṛtāḥ** | atra dvitīyam iti kriyāviśeṣaṇam | ato 'nupanītatvād vrātyā na dvijāḥ | tasmād dvijātidharmānadhikāras teṣām uktaḥ || 1.39 ||

	**yajñānāṃ tapasāṃ caiva śubhānāṃ caiva karmaṇām |**

**	veda eva dvijātīnāṃ niḥśreyasakaraḥ paraḥ || 1.40 ||**

**yajñānāṃ** pañcayajñādīnāṃ **tapasāṃ** kṛcchracāndrāyaṇādīnām anyeṣām api śubhaphalānāṃ **karmaṇāṃ** madhye **veda eva** **para** utkṛṣṭo **niḥśreyasakaraḥ** | yajñādibhyaḥ karmabhyo **[69]** vedasya nirdhāraṇam anupapannam iti vedaśabdena vedādhyayanaṃ lakṣyate | tasya ca yuktaṃ yajñādīnāṃ madhye paratvaṃ niḥśreyasakaratvān niḥśreyasakarabodhakatvāc ca | tathā ca manuḥ |

	ā ha vai sa nakhyāgrebhyaḥ paramaṃ tapyate tapaḥ |

	yaḥ sragvy api dvijo 'dhīte svādhyāyaṃ śaktito 'nvaham ||

ā nakhāgrebhyaḥ paramaṃ tapas tapyate hetyanvayaḥ | tathā |

	vedam eva japen nityaṃ yathākālam atandritaḥ |

	taṃ hy asyāhuḥ paraṃ dharmam upadharmo 'sya ucyate || 1.40 ||

_atra hetum āha |_

	**madhunā payasā caiva sa devāṃs tarpayed dvijaḥ |**

**	pitṝn madhughṛtābhyāṃ ca ṛco 'dhīte hi yo 'nvaham || 1.41 ||**

**yo dvijaḥ** pratyaham **ṛco 'dhīte sa** madhupayobhyāṃ **devān** **madhughṛtābhyāṃ ca pitṝṃs** tarpayati || 1.41 ||

	**yajūṃṣi śaktito 'dhīte yo 'nvahaṃ sa ghṛtāmṛtaiḥ |**

**	prīṇāti devān ājyena pitṝṃś ca madhunā dvijaḥ || 1.42 ||**

**yo yajūṃṣi** yathāśakty **adhīte sa ghṛtāmṛtair devān** ājyamadhubhyāṃ ca **pitṝn prīṇāti** || 1.42 ||

	**sa tu somaghṛtair devāṃs tarpayed yo 'nvahaṃ paṭhet |**

**	sāmāni tṛptiṃ kuryāc ca pitṝṇāṃ madhusarpiṣā || 1.43 ||**

**yo 'nvahaṃ sāmāni paṭhet sa somaghṛtair devān** madhusarpirbhyāṃ **ca pitṝṃs tarpayet** || 1.43 ||

**[70]**	**vākovākyaṃ purāṇaṃ ca nārāśaṃsīś ca gāthikāḥ |**

**	itihāsāṃs tathā vidyāṃ yo 'dhīte śaktito 'nvaham || 1.45 ||**

**	māṃsakṣīraudanamadhutarpaṇaṃ sa divaukasām |**

**	karoti tṛptiṃ ca tathā ptiṝṇāṃ madhusarpiṣā || 1.46 ||**

vākovākyaṃ praśnapratipraśnarūpo vedabhāgaḥ | purāṇaṃ prasiddham | nārāśaṃsya ṛgvedakhilagranthādhītā "idaṃ janā upaśruta" ityādyās tisra ṛcaḥ | gāthikā indragāthādyāḥ | itihāsā bhāratādyāḥ | vidyā madhuvidyādyāḥ | etad yaḥ pratyahaṃ yathāśakty adhīte sa māṃskṣīraudanamadhubhir devatarpaṇaṃ madhusarpiṣā ca pitṛtṛptiṃ karoti || 1.45–46 ||

	**te tṛptās tarpayanty enaṃ sarvaiḥ kamaphalaiḥ śubhaiḥ |**

**te** devādyā uktena prakāreṇa **tṛptās** tarpayitāraṃ **sarvaiḥ** kāmyamānaiḥ **phalais tarpayanti** |

	**yaṃ yaṃ kratum adhīyīta tasya tasyāpnuyāt phalam || 1.47 ||**

kratupratipādako vedabhāgaḥ **kratus** taṃ yo 'dhīte sa **tasya** kratoḥ **phalaṃ** prāpnoti || 1. 47 ||

	**trir vittapūrṇapṛthivīdānasya phalam aśnute |**

**	tapasaś ca parasyeha nityaṃ svādhyāyavān dvijaḥ || 1.48 ||**

dhanapūrṇasy sakalabhūmidānasya trir abhyastasya parasya tapasaḥ phalaṃ tadanavaratasvādhyāyavān dvijo labhate | madhunā payasetyādīnāṃ pratyakṣaiva śrutir mūlam | sā ca brahmayajñādhyayanvidhyarthavādabhūteti brahmayajñavidhir atra kalpyaḥ | tena vinārthavādānarthakyāt | sa ca brahmacāriṇo 'pīti tatprakaraṇe vākyārambhaḥ |

	apāṃ samīpe niyato naityakaṃ vidhim āśritaḥ |

	sāvitrīm apy adhīyīta gatvāraṇye samāhitaḥ || iti |

tataś cāsamarthaḥ sāvitryā brahmayajñaṃ kuryāt | samartha ṛgadibhiḥ || 1.48 ||

_dvividhaḥ khalu brahmacārī upakurvāṇo naiṣṭhikaś ca | tatropakurvāṇasya dharmā uktāḥ | naiṣṭhikasyedānīm āha |_

**[71]	naiṣṭhiko brahmacārī ca vased ācāryasaṃnidhau |**

**	tadabhāve 'sya tanaye patnyāṃ vaiśvānare 'pi vā || 1.49 ||**

upakurvāṇakabrahmacāry āśramaṃ yam icchet tam āvaset | tatra yadi brahmacaryāśramam icchet tadā naiṣṭhikabrahmacārī bhavet | niṣṭhā śarīrapātaḥ, tadavadhike brahmacarye saṃkalpaḥ kṛto yena sa naiṣṭhikabrahmacārī | sa punar ācāryasya saṃnidhau vasen na samāvarteta | ācāryābhāve tatputrasya tadabhāva ācāryapatnyās tadabhāve 'gneḥ || 1.49 ||

_tatra vasato yat phalaṃ tad āha |_

	**anena vidhinā dehaṃ sādhayan vijitendriyaḥ |**

**	brahmalokam avāpnoti na cehājāyate punaḥ || 1.50 ||**

**anena** pūrvoktena brahmacaryacaraṇena **dehaṃ** dehavantam ātmānaṃ **sādhayan** brahmaprāptiyogyaṃ kurvan **vijitendriyo** vaśī caturmukhalokam **avāpnoti** **neha** saṃsāre **punar ājāyate** | apunarāvṛttilakṣaṇaṃ phalaṃ brahmopāsakasya sato bhavati na kevalakarmaṇaḥ | tad uktam āśramān prakṛtya chāndogye: "sarva ete puṇyalokā bhavanti brahmasaṃstho 'mṛtatvam eti" iti | asyārthaḥ: sarva ete brahmaskandhāś catvāro py āśramiṇaḥ puṇyalokā bhavanti | eṣāṃ madhye yo brahmasaṃstho brahmaniṣṭhaḥ so 'mṛtatvam apunarāvṛttilakṣaṇam etīti | hārītaḥ: "dvividho brahmacārī, upakurvāṇo naiṣṭhikaś ca | tayor upakurvāṇako vyākhyātaḥ | niṣṭhāṃ ced gacched ā śarīranipātād gurāv āsīta tadabhāve gurupatnyāṃ tadabhāve guruputraṃ(tre) guruputrābhāve 'gnim evopacaret | yajñiyāḥ samidha āhṛtya saṃmārjanopalepahodbodhana-samūhanasamindhanaparyagnikaraṇaparikramopasthānahomastotranamaskārādibhir agniṃ paricaren nāgnim adhitiṣṭhen na padbhyāṃ karṣen na mukhenopadhamen nāpaścāgniṃ ca yugapad dhārayen nājīrṇabhukta ucchiṣṭo vābhyādadyān no(nā)bhyādadhed vātikrāmen na **[72]** niṣṭhīvet | vividhacarurhavirdānaviśeṣair āgneyair agnim ahar ahar indhetāmantrya gacched āhṛtya nivedayet tanmanāḥ śarīroparamānte brahmaṇaḥ sāyujyaṃ gacchati" | vasiṣṭhaḥ: "brahmacāry āśramaṃ paricared ā śarīravimokṣaṇāt | ācārye ca prete 'gniṃ paricaret saṃyatavāk caturthaṣaṣṭhāṣṭamakālabhojī bhaikṣe gurvadhīno jaṭilaḥ śikhājaṭo vā tathā trir ahno 'bhyupeyad apaḥ" | devalaḥ: "sakṛdbhojanaṃ sakṛd apsv avagāhanam ubhayakālam agnihotraṃ saṃdhyopāsanam aluptacarmakeśanakhatvaggandhamālyasnehābhyañjanaveṣālaṃkāra-cchatropānadvāhanalaṅghanaplavanadhāvanacikitsājyotiṣalakṣaṇavāstuvidyāmaṅgalapauṣṭika-śāntikarmagāndharvasaṅgasamayabandhanaśilpalekhyalekhanakārukarmaveśmakṣetradravya-dhanadhānyaparicchadaśastradyūtavyavahārājñābhāvalīlāparihāsapraṇayakuhakavismāpana-viḍambanavivādotsekaparivedanarodanavastinasyapādodvartanavarjam | guroḥ pūrvotthānaṃ jaghanyasaṃveśanaṃ praṇāmasaṃdiṣṭakaraṇam iṣṭaśuśrūṣā nityopāsanam apacitis tadbhāve tatputre dāreṣu vā tadvṛttir ā maraṇāt" | yady āpadi kṣatriyādir gurur bhavati tadā tatra nātyantikavāsaḥ | tathā brāhmaṇe 'py adhyāpanam akurvāṇe | yad āha manuḥ |

	nābrāhmaṇo gurau śiṣyo vāsam ātyantikaṃ vaset |

	brāhmaṇe cānanūcāne kāṅkṣan gatim uttamām ||

na brahmavarasmṛter agnihotrādigṛhasthadharmavidhāyakaśrutivirodho vācyaḥ, bhinnaviṣayatvāt | yo hi strīrāgavaśāt kṛtavivāhas tadviṣayāgnihotrādiśrutiḥ | brahmacaryasmṛtis tu vairāgyād andhatvādidoṣād vā vivāhānadhikṛtapuruṣaviṣayā | ata eva pākṣikatvena naiṣṭhikatvam āha manuḥ |

	 nābrāhmaṇe gurau śiṣyo vāsam ātyantikaṃ vaset |

	brāhmaṇe cānanūcāne kāṅkṣan gatim uttamām || 

na brahmacaryasmṛter agnihotrādigṛhasthadharmavidhāyakaśrutivirodho vācayaḥ, bhinnaviṣayatvāt | yo hi strīrāgavaśāt kṛtavivāhas tadviṣayāgnihotrādiśrutiḥ | brahmacaryasmṛtis tu vairāgyād andhatvādidoṣād vā vivāhānadhikṛtapuruṣaviṣayā | ata eva pākṣikatvena naiṣṭhikatvam āha manuḥ |

	yadi tv ātyantikaṃ vāso rocayeta gurau kule |

	yuktaḥ paricared enam ā śarīravimokṣaṇāt || iti |

tathā ca viṣṇuḥ |

	kubjavāmanajātyandhaklībapaṅgvārtarogiṇām |

	vratacaryā bhavet teṣāṃ yāvajjīvam anaṃśataḥ || iti |. **[73]**

na ca vivāhādikāriṇām anāśramiṇām eva japatapaḥparāyaṇānām apy avasthānam ucitam ity āha dakṣaḥ |

	anāśramī naiva tiṣṭhed abdam ekam api dvijaḥ |

	āśrameṇa vinā tiṣṭhan prāyaścittīyate hi saḥ ||

	jape home tathā dāne svādhyāye ca rataḥ sadā |

	nāsau phalam avāpnoti kurvāṇo 'py āśramāc cyutaḥ ||

āśramād āśramāntaragamanenottaraṃ parigṛhya pūrvaṃ na parigṛhṇīyād iti sa evāha |

	trayāṇām ānulomyaṃ syāt prātilomyaṃ na vidyate |

	prātilomyena yo yāti na tasmāt pāpakṛttamaḥ || iti || 1.50 ||

**iti śrīvidyādharavaṃśaprabhavaśrīśilāhāranarendrajīmūtavāhanānvayaprasūta-śrīmadaparādityadevaviracite yājñavalkīyadharmaśāstranibandhe **

**brahmacārikāṇḍaṃ (prakaraṇaṃ) samāptam**

**atha saṭīkayājñavalkyasmṛtau**

**vivāhaprakaraṇam**

_sarvasādhāraṇatvena brahmacāriprakaraṇam uktam | adhunāvasaraprāptā gṛhasthadharmā ucyante | te ca,_

_	apatnīko naro bhūpa karmayogyo na jāyate |_

_	brāhmaṇaḥ kṣatriyo vāpi vaiśyaḥ śūdra 'pi vā nṛpa ||_

_	patnī dharmārthakāmānāṃ kāraṇaṃ pravaraṃ nṛṇām ||_  **[74]**

_ityādidarśanād bhāryayā vinā na bhavanti | sā ca snānottarakālabhāvinīty āha |_

	**gurave tu varaṃ datvā snāyād vā tadanujñayā |**

**	vedaṃ vratāni vā pāraṃ nītvā hy ubhayam eva vā || 1.51||**

pūrvoktena nyāyena **vedaṃ vratāny ubhayaṃ vā pāraṃ nītvā** samāpya **snāyāt** | eteṣāṃ ca pakṣāṇāṃ śaktikālādyapekṣayā vyavasthā | yadi bhikṣāṭanādyaśakto vyādhitatayā rājadaivikādyabhibhavāsamarthaḥ, tadā vedaṃ kevalaṃ vratāny eva vā kevalāni samāpya snāyāt | ata eva vidyāsnātako vratasnātako vidyāvrasnātako iti traividhyaṃ smaryate | atas tasya snānapariṇayanottarakālam adhyayanasamāpanaṃ tadarthajñānaṃ vā | ata eva vakṣyati,

	karma smārtaṃ vivāhāgnau kurvīta pratyahaṃ gṛhī |

iti prakramya,

	vedārthān adhigacchet tu śāstrāṇi vividhāni ca || iti |

vedārthajñānaṃ cāvaśayaṃ kāryam | tathā ca vyāsaḥ |

	na vedapāṭhamātreṇa saṃtoṣaṃ kārayed dvijaḥ |

	pāṭhamātrāvasāno hi paṅke gaur iva sīdati ||

	yathā paśur bhāravāhī na tasya labhate phalam |

	dvijas tathārthānabhijño na vedaphalam aśnute ||

	vedasyādhyayanaṃ sarvaṃ dharmaśāstrasya cāpi yat |

	ajānato 'rthaṃ tat sarvaṃ tuṣāṇāṃ kha(ka)ṇḍanaṃ yathā ||

	yo 'dhītya vidhivad vedaṃ vedārthaṃ na vicārayet |

	sa sānvayaḥ śūdrasamaḥ pātratāṃ na prapadyate ||

	adhītya yat kiṃcid api vedārthādhigame rataḥ |

	svargalokam avāpnoti dharmānuṣṭhānavid dhi saḥ ||

	śrutahīnam adhīte yan neha nāmutra tad bhavet |

	śrutaṃ tu kevalam api samuddārāya kalpate ||

	samuccitaṃ stokam api śrtuādhītaṃ viśiṣyate |

	trayāṇām api varṇānāṃ kevalādhyayanād dvijāt ||

	jñānaṃ karma ca saṃyuktaṃ muktyarthaṃ kathitaṃ yathā |

**[75]**	adhītaśrutasaṃyuktaṃ tathā śreṣṭhaṃ na kevalam ||

	pāṭhamātrārditān nityaṃ dvijātīṃś cārthavarjitān |

	paśūn iva ca tān prājño vāṅmātreṇāpi nārcayet ||

	ṛkpādam apy adhītyādau nyāyatas tu tadarthavit |

	viśiṣyate śrutaṃ yasmād garīyo dharmasādhanam ||

śrutiś ca |

	sthāṇur ayaṃ bhārahāraḥ kilābhūd adhītya vedaṃ na vijānāti yo 'rtham |

	yo 'rthajña it sakalaṃ bhadram aśnute nākam eti jñānavidhūtapāpmā ||

śuṣkavṛkṣaṃ sthāṇum āhuḥ | sa yathāropitatṛṇādibhārākrānto bhavati, na ca bharabhṛtiṃ bhārabhogaṃ vā cetayamāno labhate, kevalaṃ bhārādhārabhāvāj jantur eva bhārabhāg bhavati, tathāyaṃ bhavati — yo vedādhyayanena dhāraṇāvasānena kadarthitātmāpi tadabhidheyaṃ karmāvabodhādi pradhānaprayojanānurañjitavidhyarthavādamantranāmadheyādivibhāgena na jānāti tajjñāne 'py adyāpy ayatamānaḥ | ya idānīṃ niṣpannārthāvabodhaḥ so 'dhikṛtatvāt karmapāripūrṇyāt pramādeśu prāyaścittajāgaraṇāc ca svakarmanaipuṇyāc ca sākalyena puṇyaphalaṃ kuśalaṃ dṛṣṭam aśnute | nākaṃ ca satyalokāntam adṛṣṭapuṣṭyā prāpnoty arthajñānajanitānuṣaṅgikadharmāṃśena kṣapitadṛṣṭādṛṣṭagataparipanthināśanādidoṣadūṣakopāttadūrita iti | tathā |

	uta tvaḥ paśyan na dadarśa vācam uta tvaḥ śṛṇvan na śṛṇoty enām |

	uto tvasmai tanvaṃ visasre jāyeva patya uśasī suvāsāḥ ||

asyārthaḥ: api khalv ekaḥ paśyann api na paśyati, api khalv ekaḥ śṛṇvann api na śṛṇoti, enām avidvān vācaṃ mahārthām | uto tvasmai tanvaṃ visasre tanuṃ vivṛṇute jāyeva patya uśatī suvāsāḥ | tad yathā jāyā patye kāmayamānā suvāsāḥ svam ātmānaṃ vivṛṇute, evaṃ vāg vāgvide svam ātmānaṃ vivṛṇute | manuś ca,

	yad adhītam avijñātaṃ nigadenaiva śabdyate |

	anagnāv iva śuṣkaidho na tajjvalati karhicit ||

ityādi | api ca smārtasya gṛhyādiparijñānamātrāpekṣitatvān na ca tatparijñānam anyaśāstraśravaṇādinā **[76]** na bhavati | tasya karmakramādyavabodhamātrāpekṣitatvāt | yadi śāstrāntaraśravaṇād vinā sarvatra nādhikriyate, tadāgnikāryādāv apy anadhikāro brahmacāriṇaḥ syāt | tena yad yat karoti tat taj jñātvā na yugapaj jñātveti | tasmāj jñātvā cānuṣṭhānam ity ayam api vidhiḥ parigṛhīto bhavati | kathaṃ snāyād ity āha: **gurave** pūrvoktāya **varam** abhilaṣitaṃ kātyāyanādyuktam: "gaur brāhmaṇasya varo grāmo rājanyasyāśvo vaiśyasya" ityādi gurvarthāharaṇaśaktādiviṣayam, tadanyādiviṣayam: 

	dhānyaṃ vāsāṃsi śākaṃ ca gurave prītim āharet | 

ityādi manvādilakṣitaṃ vā datvā, **tadanujñayā** vādattavaro 'pi | ata eva gautamaḥ: "vidyānte gurur arthena nimantryaḥ kṛtānujñāta(na)sya vā snānam" iti | vedapāranayanaṃ samuccaya eva vedādhyayanasya tadarthajñānena saha | ata eva "vedam adhītya cchandoviṣayān arthān buddhvā snāyāt" iti smaryate | manur api |

	tapoviśeṣair vividhair vrataiś ca vidhicoditaiḥ |

	vedaḥ kṛtsno 'dhigantavyaḥ sarahasyo dvijanmanā || iti |

adhigantavyo granthato 'rthataś ceti darśayati | vrataiś ca pūrvoktair varjayen madhumāṃsagandhamālyānī(sānī)ityādipratipāditaiḥ | tataś ca yad uktaṃ bhaṭṭena,

	tasmād gurukule tiṣṭhan madhumāṃsādi varjayan |

	jijñāsenāviruddhatvād dharmam ity avagamyate ||

iti, tad anena virudhyate, teṣāṃ samāvartanādhikatvāt | ata eva,

	agnīndhanaṃ bhaikṣacaryam adhaḥśayyāṃ guror hitam |

	ā samāvartanāt kuryāt kṛtopanayano divjaḥ |

iti niyamyate | na ca,

	gurugehād anāvṛttaḥ snātako hi na kathyate |

iti snāne samāvartanabhrāntiḥ kāryā,

	guruṇānumataḥ snātvā samāvṛtto yathāvidhi |

	udvaheta dvijo bhāryāṃ savarṇāṃ lakṣaṇānvitām ||

iti bhedasmaraṇāt | snātakaś ca manvādibhiḥ pradarśitaḥ |

	taṃ pratītaṃ svadharmeṇa brahmadāyaharaṃ pituḥ |

	sragviṇaṃ talpa āsīnam arhayet prathamaṃ gavā || iti |. **[77]**

taṃ snātakaṃ dārasaṃgrahābhimukhatayā pratītaṃ pitur brahmadāyaharam, brahma vedaḥ | anena tasyādhyayanayogaḥ khyāpyate | dāyo riktham | anena tasya yogyastvam ucyate | anyathā sarvarṇāputro 'py anyāyavṛtto na labhate keṣām iti tadabhāvaḥ | pitur dravyābhāve pratigrahādināpy avāpya pāṇigrahaṇaṃ kartavyaṃ pāṇigrahaṇādi gṛhyaṃ paricaret | anyathā pākayajñāder asiddhaḥ, tasya dravyamūlatvāt | ata eva gautamaḥ: "dravyādānaṃ vivāhasiddhyartham" iti | sragvigrahaṇaṃ vibhūṣaṇaprāptyartham | talpaṃ śayanam | tatrastham arhayet pūjayet prathamaṃ gavā | gośabdena madhuparkaṃ lakṣayati, "ṛtvijo vṛtvā madhuparkam āharet snātakāyopasthitāya rājñe ca" iti smaraṇāt | sa ca gāṃ vedayate kuruteti kārayiṣyann utsṛjety utprekṣann iti dvidhā bhavati | snātakaś ca navadhā bhidyate, saṃkalpabhedāt | tathāha manuḥ |

	sāṃtānikaṃ yakṣyamāṇam adhvagaṃ sārvavedasam |

	gurvarthapitṛmātrarthasvādhyāyārthyupatāpinaḥ |

	navaitān snātakān vidyād brāhmaṇān dharmabhaikṣukān || 1.51 ||

_tataḥ kim ity āha |_

	**aviplutabrahmacaryo lakṣaṇyāṃ striyam udvahet |**

**	ananyapūrvikāṃ kāntām asapiṇḍāṃ yavīyasīm || 1.52 ||**

naiva viplutaṃ brahmacaryaṃ yasya | viplutiḥ skhalanam | tatsaṃbhave tu prāyaścittī na tv avivāhyaḥ kiṃ tv ayaṃ viśeṣaḥ | yadi snānād adho viplutas tadāvakīrṇiprāyaścittam,

	avakīrṇī bhaved gatvā brahmacārī tu yoṣitam |

iti smaraṇāt | snānād ūrdhvaṃ yadi punas tadā sāmānyam,

	madyapāsatyavṛttā ca pratikūlā ca yā bhavet |

	vyādhitā cādhivettavyā ||

tathā,

	bhāryāyai pūrvamāriṇyai datvāgnīn antyakarmaṇi |

	punar dārakriyāṃ kuryāt ||

ityādismaraṇadarśaṇāt prāptasya punar vivāhasya viplutabrahmacaryatvāpatter aprāptir mā **[78]** prasāṅkṣīd ity atrāviplutabrahmacarya iti padaṃ pūrvatra snānakartur viśeṣaṇīyam | lakṣaṇair yuktām | lakṣaṇāni bāhyābhyantarāṇi | bāhyāni kāyasvarādigatāni | yathāha manuḥ |

	avyaṅgāṅgīṃ saumyanāmnīṃ haṃsavāraṇagāminīm |

	tanulomakeśadaśāṃ mṛdvaṅgīṃ cārubhāṣiṇīm || iti | 

daśāṃ daśanām ity artha iti | **lakṣaṇyām** ity etasmād eva viparīto tu tyājyā, yathā |

	nodvahet kapilāṃ kanyāṃ nādhikāṅgīṃ no rogiṇīm |

	nālomikāṃ nātilomnīṃ na vācāṭāṃ na piṅgalām || iti |

tathā nāmato 'pi varjyā, yathā vā |

	devanāmnīṃ nadīnāmnīṃ śailagandharvanāmikām |

	ṛkṣavṛkṣanadīnāmnīṃ dārārthe parivarjayet || iti |

yathā |

	narkṣavṛkṣanadīnāmnīṃ nāntyaparvatanāmikām |

	na pakṣyahipuṣpanāmnīṃ na vibhīṣaṇanāmikām ||

yadā punar abhyantarāṇi sūkṣmāni bhavanti tadā āśvalāyanoktā parīkṣā kāryā, tatra "buddhirūpalakṣaṇasaṃyuktām" ity uktvā svayam eva codyaṃ kṛtam "lakṣaṇāni durjñānāni" it, tasyottaram: "aṣṭau piṇḍān kṛtvā, ṛtam agre prathamam jajñe ṛte satyaṃ pratiṣṭhitam | yadi ca kumāry abhijātā tad iyam iha pratipadyatāṃ yat satyaṃ tad dṛśyatām iti piṇḍān abhimantrya kumārīṃ brūyād eṣām ekaṃ gṛhāṇeti | kṣetrāc ced ubhayataḥ satyād gṛhṇīyād annavaty asyāḥ prajā bhaviṣyatīti vidyāt | goṣṭhāt paśumatī | vedipurīṣād brahmavarcasvinī | avināśino hradāt sarvasaṃpannā | devanāt kitavī | catuṣpathād vipravājinī | iriṇād adhanyā | śmaśānāt patighnī" iti | ananyapūrvikāṃ naivānyasmai yā pūrvaṃ dattā | etac ca vāgdattāviṣayaṃ veditavyaṃ na saṃskṛtāviṣayam, tasyāḥ punarbūtvāt | yathāha manuḥ |

	yasyā mriyeta kanyāyā vācā satye kṛte patiḥ |

	tām anena vidhānena nijo vindeta devaraḥ ||  **[79]**

na ca tatra dānaṃ nivṛttam ity āśaṅkanīyam,

	adbhir vācā ca dattāyāṃ mriyetādau varo yadi |

	na ca mantropanītā syāt kumārī pitur eva sā ||

iti vasiṣṭhasmaraṇāt | evaṃ balād apahṛtāyām api veditavyam,

	balād apahṛtā mantrair api na saṃskṛtā |

	anyasmai vidhivad deyā yathā kanyā tathaiva sā ||

iti tenaivoktatvāt | etac ca prāyaścittotarakālaṃ veditavyam | kāntāṃ snātakasya kamanīyatvān manonayanānandadāyinīm | etac ca maṅgalādinirākaraṇena vidhīyate, "yatra manaḥsaktis tām udvahet" it vidhānāt | asapiṇḍānāṃ sāpiṇḍyaṃ vakṣyati | yavīyasīṃ janmataḥ pramāṇato 'pīty eke | vasiṣṭhaḥ: "gṛhastho vinītakrodhaharṣo guruṇānujñātaḥ snātvāsamānārṣeyīm aspṛṣṭamaithunām avaravayasaṃ sadṛśīṃ bhāryāṃ vindeta" | gṛhastha it bhāvini bhūtavad upacāras taddharmaprāptyarthaḥ | tenākṛtadāro 'pi gārhasthyasaṃkalpavān āśramāntarān nivṛtto gṛhasthadharmeṣv adhikriyate | na ca "brahmacārī bhūtvā gṛhī bhaved gṛhī bhūtvā vanī bhaved vanī bhūtvā pravrajet" iti niyamyate, aniyamenāśramāntarasvīkāradarśanāt | tathā ca nṛsiṃhapurāṇam |

	gurave dakṣiṇāṃ datvā sā (sa) yam icchet tam āvaset |

	viraktaḥ pravrajed vidvān || iti |

viṣṇupurāṇaṃ ca |

	gṛhītavidyo gurave datvātha gurudakṣiṇām |

	gārhasthyam icchan bhūpāla kuryād dāraparigraham ||

	brahmacaryeṇa vā kālaṃ kuryāt saṃkalpapūrvakam |

	guroḥ śuśrūṣaṇaṃ kuryāt tatputrāder athāpi vā ||

	vaikhānaso vāpi bhavet parivrāḍ atha vecchayā || iti || 1.52 ||

_viśeṣāntarāṇy āha |_

	**arogiṇīṃ bhrātṛmatīm asamānārṣagotrajām |**

**	pañcamāt saptamād ūrdhvaṃ mātṛtaḥ pitṛtas tathā || 1.53 ||**

**arogiṇīm** adīrgharogopasṛṣṭām | **bhrātṛmatīṃ** putrikātvabhayāt | yathāha manuḥ |

**[80]**	yasyās tu na bhaved bhrātā na vijñāyet vā pitā |

	nopayaccheta tāṃ prājñaḥ putrikādharmaśaṅkayā ||

ity anena guptāpi putrikā bhavati | na kevalaṃ yā paribhāṣya dīyate: 

	asyāṃ yo jāyate putraḥ sa me putro bhaviṣyati |

iti ratiputraphalā bhāryā yadi putro 'nyasya bhavati tadaikāṅgavaikalyam | putrikāṃ vakṣyati | asamānārṣagotrajām ity [samānārṣajām?] asamānagotrajām iti [c?] veditavyam | tataś ca sagotrāyāḥ sagotratvenaiva niṣedho na samānārṣāpekṣayā | evaṃ samānārṣāpi sa(na) gotram apekṣate | ata eva gautamaḥ: "asamānapravarair vivāhaḥ" iti | samānatā ca nāmataḥ saṃkhyātaś ca samuccayena bhavati na tadvaiṣamye | yatrāpi saṃkhyāsāmya. ekasya dvayor vānyatvaṃ tatrāpy asamānataiva | yatra punar āṅgirasāmbarīṣayauvanāśveti māndhātāmbarīṣayauvanāśveti vikalpena ṛṣayo bhavanti tatrāpi varjyā, samatvasya pākṣikatvāt | na cāsamānārṣagrahaṇaṃ gotraviśeṣaṇam | "asamānapravarair vivāhaḥ" iti bhedasmaraṇāt, 

	pariṇīya sagotrāṃ tu samānapravarāṃ tathā |

	tyāgaṃ kṛtvā dvijas tasyās tataś cāndrāyaṇaṃ caret ||

iti pṛthakprāyaścittāc ca | tyāgaś copabogasya na tu tasyāḥ | tathāha sumantuḥ: "mātulasutāṃ paitṛṣvaseyīṃ samānārṣagotrāṃ ca pariṇīya cāndrāyaṇaṃ caret | parityajyaināṃ bibhṛyāt" iti, etac cāmatipūrvaṃ(rve) veditavyam | "sagotrāṃ ced amatyopagacched bhātṛvad enāṃ bibhṛyāt prajātāṃ cet kṛcchrābdapādaṃ caret" iti baudhāyanaḥ | matipūrve gurutaram | yathāha gautamaḥ: "mātṛpitṛyonisaṃbaddhāgas tena nāstikaninditakarmābhyāsipatitātyāgyapatitatyāginaḥ patitāḥ" iti | manur api |

	jñātitvenānupeyās tāh patati hy upayann adhaḥ || iti |

tataś ca patitotpannaḥ patito bhavatīti labhyata eva | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">nanu</span> sagotranirākaraṇenaiva sapiṇḍaniṣedhe prāpte kim iti bhedenādhastane śloke "asapiṇḍāṃ yavīyasīm" **[81]** ity uktam | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">na</span> | etat tatsaṃtatijāyā nirākaraṇārtham | itarathāsamānārṣagotrajā tatstrīsaṃtatijā pariṇeyā bhavet | eṣā cāsapiṇḍatā mātṛpakṣe 'pi veditavyā | yathāha manuḥ |

	asapiṇḍā ca yā mātur asagotrā ca yā pituḥ |

	sā praśastā dvijātīnāṃ dārakarmaṇi maithune ||

naiva sapiṇḍā mātur yā | cakārāt pituś ca | "asagotrā ca yā" ity etāvaty ucyamāne yat pitur grahaṇaṃ karoti tat kṣetrikāputrābhiprāyeṇa | anyathā

	yasya te bījato jātās tasya te netarasya tu |

iti tat sagotrāyā vivāhyatvaṃ syāt | sā praśastā, kva, dārakarmaṇi, yad dārair vinā na bhavati | tac ca vacanād eva mā bhūd ity āha — maithune, mithunanirvartye yad ekaikasya nirvartya na bhavati pākayajñādikam | ata eva āpastambaḥ: "pāṇigrahaṇād dhi sahatvaṃ karmasu" iti | sahagrahaṇaṃ balīvardavat samānādhikāra iti darśanārtham | tataś ca bhartrāsau bhartavyāhaṃ dānādikaṃ nirvartayāmi tvam api saṃkalpaṃ kurviti, tayāpi tathaiva kāryam anyathā doṣa iti sahādhikāraḥ | ataś caikaphalabhoktṛtvaṃ phalāntaroddbhūtibādhaś ca | "asapiṇḍā ca yā mātuḥ" iti mātulādisutāpariṇayaniṣadhaḥ | mātuḥ sapiṇḍatvāt |

	pañcamāt saptamād ūrdhvaṃ mātṛtaḥ pitṛtas tathā |

iti mātṛkulān mātāmahaprabhṛtīn pañca puruṣān atītyodvāhaḥ kāryaḥ kartavya ity arthaḥ | evaṃ sapta pitṛkulāt | atra "na bhāryāṃ vindeta" ity adhikāre viṣṇuḥ: "mātṛtas tv ā pañcamāt puruṣāt pitṛtaś cāsaptamāt" iti | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">nanu</span> "asapiṇḍām" ity uktam eva kim arthaṃ punar ucyate "saptamāt pitṛtaḥ" iti | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">satyam</span> | kiṃ tu baijino 'pi saptamād iti niyamārtham | yathāha gautamaḥ: "ūrdhvaṃ tu saptamāt pitṛbandhubhyo baijinaś ca mātṛbandhubhyaḥ pañcamāt" iti | nārado 'pi |

	saptamāt pañcamād arvāg bandhubhyaḥ pitṛmātṛtaḥ |

	avivāhyā sagotrā ca samānapravarā tathā ||

paiṭhīnasiś ca: "asamānārṣeyīṃ kanyāṃ varayet | pañca mātṛtaḥ pariharet | sapta pitṛtaḥ | trīn mātṛtaḥ pañca pitṛto vā" iti | atra ca samānajātīye pañca | asamānajātīye trīn iti vyavasthito vikalpaḥ | na ca saptame pañcame vā bhavati vivāhyā | yathā,

	saptame pañcame caiva yeṣāṃ vaivāhikī kriyā |

	ye ca saṃtānajās te 'pi patitāḥ śūdratāṃ gatāḥ ||

iti viṣṇuḥ | kiṃ ca yady asamānagotratvān mātulasutāpariṇayanaṃ tadā mātṛṣvasā(sṛ)duhitur api syāt, samānanyāyāt | etad yadi smṛtīnām eva kevalānāṃ prāmāṇyam | yāvatā śiṣṭasyāpi prāmāṇyam | yathāha manuḥ |

	vedo 'khilo dharmamūlaṃ smṛtiśīle ca tadvidām |

	ācāraś caiva sādhūnāṃ vedavit smṛtiśīlatā ||

vyatirekeṇa sādhūnām ācāraṃ darśayati yena tasya śāstravirodhe 'pi prāmāṇyaṃ syāt | itarathā śīlaṃ ceṣṭitam ācāraś caiva sādhūnām iti bhedena grahaṇaṃ na syāt | sādhavaś ca darśitāḥ |

	nyāyenādhigato yais tu vedaḥ saparibṛṃhaṇaḥ |

	te śiṣṭā brāhmaṇā jñeyāḥ śrutipratyakṣahetavaḥ || iti |

na ca tatra vedavido na santi na ca tair etan na caritam | yathā ca baudhāyanena spaṣṭam evaṃvidhasyācarasya prāmāṇyaṃ darśitam: "pañcavidhā vipratipattiḥ | dakṣiṇato 'nupanītena bhāryayā ca saha bhojanaṃ paryuṣitabhojanam ucchitṣṭabhojanaṃ pitṛṣvasā(sṛ)mātuladuhitṛpariṇayanam iti | tathottarataḥ pañca | ūrṇāvikrayaḥ śīdhupānam ubhayatodadbhir vyavahāra āyudhīyakaṃ samudrayānam iti | itara itarasmin kurvan duṣyatītara itarasmin deśe prāmāṇyād ity ācārabalenaiva prāmāṇyam uktaṃ syāt | etad yady anantaraṃ na brūyān mithyaitad iti gautamaḥ | ubhayaṃ tv etan nādriyeta | śiṣṭasmṛtivirodhāt" iti | smṛtivirodhaś ca darśitaḥ: "ūrdhvaṃ mātṛbandhubhyaḥ pañcamāt" iti | "śiṣṭaḥ punar akāmātmā" iti vasiṣṭhasmaraṇāt | na śiṣṭāḥ kāmakāreṇa śāstravirodhe pravartante | **[83]** gautamagrahaṇam ekavākyapratipādanārtham, anirākaraṇāt | tathā ca vasiṣṭhaḥ: "deśakulācārā āmnāyāviruddhāḥ pramāṇam" iti | āmnāyo vedaḥ | tadavirodho 'stīti cet, <span style="text-decoration:underline;">naitat</span>, bhaginyādigamane 'pi tadavirodhadarśanād atiprasakteḥ | tasmān nāndhaparamparayā nyāyāgatasya vyavahārasya prāmānyam | yad api,

	āyāhīndra patibhir īḷetebhir yajñam imaṃ no vājasātau juṣasva |

	tṛptāṃ jahur mātulasyeva te tava bhagaḥ paitṛṣvaseyīm apām ivaughaḥ ||

iti tanmantrāṇām avidhāyakatve saty api pariṇayananirākaraṇam dyotyate | katham | kaścit prārthyate | āyāhīndrāsmadīyaṃ yajñam anyair api somapatibhir īḷitebhiḥ stotrārhaiḥ saha | āgatya ca vājasātau somarūpānnabhojanaprastāve juṣasva | somam iti saṃbadhyate | evaṃ prārthyendrastutyarthaṃ svarūpānuvādaṃ karoti — ye te somapatayo bhavatā sahāyātās te sakṛtsomapānena tṛptāḥ santaḥ somaṃ jahus tyaktavantaḥ | kim iva, yathā paitṛṣavaseyīṃ bhaginīṃ bhāryātvenātyantānabhilaṣaṇīyāṃ tyajanti svakīyamātulasya saṃbandhāyogyatayā, tadvad bhavaduddeśena somaṃ tyaktvanto nirākāṅkṣatayā | tava punar ayaṃ somabhāgo 'pām ivaughaḥ sātatyenākarmasamāpter iti | tataś cānena pratiṣedho darśitaḥ | yad api śrutau: "tṛtīyaṃ puruṣaṃ gacchāmahe" iti | tad api snugvyūhanaparatvenānyārthatvā(v)t } api ca "prajāpatiḥ svāṃ duhitaram abhidhyāyat tasyāṃ reto 'vākirat" ityādiśravaṇād atiprasaktiṃ karoti | prāyaścittadarśanāc ca |

	paitṛṣavaseyīṃ bhaginīṃ svasrīyāṃ matur eva ca |

	mātuś ca bhrātur āptāṃ ca gatvā cāndrāyaṇaṃ caret || iti |

bhaginīgrahaṇaṃ saṃdehanirāsārtham | na cāpariṇītāviṣayatvam āśaṅkanīyam | yenānantaraṃ vakti |

	etās tisras tu bhāryārthaṃ nopayaccheta buddhimān |

	jñātitvenānupeyās tāḥ patati hy upayann adhaḥ || iti |

tathā kanyādātur api niyamo 'sti, yathāha āpastambaḥ: "sagotrebhyo duhitaraṃ na prayacchen mātuś ca yonisaṃbandhebhyaḥ pituś ca saptamāt" iti, prāyaścittasmaraṇāc ca |

	mātulasya sutām ūḍhvā mātṛgotrāṃ tathaiva ca |

	samānapravarāṃ caiva dvijaś cāndrāyaṇaṃ caret || iti ||  **[84]**

mātṛgotragrahaṇaṃ pitṛsagotravan nirākaraṇārtham, janyajanakasaṃbandhasyobhayasyobhayatrāviśiṣṭatvāt | śātātapo 'pi |

	ekagotrāṃ vivāhyaiva samānapravarāṃ tathā |

	mātulasya sutāṃ caiva bhuktvā cāndrāyaṇaṃ caret || iti |

yadā cetthaṃ tadā na kutaścid bhrāntibuddhir vyākhyānāt tatpravṛtter vā saṃdehaḥ kāryaḥ śāstrasya viviktatvāt || 1.53 ||

	**daśapūruṣavikhyātāc chrotriyāṇāṃ mahākulāt |**

**	sphītād api na saṃcārirogadoṣasamanvitāt || 1.54 ||**

**daśa pūruṣā** mātṛtaḥ pañca pitṛtaś ca khyātā yasmin kule tasmāt kanyā grāhyeti niyamyate | yathā āśvalāyanaḥ: "kulam agre parīkṣeta mātṛtaḥ pitṛtaś ca" iti | idam aparaṃ viśeṣaṇaṃ **śrotiyāṇāṃ mahākulāt** | "śrotriyaś chando 'dhīte" (Pāṇ 5.2.84) ity adhyayanaśrutena śrotriyo bhavatīti śrutaṃ lakṣyati | **māhākulāt** putrapautrapaśudāsīgrāmādismṛddhād iti | evaṃ sarvaprāptau satyām apavādam āha — **sphītād api na** grāhyā **saṃcāriro**gānvitāt | saṃcāriṇaḥ śukraśoṇitānuyātā rogāḥ kuṣṭhārśaḥprabhṛtayaḥ[taiḥ], doṣaiś ca niṣpuruṣatvādibhir anvitāt | ata eva manuḥ |

	mahānty api samṛddhāni go'jāvidhandhānyataḥ |

	strīsaṃbandhe daśemāni kulāni parivarjayet || iti |

	hīnakriyaṃ niṣpuruṣaṃ niśchandolomaśārśasam |

	kṣayyāmayāvyapasmāriśvitrikuṣṭhikulāni ca || iti |

hīnakriyaṃ yathāvihitagarbhādhānādikriyārahitam | niṣpuruṣaṃ kanyājanmādibahulam | niśchando vedādhyayanarahitam | lomaśamatyulbaṇalomayuktam | arśasamarśovyādhiyuktam | hārīto pi: "śvitrikuṣṭhyudariyakṣmāmayāvyalpāyuranārśa(rarśa)sa(sā) [nārṣeyā] brahmasamānārṣeyaṃ cety etāny apatitāny api kulāni varjanīyāni bhavanti | kulānurūpāḥ prajāḥ sambhavantīty āditaḥ ṣaṭ | ayajñiyatvād anārṣeyam | adaivatvād abrahma | ekakulatvāt samānārṣeyam iti | **[85]** tasmāt sapta pitṛtaḥ parīkṣya pañca mātṛto nagnikāṃ śreṣṭhāṃ bhrātṛmatīṃ bhāryāṃ vindeta | tasmāt kulanakṣatravijñānopapannāṃ varayet" | āmayāvi atroketarasaṃcārirogavat | atra ca śvitryādīni ṣaḍ varjanīyāni | atra hetuḥ — kulānurūpāḥ prajā bhavantīti | anārṣeyam asmaryamāṇagotrapravaram | tasya ca varjyatvam ayajñiyatvāt | ayajñiyatvaṃ ca yajñeṣv asmaryamāṇagotrapravarasyānadhikārāt | abrahmāvidyamānavedādhyayanam | tadvarjyatve hetuḥ — adaivatvād iti, daivakarmaśūnyatvāt | "nagnikā daśavarṣā" it bhaviṣyatpurāṇam | yamaś ca |

	caturdaśa kulānīmāny avivāhyāni nirdiśet |

	anārṣeyaṃ brāhmaṇānām ṛtvijāṃ ca vivarjayet ||

	atyuccam atihrasvaṃ ca ativarṇaṃ ca varjayet |

	hīnāṅgam atiriktāṅgam āmayāvikulāni ca ||

	śvitrikuṣṭhikulādīnāṃ kuryād viparivarjanam |

	sadā kāmakulaṃ varjyaṃ lomaśānām ca yat kulam |

	apasmārikulaṃ yac ca yac ca pāṇḍukulaṃ bhavet ||

ṛtvijo 'tra nindyayājakāḥ | kāmakulaṃ kāmapradhānakulam | ativarṇam atikṛṣṇam atigauraṃ vā || 1.54 ||

_kiṃ ca_ |

	**etair eva guṇair yuktaḥ savarṇaḥ śrotriyo varaḥ |**

**	yatnāt parīkṣitaḥ puṃstve yuvā dhīmāñ janapriyaḥ || 1.55 ||**

etair eva guṇaiḥ pūrvoktair yukto doṣaiś ca varjito varo bhavati | savarṇa utkṛṣṭo vā yadi śrotriyo bhavati | yatnāt parīkṣitaḥ puṃstve puruṣārthasya tanmūlatvāt | parīkṣā ca nāradoktā |

	parīkṣyaḥ puruṣaḥ puṃstve nijair evāṅgalakṣaṇaiḥ |

	pumāṃś ced avikalpena sa kanyāṃ labdhum arhati ||

	subaddhajatrujānvasthisubaddhāṃsaśiroruhaḥ |

	sthūlaghāṭas tanūjatvagavilagnagatisvaraḥ ||

	reto 'sya plavate vāpsu hrādi mūtraṃ ca phenilam |

	pumān syāl lakṣaṇair ebhir viparītas tu ṣaṇḍakaḥ ||

**[86]**	caturdasavidhaḥ paaṇḍaḥ śāstre dṛṣṭo manīṣibhiḥ |

	cikitsyaś cācikitsyaś ca teṣām ukto vidhiḥ kramāt ||

	nisargaṣaṇḍo vadhraś ca pakṣapaṇḍas tathaiva ca |

	abhiśāpād guro rogād devakrodhāt tathaiva ca ||

	īrṣyāpaṇḍaś ca sevyaś ca vātaretā mukhebhagaḥ |

	ākṣiptam oghabījau ca śālīno 'nyāpatis tathā ||

	tatrādyāvapratīkārau pakṣākhyaṃ māsam ācaret |

	anukramāt trayasyāsya kālaḥ saṃvatsaraḥ smṛtaḥ ||

	īrṣyāpaṇḍādayo ye 'nye catvāraḥ samudāhṛtāḥ |

	tyaktavyās te patitavat kṣatayonyāpi ca striyā ||

	ākṣiptam oghabījābhyāṃ kṛte 'pi patikarmaṇi |

	patir anyas tato nāryā vatsarārdhaṃ pratīkṣya tu ||

	śālīnasyāpi ghṛṣṭastrīsaṃyogād bhraśyati dvi(dhva)jaḥ |

	taṃ hīnaviṣayaṃ tu strī varṣaṃ kṣiptvānyam āśrayet ||

	anyasyāṃ yo manuṣyaḥ syād amanuṣyaḥ svayoṣiti |

	labheta sānyaṃ bhartāram etat kāryaṃ prajāpateḥ ||

	apatyārthaṃ striyaḥ sṛṣṭāḥ strī kṣetraṃ bījino narāḥ |

	kṣetraṃ bījavate deyaṃ nābījī kṣetram arhati ||

subaddhaṃ suśliṣṭam, jatru grīvāskandhayoḥ saṃdhiḥ | ghāṭā grīvāpaścādbhāgaḥ | nisargapaṇḍo liṅgavṛṣaṇahīna evotpannaḥ | vadhraś cālitāṇḍaḥ | pakṣapaṇḍo yasya pakṣāntaritā ratiśaktiḥ | guror abhiśāpād eva, devakrodhād eva devanindājanitakrodhāt | īrṣyāpaṇḍaḥ svastrīviṣaya īrṣyāstambhitaretāḥ | sevyaḥ striyā bahuprakāraṃ sevyamāno jātariraṃsaḥ | vātaretā yasya ratānte liṅgena vātaniḥsaraṇamātram | mukhebhagaḥ, yaḥ paramukha eva bhagakāryaṃ karoti | ākṣiptaretā visargasamaye yasya retaḥ pratyakpravartate | moghabījo yasya garbhādānasamarthaṃ reto na bhavati | śālīno yasya dhṛṣṭastrīsaṃnipātāl liṅgapāto bhavati | anyāpatiḥ — yasya bhāryāvyatiriktāyām eva yoṣiti puṃstvam | māsam ācaret, māsaṃ yāvat pratīkṣeta | **[87]** [etebhyaḥ pūrvajñātebhyo na kanyā deyā (yadi tv ajñānād dadyāc cikitsyeṣu cikitsāṃ yāvat pratīkṣeta |] acikitsyatve datvācchidyānyasmai deyā |) yuvā na vṛddhaḥ | dhīmān abhrāntacittaḥ, sarvasya cittamūlatvāt | ata eva "buddhimate kanyām upayacchet" ity uktam | janapriyo na viraktajanaḥ, dṛṣṭādṛṣṭasya tanmūlatvāt | gautamo 'pi: "vidyācāritrabandhuśīlasaṃpannāya dadyāt" iti || 1.55 ||

_kiṃ ca_ |

	**yad ucyate dvijātīnāṃ śūdrādāropasaṃgrahaḥ |**

**	naitan mama mataṃ yasmāt tatrātmā jāyate svayam || 1.56 ||**

yad ucyate catasro bhāryā brāhmaṇasya tisro rājño dve vaiśyasyeti śūdrādāropasaṃgrahaḥ | naiva mama tanmatam | kim iti | yasmād ayaṃ tatra jāyate svayaṃ tasmāj jāya bhavati, "yad asyāṃ jāyate punaḥ" iti śruteḥ | manur api |

	hīnajātiṃ striyaṃ mohād udvahanto dvijātayaḥ |

	kulāny eva nayanty āśu sasaṃtānāni śūdratām || iti |

tathā |

	śūdrāṃ śayanam āropya brāhmaṇo yāty adhogatim |

	janayitvā sutaṃ tasyāṃ brāhmaṇyād eva hīyate || iti |

yat punar uktam,

	na brāhmaṇakṣatriyayor āpady api hi tiṣṭhatoḥ |

	kasmiṃścid api vṛttānte śūdrā bhāryopadiśyate ||

iti, tat tayor atyantapratiṣedhārthaṃ na vaiśyādiprāptyartham || 1.56 ||

_anukalpakramam āha |_

	**tisro varṇānupūrvyeṇa dve tathaikā yathākramam |**

**	brāhmaṇakṣatriyaviśāṃ bhāryāḥ svā śūdrajanmanaḥ || 1.57 ||**

yadā punaruktalakṣaṇā savarṇā nāsti pūrvā ca vinaṣṭā[na] cānāśramiṇā sthātavyaṃ na cāśramāntare 'dhikriyate sāmarthyaḍ bahudhano bālāpatyaś ca tadā tasyām avasthāyāṃ **tisro dve ekā ca** **brāhmaṇakṣatriyaviśāṃ bhāryā** varṇānupūrvyeṇa **svā** śūdrasya savarṇā punaś caturthī mukhyā sthitaiva | yathāha manuḥ |

	śūdraiva bhāryā śūdrasya sā ca svā ca viśaḥ smṛte |

**[88]**	te ca svā caiva rājñaḥ syur tāś ca svā cāgryajanmanaḥ ||

	kāmatas tu pravṛttānām imāḥ syuḥ kramaśo 'varāḥ || iti |

kāmataḥ pravṛttānāṃ na dharmataḥ, ata eva tā jaghanyāḥ | kramaśo na vyutkrameṇa, vyutkrame ca doṣo manunā darśitaḥ |

	śūdrāvedī pataty atrer utathyatanayasya ca |

	śaunakasya sutotpattyā tadapatyatayā bhṛgoḥ || iti |

atrigautamayor idaṃ mataṃ śūdrāvedī patati vedanamātreṇaiva | śaunakasya sutotpattyā, tasyāpatyeneti bhṛgoḥ | tac ca vyutkrameṇeti draṣṭavyam | itarathā,

	catustridvyekabhāgī nā varṇaśo brāhmaṇātmajā |

iti bhāgavibhāgau na syātām | na ca tatprādhānyaṃ śrāddhādidāneṣu kāryam,

	daivapitryātitheyāni tatpradhānāni yasya tu |

	nāśnanti pitaras tasya na ca svargaṃ sa gacchati ||

iti vacanāt || 1.57 ||

_vivāhān āha_ |

	**brāhmo vivāha āhūya dīyate śaktyalaṃkṛtā |**

**	tajjaḥ punāty ubhayataḥ puruṣān ekaviṃśatim || 1.58 ||**

brāhmo nāma vivāho brāhmanānāṃ ucita iti | tasminn āhūya pūrvoktalakṣaṇaṃ varaṃ varo(re) varayitavyaḥ a(vye ')rthitve jñāte śaktyālaṃkṛtya kanyā dīyate | manur api |

	ācchādya cārhayitvā ca śrutaśīlavate svayam |

	āhūya dānaṃ kanyāyā brāhmo dharmaḥ prakīrtitaḥ || iti | \
devalo 'pi |

	tato vinītāṃ kalyāṇīṃ kanyāṃ kulavayonvitām |

	alaṃkṛtyārhate dadyād vivāho brāhma ucyate ||

yamaś ca |

	adbhir yā dīyate kanyā brahmadāyeti tāṃ viduḥ ||

brahmadāyetisāmjñā śrāddhe paṅktipāvanatvavyavahārārtham | tasyāṃ jātaḥ punāty ubhayatra mātāpitṛkule puruṣān ekaviṃśatim | yadi yathoktakārī bhavati | tathā ca gautamaḥ: "punanti sādhavaḥ purāḥ" iti | atra manuḥ |

	daśa pūrvāparān vaṃśyān ātmānaṃ caikaviṃśakam |

	brāhmīputraḥ sukṛtakṛn mocayaty enasaḥ pitṝn || **[89]**

sukṛtaṃ vihitakaraṇaṃ pratiṣiddhavarjanaṃ cocyate | āśvalāyanaḥ: "tasyāṃ jāto dvādaśāvarān dvādaśa parān punāty ubhayataḥ" iti || 1.58 ||

	**yajñasthaṛtvije daivaḥ**

vivāha ity anuvartate, dīyate śaktyalaṃkṛteti ca | ṛtvije yajñaṃ kurvate dakṣiṇātvena yathāśakty alaṃkṛtya kanyā dīyata eva daivo vivāhaḥ ||

		**ādāyārṣas tu godvayam |**

varād gomithunaṃ gṛhītvā tasmai yathāśakty alaṃkṛtya kanyā dīyata ity eṣa ārṣo vivāhaḥ | śaunakaḥ: "gomithunaṃ datvopayaccheta sa ārṣaḥ" iti | 

_anayoḥ phalam āha |_

	**caturdaśa prathamajaḥ punāty uttarajaś ca ṣaṭ || 1.59 ||**

prathamavivāhajāto daivavivāhotpannaḥ sapta pūrvān saptāvarān puruṣān punāti | uttara ārṣo vivāhas tajjas trīn pūrvāṃs trīn avarān ity evaṃ ṣaṭ puruṣān punāti || 1.59 ||

	**sahobhau varatāṃ dharmam ity uktvā dīyate 'rthine |**

**	sa kāyaḥ**

ubhau saha dharmaṃ caratām ity evaṃ kanyāvarāv uktvā yathāśakty alaṃkṛtya kanyā kanyārthine dīyate yat sa kāyaḥ prājāpatyo vivāhaḥ |

_tasya phalam āha |_

		**pāvayet tajjaḥ ṣaḍvaṃśyān saha cātmanā || 1.60 ||**

tasyāṃ jātaḥ ṣaṭpūrvān ṣaḍ aparān puruṣān ātmānaṃ ca trayodaśaṃ pāvayet | atra devalaḥ |

	ete vivāhāś catvāro dharmyās toyapradhānikāḥ |

	aśulkā brāhmaṇārhāś ca tārayanti dvayoḥ kulam ||

	caturṣv eteṣu dattāyām utpannās tanayāḥ striyām |

	dātuḥ pratigrahītuś ca punanty ā saptamaṃ kulam || iti || 1.60 ||

	**āsuro draviṇādānāt**

varād draviṇam ādāyātmārthaṃ kanyārthaṃ ca pitrādibhir yat kanyārpaṇaṃ kriyate sa āsuro vivāhaḥ |

**[90]**		**gāndharvaḥ samayān mithaḥ |**

kanyāvarayor anyonyasamayāt tvaṃ me bhāryā tvaṃ me patir ity evaṃrūpād dānanirapekṣād yaḥ kanyāsvīkāraḥ sa gāndharvo vivāhaḥ |

	**rākṣayo yuddhaharaṇāt**

yuddhena kanyābandhūñ jitvā yat kanyāharaṇaṃ kanyāsvīkāraḥ sa rākṣaso vivāhaḥ |

		**paiśācaḥ kanyakāṃ chalāt || 1.61 ||**

kanyakāṃ chalād apahṛtya yat svīkaroti sa paiśāco vivāhaḥ | kecit paṭhanti "kanyakāchalāt" iti | tasyārthaḥ — kanyāchalanāt tatsvīkāraḥ paiśāco vivāha iti | ete 'ṣṭau vivāhāḥ | vivāhaśabdo yady api kanyāyāḥ saptapadātikrameṇa(maṇe) mukhyas tathāpi ṛtvijyāyāt (?) tattadgṛhyādiśāsravihitabhāryātvasādhake karmasamudāye vartate | sa ca samudāya upādhibhedād brāhmādivyapadeśaṃ labhate | tadupādhitvenaiva dānavivāhaśabdayoḥ sāmānādhikaraṇyam | yathā: "alaṃkṛtya kanyām udakapūrvaṃ dadyād eṣa brāhmo vivāhaḥ" iti | na punar eva vivāhaśabdārthaḥ | tathā sati hi: "udagayana āpūryamāṇe pakṣe kalyāṇe nakṣatre caulakarmopanayanagodānavivāhāḥ" ity uktvā yad uktam, "teṣāṃ purastāc catasra ājyāhutīr juhuyāt" iti, tan nopapadyate | na hi kanyādānāt purastād etā āhutayaḥ santi | tasmād dānavivāhayor bhedāt tadabhidhānayoḥ padayoḥ sāmānādhikaraṇyam upacāreṇaiva vyākhyeyam | yata eva dānaṃ na vivāho 'ta eva gāndharvādiṣu vivāheṣu dānam antareṇaivopayamanaṃ kanyāsvīkārātmakaṃ vivāhatvenāha śaunakaḥ: "mithaḥ samayaṃ kṛtvopayaccheta sa gāndharvaḥ" | mithaḥ parasparaṃ kanyāvarāvahaṃ te bhartā tvaṃ me bhāryeti saṃpratipattiṃ kṛtvā **[91]** kanyām upagaccheta svīkuryād iti tasyārthaḥ | tato 'tra dānaṃ na vidyate vivāhas tu bhavati | asya ca vivāhāntarebhyo bhedako dharmaḥ kanyāvarayor mithaḥ saṃpratipattiḥ | evaṃ rākṣasapaiśācayor api vavāhatvaṃ kanyādānarahitam eva draṣṭavyam | yuddhaṃ chalanaṃ ca tayor bhedakau dharmau | tad āha: "hatvā bhittvā ca śīrṣāṇi rudatīṃ rudadbhyaś ca rākṣasaḥ" | tathā paiśācam api manur āha |

	suptāṃ mattāṃ pramattāṃ vā raho yatropagacchati |

	sa pāpiṣṭho vivāhānāṃ paiśācaḥ kathito 'ṣṭamaḥ ||

evam upayamanapāṇigrahaṇaśabdavat pariṇayanaśabdo 'pi daṇḍinyāyenaiva karmasamudāye śāstreṣu prayujyate | eṣāṃ vivāhānāṃ madhye 'yam asya dharmyo varṇasyāyam adharmya ity āha manuḥ |

	ṣaḍānupūrvyā viprasya kṣatrasya caturo 'varān |

	viṭśūdrayos tu tān eva vidyād dharmyān arākṣasān ||

brāhmādīn gāndharvaparyantān vivāhān ṣaḍbrāhmaṇasya dharmād anapetān vidyāt | avarān paścād uktān āsurādīn paiśācāntāṃś caturo vivāhān kṣatriyasya | vaiśyaśūdrayor api tān eva rākṣasavarjitān vidyāj jānīyād ity arthaḥ | eṣām api madhye praśastān āha |

	caturo brāhmaṇasyādyān praśastān kavayo viduḥ |

	rākṣasaṃ kṣatriyasyaikam āsuraṃ vaiśyaśūdryoḥ ||

brāhmo daiva ārṣaḥ prājāpatyaś ceti catvāro vivāhā brāhmaṇasya praśastāḥ | āsuragāndharvau tu na praśastau, na ninditau | kṣatriyasya punā rākṣasa ekaḥ praśastaḥ | āsuragāndahrvau tu pūrvavat | vaiśyaśūdrayos tv āsura ekaḥ praśastaḥ | gāndharvas tu pūrvavat | paiśācaḥ punaḥ sarvavarṇānāṃ nindita eva,

	sa pāpiṣṭho vivāhānāṃ paiśācaḥ kathito 'ṣṭamaḥ |

ity aviśeṣasmṛteḥ | yat tu manunaivoktam,

	kṣatrasya caturo 'varān |

	viṛśūdrayos tu tān eva vidyād dharmyān rākṣasān || **[92]**

iti, tat paiśācasya brāhmaṇād anyeṣāṃ varṇānām atyantāpady anugrahārtham | tasmād brāhmaṇasyāpady api paiśācānugraho nāstīti siddham || 1.61 ||

	**prāṇir grāhyaḥ savarṇāsu gṛhṇīyāt kṣatriyā śaram |**

**	vaiśyā pratodam ādadyād vedane tv agryajanmanaḥ || 1.62 ||**

savarṇāyām uhyamānāyāṃ vareṇa tasyāḥ pāṇir grāhyaḥ | kṣatriyā brāhmaṇenohyamānā śaraṃ gṛhṇīyāt | ya(ta)thā tasyāḥ pāṇim iva taṃ śaraṃ vara upādadīta | vaiśyā tu vipreṇa kṣatriyeṇa vā pariṇīyamānā pratodaṃ balīvardakhedanam ādadīta | agyajanmaśabda utkṛṣṭavarṇamātraparaḥ | manuḥ |

	vasanasya daśā grāhyā śūdrayotkṛṣṭavedane || 1.62 ||

_kanyāpradānādhikāriṇas tatkramaṃ cāha |_

	**pitā pitāmaho bhrātā sakulyo janajī tathā |**

**	kanyāpradaḥ pūrvanāśe prakṣtisthaḥ paraḥ paraḥ || 1.63 ||**

pitrādīnāṃ kramaparipaṭhitānāṃ pūrvasya pūrvasyābhāve saty aprakṛtisthatve tū(co)ttara uttaraḥ prakṛtisthaḥ kanyāprado bhavati | aviplutabuddhiḥ prakṛtisthaḥ | aprakṣtisthena pitrāpi kṛtaṃ kanyāpradānam akṛtam eva | yad āha nāradaḥ |

	svatantro 'pi hi yat kāryaṃ kuryād aprakṛtiṃ gataḥ |

	tad apy akṛtam eva syād asvātantryasya hetutaḥ ||

svatantro 'pi pitṛtvādinā svātantryārho 'pi yady aprakṛtisthatvena paratantro bhavati tadā tatkṛtaṃ kāryaṃ vāgdattādikarmākṛtaṃ veditavyam | tathā |

	pitā dadyāt svayaṃ kanyāṃ bhrātā vānumate pituḥ |

	mātāmaho mātulaś ca sakulyo bāndhavas tathā ||

	mātra(tā)bhāve tu sarveṣāṃ prakṛtau yadi vartate |

	tasyām aprakṛtisthāyāṃ dadyuḥ kanyāṃ svajātayaḥ ||

viṣṇuḥ: "pitā pitāmaho bhrātā sakulyo mātāmaho mātā ca | iti kanyāpradāḥ pūrvābhāve prakṛtisthaḥ paraḥ paraḥ" iti || 1.63 ||

	**aprayacchan samāpnoti bhrūṇahatyām ṛtāv ṛtau |**

kanyāyāḥ pradātādhikārī tām adadad garbhahatyāṃ pratyuta samāpnoti saṃpūrṇā prāpnoti | yat tu manupravacanam,

	kāmam ā maraṇāt tiṣṭhed gṛhe kanyartumaty api |

	na tv evaināṃ prayacchet tu guṇahīnāya karhicit ||

iti, tad guṇavadvarasaṃbhave guṇahīnāya na na dātavyety evaṃparaṃ na tu kanyartudarśanam adoṣa ity evamartham | tathā hi sati vacanāntarvirodhaḥ | tathā ca kāśyapaḥ |

	pitur gene tu yā kanyā rajaḥ paśyed asaṃskṛtā |

	bhrūṇahatyā pitus tasyāḥ sā kanyā vṛṣalī smṛtā ||

vṛṣalī dharmānadhikāriṇī |

	yas tu tāṃ varayet kanyāṃ brāhmaṇo jñānadurbalaḥ |

	aśrāddheyam apāṅkteyaṃ taṃ vidyād vṛṣalīpatim ||

kanyayā cāham ṛtumatīti bāndhavebhyo nivedayitavyam ity āha nāradaḥ |

	kanyā nartum upekṣeta bāndhavebhyo nivedayet |

	na cet pradadyus tāṃ bhartre te syur brahmahabhiḥ samāḥ || iti |

atra saṃvartaḥ |

	mātā caiva pitā caiva jyeṣṭho bhrātā tathaiva ca |

	trayas te narakaṃ yānti dṛṣṭvā kanyāṃ rajasvalām ||

	**gamyaṃ tv abhāve dātṝṇāṃ kanyā kuryāt svayaṃ varam || 1.64 ||**

dātṝṇāṃ pitrādīnām abhāve svayam eva kanyā gamyaṃ gamanārhaṃ savarṇam utkṛṣṭavarṇaṃ vā pātityādidoṣarahitaṃ varaṃ bhartāraṃ kuryāt | etac ca prāgrajodarśanāt | dṛṣṭe tu tasmin pitrādiṣu satsv api svayam api kanyā varaṃ kuryāt | na pitrādiśāsanam apekṣeta | yad āha baudhāyanaḥ |

	trīṇi varṣāṇy ṛtumatī kāṅkṣeta pitṛśāsanam |

	tataś caturthe varṣe tu vindeta sadṛśaṃ patim ||

	avidyamānaṃ(ne) sadṛśaṃ(śe) guṇahīnam api vrajet ||

sadṛśo guṇavān | yat tu viṣṇunoktam,

	ṛtutrayam apāsyaiva kanyā kuryāt svayaṃ varam |

iti, tad guṇavaralābhe sati draṣṭavyam | tadalābhe tu varṣatrayam upāsanīyam | **[94]** atra manuḥ |

	alaṃkāraṃ nādadīta pitryaṃ kanyā svayaṃvarā |

	mātṛkaṃ bhrātṛdattaṃ vā steyaṃ syād yadi taṃ haret ||

varam api prati sa evāha |

	pitre ca dadyāc chulkaṃ tu kanyām ṛtumatīṃ haran |

	sa hi svāmyād atikrāmed ṛtūnāṃ pratirodhanāt ||

śulkaṃ mūlyam || 1.64 ||

	**sakṛt pradīyate kanyā haraṃs tām coradaṇḍabhāk |**

**	dattām api haret pūrvāc chreyāṃś ced vara āvrajet || 1.65 ||**

pitrādinā kanyā sakṛd eva deyā tāṃ datvāpaharan vakṣyamāṇena kanyāsteyadaṇḍena yujyate | yasmai vācā dattā tato 'nyaś cet praśastastataro labhyate tatas tasmai deyā na tu pūrvasmai | tatra gautamaḥ: "pratiśrutyādharmasaṃyuktāya na dadyāt (?)" iti | nāradaḥ |

	strīpuṃsayoś ca saṃbandhād varaṇaṃ prāg vidhīyate |

	varaṇād grahaṇaṃ pāṇeḥ saṃbandho 'yaṃ trilakṣaṇaḥ ||

varaṇaṃ pāṇigrahaṇam upabhogaś ceti trividhaḥ saṃbandhaḥ |

	tayor aniyataṃ proktaṃ varaṇād doṣadarśanāt |

	pāṇigrahaṇikā mantrā niyataṃ dāralakṣaṇam ||

	teṣāṃ niṣṭhā tu vidvadbhir vijñeyā saptame pade ||

asyārthaḥ — tayoḥ kanyāvarayor aniyatam aniyamaḥ | vṛtāpi na pariṇīyate vāgdattāpi na pradīyata ity evaṃrūpaḥ, tasya kālaṃ kāraṇaṃ ca vaktum uktam — varaṇād doṣadarśanād iti | varaṇād ūrdhvaṃ kanyāvarayor anyonyadoṣadarśanād aniyamo bhavati | varaṇād iti sāvadhāraṇaṃ vacanam | varaṇād evordhvaṃ na vivāhād ity arthaḥ | atra hetuḥ — "pāṇigrahaṇikā mantrāḥ" iti | tair mantrair utpāditabhāryātvarūpasaṃskārāyāḥ parityāgo na yukta iti | tathā |

	pratigṛhya tu yaḥ kanyāṃ varo deśāntaraṃ vrajet |

	trīn ṛtūn samatikramya kanyānyaṃ varayed varam ||

kātyāyanaḥ |

	varayitvā tu yaḥ kaścit praṇaśyet puruṣo yadā |

	raktāgamāṃs trīn atītya kanyānyaṃ varayed varam || **[95]**

vāgdattāviṣayam etad vākyadvayam | raktāgamo rajodarśanam |

	pradāya gacchec chulkaṃ yaḥ kanyāyāḥ strīdhanaṃ tathā |

	dhāryā sā varṣam ekaṃ tu deyānyasmai vidhānataḥ ||

etad api prāg vivāhād draṣṭavyam | vasiṣṭhaḥ |

	adbhir vācā ca dattāyāṃ mriyetādau varo yadi |

	na ca mantropanītā syāt kumārī pitur eva sā || iti |

na ca mantropanītā mantravatā vivāhakarmaṇopanītā prāptā, saṃskṛtā na bhavatīty arthaḥ | kātyāyanaḥ |

	pūrvadattā tu yā kanyā anyenoḍhā yadā bhavet |

	saṃskṛtāpi pradeyā syād yasmai pūrvaṃ pratiśrutā ||

ced guṇavattara iti śeṣaḥ || 1.65 ||

	**anākhyāya dadad doṣaṃ daṇḍya uttamasāhasam |**

kanyāpradaḥ kanyadoṣaṃ svayaṃ jānan vareṇāviditaṃ tasya ca pratyakṣāyogyam akathayitvā tasmai yadi prayacchati tadāsāv aśītipaṇasahasraṃ daṇḍyaḥ | kanyādoṣaṃ nārada āha |

	dīrghakutsitarogārtā vyaṅgā saṃspṛṣṭamaithunā |

	dhṛṣṭānyagatabhāvā ca kanyādoṣāḥ prakīrtitāḥ ||

sumantuḥ: "kanyā kutsitānyajātikarmaśīlā vyādhyupahatā pariṇītā yady akṣatayoniḥ syāt parityaktavyā" | kṣatayonis tu bhartavyā poṣaṇīyaiva | yat tu nāradenoktam,

	yas tu doṣavatīṃ kanyām anākhyāya prayacchati |

	tasya kuryān nṛpo daṇḍaṃ pūrvasāhasacoditam ||

iti, etat tyāganimittadoṣavyatiriktaviṣayam | paṇaśatadvayaṃ saptatyadhikaṃ pūrvasāhasaḥ | atra manuḥ |

	vidhivat parigṛhyāpi tyajet kanyām aninditām |

	vyādhitāṃ vipraduṣṭāṃ ca chadmanā copapāditām ||

vividhaṃ prakarṣeṇa ca duṣṭāṃ vipraduṣṭāṃ | varatyāgahetūn doṣān āha nāradaḥ |

	unmattaḥ patitaḥ klībo durbhagas tyaktabāndhavaḥ |

	kanyādoṣau ca yau pūrvāv eṣa doṣagaṇo vare || **[96]**

dīrghakutsitarogitvaṃ vyaṅgatā ca pūrvadoṣau |

	**aduṣṭāṃ ca tyajan daṇḍyaḥ**

aduṣṭāṃ tyāgadoṣarahitāṃ kanyāṃ tyajann uttamasāhasaṃ varo daṇḍyaḥ | atra nāradaḥ |

	pratigṛhya tu yaḥ kanyām aduṣṭām utsṛjen naraḥ |

	vineyaḥ so 'nyakāmo 'pi kanyāṃ tām eva codvahet ||

vineyo daṇḍyaḥ \

		**dūṣayaṃs tu mṛṣā śatam || 1.66 ||**

aśasteyaṃ kanyeti mithyā vadan paṇaśataṃ daṇḍyaḥ | yat tu viṣṇunoktam: "aduṣṭāṃ duṣṭām iti bruvann uttamasāhasaṃ daṇḍyaḥ" iti tad apariṇeyatvāpādakadoṣābhidhānaviṣayam iti || 1.66 ||

_punarbhūlakṣaṇam āha |_

	**akṣatā ca kṣatā caiva punarbhūḥ saṃskṛtā punaḥ |**

yā kṛtavivāhā satī kṣatayonir akṣatayonir vā kaumāreṇa bhartrā bhartrantareṇa vā yathāvidhi punar uhyate sā punarbhūḥ | yathāha manuḥ |

	sā ced akṣatayoniḥ syād gatapratyāgatāpi vā |

	paunarbhavena bhartrāsau punaḥ saṃskāram arhati ||

asyārthaḥ — klībapatitonmattādipariṇīteṣu jīvatsv aduṣṭe vā bhartari mṛte yam anyaṃ patiṃ vindate sa paunarbhano bhartā | tena punar vaivāhikavidhisaṃskṛtā punarbhūḥ | yad vā klaibyādidoṣarahitaṃ poṣaṇādisamarthaṃ kaumāraṃ patim utsṛjyānyaiḥ saha suratam ācarya punaḥ pūrvam eva patiṃ parigṛhṇāti sā gatapratyāgatā kṣatayoniś ca | sa ca bhartā paunarbhavaḥ | punarbhūdvayasya cāsya svarūpaṃ vasiṣṭha āha: "punarbhūr yā kaumāraṃ bhartāram utsṛjyānyaiḥ saha caritvā punas tasyaiva kuṛumbam āviśati sā punarbhūr bhavati | yā vā klībaṃ patitam unmattaṃ bhartāram utsṛjyānyaṃ patiṃ vindate | mṛte vā sā punarbhūr bhavati" iti | tasmāt punaḥsaṃskṛtatvaṃ punarbhūlakṣaṇam |

	**svairiṇī yā patiṃ hitvā savarṇaṃ kāmataḥ śrayet || 1.67 ||**

yā patiṃ parityajya savarṇam anyaṃ rāgato vivāhaṃ vinaivopabhogāyāśrayet sā **[97]** svairiṇī | svairiṇīgrahaṇaṃ tadvailakṣaṇyena punarbhūjñānāya | tajjñāpanaṃ ca paunarbhavasya bhartuḥ putrasya ca jñāpanārtham || 1.67 ||

_punarbhūprasaṅgāt kṣetrajaputrotpattividhānam āha |_

	**aputrāṃ gurvanujñāto devaraḥ putrakāmyayā |**

**	sapiṇḍo vā sagotro vā ghṛtābhyakta ṛtāv iyāt || 1.68 ||**

**	ā garbhasaṃbhavād gacchet patitas tv anyathā bhavet |**

**	anena vidhinā jātaḥ kṣetrajñaḥ sa bhavet sutaḥ || 1.69 ||**

mṛte jīvati patyau vā garbhādhānākṣame striyam anapatyāṃ putrakāmāṃ tadutpattiyogyāṃ gurubhiḥ prajotpattyartham (?) anujñāto bhartur jyeṣṭhaḥ kaniṣṭho vā bhrātā vā tadalābhe tatsapiṇḍaḥ sagotro vā tām atya(bhya)ktasarvāṅga ṛtukāle gacchet | garbhe jāte nivarteta | uktaprakārātikrameṇa gacchan patito bhavet | itthamutpannaḥ putraḥ kṣetrajasaṃjño bhavati | atra ca bṛhaspatiḥ |

	uktvā niyogo manunā niṣiddhaḥ svayam eva tu |

	yugahrāsād aśakyo 'yaṃ kartuṃ sarvair vidhānataḥ ||

	tapojñānasamāyuktāḥ kṛte tretāyuge narāḥ |

	dvāpare ca kalau nṝṇāṃ śaktihānir vinirmitā ||

	anekadhā kṛtāḥ putrā ṛṣibhir ye purātanaiḥ |

	na śakyās te 'dhunā kartuṃ śaktihīnatayā naraiḥ ||

manuḥ |

	kṣetrajādīn sutān etān ekādaśa yathoditān |

	putrapratinidhīn āhuḥ kriyālopān manīṣiṇaḥ ||

	ya ete 'bhihitāḥ putrāḥ prasaṅgād anyabījajāḥ |

	yasya te bījato jātās tasya te netarasya tu ||

atha brahmapurāṇam |

	mṛte bhartari yā nārī tyaktavaty atha taṃ svayam |

	savarṇāñ janayed garbhaṃ bhartuḥ paunarbhavaṃ sutam ||

	yadi sā bālavidhavā bālāt tyaktātha vā kvacit |

	tadā bhartus tu saṃskāryā gṛhītā yena kenacit ||

	tyaktā bhartṛgṛhaṃ gacched yadi doṣaṃ vinā punaḥ |

	bhratrā sā saṃskṛta(skarta)vyā ca prāyaścittādibhiḥ kramāt ||

**[98]**	strīṇāṃ punar vivāhas tu devarāt putrasaṃtatiḥ |

	svātantryaṃ ca kaliyuge kartavyaṃ na kadācana ||

	yataḥ pātakino loke narāḥ santi kalau yuge || iti || 1.68–69 ||

_vyabhicāriṇīṃ prati yat kāryaṃ tad āha |_

	**hṛtādhikārāṃ malināṃ piṇḍamātropajīvinīm |**

**	paribhūtām adhaḥ śayyāṃ vāsayed vyabhicāriṇīm || 1.70 ||**

dhane ca dharme ca nirastaiśvaryāṃ malinaśarīravastrāṃ dehadhāraṇasamarthānnamātropajīvinīm kṣitiśāyinīṃ ca kṛtvā vyabhicāriṇīṃ gṛhaikadeśe vasayet | atra manuḥ |

	vipraduṣṭāṃ striyaṃ bhartā nirundhyād ekaviśmani |

	yat puṃsaḥ paradāreṣu tac caināṃ cārayed vratam ||

nāradaḥ |

	vyabhicāre striyā mauṇḍyam adhaḥ śayanam eva ca |

kṛtaprāyaścittā tu saṃvyavahāryā bhavati,

	kṛtanirṇejnāṃś caiva na jugupset karhicit | \
iti manuvacanāt || 1.70 ||

_strīpraśaṃsām āha |_

	**somaḥ śaucaṃ dadau strīṇāṃ gandharvaś ca śubhāṃ giram |**

**	pāvakaḥ sarvamedhyatvaṃ medhyā vai yoṣito hy ataḥ || 1.71 ||**

somo devaḥ strīṇāṃ śucitvaṃ dattavān | gandharvaś ca kalyāṇīṃ giram | pāvakaḥ sarvayajñārhatvam | ato hi tā medhyā yajñārhā yoṣitaḥ | hiśabdaḥ prasiddhau || 1.71 ||

	**vyabhicāra ṛtau śuddhir garbhe tyāgo vidhīyate |**

**	garbhabhartṛvadhe cāsāṃ tathā mahati pātake || 1.72 ||**

vyabhicāre saty āsāṃ rajodarśane śuddhir bhavati | etac ca mānase vyabhicāre | yad āha manuḥ: "rajasā strī manoduṣṭā" iti | tataś ca rajodarśanāt prāg asaṃvyavahāryā | saṃvyavahārāya prāyaścittaṃ kārayitavyā | yad āha vasiṣṭhaḥ: "manasā bhartur abhicāre trirātraṃ yavakaṃ kṣīraudanaṃ vā bhuñjānādhaḥ śayīta | ūrdhvaṃ trirātrād apsu nimagnā gāytryā aṣṭaśatena śirobhiir juhuyāt | pūtā bhavatīti vijñāyate" iti | **[99]** garbhe tyāgo vidhīya iti śūdragarbhaviṣayam | yad āha vasiṣṭhaḥ |

	brāhmaṇakṣatriyaviśāṃ striyaḥ śūdreṇa saṃgatāḥ |

	aprajātā viśudhyanti prāyaścittena netarāḥ || iti |

svasyā garbhasya bhartur vā vadhe bhartrā bandhubhiś cāsāṃ tyāgaḥ kāryaḥ | cakāraḥ śāstrāntaroktatyāgahetusaṃgrahārthaḥ | atra manuḥ |

	ṛtusnātātha yā nārī bhartāraṃ nopagacchati |

	tāṃ grāmamadhye vikhyāpya bhrūṇaghnīṃ tu vivāsayet ||

vasiṣṭhaḥ |

	catasras tu parityājyāḥ śiṣyagā gurugā ca yā |

	patighnī ca viśeṣeṇa juṅgitopagatā ca yā ||

śiṣyo 'tra bhartṛśiṣyaḥ | guruḥ pitā | juṅgitaḥ patitaḥ, pratilomajo vā |

	trīṇi striyāḥ pātakāni loke dharmavido viduḥ |

	bhartur vadho bhrūṇahatyā svasya garbhasya pātanam ||

tasyās tyāgakāraṇeṣu mahāpātakeṣu strīpuruṣasādhāraṇeṣu, prātisvikeṣu tu striyās tyāgahetuṣu śiṣyagamanādiṣu sarvātmanā tyāga iti | atha vāyam arthaḥ — vyabhicāre sati yadi rajodarśanātmakam ṛtupravṛttyā garbhāvaniścaye śuddhiḥ śuddhihetuḥ prāyaścittakriyā kāryā | garbhe tu vyabhicāranimitte vyabhicāriṇyās tyaga eva na prāyaścittam | na kevalaṃ tasmin garbhe kiṃ tu svakīyasya yathā kathaṃcid upāttasya garbhasya svabhartuś ca vadhe tyāgo na prāyaścittam | mahāpātake tu tyāgo 'bhihito viśeṣa iti | mahāpātakeṣu strīpuruṣasādhāraṇeṣu satsu saṃbhogasaṃsparśasaṃbhāṣaṇasahādhikāraviṣayas tyāgaḥ kāryaḥ, na punar gṛhān nirvāsanarūpaḥ | yad āha manuḥ |

	etam eva vidhiṃ kuryād yoṣitsu patitāsv api |

	vastrānnam āsāṃ deyaṃ tu vaseyus tu gṛhāntike || iti || 1.72 ||

_adhivedanīyā āha |_

	**surāpī vyādhitā dhūrtā vandhyārthaghny apriyaṃvadā |**

**	strīprasūś cādhivettavyā puruṣadveṣiṇī tathā || 1.73 ||**

[surāpīprabhṛtayo 'dhivedanīyāḥ| evaṃvidhasu bhāryāsu bhāryāntaraṃ kartavyam **[100]** iti yāvat | surāpī madyapī | surāśabdenātra madyaṃ pratipādyate na surā | tatpānaṃ hi mahāpātakatvāt tyāgasyaiva hetuḥ syāt, nādhivedanamātrasya | ata eva manuḥ |

	madyapāsatyavṛttā ca pratikūlā ca yā bhavet |

	vyādhitā cādhivettavyā hiṃsrārthagnī ca sarvadā ||

vyādhitā dīrgharogā | dhūrtā pratārikā | vandhyā 'napatyā | arthaghnī, arthanāśikā | apriyaṃvadā paruṣabhāṣiṇī | strījananī cādhivettavyā | etāsu vidyamānāsv api bhāryāntaraṃ pariṇeyam ity arthaḥ | atra manuḥ |

	vandhyāṣṭame 'dhivettavyā daśame tu mṛtaprajā |

	ekādaśe strījananī sadyas tv apriyavādinī ||

tathā |

	yā rogiṇī syāt tu hitā saṃpannā caiva śīlataḥ |

	sānujñāpyādhivettavyā nāvajñeyā kathaṃcana ||

rogiṇīgrahaṇam aprajasaṃ strīprajāṃ copalakṣayati | ata eva smṛtyantaram |

	vyādhitāṃ strīprajāṃ vāndhyām unmattāṃ vigatārtavām |

	aduṣṭāṃ labhate tyaktuṃ tīrthato na tu dharmataḥ ||

tīrthaḥ yoniḥ | etac cākāmaviṣayam | yat punar āpastambenoktam: "dharmaprajāsaṃpanne dāre nānyān kurvīta | anyatarāpāye kurvīta | prāg agnyādheyād ādhāne hi satī karmabhiḥ saṃbadhyate" iti, tatra prāg agnyādheyād iti na vidhiḥ, kiṃ tv aucityaprāptānuvādaḥ | ata evāha baudhāyanaḥ: "etayaiva yajeta dāravyatikrama ṛtvigvyatikrame ca" iti | etayā pavitreṣṭyā śāstrīyādhivedananimittam antareṇa yad adhivedanaṃ sa dāravyatikramaḥ | tasminn eva nimitte yajeta na caitat prāg agnyādheyād upapadyate, tretāsādhyatvāt | tenāhitāgner adhivedanam astīti siddham | prāg anyādheyād adhivedane dvitīyādikāpy agnihotrādibhiḥ karmabhir adhikāritayā saṃbadhyate | yad āha āpastambaḥ: "ādhāne hi satī karmabhiḥ saṃbadhyate" iti | **[101]** yat tu viṣṇuvacanam,

	agnihotrādiyajñeṣu dvitīyā na sahācaret |

	anyathā niṣphalaṃ tasya sviṣṭaiḥ kratuśatair api ||

iti, tajjyeṣṭhāyām aduṣṭāyāṃ satyāṃ kevaladvitīyāsahādhikāraviṣayam | asavarṇadvitīyāviṣayaṃ vā | yad vāhitāgnipariṇītadvitīyāviṣayaṃ | etadviṣayam etad api |

	prathamā dharmapatnī syād dvitīyā rativardhinī |

	dṛṣṭam eva phalaṃ tatra nādṛṣṭam upapadyate || iti |

yat tu dvitīyabhāryāparigrahe punarādhānavacanam, tat pūrvabhāryāyām adharmasaṃpannāyāṃ mṛtāyāṃ veti veditavyam, na tu dvitīyavivāhamātra it | manuḥ |

	adhivinnā tu yā nārī nirgacched ruṣitā gṛhāt |

	sā sadyaḥ saṃniroddhavyā tyājyā vā kulasaṃnidhau ||

pitrādikulasaṃnidhāv ity arthaḥ || 1.73 ||

	**adhivinnā tu bhartavyā mahad eno 'nyathā bhavet |**

svagṛhe pitṛgṛhe vā vasantīti śeṣaḥ ||

	**yatrānukūlyaṃ dampatyos trivargas tatra vardhate || 1.74 ||**

dharmārthakāmās trivargaḥ | sa dampatyor ānukūlye saṃpratipattau vardhate, atas tadarthaṃ yatitavyam iti tātparyārthaḥ | mokṣo brahmayajñasyaiva gṛhasthasya na sarvasyety abhiprāyeṇoktaṃ trivarga iti || 1.74 ||

	**mṛte jīvati vā patyau yā nānyam upagacchati |**

**	seha kīrtim avāpnoti modate comayā saha || 1.75 ||**

vāśabdaḥ samuccaye | atirohitam anyat | nityasyāpi patyavyabhicārasyānuṣaṅgikaṃ phalam etad ucyate | patir api bhāryāṃ na vyabhicared iti manur āha |

	anyonyasyāvyabhicāro bhaved āmaraṇāntikaḥ |

	eṣa dharmaḥ samāsena jñeyaḥ strīpuṃsayoḥ paraḥ || iti |

ubhayor avyabhicāravidhir nityaḥ, tadatikrame prāyaścittasmaraṇāt || 1.75 ||

**[102]**	**ājñāsaṃpādinīṃ dakṣāṃ vīrasūṃ priyavādinīm |**

**	tyajan dāpyas tṛtīyāṃśam adravyo bharaṇaṃ striyāḥ || 1.76 ||**

ājñākāritvādiguṇopetāṃ bhāryāṃ parityajan dhanasya tṛtīyāṃśaṃ tasyai dāpyaḥ | rājñeti sāmarthād gamyate | bharaṇamātraparyāptadhanas tu bharaṇamātram | striyā iti caturthyarthe ṣaṣṭhī || 1.76 ||

	**strībhir bhartṛvacaḥ kāryam eṣa dharmaḥ paraḥ striyāḥ |**

bhāryābhir bhartṛvacaso 'rthaḥ kāryaḥ | tatkaraṇaṃ dṛṣṭaprayojanāyopayogatāṃ sādhayati, svayaṃ dharmaś ca bhavati | na cānyaiḥ strīdharmais tulyo 'yam | yena tair vikalpeta | kiṃ tu tata utkṛṣṭas tenaitadanurodhenaivānyadharmakaraṇam | ata eva tadvirodhino 'dharmān niṣedhati manuḥ |

	nāsti strīṇāṃ pṛthag yajño na vrataṃ nāpy upoṣitam |

	patiṃ śuśrūṣate yat tu tena svarge mahīyate || iti |

bhartṛśuśrūṣaṇenāviruddhaṃ vratādi patyanujñayā kāryam | yad āha śaṅkhaḥ: "kāmaṃ bhartur anujñayā vratopavāsādīnām ārambhaḥ" iti, etad aproṣitabhartṛkāviṣayam | yataḥ proṣitabhartṛkāṃ viṣṇudharmeṣu striyam adhikṛtya,

	bhartary evaṃ pravasite tyaktavyā patinā śubhā |

	kurvītārādhanaṃ nārī upavāsādinā hareḥ ||

iti śrutādi dṛśyate | śubhāskhalitacaritrā ||

	**ā śuddheḥ saṃpratīkṣyo hi mahāpātakadūṣitaḥ || 1.77 ||**

patiś cen mahāpātakī tadā prayaścittāpavargaṃ yāvat pratikṣyaḥ | mahāpātakayukto na śuśrūṣya ity arthaḥ | etac ca vivāhottarakālaṃ bhartuḥ pātitye sati draṣṭavyam | vivāhāt pūrvaṃ patitenoḍhāpi na bhāryā śāstrīyodvāhābhāvāt || 1.77 ||
