	**lokānantyadivaḥ prāptiḥ putrapautraprapautrakaiḥ |**

**	yasmāt tasmāt striyaḥ sevyāḥ kartavyāś ca surakṣitāḥ || 1.78 ||**

lokāś cānantyaṃ ca dyauś ceti samāhāre dvandaḥ | tataḥ ṣaṣṭhyekavacanam | **[103]** tac ca lokaprāptyānantyaprāptidyuprāptayo yathāsaṃkhyaṃ putrapautraprapautrakair bhavanti | yasmād evaṃ tasmāt putrādihetavaḥ striyaḥ sevyā ṛtukāle kartavyāś ca surakṣitāḥ | vyabhicāraparihārāya rakṣāvidhānāc ca gamayati vyabhicārotpannair naitat phalaṃ janyate iti | tathā ca śrutiḥ |

	apramattā rakṣatha tantum etam ā vaḥ kṣetre pare bījāny avāpsuḥ |

	janayituḥ putro bhavati sāṃparāye moghaṃ vettā kurute tantum etam || iti |

dyuśabdaś cātra sūryaloke vartate | tathā ca manuḥ |

	putreṇa lokāñ jayati pautreṇānantyam aśnute |

	ata putrasya pautreṇa vradhnasyāpnoti viṣṭapam ||

bradhnaḥ sūryaḥ | pitaraṃ prati vivāhitāyāḥ putrotpattes tatpitṛpitāmahagāmi phalam idaṃ śrāddhasyeva putraṃ prati vihitasya pitrāditṛptiḥ || 1.78 ||

_evaṃ putrasya śreyaskaratve 'bhihite tajjananopāyam āha |_

	**ṣoḍaśartur niśāḥ strīṇāṃ tasmin yugmāsu saṃviśet |**

rajodarśanaprabhṛtiṣoḍaśāhorātrātmakaḥ strīṇām ṛtur garbhagrahaṇakālaḥ | taṃ kālaṃ prasiddham anūdya vidadhāti "tasmin yugmāsu saṃviśet" iti | saṃviśet putraṃ janayitum, "lakṣaṇyaṃ janayet sutam" iti vākyaśeṣāt | tathā ca manuḥ |

	yugmāsu putrā jāyante striyo 'yugmāsu rātriṣu |

	tasmād yugmāsu putrārthī saṃviśed ārtave striyam || iti |

	**brahmacāry eva parvaṇy ādyāś catasras tu varjayet || 1.79 ||**

brahmacāry eva maithunavimukha eva parvaṇi pañcadaśīdvaye bhavet | "ṛtukālābhigāmī syāt," "yathākāmī bhaved vāpi" iti prasakte stryupagamane parvaparyudāso 'yam | brahmacāry eva parvaṇīti parvagrahaṇaṃ tithyantarāṇi śāstrāntaraparyudastāni saṃgṛhṇāti | tatra manuḥ |

	amāvasyām aṣṭamīṃ ca paurṇamāsīṃ caturdaśīm |

	brahmacārī bhaven nityam apy ṛtau snātako dvijaḥ ||

atrāmāvāsyāśabdasāhacaryāc caturdaśyaṣṭamīśabdau sitāsitapakṣayoś caturdaśyaṣṭamyāv āhatuḥ, na tv ṛtau | apiśabdād anṛtāv apy etās tithayo varjyāḥ | tathā, ṛtor ādyāś catasro rātrīr varjayet | **[104]** tathā ca manuḥ |

	tāsām ādyāś catasras tu ninditaikādaśī tathā |

	trayodaśī ca śeṣāḥ syuḥ praśastā daśa rātrayaḥ ||

ekādaśītrayodaśyāv ṛtor na pakṣasya | atra śaṅkhalikhitau: "na divā maithunaṃ vrajet klībā alpavīryāś ca divā prasūyante 'lpāyuṣaś ca | tasmād etat parivarjayet" iti | anṛtāv apy etat | yad āha āpastambaḥ: "gṛhamedhino vratam — ahany asaṃveśanam | nāṣṭamīcaturdaśīpañcadaśīṣu striyam upeyāt | na śrāddhe bhuktvā na datvā nopanimantritaḥ śrāddhe na vratī na dīkṣitaś ca | na devāyatanaśmaśānaśūnyālayeṣu na vṛkṣamūleṣ na divā na saṃdhyayor na malināṃ na malino nābhyaktāṃ na rogārtāṃ na rogārto na hīnāṅgī tathaiv ca vayodhikāṃ nopeyād garbhiṇīṃ nārīṃ dīrgham āyur jijīviṣuḥ" | vrataṃ prāyaścittam | garbhiṇyām icchantyāṃ na doṣaḥ | tathā ca vasiṣṭhaḥ: "api ca kāṭhake pravacane vijñāyate | api naḥ śvo vijaniṣyamāṇāḥ patibhiḥ saha śayatām iti strīṇām indradatto varaḥ" iti | baudhāyanaḥ |

	yas tu pāṇigṛhītāyā āsye gacchati maithunam |

	tasyeha niṣkṛtir nāstīty evam āha prajāpatiḥ||

hārītas tu caturthyāṃ garbhādhānam icchati: "caturthe 'hani snātāyāṃ yugmāsu vā garbhādānavad upetabrahmagarbhaṃ sa dadāti" iti | tataś vihitapratiṣiddhatvāc caturthyāṃ stryupagamanaṃ vaikalpikam | vyavasthitavikalpaś cāyam | rajonivṛttau caturthyāṃ vidhiḥ | tadanivṛttau pratiṣedhaḥ | tathā ca manuḥ |

	rajasy uparate sādhvī snānena strī rajasvalā | iti |

sādhvī garbhādhānādivihitakarmayogyety arthaḥ | devalaḥ |

	yaugapadye tu tīrthānāṃ viprādikramaśo vrajet |

	rakṣaṇārtham aputrāṃ vā grahaṇakramaśo 'pi vā ||

yoniśabdalakṣitasyartor (?) anekabhāryāsu yaugapadye varṇakrameṇa vā vivāhakrameṇa vā bhāryāṃ saṃgacched aputrāṃ vāgram ity arthaḥ | **[105]** āpastambaḥ: "mithunībhūya ca tayā saha na rātriṃ śayīta" | vṛddhaśātātapaḥ |

	ṛtau tu garbhaśaṅkitvāt snānaṃ maithuninaḥ smṛtam |

	anṛtau tu striyaṃ gatvā snānaṃ mūtrapurīṣavat ||

	dvāv etāv aśucī syātāṃ dampatī śayanaṃ gatau |

	śayanād utthitā nārī śuciḥ syād aśuciḥ pumān ||

bhartuḥ śaucam āpādayantīti śeṣaḥ | gautamaḥ: "na mithunībhūya śaucaṃ prati vilambeta" || 1.79 ||

	**evaṃ gacchan striyaṃ kṣāmāṃ madhāṃ mūlaṃ ca varjayet |**

**	sutha indau sakṛt putraṃ lakṣaṇyaṃ janayet pumān || 1.80 ||**

āhāralādhavādinā **striyaṃ kṣāmāṃ** kṛtvā maghāmūle vihāya nakṣatrāntare **susthe** candra uktaprakāreṇa **sakṛd** ṛtau gacchan praśastalakṣaṇayuktaṃ **putraṃ janayet** | candrasausthityena ca jyotiḥśāstrayuktaṃ putrajanmapradaṃ tatkālīnaṃ grahasaṃsthānaṃ lakṣyate | 

prasaṅgād rajasvalāvratāni kathyante | tatra paiṭhīnasiḥ: "trirātraṃ malavadvastradhāraṇam | na snāyān nābhyañjyān na nakhān nikṛnten na rajjuṃ sṛjen na dantān dhāven na srajaṃ dhārayen na gandhān seveta na vṛṣyāṇi na kharveṇa pibet" iti | vṛṣyāṇi vīryavardhakāni dravyāṇi | kharvo vāmahastaḥ | vasiṣṭhaḥ: "trirātraṃ rajasvalāśucir bhavati | sā nāñjyān nābhyañjyān nāpsu snāyād adhaḥ śayīta na divā svāpyāt | nāgniṃ spṛśet | na rajjuṃ sṛjen na māṃsam aśnīyān na grahān nirīkṣeta na hasen na kiṃcid ācaren na kharveṇa nāñjalinā pibet | pākṣikam | añjalinā vā pibed iti śruteḥ | lohitāyasena vā" | lohitāyasaṃ tāmram | etac ca vratajātaṃ trirātrāśaucanimittāyāṃ rajaḥpravṛttau draṣṭavyaṃ na rajomātrapravṛttau | tatra yā rātris trirātrāśucitvanimittaṃ bhavati, tām āha atriḥ |

	rajasvalā yadi snātā punar eva rajasvalā |

	aṣṭādaśadinād arvāg aśucitvaṃ na vidyate ||

**[106]**	ekonaviṃśater arvāg ekāhaṃ syāt tato dvyaham |

	triṃśatprabhṛty uttareṣu trirātram aśucir bhavet ||

eṣā ca dinasaṃkhyā snānadinapūrvikā, "snātāyāḥ" iti vacanāt | yat tu,

	caturdaśadinād arvāg aśucitvaṃ na vidyate |

ity smṛtyantaram, tena sahartupravṛttisvabhāvavaśād vyavasthām āśrityāvirodhaḥ kāryaḥ | puṃsā svasya balādhānam api kartavyam | yathāha bṛhaspatiḥ |

	striyāḥ śukre 'dhike strī syāt pumān puṃso 'dhike bhavet |

	tasmāc chukrapravṛddhyarthaṃ vṛṣyaṃ snigdhaṃ ca bhakṣayet ||

	laghvāhārāṃ striyaṃ kuryād evaṃ saṃjanayet sutam || 1.80 ||

_adhunā ṛ('nṛ)tugamananimittam āha |_

	**yathākāmī bhaved vāpi strīṇāṃ varam anusmaran |**

**	svadāranirataś caiva striyo rakṣyā yataḥ smṛtāḥ || 1.81 ||**

strīṇāṃ kāmam icchām anatikramann anṛtāv api gacchet | yataḥ strīṇām indradatto varaḥ | uktam indraṃ striyaś ca prakṛtya taittirīyake: "tā abruvan varaṃ vṛṇāmahā ṛtv iyāt prajāṃ vindāmahai kāmam ā vijanitoḥ saṃbhavāmeti tasmād ṛtv iyāt striyaḥ prajāṃ vindante kāmam ā vijanitoḥ saṃbhavanti vārevṛtaṃ hy āsām" iti | svadāra(rā)vyabhicārī bhavet | striyo vyabhicārād rakṣaṇīyā yataḥ smṛtāḥ | tadrakṣaṇaṃ ca patyur avyabhicāritvena strīṣu yathākāmitvena ca bhavati | vāśabdo 'nṛtugamanaṃ vaikalpikam āha | tataś cāgacchato 'pi strīrakṣaṇasāmarthaṃ yasyāsāv ṛtāv eva gacchet | tasya ca phalātiśayaṃ vasiṣṭha āha: "ṛtau ca gacchan vidhivac ca juhvan na brāhmaṇaś cyavate brahmalokāt" iti | itaras tu yathākāmī bhavet || 1.81 ||

	**bhartṛbhātṛpitṛjñātiśvaśrūśvaśuradevaraiḥ |**

**	bandhubhiś ca striyaḥ pūjyā bhūṣaṇācchadanāśanaiḥ || 1.82 ||**

**[107]**

bhartrādibhir bhūṣaṇavastrānnadānaiḥ striyo mānanīyāḥ | etac cāvaśyakam | asyākaraṇe pratyavāyam āha manuḥ |

	yatra nāryaḥ prapūjyante ramante tatra devatāḥ |

	yatraitās tu na pūjyante sarvās tatrāphalāḥ kriyāḥ ||

	jāmayo yāni gehāni śapanty apratipūjitāḥ |

	tāni kṛtyāhatānīva vinaśyanti samantataḥ || iti |

jāmayo bhaginyaḥ | etac ca snuṣāduhitrādyupalakṣaṇam | yad āha bṛhaspatiḥ |

	bhartrā patnī samabhyarcyā vastrālaṃkārabhūṣaṇaiḥ |

	utsave pitṛmātṛbhyāṃ śvaśrūśvaśurabandhubhiḥ ||

bhūṣaṇādīnāṃ samuccayo bhartṛviṣaya itaraviṣayau tu vikalpasamuccayau yathāsāmarthyam || 1.82 ||

_strīdharmān āha |_

	**saṃyatopaskarā dakṣā hṛṣṭā vyayaparāṅmukhī |**

**	kuryāc chvaśurayoḥ pādavandanaṃ bhartṛtatparā || 1.83 ||**

upaskaro gṛhopakaraṇaṃ darvīpīṭhi(ṭha)rādiḥ | saṃyataḥ saṃkṣipta upaskaro yayā sā saṃyatopaskarā, dakṣā śīghrakāriṇī, hṛṣṭā yathotpannena dravyeṇa saṃtuṣṭā, asadvyayaparāṅmukhī ca bhavet | śvaśrūśvaśurayoś ca pādavandanaṃ kuryāt pratyaham | bhartṛtatparā bhartṛpradhānā | atra viṣṇuḥ: "atha strīdharmāḥ | bhartuḥ samānavracāritvaṃ śvaśrūśvaśuragurudevatātithīnāṃ pūjanaṃ susaṃyatopaskaratāmuktahastatā suguptabhāṇḍatā mūlakriyāsv anabhiratir maṅgalācāratatparatā" | mūlakriyā vaśīkaraṇam | tathā pṛthvīṃ prati lakṣmīvākyam |

	nārīṣu nityaṃ suvibhūṣitāsu pativratāsu priyavādinīṣu |

	amuktahastāsu sutānvitāsu suguptabhāṇḍāsu balipriyāsu ||

	suspaṣṭaveṣāsu jitendriyāsu kalivyapetāsv avilolupāsu |

	dharmavyapekṣāsu dayānvitāsu sthitā sadāhaṃ jagatāṃ vidhātri || **[108]**

śaṅkhaḥ: "nānuktā grān nirgacchet | nānuttarīyā | na tvaritaṃ vrajet | na parapuruṣam abhibhāṣetānyatra vaṇikpravrajitavṛddhavaidyebhyaḥ | na nābhiṃ darśayet | ā gulphād vāsaḥ paridadhyāt | na stanau vivṛtau kuryāt | na hased anapāvṛtam, na bhartāraṃ na tadbandhūn vā vidviṣet | na gaṇikādhūrtāvyabhicāriṇīpravrajitekṣaṇikāmāyāmūlakuhikākārikāduḥśīlādibhiḥ sahaikatra tiṣṭhet | saṃsargeṇa hi cāritraṃ duṣyatīty ādiśanti" iti | vyāsaḥ |

	dvāropaveśanaṃ nityaṃ gavākṣāvekṣaṇaṃ tathā |

	asatpralāpo hāsyaṃ ca dūṣaṇaṃ kulayoṣitām ||

manuḥ |

	pānaṃ durjanasaṃsargaḥ patyā ca viraho 'ṭanam |

	svapno 'nyagehe vāsaś ca nārīsaṃdūṣaṇāni ṣaṭ || 1.83 ||

_kiṃ ca |_

	**krīḍāśarīrasaṃskāraṃ samājotsavadarśanam |**

**	hāsyaṃ paragṛhe yānaṃ tyajet proṣitabhartṛkā || 1.84 ||**

krīḍā dyūtādikriyā, śarīrasaṃskāraḥ snānānulepanādiḥ | samājo janamelakaḥ | utsavaḥ kaumudīprabhṛtiḥ | tayor darśanam | hāsyaṃ paragṛhe yānam etat sarvaṃ pravasite bhartari tyajet | atra śaṅkhalikhitau: "preṅkhātāṇḍavavihāravitradarśanāṅgarāgodyānayānavivṛtāsanotkṛṣṭa-pānabhojanakandukakrīḍanagandhamālyālaṃkāradantadhāvanāñjanādarśaprasādhanānām asvatantrāṇāṃ proṣitabhartṛkāṇāṃ kulastrīṇām anārambhaḥ |

	vidhāya proṣite vṛttiṃ jīven niyamasaṃsthitā |

	proṣite tv avidhāyaiva jīvec chilpair agarhitaiḥ ||"

jīvanārthaṃ vṛttiṃ vidhāya proṣite bhartari sati tadbhāryā tayā vṛttyā svalpāhararūpaṃ niyamam āsthāya jīvet | tām avidhāya proṣite jīvec chilpair agarhitair iti | yair na garhā jāyate tair eva śilpair jīved ity arthaḥ || 1.84 ||

	**rakṣet kanyāṃ pitā vinnāṃ patiḥ putras tu vārdhake |**

**	abhāve jñātayas teṣāṃ svātantryaṃ na kvacit striyāḥ || 1.85 ||**

**[109]**

**kanyāṃ** kumārīṃ **pitā rakṣet**, pālayet | **vinnāṃ** pariṇītāṃ **patiḥ** | **vārddhake tu putraḥ** | **teṣāṃ** pitrādīnām **abhāve jñātayo** bāndhavā rakṣeyuḥ | evam ukte 'pi pāratantrye yaḥ svātantryaniṣedhaḥ so 'satsu jñātiṣu rājapāratantryavidhyarthaḥ | tathā ca smṛtyantaram |

	pakṣadvayāvasāne tu rājā bhartā prabhuḥ striyāḥ |

	sa tasyā bharaṇaṃ kuryān nigṛhṇīyāt pathaś cyutām || iti || 1.85 ||

	**pitṛmātṛsutabhrātṛśvaśrūśvasuramātulaiḥ |**

**	hīnā na syād vinā bhartrā garhaṇīyānyathā bhavet || 1.86 ||**

bhartāraṃ vinā vartamānā pitrādīnām anyatamena rahitā na syāt | yadi syāc chiṣṭagarhaṇīyā bhavet | pūrveṇa vākyena pitrādibhiḥ strīrakṣā kāryety uktam | anena bhartur asaṃnidhau pitrādirahitā strī na bhaved iti vidhīyate || 1.86 ||

_uktānāṃ strīdharmāṇāṃ phalam āha |_

	**patipriyahite yuktā svācārā saṃyatendriyā |**

**	iha kīrtim avāpnoti pretya cānuttamāṃ gatim || 1.87 ||**

priyaṃ ca hitaṃ ca **priyahite** | sā patyuḥ priyahitayor udyuktoktastrīdharmacāriṇī saṃyatendriyā ca sātra loke kīrtimatī bhavati, pretya ca sarvotkṛṣṭāṃ lokagatim avāpnoti | samantarasukhadaṃ karma priyam | pariṇatisukhadaṃ hitam | atra manuḥ |

	dānāt prabhṛti yā tu syād yāvad āyuḥ pativratā |

	sā bhartṛlokam āpnoti yathaivārundhatī tathā ||

bṛhaspatiḥ |

	ārtārte mudite hṛṣṭā proṣite malinā kṛśā |

	mṛte mriyeta yā patyau sā strī jñeyā pativratā ||

mṛte maraṇaṃ tena mahāgnipraveśanenaiva | yathāha aṅgirāḥ |

	sarvāsām eva nārīṇām agniprapatanād ṛte |

	nānyo dharmo hi vijñeyo mṛte bhartari karhicit ||

	yāvan nāgnau dahed dehaṃ mṛte patyau pativratā |

	tāvan na mucyate nārī strīśarīrāt kathaṃcana ||

	sadvṛttabhāvāśritabhartṛkāṇāṃ strīṇāṃ viyogakṣatakātarāṇām |

	tāsāṃ prabhāvastimite gate kaṃ nāgnipraveśād aparo 'sti mārgaḥ || **[110]**

astamite prabhau bhartari, kaṃ gate svargaṃ gate mṛte bhartari | hārītaḥ |

	mṛte bhartari yā nārī dharmaśīlā dṛḍhavratā |

	anugacchati bhartāraṃ śṛṇu tasyās tu yatphalam ||

	tisraḥ koṭyo 'rdhakoṭī ca yāni lomāni mānave |

	tāvanty abdasahasrāṇi svargaloke mahīyate ||

	mantragrāhī yathā sarpaṃ balād uddharate bilāt |

	tadvad bhartāram ādāya mṛtaṃ yāti tapobalāt ||

	mātṛkaṃ paitṛkaṃ caiva yatra kanyā pradīyate |

	kulatrayaṃ punāty eṣā bhartāraṃ yānugacchati ||

vyāsaḥ |

	pūrvaṃ mṛtā hared agnim anvārūḍhā hared agham |

	bhartur dhanam abhāve tu jīvantī satsu bandhuṣu ||

	brahaghne vā kṛtaghne vā mitraghne yac duṣkṛtam |

	bhartuḥ punāti sā nārī tam ādāya mṛtā tu yā ||

ādāyāliṅgyety arthaḥ | ata eva kalpasūtrakāro bhartṛśarīreṇa saha saṃveśanam āha: "uttarataḥ patnīṃ saha saṃveśayanti" iti |

	dayitaṃ yānyadeśasthaṃ vṛttaṃ śrutvā pativratā |

	samārohati dīpte 'gnau tasyāḥ śaktiṃ nibodhata ||

vṛttaṃ mṛtam ity arthaḥ |

	yadi praviṣṭo narake baddhapāśaiḥ sudāruṇaiḥ |

	saṃprāpto yātanāsthānaṃ gṛhīto yamakiṃkaraiḥ ||

	tiṣṭhate vivaśo dīno veṣṭyamānaḥ svakarmabhiḥ |

	vyālagrāhī yathā sarpaṃ bilād gṛhṇāty aśaṅkitam ||

	tadvad bhartāram ādāya divaṃ yāti tapobalāt |

	tatra sā bhartṛparamā stūyamānāpsarogaṇaiḥ ||

	modate patinā sārdhaṃ yāvad indrāś caturdaśa ||

modate patinā sārdham iti vacanāt saha patyā svargopabhogaḥ patnīgāmy eva phalam iti tatkṛtasyāgnipraveśasya phalam akartā bhartā bhuṅkta it virodhaḥ suparihā(ha)raḥ | **[111]** yas tu bhartari sukhasamavāyaḥ, sa bhartṛgatād eva dharmāt | tatpratibandhakaṃ pāpaṃ patnīkṛto dharma uddharati | na ca pratibandhakoddhārakaḥ kāryaparaḥ | yas tu patyuḥ pāpakṣayaḥ patnīkṛtasya dharmasya phalam iti śrūyate tasyāpi na mukhyo 'rthaḥ, kiṃ tu gauṇaḥ, kṣaya iva kṣayaḥ patnīdharmeṇa patipāpasyānantaraṃ phaladānapratibandharūpaḥ | bṛhaspatiḥ |

	śarīrārdhaṃ smṛtā jāyā puṇyāpuṇyaphale samā |

	anvārūḍhā jīvatī(ntī) ca sādhvī bhartur hitāya sā ||

anvārohaṇaṃ ca kāmyatvād anityam | ata eva viṣṇuḥ: "mṛte bhartari brahmacaryaṃ tadanvārohaṇaṃ vā" iti | na cānvārohaṇasmṛtīnāṃ "tasmād(du) ha na purāyuṣaḥ svaḥkāmī preyāt" iti śrutivirodho vācyaḥ, bhinnaviṣayatvāt | sāmānyena śrutiḥ svecchayā maraṇaṃ niṣedhati | smṛtis tu mṛte bhartari vahnipraveśamaraṇaviśeṣaṃ vidhatte | ato bhinnaviṣayatvād avirodhaḥ | "svargakāmo yajeta," "yāvajjīvam agnihotraṃ juhuyāt" ity evamādikayā śrutyā sāmānyaviṣayayā na virodhaḥ| tathā ca brahmapurāṇam |

	mṛte bhartari satstrīṇāṃ na cānyā vidyate gatiḥ |

	nānyad bhartṛviyogārtidāhapraśamanaṃ bhavet ||

	nidhāyorasi saṃśuddhā praviśej jātavedasam |

	ṛgvedavādāt sādhvī strī na bhaved ātmaghātinī ||

	tryahāc chauce tu nirvṛtte śrāddhaṃ prāpnoti śāśvatam ||

"imā nārīr avidhavāḥ" ityādayo vedaśrutayaḥ | tasmād etāḥ smṛtayaḥ pramāṇam | na ca "na hiṃsyāt" ity anenānvarohaṇam śakyaṃ niṣeddhum | anena hi hantuḥ sakāśād anyasya hantavyasya hiṃśa pratiṣidhyate, na tu svavadharūpā | sā tu "tadmād u ha na purāyuṣaḥ" ity anena niṣidhyate | idaṃ ca sāmānyaviṣayatvād viśeṣaviṣayayānvārohaṇasmṛtyā tadvyatiriktasvavadhaniṣedhakatvena saṃkocyata ity uktam | na ca sāmānyaviṣayaśrutiviruddhā smṛtir apramāṇam iti vācyam, sāmānyaviśeṣarūpaviṣayabhedena virodhābhāvāt | viṣayābheda eva hi virodho na tu **[112]** viśeṣaviṣayabhede | tataś ca viśeṣaviṣayayā smṛtyā svamūlabhūtā śrutir viśeṣaviṣayaivānumīyate | sā ca sāmānyaviṣayaśruter balīyasī satī tasyāḥ saṃkocahetur bhavati | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">nanu</span> ca brāhmaṇyā anvārohaṇapratiṣedhaṃ smaranti, yathā tāvat paiṭhīnasiḥ |

	mṛtānugamanaṃ nāsti brāhmanyā brahmaśāsanāt |

	itareṣāṃ tu varṇānāṃ strīdharmo 'yaṃ paraḥ smṛtaḥ ||

	upakāraṃ yathā bhartur jīvantī na tathā mṛtā |

	karoti brāhmaṇī śreyo bhartuḥ śokavatī satī ||

virāṭ |

	anuvarteta jīvantaṃ na tu yāyān mṛtaṃ patim |

	jīva(ve)dbharur hitaṃ kuryān maraṇād ātmaghātinī ||

aṅgirāḥ |

	yā strī brāhmaṇajātīyā mṛtaṃ patim anuvrajet |

	sā svartam ātmaghātena nātmānaṃ na patṃ nayet ||

vyāghrapāt |

	na mriyeta samaṃ bhartrā brāhmaṇo śokamohitā |

	pravrajyāgatim āpnoti maraṇād ātmaghātinī ||

pravrajyā maithunādibhogatyāgaḥ | satyam evaṃ smaranti kiṃ tu | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">satyam</span> evaṃ smaranti kiṃ tu smarāntareṇaiteṣāṃ viṣayo vyavasthāpyate | yathāha uśanāḥ |

	pṛthakcitiṃ samāruhya na viprā gantum arhati |

	anyāsāṃ caiva nārīṇāṃ strīdharmo 'yaṃ paraḥ smṛtaḥ || iti 

tataś ca brāhmaṇyanugamananiṣedhaḥ pṛthakcitisamārohaṇaviṣayaḥ | ata eva rāmāyaṇādau brāhmaṇyādīnāṃ svabhartṛśarīrāliṅanapūrvakaṃ svaśarīradahanam upākhyāyate | ata eva kalpasūtrakāraḥ pretasyottarataḥ patnyāḥ saṃveśanam aviśeṣeṇa nityavad vidadhāti | devarādinā tutthāpanaṃ tasyāḥ putrakāmanāyāṃ vā jīvalokakāmanāyāṃ vā satyām āhuḥ | kiṃ ca na brāhmaṇītvena nimittenānugamananiṣedho bhavati | kiṃ tv asau brāhmaṇyāḥ śokanimittakaḥ | yat tu vairājam āṅgirasaṃ ca vacanaṃ brāhmaṇyā anugamanamātrapratiṣedhakam iva pratibhāti | tadviśeṣaviṣayaiḥ pratiṣedhair upasṃhriyate | tasmād vidhitaḥ pravartamānāyā brāhmaṇyā anugamanād doṣo na vidyate, śokādipravṛttāyās tu bhavaty eveti || 1.87 ||

	**satyām anyāṃ savarṇāyāṃ dharmakāryaṃ na kārayet |**

**[113]**

savarṇāyāṃ satyāṃ vidyamānāyāṃ bhāryāyām anyām asavarṇāṃ dharmakāryaṃ na kārayet | tayā saha dharmaṃ nācared ity arthaḥ | abhāve 'pi (ve tu) savarṇāyā itarayāpi sahācared ity arthasiddham | ata eva śūdrayaiva saha dharmānuṣṭhānaniṣedham āha vasiṣṭhaḥ: "kṛṣṇavarṇā vai rāmā ramaṇāyaiva na dharmāya" iti | kṛṣṇavarṇā śūdrā ||

	**savarṇāsu vidhau dharmye jyeṣṭhayā na vinetarā || 1.88 ||**

savarṇān ekatve tu jyeṣṭhāyāṃ cāduṣṭāyāṃ tayā vinā netarayā saha dharmam ācaret | jyeṣṭhayā tu saha kanīyasyo 'pi dharmaṃ kārayitavyāḥ | tathā ca āpastambaḥ: "dharmaprajāsaṃpanne dāre nānyān kurvītānyatarāpāye tu kurvīta | prāg agnyādheyād ādhāne hi satī karmabhiḥ saṃbadhyate" iti | baudhāyanaḥ: "patnīnāṃ saha saṃnahanam iti sa ha svāha baudhayana ekaikām eva saṃnahyed ekaikāṃ gārhapatyam īkṣeayed ekaikām ājyam avekṣayet" ityādi | kātyāyanaḥ |

	naikayāpi vinā kāryam ādhānaṃ bhāryayā dvijaiḥ |

	akṛtaṃ tad vijānīyāt sarvā na(nā)nvāramanti yat ||

tasmāj jyeṣṭhaiva sahadharmacāriṇī netareti vyākhyānaṃ kalpasūtradharmaśāstraviruddhatvād anādaraṇīyam | yat tu viṣṇuvacanam,

	agnihotrādiyajñeṣu dvitīyāṃ na sahācaret |

	anyathā niṣphalaṃ tasya sviṣṭaiḥ kratuśatair api ||

iti, tad asavarṇadvitīyāviṣayam, satsv agniṣu yā pariṇītā tadviṣayaṃ vā | agniṣu naṣṭeṣu punarādhānaṃ tasyā adhikartṛtvād agnihotrādiṣu sahādhikāraḥ | kātyāyanaḥ |

	agniśiṣṭādiśuśrūṣāṃ bahubhāryaḥ savarṇayā |

	kārayet tadbahutve tu jyeṣṭhā yāgarhitā bhavet ||

	yā vā syād vīrasūr āsām ājñāsaṃpādinī ca yā |

	dakṣā priyaṃvadā śuddhā tām atra viniyojayet ||

	dinakrameṇa vā karma yathājyeṣṭham aśaktitaḥ |

	vibhajya saha vā kuryur yathājñānam aśāṭhyataḥ ||

dakṣaḥ |

	dharmapatnī samākhyātā nirdoṣā yadi sā bhavet |

	doṣe sati na doṣaḥ syād anyā kāryā guṇānvitā || 1.88 ||

**[114]**	**dāhayitvāgnihotreṇa striyaṃ vṛttavatīṃ patiḥ |**

**	āhared vidhivad dārān agnīṃś caivāvilambayan || 1.89 ||**

yayā sahāgnyādhānaṃ tām uktavṛttavatīṃ mṛtāṃ patir vaitānair agnibhir yathāvidhi dāhayitvāsavarṇabhāryaś ced vidhivad **dānān āharet** | **agnīṃś cāvilambayan** | tatra savarṇadārālābhe śūdrāvarjam asavarṇayāpi sahādhānādi kāryam | yad āha viṣṇuḥ |

	mṛtāyām api bhāryāyāṃ vaidikāgniṃ na hi tyajet |

	upādhināpi tat karma yāvajjīvaṃ samāpayet ||

asyārthaḥ: vaidikair mṛtāṃ patnīṃ saṃskṛtya na tān parityajet, punar ādadhīta | savarṇadārālābhaviṣaye upādhināpi asavarṇayāpi bhāryayā yāvajjīvaṃ karma samāpayed iti | na punar ayam artho mṛtāyām api bhāryāyāṃ vaidiko 'gnir na tyājyaḥ, na tena tām dahed iti | yatas tathā sati, "śavāgnayo vā ete bhavanti ye mṛtāyāṃ bhāryāyāṃ bhriyante" iti kāṭhakagṛhyaśrutivirodho duṣparihā(ha)raḥ | tathā "upādhināpi tat karma" ity asya kuśamayyā kāñcanamayyā vā patnyā karmasamāptiḥ kāryeti nārthaḥ, patnyā apratinidheyatvāt | yad āha satyāṣāḍhaḥ: "na svāmitvasya bhāryāyāḥ putrasya deśasya kālasyāgner devatāyāḥ karmaṇaḥ śabdasya ca pratinidhir vidyate" iti | patnyāḥ kratvarthakarmakāri rūpaṃ tad yady api śakyaṃ pratinidhātum, tathāpi kuśādimayyāḥ pratikṛtes tatkāryakārtvābhāvān na tatpratinidhitvam | na hi samīpasthitimātraṃ patnīkāryam | kiṃ tu phalīkaraṇājyāvekṣaṇādi tatkāryam | tadākṣiptā ca samīpasthitiḥ | tena pūrvokta evāsyārtho nyāyyaḥ | yat punaḥ,

	anye kuśamayīṃ patnīṃ kṛtvā tu gṛhamedhinaḥ |

	agnihotram upāsante yāvajjīvam atandritaḥ ||

iti vacanam, tad agnihotrastutyartham eva na svārthavidhāyakam ukdtād dhetoḥ | **[115]**

	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">nanu</span> ca punarāhṛtānāṃ dārāṇāmagnotrādyadhikāro 'nupapanno hotṛhomānvārambhaṇīyajanyasaṃskāravirahāt | na ca saṃskārārtham anvārambhaṇīyādikaṃ svātantryeṇa śaknoti bhāryā kartum, tasyāḥ sahādhikāraniyamāt | nāpi patiḥ saṃskṛtatvāt | saṃskṛtatvaṃ ca tasya saṃskārārambhakāṇām anvārambhaṇīyādīnāṃ kratvaṅgabhūtānām anuṣṭhitatvāt | na hy anvārambhaṇīyādisaṃskāravān anvārambhaṇīyādau śāstreṇa prayujyate | [tasmād apatnīkenaivāgnihotram āhartavyam | tathā ca bahvṛcabrāhmaṇam] "tasmād apatnīko 'gnim āhare" iti | tad ayuktam | sarvāḥ khalu śrutayaḥ sapatnīkasyāgnihotrādi vidadhati | bahvṛcabrāhmaṇaṃ stutiparatvenāpy upapadyate | kiṃ ca rajasvalāyāṃ sūtikāyāṃ ca patnyām etad vacanam "apatnīko 'gnim āharet" iti, na punar avidyamānāyāṃ bhāryāyām | evaṃ ca sati na śrutyantaravirodhaḥ | nāsya vākyasya vidhāyakatvam | tasmāc chrutivirodhābhāvāt "āhared vidhivad dārān" iti smṛtivacanaṃ pramāṇam eva | tataś caitadvacanasāmarthāt pūrvasaṃskārāpabhraṃśakalpanayānvārambhaṇīyādāv asti bhartur adhikāra ity āśrayaṇīyam | ata eva baudhāyanaḥ punardārakriyāviṣayam āha: "ījānasya punar ādadhānasya saṃnayen na saṃnayed iti | saṃnayed ity eka āhuḥ | athaika āhur na saṃnayed iti [śrīrasaṃsparśī ha yajño bhavati | yadaiva punar yajetātha saṃnayet" iti] | asyārthaḥ: ījānasya kṛtasomayāgasya patnyāṃ mṛtāyām apy anyasyāṃ cāhṛtāyām agnīn ādadhānasyāhitavato 'dhvaryuḥ saṃnayen na veti saṃdeham upakramya pūrvapakṣam āha: saṃnayed ity eka āhuḥ | teṣām abhiprāyaḥ: yady api patnyāḥ somayāgajanyaḥ sāṃnāyyādhikārahetuḥ saṃskāro nāsti, tayā saha somayāgākaraṇāt | tathāpi tasyā yajamānaṃ prati guṇabhāvād yajamānasya ca saṃskāravattvāt saṃnayed eveti | 

	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">siddhāntam</span> āha: "athaika āhur na saṃnayed iti śarīrasaṃsparśī ha yajño bhavati" iti | śarīraśabdena ca śarīry ātmā lakṣyate | yajñena khalu sāṃnāyyaprayogānuguṇaḥ **[116]** saṃskāra ātmany ādhīyate | na ca yajamāne patnyāṃ ca vartamānaḥ somayāgasaṃskāraḥ sāṃnāyyayāgopayogī, na cābhinavā patnī tatsaṃskāravatīti naiva saṃneyam | yadaiva punaḥ somena yajetātha saṃnayed iti |

	tataś cottarakarmakartṛtvayogyatālakṣaṇasaṃskārādhāyakatayā somayāgatulyatvād dhotṛhomānvārambhaṇīyayor eṣaiva kalpanā yuktā | tasmāt kṛtāgnyādhānā mṛtā patnī vaitānair agnibhiḥ saṃskāryā | avidyamānadharmānuṣṭhānayogyabhāryaś cet tadyogyabhāryāntaram āhṛtyādhānaṃ kuryād itaras tv ādhānam eveti siddham | yat tu,

	dvitīyāṃ vai tu bhāryāṃ yo dahed vaitānikāgnibhiḥ |

	tiṣṭhantyāṃ prathamāyāṃ tu surāpānasamaṃ hi tat ||

iti devalavacanam, tad akṛtāgnyādheyadvitīyāviṣayam | anyathā "āhitāgnim agnibhir dahanti" iti śrutiviruddham apramāṇaṃ syāt | na ca śrutigata āhitāgniśabdaḥ smṛtuvaśād viśeṣaviṣayo bhavatīti vācyam, upāttoddeśyasamarpakatvena viśeṣaṃ praty anapekṣitatvāt | "grahaṃ saṃmārṣṭi" iti grahaśutivat || 1.89 ||

**iti śrīvidyādharavaṃśaprabhavaśrīśilāhāranarendrajīmūtavāhanānvayaprasūta-śrīmadaparādityadevaviracite **

**yājñavalkīyadharmaśāstranibandhe vivāhaprakaraṇam**

**[varṇajātivivekaprakaraṇam]**

_uktavivāhāsu patisavarṇāsu tadasavarṇāsu cotpannānāṃ tathā svairiṇīṣu pratilomotpannānāṃ saṃvyavahāropayogisaṃjñāparijñānāya prakaraṇam ārabhyate |_

	**savarṇebhyaḥ savarṇāsu jāyante hi sajātayaḥ |**

**	anindyeṣu vivāheṣu putrāḥ saṃtānavardhanāḥ || 1.90 ||**

savarṇābhyāṃ dampatibhyāṃ janitāḥ putrās tābhyāṃ samanajātayo bhavanti | putragrahaṇam apatyamātraparam | anindyeṣu vivāheṣūḍhāyām utpannāḥ putrāḥ saṃtānasya brahmavarcasādiguṇavṛddhihetavo bhavanti | atra manuḥ |

	brāhmādiṣu vivāheṣu caturṣv evānupūrvaśaḥ |

	brahmavarcasvinaḥ putrā jāyante śiṣṭasaṃmatāḥ ||

	rūpasattvaguṇopetā dhanavanto yaśasvinaḥ |

	paryāptabhogā dharmiṣṭhā jīvanti ca śataṃ samāḥ ||

	itareṣu ca śiṣṭeṣu nṛśaṃsānṛtavādinaḥ |

	jāyante durvivāheṣu brahmadharmadviṣaḥ sutāḥ ||

brāhmaṇaviṣayam etat |

	aninditaiḥ strīvivāhair anindyā bhavati prajā |

	ninditair ninditā nṝṇāṃ tasmān nindyān vivarjayet || 1.90 ||

_anulomajān āha |_

	**viprān mūrdhāvasikto hi kṣatriyāyāṃ viśaḥ striyām |**

**	ambaṣṭhaḥ śūdryāṃ niṣādo jātaḥ pāraśavo 'pi vā || 1.91 ||**

brāhmaṇāt kṣatriyādiṣu bhāryāsu mūrdhāvasiktāmbaṣṭhaniṣādasaṃjñakāḥ putrā bhavanti | niṣādasya pāraśava iti ca saṃjñā parā | gautamaḥ: "anulomānantaraikāntaradvyantarāsu jātāḥ savarṇāmbaṣṭḥograviṣādadauṣmantapārāśavāḥ (?) | asavarṇabhāryotpannā anulomajāḥ | brāhmaṇasyānantarā kṣatriyā | tasyāṃ tenotpannaḥ savarṇaḥ | kṣatriyād anantarāyāṃ vaiśyāyām ambaṣṭhaḥ | vaiśyāt tadanantarāyāṃ śūdrāyām ugraḥ | brāhmaṇād ekāntarāyāṃ vaiśyāyāṃ niṣādaḥ | kṣatriyād ekāntarāyāṃ śūdrāyāṃ dauṣmantaḥ | brāhmaṇād dvyantarāyāṃ śūdrāyāṃ pāraśavaḥ" iti | atra saṃjñāvikalpe na virodhaḥ kāryaḥ | viṣṇuḥ: "samānavarṇāsu putrāḥ samānavarṇā eva bhavanti | anulomās tu mātṛsavarṇāḥ" || 1.91 ||

	**vaiśyāśudryos tu rājanyān māhiṣyograu sutau smṛtau |**

**	vaiśyāt tu karaṇaḥ śūdryāṃ vinnāsv eṣa vidhiḥ smṛtaḥ || 1.92 ||**

kṣatriyād vaiśyāyāṃ jāto māhiṣyaḥ, śūdrāyām ugraḥ | vaiśyāc chūdrāyāṃ karaṇaḥ | "savarṇebhyaḥ savarṇāsu" ityādinā ya ukto vidhiḥ sa vinnāsu pariṇītāsu smṛto munibhiḥ | avinnāsv api jātānāṃ kṣetrajādiputrāṇāṃ varṇatvābhyupagamād vinnāsv iti śāstravihitaputrotpattiprakāropalakṣaṇārtham | yata eva teṣāṃ brāhmaṇatvam asti ata eva: "brāhmaṇā ṛtvijaḥ" ity abhidhāya "śabaleyabāhaleyaputrikāputraparakṣetrasamoḍhakānīnānujāvaradvipravarān parihāpya" iti baudhāyanaḥ parakṣetrotpannānāṃ paryudāsam āha | yat tu devalenoktam,

	dvitīyena tu yaḥ pitrā savarṇāyāṃ prajāyate |

	avarīṭa iti khyātaḥ śūdradharmā sa jātitaḥ ||

tathā,

	vratahīnās tv asaṃskāryāḥ savarṇāsv api ye sutāḥ |

	utpāditāḥ savarṇena vratyā it bahiṣkṛtāḥ ||

iti, tac chāsrasvīkṛtakṣetrajakānīnasahoḍhagūḍhotpannapaunarbhavavyatiriktaniyoga-vyabhicārotpannaputraviṣayam | ete ca mūrdhāvasiktādayo na kṣatriyādibhyo bhinnāḥ | kiṃ tu tattadbrāhmaṇādijanitopādhibhedān mūrdhāvasiktādināmabhedabhājo bhavanti | yad āha śaṅkhaḥ: "brāhmaṇena kṣatriyāyām utpannaḥ kṣatriya eva bhavati | kṣatriyeṇa vaiśyāyāṃ vaiśya eva | vaiśyena śūdrāyāṃ śūdra eva" iti || 1.92 ||

_pratilomajānāṃ nāmāny āha |_

	**brāhmaṇyāṃ kṣatriyāt sūto vaiśyād vaidehakas tathā |**

**	śūdrāj jātas tu caṇḍālaḥ sarvadharmabahiṣkṛtaḥ || 1.93 ||**

**	kṣatriyā māgadhaṃ vaiśyāc chūdrāt kṣattāram eva ca |**

**	śūdrād āyogavaṃ vaiśyā janayāmāsa vai sutam || 1.94 ||**

brāhmaṇyāṃ kṣatriyavaiśyaśūdrebhyo yathākramaṃ sūtavaidehacaṇḍālā bhavanti | eṣāṃ madhye caṇḍālaḥ sarvadharmabahiṣkṛtaḥ | sarveṣāṃ varṇānāṃ ye dharmās te sarvadharmāḥ, teṣv anadhikārī, na punaḥ sarveṣu dharmeṣv anadhikārīty arthaḥ | yat āha devalaḥ: "svajātiśodhanaṃ sarvapraṇāmas titikṣā vyavahāraśuddhir aparāvamānaṃ svabhṛtyapoṣaṇaṃ svakarmānuṣṭhānaṃ pradhānakarmavarjanam iti caṇḍāladharmāḥ" | tataś ca varṇadharmaḥ pradhānakarma, svakarma svakīyavṛttiḥ| kṣatriyā vaiśyān māgadhaṃ janayati, śūdrāt kṣattāram | vaiśyā strī śūdrād āyogavam | etābhiḥ saṃjñābhiḥ śāstrāntare saṃvyavahārāḥ | tatra manuḥ |

	sūtānām aśvasārathyam ambaṣṭhānāṃ cikitsanam |

	vaidehakānāṃ strīkāryaṃ māgadhānāṃ vaṇikpathaḥ ||

	matsyaghāto niṣādānām āyogavyasya lakṣaṇam |

tathā,

	brāhmaṇārthe gavārthe vā dehatyāgo 'nupaskṛteḥ |

	strībālābhyavapattau ca bāhyānāṃ siddhikāraṇam ||

upaskāro mūlagrahaṇam | abhyavapattir anugraḥ || 1.93–94 ||

	**māhiṣyeṇa karaṇyāṃ ca rathakāro prajāyate |**

ukto māhiṣyaḥ | vaiśyāc chūdrāyām utpannā karaṇī | tasyāṃ māhiṣyotpanno rathakāro bhavati | vaidikakarmādhikāritvād asya saṃkīrṇayonīnāṃ madhye pṛthagabhidhānam | tathā ca śaṅkhaḥ: "kṣatriyavaiśyānulomānantarotpannano rathakāras tasyejyādānopanayanasaṃskārakriyāḥ [aśvapratiṣṭhārathasūtravāsuvidyādhyayanavṛttitā ca" iti ] ||

	**asatsantas tu vijñeyāḥ pratilomānulomajāḥ || 1.95 ||**

hīnavarṇenotkṛṣṭavarṇāyāṃ janitāḥ pratilomajāḥ | uttamavarṇena hīnavarṇāyāṃ pariṇītāyāṃ utpannā anulomajāḥ | tatra pratilomajā asanto 'sādhavaḥ, varṇabāhyā (?) ity arthaḥ | anulomajās tu santaḥ sādhavaḥ, mātṛsamānavarṇatvāt kṣatriyādidharmādhikāriṇo bhavanti || 1.95 ||

	**jātyutkarṣo yuge jñeyo saptame pañcame 'pi vā |**

yugaṃ jāyāpator yugyam | tatra saptame pañcame 'pi vā pitṛsamānavarṇabhāvo jñeyaḥ | etac cānulomajastrīviṣayam, tasyāṃ bhāryātvasaṃbhavāt, na tu pratilomajāviṣayam, **[120]** tasyā varṇabāhyatvenājāyātvāt | guṇāpekṣo vikalpa udāharaṇam | uttamavarṇena hīnavarṇāyām utpannā sā(yā) strī sottamavarṇād aniṣiddhamārgeṇa striyaṃ janayati | sāpy evaṃ sāpy evam iti saptame strīpuṃsayugale jātam apatyaṃ samānavarṇaṃ pitrā bhavati ||

	**vyatyaye karmaṇāṃ sāmyam**

brāhmaṇakṣatriyādīnāṃ yāni vṛttirūpāṇi karmāṇi teṣāṃ vyatyaye vyatikrame ythā brāhmaṇasya kṣatriyavṛttiṃ vaiśyavṛttiṃ vopajīvato jātāḥ putrapaurādayo yadi tām eva vṛttim upajīvanti tadā saptame pañcame vā jātam apatyam upajīvyamānasaṃbandhivarṇātmakaṃ bhavati ||

		**pūrvacac cottarādharam || 1.96 ||**

pūrvavad varṇasaṃkaravad vṛttisaṃkarasyāpy uttarādharaṃ veditavyam | bhāvapradhāno 'yaṃ nirdeśaḥ | tataś cottaratvam adharatvaṃ vā veditavyam ity arthaḥ | ānulomyena vṛttisaṃkarasyottaratvam | yathāha vasiṣṭhaḥ: "ājīvantaḥ svadharmeṇānantarāṃ pāpīyasīṃ vṛttim ātiṣṭheran" iti | vṛttisaṃkare prātilomyam adharam | yathā—vaiśyasya kṣatravṛttupajīvanaṃ kṣatriyasya brāhmaṇavṛttyupajīvanam | ata eva "vṛttim ātiṣṭheran" ity anuvṛttau vasiṣṭhaḥ: "na tu kadācij jāyasī" iti || 1.96 ||

**iti śrīvidyādharavaṃśaprabhavaśrīśilāhāranarendrajīmūtavāhanānvaya-**

**prabhūtaśrīmadaparādityadevaviracite yājñavalkīyaśāstranibandhe**

**varṇajātivivekaprakaraṇam || 3 ||**

**atha saṭīkayājñavlkyasmṛtau**

**gṛhasthadharmaprakaraṇam (4)**

_sabhāryasya gṛhasthasya dharmeṣv adhikāra iti bhāryāparigrahaṃ saprasaṅgam abhidhāyādhunā gṛhasthadharmān āha ||_

**[121]**

	**karma smārtaṃ vivāhāgnau kurvīta pratyahaṃ gṛhī |**

**	dāyakālāhṛte vāpi śrautaṃ vaitānikāgniṣu || 1.97 ||**

**smārthaṃ** gṛhyoktaṃ **karma** **vaivāhike** vivāhasaṃskṛte **'gnau kurvīta pratyahaṃ** nityam | **gṛhī** gṛhavān | gṛhaśabdo 'yaṃ bhāryām ācaṣṭe, na śālām | "**vivāhāgnau**" iti vadan vivāhakarmaṇāgnau ko 'py atiśayo gṛhyakarmānukūla jāyata iti darśayati | na hy anyathā vivāhāgau karmasaṃpattir bhavati | agneḥ pratikṣaṇaṃ pradhvaṃsitatvā(sitvā)t | vivāhasaṃskārasya sthāyitayā tadviśiṣṭo vivāhāgnir bhavati sthāyī | tataś ca naṣṭo 'sau vaivāhikakarmaṇotpadya iti sūcitaṃ bhavati | tatra vivāhasaṃskārakāraṇāny āha kātyāyanaḥ |

	vivāhāgniṃ sabhārthaś cet sīmām ullaṅghya gacchati |

	homakālātyaye tasya punarādhānam iṣyate ||

	araṇyoḥ kṣayanāśāgnidāheṣv agniṃ samāhitaḥ |

	pālayed upaśānte 'smin punarādhānam iṣyate ||

marīciḥ |

	dūrasthe 'pi yadākasmād dhomalopaḥ prajāyate |

	kartavyaṃ punarādhānaṃ prāyaścittaṃ na vidyate ||

pravasati yajamāne samārūḍhāgniviṣayam etat | baudhāyanaḥ: "amedhyābhādhāne samāropya nirmathitvā pavamāneṣṭiḥ" | vaitānāgnviṣayam etat | "vivāhāgniś ced araṇimāṃs tathā pūrvavan nirmathya tadā pavamāneṣṭir devatābhyaś carūn pūrṇāhutīr vā kuryāt | anaraṇiś cel laukikam agnim ānīya carupravṛttiṃ kuryāt |

	acoditena pākena kṛtenoddharaṇena vā |

	laukiko 'gniḥ sa vijñeyaḥ punar ādhānam arhati ||

dāyavibhāgakālāhṛte cāgnau gṛhyaṃ karma kurvīta" | dāyaḥ pitṛdhanam | āhṛta āhitaḥ | śrautam agnihotrādikarma vaitānikeṣu gārhapatyādiṣv agniṣu kurvīta | etac ca kalpasūtragṛhyaśāstrebhyaḥ prāptam evānūdyate, dharmaśāstrapurāṇavihitānāṃ grahayajñādikarmaṇāṃ vaivāhikaśrautāgnisaṃbandhanivṛttyartham | **[122]** kātyāyanaḥ |

	nikṣipyāgniṃ svadāreṣu parikalpyartvijaṃ tathā |

	pravaset kāryavān vipro vṛthaiva na ciraṃ kvacit ||

	manasā naityakaṃ karma pravasann apy atandritaḥ |

	upaviśya śuciḥ sarvaṃ yathākālam upācaret || iti |

hārītaḥ: "nāgnivelayoḥ pravaset parvasu ca" | agnivelayor agnihotravelayor ity arthaḥ | prāyāyukādim adhikṛtya laugākṣiḥ: "sāyam āhutiṃ hutvā tadaiva prātar āhutiṃ juhuyāt" | maitrāyaṇīyapariśiṣṭam: "ṛṣayo ha sma prāyāyukā āsaṃste 'gnihotreṇātapyaṃs te samastahomān apaśyann atho dvirātrāya trirātrāya ṣaḍrātrāyāṣṭarātrāyārdhamāsāyāgnihotram ājuhuvuḥ | tasmād yāyāvara āmayāvy ārto vārdhamāsāyāgnihotraṃ juhuyāt | pakṣādau parvaṇo 'nte ca sāyaṃ ca prātar eva ca caturdaśa caturgṛhītāni sakṛdunnayanam ekā samit sakṛddhomaḥ sakṛtpāṇimārjanam ity evaṃ prātaḥ" | asyārthaḥ — ṛṣayaḥ prāyāyukāḥ pravāsaśīlā agnihotreṇa svakāle kriyamāṇena hetunātā(ta)pyann āpaddharmam apaikṣanta te samastahomān ekadaiva prayojyān apaśyan | tatra pakṣāntyadvirātre trirātre ṣaḍrātre pakṣe 'rdhamāsakāle ye homās tān sakṛd eva juhuvuḥ | tasmād anyo 'pi pravāsī vyādhyārto vārdhamāsahomaṃ kuryāt | tasya prayogaḥ — pakṣādau yajanīye 'hani sāmyaṃ caturdaśa caturgṛhītāni sakṛd unnayati | upalakṣaṇārthaṃ caitat | yathāgāminaḥ pakṣasyānte yathāpārvaṇam aupavasathyam ahas tataḥ pūrvasāyaṃkālahomo 'ntimena sāyaṃhomena vyāpto bhavati | tathā caturgṛhītasaṃkhyaṃ saṃpādayet | evam aupavasthyasyāhnaḥ prātaḥkālasya yomavyāptisaṃpādikā caturgṛhītasaṃkhyā prātarhomasamaye kāryā | prāyeṇa caturdaśasaṃkhyā tathā bhavatīti tadgrahaṇaṃ kadacit tu trayodaśasaṃkhyā pañcadaśasaṃkhyā vā yathā syād ity upalakṣaṇam |

	prāyāyuktam adhikṛtya śrutiḥ: "yāvatīr vāhutīr hoṣyant syāt tāvanti caturgṛhītāni sakṛd unnayet" || 1.97 ||

**[123]**	**śarīracintāṃ nirvartya kṛtaśaucavidhir dvijaḥ |**

**	prātaḥsaṃdhyām upāsīta dantadhāvanapūrvikām || 1.98 ||**

**śarīracintāṃ** śarīrasya sāmayatvanirāmayatvaviṣayāṃ cintāṃ **nirvartya** kṛtaśaucakriyo dvijātir gṛhī **prātaḥsaṃdhyāṃ dantadhāvanapūrvikām upāsīta** | dantānāṃ dhāvanaṃ śodhanaṃ tatpūrvaṃ yasyāḥ sā dantadhāvanapūrvikā | atra brahmacāriṇo vihitā saṃdhyā gṛhasthaṃ praty api sā prāptā | tasyā dantadhāvanapūrvkatvam anena vidhīyate | śaṅkhaḥ: "brāhme muhūrte tūtthāya mūtraprīṣotsargaṃ kuryāt" | brahmāṇḍapurāṇe |

	pratiśrayād dakṣiṇapaścimena kṣipraṃ gatvā kṣepamātraṃ śarasya |

	kuryāt purīṣaṃ tu śiro 'vaguṇṭhya na tu spṛśej jātu śiraḥ kareṇa ||

aṅgirāḥ |

	kṛtvā yajñopavītaṃ tu pṛṣṭhataḥ kaṇṭhalambitam |

	viṇmūtraṃ tu gṛhī kuryād yad vā karṇe samāhitaḥ ||

	utthāya paścime yāme rātrer ācamya codakam |

	antardhāya tṛṇair bhūmiṃ śraḥ prāvṛtya vāsasā ||

	vācaṃ niyamya yatnena niṣṭhīvocchvāsavarjitaḥ |

	kuryān mūtrapurīṣaṃ tu śucau deśe samāhitaḥ ||

dakṣaḥ |

	uṣaḥkāle tu saṃprāpte śaucaṃ kuryād yathārthavat |

	tataḥ snānaṃ prakurvīta dantadhāvanapūrvakam ||

vṛddhaparāśaraḥ |

	mukhe paryuṣite nityaṃ bhavaty aprayato naraḥ |

	tasmāt sarvaprayatnena bhakṣayed dantadhāvanam ||

kātyāyanaḥ |

	utthāya netre prakṣālya śucir bhūtvā samāhitaḥ |

	parijapya ca mantreṇa bhakṣayed dantadhāvanam ||

	āyur balaṃ yaśo varcaḥ prajāpaśuvasūni ca |

	brahma prajñāṃ ca medhāṃ ca tvaṃ me dehi vanaspate || iti |

mārkaṇḍeyaḥ |

	prakṣālya bhakṣayet pūrvaṃ prakṣālyaiva ca saṃtyajet |

	udaṅmukhaḥ prāṅmukho vā kaṣāyatiktakaṇṭakam ||

	kaniṣṭhāgrasamasthaulyaṃ sukūrvaṃ dvādaśāṅgulam |

	prātar bhuktvā ca yatavāg bhakṣayed dantadhāvanam || **[124]**

gargaḥ |

	daśāṅgulaṃ tu viprāṇāṃ kṣatriyāṇāṃ navāṅgulam |

	aṣṭāṅgulaṃ tu vaiśyānāṃ śūdrāṇāṃ saptasaṃmitam ||

	caturaṅgulamātraṃ tu nārīṇāṃ nātra saṃśayaḥ |

	prāṅmukhasya dhṛtiḥ saukhyaṃ śarīrārogyam eva ca ||

	dakṣiṇena tathā kuṣṭhaṃ paścimena parājayaḥ |

	uttareṇa gavāṃ nāśaḥ strīṇāṃ parijanasya ca ||

viṣṇuḥ: "na pālāśaṃ dantadhāvanam adyān na caiva śreṣmātakāriṣṭavibhītakadhavadhanvanajam | na kovidāraśamīpīlupippaleṅgudaguggulujam | na bandhūkanirguṇṭhīśigrubilvakatindukajam | na pāribhadravālmīkamocakyaśalmalīśaṇajam | na madhuraṃ nāmlaṃ nordhvaśuṣkam | na suśiraṃ na pūtigandhi na picchalam" | mocakyaṃ dakalījam ity arthaḥ | vyāsaḥ |

	pratipaddarśaṣaṣṭhīṣu navamyāṃ dantadhāvanam |

	parṇair anyatra kāṣṭhais tu jihvollekhais tṛṇaiś ca vā ||

	kaṇṭakikṣīravṛkṣotthaṃ dvādaśāṅgulasaṃmitam |

	kaniṣṭhakāgravatsthūlaṃ parvārdhakṛtakūrcakam ||

	dantadhāvanam uddiṣṭaṃ jihvollekhanikā tathā |

	śuddhyarthaṃ prātar utthāya bhakṣayed dantadhāvanam ||

	śrāddhe yajñe ca niyamān nādyāt proṣitabhartṛkā ||

śrāddhakartur niṣedho 'yaṃ na bhoktuḥ |

	alābhe dantakāṣṭhānāṃ niṣiddhāyāṃ tathā tithau |

	apāṃ dvādaśagaṇḍūṣair vidadhyād dantadhāvanam ||

purāṇam |

	pratipaddarśaṣaṣṭhīṣu caturdaśyaṣṭamīṣu ca |

	navamyāṃ bhānuvāre ca dantakāṣṭhaṃ vivarjayet ||

yamaḥ |

	caturdaśyaṣṭamī darśaḥ pūrṇimā saṃkramo raveḥ |

	kṣurastrītailamāṃsāni dantakāṣṭhaṃ vivarjayet ||

uśanā: "na dantakāṣṭhaṃ pāṭayen nāṅgulībhir dantān prakṣālayet" | smṛtyantara |

	pālāśaṃ kākubhaṃ dārbhaṃ naivādyad dantadhāvanam |

	adyāc cen niṣkṛtiṃ tasya vacmi gām avalokayet || **[125]**

kātyāyanaḥ |

	yathāhani tathā prātar nityaṃ snāyād atandritaḥ |

	dantān prakṣālya nadyādau gehe vai tad amantravat ||

amantravad iti mantravistaraniṣedhaparam | yato 'yam evāhāh |

	alaptvād dhomakālasya bahutvāt snānakarmaṇaḥ |

	prātaḥ saṃkṣepataḥ snānaṃ homalopo vigarhitaḥ ||

	atyantamalinaḥ kāyo navachidrasamanvitaḥ |

	sravaty eṣa divā rātrau prātaḥsnānaṃ viśodhanam ||

	prātaḥsnānaṃ praśaṃsanti dṛṣṭādṛṣṭakaraṃ hi tat ||

viṣṇuḥ |

	ya icched vipunān bhogāṃś candrasūryagrahopamān |

	prātaḥsnāyī bhaven nityaṃ dvau māsau māghaphālgunau ||

yamaḥ |

	prātaḥsnāyī ca satataṃ dvau māsau māghaphālgunau |

	devān pitṝn samabhyarcya sarvapāpaiḥ pramucyate || 1.98 ||

	**hutvāgnīn sūryadai(de)vatyāñ japen mantrān samāhitaḥ |**

śrautasmārtāgnihavanaṃ svaśāstrānusāreṇānuṣṭhāya svaśākhādhītān sūryadai(de)vatyān mantrān samāhita ekāgramanā japet | nṛsiṃhapurāṇe |

	pūrvāṃ saṃdhyāṃ sanakṣatrām upakramya yathāvidhi |

	sāvitrīm abhyaset tāvad yāvad ādityadarśanam ||

	tata āvasathaṃ prāpya homaṃ kuryāt sadā budhaḥ |

	saṃdhyākarmāvasāne tu svayaṃ homo vidhīyate ||

	svayaṃhomaphalaṃ yat syāt tad anyena na labhyate |

	ṛtvikputro gurur bhrātā bhāgineyo 'tha viṭpatiḥ ||

	etair eva hutaṃ yat syāt tad dhutaṃ svayam eva tu ||

viṛpatir jāmātā | śraute tv ādhānartvijāṃ madhya eko 'ntevāsi vā juhuyāt | tahāha āśvalāyanaḥ: "svayaṃ parvaṇi vā juhuyāt | ṛtvijām eka itaraṃ kālam antevāsī vā" | manuḥ |

	naiva kanyā na yuvatir nālpavidyo na bāliśaḥ |

	hotā syād agnihotrasya nārto nāsaṃskṛtas tathā ||

yat tu śaunakavacanam, **[126]** "pāṇigrahaṇādi gṛhyaṃ paricaret svayaṃ patny api vā putraḥ kumāry antevāsī vā", tad vaitānaviṣayeṇa mānavena na virudhyate, gṛhyaviṣayatvāt tasya | evam anāmnā(māmnā)tadakṣiṇāni ṛtvijaiva kāryāṇi | anāmnātadakṣiṇāni svayam āpady ṛtvijā | kātyāyanaḥ |

	asamakṣaṃ tu dampatyor hotavyaṃ nartvigādinā |

	bhaved apy asamakṣaṃ tu tayor hutam anarthakam ||

varāhapurāṇe |

	udayān niḥsṛtaṃ sūryaṃ yas tu bhaktyā naro dvijaḥ |

	dadhyakṣatāñjalībhis tu tisṛbhiḥ pūjayec chuciḥ ||

	tasya bhāvaprasannasya hy aśubhaṃ yat samārjitam |

	tatkṣaṇād eva nirdagdhaṃ bhasmī bhavati tasya tat ||

dakṣaḥ |

	devakāryaṃ tataḥ kṛtvā gurumaṇḍaladarśanam |

	devakāryasya sarvasya pūrvāhṇas tu vidhīyate ||

viṣṇupurāṇam |

	svācārāṃś ca tataḥ kuryāt pumān keśaprasādhanam |

	ādarśāñjanamaṅgalyadūrvādyālabhanāni ca ||

brahmāṇḍapurāṇe |

	svam ātmānaṃ ghṛte paśyed yadīcchec cirajīvitam |

kātyāyanaḥ |

	pāpiṣṭhaṃ durbhagaṃ mattaṃ nagnam utkṛttanāsikam |

	prātar utthāya yaḥ paśyet tat kaler upalakṣaṇam ||

	śrotriyaṃ subhagaṃ gāṃ ca hy agnim agnicitaṃ tathā |

	prātar utthāya yaḥ paśyed āpadbhyaḥ sa pramucyate ||

	**vedārthān adhigacchec ca śāstrāṇi vividhāni ca || 1.99 ||**

**vedārthān adhigacched** it sādhyasya nirdeśaḥ | **śāstrāṇi vividhānīti** sādhanasya | śāstrāṇy adhigacched vedārthān adhigantum iti vākyārtho bhavati | evaṃ ca vedārthādhigamopāyabhūtānām eva nigamaniruktavyākaraṇamīmāṃsādīnāṃ śāstrāṇāṃ parigraho na bauddhaśāstrādīnām | ata eva tadadhigamam upapātakatvena vakṣyati | smṛtyartho vedārthaśabdenaiva gṛhītaḥ | vedārthānuṣṭhānatvāt tadadhigamasya vedādidhāraṇam arthasiddham | ata evopapātakavarge "adhītasya ca nāśanam" iti vakṣyati | dakṣaḥ |

	vedasvīkaraṇaṃ pūrvaṃ vicāro 'bhyasanaṃ japaḥ |

	taddānaṃ caiva śiṣyebhyo vedābhyāso hi pañcadhā || **[127]**

ata eva manuḥ |

	buddhivṛddhikāraṇy āśu dhanyāni ca hitāni ca |

	nityaṃ śāstrāṇy avekṣeta nigamāṃś caiva vaidikān ||

	vedasya pāraṃ gatvā tu bhūyo bhūyas tam abhyaset |

	śāstraṃ ca vimalaṃ kuryān na cādhītya tyajet punaḥ ||

niyamāḥ padārthanirṇayahetavo nighaṇṭuprabhṛtayaḥ || 1.99 ||

	**upeyād īśvaraṃ caiva yogakṣemārthasiddhaye |**

yogo 'pekṣitalābhaḥ, kṣemas tadrakṣaṇam | yogakṣemārthasiddhyarham īśvaraṃ tatprayojanasaṃpādanasamartham upeyād upagacchet | gautamaḥ: "yogakṣemārtham īśvaram adhigacchen nānyam anyatra devagurudhārmikebhyaḥ" | manuḥ |

	daivatāny adhigacchet tu dhārmikāṃś ca dvijottamān |

	īśvaraṃ caiva rakṣārthaṃ gurūn eva ca parvasu ||

	**snātvā devān pitrṝṃś caiva tarpayed arcayet tathā || 1.100 ||**

madhayṃdine yathāvidhi snātvā yathāvidhi **devān pitṝṃs tarpayet** | cakārād ṛṣīn manuṣyāṃś ca | tathā devādīn arcayet pūjayet | śaṅkhaḥ |

	nityaṃ naimittikaṃ kāmyaṃ kriyāṅgaṃ malakarṣaṇam |

	kriyāsnānaṃ tathā ṣaṣṭhaṃ ṣoḍhā snānaṃ prakīrtitam ||

	asnātas tu pumān nārho japyāgnihavanādiṣu |

	prātaḥsnānaṃ tadarthaṃ tu nityasnānaṃ prakīrtitam ||

	caṇḍālaśavayūpādi spṛṣṭvāsnātāṃ rajasvalāṃ |

	snānārhas tu yataḥ snāti snānaṃ naimittikaṃ hi tat ||

	puṣpa(pya)snānādikaṃ yat tu daivajñavidhicoditam |

	tad dhi kāmyaṃ samuddiṣṭaṃ nākāmas tat prayojayet ||

	japtukāmaḥ pavitrāṇi arcirṣyan devatāh pitṝn |

	snānaṃ samācared yas tu(ttu) kriyāṅgaṃ tat prakīrtitam ||

	malāpakarṣaṇaṃ nāma snānam abhyaṅgapūrvakam |

	malāpakarṣaṇārthā tu pravṛttis tasya nānyathā ||

**[128]**	saraḥsu devakhāteṣu tīrtheṣu ca nadīṣu ca |

	kriyāsnānaṃ samuddiṣṭaṃ snānaṃ tatra kriyā matā ||

snānam etat | kriyā kāryatayā vihitety arthaḥ |

	tatra kāmyaṃ tu kartavyaṃ yathāvad vidhicoditam |

	nityaṃ naimittikaṃ caiva kriyāṅgaṃ malakarṣaṇam ||

	tīrthābhāve tu kartavyam uṣṇodakaparodakaiḥ |

	snātasya vahnitaptena tathaiva paravāriṇā ||

	śarīraśuddhir vijñeyā na tu snānaphalaṃ labhet |

	adbhir gātrāṇi śudhyanti tīrthsnānād bhavet phalam ||

	saraḥsu devakhāteṣu tīrtheṣu ca nadīṣu ca |

	snānam eva kriyā yasmāt snānaṃ puṇyatamaṃ smṛtam ||

dakṣaḥ |

	caturthe tu tathā bhāge snānārthaṃ mṛdam āharet |

	tilapuṣpakuśādīni snānaṃ vā kṛtrime jale ||

	mṛttikā sapta na grāhyā valmīke bhūṣikāsthale |

	antarjale śmaśāne ca vṛkṣamūle surālaye ||

	parasnānāvaśiṣṭā ca śreyaskāmaiḥ sadā budhaiḥ ||

aṣṭadhā vibhaktasyāhnaś caturthabhāge mṛdāharaṇaṃ kuryād ity arthaḥ | śātātapaḥ |

	śucau deśe tu saṃgrāhyā śarkarāśmādivarjitā |

	raktā gaurī tathā śvetā mṛttikā trividhā smṛtā ||

yogayājñavalkyaḥ |

	śṛṇuṣva vakṣyate snānaṃ sarvapāpapraṇāśanam |

	mṛttikāṃ gomayaṃ darbhān puṣpāṇi surabhīṇi ca ||

	āhared yāvadarthāni snānārthaṃ prayataḥ śuciḥ |

	gatvodakāntaṃ vidhivat sthāpayet tu pṛthak kṣitau ||

	tridhā kṛtvā mṛdaṃ tāṃ tu gomayaṃ tu vicakṣaṇaḥ |

	adhamottamamadhyānām aṅgānāṃ kṣālanaṃ tu taiḥ ||

	bhāgaiḥ pṛthak pṛthak kuryāt kṣālane mṛdasaṃkaraḥ ||

dakṣaḥ |

	malāpakarṣaṇaṃ pārśve mantratas tu jale smṛtam |

	saṃdhyāsnānaṃ tūbhayataḥ snānadeśāḥ prakīrtitāḥ ||

pārśve taṭe | **[129]** śaunakaḥ |

	nadītīre śucau deśa āharen mṛttikāṃ kuśān |

	prayato mṛdam ādāya dūrvāpāmārgagomayān ||

	ekadeśe tataḥ kuryān mṛdā snānaṃ tataḥ param ||

vasiṣṭhaḥ |

	mṛdaikayā śiraḥ kṣālyaṃ dvābhyāṃ nābhes tathopari |

	adhaś ca tisṛbhiḥ kāyaḥ ṣaḍbhiḥ pādau tathaiva ca |

	kṣālayet sarvakāyaṃ tu dvir ācamya yathāvidhi ||

śaunakaḥ: "gāyatryādityā ava hi khyātāto devā it mṛdam abhimantrayet" | gāyatryā ṛṣyādi prasiddham | ādityā ava hi khyāteti trita ṛṣiḥ | ādityā devatā | jagatī chandaḥ | "ādityā ava hi khyātādhi kulād iva spaśaḥ | sutīrtham arvato yathānu no neṣathā sugamanehaso va ūtayaḥ suūtayo va ūtayaḥ" | ato devā iti medhātithiṛṣiḥ | viṣṇur devatā | gāyatrī chandaḥ | "ato devā avantu no yato viṣṇur vi cakrame | pṛthivyāḥ sapta dhāmabhiḥ | tataḥ "yata indra," "svastidā viśaspatiḥ," "vi rakṣo vi mṛdhaḥ," "idaṃ su me janitaḥ" iti mṛdaṃ pratimantraṃ pratidiśaṃ kṣipet pūrvādikrameṇa | tato yata indreti bharga ṛṣiḥ | indro devatā | bṛhatī chandaḥ |

	yata indra bhayāmahe tato no abhayaṃ kṛdhi |

	maghavañ chagdhi tava tan na ūtibhir vi dviṣo vi mṛdho jahi ||

svastidā viśaso bhāradvājaṛṣiḥ | indro devatā | anuṣṭup chandaḥ |

	svastidā viśaspatir vṛtrahā vimṛdho vaśī |

	vṛṣendraḥ pura etu naḥ somapā abhayaṃkaraḥ ||

	vi rakṣo vi mṛdho jahi vi vṛtrasya hanū ruja |

	vi manyum indra vṛtrahann amitrasyābhidāsataḥ ||

idaṃ su me vimada ṛṣiḥ | indro devatā | triṣṭup chandaḥ |

	idaṃ su me jaritarā cikiddhi pratīṣaṃ śāpaṃ nadyo vahanti |

	lopāśaḥ siṃhaṃ pratyañcamatsāḥ kroṣṭā varāhaṃ viratakta kakṣāt ||

vasiṣṭhaḥ |

	tataḥ saṃmārjanaṃ kuryān mṛdā pūrvaṃ tu mantravat |

	aśvakrānte rathakrānte viṣṇukrānte vasuṃdharā ||

	uddhṛtāsi varāheṇa kṛṣṇena śatabāhunā |

**[130]**	mṛttike tvāṃ ca gṛhṇāmi prajayā ca dhanena ca ||

	mṛttike brahmadattāsi kāśapenābhimantritā |

	mṛttike hara me pāpaṃ yan mayā duṣkṛtaṃ kṛtam ||

	mṛttke dehi me puṣṭiṃ tvayi sarvaṃ pratiṣṭhitam ||

aśvakrānta ityādīnāṃ yajvaka ṛṣiḥ | mṛttikā devatā | anuṣṭup dhandaḥ |

	punaś ca gomayenaivam agram agram iti bruvan |

	agram agram carantīnām oṣadhīnāṃ vane vane ||

	tāsām ṛṣabhapatnīnāṃ pavitraṃ kāyaśodhanam |

	tvaṃ me rogāṃś ca śokāṃś ca pāpaṃ ca nuda gomaya ||

agram agram iti viśvāmitra ṛṣiḥ | gomayo devatā | anuṣṭup chandaḥ |

	kāṇḍāt kāṇḍāt iti dvābhyām aṅgam aṅgam upaspṛśet |

dūrvayeti śeṣaḥ |

	kāṇḍāt kāṇḍāt prarohantī paruṣaḥ paruṣaḥ pari |

	evā no dūrve pra tanu sahasreṇa śatena ca ||

	yā śatena pratanoṣi sahasreṇa virohasi |

	tasyās te devīṣṭake vidhema haviṣā vayam || iti |

agnir ṛṣiḥ | dūrvā devatā | anuṣṭup dhandaḥ | tathā |

	apāchamayakilbiṣam apakṛtyam apor apaḥ (?) |

	apāmārga tvam asmākam apa duḥsvapnyaṃ(pniyaṃ)suva ||

iti sindhudvīpadṛṣṭayāpāmārgadevatayānuṣṭubhā mārgeṇāṅgam aṅgam upaspṛśet | śaunakaḥ: "atha hiraṇyaśṛṅgayāpo devaripsvantar ity apa upasthāya sumitrā na ity apaḥ spṛṣṭvā durmitrā iti bahiḥ kṣipet" | hiraṇyaśṛṅgayeti dīrghatapā ṛṣiḥ | indro devatā | triṣṭup chandaḥ | āpo devīr upahvaya iti medhātithir ṛṣiḥ | āpo gāyatrī | apsv antariti śunaḥśepaḥ, sumitrā na iti durmitrā iti ca vāmadevaḥ, āpo devatāḥ | yajuṣī chandaḥ | tataḥ,

	indraśuddhādayaś cāpaḥ praviśya manasā japet |

	tatraiva gāyet sāmāni api vā vyāhṛtīr japet ||

	śivena meti(mā) japitvedam āpa ity apa āplavet || **[131]**

āpo asmān iti śeṣaḥ | "yā sūrya iti samāpayet | 'tarat sa mandī,' 'samudrajyeṣṭhā,' iti sūktābhyāṃ yat kiṃ cedam imaṃ me gaṅga iti pāvanam" | kuśair iti śeṣaḥ | tatra — "eto nv indram" iti ṛcas tiraścīnāṅgirasa indro 'nuṣṭup | śivena mā cakṣuṣety agniḥ | āpo jagatī | idam āpa ity ambarīṣaḥ sindudvīpa āpo 'nuṣṭup | āpo asmān iti vāmadeva āpas tiṣṭup | yāh sūryo raśmibhir vasiṣṭha āpas triṣṭup | [tarat sa mandīr iti gāyatrī | samudrajyeṣṭhā iti catur ṛcaṃ sūktam |vasiṣṭha āpas triṣṭup |] yat kiṃcedam iti vasiṣṭho varuṇas triṣṭup | imaṃ me gaṅga iti sindhukṣit praiyamedho nadyo jagatī | tataḥ,

	snātvācānto vārimadhye triḥ paṭhed aghamarṣaṇam |

"ṛtaṃ ca" iti tṛcā(cenā)ghamarṣaṇam | asyā aghamarṣaṇa ṛṣiḥ | bhāvavṛttam | anuṣṭup | caturviṃśatimatāt |

	snānād anantaraṃ tāvat tarpayet pitṛdevatāḥ |

	uttīrya pīṣayed vastraṃ saṃdhyākarma tataḥ param ||

purāṇāt |

	nityaṃ naimittikaṃ kāmyaṃ trividhaṃ snānam ucyate |

	tarpaṇaṃ tu bhavet tasya aṅgatvena prakīrtitam ||

kārṣṇājiniḥ |

	nābhimātre jale sthitvā cintayed gatamānasaḥ |

tarpayec ceti śeṣaḥ | nṛsiṃhapurāṇam |

	pitrarṣi(tṝṣi)gaṇadevādīn adbhiḥ saṃtarpayet tataḥ |

	devān devagaṇāṃś caiva munīn munigaṇān api ||

	pitṝn pitṛgaṇāṃś caiva nityaṃ saṃtarpayet tataḥ |

	dadyāt sarvagrahebhyaś ca ṛṣibhyaś ca jalaṃ tataḥ ||

	kṛtāpasavyaḥ svadhayā pitṛbhyas tadanantaram ||

purāṇāt |

	tarpaṇaṃ devatānāṃ tu kṛtvā vai prāṅmukhaḥ śuciḥ |

	adhikārī bhavet paścāt pitṝṇāṃ tarpaṇe sadā ||

yogayājñavalkyaḥ |

	ato 'nyathā cet savyena tilān kṛtvā vicakṣaṇaḥ |

	dakṣiṇe pitṛtīrthena jalaṃ siñced yathāvidhi ||

ataḥ sthalasthatarpaṇāt | anyathā jalathatarpaṇa ity arthaḥ | tathā ca smṛtyantaram |

**[132]**	bāhuṃ pūrṇaṃ tilaiḥ kṛtvā jalathas tarpayet pitṝn |

	sthalasthena na kartavyaṃ pitṝṇāṃ tṛptim icchatā ||

	muktahastena dātavyaṃ na mudrāṃ tatra darśayet ||

mudrā pradeśinyaṅguṣṭhāgrasaṃyogaḥ | vyāghraḥ |

	ubhābhyām atha hastābhyām udakaṃ yaḥ prayacchati |

	sa mūḍho narakaṃ yāt kālasūtram avākśirāḥ ||

yamas tu |

	dvau hastau yugmataḥ kṛtvā pūrayed udakāñjalim |

	gośṛṅgamātram uddhṛtya jalamadhye jalaṃ kṣipet ||

atra vyavasthām āha kārṣṇājiniḥ |

	śrāddhe vivāhakāle tu pāṇinaikena dīyate |

	tarpaṇe tūbhayenaiva vidhir eṣa purātanaḥ || iti |

atha vā āśvalāyanīyā dakṣiṇenaikahastena kuryur dakṣiṇaṃ pratīyād anādeśa iti paribhāṣābalāt | gobi(bhi)laḥ |

	śuklais tu tarpayed devān manuṣyāñ śabalais tilaiḥ |

	pitṝṃs tu tarpayet kṛṣṇais tarpayaṃs tu sadā dvijaḥ ||

	aṅgasthair yad tilaiḥ kuryād devatāpitṛtarpaṇam |

	rudhiraṃ tad bhavet toyaṃ pradātā kilbiṣī bhavet ||

	romasaṃsthāṃs tilān kṛtvā yas tu tarpayet pitṝn |

	pitaras tarpitās tena rudhireṇa malena ca ||

tataś cālomakāṅgastatilais tarpaṇaṃ na doṣāya | sthalatarpaṇaviṣayam etat | marīciḥ |

	tilānām apy abhāve tu suvarṇarajatānvitam |

	tadabhāve niṣiñcet tu darbhair mantreṇa vā punaḥ ||

	saptabhyāṃ ravivāre ca gṛhī janmadine tathā |

	bhṛtyaputrakalatrārthī na kuryāt tilatarpaṇam ||

	pakṣayor ubhayor janmasaptamyāṃ niśi saṃdhyayoḥ |

	vidyāputrakalatrārthī tilān pañcasu varjayet ||

	nimbasya bhakṣaṇaṃ tailaṃ tilais tarpaṇam añjanam |

	saptamyāṃ naiva kurvīta tāmrapātre ca bhojanam || **[133]**

ṣaṭtriṃśanmatāt |

	gajāśvarathapṛṣṭhe tu nāvyaṅge ceṣṭakācite |

	na tarpayet pitṝn devān na sthalasthaḥ sthale kvacit ||

hārītaḥ |

	ārdravāsā jale kuryāt tarpaṇācamanaṃ japam |

	śuṣkavāsāḥ sthale kuryāt tarpaṇācamanaṃ japam ||

viṣṇuḥ |

	sthale sthitvā jale yas tu prayacched udakaṃ naraḥ |

	nopatiṣṭhati tadvāri pitṝṇāṃ tan nirarthakam ||

	yathāśuci sthalaṃ vā syād udake devatāḥ pitṝn |

	tarpayet tu yathākāmam apsu sarvaṃ pratiṣṭhitam ||

kārṣṇājiniḥ |

	devatānāṃ pitṝṇāṃ ca jale dadyāj jalāñjalim |

	asaṃskṛtapramītānāṃ sthale dadyāj jalaṃ punaḥ ||

tataś ca sthalasthitenāsaṃskṛtāya jalāñjalir deya ity api jñeyam |

	snānavastraṃ tataḥ pīḍyaṃ punar ācamanaṃ caret |

	ye caivāsmatkule jātā aputrā gorajā mṛtāḥ ||

	te gṛhṇantu mayā dattaṃ vastraniṣpīḍanodakam ||

iti vastraniṣpīḍanamantraḥ | hārītaḥ |

	jalārdravāsāḥ sthalago ya ācāmen narādhamaḥ |

	vastraniścotanaṃ tasya pretās tatra pibanti hi ||

dakṣaḥ |

	snātvācāmed yadā vipraḥ pādau kṛtvā jale sthale |

	ubhayor apy asau śuddhas tataḥ kāryakṣamo bhavet ||

vyāghraḥ |

	jalāśayād vrajet tīvram āpo asmān ṛcaṃ paṭhan |

	tato vastradvayaṃ śuddhaṃ gṛhītvā dvir upaspṛśet ||

jābāliḥ |

	snātvā saṃgṛhya vastraṃ ca jaṅghe śodhye mṛdambhasā |

	snānaṃ kṛtvārdravāsās tu viṇmūtraṃ kurute yati ||

	prāṇāyāmatrayaṃ kṛtvā punaḥ snānena śudhyati ||

gobi(bhi)laḥ |

	snāto na mārjayed aṅgaṃ nāpasavyena pāṇinā |

	na ca nirdh(dhū)nayet keśān ācāmen naiva cotthitaḥ ||

vyāsaḥ |

	na cānulimped asnāto vāso 'py evaṃ na nirdhunet |

	ārdra eva tu vāsāṃsi snātvā seveta mānavaḥ ||

**[134]**	yat snānavastreṇa mukhaṃ vimṛjyate snātvā ca yat khādati dantadhāvanam |

	anyonyapṛṣṭena yadopalipyate (?) tad eti kṛtvā prajahāti lakṣmīḥ ||

satyavrataḥ |

	ūrdhvapuṇḍro mṛdā śubhro lalāṭe yasya dṛśyate |

	caṇḍāle 'pi sa śuddhātmā pūjya eva na saṃśayaḥ ||

vyāsaḥ |

	ādāya parayā bhaktyā gaṅgātīrodbhavāṃ mṛdam |

	yaś carcayati gātrāṇi tasya dharmo mahān bhavet ||

uśanāḥ

	snātvā śiro nāvadhunen nāṅgebhyas toyam uddharet |

	na ca pūrvadhtaṃ vāso na tailaṃ na vasāṃ spṛśet ||

yogayājñavalkyaḥ |

	abhāve dhautavastrasya śāṇakṣaumāvikāni ca |

	kutapaṃ yogapaṭṭaṃ vā dvivāsā yena tad bhavet ||

kutapaḥ kambalaḥ | uttarīyaviṣayam etat | tathā |

	yo 'sau vistaraśaḥ prokto snānasya vidhir uttamaḥ |

	asāmarthyān n kuryāc cet tatrāyaṃ vidhir ucyate ||

	snānam antarjalaṃ caiva mārjanācamane tathā |

	jalābhimantraṇaṃ caiva tīrthasya parikalpanam ||

	aghamarṣaṇasūktena trir āvṛttena nityaśaḥ |

	snānācaraṇam ity etad upadiṣṭaṃ mahātmabhiḥ ||

tathā |

	asāmarthyāc charīrasya kālaśaktyādyapekṣayā |

	mantrasnānād itaḥ sapta kecid icchanti sūrayaḥ ||

	māntraṃ bhaumaṃ tathāgneyaṃ vāyavyaṃ divyam eva ca |

	vāruṇaṃ mānasaṃ caiva sapta snānāny anukramāt ||

	āpohiṣṭhādibhir māntraṃ mṛdālambaś ca pārthivam |

	āgneyaṃ bhasmanā snānaṃ vāyavyaṃ gorajaḥ smṛtam ||

	yat tu sātapavarṣeṇa tad divyaṃ snānam ucyate |

	vāruṇaṃ cāvagāhaṃ tu (has tu) mānasaṃ viṣṇucintanam ||

	śastasnānaṃ samuddiṣṭaṃ mantrasnānāt krameṇa tu |

	kālād deśād asāmarthyāt sarvaṃ tulyaphalaṃ smṛtam ||

**[135]**	mānasaṃ pravaraṃ snānaṃ kecid icchanti sūrayaḥ |

	ātmatīrthapraśaṃsāyāṃ vyāsena paṭhitaṃ yataḥ ||

tathā |

	śaṃ na āpas tu drupadād āpohiṣṭhāghamarṣaṇam |

	etaiś caturbhir ṛṅmantrair mantrasnānam udāhṛtam ||

	aprāyatye samutpanne snānam eva tu kārayet |

	pūrvoddiṣṭais tathā mantrair anyathā mārjanaṃ bhavet ||

jābālaḥ |

	aśiraskaṃ bhavet snānaṃ snānāśaktau tu kāmikam |

	ārdreṇa vāsasā vāpi mārjanaṃ daihikaṃ viduḥ ||

kātyāyanaḥ |

	māsadvayaṃ śrāvaṇādi sarvā nadyo rajasvalāḥ |

	tāsu snānaṃ na kurvīta varjayitvā samudragāḥ ||

	dhanuḥsahasrāṇy aṣṭau ca gatir yāsāṃ na vidyate |

	na tā nadīśabdavahā gartās te parikīrtitāḥ ||

	upākarmaṇi cotsarge pretasnāne tathaiva ca |

	candrasūryagrahe caiva rajodoṣo na vidyate ||

	svardhuny ambhaḥsamāni syuḥ sarvāṇy ambhāṃsi bhūtale |

	kūpasthāny api somārkagrahaṇe nātra saṃśayaḥ ||

svardhunī gaṅgā | devalaḥ |

	rāhudarśanasaṃkrāntivivāhātyayavṛddhiṣu |

	snānadānādikaṃ kuryur niśi kāmyavrateṣu ca ||

	nadyām astamaye snānaṃ varjayet tu sadā budhaḥ |

	nadyāṃ snātvā nadīm anyāṃ na praśaṃset tu dharmavait ||

manuḥ |

	na snānam ācared bhuktvā nāturo na mahāniśi |

	na vāsobhiḥ sahājasraṃ nāvijñāte jalāśaye ||

nārāyaṇaḥ |

	upvītī baddhaśikhaḥ samāgamya yathāgamam |

	pavitrāpāṇir oṃkāraṃ yajñeśaṃ manasā smaret ||

	prātaḥsaṃdhyāvidhānena chanda ārṣa ca daivatam |

	smṛtvā cāyamya ca prāṇān ācāmed dharbhapāṇinā ||

	āpaḥ punantu mantreṇa āpo hi ṣṭheti mārjanam |

**[136]**	prakṣipya cāñjaliṃ samyag ud u tyaṃ citram ity api |

	tac cakṣur deva iti ca haṃsaḥ śuciṣd ity api ||

	evaṃ japed ūrdhvabāhuḥ sūryaṃ paśyan samāhitaḥ |

	gāyatryā tu yathāśakti hy upasthāya divākaram ||

	noccair japyaṃ budhaḥ kuryāt sāvitryā ca viśeṣataḥ || iti 

bṛhaspatiḥ |

	manaḥsaṃharaṇaṃ śaucaṃ maunaṃ mantrārthacintanam |

	avyagratvam anirvedo japasaṃpattihetavaḥ || 1.100 ||

_brahmayajñam āha |_

	**vedātharvapurāṇāni setihāsāni śaktitaḥ |**

**	japayajñārthasiddhyarthaṃ vidyāṃ cādhyātmikīṃ japet || 1.101 ||**

vedān ṛgvedādīn atharvavedapurāṇānītihāsān bhāratādīn **vidyām ādhyātmikīm** adhyātmasaṃbandhinīm | upaniṣadgrantham ity arthaḥ | **śaktito** yathāśakti **japet** | **japayajñārthasiddhyarthaṃ** brahmayajñasiddhyartham | adhyātmavidyāyāḥ pṛthag upādānaṃ prādhānyārtham | vedety ukte 'tharvagrahaṇaṃ vṛttapūraṇārtham | tathāṅgirasām upalakṣaṇārtham | śrutau "yad atharvāṅgiraso medasaḥ kulyāḥ" iti śravaṇāt | manuḥ |

	apāṃ samīpe niyato naityakaṃ vidhim āsthitaḥ |

	sāvitrīm apy adhīyīta gatvāraṇyaṃ samāhitaḥ ||

	ādāv ārabhya vedaṃ tu snātvopary upari kramāt |

	yad adhīte 'nvahaṃ śaktyā sa svādhyāya iti smṛtaḥ ||

śaunakaḥ: "prāg vogag vā grāmān niṣkramyāpa utplutya yajñopavīty aklinnavāsā darbhāṇāṃ mahad upastīrya prākkūlānāṃ teṣu prāṅmukha upaviśyopasthānaṃ kṛtvā dakṣiṇottarau pāṇī saṃdhāya sapavitrapāṇir dyāvāpṛthivyoḥ saṃdhim īkṣamāṇaḥ saṃmīlya yathā vā yuktam ātmānaṃ manyeta tathā yukto 'dhīyīta svadhyāyam | oṃpūrvā vyāhṛtīḥ sāvitrīm anvāha paccho 'rdharcaśaḥ sarvām iti tṛtīyām" | yuktaḥ samāhitaḥ | tathā: "sa yāvan manyeta tāvad adhīty(tyai)tayā paridadhāti namo brahmaṇa iti" | paridhānaśabdān nirabhyāso bhavati | **[137]** bṛhaspatiḥ |

	sa cārvāk tarpaṇāt kāryaḥ paścād vā prātar āhuteḥ |

	vaiśvadevāvasāne vā nanyad eti nimittataḥ ||

saḥ, brahmayajña ity arthaḥ | manuḥ |

	naityake nāsty anadhyayo brahmamantraṃ hi tat smṛtam |

	brahmāhutihutaṃ puṇyam anadhyāyavaṣaṭkṛtam ||

tathā |

	vedopakaraṇe caiva svādhyāye caiva naityake |

	nānurodho 'sty anadhyāye homamantreṣu caiva hi ||

vedopakaraṇaṃ vedāṅgam | āpastambaḥ: "atha yadi vāto vā vāyāt stanayed vā vidyotate vā visphūrjed vaikām ṛcam ekaṃ vā yajur ekaṃ vā sāmābhivyāharet | bhūr bhuvaḥ svaḥ satyaṃ tapaḥ śraaddhāyāṃ juhomīti vaitat te no haivāsyaitad ahaḥ svādhyāyatapāpto bhavati" | atra ca vāto vāyād ityādyanadhyāyopalakṣaṇam | brahmayajñānantaraṃ devāditarpaṇaṃ kāryam | tathā ca bṛhaspatiḥ |

	brahmayajñaprasiddhyarthaṃ vidyāṃ cādhyātmikīṃ japet |

	japtvā vā praṇavaṃ vāpi tatas tarpaṇam ārabhet ||

	vasitvā vasanaṃ śuklaṃ sthale vistīrṇabarhiṣi |

	vidhiyajñas tarpaṇaṃ kuryāṇ na pātre tu kadācana ||

	pātrād vā mūlam ādāya śubhe pātrāntare kṣitau |

	jalapūrṇe 'tha vā garte na sthale tu vibarhiṣi ||

yogayājñavalkyaḥ |

	yady uddhṛtaṃ niṣiñceta tilān saṃmiśrayej jale |

	anyathā vāmahaste tu tatas tarpaṇam ācaret ||

tathā |

	anvārabdhena savyena nāmnā gotreṇa cāpy atha |

	āvāhya pūrvavan mantrair āstīrya ca kuśāñ śubhān ||

	prāgagreṣu surān devān dakṣiṇāgreṣu vai pitṝn |

	savyaṃ jānu tathānvācya pāṇibhyāṃ dakṣiṇāmukhaḥ || **[138]**

pūrvavan mantraiḥ pūrva(rvṃ) yājñavalkyasaṃhitāyāṃ śrāddhaprakaraṇa uktaiḥ "viśve devāsa āgata" "uśantas tvā" ityādyuktaiḥ (dibhiḥ) |

	viśve devāsa āgata śṛṇutā ma imaṃ havam |

	edaṃ barhir niṣīdata ||

	uśantas tvā havāmaha uśantaḥ samidhīmahi |

	uśannuśata ā vaha pitṝn haviṣe attave || iti |

kātyāyanaḥ |

	devāṃs tu devatīrthena tarpayed akṣatodakaiḥ |\

vyāsaḥ |

	ekaikam añjaliṃ devā dvau dvau tu sanakādayaḥ |

	arhanti pitaras trīṃs trīn striyas tv ekaikam añjalim ||

likhitaḥ: "ubhābhyām api hastābhyāṃ saṃvṛtāṅguṣṭhakābhyāṃ prāṅmukho yajñopavītī prāgagraiḥ kuśair devatātarpaṇaṃ devatīrthena kuryāt" | yogayājñavalkyaḥ |

	brahmāṇaṃ tarpayet pūrvaṃ viṣṇuṃ rudraṃ prajāpatim |

	devāṃś chandāṃsi vedāṃś ca ṛṣīṃś caiva tapodhanān ||

	ācāryāś caiva gandharvān ācāryatanayāṃs tathā |

	saṃvatsaraṃ sāvayavaṃ devīś cāpsarasas tathā ||

	tathā devān nagān nāgān sāgarān parvatāṃs tathā |

	sarito 'tha manuṣyāṃś ca yakṣān rakṣāṃsi caiva hi ||

	piśācāṃś ca suparṇāṃś ca bhūtāny atha paśūṃs tathā |

	vanaspatīṃś cauṣadhīś ca bhūtagrāmaṃ caturvidham ||

viṣṇusamuccyāt |

	tataḥ kṛtvā nivītaṃ tu yajñasūtram atandritaḥ |

	prājāpatyena tīrthena manuṣyāṃs tarpayet pṛthak ||

kārṣṇājiniḥ |

	sanakaś ca sanandaś ca tṛtīyaś ca sanātanaḥ |

	kapilaś cāsuriś caiva voḍhaḥ pañcaśikhas tathā ||

	ete brahmasutāḥ sapta manuṣyāḥ parikīrtitāḥ ||

padmapurāṇāt |

	marīcim atryaṅgirasau pulastyaṃ pulahaṃ kratum |

	pracetasaṃ vasiṣṭhaṃ ca bhṛguṃ nāradam eva ca ||

baudhāyanaḥ: "atha dakṣiṇataḥ prācīnāvītī pitṝn svadhā namas tarpayāmi | pitāmahān svadhā namas tarpayāmi | prapitāmahān svadhā namas tarpayāmi | mātṝḥ svadhā namas tarpayāmi" ityādi | **[139]** tathā: "anutīrtham apa upasiñcati ūrjaṃ vahantīr amṛtaṃ ghṛtaṃ madhu payaḥ kīlālaṃ parisrutaṃ svadhā stha tarpayata tṛpyata tṛpyata" ityādi | purāṇāt punar avasānāñjalimantraḥ |

	ye me kule luptapiṇḍāḥ putradāravivarjitāḥ |

	teṣāṃ hi dattam akṣayyam idam astu tilodakam ||

matsyapurāṇe |

	devāsurās tathā yakṣā nāgā gandharvarākṣasāḥ |

	piśācā guhyakāḥ siddhāḥ kūṣmāṇḍās taravaḥ khagāḥ ||

	jalecarā bhūnilayā vāyvādhārāś ca jantavaḥ |

	tṛptim ete prayāntv āśu maddattenāmbunākhilāḥ ||

	narakeṣu ca sarveṣu yātanāsu ca ye sthitāḥ |

	teṣām āpyāyanāyaitad dīyate salilaṃ mayā ||

	ye 'bāndhavā bāndhavā vā ye 'nyajanmani bāndhavāḥ|

	te tṛptim akhilā yāntu yaś cāsmatto 'bhivāñchati ||

yogayājñavalkyaḥ |

	kavyavāḍ analaḥ somo yamaś caivāryamā tathā |

	agniṣvāttāḥ somapāś ca tathā barhiṣado 'pi ca ||

	yadi syāj jīvapitṛka etān vidyāt tadā pitṝn |

	yebhyo vāpi pitā dadyāt tebhyo vāpi pradāpayet ||

	vasūn rudrāṃs tathādityān namaskārasvadhānvitān |

	etāṃś caiva pramītāṃś ca pramītapitṛko dvijaḥ ||

tarpeyed iti śeṣaḥ | kavyāvāham analaṃ tarpayāmīti prayogaḥ | asamarthasya saṃkṣepatarpaṇam āha viṣṇupurāṇam |

	ā brahmastambaparyantaṃ jagat tṛpyatv iti bruvan |

	dadyāt payoñjalīṃs trīṃs tu kurvan saṃkṣepatarpaṇam ||

yogayājñavalkyaḥ |

	niṣpīḍya snānavastraṃ tu prakṣālya prayataḥ śuciḥ |

	devānām arcanaṃ kuryād brahmādīnām amatsaraḥ ||

	viṣṇur brahmā ca rudraś ca viṣṇur devo divākaraḥ |

	tasmāt pūjyatamaṃ nānyam ahaṃ manye janārdanāt || \

**[140]**	dadyāt puruṣasūktena yaḥ puṣpāṇy apa eva vā |

	arcitaṃ syāj jagad idaṃ tena sarvaṃ carācaram ||

pūjāyām asamarthasyaitat | brahmayajñānantaraṃ nṛsiṃhapurāṇe |

	tato 'rghyaṃ mānave dadyāt tilapuṣpajalānvitam |

	utkṣipya mūrdhaparyantaṃ haṃsaḥ śuciṣad ity api ||

	jale devaṃ namaskṛtya tato gṛhagataḥ punaḥ |

	vidheḥ puruṣasūktasya tatra viṣṇuṃ samarcayet ||

haṃsaḥ śuciṣad iti vāmadeva ṛṣiḥ | jagatī chandaḥ | sūryo devatā | tathā |

	apsv agnau hṛdaye sūrye sthaṇḍile pratimāsu ca |

	ṣaṭsv eteṣu hareḥ samyagarcanaṃ munibhiḥ smṛtam ||

	agnau kriyāvatāṃ devo divi devo manīṣiṇām |

	pratimāsv alpabuddhīnāṃ yogināṃ hṛdaye hariḥ ||

	āpa āyatanaṃ tasya tasmāt tāsu sadā hariḥ |

	tasya sarvagatatvāc ca sthaṇḍile bhāvitātmanaḥ ||

	a(ā)nuṣṭubhasya sūktasya triṣṭubha(ba)ntasya devatā |

	puruṣō yo jagadbījam ṛṣir nārāyaṇaḥ smṛtaḥ ||

	prathamāṃ vinyased vāme dvitīyāṃ dakṣiṇe kare |

	tṛtīyāṃ vāmapāde tu caturthīṃ dakṣiṇe nyaset ||

	pañcamīṃ vāmajānau tu ṣaṣṭhīṃ vai dakṣiṇe nyaset |

	saptamīṃ vāmakukṣau tu aṣṭamīṃ dakṣiṇe nyaset ||

	navamīṃ nābhimadhye tu daśamīṃ hṛdaye tathā |

	ekādaśīṃ kaṇṭhadeśe vāmabāhau tu dvādaśīm ||

	trayodaśīṃ dakṣiṇe tu āsyadeśe caturdaśīm |

	akṣṇoḥ pañcadaśīṃ caiva ṣoḍaśīṃ mūrdhni vinyaset ||

	evaṃ nyāsavidhiṃ kṛtvā paścād dhyānaṃ samācaret |

	ādyayāvāhayed devam ṛcā tu puruṣōttamam ||

	dvitīyayāsanaṃ dadyāt pādyaṃ caiva tṛtīyayā |

**[141]**	arghyaṃ caturthyā dātavyaṃ pañcamyācamanīyakam ||

	ṣaṣṭhyā snānaṃ pradātavyaṃ saptamyā vastram eva ca |

	yajñopavītam aṣṭamyā navamyā tv anulepanam ||

	puṣpaṃ daśamyā dātavyam ekādaśyā tu dhūpakam |

	dvādaśyā dīpakaṃ dadyāt trayodaśyā nivedanam ||

	caturdaśyā namaskāraṃ pañcadaśyā pradakṣiṇam |

	arcayitvā tu deveśaṃ ṣoḍaśyā ca visarjanam ||

	snāne vastre ca naivedye dadyād ācamanīyakam |

	ṣaṇmāsāt siddhim āpnoti evam eva samarcayan ||

	dhyeyaḥ sadā savitṛmaṇḍalamadhyavartī

		nārāyaṇaḥ sarasijāsanasaṃniviṣṭaḥ |

	keyūravān kanakakuṇḍalavān kirīṭī

		hārī hiraṇmayavapur dhṛtaśaṅkhacakraḥ || iti |

yogayājñavalkyaḥ |

	evaṃ saṃpūjya deveśaṃ kṣaṇaṃ dhyātvā nirañjanam |

	tato 'valokayed arkaṃ haṃsaḥ śuciṣad ity ṛcā ||

	sa yāti brahmaṇaḥ sadma snātvekṣitvā na yāty adhaḥ ||

narasiṃhapurāṇe |

	aṣṭākṣareṇa deveśaṃ narasiṃhaṃ tathā svayam |

	gandhapuṣpādibhir nityam arcayed acyutaṃ naraḥ ||

	sarvārthadāyī mantro 'yaṃ sarvapāpaharaḥ paraḥ |

	sarvaduḥkhaharaḥ śrīmān sarvaśāntikaraḥ smṛtaḥ ||

	aṣṭākṣarasya mantrasya ṛṣir nārāyaṇaḥ smṛtaḥ |

	chandaś ca devī gāyatrī paramātmā ca devatā ||

	gandhapuṣpādisakalam anenaiva nivedayet |

	pratimābhyarcito viṣṇuḥ prīto bhavati tatkṣaṇāt ||

	kiṃ tasya bahubhir mantraiḥ kiṃ tasya bahubhir makhaiḥ |

	oṃ namo nārāyaṇāyeti mantraḥ sarvārthasādhakaḥ ||

purāṇāt |

	śivaṃ bhāskaram agniṃ ca keśavaṃ kauśikīm api |

	tāyinaṃ cārcayen naiti devalokād adho gatim || **[142]**

kauśikī durgā | tāyī buddhaḥ || 1.101 ||

_brahmayajñam uktvā mahāyajñān āha |_

	**balikarmasvadhāhomasvādhyāyātithisatkriyāḥ |**

**	bhūtapitramarabrahmamanuṣyāṇāṃ mahāmakhāḥ || 1.102 ||**

balikarma bhūtayajñaḥ | svadhā pitṛyajñaḥ | pitṛbhyo 'nnādidānaṃ svadhāśabdenopalakṣyate | laukike 'gnāv u(au)pāsane vā sāyaṃ prātar atra homo devayajñaḥ | svādhyāyo 'dhyayanaviśeṣo brahmayajñaḥ | atithipūjanaṃ manuṣyayajñaḥ | eṣām eva saṃjñānvayam āha manuḥ |

	ahutaṃ ca hutaṃ caiva tathā prahutam eva ca |

	brāhmaṃ hutaṃ prāśitaṃ ca pañca yajñāḥ prakīrtitāḥ ||

	japo 'huto huto homaḥ prahuto bhautiko baliḥ |

	brāhmaṃ hutaṃ dvijāgryārcā prāśitaṃ pitṛtarpaṇam || 1.102 ||

	**devebhyaś ca hutād annac cheṣād bhūtabaliṃ haret |**

devebhyo 'nneṣṭau havyaṃ hutaśeṣād annād bhūtebhyo baliṃ haret | annam atra pakvam | tathā |

	śālāgnau vipaced annaṃ laukike vāpi nityaśaḥ |

	yasminn eva paced annaṃ tasmin homo vidhīyate ||

	laukike vaidike vāpi hutotsṛṣṭe jale kṣitau |

	vaiśvadevaḥ prakartavyaḥ pañcasūnāpanuttaye ||

āśvalāyanaḥ: "atha sāyaṃ prātaḥ siddhasya haviṣyasya juhuyāt" | kātyāyanaḥ |

	haviṣyeṣu yavā mukhyās tadanu vrīhayaḥ smṛtāḥ |

	māṣakodravagaurādīn sarvālābhe 'pi varjayet ||

āpastambaḥ: "na kṣāralavaṇahomo vidyate | parānnasaṃsṛṣṭasya haviṣyasya homaḥ | udīcīnaṃ bhasmāpohya tasmiñ juhuyāt | taddhutam ahutam agnau bhavati" iti | tasyārthaḥ — kṣāralavanaparānnasaṃsṛṣṭahaviṣyeṇa homo 'gnau na kāryaḥ | "āryā annasaṃskartāraḥ syuḥ | hāsaṃ śvāsaṃ kṣavathum abhimukho 'nnaṃ varjayet | **[143]** keśān aṅgaṃ vāsaś cālabhyāpa upaspṛśet | āryādhiṣṭhitā vā śūdrāḥ saṃskartāraḥ syuḥ" | tathā: "parokṣam annaṃ saṃskṛtam agnāv adhiśrityādbhiḥ prokṣet tad eva pavitram ity ācakṣate" | dakṣaḥ |

	pañcame ca tathā bhāge saṃvibhāgo yathārhataḥ |

	pitṛdevamanuṣyāṇāṃ kīṭānāṃ copadiśyate ||

vyāsaḥ |

	vaiśvadevaṃ prakurvīta svaśākhāvihitaṃ tataḥ |

	saṃskṛtānnair haviṣyaiś ca haviṣyavyañjanānvitaiḥ ||

	tair evānnair baliṃ dadyāc cheṣam āplāvya vāriṇā |

	kṛtāpasavyaḥ svadhayā sarvaṃ dakṣiṇato haret ||

āpastambaḥ: "balīnāṃ tasya deśasaṃskāro hastena parimṛjyāvokṣya nyupya paścāt pariṣecanam" || 

	**annaṃ bhūmau śvacaṇḍālavāyasānāṃ vinikṣipet || 1.103 ||**

śvādīnām annaṃ bhūmau nikṣipet | caṇḍālaśabdaḥ patitādiparigrahārthaḥ | tathā ca manuḥ |

	śunāṃ ca patitānāṃ ca śvapacāṃ pāparogiṇām |

	vāyasānāṃ krimīṇāṃ ca śanakair nikṣiped bhuvi ||

atra patitagrahaṇaṃ kapālapāṇyādiparigrahārtham | tathā ca bramāṇḍapurāṇam |

	pūrvaṃ devair jitā daityāḥ saṃgrāmāc ca parājitāḥ |

	kapālapāṇayo jagmuḥ kecin nagnavratās tataḥ ||

	kecin muṇḍās tv añjitākṣāḥ kaṣāyavasanās tataḥ |

	sāntva(tva)tāś ca durācārāḥ śaucārārabahiṣkṛtāḥ ||

	narāsthikeśasaṃchannāḥ kecid vyājena dānavāḥ |

	anāśramī vratasthaś ca jaṭī muṇḍī vṛthā ca yaḥ ||

	prāyaścittādikaṃ yaś ca mūlyena kathayen naraḥ |

	nirghṛṇo bhinnamaryādo nāstiko vedanindakaḥ ||

	rogiṇāṃ vratināṃ yaś ca satriṇāṃ vātha nindakaḥ |

	ṛṣīṇām atha devānāṃ nindaty ātmānam eva yaḥ ||

**[144]**	prakhyāpayati yo vipro nābhimānaś ca vedayet |

	kitavo madyapaś caiva kratūnāṃ krayavikrayī ||

	vaṇig vārdhuṣiko grāmapreṣakaḥ piśunas tathā |

	agāradāhī garadaḥ kuṇḍāśī somavikrayī ||

	sāmudrakṛc chidrakṛc ca tailikaḥ kūṭakārakaḥ |

	guroś cālīkanirbandhī guror vañcayitā khalaḥ ||

	mattaś cojjhitavedaś ghātako gurutalpagaḥ |

	saṃkarastrīrato bandhur nārīṇāṃ lampaṭas tathā ||

	nikṣepahārī māyāvī tathā kāyacikitsakaḥ |

	krīṇan yo nindate(ti) dravyaṃ vikrīṇaṃś ca praśaṃsati ||

	strībālabrāhmaṇānāṃ ca hantā goghnaḥ prapañcavān |

	varṇasaṃkarakṛd yaś ca kārukaś ca vikarmakṛt ||

	svajātidharmasaṃtyāgī parakarmarataś ca yaḥ |

	pibec chukraṃ ca ya puṃsāṃ sa ca duṣṭo mukhebhagaḥ ||

	ete daityāḥ samākhyātā na tu sṛṣṭāḥ svayaṃbhuvā |

	yajñeṣu rakṣasāṃ bhāgo deya ity eva saṃsmaran ||

	vighnebhyo bhūtimadbhyaś ca tebhyo dadyād gṛhād balim |

	brāhmaṇaḥ syāt kṛtayugaṃ pitaras tatra devatāḥ ||

	tretāyugaṃ kṣatriyaś ca tatra pūjyāś ca devatāḥ |

	vijñeyaṃ dvāparaṃ vaiśyas tatra buddhas tu pūjyate ||

	śūdraḥ kaliyugaṃ tatra pūjyāḥ pāṣaṇḍijātayaḥ || iti |

bhūtabalidāne mantraḥ |

	ye bhūtāḥ pracaranti divā naktaṃ balim icchanto vitudasya preṣyāḥ |

	tebhyo baliṃ puṣṭikāmo harāmi mayi puṣṭiṃ puṣṭipatir dadhātu || iti |

vyāsaḥ |

	aindravāruṇavāvavyā yāmyā vai nairṛtās tathā |

	vāyasāḥ pratigṛhṇantu imaṃ piṇḍaṃ mayārpitam ||

	śvānau dvau śāva(śyāma)śabalau vaivasvatakulodbhavau |

	datvānena vidhānena baliṃ paścād upaspṛśet || **[145]**

annahomaprabhṛti śvādibhyo 'nnaprakṣepaparyantaṃ vaiśvadevākhyaṃ karma sāyaṃ prātaḥ kartavyam | yad āha manuḥ |

	sāyam annasya siddhasya patny amantraṃ baliṃ haret |

	vaiśvadevaṃ hi nāmaitat sāyaṃ prātar vidhīyate ||

kartṝṇāṃ puṃsām alābhe patnī vaiśvadevaṃ mantrarahitaṃ kuryāt | baligrahaṇaṃ vaiśvadevopalakṣaṇārtham | tathā ca gautamaḥ |

	sāyaṃ prātar vaiśvadevaḥ kartavyo balikarma ca |

	anaśnatāpi satatam anyathā kilbiṣī bhavet ||

tasya prātar upakramaḥ sāyam apavargaḥ | yad āha laugākṣiḥ: "divācarebhyo bhūtebhya iti divā | naktaṃcarebhyo bhūtebhya iti naktam" || 1.103 ||

	**annaṃ pitṛmanuṣtebhyo deyam apy anvahaṃ jalam |**

annaṃ pitrādibhyo 'nvahaṃ pratidinaṃ deyam | putrikāputreṇa tu mātāmahādibhyas tribhyo dvyāmuṣyāyaṇais tūbhayebhyaḥ | tad āya vyāghraḥ |

	dadyān mātāmahaśrāddhaṃ niyamāt putrikāsutaḥ |

	ubhayor atha saṃbandhāt (?) kuryāt sa ubhayor api ||

asyām utpannam apatyaṃ tava mama svadhākaraṃ bhavatv iti kanyādātur vareṇa saha saṃpratipattau kṛtavivāhāyāḥ putra ubhayasaṃbaddhaḥ | manuṣyebhyo 'tithibhyo 'nvahaṃ pratidinaṃ deyam | anvaham iti pratyekam abhisaṃbadhyate | annābhāve jalam | atrānvaham iti vidhīyate 'nyad anūdyate | manuḥ |

	kuryād ahar ahaḥ śrāddham annādyenodakena vā |

	payomūlaphalair vāpi pitṛbhyaḥ prītim āharan ||

laghuhārītaḥ |

	nityaśrāddham adaivaṃ syād arghyapiṇḍādivarjitam |

matsyapurāṇe |

	nityaṃ tāvat pravakṣyāmi arghyāvāhanavarjitam |

	adaivaṃ tad vijānīyāt pārvaṇaṃ parvasu smṛtam ||

kātyāyanaḥ |

	apy ekam āśayed vipraṃ pitṛyajñārthasiddhaye |

	adaivaṃ nāsti ced anyo bhoktā bhojyam athāpi vā ||

	abhyuddhṛtya yathāśakti kiṃcid annaṃ yathāvidhi |

	pitṛbhyo 'tha manuṣyebhyo dadyād ahar ahar dvijaḥ ||

	pitṛbhya idam ity uktvā svadhākāraṃ ca kārayet || **[146]**

adaivam ityantam ekaṃ vākyam | nāsti ced anya ity aparam | devalaḥ |

	aghṛtaṃ bhojayan vipraḥ svagṛhe sati sarpiṣi |

	paratra nirayaṃ ghoraṃ gṛhasthaḥ pratipadyate ||

	miṣṭam annaṃ svayaṃ bhuktvā paścāt kadaśanaṃ laghu |

	brāhmaṇaṃ bhojayan vipro nirayaṃ viram āvaset ||

śātātapaḥ |

	bhūtayajñas tathā śrāddhaṃ nityaṃ tv atithitarpaṇam |

	krameṇānena kartavyaṃ svādhyādhyayanaṃ sadā ||

nityam iti śrāddhaviśeṣaṇam | pracetāḥ |

	nāgnaukaraṇaṃ nāvāhanaṃ na piṇḍā na visarjanam |

	anuvrajyā dakṣiṇā ca tribhyaś cātithikalpanam ||

tribhyaś cādhikasya viprasyādhigatasyātithitvaṃ kalpyam | mārkaṇḍeyapurāṇam |

	kuryād ahar ahaḥ śrāddham annādyenodakena vā |

	pitṝn uddiśya viprāṃs tu bhojayed vipram eva vā ||

nārāyaṇaḥ |

	niyujyaikam anekaṃ vā śrotriyaṃ prāṅmukhaṃ sadā |

	nivītī tadgatamanā ṛṣīn dhyāyan samāhitaḥ ||

	āsanaṃ cārghyadānaṃ ca bhuktavadvācanaṃ tataḥ |

	svaśaktyā cānnam uddhṛtya hantety evaṃ prakalpayet ||

	**svādhyāyaṃ cānvahaṃ kuryān na paced annam ātmane || 1.104 ||**

svaśākhādhyayanaṃ svādhyāyo na tu svaśākhaiva, tasyā akāryatvāt | tataś ca svaśākhādhyayanam anvaham anudinaṃ kuryāt | brahmayajñasyaitat punar vacanam anvaham iti guṇavidhānārtham | tathātmārtham annaṃ na pacet | atrātmanaḥ kaivalyaṃ vivakṣitam | tena devādīnām ātmanaś ca kṛte pāko na doṣāya | yad āha manuḥ |

	devātithibhṛtyānāṃ pitṝṇām ātmanaś ca yaḥ |

	na nirvapati pañcānām ucchvasan na sa jīvati ||

evaṃ ca |

	aghaṃ sa kevalaṃ bhuṅkte yaḥ pacaty ātmakāraṇāt |

iti svavākyenāvirodhaḥ | ata eva śrutiḥ: "kevalāgho bhavati kevalādī" iti || 1.104 ||

	**bālasvavāsinīvṛddhagarbhiṇyāturakanyakāḥ |**

**	saṃbhojyātithibhṛtyāṃś ca dampatyoḥ śeṣabhojanam || 1.105 ||**

**[147]**

bālādīn atithīṃś ca bhojayitvā bhuktāvaśiṣṭaṃ dampatī bhuñjīyātām | asāmarthyād bālas tathā vṛddhaḥ, pariṇītā kanyā pitṛgṛhe sthitā svavāsinī, garbhapuṣṭyarthaṃ garbhiṇī kṣīṇatvād āturo vacanād atithir gṛhavyāpārasādhakatvād bhṛtyāḥ | manuḥ |

	suvāsinīḥ kumārīś ca rogiṇo garbhiṇīs tathā |

	atithibhyo 'gra evainān bhojayed avicārayan ||

	adatvā tu ya etebhyaḥ pūrvaṃ bhuṅkte 'vicakṣaṇaḥ |

	sa bhuñjāno na jānāti śvagṛdhrair jagdhim ātmanaḥ ||

śvabhir gṛdhraiś cātmānaṃ bhakṣyamāṇaṃ na jānātīty arthaḥ | tataś ca bālaprabhṛtibhiḥ saha bhojanaṃ na pratyavāyāyeti || 1.105 ||

	**apośānenopariṣṭād adhastāc caiva buñjatā |**

**	anagnam amṛtaṃ caiva kāryam annaṃ dvijanmanā || 1.106 ||**

apo'śāney upanetā māṇavakaṃ preṣyati | tena ca preṣeṇa tadartho 'tra lakṣyate — apośāneneti | tataś cāpośānena bhojanād ūrdhvaṃ purastāc ca kriyamāṇenānnam anagnam amṛtaṃ ca dvijātinā kāryam | vṛddhaśātātapaḥ |

	paridhānam apośānaṃ pūrvam ācchādanaṃ param |

	bhavaty annam anagnaṃ hi sottarīyaṃ tathāmṛtam ||

baudhāyanaḥ |

	upalipte same sthāne śucau ślakṣṇasamanvite |

	caturaśraṃ trikoṇaṃ tu vartulaṃ cārdhacandrakam ||

	kartavyam ānupūrvyeṇa brāhmaṇādiṣu maṇḍalam ||

brahmapurāṇe |

	annaṃ dṛṣṭvā praṇamyādau prāñjaliḥ kathayet tataḥ |

	asmākaṃ nityam astv etad iti bhaktyātha vandayet ||

baudhāyanaḥ: "sarvāvaśyakāvasareṣu prakṣālitapāṇipādo 'pa ācamya śucau saṃvrtte deśe prāṅmukha upaviśyoddhṛtam āhriyamāṇaṃ bhūr bhuvaḥ svar om ity upasthāya vācaṃ yacchen nyastaṃ tu mahāvyāhṛtibhiḥ | pradakṣiṇam annam udakaṃ pariṣicya savyena pāṇināvimuñcann amṛtopastaraṇam asīti purastād apaḥ pītvā pañcānnena prāṇāhutīr **[148]** juhoti śraddhāyāṃ prāṇe niviṣṭo 'mṛtaṃ juhomi śivo mā viśāpradāhāya prāṇāya svāhā" | apāne vyāna udāne samāne niviṣṭa ityādi yathāliṅgam anuṣaṅgaḥ | "evaṃ pañcānnena tūṣṇīṃ bhūyo vratayet | prajāpatiṃ manasā dhyāyet | athāpy udāharanti:

	āsīnaḥ prāṅmukho 'śnīyād vāgyato 'nnam aktsayan |

	askandayaṃs tanmanāś ca bhuktvāgniṃ samupaspṛśet ||

hutānumantraṇam ūrdhvahastaḥ samācaret | śraddhāyāṃ niviśyāmṛtaṃ hutaṃ śivo mā śivam āviśa prāṇam annenāpyāyasva" | śraddhāyām apāne śraddhāyāṃ vyāne śraddhāyām udāne śraddhāyāṃ samāne niviśyetyādi yathāliṅgam anuṣaṅgaḥ | "brahmaṇi ma ātmāmṛtatvāyety akṣareṇātmānaṃ yojayet | sarvatra kratuyājinām ātmayājī viśiṣyate | sa evam evāha rahaḥ sāyaṃ prātar juhuyād adbhir vā sāyam" | tathā |

	brahmacārī gṛhasthaś ca yo 'naśnaṃs tu tapaś caret |

	prāṇāgnihotralopena avakīrṇī bhavet tu saḥ ||

"anyatra prāyaścittāt prāyaścitte tad eva vidhānam" | prāyaścitte tad eva vidhānam iti, prāyaścitte kartavyam ity arthaḥ | "athāpy udāharanti —

	antarā prātarāśaṃ ca sāyamāśaṃ tathaiv ca |

	sadopavāsi bhavati yo na bhuṅkte kadācana ||"

āpastambaḥ: "ācamya cordhvaṃ pāṇī dhārayed ā prodakībhāvāt | tato 'gnim upaspṛśet" | pragatam udakaṃ yāmyāṃ tau prodakau | hārītaḥ: "na kārṣṇāyase mṛnmaye vāśnīyāt" | viṣṇuḥ: **[149]** "na gobrāhmaṇoparāge 'śnīyāt | na rājavyasane pravasitaś cāgnihotrī yadāgnihotraṃ kutaṃ manyeta tadāśnīyāt | yadā kṛtaṃ manyeta vaiśvadevam api parvaṇi ca yadā parvakṛtaṃ manyeta | nāśnīyāc cājīrṇe nārdharātre na madhyāhne na saṃdhyayoḥ | nārdravāsā naikavāsā na nagno na bhinnāsanagato na śayanagato na bhinnabhājane noddhṛtasnehaṃ na divā dhānā na rātrau tilasaṃbaddhaṃ dadhi na saktūn na kovidāravaṭapippalaśaṇaśākaṃ nādatvā nāhutvā nārdrapādo nānārdrakaramukhaś ca nocchiṣṭo ghṛtam ādadyāt | na candrārkatārakā nirtīkṣeta na mūrdhānaṃ spṛśet | sragvy anuliptaś ca na niḥśeṣakṛt syād anyatra dadhimadhusarpiḥpayaḥsaktupalalodakebhyaḥ | 

	nāśnīyād bhāryayā sārdhaṃ nākāśe na tathotthitaḥ |

	bahūnāṃ prekṣamāṇānāṃ naikasmin bahavas tathā ||

	śūnyālaye vahnigṛhe devāgāre kathaṃcana ||

tāmrarajatasuvarṇaśaṅkhasphaṭikāśmanāṃ bhinnam abhinnam ity adoṣaḥ" | mārkaṇḍeyaḥ |

	nyastapātras tu bhuñjīta pañca grāsān mahāmune |

	śeṣam uddhṛtya bhoktavyaṃ śrūyatām atra kāraṇam ||

	vipruṣāṃ copasaṃsparśaḥ pādacailarajas tv adhaḥ |

	mukhena bhuṅkte vipro 'pi pitrarthe na tu lipyate ||

paitṛke bhojane bhūmipātrapratiṣṭhāpanaṃ na lepanīyam ity arthaḥ | viṣṇupurāṇe |

	aśnīyāt tanmanā bhūtvā pūrvaṃ tu madhuraṃ rasam |

	lavaṇāmlau tathā madhye kaṭutiktādikāṃs tathā ||

	prāg dravyaṃ puruṣo 'śnīyān madhye na kaṭhināśanaḥ |

	ante punar dravāśī tu balārogye na muñcati ||

śātātapaḥ |

	vidyamānena hastena brāhmaṇo 'jñānadurbalaḥ |

	toyaṃ pibati vaktreṇa śvāsau jāyeta nānyathā ||

	uddhṛtya vāmahastena yas toyaṃ pibati dvijaḥ |

	surāpānena tattulyaṃ manur āha prajāpatiḥ ||

	hastau prakṣālya gaṇḍūṣaṃ yaḥ pibed avicakṣaṇaḥ |

	sadevāṃś ca pitṝṃś caiva ātmānaṃ caiva ghātayet ||

gaṇḍūṣo bhojanānnaculakaḥ | **[150]** brahmapurāṇe |

	yas tu pāṇitale bhuṅkte yas tu phūtkārasaṃyutam |

	prasṛtāṅgulibhir yaś ca tasya gomāṃsavac ca tat ||

	nājīrṇe bhojanaṃ kuryāt syāc cen nātibubhukṣitaḥ |

	hastyaśvarathayānoṣṭraprāsādastho na bhakṣayet ||

	śmaśānābhyantarastho vā devālayagato 'pi vā |

	śayanastho na bhuñjīta na pāṇisthaṃ na cāsane ||

	nārdravāsā nārdraśirā na vāyajñopavītavān |

	na prasāritapādo na pādāropitapādakaḥ ||

	nāvasaktikasaṃsthaś ca na ca paryaṅkikāsthitaḥ |

	na veṣṭitaśirāś cāpi notsaṅgakṛtabhājanaḥ ||

	naikavastro duṣṭamadhye sopānatkaḥ sapādukaḥ |

	na carmopari saṃsthaś ca carmaveṣṭitapārśvavān ||

	grāsaśeṣaṃ ca nāśnīyāt pītaśeṣaṃ piben na ca |

	śākamūlaphalekṣūṇi dantacchedena bhakṣayet ||

	secayen nānnam annena vikṣiptaṃ pātrasaṃsthitam |

	bahūnāṃ bhuñjatāṃ madhye na cāśnīyāt tvarānvitaḥ ||

	vṛthā na vikired annaṃ nocchiṣṭaḥ kutracid vrajet ||

śaṅkhaḥ: "nāniyukto 'grāsanaṃ gacchet | nāgrāsanasthaḥ prathamam aśnīyāt | nādhikaṃ dadyān na pratigṛhṇīyāt" | bṛhaspatiḥ |

	na spṛśed vāmahastena bhuñjāno 'nnaṃ kadācana |

	na pādaṃ na śiro bastiṃ na padā bhājanaṃ spṛśet ||

āpastambaḥ: "manāg bhuñjīta tathā prāsādakṛtabhūmau bhuñjīta" | devalaḥ |

	bhuktocchiṣṭaṃ samādāya sarvasmāt kiṃcid ācamet |

	ucchiṣṭabhāgadheyebhyaḥ sodakaṃ nirvaped bhuvi ||

atra mantraḥ |

	raurave 'puṇyanilaye padmārbudanivāsinām |

	prāṇināṃ pūrvabhūtānām akṣayyam upatiṣṭhatām || iti |

	bhuktvācāmed yathoktena vidhānena samāhitaḥ |

	śodhayen mukhahastau ca mṛdbhir gharṣaṇair atha || **[151]**

vyāsaḥ |

	adbhiḥ prāṇān samālabhya nābhiṃ pāṇitalena ca |

	bhuktvā caiva pratiṣṭheta na cāpy ārdreṇa pāṇinā ||

	ācānto 'py aśucis tāvad yāvat pātram anuddhṛtam |

	uddhṛte 'py aśucis tāvad yāvan nonmṛjyate mahī ||

viṣṇupurāṇe |

	svasthaḥ praśāntacittas tu kṛtāsanaparigrahaḥ |

	abhiṣṭadevatānāṃ tu kurvīta smaraṇaṃ naraḥ ||

	agnir āpyayayan dhātuṃ pārthivaṃ pavaneritaḥ |

	dantāvakāśaṃ nabhasā jarayatvastu me mukham ||

	annaṃ balāya me bhūmer apām agnyanilasya ca |

	bhavatv etat pariṇatau mamāstu vihitaṃ sukham ||

	prāṇāpānasamānānām udānavyānayos tathā |

	annaṃ puṣṭikaraṃ cāstu mamāstu vihitaṃ sukham ||

	agastir agnir vaḍavānalaś ca bhuktaṃ mayānnaṃ jarayan tv aśeṣam |

	sukhaṃ ca me tat parimāṇasaṃbhavaṃ yacchantv arogo mama cāstu dehe ||

	viṣṇuḥ samastendriyadehabhedapradhānabhūto bhagavān yathaikaḥ |

	satyena tenānnam aśeṣam antarād ārogyado me pariṇāmam etu ||

	viṣṇur attā tathaivānnaṃ pariṇāmaś ca vai yathā |

	satyena tena madbhuktaṃ jīryatv annam idaṃ tathā ||

	ity uccārya svahastena parimṛjya tathodaram |

	anāyāsapradāyīni kuryāt karmāṇy atandritaḥ ||

	nādyāt sūryagrahāt pūrvam ahni sāyaṃ śaśigrahāt |

	grahakāle ca nāśnīyāt snātvāśnīyāc ca muktayoḥ |

	snātvā dṛṣṭvā pare 'hany adyād grastās tamitayos tathā ||

smṛtyantaram |

	bhuktvāṅgulitalaṃ ghṛṣṭvā netrayor yat pradīyate |

	acireṇaiva tad vāri timirāṇi vyapohati ||

tathā |

	śaryātiṃ ca sukanyāṃ ca cyavanaṃ śakram aśvinau |

	bhojanānte smaren nityaṃ cakṣurogair bādhyate || 1.106 ||

**[152]**

	**atithitve tu varṇānāṃ deyaṃ śaktyānupūrvaśaḥ |**

brāhmaṇādīnāṃ varṇānām atithibhāve sati brāhmaṇādikrameṇa te bhojayitavyāḥ, yadi śaknuyāt | aśaktasya brāḥmaṇātithibhojanaṃ niyatam | yad āha baudhāyanaḥ: "athātaḥ pañca mahāyajñās tāny eva mahāsatrāṇi, devayajñaḥ pitṛyajño brahmayajño bhūtayajño manuṣyayajña ity ahar ahar devebhyaḥ svāhā kuryād odapārād athainaṃ pitṛyajñaṃ samāpnoti | ahar ahaḥ svādhyāyam adhīyītā praṇavād athainaṃ brahmayajñaṃ samāpnoti | ahar ahar bhūtebhyo baliṃ hared ā puṣpebhyo 'thainaṃ bhūtayajñaṃ samāpnoti | ahar ahar brāhmaṇebhyo 'nnaṃ dadyād ā mūlaphalaśākebhyo 'thainaṃ manuṣyayajñaṃ samāpnoti" | ataś cātithipūjāyā akaraṇe nindā brāhmaṇātithipūjanākaraṇaviṣayaiva | yad āha viṣṇuḥ |

	atithir yasya bhagnāśo gṛhasthasya tu gacchati |

	tasmāt sukṛtam ādāya duṣkṛtaṃ tu prayacchati ||

ata eva manuḥ kṣatriyādīnām icchayātithyaṃ kāryam ity āha |

	yadi tv atithidharmeṇa kṣatriyo gṛham āvrajet |

	bhuktavatsu tu vipreṣu kāmaṃ tam api bhojayet ||

	vaiśyaśūdrāv api prāptau kuṭumbe 'tithidharmiṇau |

	bhojayet saha bhṛtyais tāv ānṛśaṃsyaṃ prayojayan || iti |

ānṛśaṃsyam anaiṣṭhuryam ||

	**apraṇodyo 'tithiḥ sāyam api vāgbhūtṛṇodakaiḥ || 1.107 ||**

sāyamagato 'tithir apraṇodyo 'pratyākhyeyaḥ | āśayitavya ity arthaḥ | yad āha manuḥ |

	apraṇodyo 'tithiḥ sāyaṃ sūryoḍho gṛhamedhinā |

	kāle prāptas tv akāle vā nāsyānaśnan gṛhī vaset || iti |

aśanābhāve tu vāgbhūtṛṇodakair apy apraṇodyaḥ | apy etair ātithyaṃ kuryād ity arthaḥ | tathā ca āpastambaḥ: "kāle svāminnāv annārthinaṃ na pratyācakṣīyātām annābhāve bhūmir udakaṃ tṛṇāni kalyāṇī vāg ity etāni" || 1.107 ||

	**satkṛtya bhikṣave bhikṣā dātavyā savratāya ca |**
