**[153]**

bhikṣave yataye savratāya brahmacāriṇe ca satkṛtya pūjayitvā bhikṣā deyā | grāsaparimitam annaṃ bhikṣā | nṛsiṃhapurāṇe |

	bhikṣāṃ ca bhikṣave dadyāt parivrāḍbrahmacāriṇe |

	akalpitānnād uddhṛtya sarvavyañjanasaṃyutam ||

	akṛte vaiśvadeve tu bhikṣārthaṃ gṛham āgate |

	uddhṛtya vaiśvadevārthaṃ bhikāṃ datvā visarjayet ||

gautamaḥ: "svastivācya bhikṣādānam appūrvam" appūrvam udakapūrvam | yativiṣayam etat | mārkaṇḍeyapurāṇe |

	grāsapramāṇā bhikṣā syād agraṃ grāsacatuṣṭayam |

	agraṃ caturguṇaṃ tat tu hantakāraṃ vidur budhāḥ ||

	bhojanaṃ hantakāraṃ vā agraṃ bhikṣām athāpi vā |

	adatvā tu na bhoktavyaṃ yathāvibhavam ātmanaḥ ||

nityaśrāddhātithyābhyāṃ karmāntaram etat | viṣṇuḥ: "bhikṣukābhāve cāgraṃ gobhyo dadyād agnau vā prakṣipet | bhukte 'py anne vidyamāne na bhikṣukaṃ pratyācakṣīta" | gṛhasthena bhukte 'py anne tasmin vidyamān ity arthaḥ | cakārād gogrāsādisaṃgrahaḥ | yad āha ṛṣyaśṛṅgaḥ |

	gavāṃ grāsaṃ ca kurvīta nityam eva dine dine |

mahābhārate |

	ghāsamuṣṭiṃ paragave sānnaṃ dadyāt tu yaḥ sadā |

	akṛtvā svayam āhāraṃ svargalokaṃ sa gacchati ||

brahmapurāṇe |

	saurabheyyaḥ svargahitāḥ pavitrāḥ puṇyarāśayaḥ |

	pratigṛhṇantu me grāsaṃ gāvas trailokyamātaraḥ ||

	dadyād anena mantreṇa gavāṃ grāsaṃ sadaiva hi |

	gavāṃ kaṇḍūyanaṃ ghāsaṃ grāsam āhnikam eva vā ||

	datvā bhaven nṛṇāṃ puṇyaṃ gopradānasamaṃ nṛṇām ||

bhikṣādānaṃ naivedādidānopalakṣaṇam | yad brahmapurāṇam |

	viprebhyaś cātha tad deyaṃ brahmaṇe yan niveditam |

	vaiṣṇavaṃ sātvatebhyaś ca bhasmāṅgebhyaś ca śāṃbhavam ||

	sauraṃ gobhyaś ca śāktebhyo devībhyo yan niveditam |

**[154]**	strībhyaś ca deyaṃ mātṛbhyo yad yat kiṃcin nivedyate ||

	bhūtapretapiśācebhyo yat tad bhūmau nidhāpayet ||

	**bhojayec cāgatān kāle sakhisaṃbandhivāndhavān || 1.108 ||**

sakhā mitram | saṃbandhinaḥ śvaśuravivāhyādayaḥ | bāndhavā mātṛpakṣyāḥ | etān bhojanakāle prāptān bhojayet | bhuktavati gṛhasthe prāptān prati manur āha |

	itarān api sakhyādīn saṃprītyā gṛham āgatān |

	prakṛtyānnaṃ yathāśakti bhojayet saha bhāryayā ||

ataś ca vākyād gamyate bhuktavati bhartari bhāryā bhuñjīteti || 1.108 ||

	**mahokṣaṃ vā mahājaṃ vā śrotriyāyopakalpayet |**

**	satkriyānvāsanaṃ svādubhojanaṃ sūnṛtaṃ vacaḥ || 1.109 ||**

mahāntam ukṣāṇaṃ balīvardaṃ tadalābhe 'jaṃ śrotriyāya madhuparkārhāya gṛham āgatāyopakalpayet pacet saṃskuryād iti yāvat | tathā ca śrutiḥ: "atithir vā eṣa etasyāgacchati yaḥ somaḥ krītas tasmād etad yathā rājñe vā brāhmaṇāya vā mahokṣaṃ vā mahājaṃ vā pacet tad u ha mānuṣam" iti | tathā ca bahvṛcabrāhmaṇam: "yāvantaḥ khalu vai rājānam anuyanti tebhyaḥ sarvebhya ātithyaṃ kriyate 'gniṃ manthanti some rājany āgate tad yathaivādo manuṣyarāja āgate 'nyasmin vārhaty ukṣāṇaṃ vā vehataṃ vā kṣadanta evam evāsmā etat kṣadante yad agniṃ manthanty agnir ha devānāṃ paśuḥ" | tataś ca yaḥ kaścid āha śrotiryāyopakalpayed vācā pratipādayen na tu hiṃsyād iti, tac chrutiviruddham | na "na hiṃsyāt sarvabhūtāni" iti niṣedho madhuparkāṅgabhūtāṃ hiṃsām upasaṃkrāmaty agnīṣomīyahiṃsām iva | ata eva manuḥ|

	madhuparke ca some ca pitṛdaivatakarmaṇi |

	atraiva paśavo hiṃsyā nānyatrety abravīn manuḥ ||

tathā ca gṛhyakṛc chaunakaḥ: "ācāntodakāya gāṃ vedayante hato me pāpmā pāpmā me hata it japitvoṃ kuruteti kārayiṣyan mātā rudrāṇāṃ duhitā vasūnām iti japitvom utsṛjatety utsrakṣyan nāmāmso madhuparko bhavarti" | **[155]** atra mahokṣamahājopakalpanamukhena madhuparko vidhīyate | tathā satkriyā pūjā, anvāsanaṃ tasminn upaviṣṭa upaveśanam | svādubhojanaṃ sarpiṣmad annam | tathā ca vasiṣṭhaḥ: "athāpy udāharanti — kṣatriyāyābhyāgatāya sarpiṣmad annam pacatīti" | sūnṛtaṃ vacaḥ kalyāṇī vāg ity etāni kartavyāni || 1.109 ||

	**pratisaṃvatsaraṃ tv arghyāḥ snātakācāryapārthivāḥ |**

**	priyo vivāhyaś ca tathā yajñaṃ praty ṛtvijaḥ punaḥ || 1.110 ||**

pratyabdaṃ snātakādayo 'rghyā madhuparkeṇa pūjyāḥ | snātakaḥ samāvṛttaḥ | ācārya uktalakṣaṇaḥ | pārthivo rājanyaḥ | priyo manojñaḥ | vivāhyaḥ snuṣāyā jāmātuś ca pitā | ṛtvija uktalakṣaṇāḥ | te sāṃvatsarikamadhuparkapūjitāḥ pratiyajñaṃ punar arghyāḥ | cakāraḥ śvaśurādiparigrahārthaḥ | tathā ca śaunakaḥ: "ṛtvijo vṛtvā madhuparkam āharet | snātakāyopasthitāya rājñe cācāryaśvaśurapitṛvyamātulānāṃ ca" iti | atra copathitagrahaṇāt snātakādayo gṛham āgatā evārhaṇīyā iti gamyate | snātakapārthivādīnāṃ śrotriyatve saty arhaṇam, anyathā

	mahokṣaṃ vā mahājaṃ vā śrotriyāyopakalpayet |

iti virodhaḥ syāt || 1.110 ||

_atithau śrotriye ca yathā vartitavyaṃ tathoktam | adhunā tayor lakṣaṇam āha |_

	**adhvanīno 'tithir jñeyaḥ śrotriyo vedapāragaḥ |**

tathā ca manuḥ |

	ekarātraṃ hi nivasann atithir brāhmaṇaḥ smṛtaḥ |

	anityaṃ hi sthito yasmāt tasmād atithir ucyate ||

yaś ca yathāvidhi vedādhyayanasya pāraṃ gatavān sa śrotriyaḥ | vedaśabdenātra svaśākhocyate | tathā ca āpastambaḥ: "dharmeṇa vedānāṃ caikaikam adhītya śrotriyo bhavati" | adhyetṛbhedenaikam iti vīpsopapattiḥ | ata eva baudhāyanaḥ: "ekāṃ śākhām adhītya śrotriyo bhavati" iti ||

	**mānyāv etau gṛhasthasya brahmalokam abhīpsataḥ || 1.111 ||**

**[156]**

etāv atithiśrotriyau brahmalokakāmena gṛhasthena mānyau pūjyau | nityasyāpy asyānuṣaṅgikaṃ phalam etad iti vacanasāmarthād gamyate | śrotriyasya snātakapārthivatvādiviśiṣṭasya madhuparkarūpam arhaṇam uktaṃ śrotriyatvamātreṇātithitvamātreṇa vā viśiṣṭasya mānanam anena phalāya vidhīyata ity anusaṃdheyam || 1.111 ||

_kiṃ ca_ |

	**parapākarucir na syād anindyā mantraṇād ṛte |**

anindyam āmantrayitāraṃ varjayitvā parasyānnaṃ nābhilaṣet | kātyāyanaḥ: "anindyenāmantrito nāpakramet | āmantrito vānyad annaṃ na pratigṛhṇīyāt || 

	**vākpāṇipādacāpalyaṃ varjayec cātibhojanam || 1.112 ||**

vāgādīnāṃ cāpalyam asaṃyatatvaṃ varjayet | atra gautamaḥ: "na śiśnodarapāṇipādacakṣurvākcāpalāni kuryāt | atibhojanaṃ ca varjayet", anārogyādihetutvāt | tathā ca manuḥ |

	anārogyam anāyuṣyam asvargyaṃ cātibhojanam |

	apuṇyaṃ lokavidviṣṭaṃ tasmāṭ tat parivarjayet ||

brahmapurāṇe |

	kuryātkṣīrāntam āhāraṃ na tu paścāt pibed dadhi |

	jaṭharaṃ pūrayed ardham annair bhāgaṃ jalena ca ||

	vāyoḥ saṃcaraṇārthāya caturtham avaśeṣayet || 1.112 ||

	**atithiṃ śrotriyaṃ tṛptam ā sīmāntam anuvarjet |**

atithiṃ śrotriyaṃ ca tṛptaṃ santam ā sīmāntaṃ yāvad anuvrajet | trividhā sīmā — vāstusīmā, grāmasīmā, kṣetrasīmeti | sā cānuvrajanīyaguṇāpekṣayā vyavasthāpanīyā | yad āha manuḥ |

	āsanāvasathau śayyām anuvrajyām upāsanam |

	uttameṣūttamaṃ kuryād dhīne hīnaṃ same samam || iti |

gacchato 'nuvrajyoktā | yadi kuto 'pi hetor nivasati tadā yat kāryaṃ tad āha śaṅkhaḥ: **[157]** "sahāsīta pradoṣe 'nujñāpya śayīta pūrvaṃ pratibudhyeta prasthitam anuvrajet | samabhyanuñjāto nivarteta" ||

	**ahaḥśeṣaṃ samāsīta śiṣṭair iṣṭaiś ca bandhubhiḥ || 1.113 ||**

ahaḥśeṣam avaśiṣṭadinabhāgaṃ śiṣṭair uktalakṣaṇair iṣṭaiḥ priyaiś ca bandhubhiś ca saṃbandhibhir āsīta | tatra dakṣaḥ |

	bhuktvā tu sukham āsthāya tad annaṃ pariṇāmayet |

	itihāsapurāṇābhyāṃ ṣaṣṭhasaptamakau nayet ||

	aṣṭame lokayātrā tu bahiḥ saṃdhyā tataḥ param || iti ||

lokayātrā lokasthitiḥ || 1.113 ||

	**upāsya paścimāṃ saṃdhyāṃ hutvāgnīṃs tān upāsya ca |**

**	bhṛtyaiḥ parivṛto bhuktvā nātitṛptyātha saṃviśet || 1.114 ||**

paścimāṃ sāyaṃ saṃdhyāṃ yathāvidhi upāsya vanditvāgnīn vaitānān aupāsanaṃ vā vidhivad dhutvā tān upāsyārādhya taddai(dde)vatyam amantrajapādinā bhṛtyaiḥ putrādibhiḥ parivṛtaḥ samāvṛto 'natitṛptyā bhuktvāvaśyakakāryāntaraṃ kṛtvā saṃviśet, svāpārthaṃ śayyāyām aṅgayaṣṭiṃ vinyaset | dakṣaḥ |

	homo bhojanakālaś ca yaś cānyad gṛhakṛtyakam |

	kṛtvā caiva tataḥ paścāt svādhyāyaṃ kiṃcid ācaret ||

	pradoṣapaścimau yāmau vedābhyāsena tau nayet |

	yāmadvayaṃ śayānas tu brahmabhūyāya kalpate ||

āpastambaḥ: "sadā niśāyāṃ dārān praty alaṃkurvīta" | dāraśabdenātra jyeṣṭhā sadbhāryocyate | tāṃ pray evātmānam alaṃkurvīta | nānyāṃ prtītyarthaḥ | viṣṇuḥ: "nārdrapādaḥ svapyān nottarāparaśirā na nagno nānuvaṃśaṃ nākāśe na pālāśe śayane na pañcadārukṛte na gajabhagnakṛte na cchinne nāgnipluṣṭe na ghaṭasiktadrumaje na śmaśānaśūnyālayadevatāyataneṣu na capalamadhye nārimadhye na **[158]** dhānyagoguruhutāśanasurāṇām upari nocchiṣṭo na divā svapyāt | na saṃdhyāyāṃ na sabhasmani deśe nārdre na parvatamastake" | uśanā: "na tailābhyaktaśirāḥ svapet | nādīkṣitaḥ kṛṣṇacarmaṇi" | kṛṣṇo 'tra hariṇaḥ || 1.114 ||

	**brāhme muhūrte cotthāya cintayed ātmano hitam |**

rātrer upāntyo muhūrto brāhmaḥ, tasminn utthāya nidrāṃ hitvātmano hitaṃ cintayed vimṛśet | śreyaś ca trivargātmakam | yad āha manuḥ |

	dharmārthāv ucyate śreyaḥ kāmārthau dharma eva ca |

	artha eveha vā śreyāṃs trivarga iti tu sthitiḥ ||

dharmāthakāmās trivargaḥ | tathaitac ca śreyo 'dyetthaṃ mayā sādhanīyam iti cintayet paribhāvayet |

	brāhme muhūrte bhudhyeta dharmārthāv anucintayet |

	kāyakleśāṃś ca tanmūlān vedatattvārtham eva ca ||

vyāsaḥ |

	kiṃ nu me syād idaṃ kṛtvā kiṃ nu me syād akurvataḥ |

	iti saṃcintya kāryāṇi dhīraḥ kurvīta vā na vā ||

	utthyāyotthāya boddhavyaṃ kim adya sukṛtaṃ kṛtam |

	dattaṃ vā dāpitaṃ vāpi vāksatyā vāpi bhāṣitā ||

	utthāyotthāya boddhavyaṃ mahad bhayam upasthitam |

	maraṇavyādhiśokānāṃ kim adya nipatiṣyati ||

	yasyāṃ rātryāṃ vyatītāyāṃ na kiṃcic chubham ācaret |

	tam eva vandhyaṃ divasam iti vidyād vicakṣaṇaḥ ||

	**dharmārthakāmān sve kāle yathāśakti na hāpayet || 1.115 ||**

dharmāṅgabhūte kāle dharmaṃ kuryāt | na tadbhādha(dhe)nārthakāmau | evaṃ dharmāviruddhe 'rthakāle **[159]** 'rtham eva | tathā tadubhayānavaruddhe kāle kāmam | itthaṃ yathāśakti dharmārthakāmebhyo na hāpitā bhavanti | tathā ca gautamaḥ: "na pūrvāhṇamadhāhnān aphalān kuryād yathāśakti dharmārthakāmebhyas teṣu tu dharmottaraḥ syāt" | manuḥ |

	parityajed arthakāmau syātāṃ dharmavivarjitau |

	dharmaṃ cāpy asukhodarkaṃ lokasaṃkruṣṭam eva ca || 1.115 ||

_mānyatvanimittāni sakramakāny(ṇy) āha |_

	**vidyākarmavayobandhuvittair mānyā yathākramam |**

**	etaiḥ prabhūtaiḥ śūdro 'pi vārdhake mānam arhati || 1.116 ||**

vidyādibhis tadvanto vayobandhuvittair yathānirdeśakarmaṃ mānyā bhavanti | karmavayobandhuvittavidbhir vidyāvān mānyo vayobandhuvittavadbhiḥ karmavān bandhuvittavadbhyāṃ vayasvān | evaṃ vittavatā bandhumān na punar anyathā | vidyā purāṇanyāyety atroktā | karma vihitakriyā | vayo mānayitṛvayo'pekṣayādhikam | bandhavo jñātayaḥ | vittam arthaḥ | etair yuktā dvijā mānyā bhavanti | vidyādimatāṃ samavāye yathākramaṃ kramānatikrameṇa mānaḥ kāryaḥ, pūrvaṃ pūrvam uttarād garīya ity arthaḥ | etaiḥ karmādibhir guṇaiḥ pratyekaṃ prabhūtair yukto vārdhake sati śūdro namaskāravyatiriktaṃ mānam arhati | vārdhakam atrāśīter uttaram | yad āha gautamaḥ: "śūdro 'py aśītiko varaḥ" iti | tathā jātir api mānyatvahetur ity āha sa eva: "vittabandhukarmajātividyāvayāṃsi mānyāni parabalīyāṃsi | śrutaṃ tu sarvebhyo garīyas tanmūlatvād dharmasya" | jātir mānyatvakāraṇam | utkṛṣṭaguṇavidyāyuktas tu hīnajātir apy utkṛṣṭajāter mānyo bhavati | yad āha manuḥ |

	vittaṃ bandhur vayaḥ karma vidyā bhavati pañcamī |

	etāni mānyasthānāni garīyo yad yad uttaram ||

	pañcānāṃ triṣu varṇeṣu bhūyāṃsi guṇavanti ca |

	yatra syuḥ so 'pi mānārhaḥ śūdro 'pi daśamīṃ gataḥ ||

varṣaśatasyottamo daśamo bhāgo daśamī | saṃkhyāto bhūyāṃsi, prakarṣato guṇavanti | **[160]** tena jātim anādṛtya bahuvidyo 'lpavidyena mānyaḥ | prakṛṣṭavidyaś cāprakṛṣṭavidyena | evaṃ karmādiṣv api || 1.116 ||

	**vṛddhabhārinṛpasnātastrīrogivaracakriṇām |**

**	panthā deyo nṛpas teṣāṃ mānyaḥ snātas tu bhūpateḥ || 1.117 ||**

vṛddho daśamīsthaḥ, "cakriṇo daśamīsthasy" iti [smṛtiḥ] | vayaso 'ntimāvasthā daśamī | bhārī bhāravān | nṛpo rājanyaḥ | snātaḥ snātakaḥ | strīrogiṇau prasiddhau | varaḥ kanyām udvoḍhuṃ pravṛttaḥ | cakrī śakaṭavāhakaḥ | eṣāṃ panthā deyaḥ | pathi militeṣv eteṣu mārgād apasartavyam iti | pathi teṣāṃ. samavetānāṃ nṛpo mānyaḥ | nṛpasya ca snātako mānyaḥ sa ced brāhmaṇaḥ | yad āha āpastambaḥ: "rājñaḥ panthā brāhmaṇena sametya tu brāhmaṇasyaiva panthā yānasya bhārābhinihitasyāturasya striyā iti sarvair dātavyo varṇajyāyasāṃ cetarair varṇair aśiṣṭapatitamattonmattānām ātmasvastyayanārthena sarvair eva dātavyaḥ" iti | strī cātra garbhiṇī jñeyā | yad āha baudhāyanaḥ |

	panthā deyo brāhmaṇāya gave rājñe hy acakṣuṣe |

	vṛddhāya bhārataptāya garbhiṇyai durbalāya ca ||

śaṅkhalikhitau: "panthā deyo bālapravrajitavidyāśilpaguṇaprakṛṣṭebhyaḥ" iti || 1.117 ||

	**ijyādhyayanadānāni vaiśyasya kṣtriyasya ca |**

**	pratigraho 'dhiko vipre yājanādhyāpane tathā || 1.118 ||**

ijyādikarmāṇi vaiśyakṣatriyayoḥ, cakārād viprasyāpi dharmasādhanāni | pratigrahādīni tu viprasyaiva vṛttisādhanāni | adhikatvaṃ pratigrahāder apy asādhāraṇyam | brāhmaṇasyaiva pratigrahādir ity arthah | ata eva vipra iti viṣayasaptamī | ananyatrabhā(nyabhā)vaś ca viṣyaḥ | ato brāhmaṇasyaiva pratigrahādivṛttitrayam | yat punaḥ: "abrāhmaṇād adhyayanam āpatkāle vidhīyate" iti, tad adhyāpanamātrakartṛtvam abrāhmaṇasyābhyanujānāti, na tu vṛttitvam api | ata evānantaram āha manuḥ |

	anuvrajyā ca śuśrūṣā yāvad adhyayanaṃ guroḥ | iti | **[161]**

anuvrajyaiva śuśrūṣety arthaḥ | abrāhmaṇo brāhmaṇasya yāvad adhyayanaṃ tāvad eva guruḥ | paścād brāhmaṇa evādhyāpito guruḥ | yad āha gautamaḥ: "āpatkalpo brāhmaṇasyābrāhmaṇād vidyopayogas tadanugamanaṃ śuśrūṣā | samāpte brāhmaṇo guruḥ" iti | evaṃ ca: "ajīvantaḥ svadharmeṇānantarāṃ pāpīyasīṃ vṛttim ātiṣṭheran na tu kadācij jyāyasīm" iti vasiṣṭhavacanam(naṃ nā)samañjasaṃ bhavati | ijyādhayanam ity atrejyāgrahaṇena dānādhyayanavyatiriktā dvijātidharmā lakṣyate || 1.118 ||

	**pradhānaṃ kṣatriye karma prajānāṃ paripālanam |**

pradhānaṃ mukhyaṃ kṣtriye prajānāṃ paripālanam | pradhānaṃ prajāparipālanākhyaṃ karma dharmahetutvāc ca | vakṣyati hi — puṇyaṣaḍbhāgam ādatta ityādinā prasaṅgataḥ puṇyaṣaḍbhāgasyārthaṣaḍbhāgasya copādānam iti ||

	**kusīdaṃ kṛṣivāṇijye pāśupālyaṃ viśaḥ smṛtam || 1.119 ||**

kusīdaṃ svarṇāder vṛddhyupajīvanam | kṛṣiḥ prasiddhā | vāṇijyaṃ vaṇikkarma | tataś ca dhānyādi smardhaṃ gṛhītvā mahārghaṃ dīyata iti vāṇijyam | pāśupālyaṃ paśurakṣaṇam | tat sarvaṃ vaiśyasya mukhyaṃ vṛttikarma || 1.119 ||

	**śūdrasya dvijaśuśrūṣā tayājīvan vaṇig bhavet |**

**	śilpair vā vividhair jīved dvijātihitam ācaret || 1.120 ||**

śūdrasya dvijaśuśrūṣā mukhyā vṛttiḥ | brāhmaṇaśuśrūṣā tu dharmo 'pi | yad āha manuḥ |

	viprasevaiva śūdrasya viśiṣṭaṃ karma kīrtyate |

	yad ato 'nyad dhi kurute tad bhavet tasya viṣphalam ||

viśiṣṭam utkṛṣṭam | dharmavṛttihetutvāt | niṣphalaṃ dharmarahitam ity arthaḥ | tataś ca kṣatriyavaiśyasevā śūdrasya vṛttyarthaiva | tad āha sa eva |

	śūdras tu vṛttim ākāṅkṣan kṣatram ārādhayed yadi |

	dhaninaṃ cāpy upārādhya vaiśyaṃ śūdro jijīviṣuḥ ||

**[162]**	svargārtham ubhayārthaṃ vā brāhmaṇaṃ na virodhayet |

	yā tu brāhmaṇaśabdasya sā hy asya kṛtakṛtytā ||

dvijaiś ca tasya yathāśakti vṛttir vidheyety āha sa eva |

	prakalpyate 'sya tair vṛttiḥ svakuṭumbādy athārhataḥ |

	śaktiṃ cāvekṣya dākṣyaṃ ca bhṛtyānāṃ ca parigraham ||

	ucchiṣṭam annaṃ dātavyaṃ jīrṇāni vasanāni ca |

	pulākāś caiva dhānyānāṃ jīrṇāś caiva paricchadāḥ ||

apuṣṭataṇḍulāni dhānyāni pulākāḥ | paricchada upakaraṇaṃ | tayā dvijaśuśrūṣayā na jīvaṃs tadā vaṇig bhavet | vaṇijyayā jīved ity arthaḥ | śilpair vā vividhaiś citrakarmādibhir jīvet,

	aśknuvaṃs tu śuśrūṣāṃ śūdraḥ kartuṃ dvijanmanām |

	putradārātyaye prāpte jīvet kārukakarmabhiḥ ||

iti ca smaraṇāntarāt | tathā: "yādṛśena karmaṇā kriyamāṇena dvijātiśuśrūṣānarho na bhavati tāni karmāṇi pracaraṇīyāni | yaiḥ pracaritaiḥ śuśrūṣyante dvijātayas tāni śilpāni kārukarmāṇi ca" iti, tatrāpi dvijātihitam ācaraṇīyam | tathā ca devalaḥ: "śūdradharmo dvijātiśuśrūṣā pāpavarjanaṃ kalatrādipoṣaṇaṃ karṣaṇapaśupālanabhārodvahanapaṇyavyavahāracitrakarmanṛttagīta-veṇuvīṇāmurajamṛdaṅgavādanāni" iti | śūdrādhikāre narasiṃhapurāṇam |

	ayācitaḥ pradātā syāt kṛṣiṃ vṛttyartham āśrayet |

	purāṇaṃ śṛṇuyāc caiva narasiṃhasya pūjanam ||

mahābhārate |

	dūrāc chūdreṇopacaryo brāhmaṇo 'gnir iva jvalan |

	saṃspṛśya paricaryas tu vaiśyena kṣatriyeṇa ca ||

purāṇaśravaṇavidhau bhaviṣyatpurāṇe |

	śūdrāṇāṃ purato vaiśyā vaiśyānāṃ kṣatriyās tathā |

	kṣatriyāṇāṃ tathā viprāḥ śṛṇvanty ekāgrataḥ sthitāḥ || 1.120 ||

_śūdravṛttīr abhidhāya dharmam āha_ |

	**bhāryāratiḥ śucir bhṛtyabhartā śrāddhakriyāparaḥ |**

**	namaskāreṇa mantreṇa pañca yajñān na hāpayet || 1.121 ||**

bhāryāyām eva ratir yasya sa yathoktaḥ | anena ca bhāryāvyabhicāraparihāro dharmatvenāsya vidhīyate | **śuciḥ** śāstrīyaśaucakartā syāt | **bhṛtyabhartā** bhṛtyānāṃ putrakalatrādīnāṃ poṣakaḥ | **śrāddhakriyāparaḥ** śrāddhānuṣṭhānaniṣṭhaḥ | uktān pañca yajñān namaskārātmakena **mantreṇa** kuryāt, **na** punar anadhītamantratvena tān **hāpayet** tyajet | mantraśabdo 'tra sakalamantrakāryanamaskāraviniyogārthaḥ | anyathā samānārthatayā svāhākārasvadhākārayor eva kārye syāt | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">nanu</span> ca śūdro 'nagniḥ katham agnisādhyakarmādhikārī syāt | na cāsya vivāhāgnir astīti vācyam | śūdrasya vivāhahomābhāvāt | na hy amantrako 'sti homaḥ | na ca śūdro mantravān | namaskāraś ca pañcayajñeṣv eva mantrakāre vidhīyate | na vivāhe 'pi | tasmād agnisādhyeṣu kāryeṣ vaktavyo 'syādhikārahetuḥ | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">ucyate</span> — anagner api śūdrasya vaiśvadevādikarmāṇi laukike 'gnau kāryāṇi taṃ praty eveha vihitatvāt | yathā niṣādasthapatīṣṭiḥ | kiṃcid dvijātīnām api vaiśvadevakarma na vivāhāgniniyataṃ kiṃ punaḥ śūdrasya | yat tu gautamena śūdram adhikṛtyoktam: "pākayajñaiḥ svayaṃ yajetety eke", tal laukikāgniviṣayam || 1.121 ||

_adhunā sarvavarṇasādhāraṇaṃ dharmam āha |_

	**ahiṃsā satyam asteyaṃ śaucam indriyanigrahaḥ |**

**	dānaṃ damo dayā kṣāntiḥ sarveṣāṃ dharmasādhanam || 1.122 ||**

ahiṃsāvihitavadhavarjanam | satyaṃ yathārthavacanam | tac ca bhūtahitam eva yojyam, "satyaṃ bhūtahitaṃ proktam" iti vyāsavacanāt | satyam api priyam eva vācyam,

	satyaṃ bhūyāt priyaṃ brūyān na brūyāt satyam apriyam |

	priyaṃ ca nānṛtaṃ brūyād eṣa dharmaḥ sanātanaḥ ||

iti manuvacanāt | asteyam adattāsvīkāraḥ | śaucam abhakṣyaparihārādi | tathā |

	śaucaṃ tu dvividhaṃ proktaṃ bāhyam ābhyantaraṃ tathā | \
	mṛjjalābhyāṃ smṛtaṃ bāhyaṃ bhāvaśuddhis tathāntaram ||

indriyanigraho niṣiddhebhyo viṣayebhya indriyānāṃ nivāraṇam | dānaṃ **[164]** pratyupakānānapekṣayā pātre svadhanapratidānam | damo niṣiddhān manovyāpāroparamaḥ | dayā bhūtahitaiṣitvam | kṣāntiḥ kṣamā kopavarjanam | "kṣamā dvaṃdvasahiṣṇutvam" iti smṛtyantaram | damaḥ kṣaṃārjavaṃ dānam iti tu pāṭhe — ārjavam akauṭilyam, samacittatā vā, "ārjavaṃ samacittatā" iti vacanāntarāt | sarveṣām eva varṇānām ahiṃsādi pratyekaṃ dharmasādhanaṃ bhavati, teṣām evātra prakṛtatvāt | dharmo 'trāpūrvātmako 'bhimataḥ | atra vyāsaḥ |

	ānṛśaṃsyam ahiṃsā ca prasādaḥ saṃvibhāgitā |

	śrāddhakarmātitheyaṃ ca satyam akrodha eva ca ||

	sveṣu dāreṣu saṃtoṣaḥ śaucaṃ nityānasūyatā |

	ātmajñānaṃ titikṣā ca dharmaḥ sādhāraṇo nṛpa ||

tathā |

	satyaṃ damas tapaḥ saṃtoṣo hrīḥ kṣamārjavam |

	jñānaṃ śamo dayā dhyānam eṣa dharmaḥ sanātanaḥ ||

	satyaṃ būtahitaṃ proktaṃ manaso damanaṃ damaḥ |

	tapaḥ svadharmavarjitvaṃ śaucaṃ saṃkaravarjanam ||

	saṃtoṣo viṣayatyāgo hrīr akāryanivartanam |

	kṣamā dvandvasahiṣṇutvam ārjavaṃ samacittatā ||

	jñānaṃ tattvārthasaṃbodhaḥ śamaś cittapraśāntatā |

	dayā bhūtahitaiṣitvam eṣa dharmaḥ sanātanaḥ ||

bṛhaspatiḥ|

	dayā kṣamānasūyā ca śaucānāyāsamaṅgalam |

	akārpaṇyam aspṛhatvaṃ sarvasādhāraṇāni tu ||

	pare vā bandhuvarge vā mitre dveṣṭari vā sadā |

	āpanne rakṣitavyaṃ tu dayaiṣā parikīrtitā ||

	brāhmo cādhyātmike caiva duḥkhe cotpādite kvacit |

	na kupyati na vā hanti sā kṣamā parikīrtitā ||

	na guṇān guṇino hanti stauti mandaguṇān api |

	nānyadoṣeṣu ramate sānasūyā prakīrtitā ||

	abhakṣyaparihāraś ca saṃsargaś cāpy aninditaiḥ |

	svadharme ca vyavasthānaṃ śaucam etat prakīrtitam ||

**[165]**	śarīraṃ pīḍyate yena suśubhenāpi karmaṇā |

	atyantaṃ tan na kartavyam anāyāsaḥ sa ucyate ||

	praśastācaraṇaṃ nityaṃ nāpraśastapravartanam |

	etad dhi maṅgalaṃ proktam ṛṣibhis tattvadarśibhiḥ ||

	stokād api pradātavyam adīnenāntarātmanā |

	ahany ahani yat kiṃcid akārpaṇyaṃ tad ucyate ||

	yathotpannena saṃtoṣaḥ kartavyo hy annavat tu vā |

	parasyācintayitvārthaṃ sāspṛhā parikīrtitā ||

śarīram atyantaṃ pīḍayate yena tan na kartavyam ity arthaḥ || 1.122 ||

	**vayobuddhyarthavāgveśaśrutābhijanakarmaṇām |**

**	ācaret sadṛśīṃ vṛttim ajihmām aśaṭhāṃ tathā || 1.123 ||**

vayaḥ śarīrāvasthā bālyayauvanādiḥ | buddhiḥ prajñā | artho vittam | vāg bhāṣaṇam | veśo vastrakacādivinyāsaḥ | śrutaṃ gurutaḥ purāṇādividyādhigamaḥ | abhijanaḥ kulam | karma yogādi | eṣāṃ vṛttiṃ sthitiṃ sadṛśīṃ parasparānurūpām amatsarām ajihmām akuṭilām aśaṭhāṃ vācaret | etad uktaṃ bhavati — vayaḥkarmārthaśrutābhijanānāṃ pratyekam anurūpaveśabhāṣaṇabuddhivṛttiḥ kāryeti | tathā ca bṛhaspatiḥ |

	yathā vidyā yathā karma yathā vittaṃ yathā vayaḥ |

	janas tathaiva vartena veśādibhir anuddhataḥ || 1.123 \\

_evaṃ prasaṅgenābhidhāya prakṛtaṃ dvijaṃ praty āha |_

	**traivārṣikādhikānno yaḥ sa somaṃ hi pibed dvijaḥ |**

varṣatrayaṃ yāvad bhṛtyabharaṇaparyāptād annād adhikaṃ yasya vidyate sa dvijaḥ somaṃ pibet | somena yajetety arthaḥ | manau tu viśeṣaḥ |

	yasya traivāṣikaṃ bhaktaṃ paryāptaṃ bhṛtyatṛptaye |

	adhikaṃ vāpi vidyeta sa somaṃ pātum arthati ||

	atas tv alpīyasi dravye yaḥ somaṃ pibati dvijaḥ |

	sa pītasomapūrvo 'pi na tasyāpnoti tat phalam || **[166]**

nityasomayāgaviṣayam etat | yata āha viṣṇuḥ: "traivārṣikānnaḥ pratyabdaṃ somena yajeta | abhāve vaiśvanaryā" iti | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">nanu</span> "dvādaśa rātrīr dīkṣito bhṛtiṃ cinvīta" iti vidhisāmarthyād yācitenaiva ṛtvijāṃ bhṛtiḥ kāryeti vyarthas traivārṣikādhikānno ya iti vacanārambhaḥ | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">maivam</span> | etadvākyārambyasāmarthād evaitad gamyate — bhikṣamāṇasyālābhe 'lpalābhe vā pūrvārjitenāpi dhanena yathoktaṃ dakṣiṇādānaṃ kāryaṃ na punar adānam, dakṣiṇālpadānaṃ veti | yat tu kalpasūtrādau śrutau ca "dātavyaiva yajñe dakṣiṇā bhavaty alpikāpi" ityādivacanam, tatraivārṣikānnenādhikāriṇā prārabdhe kratau vinaṣṭe pūrvārjite dhane bhikṣitasya cāparyāptau draṣṭavyam | atha vā sadasy aprasarpakātreyādibhyo dānaṃ brāhmaṇabhojanaṃ ca prāgarjitenaiva dhanena kāryaṃ na tu yācitena | tasya dakṣiṇādāna eva niyogād ity arthavān niyamāya vākyārambhaḥ | 

	**prāksaumikīḥ kriyāḥ kuryād yasyānnaṃ vārṣikaṃ bhavet || 1.124 ||**

somayāgānuṣṭhānāt prāg yāḥ kriyā aganihotrādyās tāḥ sati vārṣike bhṛtyabharaṇasamarthe 'nne kāryāḥ | etac ca kāmyaviṣayaṃ na nityaviṣayaṃ tac chrutivirodhaprasaṅgāt || 1.124 ||

	**pratisaṃvatsaraṃ somaḥ paśuḥ pratyayanaṃ tathā |**

**	kartavyāgrayaṇeṣṭiś ca cāturmāsyāni caiva hi || 1.125 ||**

**	eṣām asaṃbhave kuryād iṣṭiṃ vaiśvānarīṃ dvijaḥ |**

saṃvatsare saṃvatsare somayāgaḥ kartavyaḥ | paśuyāgaś cāyane 'yane | tathāgrayaṇeṣṭir navair vrīhibhiḥ śyāmākair yavaiś ca kuryāt | "sasyānte navasasyeṣṭyā" ity atra ca sasyaśabdena śaradvasantau lakṣyete | prāyeṇa hi tara(sya) śaradvasantayoḥ purāṇayor anto bhavatīti | ata eva āśvalāyanaḥ: "yadā varṣasya tṛptaḥ syād athāgrayaṇena yajeta" iti | etac ca vrīhyāgrayaṇaviṣayam | yavāgrayaṇaṃ tu vasanta eva | tatraiva hi teṣāṃ navatvam | śyāmākāgrayaṇaṃ śaradi varṣāsu vā | ubhayatra teṣāṃ navatvāt | tathā cāturmāsyāni svakāle kartavyāni | "atha cāturmāsyāni caitryāṃ paurṇamāsyāṃ phālgunyām" iti laugākṣiḥ | etāvatā somayāgādīni karmāṇy **[167]** anūdyālpadhanatvenaiṣām asaṃbhave tatkārye vaiśvānarīṃ vaiśvānaradai(de)vatyām iṣṭiṃ kuryād iti vidadhāti | iṣṭiśabdaḥ somakārye kriyamāṇāyām api vaiśvānaryāṃ śrautavaiśvānareṣṭyaṅgavargaprāptyarthaḥ | anyathā "tatkāryāpattyā taddharmalābhaḥ" iti iti nyāyāt saumikadharmaprāptiḥ syāt | smārtatvena vā smārtītikartavyatā syāt | yat tu manuvākyam,

	iṣṭiṃ vaiśvānarīṃ nityaṃ nirvaped abdaparyaye |

	kḷptānāṃ paśusomānāṃ niṣkṛtyartham asaṃbhave ||

iti, tad api somādikārya eveṣṭiṃ vidadhāti | na tu paścātkaraṇaprāyaścittatayā niṣkṛtiśabdastu(śru?)ter niṣkṛtisaṃbhavenāvaśyakartavyatām iṣṭer ācaṣṭe | ata evānantaram āha |

	āpatkalpena yo dharmaṃ kurute 'nāpadi dvijaḥ |

	sa nāpnoti phalaṃ tasya paratreti vicāritam ||

	viśvaiś ca devaiḥ sādhyaiś ca brāhmaṇaiś ca maharṣibhiḥ |

	āpatsu maraṇād bhītair vidheḥ partinidhiḥ kṛtaḥ || iti |

ataś ca vaiśvānarīyeṣṭiḥ prainidhir na tu prāyaścittam iti gamyate | atra caiṣām iti somādīnāṃ cāturmāsyāntānāṃ parāmarśo na tu paśusomayor eva, prakaraṇāviśeṣāt | yat tu manunoktam: "kḷptānāṃ paśusomānām" iti, tat pradarśanārtham, anyathā bahuvanānupapatteḥ | somādīnāṃ pratyekasaṃbhavabhedeneṣṭiḥ prayojyā dravyābhāvāt pāścātyasaṃbhave vaiśvānarī na tu hetvantarāt | tathā ca śaṅkhaḥ |

	traivārṣikādhikānnas tu pibet somam atandritaḥ |

	iṣṭiṃ vaiśvānarīṃ kuryāt tathaivālpadhano dvijaḥ || iti || 1.125 ||

	**hīnakalpaṃ na kurvīta sati dravye phalapradam || 1.126 ||**

adhikāriṇaṃ prati sarvāṅgopasaṃhārī prayogavidhiḥ śakyāṅgopasaṃhārī ca | tatra śakyāṅgopasaṃhāriṇaḥ prayogavidher yad viṣayībhūtaṃ karma tad dhīnakalpam | yatra tatphalapradaṃ kāmyaṃ karma tad dhīnakalpaṃ na kāryam | atra hetuḥ sati dravye phalapradam iti | dravye sati phalapradaṃ yasmād bhavati | dravyaśabdaḥ sarvāṅgopalakṣaṇārthaḥ | sati dravye sati sarvāṅgānuṣṭhāne karma phalapradaṃ bhavati yasmāt | atra ca phalapradaśabdaḥ **[168]** sakṛc cāritaḥ kākākṣinyāyena hetuhetumadbhyāṃ saha saṃbadhyate | phalapradaṃ karma hīnakalpaṃ na kāryam | sati dravye tat phalapradaṃ bhavati | [tathā ca manuḥ:

	prabhuḥ prathamakalpasya yo 'nukalpenu(na) vartate |

	na sāṃparāyikaṃ tasya durmater vidyate phalam || ]

atra ca sati dravya iti prathamakalpasāmarthyopalakṣaṇārtham || 1.126 ||

	**caṇḍālo jāyate yajñakaraṇāc chūdrabhikṣitāt |**

**	yajñārthaṃ labdham adadad bhāsaḥ kako 'pi vā bhavet || 1.127 ||**

yo yajñārthaṃ śūdrād bhikṣeta sa pretya caṇḍālo bhavati | tathā ca manuḥ |

	na yajñārthaṃ dhanaṃ śūdrād vipro bhikṣeta dharmavit |

	yajamāno hi bhikṣitvā caṇḍālaḥ pretya jāyate ||

	ye śūdrāf abhigamyārthaṃ hy agnihotram upāsate |

	ṛtvijas te hi śūdrasya brahmavādiṣu garhitāḥ ||

	teṣāṃ satatayajñānāṃ vṛṣalān upasevinām |

	padā mastakam ākramya dātā durgāṇi saṃtaret ||

śūdrād dhanam uapādāyāgnīn ya upādhatte tadviṣayam etad vākyadvayam | tathā ca yajñārthaṃ labdhaṃ dhanaṃ samagraṃ yajñopayogi yo na karoti sa bhāsaḥ kāko vā bhavet | bhāsaḥ pakṣiviśeṣaḥ | atra manuḥ |

	yajñārtham arthaṃ bhikṣitvā yo na sarvaṃ prayacchati |

	sa yāti bhāsatāṃ vipraḥ kākatāṃ vā śataṃ samāḥ || 1.127 ||

	**kusūlakumbhīdānyo vā tryāhiko 'śvastano 'pi vā |**

**	jīved vāpi śiloñchena śreyān eṣāṃ paraḥ paraḥ || 1.128 ||**

kusūlaṃ koṣṭhikā tatparimitam eva dhānaṃ yasya sa kusūladhānyaḥ, kusūlād ūnaparimāṇaṃ dhānyāvapanaṃ kumbhī tatparimāṇadhānyo vā gṛhastho bhavet | tryahanirvāhaparyāptam **[169]** eva dhānaṃ yasya sa tryāhikaḥ, sa vā syāt | aśvastananirvāhadhānyaṃ vidyate yasya so 'śvastanaḥ, sa vā syāt | parityaktavrīhyādiikaṇaśa u(ṇiśo)pādānaṃ śilam | patitai(kai)kakaṇa(syopādāna]m uñcham | śilaṃ coñchaṃ ca śiloñcham, tena vā jīvet | eṣām uktavṛttimatāṃ paraḥ paraḥ pūrvasmāt pūrvasmāc chreyān, atiśayena praśastaḥ | svargādilokajayakāraṇam, dharmātiśayavattvāt | atra ca manuḥ ||

	kusūladhānyako vā syāt kumbhīdhānyaka eva vā |

	tryahaihiko vāpi bhaved aśvastanika eva vā ||

	caturṇām api caiteṣāṃ dvijānāṃ gṛhamedhinām |

	jyāyān paraḥ paro jñeyo dharmato lokajittamaḥ ||

	ṣaṭkarmako bhavet teṣāṃ tribhir anyaḥ pravartate |

	dvābhyām ekaś caturthas tu brahmasattreṇa jīvati ||

ṣaṭkarmaśabdena yajanayājanādīni brāhmaṇakarmāṇi nirdiśati tadantargatasya pratigrahādivṛttitrayasya vidhānārtham | tribhir anyaḥ pravartata iti kumbhīdhānyasyāpi vṛttitrayavidhiḥ | dvābhyām eka iti tryahaihikasya yājanādhyāpanānujñā | pratigraho 'pi kutsitād api syād iti tadvarjanam | caturtho 'śvastanaḥ sa brahmasattreṇādhyāpanena jīved iti | evaṃ ca brāhmaṇasyaiva kusūladhānyatvādayo dharmāḥ | na hy anyasya pratigrahādivṛttisaṃbhavaḥ || 1.128 ||

**iti śrīvidyādharavaṃśaprabhavaśrīśilāhāranaredrajīmūtavāhanānyayaprabhūta-**

**śrīmadaparādityadevaviracite yājñavalkyadharmaśāstranibandhe**

**gṛhasthadharmaprakaraṇam**

**atha saṭīkayājñavalkyasmṛtau**

**snātakavrataprakaraṇam — 5**

	**na svādhyāyavirodhyartham īheta na yatas tataḥ |**

**	na viruddhaprasaṅgena saṃtoṣī ca bhavet sadā || 1.129 ||**

svādhyāyādhigamavirodhinam arthaṃ necchet | tadavirodhinam api yatas tato neheta, yatas tato niṣiddhaād dātur ity arthaḥ | na ca viruddhena karmaṇā dyūtādinā prasaṅgena ca gītādinā | prasaṅga āsaktiḥ | taddhetutvād gītādiḥ prasaṅgaḥ | atha vā prasaṅgo 'niṣṭāṣatteḥ, **[170]** yady asmai naitad dadamīdaṃ me 'niṣṭam eṣa kariṣyatīty evaṃ bhayajananarūpaḥ | yathotpannena ca saṃtoṣī saṃtuṣṭo bhavet | atra ca manuḥ |

	saṃtoṣaṃ param āsthāya sukhārthaṃ saṃyato bhavet |

	saṃtoṣamūlaṃ hi sukhaṃ duḥkhamūlaṃ viparyayaḥ ||

atra ca prakaraṇe prativākyam idaṃ kāryam idaṃ varjanīyam iti pratipādanadvāreṇa tadviṣayaḥ saṃkalpa idaṃ kariṣye nedaṃ kariṣya iti manovyāpārarūpo vrataśabdavācyo vidhīyate | "tasya vratam" ity upakramya śrutāv eṣāṃ vidhānāt | ata eva vasiṣṭhaḥ: "athātaḥ snātakasya vratāni" ity ārabhyaitāni vihitavān | ete ca saṃkalpāḥ samāvartanānantaram eva kāryāḥ snātakaṃ prati vihitatvāt || 1.129 ||

_yato 'rtha īhitavyastam āha |_

	**rājāntevāsiyājyebhyaḥ sīdann icched dhanaṃ kṣudhā |**

kṣudhāavasīdan rājādīnām anyatamād **dhanam icchet** | pratigrahādinā lipseta | rājagrahaṇaṃ viśuddhasya dātur upalakṣaṇārtham |

	**dambhihaitukapāṣaṇḍibakavṛttīṃś ca varjayet || 1.130 ||**

lokavaśīkaranārthaṃ dharmakārī dambhī, hetvāśrayaṇena śrutismṛtyuktadharmadūṣayitā yuktibalena sarvatrasaṃśayakārī ca haitukaḥ, vedabāhyāgamavihitakārī pāṣaṇḍī | uktāśramavyatiriktaś ca bakasya vṛttir eva vṛttir yasya sa bakavṛttiḥ | etān varjayet | ebhir na saṃvyavahreyur ity arthaḥ | manuḥ |

	pāṣaṇḍino vikarmasthān baiḍālavratikāñ śaṭhān |

	haitukān bakavṛttīṃś ca vāṅmātreṇāpi varjayet ||

niṣiddhakāriṇo vikarmasthān | baiḍālavratikādīn sa evāha |

	dharmadhvajī sadālubdhaś chadmiko lokadāṃbhikaḥ |

	baiḍālavratiko jñeyo hiṃsraḥ sarvābhisaṃdhikaḥ ||

	yasya darmadhavjo nityaṃ surādhvaja ivocchritaḥ |

	pracchannāni ca pāpāni baiḍālaṃ nāma tadvratam ||

	adhodṛṣṭinaikṛtikaḥ svārthasādhanatatparaḥ |

	śaṭho mithyāvinītaś ca bakavṛttir udāhṛtaḥ ||

śaṭhaḥ stabdhaḥ | **[171]** atra viṣṇudharmeṣu pṛṣṭapāṣaṇḍilakṣaṇaṃ kathaṃcit pāṣaṇḍidarśanasaṃlāpasparśanaprāyaścittasaṃjātajijñāsaṃ dālbhyaṃ prati pulastyaṃ uvāca |

	śrutismṛtyuditaṃ dharmaṃ varṇāśramavibhāgajam |

	ullaṅghya ye pravartante svecchayā kūṭayuktibhiḥ ||

	vikarmābhiratā mūḍhā yuktiprāgalbhyadurmadāḥ |

	pāṣaṇḍinas te duḥśīlā narakārhā naradhamāḥ ||

	tāṃs tu pāṣaṇḍinaḥ pāpān vikarmasthāṃś ca mānavān |

	baiḍālavratinaś caiva nityam eva ca nāpalapet ||

	saṃbhāṣyaitāñ śuciṣadaṃ cintayed acyutaṃ budhaḥ |

	śarīram antaḥkaraṇopaghātair vācaś ca viṣṇur bhagavān aśeṣam |

	śamaṃ nayantv astu mameha śarma pāpād anante hṛdi saṃniviṣṭe ||

	antaḥ śuddhiṃ bahiḥ śuddhiṃ śuddho 'ntar mama yo 'cyutaḥ |

	sa karotv amale tasmiñ śucir evāsmi sarvadā ||

	bāhyopaghātād anagho vidvāṃś ca bhagavān ajaḥ |

	śuddhiṃ nayatv anantātmā viṣṇuś cetasi saṃsthitaḥ ||

	etat saṃbhāṣya japtavyaṃ pāṣaṇḍibhir ihādhamaiḥ |

	namaḥ śucipade coktvā sūryaṃ paśyec ca vīkṣitaiḥ ||

tathā |

	pāṣaṇḍino durācārā duṣṭānnaguṇavādinaḥ |

	asaṃskṛtānnabhoktāro vrātyāḥ saṃskāravarjitāḥ ||

	pāṣaṇḍāḥ pāpakarmāṇo dāmbhikāḥ śaṭhabuddhayaḥ |

	varṇasaṃkarakartāro dharmavyājopajīvinaḥ ||

	niḥśaucā vakrmatayo nānyad astīti vadinaḥ |

	evaṃvidhās te sanmārgād vedaproktād bahiṣkṛtāḥ ||

	kriyākalāpaṃ nindanta ṛgyajuḥsamalakṣaṇam |

	ātmānaṃ ca parāṃś caiva kurvanti narakasthitau ||

	teṣāṃ darśanasaṃbhāṣasparśanāni naraiḥ sadā |

	parityājyāni dṛṣṭe ca proktaṃ saṃbhāṣaṇe tathā ||

	saṃsparśe ca budhaḥ snātvā śuddhe(dhye)c chuciṣadaṃ smaran |

	adhamānāṃ sadaivaiṣām ālāpasparśanaṃ tyajet ||

**[172]**	prākṛto 'pi janaḥ kiṃ tu yaḥ sadācārapālakaḥ |

	yatas te vaidikaṃ karma nindanty akṛtabuddhayaḥ ||

	pāṣaṇḍinām aśeṣāṇām aprītir vedakarmaṇi |

	te hy adhogāminaḥ proktā āsuraṃ bhāvam āśritāḥ ||

tathā |

	tanmohitānām acirād viveko yāti saṃkṣayam |

	kṣīṇajñānā vikarmāṇi kurvanty ahar ahar narāḥ ||

	nijavarṇātmakaṃ dharmaṃ parityajya vimohitāḥ |

	dharmabuddhyā tataḥ pāpaṃ kurvanty ajñānamohitāḥ ||

	jñānāvalepaś tatraiva tatas teṣāṃ prajāyate |

	suhṛdbhir vāryamāṇās te paṇḍitaiś ca dayālubhiḥ ||

	prayacchanty uttaraṃ mūḍhāḥ kūṭayuktasamanvitam |

	tatas te svayam ātmānam anyaṃ calpamatiṃ naram ||

	vikarmaṇāṃ yojayantaś cyāvayanti svadharmataḥ ||

viṣṇupurāṇam |

	kriyāhānir gṛhe yasya masam ekaṃ prajāyate |

	tasyāvalokanāt sūryaṃ paśyeta matimān naraḥ ||

	kiṃ punar yas tu saṃtyaktatrayīḥ (yiḥ) sarvātmanā dvijaḥ |

	pāṣaṇḍiyogibhiḥ pāpair vedavādavirodhibhiḥ ||

	pāṣaṇḍino vikarmasthān baiḍālavratikāñ śaṭhān |

	haitukān bakavṛttīṃś ca vāṅmātreṇāpi nārcayet ||

	budhair ālāpasaṃsargasahāsyāś cātipāpibhiḥ |

	pāṣaṇḍibhir durācarais tasmāt tān parivarjayet ||

	ete nagnās tathā khyātā dṛṣṭvā śrāddhopaghātakāḥ |

	eṣāṃ saṃbhāṣanāt puṇyaṃ dinam ekaṃ praṇaśyati ||

	etān pāṣaṇḍinaḥ pāpān nityam eva tu nālapet |

	puṇyaṃ naśyanti saṃbhāṣād eteṣāṃ taddinodbhavam ||

skandapurāṇe |

	kṛtaghnaṃ mānavaṃ dṛṣṭvā nārakeṣv api kutsitam |

	śuddhyarthaṃ devi draṣṭavyāḥ somānaladivākarāḥ ||

somādīnāṃ yathāsaṃbhavaṃ vikalpaḥ || 1.130 ||

	**śuklāmbaradharo nīcakeśaśmaśrunakhaḥ śuciḥ |**

śuklavastradharo bhavet | tathā nīcakeśādiś ca bhavet | nīcāni kṛttāni keśaśmaśrunakhāni yasya sa tathoktaḥ | tathā śuciḥ prayataḥ sarvadā syāt | gautamaḥ: "na raktam ulbaṇam anyddhṛtaṃ vā vaso bibhṛyāt | nirṇijya tu kāmam" | anyadhṛtaṃ tu prakṣālya kāmaṃ bibhṛyād ity arthaḥ | mānave 'paro viśeṣaḥ |

	na jīrṇamalavadvāsā bhavec ca vibhave sati |

tathā |

	upānahau ca vāsaś ca dhṛtam anyair na dhārayet |

	upavītam alaṃkāraṃ chatraṃ kanakam eva ca ||

viṣṇupurāṇe |

	sadānupahataṃ vastraṃ praśastrāś ca tathauṣadhīḥ |

	gāruḍāni ca ratnāni bibhṛyāt prayato naraḥ ||

mārkaṇḍeyapurāṇe |

	na cāpi raktavāsāḥ syāc citrāsitadharo 'pi vā |

	na ca kuryād viparyāsaṃ vāsasor na ca bhāṣaṇe ||

	varjyaṃ ca vidaśaṃ vastram atyantopahataṃ ca yat ||

mahābhārate |

	anyad eva bhaved vāsaḥ śayanīye 'nyad eva tu |

	anyad rathyāsu devānām arcāyām anyad eva hi ||

	**na bhārādarśane 'śnīyān naikavāsā na saṃsthitaḥ || 1.131 ||**

bhāryāṃ paśyaṃs tayā ca dṛśyamānas tathaikavāsāś ca tiṣṭhan nāśnīyāt || 1.131 ||

	**na saṃśayaṃ prapadyeta nākasmād apriyaṃ vadet |**

**	nāhitaṃ nānṛtaṃ caiva na stenaḥ syān na vārdhuṣī || 1.132 ||**

saṃśayaṃ jīvanasaṃśayaṃ na prapadyeta | atha vā niścite 'rthe saṃśayam atiśaṅkāṃ na kuryāt | apriyam ahitam | anṛtaṃ ca śāstrīyakāraṇaṃ vinā na vadet | steno vā vārdhiṣī vā na syāt | manuḥ |

	nāvinītair vrajed dhuryair na cakṣurvyādhipīḍitaiḥ |

	na bhinnaśṛṅgākṣikhurair na vāladhivirūpitaiḥ ||

	nātikālyaṃ nātisāyaṃ nātimadhyaṃdine sthite |

	nājñātena ca saṃgacchen naiko na vṛṣalaiḥ saha ||

	gavāṃ ca yānaṃ pṛṣṭhena sarvadaiva vigarhitam || **[174]**

viṣṇuḥ: "na rātrau vṛkṣamūlam adhitiṣṭhet | na sūnābandhanāgārau na vṛtha ca nadīṃ taret | na devatābhyaḥ pitṛbhyaś codakam apradāya kūlam adhitiṣṭhet | na kūpam avalokayet | na laṅghayet | naiko 'dhvānaṃ prapadyeta | nādhārmikaiḥ sārdhaṃ na dviṣadbhiḥ | na saṃdhyayor nāsaṃnihitapānīyaṃ nātitūrṇaṃ na saṃtatam" | baudhāyanaḥ: "na patitena stryā cādhvānaṃ vrajet" | viṣṇupurāṇe |

	varṣātapādiṣu chatrī daṇḍī rātryaṭavīṣu ca |

	śarīratrāṇakāmo vai sopānatkaḥ sadā vrajet ||

	nordhvaṃ na tiryag dūraṃ vā nirīkṣaṇ paryaṭad budhaḥ |

	yugamātraṃ mahīpṛṣṭhaṃ naro gacched vilokayan ||

tathā |

	na duṣṭaṃ yānam ārohet kūlacchāyāṃ na saṃśrayet |

	naikaḥ śūnyāṭavīṃ gacchen na ca śūnye gṛhe vaset ||

devīpurāṇe |

	nāsahāyo vrajed rātrau notpathe na catuṣpathe ||

āpastamba: "na śrotriyam anabhibhāṣya vyativrajed araṇyaṃ na striyam" | paiṭhīnasiḥ: "na gobrāhmaṇāgnyantareṇa vyapeyāt | anujñāpya vā vrajet | yamaḥ: 

	saṃnikṛṣṭāv adhīyānau yo 'ntarā vrajati dvijaḥ |

	sa bhāsarāsabhānāṃ ca yoniṃ na vrajati pāpakṛt || iti |

"nākasmād apriyaṃ vadet" ity uktam, tatprasaṅgād anyad apy ucyate | tatra "doṣāḥ" ity anuvṛttau devalaḥ: "tatra paruṣavacanam apavādaḥ paiśunyam anṛtaṃ vṛthālāpo niṣṭhuram iti vāṅmayāś ca ṣaṭ | pareṣāṃ deśakulajātividyāśilparūpavṛttāvāraparicchadaśarīrakarmājīvanānāṃ tat pratyakṣaṃ doṣavacanam |

	yac cānyat krodhasaṃtrāsajananaṃ ninditaṃ vacaḥ |

	paruṣaṃ tac ca vijñeyaṃ tathānyac ca tathāvidham ||

	cakṣuṣmān iti luptākṣaṃ caṇḍālaṃ brāhmaṇeti ca |

	praśaṃsānindanaṃ dveṣāt paruṣāt tad viśiṣyate ||

	vṛṣalaṃ vṛṣalety uktvā patitaṃ patiteti vā |

	satyenāpi ca doṣaḥ syān mithyā dviguṇabhāg bhavet ||

teṣām eva paruṣavacanānāṃ prokṣam udāharaṇam apavādaḥ | gurunṛpanibandhubhartṛmitrasakāśe **[175]** 'rthopaghātārthaṃ doṣopākhyāpanaṃ paiśunyam | anṛtaṃ dvividham: asatyaṃ visaṃvādaś ceti | tatra dṛṣṭaśrutānumitānām anyathā vacanam asatyam | prāgabhyupagatānām asaṃpravartanaṃ visaṃvādaḥ" iti |

	rāgād dveṣād bhayāl lobhād dākṣiṇyāc chaṅkayā hriyā |

	dambhāt pramādataś cāpi narasyotpadyate 'nṛtam ||

	paraprāṇopaghātāc ca paradravyāpahārataḥ |

	viśiṣṭo 'nṛtavādas tu na vṛthā kathanādiṣu ||

	tasmād anṛtahetūṃs tān nātmany utpādayet kvacit |

	utpannān vā praśamayet kāraṇais tadvighātibhiḥ ||

	deśarājapravādāc parārthaparikalpanāt |

	narmahāsaprasaṅgāc ca vijñeyaṃ vyarthabhāṣaṇam ||

	guhyāṅganāṅgasaṃjñānāṃ vacanaṃ niṣṭhuraṃ viduḥ |

	yad anyad vā vaco nīcaṃ strīpuṃsor maithunāśrayam ||

	ity evaṃ ṣaḍvikalpasya duṣṭavākyasya bhāṣaṇam |

	iha cāmutra tat tyaktvā nānā(na)rtham adhigacchati ||

	hitāhitaṃ manuṣyāṇāṃ kevalaṃ vacasi sthitam |

	tasmāt saṃyojayed vācam apramattaḥ parīkṣya ca ||

	duścikitsyatamaṃ paścād duruktaṃ hi vaco bhavet |

	kṣipraṃ vinipatec cāpi vacanaṃ doṣasaṃhitam ||

atra yamaḥ |

	pratyakṣaṃ vā parokṣaṃ vā patitaṃ yadi paśyati |

	pratyādeśo na kartavyo rakṣed ātmānam ātmanā ||

kenāpi pramāṇena viditaṃ patitaṃ na pratyādiśet, na kathayed ity arthaḥ | tatsaṃyogād ātmānaṃ rakṣet |

	yāni mithyābhiśastānāṃ patanty aśrūṇi rodanāt |

	tāni putrān paśūn ghnanti tūrṇaṃ mithyābhiśaṃsinām ||

dakṣaḥ |

	anṛtaṃ pāradāryaṃ ca tathābhakṣyasya bhakṣaṇam |

	agamyāgamanaṃ caiv hiṃsā steyaṃ tathaiva ca ||

	aśrautadharmācaraṇaṃ maitradharmabahiṣkṛtam |

	etāni nava karmāṇi niṣiddhāni vivarjayet || **[176]**

maitraṃ maitrī | bahiṣkaraṇaṃ tyāgaḥ | devalaḥ |

	gṛhe pararahasyāni naivopaśṛṇuyāt kvacit |

	na brūyāt pararandhrāṇi prakāśe janasaṃsadi ||

yamaḥ |

	naiva brūyān na śṛṇuyād duṣṭavākyaṃ kathaṃcana |

	brāhmaṇānāṃ viśeṣeṇa kadacid api kenacit ||

	duṣṭavākyaṃ na vaktavyaṃ brāhmaṇānāṃ kathaṃcana |

	tūṣṇīm āsīta nindāyāṃ na brūyāt kiṃcid uttaram ||

	brāhmaṇānāṃ parīvādaṃ naiva kuryān na kārayet |

	yad brāhmaṇeṣu kuśalaṃ tad evāśu samācaret ||

	brāhmaṇānāṃ parīvādo nindā yatra pravartate |

	karṇau tatra pidhātavyau gantavyaṃ vā tato 'nyataḥ || 1.132 ||

_kiṃ ca |_

	**dākṣāyaṇī brahmasūtrī veṇumān sakamaṇḍaluḥ |**

dākṣāyaṇaṃ suvarṇam, brahmasūtraṃ yajñopavītam, veṇur vaṃśaḥ | etadvān kamaṇḍalusahitaś ca bhavet | manuḥ |

	vaiṇavīṃ dhāreyad yaṣṭiṃ sodakaṃ ca kamaṇḍalum |

	yajñopavītaṃ vedaṃ ca śubhe raukme ca kuṇḍale ||

vedo darbhamuṣṭiḥ | raukme sauvarṇe | laugākṣiḥ: "anupasṛṣṭaṃ suvarṇaṃ dhārayet" | anupasṛṣṭaṃ kālikārahitam | baudhāyanaḥ: "snātako 'ntarvāsāḥ sottarīyaṃ vaiṇavaṃ daṇḍaṃ dhārayet sodakaṃ ca kamaṇḍalum | dve yajñopavīte uṣṇīṣam ajinam upary upānahau chatraṃ ca" | 

_api ca |_

	**kuryāt pradakṣiṇaṃ devamṛdgovipravanaspatīn || 1.133 ||**

devādīn pradakṣiṇaṃ kuryāt | dakṣiṇahastabhāge kurvan gacched ity arthaḥ | manuḥ |

	mṛdaṃ gāṃ daivataṃ vipraṃ ghṛtaṃ madhu catuṣpatham |

	pradakṣiṃaṃ prakurvīta prajñātaṃś ca vanaspatīn ||

mṛdam uddhṛtām | mārkaṇḍeyaḥ |

	catuṣpathaṃ namaskuryāt prakhyātāṃś ca vanaspatīn |

	maṅgalyāni ca sarvāṇi pathi kuryāt pradakṣiṇam ||

	amaṅgalyāni vāmāni kartavyāni vijānatā || iti |

	auṣadhāni niyuktāni dhānyaṃ kṛṣṇaṃ ca yad bhavet |

	kārpāsaṃ ca tṛṇaṃ suṣkaṃ śuṣkagomayam eva ca ||

	indhanaṃ ca tathāṅgāraṃ yatra sarpau tathāśubhau |

	abhyakto malinaḥ pāṇḍus tathā nagnaś ca mānavaḥ ||

	muktakeśo gadārtaś ca kaṣāyāmbaradhārakaḥ |

	unmattakas tathā ṣaṇḍo dīnaś cātha napuṃsakam ||

	ayaḥ paṅkaṃ tathā carma keśābandhanam eva ca |

	tathaivoddhṛtasārāṇi piṇyākadīni yāni ca ||

	caṇḍālaśvapacādyāś ca narā bandhanapālakāḥ |

	vadhakāḥ pāpakarmāṇo garbhiṇī strī tathāturaḥ||

	tuṣabhasmakapālāsthibhinnabhāṇḍāni yāni ca |

	riktāni caiva bhāṇḍāni mṛtaṃ sākrandam eva ca ||

	evamādīni cānyāni aśastāny abhidarśane |

	aśasto vādyaśabdaś ca bhinnabhairavajharjharaḥ ||

	ehīti purataḥ śabdaḥ śasyate na tu pṛṣṭataḥ |

	gaccheti paścād dharmajña purastāt tu vigarhitaḥ ||

	kva yāsi tiṣṭha mā gaccha kiṃ te tatra gatasya ca |

	anye śabdāś ca ye 'niṣṭās te vipattikarāḥ smṛtāḥ ||

	dhvajādiṣu tathā sthānaṃ kravyādīnāṃ vigarhitam |

	skhalanaṃ vāhanānāṃ ca vastrasaṃghas tathaiva ca ||

	nirgacchataś ca dvārādau śirasy āhananaṃ bhavet |

	chatradhvajādivastrāṇāṃ patanaṃ cāśubhaṃ bhavet ||

	vāyuś ca karkaśo rūkṣaḥ sarvadigbhyaḥ samutthitaḥ |

	pratilomas tathā nīco vijñeyo bhayakṛd dvijaḥ ||

	anukūlo mṛduḥ snigdhaḥ sukhasparśaḥ śubhāvahaḥ |

	krūrā rūkṣasvarāś caṇḍāḥ kravyādāś ca vigarhitāḥ ||

**[178]**	apraśaste tathā jñeye pariveśa(ṣa)pravarṣaṇe |

	dṛṣṭe nimitte prathamam amaṅgalyavināśanam ||

	śaṃkaraṃ saṃstuyād vidvāṃs tathaiva madhusūdanam |

	dvitīyaṃ tu tato dṛṣṭe pratīpaṃ praviśed gṛham ||

sahajaṃ napuṃsakam | pumān eva kāraṇāntarāḍ apetapuṃstvaḥ ṣaṇḍaḥ |

	atheiṣṭāni praavakṣyāmi maṅgalāni tathānagha |

	śvetāḥ sumanasaḥ śreṣṭāḥ pūrṇakuṃbhas tathaiva ca ||

	jalajāni ca puṣpāṇi māṃsaṃ matyāś ca bhārgava |

	gāvas turaṅgamātaṅgau baddha ekapaśus tv ajaḥ ||

	tridaśāḥ suhṛdo viprā jvalitaś ca hutāśanaḥ |

	gaṇikāś ca mahābhāga dūrvā cārdraṃ ca gomayam ||

	rukmaṃ rūpyaṃ tathā tāmraṃ sarvaratnāni cāpy atha |

	oṣadhayo 'pi ca dharmajña vacā siddhārthakās tathā ||

	nṛvardhamānayānaṃ ca bhadrapīṭhaṃ tathaiva ca |

	khaḍgaṃ cakraṃ patākāṃ ca mṛdam āyudham eva ca ||

	rājaliṅgāni sarvāṇi śavaṃ ruditavarjitam |

	ghṛtaṃ dadhi payaś caiva phalāni vividhāni ca ||

	svastikaṃ vardhamānaṃ ca nadyāvartaṃ sakaustubham |

	nadyaś ca citravinyastā maṅgalāni parāṇi ca ||

	akṣatāś ca tathā mukhyās tathā darpaṇam eva ca |

	añjanaṃ rocanā caiva bhṛṅgāraṃ mākṣikaṃ tathā ||

	śaṅkham ikṣus tathā bhakṣyā vācaś caiva tathā śubhāḥ |

	vāditrāṇāṃ śubhaḥ śabdo gambhīraś ca manoharaḥ ||

	gāndhāraṣaḍjaṛṣabhā ye ca śabdās tathā svarāḥ |

	medhāḥ śastāḥ śubhāḥ snigdhā gajabṛṃhitaśabditāḥ ||

	anulomā taḍicchastā śakracāpaṃ tathaiva ca |

	anulomā grahāḥ śastā dikpatis tu viśeṣataḥ ||

	āstikyaṃ śraddadhānatvaṃ tathā pūjyābhipūjanam |

**[179]**	śastrāny etāni dharmajña yac ca syān manasaḥ śubham ||

	manasas tuṣṭir evātra paraṃ vrajanakāraṇam |

	ekataḥ sarvaliṅgāni manasas tuṣṭir ekataḥ ||

	yānotsukatvaṃ manasaḥ praharṣaḥ susvapnalābho vijayapravādaḥ |

	maṅgalyasiddhipravaṇaṃ manaś ca jñeyāni nityaṃ vijayāvahāni ||

ārūḍhanaraṃ yānaṃ nṛvardhamānam | devasnānārthaṃ pīṭhaṃ bhadrapīṭham | nandyāvartādayaḥ suvarṇadārvādikṛtāḥ saṃniveśā jyotiḥśāstravāstuvidyāprasiddhāḥ | viṣṇuḥ: "vyaṅgaṃ dṛṣṭvā nivarteta viraktamuṇḍajaṭilavāmanapravrajitāṃś ca lavaṇarajjunigaḍāṃś ca | vīṇācandanārdraśākoṣṇīṣālaṃkārakumārīs tu prasthānakāle 'bhinandet" iti || 1.133 ||

	**na meheta nadīchāyāvartmagoṣṭhāmbubhasmasu |**

nadyādiṣu mehanaṃ mūtrapurīṣotsargaṃ na kuryāt | nadyām anudakāyām | sodakāyāṃ punar ambugrahaṇād eva niṣedhaḥ siddhaḥ | chāyāyāṃ lokopajīvyāyām | tathā ca vasiṣṭhaḥ: "na nadyāṃ mehanaṃ kuryān na pathi na ca bhasmani | na gomaye na kṛṣṭe nopte na śādvalopajīvyacchāyāsu" | goṣṭho govrajaḥ | tathā manuḥ |

	na mūtraṃ pathi kurvīta na bhasmani na govraje |

	na phālakṛṣṭe na jale na cityāṃ na ca parvate ||

	na jīrṇadevāyatane na valmīke kadācana |

	na sasattveṣu garteṣu na gacchan na pathi sthitaḥ ||

	na nadītīram āsādya na ca parvatamastake ||

parvatagrahaṇe saty api yat parvatamastakagrahaṇaṃ tad atyantāpadi mastakād anyatrānugrahārtham | yamas tu |

	tuṣāṅgārakapālāni devatāyatanāni ca |

	rājamārgaśmaśānāni kṣetrāṇi ca khalāni ca ||

devalaḥ: "na catvaropadvārayor mūtrapurīṣe kuryāt | na kṛṣṭakṣetre na sasyapūrṇe na yajñabhūmau na yajñiyānāṃ vṛkṣāṇām adhastāt" | **[180]** viṣṇuḥ: "noṣare na parāśucau | nodyānodakasamīpayoḥ | nākāśe mūtrapurīṣe kuryāt" | śaṅkhalikhitau: "nāsaṃvṛte mūtrapurīṣe utsṛjet | na sāntarvāsā na nirvāsāḥ" |

	**na pratyagnyarkagosomasaṃdhyāmbustrīdvijanmanaḥ || 1.134 ||**

agnyādīn prati agnyādyabhimukhas tān paśyan va na mehet | tathā ca gautamaḥ: "na vāyvagniviprādiyāpo devatā gāś ca prati paśyan vā mūtrapurīṣāmedhyāny udasyet | naitā devatāḥ prati pādau prasārayet" | yamaḥ |

	praty ādityaṃ na meheta na paśyed ātmanaḥ sakṛt |

	dṛṣṭvā sūryaṃ nirīkṣeta gām agniṃ brāhmaṇaṃ tathā ||

	praty adityaṃ praty anilaṃ prati gāṃ ca prati dvijam |

	prati somaṃ prati jalaṃ prati saṃdhye ca nityaśaḥ ||

	hanti mehayataḥ prajñāṃ prati panthānam eva ca |

	mehayanti ya etāṃś ca te bhavanti gatāyuṣaḥ ||

āpastambaḥ: "na sopānatko mūtrapurīṣe kuryāt" || 1.134 ||

_kiṃ ca |_

	**nekṣetārkaṃ na nagnāṃ strīṃ na ca saṃsṛṣṭamaithunām |**

**	na ca mūtraṃ purīṣaṃ vā nāśucī rāhutārakāḥ || 1.135 ||**

sūryaṃ vivastrāṃ strīṃ striyam, tathā saṃbaddhamaithunām, mūtraṃ purīṣaṃ ca na paśyet | aśuciś ced rāhutārakāś ca | manuḥ |

	nekṣetodyantam ādityaṃ nāstaṃ yāntaṃ kadacana |

	nopasṛṣṭaṃ na vāristhaṃ na madhyaṃ nabhaso gatam ||

viṣṇuḥ: "nādityam īkṣeta vāsasātirohitaṃ na cādarśajalādyupagatam" | hārītaḥ: "na nagnāṃ striyaṃ puruṣaṃ vā vīkṣeta nodayāstamayau candrārkau" | gautamaḥ: "na nagnāṃ parayoṣitam īkṣeta" | āśvalāyanaḥ: "na nagnāṃ striyam īkṣetānyatra maithunāt" | svabhāryāviṣayam etat | manuḥ |

	nāśnīyād bhāryayā sārdhaṃ nainām īkṣeta cāśnatīm |

	kṣuvantīṃ jṛmbhamāṇāṃ vā na cāsīnāṃ yathāsukham ||

**[181]**	nāñjayantīṃ svake netre na cābhyaktāmanāvṛtām 

	na paśyet prasuvantīṃ vā tejaskāmo dvijottamaḥ ||

viṣṇuḥ: "na kruddhasya guror mukham īkṣeta | na tailodakayoḥ svāṃ chāyāṃ na malavatyādarśe na patnīṃ bhojanasamaye na striyaṃ nagnāṃ kaṃcana mehamānaṃ na cālānabhraṣṭaṃ kuñjaraṃ na ca viṣamasthaṃ vṛṣādiyuddhaṃ nonmattaṃ na mattam" | devalaḥ:

	patitavyaṅgacaṇḍālocchiṣṭān vā nāvalokayet |

	anudṛṣṭigatair etair asaṃbhāṣo nṛṇāṃ varam || 1.135 ||

	**ayaṃ me vajra ity evaṃ sarvaṃ mantram udīrayan |**

**	varṣaty aprāvṛto gacchet svapet pratyakśirā na ca || 1.136 ||**

deve varṣaty aprāvṛtaśirāḥ "ayaṃ me vajraḥ pāpmānam apahanat" iti mantram uccārayan gacchet | pratyakśirāḥ svāpaṃ ca varjayet || 1.136||

_api ca |_

	**ṣṭhīvanāsṛkśakṛnmūtraviṣāṇy apsu na nikṣipet |**

**	pādau pratāpayen nāgnau na cainam abhilaṅghayet || 1.137 ||**

ṣṭhīvanaṃ mukhena tyajyamānaṃ lālādi, asṛg rudhiram, śakṛt purīṣam, mūtraviṣe prasiddhe | retāṃsīti pāṭhe reto 'pi prasiddham | etāny udake na saṃkṣipet | pādapratāpanābhilaṅghane agniṃ prati na kuryāt | yamaḥ |

	caityavṛkṣaṃ na vā chindyān nāpsu śleṣmāṇam utsṛjet |

	na śukraṃ na viṣaṃ mūtraṃ na purīṣaṃ na lohitam ||

	nāsthibhasmakapālāni na keśān na ca kaṇṭakān ||

citau bhavo vṛkṣaś caityaḥ | [citiḥ] śmaśānam | manuḥ |

	nāgniṃ mukhenopadhamen nagnāṃ nekṣeta ca striyam |

	nāmedhyaṃ prakṣiped agnau na ca pādau pratāpayet ||

	adhastān nopadadhyāc ca na cainam abhilaṅghayet |

	na cainaṃ pādataḥ kuryān na prāṇābhādham ācaret ||

kātyāyanaḥ |

	juhūṣaṃś ca hute caiva pāṇisūrmīsphyadārubhiḥ |

	na kuryād agnidhamanaṃ na kuryād vyajanādinā ||

**[182]**	mukhenaiva dhamed agniṃ mukhād eva vyajāyata |

	nāgniṃ mukheneti ca yal laukikaṃ yojayanti tat ||

viṣṇuḥ: "nāsṛṅ na viṣam agnau prakṣipet" | devalaḥ |

	agnau na prakṣiped agnim adbhir na śamayet tathā ||

āpastambaḥ: "agniṃ nāprayata āsīded iṣumātrād ity eke khaṭvāyāṃ ca nopadadhyāt" | gautamaḥ: "nāgnim apaś ca yugapad dhārayet" || 1.137 ||

_api ca_ |

	**jalaṃ piben nāñjalinā śayānaṃ na prabodhayet |**

**	nakṣaiḥ krīḍeta dharmaghnair vyādhitaiś ca na saṃviśet || 1.138 ||**

savyadakṣiṇau hastau yuktāv añjaliḥ | tena jalaṃ na pibet | śayānaṃ nidritaṃ na prabodhayet | akṣair na krīḍet | dharmaghnaiḥ patitādibhir vyādhitaiś ca puruṣaiḥ saha na saṃviśet | atra ca saṃveśanaṃ saṃkaropalakṣaṇārtham | ata eva manuḥ |

	na saṃviśeta patitair na caṇḍālair na pukkasaiḥ |

	na mūrkhair nāvaliptaiś ca nāntyair nāntyavasāyibhiḥ ||

	sahāsanaṃ bhojanaṃ ca patitaiḥ saha varjayet |

	upapātakibhiś cānyaiḥ kurvadbhiḥ karma ninditam ||

krīḍāgrahaṇaṃ vyasanamātropalakṣaṇārtham | tathā ca manuḥ |

	na nṛtyen naiva gāyec ca na vāditrāṇi vādayet |

	nāsphoṭayen na kṣveḍec ca na ca raktaṃ virāgayet ||

raktam anuraktam | aniṣiddhe 'rthe na virāgayet | virāgayuktaṃ na kuryād ity arthaḥ | tathā |

	na kurvīta vṛthā ceṣṭāṃ na vāryañjalinā pibet |

	notsaṅge bhakṣayed bhakṣyaṃ na jātu syāt kutūhalī ||

nityayoge 'tiśaye vā pratyayaḥ || 1.138 ||

_kiṃ ca_ |

	**viruddhaṃ varjayet karma pretadhūmaṃ nadītaram |**

**	keśabhasmāṅgārajalakapāleṣu na saṃsthitam || 1.139 ||**

**[183]**

āyurārodyādiviruddhaṃ karma pretadhūmaṃ nadītaraṇaṃ ca keśādiṣv avasthānaṃ ca varjayet | manuḥ |

	bālātapaṃ pretadhūmaṃ varjyaṃ bhinnaṃ tathasanam |

	na cchindyān nakharomāṇi dantair notpāṭayen nakhān ||

	na mṛlloṣṭaṃ na mṛdnīyān na chindyat karajais tṛṇam |

	na karma niṣphalaṃ kuryān nāyatyām asukhodayam ||

	loṣṭamardī tṛṇacchedī nakhakhādī ca yo naraḥ |

	sa vināśaṃ vrajaty āśu sūcako 'sucir eva ca ||

āyatiḥ pariṇāmaḥ | karmaśabdenatra saṃkalpa ucyate | tasya niṣphalatāṃ mithyātvaṃ saṃkalpitānuṣṭhānarūpaṃ na kuryāt | loṣṭamardanādiṣu tācchīlyaṃ varjyam | tathā |

	na saṃhatābhyāṃ pāṇibhyāṃ kaṇḍūyetātmanaḥ śiraḥ |

	na spṛśec cainad ucchiṣṭo na ca snyāyad vinā tataḥ ||

tataḥ śirasā vinety arthaḥ |

	keśagrahān prahārāṃś ca śirasy etāni varjayet |

	śiraḥsnātaś ca tailena nāṅgaṃ kiṃcid upaspṛśet ||

tailena śiraḥsnātas tenaiva tailena nāṅgaṃ kiṃcid upaspṛśed ity anvayaḥ | atha vānyenāpi tailena tad ahar aṅgaṃ nopaspṛśet | viṣṇuḥ: "na saṃhatābhyāṃ pāṇibhyāṃ śira udaraṃ ca kaṇḍūyeta" | nadītaraṇaṃ cātra bāhubhyāṃ sāṃśayikaplavena [ca] varjayet | tathā ca manuḥ: "na bahubhyāṃ nadīṃ taret" | vasiṣṭhaḥ: "nāvaṃ ca sāṃśayikīṃ nādhirohet" | manuḥ |

	adhitiṣṭhen na keśāṃś ca bhasmāsthikapālikāḥ |

	na kārpāsāsthi na tuṣān dīrgham āyur jijīviṣuḥ ||

tathā |

	udvartanam apasthānaṃ (?) bhaktaṃ viṇmūram eva ca |

	śleṣmaniṣṭhyūtavāntāni nādhitiṣṭhet tu kāmataḥ ||

viṣṇuḥ: "na catuṣpatham adhitiṣṭhen na rātrau vṛkṣamūlaṃ na śūnyālayaṃ na sūnābandhanāgāram" | gautamaḥ: "amedhyaṃ nadhitiṣṭhet" | śaṅkhalikhitau: "nāheḥ padam adhitiṣṭhet | na tṛṇaśarkarākūṭeṣu tiṣṭhet" | padaṃ sathānam | **[184]** āpastambaḥ: "pāṇisamūhaṃ brāhmaṇasya nāprokṣitam adhitiṣṭhet" | brāhmaṇena pāṇinopaliptam aprokṣitaṃ nadhitiṣṭhed ity arthaḥ || 1.139 ||

_kiṃ ca_ |

	**nācakṣīta dhayantīṃ gāṃ nādvāreṇa viśet kvacit |**

**	na rājñaḥ pratigṛhṇīyāl lubdhasyocchāśtravartinaḥ || 1.140 ||**

dhayantīṃ vatsaṃ pāyayantīṃ gāṃ parasmai nācakṣīta na kathayet | dvāraṃ vihāya grāmaṃ na praviśet | lubdhasya sati dhane vyayam akurvāṇasyocchāstravartino 'tikrāntaśāstrasya ca rājño dhanaṃ na pratigṛhṇīyāt | baudhāyanaḥ: "gāṃ pāyayantīṃ na parsmai brūyāt" | manuḥ |

	advāreṇa ca nātīyād grāmaṃ vā veśma vāvṛtam | 

gautamaḥ: "na mlecchāśucyadhārmikaiḥ saha saṃbhāṣeta | saṃbhāṣya puṇyakṛto manasā dhyāyet | brāhmaṇena saha vā saṃbhāṣeta | adhenuṃ dhenuṃbhavyeti brūyāt | abhadraṃ bhadram iti brūyāt | kapālaṃ bhagālam iti | maṇidhanur itīndradhanuḥ | gāṃ dhayantīṃ parasmai nācakṣīta | na caināṃ vārayet" | viṣṇuḥ: "na parakṣetre carantīṃ gām ācakṣīta notpātaṃ pradarśayet" | manuḥ: "kulākulaṃ rahasyārthaṃ saṃcaren nānimittitaḥ" | kulaṃ gṛham | vasiṣṭhaḥ: "nāvṛto yajñaṃ gacched yadi vrajet pradakṣiṇaṃ punar āvrajet" | gautamaḥ: "na yajñam avṛto gacched darśanāya tu kāmam" | manuḥ: "namaskartuṃ vrajet kāmaṃ didṛkṣur yajñakarma vā" || 1.140 ||

	**pratigrahe sūnicakridhvajiveśyānarādhipāḥ |**

**	duṣṭā daśaguṇaṃ pūrvāt pūrvād ete yathottaram || 1.141 ||**

pratigrahaviṣaye sūniprabhṛtīnāṃ yo ya uttaraḥ sa pūrvasmād daśaguṇadoṣo bhavati | **[185]** atas tatpratigraho daśaguṇadoṣo bhavati | atas tatpratigrahaṃ varjayet | sūnā prāṇivadhasthānam, tadvān sūnī prāṇighatakaḥ | cakrī tailikaḥ | dhvajī surāvikrayī | parahṛdayaṃ vivaśayatīti veśyā | yad vā veśena jīvatīti veśyā | veśaḥ śṛṅgāraḥ | narādhipo rājā | sa ca pūrvoktaviśeṣaṇa eva duṣṭaḥ, tadīyasya pratigrahasya niṣiddhatvāt | tathā ca manuḥ |

	daśa sūnāsahasrāṇi yo vāhayati saunikaḥ |

	tena tulyaḥ smṛto rājā ghoras tasya pratigrahaḥ ||

	yo rājñaḥ pratigṛhṇāti lubdhasyocchāśtravartinaḥ |

	sa paryāyeṇa yātīmān narakān ekaviṃśatim ||

	tāmisram andhatāmisraṃ mahārauravarauravau |

	narakaṃ kālasūtraṃ ca mahānarakam eva ca ||

	saṃjīvanaṃ mahāvīciṃ tāpanaṃ saṃpratāpanam |

	saṃghātaṃ ca sakākolaṃ kuḍmalaṃ pūtimṛttikam ||

	lohaśaṅkum ṛbīsaṃ ca panthānaṃ śalmalāṃ nadīm |

	asipatravanaṃ caiva lohacārakam eva ca ||

	etad vidanto vidvāṃso brāhmaṇā brahmavādinaḥ |

	na rājñaḥ praigṛhṇanti pretya śreyo'bhikāṅkṣiṇaḥ || 1.141 ||

_adhyayanavidhyaṅgāny āha_ |

	**adhyāyānām upākarma śrāvaṇyāṃ śravaṇena vā |**

**	hastenauṣadhibhāve vā pañcamyāṃ śrāvaṇasya tu || 1.142 ||**

adhītanta iti adhyāyāḥ svādhyāyāḥ | teṣāṃ saṃskārakam upākarmākhyaṃ karma śrāvaṇyāṃ paurṇamāsyāṃ kāryam | candramasā yuktaḥ śravaṇo nakṣatraṃ yasyāṃ sā śrāvaṇī | atha vā śravaṇe nakṣatre saptamyarthe śravaṇaśabdād enapratyayaḥ | atha vā śrāvaṇasya pañcamyāṃ haste nakṣatre copākarma kāryam oṣadhibhāve sati | oṣadhīnāṃ vrīhiprabhrtīnāṃ bhavaḥ prādurbhāvo 'ṅkurodaya iti yāvat | etac ca viśeṣaṇaṃ śrāvaṇīśravaṇayor api grāhyam | yadā śrāvaṇyāṃ na prādurbhāvas tadā bhādrapadaśravaṇena kāryam | atra manuḥ |

**[186]**	śrāvaṇyāṃ prauṣṭhapadyāṃ vāpy upākṛtya yathāvidhi |

	yuktaś chandāṃsy adhīyīta māsān vipro 'rdhapañcamān ||

dhandāṃsy upākṛtya tān eva pañcamān eva māsān adhīyīta | ardhaḥ pañcamo maso yeṣāṃ te tathoktāḥ | upākarmaprabhṛti sārdhāṃś caturo māsāñ śuklakṛṣṇapakṣeṣu nirantaraṃ svādhyāyam adhīyītety arthaḥ | purāṇāt |

	upākarmaṇi cotsarge yathākālaṃ sametya ca |

	ṛṣīn darbhamayān kṛtvā pūjayet tarpayet tataḥ ||

tathā |

	gautamādin ṛṣīn sapta kṛtvā darbhamayān dvijaḥ |

	pūjayitvā yathāśakti tarpayed ṛcam uddharet ||

gṛhasthasyāpi grahaṇādhyayanādhikāraṃ jñāpayituṃ tatprakaraṇe 'dhyayanavidhiḥ | ata eva śaunakaḥ: "samavṛtto brahmacārikalpena yathānyāyam itare | jāyopeyety eke" iti || 1.142 ||

_utsarjanavidhim āha_ |

	**pauṣamasasya rohiṇyām aṣṭakāyām athāpi vā |**

**	jalānte chandasāṃ kuryād utsargaṃ vidhivad bahiḥ|| 1.143 ||**

puṣyeṇa yuktā paurṇamāsī pauṣī sā yasmin māsi sa pauṣaḥ | tasya rohiṇyāṃ candrayuktāyāṃ tasyaiva cāṣṭakāyāṃ kṛṣṇāṣṭamyām ity arthaḥ | jalānte jalasaṃnidhau grāhmād bahiś chandasāṃ vedānām utsargaṃ parityāgaṃ kuryāt | atra chandobhis tadadhyayanaṃ lakṣyate | yena prakāreṇopākarmaprabhṛti śuklakṛṣṇapakṣeṣu vedādhyayanaṃ kṛtaṃ tatprakāram idānīṃ parityajet, na tu sarvātmanā | ata eva manuḥ |

	ataḥ paraṃ tu chandāṃsi śukleṣu niyataḥ paṭhet |

	vedāṅgāni rahasyaṃ ca kṛṣṇapakṣeṣu saṃpaṭhet ||

ity utsargānantaraṃ karmādhyayane prakārāntaram uktavān | utsargaś ca yathāvidhi yathāgṛhyaśāstrāt kartavyaḥ | atra ca manuḥ |

	puṣye tu chandasāṃ kuryād bahir utsarjanaṃ dvijaḥ |

	māghaśuklasya vā prāpte pūrvāhṇe prathame 'hani ||

śrāvaṇyāṃ yady upākaraṇaṃ tadotsarjanaṃ pauṣasya śuklapratipadi pūrvāhṇe | atha proṣṭhapadyāṃ tadā māghasya || 1.143 ||

**[187]**

_upākarmaṇy utsarge ca kṛte 'dhyayanakālavidhiśeṣatvena dinaviśeṣaparyudasam āha_ |

	**tryahaṃ preteṣv anadhyāyaḥ śiṣyartviggurubandhuṣu |**

**	upākarmaṇi cotsarge svaśakhāśrotriye tathā || 1.144 ||**

tryaham ahorātratrayam anadhyāyo 'dhyayanavarjanaṃ kāryam | atra nimittaṃ śiṣyartviggurubandhuṣu preteṣv iti | gurur ācāryo grāhyaḥ | tathā ca manuḥ |

	trirātram āhur āśaucam ācārye saṃsthite sati | iti |

bandhavo 'trāsapiṇḍāḥ, sapiṇḍeṣu daśāhādividhānāt | upākarmotsargayoḥ kṛtayos trirātram anadhyāya ity anuṣaṅgaḥ | manus tūtsarge pakṣiṇīm ekāhaṃ trirātraṃ ca vikalpenānadhyāyam āha |

	yathāśāstraṃ tu kṛtvaivam utsargaṃ vidhivad bahiḥ |

	viramet pakṣiṇīṃ rātriṃ yad vāpy ekam aharniśam || iti |

svaśākhāyāḥ śrotriyo 'dhyetari mṛte tathā tryaham anadhyāya ity arthaḥ | āpastambaḥ: "śrāvaṇyāṃ paurṇamāsyām anadhyāyam upākṛtya māsaṃ pradoṣe nādhīyīta | tathā pravacanayukto varṣāśaradaṃ mauthunaṃ varjayet | tathopākaraṇādi | ā utsarjanād adhyāpayitur niyamo lobhasaṃharaṇaṃ māṃsaṃ śrāddhaṃ maithunaṃ varjayet | ṛtāv eva jāyāṃ yāyāt" | samāvṛttaviṣayam etat | ata eva śaunakaḥ: "adhīyīta samāvṛtto brahmacārikalpena yathānyāyam itare jāyopeyety eke, prājāpatyaṃ tat" iti | tajjāyopagamanaṃ prājāpatyam ity arthaḥ || 1.144 ||

**[188]**

_kiṃ ca_ |

	**saṃdhyāgarjitanirghātabhūkampolkānipātane |**

**	samāpya vedaṃ dyuniśam āraṇyakam adhītya ca || 1.145 ||**

sāyaṃ prātaḥ saṃdhyayor meghadhvanāv asaṃdhyayor api nirghāte bhūmicalana ulkāpāte vedādhyayanaṃ samāpyāraṇyakavedabhāgaṃ cādhītya dyuniśam ahorātram anadhyāyaḥ kāryaḥ | hārītaḥ: "sāyaṃsaṃdhyāstanite rātriṃ nādhīyīran | prātaḥsaṃdhyāstanite cāhorātram" | āpastambaḥ: "saṃdhāvanu stanite rātrim | svapnaparyantaṃ vidyuti | upavyuṣaṃ yāvatā gāṃ kṛṣṇāṃ rohiṇīm iti śamyāprāsād vijānīyād etasmin kāle vidyotamāne sapradoṣam ahar anadhyāyaḥ | dahre 'pararātre stanayitnunā | ūrdhvam ardharātrād ity eke" | asyārthaḥ: saṃdhāvanu ahorātrasaṃdhilakṣite kāle stanite meghadhvanau rātrim antarāṃ nadhīyīta | svapnaparyantaṃ svapnavarjanāntaṃ yāvat | ānyāyyād utthānād ity arthaḥ | upavyuṣam apavyuṣasi vidyuti dyotamānāyām | atha vā śamyāprāsaparimite deśe sthitā gauḥ kṛṣṇā lohiteti vā vijñāyate | yadāpararātre dyotamānāyāṃ vidyuti pradoṣasahitam ahar anadhyāyaḥ | dahre 'lpe 'pararātre stanayitnunā gargitena nimittena sapradoṣam ahar anadhyāyaḥ | atha vordhvam ardharātrāt stanayitnau jāte sapradoṣam ahar anadhyāya iti | manus tu nirghāgādiṣv ākālikam anadhyāyam āha |

	nirghāte bhūmicalane jyotiṣāṃ cāpasarjane |

	etān ākālikān vidyād anadhyāyān ṛtāv api ||

ṛtāv api varṣāsv apīty arthaḥ | ākāliko nimittasamayaparyantaḥ | tathā |

	cauraur upaplute grāme saṃbhrame cāgnikārite |

	ākālikam anadhyāyaṃ vidyāt sarvādbhuteṣu ca || iti |

tataś cākālikāhorātrayor vikalpaḥ | evaṃ kalpāntareṣv api | yamaḥ |

	śakradhvajanimitteṣu ulkāpāte tathaiva ca |

	anadhyāyas trirātraṃ tu bhūmikampe tathaiva ca || **[189]**

vasiṣṭhaḥ: "ulkāvidyutsamāse trirātram ulkāvidyutsajyotiṣam apartāv ākālikam" | ulkāyāṃ vasante varṣāsu vidyuti dṛṣṭāyām sajyotiṣam anadhyāyaḥ | divety arthaḥ | apartāv uktād ṛttor anyatra vidyuty ulkāyāṃ vā dyotamānāyām akālike dvitīye 'hani darśanakālaṃ yāvad anadhyāyāḥ kartavya ity arthaḥ || 1.145 ||

_api ca_ |

	**pañcadaśyāṃ caturdaśyām aṣṭamyāṃ rāhusūtake |**

**	ṛtusaṃdhiṣu bhuktvā vā śrāddikaṃ pratigṛhya vā || 1.146 ||**

śuklakṛṣṇayoḥ pakṣayoḥ pañcadaśyāṃ caturdaśyām aṣṭamyāṃ ca tathā rāhusūtake candrasūryopagāga ṛtusaṃdhiṣu ṛtūnāṃ vasantādīnāṃ parasparasaṃdhiṣu śrāddhikaṃ bhuktvā pratigṛhya cāhorātram anadhāyaḥ kāryaḥ | rāhusūtakaṃ rāhudarśanam | śrāddhasaṃbaddhaṃ śrāddhikam | tatpakvaṃ bhuktvāmaṃ ca pratigṛhyāhorātraṃ nādhīyīta | nṛsiṃhapurāṇāt |

	mahānavamyāṃ dvādaśyāṃ bharaṇyām api caiva hi |

	tathākṣatatṛtīyāyāṃ śiṣyān nādhyāpayed dvijaḥ ||

	māghamāse tu saptamyāṃ rathākhyāyāṃ tu varjayet |

	nīyamānaṃ śavaṃ dṛṣṭvā mahīsthaṃ vā dvijottamaḥ ||

mahānavamī, aśvayukśuklapakṣasya | mahādvādaśī kārtikaśukapakṣasya | bharaṇī proṣṭhapadyanantarā | akṣatatṛtīyā vaiśākhaśuklapakṣasya | rathākhyā saptamī māghaśuklapakṣasya | nādhīyītey anuvṛttau gautamaḥ: "kārtikīphālgunyāṣādhīpaurṇamasīs tisro 'ṣṭakās trirātram anatyām eke" | uktapaurṇamāsīprabhṛtitrirātram ity arthaḥ | aṣṭakāśabdenāṣṭakākarmāṅgabhūtaṃ saptamyāditrirātram upalakṣyate | antyāṣṭakā māghī | tām evānadhyayananimittām eka āhuḥ | pāiṭhīnasiḥ: "pauṣaprabhṛtayaḥ kṛṣṇe bhavā tisro 'ṣṭakā mārgaśīrṣaprabhṛtaya ity eke" | śaunakas tu: "hemantaśiśirayoś caturṇām aparapakṣāṇām aṣṭamīṣv aṣṭakāḥ" ity āha | śātātapaḥ: 

	pañcadaśyāṃ caturdaśyām aṣṭakāsu mahotsave |

	pradoṣe ca trayodaśyām aṣṭamyāṃ pratipady api || **[190]**

	medhākāmas trayodaśyāṃ caturdaśyāṃ ca sarvadā |

	saptamyāṃ ca pradoṣeṣu na smaren nāpi kīrtayet ||

manuḥ |

	pratigṛhya dvijo vidyān ekoddiṣṭasya ketanam |

	tryahaṃ na kīrtayed brahma rājño rāhoś ca sūtake ||

	yāvad ekānudiṣṭasya gandho lepaś ca tiṣṭhati |

	viprasya viduṣo dehe tāvad brahma na kīrtayet ||

ketanaṃ nimantraṇam | ekānudiṣṭam ekoddiṣṭam | evaṃ ca rāhusūtaka ekāhatrirātrayor vikalpaḥ | rāhusūtakaṃ rāhudarśanam | ata eva hārītaḥ: "upādhyāye rājani ca mṛte śrotriye ca mṛte sabrahmacāriṇi ca candrārakayo rāhudarśane śakradhvajapatana ācārye ca mṛte trirātram" iti || 1.146 ||

_kiṃ ca_ |

	**paśumaṇḍūkanakulaśvāhimārjāramūṣakaiḥ |**

**	kṛte 'ntare tv ahorātraṃ śakrapāte tathōcchraye || 1.147 ||**

antaraṃ śiṣyopādhyāyayor madhyato gamanam | tasmin paśumaṇḍūkadibhiḥ kṛte 'horātram anadhyāyaḥ | madhyagamanāt prabhṛti sūryodayaṃ yāvad ity arthaḥ | tathā śakrapāte śakrocchāyopalakṣite kāle | proṣṭhapadyanantaraṃ bharaṇyāṃ śrakrapātaḥ | proṣṭhapadasyaiva śukladvādaśyāṃ śakrocchrāyaḥ | tad āha gargaḥ |

	siṃhaṃ gate dinakare sitacārupakṣe haryādyapādam upagacchati vai śaśāṅke |

	uttiṣṭhate vividhamandiravṛndavandyo yāmyāṃ tato diśi niṣīdati vajrapāṇiḥ || iti |

atra ca hariśabdena haridaivataṃ śravaṇam upalakṣyate | tad api ca pradarśanārtham | yataḥ sa evāha |

	dvādaśyāṃ tu site pakṣe māsi proṣṭhapade tathā |

	sakram utthāpayed rājā visvaśravaṇavāsave || iti |

viśvaśabdena vaiśvadevam uttarāṣāḍhānakṣatram upalakṣyate | vāsavaśabdena vasudaivataṃ dhaniṣṭhānakṣatram | tena dvādaśyām eva śakrocchrāyaḥ | gautamaḥ: **[191]** "antarāgamane punar upasadanam | śvanakulamaṇḍukamārjārāṇāṃ tryaham upavāso vipravāsaś ca | prāṇāyāmo ghṛtaprāśanaṃ cetareṣām | śmaśānādhyayane caivam" | yena kenacid antarā gamane kṛta upasadanaṃ kāryam | upasadanaṃ ca pāṇinā pāṇim upasaṃgṛhyetyādinā yat pratyahaṃ vihitaṃ tad eva punaḥ kartavyam | śvādyantarāgamane trirātram upavāsaḥ | tryahaṃ ca vivased iti | yat tu vasiṣṭhaḥ: "adhīyānānām antarāgamane 'horātram abhojanam | trirātram anabhiṣeko vivāsā(sa)ś cānyonyena śvamārjāranakulaśīghragāṇāṃ tv ahorātram" ity āha, tat trirātropavāsāsamarthaviṣayam | prāṇāyāmo ghṛtaprāśanaṃ cetareṣām iti | śvādivyatiriktānām antarāgamana ity arthaḥ || 1.147 ||

_kiṃ ca_ |

	**śvakroṣṭugardabholūkasāmabāṇārtaviḥsvane |**

**	amedhyaśavaśūdrāntyaśmaśānapatitāntike || 1.148 ||**

**	deśe 'śucāv ātmani ca vidyutstanitasaṃplave |**

**	bhuktvārdrapāṇir ambho'ntar ardharātre 'timārute || 1.149 ||**

**	pāṃsuvarṣe diśāṃ dāhe saṃdhyānīhārabhītiṣu |**

**	dhāvataḥ pūtigandhe ca śiṣṭe ca gṛham āgate || 1.150 ||**

**	kharoṣṭrayānahastyaśvanauvṛkṣeriṇarohaṇe |**

**	saptatriṃśad anadhyāyān etāṃs tātkālikān viduḥ || 1.151 ||**

śvādīnāṃ niḥsvane śabde śrūyamāṇe tatkālam anadhyāyaḥ | kroṣṭā gomāyuḥ | ulūko 'maṅgalyapakṣī | bāṇo vīṇāviśeṣaḥ | ārto duḥkhitaḥ | śvādayaḥ prasiddhāḥ | tathāmedhyādīnām antike saṃnidhāne | antyaḥ śudrān niṣkṛṣṭaḥ | tathā deśasyātmanaś cāśauce, tathā vidyutsaṃplave | saṃplavaḥ punaḥ punar bhavanam | tathā bhuktvā yāvad ārdrapāṇiḥ | tathāmbhaso madhye, ardharātre rātrer madhame yāmadvaye ca, tathātimārute 'tiśayena vāti vāyau | tathā pāṃsuvarṣe 'dbutaviśeṣe diśāṃ dāhe ca tathā saṃdhyayoḥ, tathā nīhāre dhūmikāyāṃ, bhītau ca caurādikṛtāyām | tathā ghāvato 'nadhyāyaḥ | tathā pūtigandhe, tathoktalakṣaṇe śiṣṭe gṛham āgate, kharādīnām ārohaṇe ca | yānaṃ rathādi | iriṇam ūṣaram | etāñ śvakroṣṭuprabhṛtiniḥsvanādinimittān saptatriṃśad andhāyāṃs tātkālikān nimittakāle kartavyān vidur munayaḥ | atra viśeṣaḥ | tathā manuḥ | 

**[192]**	sāmadhvanāv ṛgyajuṣī nādhīyīta kadācana |

anadhyāyānuvṛttau baudhāyanaḥ: "nṛtyagītavāditraruditaśabdeṣu tāvantaṃ kālam ārtau ca" | āpastambaḥ: "śmaśāne sarvataḥ śamyāprāsāt | śmaśānavac chūdrapatitau samānāgāra ity eke | śūdrāyāṃ tu prekṣaṇapratiprekṣaṇayor anadhyāyaḥ | brahmādhyeṣyamāṇo malavadvāsasecchan saṃbhāṣituṃ brāhmaṇena saṃbhāṣya tayā saṃbhāṣeta saṃbhāṣya tu brāhmaṇenaiva saṃbhāṣyādhīyīta" | yamaḥ |

	śleṣmāntakasya chāyāyāṃ śalmaler madhukasya ca |

	kadācid api nādhyeyaṃ kovidārakapitthayoḥ |

tathā |

	na saṃgrāme na senāyāṃ vivāde kalahe tathā |

hārītaḥ: "brāhmaṇāgamane 'rghyādīni datvānujñāpyādhīyīran" | tathā |

	na vṛkṣastho na tīrthastho na cāpsu na sabhāsu ca |

	bahusaṃkīrṇamadhe ca nādhīyīta kacācana ||

	śayānaḥ prauḍhapādaś ca kṛtvā caivāvasakthikām | \
	nādhīyītāmiṣaṃ jagdhvā sūtakānnādyam eva ca ||

tathā |

	śvakharoṣṭre ca rudati paṅktau na ca paṭhed dvijaḥ |

	nādhīyīta śmaśānānte grāmānte govraje 'pi vā ||

tathā |

	rudhire ca srute gātrāc chastreṇa ca parikṣate |

gautamaḥ: "ūrdhvaṃ bhojnād utsave prādhītasya niśāyāṃ caturmuhūrtaṃ nityam eke nagarotsave | upanayanād ūrdhvaṃ bhojanād ahorātram anadhyāyaḥ prādhītasyādhyayane prathamaṃ pravṛttasya bhojanād ūrdhvam anutsave 'pi pūrvavad anadhyāyaḥ" | niśāyāṃ caturmuhūrtam | etac ca trayodaśyām | tathā ca uśanā: "trayodaśyāṃ prathamāṃś caturo muhūrtān nādhīyīta" | tasyānadhyāya ity anuvṛttau vasiṣṭhaḥ: "mithunavyapetāyāṃ ca śayyāyāṃ vāsasā ca mithunavyapetenānirṇiktena" iti | sarve caite 'nadhyāyā dharmanaipuṇakāmena vidyānaipuṇakāmena ca varjanīyāḥ, pratyavāyāviśeṣāt | tathā ca yamaḥ |

**[193]**	chidrāny āhutir dvijātīnām adhyāyān manīṣiṇaḥ |

	chidrebhyaḥ sravati brahma brāhmaṇena yad arjitam ||

	āyuḥ prajāṃ paśūn medhāṃ kṛntāmi sukṛtaṃ ca yat |

	anadhyāyeṣv abhyasato brahma vyāharatas tathā ||

yat tu manuvacanam,

	dvāv eva varjayen nityam anadhyāyau prayatnataḥ |

	svādhyāyabhūmiṃ cāśuddhām ātmānaṃ cāśuciṃ dvijaḥ ||

iti, tad brahmayajñādhyayanaviṣayam, tatprakaraṇādhītavacanamūlatvāt | brahmayajñaṃ prakṛtya hi taittirīyakāḥ samāmananti: "tasya vā etasya yajñasya dvāv anadhyāyau yad ātmāśucir yad deśaḥ" iti || 1.148–151 ||

_evam anadhyāyān uktvā prakṛtam āha_ |

	**devartviksnātakācāryarājñāṃ chāyāṃ parastriyāḥ |**

**	nākrāmed raktaviṇmūtraṣṭhīvanodvartanāni ca || 1.152 ||**

devādīnāṃ chāyāṃ raktādīni ca nākrāmen nādhitiṣṭhet | ṛtvigācāryayoḥ snātakopādānenaiva grahaṇasiddhau pṛthagupādānāt snātakaśabdo 'cirasamāvṛtte vartate | yad vā ṛtvigācāryābhyām anyasnātakasya chāyāyām anākramaṇa(ṃ?) mantavyam | devā devapratimāḥ | ṣṭhīvanaṃ mukhapracyutaṃ lālādi | udvartanam aṅgotsādanadravyam | atra manuḥ |

	devatānāṃ guro rājñaḥ snātakācāryayos tathā |

	nākrāmet kāmataś chāyāṃ babhruṇo dīkṣitasya ca ||

babhru kapilaṃ gavādi yamaḥ |

	devadvijaguruprājñasnātakācāryamantriṇām |

	nākrāmet krāmataś chāyāṃ kapilasya ca guror api ||

	svāṃ tu nākrāmec chāyāṃ klībena patitena ca |

	caṇḍālena dviṣadbhiś ca nityaṃ rogānvitena ca ||

viṣṇuḥ: "brāhmaṇadevagurubandhudīkṣitānāṃ chāyāṃ nātikrāmet" | prasaṅgād anyad apy ucyate, tatra manuḥ |

	madhyaṃdine ca rātrau ca śrāddhaṃ bhuktvā ca sāmiṣam |

	saṃdhyayor ubhayoś caiva na seveta catuṣpatham || **[194]**

tathā |

	vairiṇaṃ nopaseveta sahāyāṃś caiva vairiṇaḥ |

	adhārmikaṃ taskaraṃ ca parasyaiva ca yoṣitam ||

śaṅkhalikhitau: "noddhatakuhakaiḥ sahaikatas tiṣṭhet" || 1.152 ||

_kiṃ ca_ |

	**viprāhikṣatriyātmāno nāvajñeyāḥ kathaṃcana |**

viprasarpakṣatriyā ātmā ca nāvamantavyāḥ | atra manuḥ |

	kṣatriyaṃ caiva sarpaṃ ca brāhmaṇaṃ ca bahuśrutam |

	nāvamanyeta vai bhūṣṇuḥ kṛśān api kadācana ||

	etat trayaṃ hi puruṣān nirdahaty avamānitam |

	tasmād etat trayaṃ nityaṃ nāvamanyeta buddhimān ||

	nātmānam avamanyeta pūrvābhir asamṛddhibhiḥ |

	ātmānaṃ na śaped roṣān nirukko na svaped divā ||

	na naktaṃ vilikhed bhūmiṃ gāś ca rātrau na saṃspṛśet ||

tathā |

	brāhmaṇān nṛpatīn vṛddhān svāṃś ca śāntāñ śiśūn api |

	nākrośen nāvamanyeta pūjayed daivataṃ tathā ||

kiṃ ca |

	**ā mṛtyoḥ śriyam ākāṅkṣen na kiṃcin marmaṇi spṛśet || 1.153 ||**

yāvajjīvaṃ sriyam anvicchet | tataś ca tāṃ durlabhāṃ matvā tadupāyānuṣṭhāne mandādareṇa na bhavitavyam iti tātparyārthaḥ | tathā ca kam api śatrum udāsīnaṃ vā marmaṇi na spṛśet | paradoṣaprakāśanaṃ varjayed ity arthaḥ | tathā ca manuḥ |

	hīnāṅgān atiriktāṅgān vidyāhīnān vayo'tigān |

	rūpadraviṇahīnāṃś ca jātihīnāṃś ca nākṣipet || 1.153 ||

_api ca_ |

	**dūrād ucchiṣṭaviṇmūtrapādāmbhāṃsi samutsṛjet |**

dūrato gṛhād ucchiṣṭādīni prakṣipet ||

_kiṃ ca_ |

	**śrutismṛtyuditaṃ samyaṅ nityam ācāram ācaret || 1.154 ||**

tathācāro nāma laukikakarmāśrayaḥ puruṣaniḥśreyasopakārasya vidhiḥ **[195]** pratiṣedho vā | tatra śrutivihitā ācārā golakṣaṇaprabhṛtayaḥ | yathā kartarī karṇakartavya ityādayaḥ | ācāraviṣayāṇi tu smṛtivākyāni pradarśyante | tatra vyāsaḥ |

	śrīkāmaḥ sarvadā snānaṃ kurvītāmalakair naraḥ |

	saptamīṃ pañcamīṃ caiva parvakālaṃ vivarjayet ||

parvātrāmāvāsyā | yad āha sa eva |

	amāvāsyānavamyoś ca saptamyāṃ ca viśeṣataḥ |

	dhātrīphalāni yatnena dūrataḥ parivarjayet ||

dhātrī — āmalakī | tathā |

	saptamyāṃ na spṛśet tailaṃ nīlavastraṃ na dharayet |

	na dhātryāmalakaiḥ snāyān na kuryāt kalahaṃ naraḥ ||

	vīryahāniḥ prajāhānir yaśohānis tathaiva ca |

	hanty etat tritayaṃ yasmāt tasmād dhātrīṃ vivarjayet ||

tathā |

	ṣaṣṭhy aṣṭamī pañcamī pakṣadvayacaturdaśī |

	atra saṃnihitaṃ pāpaṃ taile māṃse kṣure bhage ||

	ṣaṣṭyāṃ tailam anāyuṣyam aṣṭamyāṃ piśitaṃ tathā |

	caturdarśyāṃ kāmabhogam amāvāsyā kṣurakriyā ||

	māṃsāśane pañcadaśī tailābhyaṅge caturdaśī |

	aṣṭamī grāmyadharme ca jvalantam api pātayet ||

grāmyadharmo maithunam |

	tailaṃ na saṃspṛśed āmaṃ vṛkṣādīṃś chedayen na ca |

	pakṣādau ca ravau ṣaṣṭhyāṃ viriktāyāṃ tathā tithau ||

	daśamyāṃ tailam apṛṣṭvā na snāyād avicakṣaṇaḥ |

	catvāri tasya naśyanti āyuḥ prajñā yaśo dhanam ||

	mohāt pratipadaṃ ṣaṣṭhīṃ kuhūṃ raktāṃ tathā tithim |

	tailenābhyajyamānas tu caturbhir apahīyate ||

	pañcamīṃ daśamīṃ caiva paurṇamāsīṃ trayodaśīm |

	tṛtīyāṃ caiva yas tailaṃ naraḥ samupasevate ||

	abhyaṅgāt sparśanād vāpi bhakṣaṇāc ca tathaiva ca |

	caturṇāṃ tasya vṛddhiḥ syād dhanāpatyabalāyuṣām || **[198]**

vṛddhamanuḥ |

	āhāraṃ maithunaṃ nidrāṃ saṃdhyākāle vivarjayet |

	karma vādhyayanaṃ vāpi tathā dānapratigrahau ||

	āhārād vyādhim āpnoti garbho raudraś ca maithunāt |

	svapanaḥ syād alakṣmīkaḥ karma caivātra niṣphalam ||

	adhyetā narakaṃ yāti dānān nāpnoti tatphalam |

	pratigrahī bhavet pāpī tasmāt saṃdhyāsu varjayet ||

śātātapaḥ |

	amā vai somavāreṇa ravivāreṇa saptamī |

	caturthī bhaumavāreṇa viṣuvatsadṛśaṃ phalam ||

	amāvāsyā bhaved vāro yadā bhūmisutasya vai |

	jāhnavīsnānamātreṇa gosahasraphalaṃ bhavet ||

vṛddhavasiṣṭhaḥ |

	sarveṣām eva varṇānāṃ sūtakaṃ rāhudarśane |

	sacailaṃ ca bhavet snānaṃ sūtakānnaṃ ca varjayet ||

sūtakānnaṃ rāhusūtakānnam | tathā |

	tridaśāḥ sparśasamaye tṛpyanti pitaras tathā |

	manuṣyā madhyakāle ca mokṣakāle ca rākṣasāḥ ||

sparśakāla eva devapitṛdai(de)vatyaṃ karma kuryād ity arthaḥ | tathā |

	pracchannāni ca dānāni jñānaṃ ca nirahaṃkṛtam |

	tapāṃsi ca suguptāni teṣāṃ phalam anantakam ||

tathā |

	ekā gauḥ svasthacittasya āturasya ca yacchatam |

	sahasraṃ mriyamānasya tac ca tāni ca tatsamam ||

tathā |

	kanakāśvatilā nāgā dāsīgṛhamahīrathāḥ |

	kanyakā kapilā ceti mahādānāni vai daśa ||

	datvā yo 'nusmared dānaṃ pratigṛhya ca yācate |

	ubhau tau narakaṃ yātaḥ pratigrāhakayācakau ||

anusmaraṇaṃ paścāttāpaḥ | tathā |

	sarvatra guṇavaddānaṃ śvapākādiṣv api sthitam |

	deśe kāle vidhānena pātre dattaṃ viśeṣataḥ ||

**[199]**	asato 'pi samādāya sādhubhyo yaḥ prayacchati |

	dhanasvāminam ātmānaṃ sa tārayati dustarāt ||

tathā |

	dvāv evāpsu praveṣṭavau gale baddhvā mahāśilām |

	dhanavantam adātāraṃ daridraṃ cātapasvinam ||

tathā |

	upāvṛttasya pāpebhyo yas tu vāso guṇaiḥ saha |

	upavāsaḥ sa vijñeyaḥ sarvabhogavivarjitaḥ ||

	puṣpālaṃkāravastrāṇi gandhamālyānulepanam |

	upavāse na duṣyet tu dantadhāvanavarjitam ||

	upavāse tathā śrāddhe na khāded dantadhāvanam |

	dantānāṃ kāṣṭhasaṃyogo hanti sapta kulāni vai ||

tataś ca patrādinopavāse dantadhāvanaṃ kāryam | śrāddhe bhoktā ca na tu kāṣṭhena | devalaḥ |

	brahmacaryaṃ tathā śaucaṃ satyam āmiṣavarjanam |

	vrateṣv etāni catvāri variṣṭhānīti niścayaḥ ||

	strīṇāṃ tu pre(vī)kṣanāt sparśāt tābhiḥ saṃkathanād api |

	niṣyandate brahmacaryaṃ na dāreṣv ṛtusaṃkramāt ||

atrāyam arthaḥ: strīṇāṃ parastrīṇāṃ vīkṣaṇāt svabhāvena cittenety arthaḥ | tābhir anyastrībhir eva saṃkathanāt saṃyogapralāpāc ca brahmacaryaṃ daśamyādyupavāsanimittaṃ niṣyandate naśyatīty arthaḥ | na dāreṣv ṛtusaṃkramād iti | dāreṣu vīkṣaṇāt sparśāt saṃkathanāt svagṛhavyavahārakathāprapañcāc ca tad brahmacaryaṃ na naśyati, tathartusaṃkramāt | saṃkramaṇaṃ saṃtānotpādanārthaṃ saṃbhoga ṛtoḥ saṃkramas tasmād api vratādau sevyamānād brahmacaryaṃ na niṣyandate na naśyatīti | svadāreṣu vīkṣaṇāder brahmacaryaniṣyandābhāva upavāseṣv asidhārāvratanimittatvād iti |

	asakṛjjalapānāc ca tāmbūlasya ca bhakṣaṇāt |

	upavāsaḥ praduṣyet tu divā svāpāc ca maithunāt ||

maithunaṃ cātrartukālavyatiriktaviṣayam |

	sāyam ādyantayor ahnoḥ sāyaṃ prātaś ca madhyame |

	dharmopavāsī kurvīta naiva bhakacatuṣṭayam ||

dharmagrahaṇaṃ prāyaścittasya vyudāsārtham |

**[200]**	daśamyām ekabhaktas tu māṃsamaithunavarjitaḥ |

	ekādaśyām upavaset pakṣayor ubhayor api ||

	gṛhītvaudumbaraṃ pātraṃ vāripūrṇam udaṅmukhaḥ |

	upavāsaṃ tu gṛhṇīyād yad vā saṃkalpayed budhaḥ ||

	devatās tasya tuṣyanti kāmitaṃ tasya sidhyati |

	anyathā tu vṛthā martyāḥ kliśyanti svalpabuddhayaḥ ||

audumbaraṃ tāmram | yad vopavāsād anyad vrataṃ saṃkalpayed ity arthaḥ |

	ekādaśyāṃ nirāhāro bhūtvāham apare 'hani |

	bhokṣyāmi puṇḍarīkākṣaḥ gatir mama bhavācyuta ||

purāṇāt |

	keśavo mārgaśīrṣe syāt pauṣe nārāyaṇaḥ smṛtaḥ |

	mādhavo māghamāse tu govindaḥ phālgune tathā ||

	caitre māse bhaved viṣṇur vaiśākhe madhusūdanaḥ |

	trivikramo jyeṣṭhamāsa āṣāḍhe vāmano bhavet ||

	śrāvaṇe śrīdharo jñeyo kṛṣīkeśas tataḥ param |

	padmanābhaś cāśvayuje tato dāsodaro mataḥ ||

	sarveṣv eva tu maseṣu narakārir malimluce |

	śrīr vai vāgīśvarīkāntākriyāśaktivibhūtayaḥ ||

	icchā prītī ratiś caiva māyā dhīr mahimeti ca |

	etābhiḥ śaktibhiḥ śukladvāsaśīṣu saha kramāt ||

	vāsudevo dvādaśasu pūjanīya upoṣitaiḥ |

	tathaiva kṛṣṇapakṣe tu śaktiyukto 'rcyate dvijaiḥ ||

	kṛṣṇo 'nanto 'cyutaś cakrī vaikuṇṭho 'tha janārdanaḥ |

	upendro yajñapuruṣo vāsudevas tathā hariḥ ||

	yogīśvaro dvādaśamaḥ(kaḥ) puṇḍarīkākṣa eva ca |

	rukmiṇī ca priyā prītiḥ śaktiḥ siddhiś ca pañcamī ||

	tathā śrīr mahimā lakṣmīḥ kāntiś ca navamī matā |

	prāptiḥ prākāmyasaṃjñā ca laghimā dvādaśī smṛtā ||

tathā |

	uccārayed vratasyānte devasya purataḥ sthitaḥ |

	ajñānatimirāndhasya vratenānena keśava ||

**[201]**	prasādābhimukho bhūtvā jñānacakṣuḥprado bhava |

	yaj janmanaḥ prabhṛti dehalayāntam ajñaḥ pāpaṃ karomi vapuṣā manasā ca vācā |

	kleśopatāpitamatis tripadais trirūpaṃ tan nāśayācyuta mama vratasuprasanna ||

	ajñānāndhena yat kiṃcin mayā khaṇḍaṃ vrataṃ kṛtam |

	bhagavaṃs tvatprasādena tad akhaṇḍam ihāstu me ||

	yathākhaṇḍaṃ jagat sarvaṃ tvam eva puruṣottama |

	tathā khaṇḍam akhaṇḍaṃ me vrataṃ bhavatu keśava || iti |

tathā |

	na śaṅkhena pibet toyaṃ nāśnīyāt kūrmasūkarau |

	ekādaśyāṃ na bhuñjīta pakṣayor ubhayor api ||

etat putravadgṛhivyatiriktaviṣayam | yata uktaṃ smṛtyantare |

	kṛṣṇapakṣe tu saṃkrāntyāṃ grahaṇe vāpi putravān |

	upavāsaṃ na kurvīta sutabandhudhanakṣayāt ||

matsyapurāṇāt |

	dinakṣaye 'rkasaṃkrāntyāṃ grahaṇe candrasūryayoḥ |

	upavāsaṃ na kurvīta putrapautrasamanvitaḥ ||

kūrmapurāṇāt |

	saṃkrāntyāṃ kṛṣṇapakṣe ca raviśukradine tathā |

	ekādaśyāṃ na kurvīta upavāsaṃ sapāraṇam || 

ityādi | yat tu,

	brahmahā sa surāpaḥ syāt svasteyī gurutalpagaḥ |

	vivecayati yo mohād ekādaśyau sitāsite ||

iti purāṇavacanam, yat tu (cca) viṣṇudharmottare,

	atikrāmati yo mohād ekādaśyāu sitāsite |

	upavāse sa mūḍhātmā viṣṇulokaṃ na paśyati ||

iti, yac ca matsyapurāṇam,

	ekādaśyāṃ nirāhāro yo bhuṅkte dvāsaśīdine |

	śukle vā yadi vā kṛṣṇe tadvrataṃ vaiṣṇavaṃ mahat ||

iti, tat putravadgṛhasthavyatiriktaviṣayam | yathā kṛṣṇaikādaśyādau putravato gṛhasthasyānadhikāraḥ, tathā dinakṣaye 'pi | tad uktaṃ kūrmapurāṇe |

**[202]**	dvau tithyantāv ekavāre yasmin syāt sa dinakṣayaḥ |

	tasmin snānaṃ japo homo nopavāso gṛhāśrame ||

prakrāntaikādaśīvratasyāsāmarthye varāhapurāṇam |

	asāmarthye śarīrasya vrate ca samupasthite |

	kāreyed dharmapatnīṃ vā putraṃ vā niyamānvitam ||

ekādaśīvrataṃ sūtake mṛtake 'pi na tyājyam | yat uktaṃ tatraiva |

	paramāpadam āpanno harṣe vā samupasthite |

	sūtake mṛtake caiva na tyājyaṃ dvādaśīvratam ||

tathā |

	sūtake 'pi naraḥ snātvā praṇamya manasā harim |

	ekādaśyāṃ na bhuñjīta vratam evaṃ na lupyate ||

	dvādaśyāṃ tu tathā bhuktvā sūtakānte janārdanam |

	pūjayitvā vidhānena bhojayec ca dvijottamam ||

	mṛtake 'pi na bhuñjīta ekādaśyāṃ sadā naraḥ |

	dvādaśyāṃ tu samaśnīyāt snātvā viṣṇuṃ praṇamya ca ||

ekādaśīvratasya kathaṃcid atikrame yat kāryaṃ tad varāhapurāṇa evoktam |

	ekādaśī viplutā cet parato dvādaśī sthitā |

	upoṣyā dvādaśī tatra yadīcchet paramaṃ padam ||

viplutā kenāpi hetunātikrāntopavāsā | nityaṃ caikādaśīvratam iti tatraivoktam |

	ekādaśyāṃ na bhuñjīta pakṣayor ubhayor api |

	ekādaśyāṃ tu bhuñjāno viṣṇulokaṃ na paśyati || iti |

kāmyasyāpy asamāpane doṣam āha |

	parigṛhya vrataṃ samyag ekādaśyām upoṣaṇam |

	na samāpayate yas tu sa yāti narakaṃ naraḥ ||

vratāntare 'py āha |

	yo gṛhītvā vrataṃ mohād ekādaśyādikaṃ naraḥ |

	na samāpayate tasya gatiḥ gatiḥ pāpīyasī bhavet ||

anutpannaputreṇāviśeṣeṇaivaikādaśīvrate prakrānte sati putre jāte pratiṣiddhopavāsareṣu yat kartavyaṃ tad uktaṃ vāyupurāṇe |

**[203]**	upavāsaniṣedhe tu bhakṣyaṃ kiṃcit prakalpayet |

	na duṣyaty upavāsena upavāsaphalaṃ bhavet ||

bhakṣyaprakalpanam iti (mapi) tatraivoktam |

	naktaṃ haviṣyānnam anodanaṃ vā phalaṃ tilāḥ kṣīram athāmbu vājyam |

	yat pañcagavyaṃ yadi vāpi vāyuḥ praśastam atrottaram uttaraṃ ca ||

naktaṃ cā(ca) niyata eva kāle kāryam,

	yadā tu pāṅmukhī chāyā puruṣād dviguṇā bhavet |

	tadā naktaṃ vijānīyād anaktaṃ tv anyathā bhavet ||

iti smṛtyantaradarśanāt | yad api smṛtyantarm uktam (?),

	ekādaśyāṃ na bhuñjīta pakṣayor ubhayor api |

	vanasthayatidharmo 'yaṃ śuklām eva sadā gṛhī ||

iti, tatrāpi gṛhiśabdaḥ putravadgṛhiviṣayaḥ, pūrvoktavacanānurodhāt | vanasthādiśabdaḥ pradarśanārthaḥ | tenāputraṃ gṛhiṇam api saṃgṛhṇāti | dinakṣayaviśeṣe naktavidhim āha |

	ekādaśī kalā mātrā dvādaśī ca kṣayaṃ gatā |

	kṣīṇā sā dvādaśī jñeyā naktaṃ tatra vidhīyate ||

putravadgṛhiviṣayaś cāyaṃ niyamaḥ | aputras tūpavased eva | tad uktaṃ purāṇe |

	ekādaśī dvādaśī ca rātryante ca trayodaśī |

	tatra kratuśataṃ puṇyaṃ trayodaśyāṃ tu pāraṇam || iti |

	daśamy ekādaśī viddhā dvādaśī ca kṣayaṃ gatā |

	naktaṃ tatra prakurvīta nopavāso vidhīyate ||

ayam arthaḥ — ekādaśīdine daśamī vidyate dvādaśīdine tu naikādaśī trayodaśīdine ca na dvādaśī tatra naktaṃ kuryān nopavāsam iti | iti ślokadvaya eka eva viṣayo 'putravatputravadgṛhibhedenokta iti vicāryam | yadā punaḥ saṃpūrṇaikādaśī bhūtvā dvitīyadine punar bhavet | tṛtīyadine ca dvādaśī tadā pūrvām ekādaśīṃ hitvā dvitīyām upavaset | yad uktaṃ smṛtyantare,

**[204]**	kalā kāṣṭhāpi dvādasyā yadi yād apare 'hani |

	dvādaśa dvādaśīh(rha)nti pūrvasyām pāraṇe kṛte || iti |

asminn eva viṣaye yadi tṛtīye 'hani dvādaśī na dṛśyate tadā gṛhiṇaḥ pūrvasyām ekādaśyām upavāsaḥ | yater uttarasyām | yad uktaṃ purāṇe,

	saṃpūrṇaikādaśī yatra prabhāte punar eva sā |

	uttarāṃ tu yatiḥ kuryāt purvām upavased gṛhī ||

asminn eva viṣaye yateḥ pāraṇānugrahaṃ smarati |

	saṃpūrṇaikadaśī yatra prabhāte punar eva sā |

	tatra kratuśataṃ puṇyaṃ trayodaśyāṃ tu pāraṇam || iti |

tathā ca skandapurāṇe |

	kalāpy ekādaśī yatra dvādasyanugatā bhavet |

	dinakṣaye 'pi sā pūjyā yatīnām uttamā tithiḥ ||

yad api baudhāyanenoktam,

	kalāpy ekādaśī yatra parato dvādaśī bhavet |

	tatra kratuśataṃ puṇyaṃ trayodaśyāṃ tu pāraṇam || iti,

	ekādaśīṃ kalāyuktām upoṣya dvādaśīṃ naraḥ |

	trayodaśyāṃ tu yo bhuṅkte viṣṇusāyujyam ṛcchati ||

iti, tad api yativiṣayam eva, viṣṇusāyujyaphalaśravaṇāt | kratuśatapuṇyavidhānaṃ tu stutiparaṃ na svārthavidhiparam | yad api skandapurāṇe |

	dinakṣaye 'rkasaṃkrāntyāṃ grahaṇe candrasūryayoḥ |

	upavāsas tu kartavyo viṣṇusāyujyam i(ṛ)ccchati ||

iti, tad api putravadgṛhivyatiriktamumukṣupuruṣaviṣayam | ekasminn eva śloke caite ślokās trayodaśīpāraṇaniṣedhasūcakāḥ putravato gṛhasthasyeti jñeyam | iti atra gṛhasthayativyavsthā | yad api kūrmapurāṇe,

	dvispṛg ekādaśī yatra tatra saṃnihito hariḥ |

	tām evopavaset kāmam akāmo viṣṇutatparaḥ ||

iti, tad api pūrveṇa samānaviṣayam | ye tu putriṇo gṛhiṇas teṣām asyāṃ naktavidhir ity anusaṃdheyam | daśamīṃ dvādaśīṃ ca yā spṛśati sā dvispṛk | **[205]** yat tu nāradenoktam,

	daśamīśeṣasaṃyuktām upoṣya dvādaśīṃ kila |

	saṃvatsarakṛteneha naro dharmeṇa mucyate ||

iti, tathā,

	daśamyanugatā yatra tithir ekādaśī bhavet |

	tatrāpatyavināśaḥ syāt paretya narakaṃ vrajet ||

iti, tad dvitīye 'hany ekādaśyāṃ satyāṃ veditavyam | tadabhāve tu putravatāṃ gṛhiṇāṃ daśamīviddhaikādaśyāṃ nakam anyeṣām upavāsa ity uktaṃ bhavet | ata eva mahābhāratam |

	daśamīśeṣasaṃyuktā gāndhāryā samupoṣitā |

	tasyāḥ putraśataṃ naṣṭaṃ tasmāt tāṃ parivarjayet ||
