śalyaparihāre tu phalam avikalam,

	viśalyā dvādaśī yatra tatra saṃnihito hariḥ |

	upoṣyaikām api hi tāṃ garbhavāsaṃ na paśyati |

iti tatra smaraṇāt | yas tu trayodaśyāṃ pāraṇaniṣedho yathā kūrmapurāṇe tāvat,

	ekādaśyām upoṣyaiva dvādaśyāṃ pāraṇaṃ smṛtam |

	trayodaśyāṃ na tat kuryād dvādaśadvādaśīkṣayāt ||

skandapurāṇe,

	upoṣyaikādaśīṃ yas tu taryodaśyāṃ tu pāraṇam |

	karoti tasya naśyanti dvādaśyo dvādaśaiva tu ||

ityādiḥ, sa gṛhiviṣayaḥ | trayodaśīpāraṇaṃ yatraikādaśyām āśrīyamāṇāyāṃ prasajyate tāṃ gṛhī nopavased iti tasyārthaḥ | ata evoktam |

	uttarāṃ tu yatiḥ kuryāt pūrvām upavased gṛhī | iti |

yas tu trayodaśīpāraṇavidhiḥ, yathā tāvad baudhāyanīye,

	kalāpy ekādaśī yatra parato dvādaśī bhavet |

ityadiḥ, sa brahmacārivanasthaviṣayaḥ | ekādaśīdvaidhe sati dvitīyaikādaśī vrātyādinā kāryeti tasya tātparyam | trayodaśīpāraṇaniṣedhaś codayavyāpinyāṃ dvādaśyām asatyāṃ veditavyaḥ, na punas tasyāṃ satyām api trayodaśīsamaye pāraṇanivāraṇaparaḥ | tathā saty adṛṣṭārthaḥ syāt | anyathā punar ekādaśīdvaidhe saty ekasyāṃ gṛhiṇopavasaḥ kārya ity apekṣitārthavidhāyakaḥ san dṛṣṭārthaḥ | **[206]** mārkaṇḍeyaḥ |

	ekabhaktena naktena tathaivāyācitena ca |

	upavāsena dānena na nirdvādaśiko bhavet ||

atraikabhaktādividhānam upavāsāsamarthaṃ pratiṣiddhopavāsaṃ vā prati draṣṭavyam | putravato gṛhiṇo yasyām ekādaśyāṃ kṛṣṇapakṣārkasaṃkrāntidinakṣayavaśād upavāso viṣiddhas tasyām api kṛcchrādyanuṣaṅgaprāptau na niṣidhyate | yad āha smṛtimīmāṃsāyāṃ jaiminiḥ,

	āditye 'hani saṃkrāntau grahaṇe candrasūryayoḥ |

	upavāso na kartavyo gṛhiṇā putriṇā tathā ||

	tannimittopavāsasya niṣedho 'yam upāhṛtaḥ |

	nānuṣaṅgakṛto grāhyo yater nityam upoṣaṇam || iti |

tannimittopavāsasyety ayaṃśabdaḥ prakṛtatvād ekādaśīviṣayaḥ, na śuddhādityā(tya)dinādiviṣayaḥ | ādityadinasaṃkrāntyor ekādaśyupavāsaniṣedhaṃ prati nimittatvenātropādād dhy aprakṛtatvam | rāhudarśanasya tv ekādaśyām asaṃbhavāt pṛthag evopavāsaniṣedhahetutvam | tan na kṛcchrādyanuṣaṅgaprāptopavāsakṛto niṣedho 'tra grāhyaḥ | yataḥ parivrājakasya nityam aniṣiddham upoṣaṇam | 

	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">anye punar</span> anyathā paṭhanti varṇayanti ca:

	āditye 'hani saṃkrāntau grahaṇe candrasūryayoḥ |

	pāraṇaṃ copavāsaṃ ca na na kuryāt putravān gṛhī ||

tannimittopavāsasyādityavārābhi(di)nimittasyopavāsasya niṣedho naikādaśīnimittasyāvarjanīyādityavārādyanuṣaṅgagatasya | yasmān nityam ekādaśyām upoṣaṇam iti | atra vyākhyāyate — āditye 'hanītyādivākyam ekādaśyupavāsaprakaraṇapaṭhitam asati virodhe prakaraṇaṃ bādhitvā vyākhyeyam | hetuś copavāsanityatvarūpo na samañjasaḥ | yato nityasyāpi ṣoḍaśigrahaṇāder dṛśyate pratiṣedhaḥ | na cāsya nañaḥ prasajyapratiṣedhatvam | kiṃ tu paryudāsavṛttitvam | tathā saty upavāsavidhinaikavākyatā | pratiṣedhe tu nānāvākyatvam | tasmāt sadṛśavastuparigrahakārī paryudāsaḥ | api ca — 

	pradhānatvaṃ vidhau yatra pratiṣedhe 'pradhānatā |

	paryudāsaḥ sa vijñeyo yatrottarapadena nañ || **[207]**

yathābrāhmaṇam ānaya |

	aprādhānyaṃ vidhau yatra pratiṣedhe pradhānatā |

	prasajyapratiṣedho 'yaṃ kriyayā saha yatra nañ ||

yathāśrāddhabhojī | paryudāsavṛttiś caivaṃ vyākhyeyā | putravadgṛhivyatirikta ādityavārādiyuktāyām ekādaśyām upavaset | atha vā putravān gṛhastha upavāsād anyat tadā vrataṃ kuryād iti | evaṃ ca tasyām ādityadinādiyuktāyām ekādaśyām upavāsavidhir eva nastīti "na kuryāt putravān gṛhī" ity anena pratipādyate | yathā "dīkṣito na dadāti na juhoti" iti na punar vihitaḥ san pratiṣidhyate | tasmāt pūrvaiva vyākhyā jyāyasī | yat tu hārītenoktam,

	trayodaśyāṃ yadā na syād dvādaśī ghaṭikādvayam |

	daśamyaikādaśī miśrā saivopoṣyā sadā tithiḥ || 

iti, yad api ṛṣyaśṛṅgeṇoktam,

	pāraṇāhe na labhyeta dvādaśī kalayāpi cet |

	tadānīṃ daśamīviddhāpy upoṣyaikādaśī tithiḥ ||

iti, yad api matsyapurāṇam,

	ekādaśī daśāviddhā parato 'pi na vardhate |

	gṛhibhir yatibhiś caiva saivopoṣyā sadā tithiḥ ||

iti, tat sarvam aputrāṇāṃ gṛhiṇām upavāsavidhāyakaṃ vacanajātaṃ draṣṭavyam | saputrāṇāṃ punar asmin viṣaye naktavidhiḥ pardarśita eva | kūrmapurāṇam |

	kāṃsyaṃ māṃsaṃ masūraṃ ca caṇakaṃ koraduṣakān |

	śākaṃ madhu parānnaṃ ca upāvatsyan vivarjayet ||

upāvatsyann upavasann ity arthaḥ | kāṃsyaṃ kāṃsyapātre bhojanam | tataś ca daśamyām etad vratam | matsyapurāṇam |

	kāṃsyaṃ māṃsaṃ surāṃ kṣaudraṃ tailaṃ vitathabhāṣaṇam |

	vyāyāmaṃ pravāsaṃ ca divā svapnam athāñjanam ||

	tilapiṣṭaṃ masūraṃ ca dvādaśaitāni vaiṣṇavaḥ ||

tyajed iti śeṣaḥ |

	kāṃsyamāṃsaparakīyabhojanakṣāratailamadhumadyamaithunam |

	dvādaśīṣu parivarjayan naraḥ kaṃsasūdanatanau nilīyate ||

viṣṇuḥ: "mārgaśīrṣaśuklaikāsaśyām upoṣito dvādaśyāṃ bhagavantaṃ vāsudevam abhyarcayet | puṣpadhūpānulepanadīpanaivedyair vahnibrāhmaṇatarpaṇaiś ca vratam etat saṃvatsaraṃ pūrṇaṃ kṛtvā pāpebhyaḥ pūto bhavati | yāvajjīvaṃ kṛtvā śvetadvīpam āpnoti | ubhayapakṣe dvādaśīty evaṃ saṃvatsareṇa svargalokaṃ prāpnoti | yāvajjīvaṃ viṣṇulokam" | tathā |

	pañcadaśī paurṇamāsī pañcamīdvādaśīdvayam |

	saṃvatsaram abhuñjānaḥ satataṃ vijitendriyaḥ ||

	mucyate sarvapāpebhyaḥ svargalokaṃ ca gacchati ||

purāṇāt |

	caitrāṣāḍhāśvayukpauṣadvādaśyaḥ sitapakṣagāḥ |

	etā viśiṣṭā ubhayadvādaśyo nāmataḥ smṛtāḥ ||

tathā |

	māghamāsasya śuklā yā dvādaśī paramā tithiḥ |

	bhīmasenadvādaśī sā dvādaśībhyo viśiṣyate ||

yamaḥ |

	ayane viṣuve caiva candrasūryagrahe tathā |

	kṛtopavāsāḥ salilaṃ sarvapāpaiḥ pramucyate ||

	kṛtopavāsāḥ salilaṃ ye yugādidineṣu ca |

	dāsyantyannādisahitaṃ teṣāṃ lokā mahodayāḥ ||

	dṛśyete sahitau yasyāṃ divi candrabṛhaspatī |

	paurṇamāsī tu mahatī proktā sāṃvatsareṇa sā ||

	tasyāṃ dānopavāsādyam akṣayaṃ parikīrtitam |

	tathaiva dvādaśī śuklā yā syāc chravaṇasaṃyutā ||

sāṃvatsaro jyotirvit | smṛtyantare |

	māsākhyarkṣe candragurū tasmāt pañcadaśe raviḥ |

	pūrṇimā jīvavāre tu mahāśabdā tu sā tithiḥ ||

	harikṣetre ca gaṅgāyāṃ samudre naimiṣe tathā |

	mahāśabdatithau snānaṃ dānaṃ śrāddham anantakam ||

atha śrīśravaṇadvādaśīnirṇayaḥ |

	yadā ca śukladvādaśyāṃ nakṣatraṃ śravaṇaṃ bhavet |

	tadā sā tu mahāpuṇyā dvādaśī vijayā smṛtā ||

**[209]**	yadānyasyām api tithau śubhāyāṃ śravaṇaṃ bhavet |

	homas tatropavāsaś ca sahasrāśvaphalapradaḥ ||

	śravaṇe saṃgamāḥ puṇyāḥ kurukṣetrasamā matāḥ |

	veśeṣād budhasaṃyukte tṛtīyāyāṃ viśeṣataḥ ||

	budhaśravaṇasaṃyuktā tṛtīyā yadi labhyate |

	tatra dānopavāsādyam akṣayaṃ parikīrtitam ||

	śravaṇena sitā tatra dvādaśī labhyate kvacit |

	upoṣyaikādaśīṃ tatra dvādaśyām arcayed dharim ||

	yāḥ kāścit tithayaḥ proktāḥ puṇyā nakṣatrayogataḥ |

	tāsv eva tad vrataṃ kuryāc chravaṇadvādaśīṃ vinā ||

śravaṇadvādaśyāṃ vihitam ekādaśyāṃ kuryād ity arthaḥ | tathā ca matsyapurāṇam |

	dvādaśyāṃ śuklapakṣe tu nakṣatraṃ śravaṇaṃ yadi |

	upoṣyaikādaśīṃ tatra dvādaśyām arcayed dharim ||

etac caikādaśyaviddhāyāṃ śravaṇadvādaśyāṃ veditavyam | tadviddhā tu dvādaśyaivopoṣyā | tad uktaṃ tatraiva |

	dvādaśī śravaṇāspṛṣṭā spṛśed ekādaśīṃ yadi |

	sa eva vaiṣṇavo yogo viṣṇuśṛṅkhalasaṃjñitaḥ ||

	tasminn upoṣya vidhivan naraḥ saṃkṣīṇakalmaṣaḥ |

	prāpnoty anuttamāṃ siddhiṃ punarāvṛttidurlabhām ||

śavaṇāspṛṣṭā śravaṇasaṃyuktā | śravaṇāśabdaḥ strīliṅgo 'py asti | śravaṇa(ṇā)spṛṣṭeti vadan svalpe 'pi śravaṇayoge dvādaśyupavāsādiyogyā bhavatīti gamayati | tathā ca matsyapurāṇam |

	dvādaśī śravaṇāspṛṣṭā kṛtsnā puṇyatamā smṛtā |

	na tu sā tena saṃyuktā tāvaty eva praśasyate ||

ekādaśīrahitāpi śravaṇadvādaśy upoṣyā | yad āha mārkaṇḍeyaḥ |

	śravaṇarkṣasamāyuktā dvādaśī yadi labhyate |

	upoṣyā dvādaśī tatra trayodaśyāṃ tu pāraṇam || iti | **[210]**

ayam anupakrāntaikādaśīvratavidhiḥ | tadupakrame tv ekādaśyām evopavāsaḥ | dvādaśyāṃ tu pūjāmātravidhiḥ | tad uktam |

	asamāpte vrate pūrve naiva kuryād vratāntaram || iti |

yas tūpavāsadvayāsamarthas taṃ prati bhaviṣyottare vihitam |

	upoṣya dvādaśīṃ puṇyāṃ viṣṇuṛkṣeṇa saṃyutām |

	ekādaśyo(śyu)dbhavaṃ puṇyaṃ naraḥ prāpnoty asaṃśayam ||

	evam ekādaśīṃ muktvā dvādaśīṃ samupoṣayet |

	pūrvopavāsanaṃ puṇyaṃ naraḥ prāpnoty asaṃśayam ||

na hi śravaṇadvādaśyāṃ pāraṇāsaṃbhavāc copavāsajo doṣaḥ |

	ekādaśīm upoṣyaiva dvādaśīṃ samupoṣayet |

	na cātra vidhilopaḥ syād ubahor daivataṃ hariḥ ||

iti viṣṇuśṛṅkhalapakṣe punar ekasmād evopavāsāc chravaṇadvādaśīvratakāryaṃ ca prasaṅgāt sidhyati | viṣṇurahasyam |

	dvādaśyām upavāso 'tra trayodaśyāṃ tu pāraṇam |

	niṣiddham api kartavyam ājñeyaṃ pārameśvarī ||

tathā |

	śravaṇena samāyuktā māsi bhādrapade hi yā |

	dvādaśī sā mahāpuṇyā nāmnā tu vijayā smṛtā ||

	tasyāṃ snāto vidhānena sarvatīrthaphalaṃ labhet |

	arcayitvācyutaṃ bhaktyā labhet puṇyaṃ daśābdikam || iti 

tathā śrījanmāṣṭamīvicāraḥ |

	prājāpatyarkṣasaṃyuktā yā syān nabhasi cāṣṭamī |

	muhūrtam api labhyeta upoṣyā sā mahāphalā ||

prājāpatyarkṣaṃ rohiṇī | nabhasi śrāvaṇe | tathā |

	muhūrtam apy ahorātre yasmin yuktaiva labhyate |

	aṣṭamīṃ rohiṇīm ṛkṣaṃ supuṇyāṃ tām upāvaset ||

atrāṣṭamyāḥ prādhānyam | rohiṇī tu tadviśeṣaṇam | na ca sātatyena **[211]** nakṣatrayogo 'trāpekṣaṇīyaḥ | muhūrtam apīti vacanāt | na ca saptamīviddhāpy eṣā tyājyā | tad uktaṃ bhaviṣyatpurāṇe |

	kāryā viddhāpi saptamyā rohiṇīsahitāṣṭamī |

	tatropavāsaṃ kurvīta tithibhānte ca pāraṇam || iti |

asyārthaḥ — yadi saptamī muhūrtamātraṃ parato rohiṇyālpakālavyāptāṣṭamī dvitīyadine tu naivāṣṭamī rohiṇī ca kaṃcit kālaṃ vidyata eva, tadā saptamīviddhāṣṭamī kāryā | pāraṇaṃ tu navamīdine nakṣatre vyatīta it | yadā punar dvitīyadine 'lpam api kālam aṣṭamī vidyate tadā saptamīviddhāṣṭamī tyājyā | tad uktaṃ padmapurāṇe |

	varjanīyā prayatnena saptamīsaṃyutāṣṭamī |

	aviddhāyāṃ sa kṛṣṇāyāṃ jāto devakinandanaḥ ||

	pūrvaviddhā yathā nandā varjitā śravaṇānvitā |

	tathāṣṭamī pūrvaviddhā saṛkṣāpi hi varjitā ||

	pūrvaviddhāṣṭamī yā tu udaye prathame 'hani |

	muhūrtenāpi saṃyuktā saṃpūrṇā sāṣṭamī bhavet ||

	saptamīsaṃyutāṣṭamyāṃ bhūtvā ṛkṣaṃ dvijottama |

	prājāpatyaṃ dvitīye 'hni muhūrtaṃ vai bhaved yadi ||

	tadā vrataṃ dvitīye 'hni proktaṃ vyāsādibhiḥ purā || iti |

pūrvaviddhāṣṭamīti | aṣṭamīdine truṭimātreṇāpi saptamyā viddhā sūryodayaspṛṣṭāṣṭamī cet syān nāṣṭamītvena grāhyā | navamīdine ghaṭikādvayam api cet syāt saiva paripūrṇāṣṭamī bhaved ity arthaḥ | bhaviṣtatpurāṇam |

	aṣṭamyāṃ cātha rohiṇyāṃ na kuryāt pāraṇaṃ kvacit |

	hanyāt purā kṛtaṃ kṛṭsnam upavāsārjitaṃ phalam ||

	tithir aṣṭaguṇaṃ hanti nakṣatraṃ ca caturguṇam |

	tasmāt prayatnataḥ kuryāt tithibhānte ca pāraṇam ||

bhānto nakṣatrāntaḥ | **[212]** tathā |

	jayantyām upavāsaś ca mahāpātakanāśanaḥ |

	sa kāryaḥ sumahābhaktyā pūjanīyaś ca keśavaḥ ||

śrāvaṇakṛṇāṣṭamī rohiṇīyuktā jayantī ||

**iti śrījanmāṣṭamīnirṇayaḥ ||**

mārkaṇḍeyaḥ |

	siṃhāditye kṛṣṇa(śukla?)pakṣe caturthyāṃ candradarśanam |

	mithyābhidūṣaṇaṃ kuryāt tasmāt paśyen na taṃ tadā ||

purāṇāt |

	śuklāṣṭamyāṃ tu mādhasya dadyād bhīṣmāya yo jalam |

	saṃvatsarakṛtaṃ pāpaṃ tatkṣaṇād eva muñcati ||

	vaiyāghrapadyagotrāya sāṃkṛtyapravarāya ca |

	aputrāya dadāmy etat salilaṃ bhīṣmavarmaṇe ||

	kṛtvā nīrājanaṃ rājā balavṛddhyai yathābalam |

	śobhanaṃ khañjanaṃ paśyej jalagoṣṭhādisaṃnidhau || \
	na raktaṃ khañjanaṃ paśyen na pītaṃ kṛṣṇam eva vā |

	pūrṇasvastikabhadrāṇāṃ paśyed anyatamaṃ nrpaḥ ||

padmapurāṇāt |

	tulāmakarameṣeṣu prātaḥsnāyī sadā bhavet |

	brahmacaryaṃ haviṣyānnaṃ mahāpātakanāśanam ||

tathā |

	tulāyāṃ tilatailena sāyaṃsaṃdhyāsamāgame |

	aṣṭāṅgadīpaṃ yo dadyān māsam ekaṃ nirantaram ||

	samyak śrīpataye bhaktyā sa śriyā na viyujyate |

	dāmodarāya nabhasi tulāyāṃ lohayā saha ||

	pradīpaṃ tu prayacchāmi namo 'nantāya vedhase ||

iti dīpadānamantraḥ | nabhasy ākāśa ity arthaḥ | tathā |

	kārttike navamī śuklā pitṝṇām utsavāya sā |

	tasyāṃ snānaṃ hutaṃ dattam anantaphaladaṃ bhavet ||

liṅgapurāṇāt |

	aṣṭamyāṃ ca caturdaśyāṃ yaḥ śivaṃ saṃśitavrataḥ |

	mumukṣuḥ pūjayonnityaṃ sa labhetepsitaṃ phalam ||

viṣṇuḥ |

	sūryagrahaṇatulyā ca śuklā mādhasya saptamī |

	aruṇodayavelāyāṃ tasyāṃ snānaṃ mahāphalam || **[213]**

tathā |

	māghamāsasya saptamyām udayaty eva bhāskare |

	vidhivat tatra ca snānaṃ mahāpātakanāśanam ||

tathā |

	punarvasau budhopetā caitramāsasitāṣṭamī |

	srotaḥsu vidhivat snātvā vājapeyaphalaṃ labhet ||

	aśokair arcayed ugram aśokakalikāṃ pibet ||

ugraḥ śivaḥ |

	caitre māsi sitāṣṭamyāṃ ye pibanti punarvasau |

	aśokasyāṣṭakalikāṃ na te śokam avāpnuyuḥ ||

	tvām aśoka śivābhīṣṭaṃ madhumāṃ(mā)sasamudbhavam |

	pibāmi śokasaṃtyaktaṃ mām aśokaṃ sakā kuru |||

iti pānamantraḥ | tathā |

	caitrakṛṣṇacaturdaśyām aṅgārakadinaṃ yadā |

	piśācatvaṃ punar na syād gaṅgāyāṃ snānam abhojanam ||

mārkaṇḍeyaḥ |

	ekādaśyāṃ site pakṣe ṛkṣaṃ caiva punarvasuḥ |

	nāmnā sā vijayā khyātā tithīnām uttamā tithiḥ ||

	ekādaśyāṃ site pakṣe puṣyarkṣaṃ yadi sattama |

	dvādaśyāṃ vā tadāśeṣapapakṣayakaraṃ dvayam ||

vyāsaḥ |

	śuklapakṣe tṛtīyāyāṃ caturthyāṃ caiva bhārata |

	pañcamyāṃ kṛṣṇapakṣasya snātaḥ kim anuśocate ||

	śukle vā yadi vā kṛṣṇe caturthī vā caturdaśī |

	bhaumavāreṇa puṇyāsau somavāre kuhūr yathā ||

tathā |

	amā vai somavāreṇa ravivāreṇa saptamī |

	caturthī bhaumavāreṇa viṣuvat sadṛśaṃ phalam ||

	sinīvālī kuhūr vāpi yadi somadine bhavet |

	gosahasraphalaṃ dadyāt snānaṃ vai mauninā kṛtam ||

	dvijendrasutasaṃyuktā paripūrṇā sitāṣṭamI |

	tasyāṃ niyamakartāro na syuḥ khaṇḍitasaṃpadaḥ ||

dvijendrasutaḥ somasutaḥ | budha iti yāvat | **[214]** tathā |

	bṛhaspatidvitīyāyāṃ śuklāyāṃ vidhipūjanam |

	kṛtvā naktaṃ samaśnīyāl labhed bhūmim abhīpsitām ||

vidhir brahmā, tatpūjanaṃ ca gāyatryā kāryam | atha prasaṅgāt khaṇḍatithiviṣayāṇi kānicid vākyāni likhyante | tatra pratipādāditithiṣu yāny avaśyakāryāṇi karmāṇi tāni tāsāṃ dvaividhye sati kiṃ sūryodayavyapinīṣu kāryāṇi kiṃ vā tadastamayavyāpinīṣv iti saṃśaye pakṣadvaye 'py anugrāhakāṇi kānicid vākyāni dṛśyante | yad āha devalaḥ |

	yāṃ tithiṃ samanuprāpya astaṃ yāti divākaraḥ |

	sā tithiḥ sakalā jñeyā snānadānajapādiṣu ||

	yāṃ tithiṃ samanuprāpya udayaṃ yāti bhāskaraḥ |

	sā tithiḥ sakalā jñeyā dānādhyayanakarmasu ||

	āgatāṃ tithim utsṛjya tithiśeṣaṃ na yojayet |

	jvalantam agnim utsṛjya na hi bhasmani hūyate ||

etadvirodhaparihārāya viṣṇudharmottare śivagītāḥ |

	ekādaśy aṣṭamī ṣaṣṭhī dvitīyā ca caturdaśī |

	trayodaśī amāvāsyā upoṣyāḥ syuḥ parānvitāḥ ||

atra kṛṣṇapakṣasyaiva trayodaśīcaturdaśyau grāhye | tathā ca nigamaḥ |

	ṣaṣṭhy aṣṭamī tathā darśaḥ kṛṣṇapakṣe trayodaśī |

	etāḥ parayutāḥ pūjyāḥ parāḥ pūrvayutās tathā ||

parā uttarāḥ | tataś ca ṣaṣṭhyādīnāṃ yathāsaṃkhyaṃ parāḥ saptamīnavamīcaturdaśīpratipado bhavanti | tathā |

	ekādaśy aṣṭamī ṣaṣṭhī śuklapakṣe caturdaśī |

	pūjyāḥ parameṇa saṃyuktāḥ ||

pareṇa tithinety arthaḥ | tathā |

	yugmāgniyugabhūtānāṃ ṣaṇmunyor vasurandhrayoḥ |

	rudreṇa dvādaśī yuktā caturdaśyā ca pūrṇimā ||

**[215]**	pratipatsv apy amāvāsyā tithyor yugmaṃ mahāphalam |

	etad vyastaṃ mahādoṣaṃ hanti puṇyaṃ purākṛtam ||

atra tithyor yugmam ity abhidhānād yugmāgnyādiśabdā dvitīyātṛtīyāditithiviśeṣopalakṣaṇārthā vijñāyante | tataś ca yugmāgnyor dvitīyātṛtīyayor yugmabhūtānāṃ caturthīpañcamyor yugmam ity evaṃ tithiyugmanirdeśo draṣṭavyaḥ | evaṃ ca sati daśamīśuklatrayodaśīśuklapratipadāṃ pūrvottaratithiyugmāni tyājyāni bhavanti | yac ca devalavacanam: "yāṃ tithiṃ samanuprāpya" ityādi tad yāsāṃ tithīnāṃ dvitīyādīnām uttaratithividdhānām upādeyatvam uktaṃ tadviṣayaṃ grāhyam | yac ca tenaivoktam,

	yāṃ tithiṃ samanuprāpya astaṃ yāti divākaraḥ |

iti, tad api yās tithayaḥ pūrvatithividdhāḥ satyo grāhyās tadviṣayam | yac ca baudhāyanenoktam,

	sā tithis tad ahorātraṃ yasyām abhyudito raviḥ |

	vardhamānasya pakṣasya hrāse 'py astamayaṃ prati ||

tat paraviddhatvena pūjānāṃ dvitīyāditithīnām udayavyāpinīnām upādeyatvam anūdya tāsām eva kṣayagāmitvenodayavyāpitve 'sati pūrvaviddhatve 'py upādeyatāṃ vidhatte | yadā punar dvitīyādivihitaṃ karma samagram udayavyāpidvitīyādau kartum aśakyaṃ tadviparītāyāṃ ca śakyaṃ tadā kiṃ kāryam ity apekṣite bhaviṣyatpurāṇam |

	vratopavāsasnānādau ghaṭikaikā yadā bhavet |

	udaye sā tithir grāhyā viparītāpi paitṛke || iti |

yat tu mārkaṇdeyenoktam,

	śuklapakṣe tithir grāhyā yasyām abhyudito raviḥ |

	kṛṣṇapakṣe tithir grāhyā yasyām astamito raviḥ ||

iti, tatra śuklapakṣaśabdena devakāryam upalakṣyate, tasya prāyaḥ śuklapakṣe vihitatvāt | kṛṇapakṣaśabdena ca pitṛkāryam | devakāryaṃ ca yad (?) udayavyāpinyāṃ vidhīyate tat pratiṣiddhatithivedhānatikrameṇa grāhyam | pitṛkārye punar aparāhṇavyāpinī vedhavidhim anādṛtyaiva grāhyā | yat smṛtyantare,

	madhyāhnavyāpinī yā syāt tithiḥ pūrvā parāpi vā |

	tatra karmāṇi kurvīta vṛddhihrāsāv akāraṇam || iti |

idaṃ caikoddiṣṭaviṣayam, tasya madhyāhne vihitatvāt | "śrāddhādāv āparāhṇikī" iti vacanāt paitṛke karmaṇi tithivedho na duṣyatīti gamyate | ata evaopavāsayogyatāṃ vedhaviśeṣe tithiviśeṣāṇām āha gārgyaḥ | **[216]**

	ekādaśy aṣṭamī ṣaṣṭhī pūrṇamāsī caturdaśī |

	amāvāsyā tṛtīyā ca tā upoṣyāḥ parānvitāḥ ||

pāriśeṣyād anyāḥ pūrvaviddhā evopavāse grāhyā iti gamyate | yat tu nigamavākyam: "yugmāgniyugabhūtāni" ityādau paurṇamāsītṛtīyayoḥ pūrvaviddhayor upādeyatvam uktam, tad ekādaśy aṣṭamītyādigārgyavacanāvirodhenopavāsavyatiriktakarmaviṣayaṃ grāhyam | caturdaśyāś ca śuklāyā eva paraviddhāyāḥ pūjyatā | yad āha baudhāyanaḥ |

	ekādaśy aṣṭamī ṣaṣṭḥī śuklapakṣe caturdaśī |

	pūjyāḥ pareṇa saṃyuktāḥ parāḥ pūrveṇa saṃyutāḥ || iti |

kṛṣṇacaturdaśī tu paraviddhā heyaiva,

	etad vyastaṃ mahādoṣaṃ hanti puṇyaṃ parākṛtam |

iti vacanasāmarthāt | dvitīyāditithīnāṃ pūrvatithivedhe sati dvitīye 'hany avaśyaṃ ṣaṣṭhyāditithir niḥsaratīti tādṛśe viṣaye nāgādivedho heya ity evaṃparam | yadā tu svalpayā pañcamyādikayā tithyā ṣaṣṭhyādividdhāpi ṣaṣṭhyādir upādeyā | kāmyāny api karmāṇi prakrāntāni santy āvaśyakāny eva | evaṃ ca sati dvādaśāṣṭādaśādiśabdāḥ ṣaṣṭhyādīnāṃ paraviddhatvasaṃbhavajñāpanārthā na vivakṣitasvārthā ity evaṃ vidheyam | "dikpañcadaśābhis tathā" ity atra dig iti daśamīty arthaḥ | nakṣatre tūpavasanīye kim astamayavyāpi tad grāhyam anyathā veti saṃśaye śaṃkaragītāḥ |

	upoṣitavyaṃ nakṣatraṃ yasminn astam iyād raviḥ |

	yatra vā yujyate nā(rā)ma niśīthaṃ śaśinā saha || iti |

etac ca tithiviśeṣayogānapekṣe nakṣatra evopoṣitavye draṣṭavyam | yatra tu nakṣatrayuktā tithis tithiyuktaṃ vā nakṣatraṃ karmāṅgatayā vihitaṃ tatrodayaprabhṛti sātatyena tadyogo 'pekṣaṇīyo rohiṇyaṣṭamīṃ śravaṇadvādaśīṃ ca vihāya | tataś cāyam arthaḥ siddho bhavati — āvaśyakavratādikarmakāle labhyamānā tithir niṣiddhavedhā heyā | upādeyavedhā tu karmakālāvyāpiny api svīkāryeti | nityaṃ naimittikaṃ ca karmāvaśyakaṃ prakrāntaṃ ca sadāvaśyakam eva | prakramyamāṇaṃ tu tat saṃkalpakālavyāpinyām **[217]** eva vihitāyāṃ tathāvārambhaṇīyam, saṃkalpasyaiva vratatvāt | sa caucityāt prātar eva kāryaḥ | manuḥ |

	vedotitaṃ svakaṃ karma nityaṃ kuryād atandritaḥ |

	tad dhi kurvan yathāśakti prapnoti paramāṃ gatim ||

nityam akāmyam ity arthaḥ | parmā gatir muktiḥ | karma ca paramātmajñānasahitaṃ kriyamāṇaṃ muktaye kalpata iti vyākhyeyam, vacanāntaravaśāt | tathā |

	indriyārtheṣu sarveṣu na prasajyeta kāmataḥ |

	atiprasaktiṃ caiteṣāṃ manasā saṃnivartayet ||

tathā |

	agnihotraṃ ca juhuyād ādyante dyuniśoḥ sadā |

	darśane(rśena) cārdhamāsānte pūrṇamāsena caiva hi ||

	sasyānte navasasyeṣṭyā tathartvante dvijo 'dhvaraiḥ |

	caturṣu caturṣu maseṣu cāturmāsyādiyāgaiḥ |

	paśunā hy ayanasyānte samānte saumikair makhaiḥ ||

ahnor niśāyāś cādyantāv agnihotraprayogaṃ prati kālatvena vidhānād yogyāv iti tābhyāṃ svasaṃbandhī pūrva uttaraś ca kāla upalakṣito 'tra vidhīyate | ata evāparāhṇe sāyaṃhomasyopakramaḥ | pradoṣe tu samāptiḥ | uditahomināṃ punarudita āditye | evam ardhamāsāntasyāpy atyantasūkṣamatvād darśapūrṇamasaprayogasamarthakālalakṣakatvam | ata eva kalpasūtrakārāḥ |

	pakṣāntā upavastavyāḥ pakṣādayo 'bhiyaṣṭavyāḥ | iti |

pakṣāntaḥ pañcadaśī, pakṣādiḥ pratipat | tatropavāsas tīrthasnānāgnyanvādhānādikarmakalāpaḥ pāṇisaṃsparśanādiprayogo 'bhījyā | etac ca pratipatpañcadaśyoḥ sūryodayāstamayavyāpitve sati tathā kṛṣṇaśuklapratipadoś candrasyādarśanapūrṇodayavattve sati draṣṭavyam | yadā punar ekasminn evāhani pūrṇaś candra udeti na dṛśyate vā tadā tad ahar eva yāgaḥ | yad āha āpastambaḥ: "yad ahaḥ purastāc candramāḥ pūrna utsarpet tāṃ pūrṇamāsīm upavasec chvaḥ pūriteti vā" | tathā: "yad ahar na dṛśyate tad ahar amāvāsyā vā śvo na draṣṭāra iti vā" iti | yadapy (yadyapy) upavāsaś candramasaṃ vāvijñāya saṃpūrṇaṃ vā vijñāyāgnīn anvadadhātīyādibhir **[218]** vacanaiś candrādarśanasaṃpūrṇodayavaty ahani vihitaḥ | tathāpi yāgasya pradhānyāt tatkāle darśanādibhir yathā na bādhyate tathopavasathasya kālo grāhyaḥ, "aṅgaguṇavirodhe ca tādarthyāt" it nyāyāt | tasmād atikṣaye tithīnāṃ yasminn evāhorātre candrasyādarśanaṃ pūrṇodayo vā bhavati tadādṛśyamāne candramasyamāvāsyopavāsaḥ | yadā tu dinadvayavyapi candrādarśanaṃ pūrṇodayo vā bhavati tatraiva vā viṣaye pratipatpañcadāśyor divā saṃdhiś cat syāt tadā pūrvedyur upoṣya divāsaṃdhimaty ahani yaṣṭavyaṃ nottaredyuś candradarśanādiyukte 'pi saṃdhimaty ahanījyayā hi saṃdhisaṃnidhir anugṛhīto bhavati | candrādarśanādiyuktottaredyur iṣṭau ca viprakṛṣṭaḥ | viprakṛṣṭaś ca (-ṣṭāc ca) yāgakālāt saṃnikṛṣṭo yāgakālo jyāyān | "divāsaṃdhiyuktāyāṃ haviṣā paurṇamāsyāṃ yajetāmāvasyam (?) amāvāsyāyāṃ yajeta" iti śrutiḥ | pūrṇamāsyamāvāsyāśabdau hi pañcadaśyoḥ prasiddhau na tu pratipadi | ata eva "saṃdhim abhito yajeta" iti śrutyantaram | abhita ubahata ity arthaḥ | tatra divāsaṃdhau saṃdheḥ pūrvatra yāgo rātrisaṃdhau tūttaratra pūrvahṇe | sarveṣv api ca pakṣeṣu yāgaḥ prātaḥkāla eva, "atha prātaḥ prātarhute 'gnihotre" ityādivakyāt | ata eva baudhāyanaḥ: "atrodāharanty ūrdhvaṃ madhyarātrāt pūrṇamasyāṃ candramāḥ pūryate | sa etaṃ cāpararātraṃ pūrṇo bhavati | sarvaṃ cāhar uttarasyā rātrer ā madhyarātrād athāmāvāsyāyām aupavasathye 'hany ūrdhvaṃ madhyaṃdināc candramasādityo rabhate sa evaṃ cāparāhṇaṃ na bhavati | sarvāṃ ca rātrim uttarasya cāhna ā madhyaṃdinād etaṃ saṃdhim abhito yajeta" iti | asyārthaḥ — atrodāharanti śrutim iti śeṣaḥ | pūrṇamāsyām iti viṣayanirdeśaḥ | ūrdhvaṃ madhyarātrāc candramāḥ pūryate pūrṇamāsī pravartata ity uktaṃ bhavati | saitam apararātram anantaraṃ ca sarvam ahar uttarasyā rātrer ā madhyarātrād anuvartate  tato vicchidyate so 'yaṃ rātrisaṃdhir uktaḥ | athāmāvāsyāviṣayte | aupavasathīye(thye) 'hanit yāgadināt pūrvedyur ūrdhvaṃ madhaṃdināc candramasādityo rabhate 'māvāsyā pravartate | saitam aparāhṇam anantarāṃ sarvāṃ rātrim uttarasyāhna ā madhyaṃdinād anuvartate | tataḥ pratipad bhavati | sa eṣa divāsaṃdhir etaṃ rātrisaṃdhim **[219]** abhivyāpya saṃdheḥ pūrvedyur agnīn anvādhāyottaredyur yajeta | tathaitaṃ divāsamdhim abhilakṣya tadahaḥ prātar yajata iti | evaṃ śrutim udāhṛtya tadgatau madhyarātramadhaṃdinaśabdau vyākhyātum āha: "rātrir hi pūrṇamāsyāṃ saṃdheyā bhavaty ahar amāvasyāyām" iti | tena śrutigatau madhyarātamadhaṃdinaśabdau rātrisaṃdhidivāsaṃdhyor upalakṣakau na vivakṣitāv iti pratipaditaṃ bhavati | anayoś ca pūrṇamāsyamāvāsyāviṣayaśrutyoḥ pradarśanārthatvaṃ vaktum uttaraṃ sūtram: "dve paurṇamāsyau dve amāvasye pūrvāṃ pūrvāṃ | paurṇamāsīm uttarām uttarām amāvasyām"| iti | ayam arthaḥ — rātrisaṃdhidivāsaṃdhimatyau dve pūrṇamāsyau | tatra divāsaṃdhiḥ pūrvāmāvāsyā pūrṇamāsī vā, rātrisaṃdhis tūttarā | tatra pūrvāmāvāsyoktā na tu pūrṇamāsī tām upamāvyājenāha — pūrvāṃ pūrvāṃ pūrṇamāsīm iti | ayam arthaḥ — pūrvām avāvāsyām iva pūrvām paurṇavāsīṃ jānīyād iti | tataś ca divāsaṃdhim asyāṃ pūrṇamāsyāṃ yāgaḥ pūrvedyur upavāsa iti siddham | tathottarā pūrṇamāsy uktā na tv amāvāsyā tāṃ pūrṇamāsīṃ nirūpayann āha: uttarām uttarām amāvāsyām iti | uttarāṃ pūrṇamāsīm itvoktām uttarām amāvāsyāṃ jānīyād iti | tataś ca rātrigatam amāvāsyāpratipatsaṃdhim upavāsayāgayor madhye kuryād ity arthaḥ | evaṃ tāvat saṃdhisaṃnidhir evānugrāhyo na tūpavasathasya candrādarśanasaṃpūrṇodayakālatvam iti baudhāyanamatam | 

	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">kecit</span> tu kalpasūtrakārā divāsaṃdhimaty ahany upavāsaḥ kāryaḥ | uttaredyuś ca yāgaḥ | yadi tasminnahani candrasyādarśanaṃ saṃpūrṇodayo vā syād ity āhuḥ | tatrobhāv api śastrārthāv aviśeṣāt | kiṃ tu yatsūtrapratyayena ye 'nutiṣṭhanti teṣāṃ tad ukta eva śāstrārtha uditānuditaśāstrārthavd iti | piṇḍapitṛyajñe tu yad aupavasathya evāhani nāparāhṇe 'māvāsyāsti tadā saṃdehaḥ | kim aupavasathya evāhani sa kārya uta yajanīya iti | tatra <span style="text-decoration:underline;">kecid</span> āhuḥ: "tasmāt pūrvedyuḥ pitṛbhyaḥ kriyata uttaram ahar devān yajante | pitṛbhya etad yajñaṃ niṣkrīya yajamānaḥ pratanute" ityādiśrutivākyabalāt, tathāgnyādhānaṃ prakṛtya "athāparāhṇe piṇḍapitṛyajñena caranti" iti kalpasūtrakāravacanād aupavasthya evāhani kārya iti | yat punaḥ **[220]** "amāvāsyāyām aparāhṇe piṇḍapitṛyajñena caranti" iti vacanam, tatrāmāvāsyāśabda aupavasathyadinopalakṣaṇārtho 'nyathā pūrvoktavacanavirodhaḥ syād iti | 

	<span style="text-decoration:underline;">tad asat</span> | na hy amāvāsyāyām aparāhṇa ity atrāmāvāsyāśabda aupavasathyam ahar upalakṣayatīti | kiṃ ca na pramāṇam asti | atra hy amāvāsyāśabdārtho 'ṅgatvena vidhīyate | na ca vidhau lakṣaṇocitā | tasmāt "pūrvedyuḥ pitṛbhyaḥ kriyate" ity atra pūrvedyuḥśabdo 'nuvādako 'rthavādatvāt | anuvadakasya yathāprāptilakṣaṇāśrayaṇam adoṣaḥ | tena pūrvedyuḥśabdo 'māvāsyām upalakṣayati, tasyām eva pitṛyajñasya vihitatvāt | bhavati cāmāvāsyā saṃpūrṇā satī yajanīyadināpekṣayā pūrvedyuḥśabdabodhyā | yac ca "athāparāhṇe piṇḍapitṛyajñena caranti" iti, tad aupavasathye 'hany aparāhṇavyāpy amāvāsyāviṣayaṃ grāhyam | "bhūte kavyādikī kriyā" ity etad api tadviṣayam eva, na punaḥ śuddhacaturdaśyupavāsadinaviṣayam, amāvāsyāvidhāyakadinaśrutivirodhāt | tasmāc chuddhacaturdaśyupavāsapakṣe yajanīya evāhany aparāhṇe 'māvāsyāyāṃ dakṣiṇāgnim uddhṛtya piṇḍapitṛyajñaḥ kāryaḥ | kramas tv agnyanvādhānena saha tasya na kḷptaḥ | aṅgatve 'pi na kḷpta eva yataḥ kālādiviśiṣṭatayā prāpteṣu padārtheṣu kramaḥ kalpyate | ata eva "amāvasyāyāṃ pūrvedyur vediṃ karoti" iti vediprakarṣe tataḥ prācāṃ padārthānām apratikarṣa iti | manuḥ |

	na śūdrāya matiṃ dadyān nocchiṣṭaṃ na haviṣkṛtam |

	na cāsyopadiśed dharmān na cāsya vratam ādiśet ||

	yo hy asya dharmam ācaṣṭe yaś caivādiśati vratam |

	so 'saṃvṛtaṃ nāma tamaḥ saha tenaiva gacchati ||

vrataṃ prāyaścittam | yamaḥ |

	vṛṣalādhyāpakaś caiva vṛṣalādhyāpitaś ca yaḥ |

	tāv ubhau narake ghore vasetāṃ śaradāṃ satam ||


    śaṅkhalikhitau: "kṛsarapāyasāpūpasāṃsadadhimadhughṛtakṛṣṇājināni śūdrebhyo na dadyān nopaskṛtaṃ kiṃcid anyatra prakṛtāt" | āpastambaḥ: "nābrāhmaṇāyocchiṣṭaṃ prayacchet | dantāṃsthaptvā tad etasminn avadhāya prayacchet." | **[221]** dantāṃsthaptvā dantair avalikhya tad dantalagnam annam ucchiṣṭe vidhāya prayacched ity arthaḥ | tathā krodhādīn bhūtadāhīyān doṣān varjayet | tān sa evāha: "bhūtadāhīyān doṣān udāhariṣyāmaḥ krodho harṣo [roṣo] lobho moho dambho droho mṛṣodyam atyāśaparivādāvasūyākāmamanyurānātmyam ayogaḥ" iti | tatra pitrādiṣv ananuśāsanīyeṣu kopaḥ krodhaḥ | harṣo garvaḥ | anuśāsanīyeṣu kopo roṣaḥ | vihitadhanavyayaparāṅmukhatvaṃ lobhaḥ | anyāyārjanaṃ ca | aviveko mohaḥ | atyāśo 'tyaśanam | manuḥ śokaḥ | ānātmyaṃ nairātmyabuddhiḥ | vihiteṣv asamādhir ayogaḥ | hārītaḥ: "audararaitasakāmajakrodhajārthajān agnīn yathāvan niyacchet | audarāt sarvakāmakarmendriyabhāvadoṣāḥ saṃbhavanti | yair upaspṛṣṭo sattvaśuddhir ity ācāryāḥ | atha pauṃsnāt sāhasād retas tasya bījaṃ tad anṛtāv utsarge doṣaḥ syād ṛtāv utsarge tad brahmacaryeṇa vyākhyātam | tad evādiprakṛtatvāj jagataḥ prathamaṃ saṃkalpāt kāmaḥ saṃbhavaty āśayāt pravartate | snehāgnir badhnāti sa icchālakṣaṇo naikavidhaḥ kāmo yenābhibhūto 'tṛpta eva kāmānāṃ loke hy anekajanmasaṃsāre kāmāvarte nimajjati | sa eko 'nalaḥ kāmaḥ | kāmo hi bhagavān vaiśvānara iti śrutiḥ | tasya saṃkalpo niyamanam | sa vyākhyātaḥ | kāmagītau cātra ślokau bhavata:

	pravṛttau vā nivṛttau vā sarvataḥ pratibhūr aham |

	sarvārtheṣu yathārtho 'haṃ madṛte nāsti kiṃcana ||

	yo māṃ yathārthaṃ sarvārthe sarvabhūteṣu paśyati |

	so 'dhvanaḥ pāram āpnoti netare kāmavādinaḥ || iti |


    krodhāgninā paribhūtaḥ sveṣām apy abahumato 'nabhigamanīyo 'viśvasanīyaś ca bhavati | kāryākāryavācyāvācyāni na vitarkayati | hitavādino gurūn atikrāmaty āviṣṭaḥ pretalokāyātmānaṃ gamayati | tatra ghorāṃ nirayaprāyāṃ yātanām anubhūya krūrakravyādāsu tiryagyoniṣu jāyate | tatra sarvāsāṃ prajānāṃ vācyo bhavati | kramaśo manuṣyatāṃ prāpya **[222]** sarvajanavidviṣṭatām upaiti | krodho hi tamorūpaḥ | tasya kṣamā niyamanam | sa vyākhyātaḥ | lobhāgninābhibhūtaḥ puṇyārtheṣv (?) upayujyamānam atikrāmantam ātmānaṃ manyate | asadvittānām apy upādānam icchati | tatrārthānuṣaṅgāt so 'pi tiryagyoniṣu jāyate | lobho hi tamorūpaḥ | tasya saṃtoṣo niyamanam | so 'pi vyākhyātaḥ | evaṃ hy āha |

	audaro raitasaś cāgniḥ kāmajaḥ krodhajo 'rthajaḥ |

	ete vai nirjitā yena sa vai pañcatapāḥ smṛtaḥ ||

	vacovegaṃ manasaḥ krodhavegaṃ jihvāvegaṃ codaropasthavegam |

	etān vegān dharayed yas tu vipras taṃ vai brūyur brahmiṣṭhaṃ vā muniṃ vā ||"

pauṃsnāt puruṣavyāpārāt | sāhasād balodbhavāt | tasya puṃsaḥ | tadanṛtāv iti | tat tasmād evaṃ tadbrahmacaryeṇeti | tad eveti | parvāparvasādhāraṇaṃ svadāragamanarūpam ādyaṃ tad eva parvavarjanarūpaṃ dvitīyam | evam ṛtugamananiyamātmakaṃ tṛtīyam ūrdhvaretaskatvaṃ caturtham | saṃkalpo viṣayasaundaryajñānam | kāmo viṣayecchā | āśayaḥ paunaḥpunyena bhāvanam | naṣṭaṃ nāśam | upayuṅkta ākāṅkṣate | viṣṇuḥ |

	trividhaṃ narakasyeha dvāraṃ nāśanam ātmanaḥ |

	kāmaḥ krodhas tathā lobhas tasmād etat trayaṃ tyajet ||

āpastambaḥ: "manasā vācā ghrāṇena cakṣuṣā śrotreṇa tvakśiśnodarārambhanānāsravān parivṛñjāno 'mṛtatvāya kalpate" | manaḥprabhṛtīnām ārambhāṇāṃ vyāpārān āsrāvān puruṣaḥ saṅgahetūn parivṛñjānaḥ parityajann amṛtatvāya muktaye kalpate samartho bhavati | devalaḥ: "athātaḥ pāpadoṣān manovākśarīrajān vyākhyāsyāmaḥ | tatra moharāgadveṣamānalobhamadaśokamamatvāhaṃkārabhayaharṣamoghacintāś ceti dvādaśa mānasāḥ | 

	teṣāṃ ca trividho mohaḥ saṃbhavaḥ sarvapāpmanām |

	ajñānaṃ saṃśayajñānaṃ mithyājñānam iti trikam ||

	vijñānaṃ sarvavidyānām arthānāṃ svayam ūhanam |

	doṣair adarśanaṃ ceti jñānam ajñānam anyathā ||

	aśreyaḥśreyasor madhye bhramaṇaṃ saṃsayo bhavet |

	mithyājñānam iti prāhur ahite hitadarśanam ||

**[223]**	bhavaty adharmād ajñānam avidyā tac ca saṃśayaḥ |

	ubhābhyām anyathājñānaṃ pāpiṣṭham upajāyate ||

	ajñānād duḥkhasaṃprāptiḥ saṃśayād badhyate punaḥ |

	mithyājñānāt pataty evaṃ mūḍhas tāmisrayoniṣu ||

manuḥ |

	ācāryaṃ ca pravaktāraṃ pitaraṃ mātaraṃ gurum |

	na hiṃsyād brāhmaṇaṃ gāś ca sarvāṃś caiva tapasvinaḥ ||

	brāhmaṇāyāvagūryaiva dvijātir vadhakāmyayā |

	śataṃ varṣāṇi tāmisre narake parivartate ||

	tāḍayitvā tṛṇenāpi saṃrambhān matipūrvakam |

	ekaviṃśatim ājātīḥ pāpayoniṣu jāyate ||

	ayudhyamānasyotpāda brāhmaṇasyāsṛg aṅgataḥ |

	duḥkhaṃ sumahad āpnoti pretyāprājñatayā naraḥ ||

	śoṇitaṃ yāvataḥ pāṃsūn saṃgṛhṇāti mahītalāt |

	tāvanty abdasahasrāṇi tatkartā narake vaset ||

	na kadācid dvije tasmād vidvān avagured api |

	na tāḍayet tṛṇenāpi na gātrāt srāvayed asṛk ||

	avagūrya tv abdaśataṃ sahasram abhihanya tu |

	jighāṃsayā brāhmaṇasya narakaṃ pratipadyate ||

devalaḥ |

	nāvagāhed apo nagno vahniṃ nābhivrajet padā |

	śiro'bhyaktāvaśiṣṭena tailenāṅgaṃ na lepayet ||

vasiṣṭhaḥ: "neṣṭakābhiḥ phalāni śātayet | na phalena phalam | na kalkakuhako bhavet" | 

kalko dambhaḥ | kuhako vaśīkārādis tadvān na bhaved ity arthaḥ |

"na mlecchabhāṣāṃ śikṣeta" | devalaḥ: "nāvekṣetāśuciḥ kūpaṃ gharṣayen na padā padam" | 

tathā |

	suhṛnmaraṇam ārtiṃ vā na svayaṃ śrāvayet parān |

	atibhogena mitrāṇi bāliśyān naiva pīḍayet ||

	dākṣiṇyād dhi daridro 'pi sahate mitrapīḍanam || **[224]**

manuḥ |

	yad yat paravaśaṃ karma tat tad yatnena varjayet |

	yad yad ātmavaśaṃ tu syāt tat tad yatnena sevayet ||

	sarvaṃ paravaśaṃ duḥkhaṃ sarvam ātmavaśaṃ sukham |

	etad vidyāt samāsena lakṣaṇaṃ sukhaduḥkhayoḥ ||

	yat karma kurvato 'sya syāt paritoṣo 'ntarātmanaḥ |

	tat prayatnena kurvīta viparītaṃ tu varjayet ||

yat karma dharmam ity arthaḥ | śaṅkhalikhitau |

	"āpatsv api hi kaṣṭāsu parasvaṃ kāmayeta na |

	nābhakṣyaṃ bhakṣayet kiṃcin na pūrvacaritaṃ caret ||

	narṣipitṛdevatāḥ kīrtayet |

svakīyān ṛṣīn iṣṭadevatāḥ pitṝṃś ca na kīrtayed ity arthaḥ | 

	"nāgādhodakam avagāheta | na striyaṃ vivasanām īkṣeta | na puruṣam anyatra 

	svābhāvyāt" | 

svābhāvyād akāmata ity arthaḥ |


        "na pādena pādaṃ prakṣālayet | na darbhaiḥ parimṛjyāt | na mahājanavirodhaṃ kuryāt | na goṣṭhībhiḥ saṃbadhyet | na gaṇabandhusamavāyaṃ praviśet | nāyājyaṃ yājayet | nānuyogaṃ prabrūyāt" |

anuyogo dhanadānārtham anuvākam adhīṣvety adhyayanādeśaḥ |


        "na brahmavikrayam icchet | na vāhyamāne vāhaya gām iti brūyān na pariṣanmadhye svairavāk syāt" |

pariṣatkāryānuvāditvaṃ svairavāktvam |

	"nāniyukto 'grāsanaṃ gacchen nābhyadhikaṃ dadyān na pratigṛhṇīyāt" |

bhojyam. iti śeṣaḥ |

	"nonmattamūkān saṃskuryāt" |

nopanayītety arthaḥ |

	"na vadhabandhasamavāyaṃ gacchet" |

vadhabandhaprayojanaṃ samavāyaṃ melakaṃ na gacchet |

	"na dāvam" |

dāvo vanavahniḥ |

	"na dampatyor antaram | narṣīṇāṃ prabhavaṃ na nadīnāṃ na mahātmanām" |

prabhava utpattisthānam | **[225]**


        "na madyaṃ dadyāt | na pratigṛhṇīyāt | na dharmaṃ khyāpayet | nādharmaṃ saṃvṛtaṃ kuryāt | nāpasavyaṃ paridadyāt | na bhūmiṃ vilikhet | na pādenābhihanyāt | nāṅgamukhavāditrāṇi kuryāt | na kūpaśvabhrāṇi vilokayet | na lokavidviṣṭāni samācaret | sarvaṃ viruddhaṃ pariharet" |

hārītaḥ: 	"na gor mūtrapurīṣābhyām udvijet | na pathi śikhā visṛjet" |

śikhāḥ keśāḥ |


        vrīhinikaṣaṇatṛṇakuṭṭanaloṣṭacandanalekhanakarajadaśanavīṇāvādanāni varjayet | ātmastavāvamānāṃś ca madyaśuktavikārāṃś ca varjayet | na raktām agandhāṃ srajam ābadhnīyāt | anyatra kāñcanakamalakuvalebhyaḥ | nāśuciklinnapūtibhir dārubhir agnim indhīta | nāgnivelayoḥ pravaset | parvasu cāpatsu proṣito 'gnivelāyāṃ vāgyatas tāṃ pratidiśaṃ manasā dhyāyet | anupasthāya mantrato hutaṃ jñātvā prati va enā ity upasthāyābhibhāṣeta |


        	prati va enā namasāham emi sūktena bhikṣe sumatiṃ surāṇām |


        	rarāṇa tā maruto vedyābhir nihelo dhatta vi mucadhvam aśvān ||


        nādarbham agniṃ paricaret | nāyajñiyair juhuyāt | hutaśeṣaṃ brāhmaṇāya dadyāt | māṣamasūramadhumāṃsaparannamaithunāni vratye 'hanit varjayet |

vratyam agnyanvādhānadinam |


        noccair niśāyām abhibhāṣeta | nottarīyāntarīyavinimayaṃ kuryāt | na devagurubrāhmaṇaparīvādaṃ kuryāt | na caiṣāṃ dīyamānaṃ prati vārayet | steyino hi pramītāḥ pūrvadhaninām upakārāya jāyante | tasmān na steyaṃ kuryān na kārayet | nāvamanyeta |


        	nindāṃ mṛtyupadaṃ prāhur nikṛtiṃ tamasaḥ padam |


        	sarvabhūtātmabhūtatvād ārjavaṃ brahmaṇaḥ padam ||


        pāpād vopasargād vyādhisaṃkramaṇayogāt siddhyadarśanāc ca tasmāt pṛthakśaucāḥ śreyāṃsaḥ |


        	āsanaṃ śayanaṃ yānam antardhāya samācaret |


        	na caikabhojanaṃ prāhur brāhmaṇānāṃ svakair api ||

vyāsaḥ |

	yūkāmatkuṇadaṃśādīn khādataḥ svātmanas tanum |

	putravat parirakṣanti te narāḥ svargagāminaḥ(ṇaḥ) || **[226]**

kālikāpurāṇe |

	sopānatko devagṛham āruhed yas tu mānavaḥ |

	sa yāti narakaṃ ghoraṃ tāmisraṃ nāma namataḥ ||

bṛhaspatiḥ |

	ekapaṅktyupaviṣṭā ye na spṛśanti parasparam |

	bhasmanā kṛtamaryādā na teṣāṃ saṃkaro bhavet ||

	agninā bhasmanā caiva salilena viśeṣataḥ |

	dvāreṇa stambhamārgeṇa ṣaḍbhiḥ paṅktir vibhidyate || iti |

hārītaḥ |

	śuciṃ devāś ca rakṣanti rakṣanti pitaraḥ śucim |

	śucer bibhyati rakṣāṃsi ye cānye duṣṭacāriṇaḥ ||

	bhraṣṭaśaucaṃ naraṃ dṛṣṭvā prahiṃsantīha rakṣasāḥ |

	yakṣāḥ piśācā bhūtāni ye cāne 'py evamādayaḥ ||

	jñānaṃ dānaṃ tapas tyāgo mantrakarmavidhikriyāḥ |

	maṅgalācāraniyamāḥ śaucabhraṣṭasya niṣphalāḥ ||

	dvau māsau pāyayed vatsaṃ tṛtīye dvistanaṃ duhet |

	caturthe tristanaṃ śeṣaṃ yathānyāyaṃ yathābalam ||

	nastanaṃ damanaṃ bāle vāhanaṃ ca na śasyate |

	vṛddhānāṃ durbalānāṃ ca prajāpativaco yathā ||

nastanaṃ nāsikābhedaḥ | tathā |

	vṛddhān nātivadej jātu na ca saṃpreṣayed api |

	nāsīnaḥ syāt sthiteṣv evam āyur asya nirasyati ||

tathā |

	gṛhe pārāvatā dhanyāḥ śukā vai śārikās tathā |

	gṛha ete praśastāḥ syus tathā vai tailapāyikāḥ ||

	upadīpakāś ca gṛdhrāś ca kapotā bhramarās tathā |

	nivaseran yadā tatra śāntim eva tadācaret ||

	amaṅgalyāni caitāni divākrośo mahātmanām |

	mahātmanāṃ ca guhyāni vaktavyāni na karhicit ||

	pānīyasya kriyā naktaṃ na kāryā bhūtim icchatā |

	bhuktvā prasādhanaṃ varjyaṃ varjyāś ca niśi saktavaḥ ||

	prāṅmukhaḥ śmaśrukarmāṇi kārayet tu sadā naraḥ |

	udaṅmukho vā rājendra tathāyur vindate mahat || **[227]**

tathā |

	sutastriyāś ca śayanaṃ saha bhojyaṃ ca varjayet |

	āhāraṃ maithunaṃ nidrāṃ saṃdhyakāle vivarjayet ||

	karma cādhyayanaṃ caiva tathā dānapratigrahau |

	gokharoṣṭraṃ ca nārohen na ca gacched divā striyam ||

	snānaṃ caṅkramaṇaṃ svapnaṃ digvāsā na samācaret ||

viṣṇuḥ: "na sarvaśastraiḥ krīḍeta devabrāhmaṇaśāstramahātmanāṃ parivādaṃ varjayet | parvasu na tṛṇam api cchindyāt" | viṣṇupurāṇam |

	virodhaṃ nottamair gacchen nādhamaiś ca sadā budhaḥ |

	vivādaś ca vivāhaś ca tulyarūpair nṛpeṣyate ||

smṛtyantaram |

	madyavikrayasaṃdhānadānādānāni nācaret |

uśanā |

	tithiṃ pakṣasya na brūyān na nakṣatrāṇi nirdiśet |

āpastambaḥ |

	saṃpādayati yo vipraḥ snānaṃ tīrthaphalaṃ japam |

	saṃpādī badhyate doṣais tasya saṃpadyate phalam ||

paiṭhīnasiḥ |

	apeyaṃ hi sadā toyaṃ rātrau madhyamayāmayoḥ |

	snānaṃ caiva na kartavyaṃ tathaivācamanakriyā ||

	mattapramattonmattapatitaiḥ saha saṃbhāṣaṃ na kurvīta |

pramattaḥ pramādaśīlaḥ |

	nāpuṣpitaṃ vṛkṣam ārohet | tathā nānyasmai dīyamānaṃ prati vadet ||

mārkaṇḍeyaḥ |

	baliṃ snānabhuvaṃ caiva śmaśānabalim eva ca |

	na gacched bandhanāgāraṃ vadhyabhūmiṃ ca garhitām ||

	antaḥpuraṃ vittagṛhaṃ paradyūtagṛhaṃ tathā |

	nordhvajānuś ciraṃ tiṣṭhed vatsatantrīṃ ca na laṅghayet ||

	samālyo nācaret snānaṃ na dvivāsā vikāraṇam |

vikāraṇaṃ nirnimittam |

	mlecchaveśo na kartavyo mlecchabhāṣā tathaiva ca ||

	nāsaṃvṛtamukhaḥ kuryād dh(gh)āsyaṃ jṛmbhāṃ tathaiva ca |

	gopayej janmanakṣatraṃ dhanasāraṃ gṛhe malam ||

**[228]**	vegarodho na kartavyas tv anyatra krodhavegataḥ |

	nopekṣitavyo vyādhiḥ syān mṛtyur alpo 'pi bhārgava ||

	na huṃ kuryāc chavaṃ pūrvaṃ bibhṛyān nāgnivāriṇī ||

śaṅkhalikhitau: "nāpo 'gniṃ caikato dhārayet" | ekata ekasmin hastapādau | mārkaṇḍeyaḥ |

	na bhuktamātrasyāyasyen nīcasevāṃ ca varjayet |

	pādaṃ padā ca nākrāmen na kaṇḍūyen na śodhayet ||

	vedaśāstranarendrāgnidevanindāṃ vivarjayet |

	nirāsanasya suptasya tiṣṭhataś ca tathaiva ca ||

	tathā bhuktavato nityaṃ snātasya ruṣitasya ca |

	yātrāyuddhotsukasyāpi śmaśrukarma vivarjayet ||

	puṣpāṇy akālarūḍhāni phalāny api tathaiva ca |

	vikāravac ca yat kiṃcit tat prayatnena varjayet ||

vikāravad adbhutam |

	divā kapitthacchāyāṃ ca rātrau dadhi śamīṃ tathā |

	kārpāsaṃ dantakāṣṭhaṃ ca śakrād api harec chriyam ||

	aṣṭamīṃ ca tathā ṣaṣṭhīṃ navamīṃ ca caturdaśīm |

	varjayec chiraso 'bhyaṅgaṃ parvasaṃdhiṃ tathaiva ca ||

	tathaivāmalakaiḥ snānaṃ saptamīṣu vivarjayet |

	vinā tu satataṃ snānaṃ na snāyād daśamīṣu ca ||

	amāvasyāsu sarvāsu navavastraṃ na dhārayet |

	gogajāśvājapuccheṣu kharasya ca viśeṣataḥ ||

	yal lagnam udakaṃ tasmād vipruṣaṃ dūratas tyajet |

	śūrpavātanakhāgrāmbu snānavastraghaṭodakam ||

	mārjanīreṇukeśāmbu hanti puṇyaṃ purā kṛtam |

	mālyānulepanād agraṃ na pradadyāt tu kasyacit ||

	anyatra devatāvipragurubhyo bhṛgunandana |

	na gacched garbhiṇīṃ nārīṃ malināṃ sitamūrdhajām ||

	rajasvalāṃ bhuktavatīṃ nāyonau na bubhukṣitaḥ |

	na svaped yeṣu deśeṣu teṣu deśeṣu cāpy atha ||

	dīkṣito varjayed yatnāt kṛtvā śrāddhaṃ ca mānavaḥ | **[229]**

dīkṣito 'nunmuktadīkṣaḥ | purāṇāt |

	kriyāṃ yaḥ kurute mohād anācamyeha nāstikaḥ |

	bhavanti hi vṛthā tasya kriyāḥ sarvā na saṃśayaḥ ||

śātātapaḥ |

	ajāvireṇusaṃsparśād āyur lakṣmīś ca hīyate |

	śvakākoṣṭrakharolūkasūkaragrāmyapakṣiṇām ||

baijavāpaḥ |

	rathāśvagajadhānyānāṃ gavāṃ caiva rajaḥ śubham |

	apraśastaṃ samūhinyajāvirāsabhavāsasām ||

samūhinī mārjanī | ṣaṭtriṃśanmatāt |

	prakṣālya hastau gṛhṇīyād oṣadhyamalake naraḥ |

	śraso muṇḍanaṃ kṛtvā punaḥ prakṣālayet tu tat ||

manuḥ |

	maṅgalācārayuktaḥ syāt prayatātmā jitendriyaḥ |

	japec ca juhuyāc caiva vinipāto na vidyate ||

	vedam evābhyasen nityaṃ yathākālam atandritaḥ |

	taṃ hy asyāhuḥ paraṃ dharmam upadharmo 'nya ucyate ||

	vedābhyāsena satataṃ śaucena tapasaiva ca |

	adroheṇa ca bhūtānāṃ jātiṃ smarati paurvikīm ||

	paurvikīṃ saṃsarañ jātiṃ brahmaivābhyasate punaḥ |

	brahmābhyāsena cānantam ajasraṃ phalam aśnute ||

	sāvitrāñ jātihomāṃś ca kuryāt parvasu nityaśaḥ ||

jātir janma | savitṛdai(de)vatyān duritaśāntiprayojanān ājyahomān kṛṣṇaśuklapañcadaśīṣu sadā kuryād ity arthaḥ |

	aṣṭakāsu pitṝn arcen nityam anvaṣṭakāsu ca |

svagṛhyoktavidhāneneti śeṣaḥ | nityaṃ sarvadety arthaḥ |

	abhivādya ca vṛddhāṃś ca dadyāc caivāsanaṃ svakam |

	kṛtāñjalir upāsīta gacchataḥ pṛṣṭhato 'nviyāt ||

	nāstikyaṃ vedanindāṃ ca devatānāṃ ca kutsanam |

	dveṣaṃ stambhaṃ ca mānaṃ ca krodhaṃ taikṣṇyaṃ ca varjayet || **[230]**

nāsti daivam iti matir yasya sa nāstikaḥ | tasya bhāvo nāstikyam | vederṣyāprāmāṇyādhyavasāyo nindā | devatānāṃ brahmādīnāṃ kutsanaṃ nindanam | yathā — brahmā duhitaram agāt | īśo brahmaṇaḥ śiraś cicchedeti | stambho 'haṃkārād apraṇāmaḥ | māno 'haṃkāraḥ | krodho 'kṣamā | taikṣṇyaṃ vākpāruṣyam |

	adhārmiko naro yo hi yasya cāpy anṛtaṃ dhanam |

	hiṃsāratiś ca yo nityaṃ nehāsau sukham edhate ||

	na sīdann api dharmeṇa mano 'dharme niveśayet |

	adhārmikāṇāṃ pāpānām āśu paśyan viparyayam ||

	nādharmaś carito loke sadyaḥ phalati gaur iva |

	śanair āvartamānas tu kartur mūlāni kṛntati ||

	yadi nātmani putreṣu no cet pautreṣu naptṛṣu |

	na tv evaṃ hi kṛto dharmaḥ kartur bhavati niṣphalaḥ ||

	na dharmasyāpadeśena pāpaṃ kṛtvā vrataṃ caret |

	vratena pāpaṃ pracchādya kurvan strīśudradambhanam ||

dharmacchalena prāyaścittaṃ na kuryād ity arthaḥ |

	aliṅgī liṅgaveśena yo vṛttim upajīvati |

	sa liṅgināṃ haraty enas tiryagyonau ca jāyate ||

āśramiṇo liṅginaḥ | teṣāṃ liṅgair daṇḍādibhiḥ svayam aliṅgī tadvṛttiṃ bhikṣāpratigrāhādikāṃ ya upajīvati sa āśramiṇāṃ pāpaṃ tiryagyoniṃ cāśnute |

	yamān seveta satataṃ na nityaṃ niyamān budhaḥ |

	yamān pataty akurvāṇo niyamān kevalān bhajan ||

	śaucam ijyā tapo dānaṃ svādhyāyopasthanigrahau |

	vratopavāsau maunaṃ ca snānaṃ ca niyamā daśa ||

	ānṛśaṃsyaṃ kṣamā satyam ahiṃsā dama ārjavam |

	dhyānaṃ prasādo mādhuryaṃ mārdravaṃ ca yamā daśa ||

	na vismayet tapasā vaded dṛṣṭyā ca nānṛtam |

	nārto 'py apavaded viprān na dattaṃ parikīrtayet ||

	yajño 'nṛtena kṣarati tapaḥ kṣarati vismayāt |

	āyur viprāvamānena dānaṃ tu parikīrtanāt || **[231]**

vismayaḥ ślāghā | evamādiśrutismṛtibhya ācāro veditavyaḥ | sarvaś ca snātakenāvaśyaṃ kāryaḥ | tad āha manuḥ |

	ācārāl labhate hy āyur ācārād īpisitāḥ prajāḥ |

	ācārād dhanam akṣayyam ācāro hanty alakṣaṇam ||

	durācāro hi puruṣo loke bhavati ninditaḥ |

	duḥkhabhāgī ca satataṃ vyādhito 'lpāyur eva ca ||

	sarvalakṣaṇahīno 'pi sarvadācāravān naraḥ |

	śraddadhāno 'nasūyaś ca śataṃ varṣāṇi jīvati || 1.154 ||

_kiṃ ca_ |

	**gobrāhmaṇānalānnāni nocchiṣṭo na padā spṛśet |**

ucchiṣṭo gavādi na spṛśet | anucchiṣṭo 'pi padā | ucchiṣṭo 'trāśuciḥ | manuḥ |

	spṛṣṭvaitāni śucir nityam adbhir prāṇān upaspṛśet |

	gātrāṇi caiva sarvāṇi nābhiṃ pāṇitalena tu ||

prāṇaśabdenātra tatsthānāni mūrdhanyacchidrāṇi śrotrādīni lakṣyante | gātraśabdenāpy uromūrdhaskandhā ucyante | tatsparśasyācamanaprakaraṇe śuddhihetutvadarśanāt | śuddhyarthaṃ cedaṃ prāṇādisparśanaṃ vidhīyate ||

_kiṃ ca_ |

	**na nindātāḍane kuryāt**

parasya nindāṃ tāḍanaṃ ca na kuryāt |

_atrāpavādam āha_ |

		**putraṃ śiṣyaṃ ca tāḍayet || 1.155 ||**

śikṣārtham anayos tāḍanānugraho nānyathā | tad āha manuḥ |

	parasya daṇḍaṃ nodyacchet kruddho nainaṃ nipātayet |

	anyatra putrāc chiṣyād vā śikṣārthaṃ tāḍayet tu tau ||

śiṣyaḥ śāsanīyaḥ | putrasya pṛthaggrahaṇaṃ gobalīvardanyāyena | ata eva viṣṇuḥ: "śāsyaṃ śāset tāḍayet" iti śāsyaśabdam eva prayuktavān | atra niyamam evāha |

	adhobhāge śarīrasya nottamāṅge na vakṣasi |

	ato 'nyathā tu praharan pāpayukto bhaven naraḥ || **[232]**

śarīrasyādhobhāge nābher adhastāt tāḍayet | uttamāṅge śirasi vakṣasi na tāḍayet | adhobhāganiyamenaiva śirovakṣasor vyāvṛttisiddhau tayoḥ pṛthaṅniṣedhas tato 'nyatrottarakāye pi tāḍananugrahārthaḥ | ata eva viṣṇuḥ: "śāsyaṃ tāḍayet taṃ tu veṇudalena rajjvā vā pṛṣṭhata eva" iti | anyathā praharan gurur api pāpavān syāt || 1.155 ||

	**karmaṇā manasā vācā yatnād dharmaṃ samācaret |**

atra yatnād iti vidhīyate | anyad anūdyate | tathā ca sati karmaṇetipadam anuvācakatvād vāṅmanaḥśabdasāhacaryāc ca lakṣaṇayā śarīre vartate | tataś cāyam artho bhavati — śarīreṇa yaṃ dharmaṃ tapaścaryādikam ācaret, yaṃ ca manasā yāgadānādikam, yaṃ ca vācā vedādhyayanādikam, taṃ yatnād ādarāt samācaret, na pramādyed ity arthaḥ | dharmasya sarvapuruṣārthahetutvāt | ata eva manuḥ |

	dharmaṃ śanaiḥ saṃcinuyād valmīkam iva vaprikāḥ |

	na putradāraṃ na jñātir dharmas tiṣṭhati kevalaḥ ||

	ekaḥ prajāyate jantur eka eva vilīyate |

	eko 'nubhuṅkte sukṛtam eka eva ca duṣkṛtam ||

	mṛtaṃ śarīraṃ saṃtyajya kāṣṭhaloṣṭasamaṃ kṣitau |

	vimukhā bāndhavā yānti dharmas tam anugacchati ||

	tasmād dharmaṃ sahāyārthaṃ nityaṃ saṃcinuyāc chanaiḥ ||

atrāpavādam āha |

	**asvargyaṃ lokavidviṣṭaṃ dharmyam apy ācaren na tu || 1.156 ||**

asvargyam anāmuṣmikam aihikaphalaṃ laukikair vidviṣṭaṃ ninditaṃ dharma(rmya)m api śāstravihitam api nācared abhicārādikam | vihito hi baudhāyanenābhicāraḥ kvacid iṣyate | yathā: "ṣaṭsv anabhicaran patati" iti | manur api |

	kṣatriyo bāhuvīryeṇa tared āpadam ātmanaḥ |

	dhanena vaiśyaśūdrau tu japahomair dvijottamaḥ ||

	svavīryād rājavīryāc ca svavīryaṃ balavattaram |

	tasmāt svenaiva vīryeṇa nigṛhṇīyād arīn dvijaḥ || iti | **[233]**

tasmād abhicāro madhuparkādau govadho vidhvāniyogaḥ śūdrāvivāha ityādayo 'svargyatvāl lokavidviṣṭatvād vihitā api na kāryā viśeṣeṇa kaliyuge | ata eva smaranti |

	gopaśuṃ devarāt putraṃ satrayāgaṃ kamaṇḍalum |

	surāprayogaṃ bhikṣuṃ ca na kurvīta kalau yuge ||

bhikṣuḥ paramahaṃsaḥ | tathā |

	akṣatā naramedhaś ca goyajñaś ca kamaṇḍaluḥ |

	devarāc ca sutotpattiḥ kalau pañca vivarjayet ||

ata eva madhuparke 'nukalpasmaraṇam | yan mārkaṇḍeyaḥ |

	mādhuparkikapaśvarthe tato mātrāṃ nivedayet |

	sahiraṇyaṃ bījapātraṃ draviṇena sadaiva tu ||

	paśuḥ kalau na kartavya ity āha bhagavān bhṛguḥ ||

mādhuparkikapaśur atra gaur eva | madhuparke "tasmā asipāṇir gāṃ prāha" ityādau gohananakriyāniyogādeḥ smaraṇāt kalau gohanansya niṣedhopapatteś ca || 1.156 ||

	**mātṛpitratithibhrātṛjāmisaṃbandhimātulaiḥ |**

**	bālavṛddhāturācāryavaidyasaṃśritabāndhavaiḥ || 1.157 ||**

**	ṛtvikpurohitāmātyabhāryādāsasanābhibhiḥ |**

**	vivādaṃ varjayitvā tu sarvāṃl lokāñ jayed gṛhī || 1.158 ||**

mātrādibhir vivādaṃ kalahaṃ varjayitvā sarvān bhūrādīṃl lokāñ jayati bhuṅkte | jāmayo bhaginīprabhṛtayaḥ svavāsinyaḥ | saṃbandhino vaivāhyāḥ | vaidyo bhiṣag vedavidyāvān vā | saṃśrita āśritaḥ śiṣya iti yāvat | sanābhayaḥ sapiṇḍāḥ | anye prasiddhāḥ | manus tūktavivādān varjayataḥ sarvapāpakṣayam ācāryādibhir jitasya ca brahmalokādijayaphalam āha |

	bālavṛddhātuair vaidyair jñātisaṃbandhibāndhavaiḥ |

	mātāpitṛbhyāṃ jāmībhir bhrātrā putreṇa bhāryayā ||

	duhitrā dāsavargeṇa vivādaṃ na samācaret ||

	etāṃs tyajan vivādāṃś ca sarvapāpaiḥ pramucyate |

	etair jitaiś ca jayati sarvāṃl lokān imān gṛhī ||

atra caitair iti vakṣyamāṇācāryābhiprāyam |

**[234]**	ācāryo brahmalokeśaḥ prājāpatye pitā prabhuḥ |

	atithis tv indralokeśo devalokasya cartvijaḥ ||

	jāmayo 'psarasāṃ loke vaiśvadevasya bāndhavāḥ |

	saṃbandhino 'pāṃ lokasya pṛthivyā mātṛmātulau ||

	ākāśeśās tu vijñeyā bālavṛddhakṛśāturāḥ |

	bhrāta jyeṣṭhaḥ samaḥ pitrā bhāryā putraḥ svikā tanuḥ ||

	chāyā svo dāsavargas tu duhitā kṛpaṇaṃ param |

	tasmād etair adhikṣiptaḥ sahetāsaṃjvaraḥ sadā ||

kṛpāviṣayaḥ (?) | asaṃjvaro 'saṃtaptaḥ || 1.157 ||

_api ca_ |

	**pañca piṇḍān anuddhṛtya na snāyāt paravāriṣu |**

parakīyavāribhyaḥ pañca piṇḍān anuddhṛtya bahir anutkṣipya teṣu snānaṃ na kuryāt | anena cārthād vakṣyamāṇamukhyasnānāṅgajalālābhe paravāriṣv api piṇḍoddharaṇapūrvakaṃ snānaṃ vidhīyate | yāni tu jalāni svāminā yathāśāstraṃ paropakārāyotsṛṣṭāni tebhyaḥ piṇḍā noddhartavyāḥ, parakīyatvābhāvāt | atra manuḥ |

	parakīyanipāneṣu na snāyād dhi kadācana |

	nipānakartuḥ snātvā tu duṣkṛtāṃśena lipyate ||

baudhāyanaḥ |

	na kadācid budhaḥ snāyāt parakhāte jalāśaye |

	ananuddhṛtya kūpe vā mṛtpiṇḍān pañca sapta vā ||

_idānīṃ mukhyāni snānāṅgajalāny āha_ |

	**snāyān nadīdevakhātahradeśu ca saraḥsu ca || 1.159 ||**

nadyādiṣu snāyāt | nadī sravantī | devaiḥ khātam iti yat smaryate tad devakhātam | nadījalam avicchinnapravāhaṃ hradaḥ | saraḥ sthāvaram akṛtrimaṃ jalam | cakārād gartaprasravaṇādiṣv api | tathā ca manuḥ |

	nadīṣu devakhāteṣu hradeṣu ca saraḥsu ca |

	snānaṃ samācaren nityaṃ gartaprasravaṇādiṣu ||

gartasvarūpam āha kātyāyanaḥ |

	dhanuḥsahasrāṇy aṣṭau ca gatir yāsāṃ na vidyate |

	na tā nadīśabdavahā gartās te parikīrtitāḥ || iti | **[235]**

na tā āpo nadīśabdavahā ity arthaḥ | parvatādeḥ stoko jalapravāhaḥ prasravaṇam | atra ca prāśastyakramam āha mārkaṇḍeyaḥ |

	bhūmiṣṭham uddhṛtāt puṇyaṃ tataḥ prasravaṇodakam |

	tato 'pi sārasaṃ puṇyaṃ tasmān nādeyam ucyate ||

	tīrthatoyaṃ tataḥ puṇyaṃ nāṅgaṃ puṇyaṃ tu sarvataḥ ||

yogayājñavalkyaḥ |

	prabhūte vidyamāne tu udake sumanohare |

	nālpodake dvijaḥ snāyān nadīṃ cotsṛjya kṛtrime ||

	trirātraphaladā nadyo yāḥ kāścid asamudragāḥ |

	samudragās tu pakṣasya māsasya saritāṃ patiḥ ||

trirātraphaladās trirātropavāsaphaladā ity arthaḥ | evaṃ pakṣamāsayor api | prasaṅgāt samudrasnānādiviṣayaṃ kiṃcid ucyate | tatra smṛtyantaram |

	aśvatthasāgarau caiva na spraṣṭavyau kadācana |

	aśvatthaṃ mandavāreṣu sāgaraṃ parvaṇi spṛśet ||

mandaḥ śanaiścaraḥ | parvāmāvāsyā pūrṇamāsī ca | tathā |

	sindhoḥ setoḥ sarasvatyā gaṅgāyāḥ puruṣottamāt |

	nāparvaṇi sarinnāthaṃ spṛśed anyatra kutracit ||

tathā |

	kartuṃ pravṛtto vidhivat snānaśrāddhādikāṃ kriyām |

	kṛttiṃ pratyabhimantryeha kṣipet pāṣāṇasaptakam ||

	pippalādasamutpanne kṛtte lokabhayaṃkari |

	pāṣāṇaṃ te mayā dattam āhārārthaṃ prakalpitam ||

vyāsaḥ |

	agniś ca te yonirilā ca deho retodhā viṣṇur amṛtaṃ ca nābhiḥ |

	etad bruvan pāṇḍava satyavākyaṃ tato 'vagāheta patiṃ nadīnām ||

	ājanmaśatasāhasraṃ yat pāpaṃ kurute kvacit |

	mucyate sarvapāpebhyaḥ snātvaivaṃ lavaṇāmbhasi ||

	anyathā tu kuruśreṣṭha devayonir apāṃ patiḥ |

	kuśāgreṇāpi kaunteya na spraṣṭavyo mahodadhiḥ ||

smṛtyantaram |

	vapanaṃ copavāsaṃ ca sarvatīrtheṣu karayet |

marīciḥ |

	nabhonabhasyayor madhye sarvā nadyo rajasvalāḥ |

	tāsu snānaṃ na kurvīta devarṣipitṛtarpaṇam || **[236]**

mārkaṇḍeya |

	ādityaduhitā gaṅgā plakṣajātā sarasvatī |

	rajasā nābhibhūyante ye cānye nadasaṃjñakāḥ ||

kurukṣetre yā sarasvatī sā plakṣajātā | smṛtyantarāt |

	kālindī gomatī gaṅgā pavitrā devanirmitā |

	sāmānyād guṇayogāc ca rajo nābhibhavaty ataḥ ||

nigamaḥ |

	gaṅgā dharmadravaḥ puṇyā yamunā ca sarasvatī |

	antargatarajoyogāḥ sarvāheṣu ca cāmalāḥ ||

gārgyaḥ |

	pratyāvṛtte 'mbhasi snānaṃ varjyaṃ nadyāṃ dvijātibhiḥ |

	tasyāṃ rajakatīrthaṃ ca daśahastena copari ||

nigamaḥ |

	pratisroto rajoyogo rathyājalaniveśanam l

	gaṅgāyāṃ na praduṣyanti sa hi dharmadravaḥ svayam ||

	yāḥ śoṣam upagacchanti grīṣme kusarito bhuvi |

	tāsu snānaṃ na kurvīta prāvṛṣy ambudarśanāt ||

yogayājñavalkyaḥ |

	agrāhyās tv agrimā āpo nadyāḥ prathamavegitaḥ |

	prakṣobhitāś ca kenāpi pārśvatīrthaviniḥsṛtāḥ ||

agrimā navāḥ | tathā ca smṛtyantaram |

	ajā gāvo mahiṣyaś ca brāhmaṇyaś ca prasūtikāḥ |

	daśarātreṇa śudhyanti bhūmiṣṭhaṃ ca navodakam ||

tīrthaṃ jalāvataraṇamārgaḥ | vyāsaḥ |

	nadyā yac ca paribhraṣṭaṃ nadyā yac ca vivarjitam |

	gatapratyāgataṃ yac ca tat toyaṃ parivarjayet ||

	nadyām astamite snānaṃ varjayet sarvadā naraḥ |

	nadyāṃ snāto nadīm anyāṃ na praśaṃseta dharmavit ||

	antardhāya ca na snāyān na ca tīrthe jalāntare |

	na meheta jaladroṇyāṃ snātuṃ ca na nadīṃ taret ||

asyārthaḥ — nadīto bhraṣṭaṃ nadyā vinirgatya tato vicchinnaṃ nadyā saha saṃgamārtham abhipravṛttaṃ tad asaṃgataṃ yat tat tayā varjitam āvarte gatapratyāgatam | antardhāya vastrādinā | tīrthāntare ca tīrthāntarajalena na snāyād iti || 1.159 ||

_kiṃ ca_ |

	**paraśayyāsanodyānagṛhayānāni varjayet |**

**[237]	adattāni**

paraśayyādīni pareṇādattāni varjayet | tadupajīvanaṃ varjayed ity arthaḥ | udyānam upavanam | prasiddham anyat | atra manuḥ |

	yānaśayyāsanāny asya kūpodyānagṛhāṇi ca |

	adattāny upayuñjāna enasaḥ syāt turīyabhāk ||

**iti śrīvidyādharavaṃśaprabhavaśrīśilāhāranarendrajīmūtavāhanānvayaprabhūta-**

**śrīmadaparādityadevaviracite yājñavalkīyadharmaśāstranibandhe**

**snātakavrataprakaraṇam || 5 ||**

**atha saṭīkayājñavalkyasmṛtau**

**bhojyābhojyabhakṣyābhakṣyaprakaraṇam || 6 ||**

_adhunā bhojyābhojyabhakṣyābhakṣyaprakaraṇam ārabhate | tatrābhojyāny āha |_

		**agnihīnasya nānnam adyād anāpai || 1.160 ||**

saty apy adhikāre śrautasmārtāgniparigraham akurvata utsṛṣṭāgneś cānnam anāpadi na bhuñjīta || 1.160 ||

	**kadaryabaddhacaurāṇāṃ klībaraṅgāvatāriṇām |**

**	vaiṇābhiśastavārdhuṣyagaṇikāgaṇadīkṣiṇām || 1.161 ||**

**	cikitsakāturakruddhapuṃścalīmattavidviṣām |**

**	krūrograpatitavrātyadāmbhikocchiṣṭabhojinām || 1.162 ||**

**	avīrastrīsvarṇakārastrījitagrāmayājinām |**

**	śastravikrayakarmāratantuvāyaśvavṛttinām || 1.163 ||**

**	nṛśaṃsarājarajakakṛtaghnavadhajīvinām |**

**	cailadhāvasurājīvasahopapativeśmanām || 1.164 ||**

**	eṣām annaṃ na bhoktavyaṃ somavikrayiṇas tathā |**

**[238]**

kadaryādīnāṃ somavikrayiṇaś cānnaṃ na bhoktavyam | kadaryo yo lobhād vidyamānam api dhanaṃ na bhuṅkte na ca dadāti | tad uktam |

	ātmānaṃ dharmakṛtyaṃ ca putradārāṃś ca pīḍayan |

	lobhād yaḥ pitarau bhṛtyān sa kadarya iti smṛtaḥ ||

baddho nigaḍitaḥ | cauraḥ stenaḥ | klībaḥ paṇḍaḥ | raṅgāvatārī naṭādiḥ | vaiṇo vīṇāvādanajīvī, veṇucchedanajīvī vā | abhiśastaḥ pāpakāritvenādhikṣiptaḥ | vārdhuṣyaṃ niṣiddhavṛddhyupajīvanam | tena ca tadvāṃl lakṣyate | ātmastutiparanindākartā vā vārdhuṣikaḥ | tathā ca viṣṇuḥ |

	yas tu nindet paraṃ jīvaṃ praśaṃsaty ātmano guṇān |

	sa vai vārdhuṣiko nāma brahmavādiṣu garhitaḥ || iti ||

gaṇikā veśyā | gaṇaḥ saṅghaḥ | tadannam anyasyābhojyam | dīkṣī dīkṣitaḥ, tasya ca prāg agnīṣomīyavapāhomād abhojyānnatā | tathā ca śrutiḥ: "aśitavyaṃ vapāyāṃ hutāyām" iti | āpastambas tu "pūrvam api vapāhomād yajñārthe dravye pṛthak kṛte yad avaśiṣṭaṃ tad dīkṣitasyāpi bhoktavyam" ity āha | dīkṣitaḥ krītarājakaḥ | agnīṣomīyasaṃsthāyām eva vapāyāṃ hutāyāṃ dīkṣitasya bhoktavyam | "yajñārthe vā nirdiṣṭe śeṣād bhuñjīran" iti brāhmaṇam iti | cikitsakaś cikitsāvṛttiḥ | asamyakcikitsaka itaro 'pi | āturo rogārtaḥ | kruddhaḥ kupitaḥ | puṃścalī vyabhicāriṇī | matto dhanādinā | viprād anyo madyena vā | vidviṭ śatruḥ | krūraḥ sthirakrodhaḥ | ugraḥ paraduḥkhotpādanapaṭuḥ | kṣatriyāc chūdrāyām utpanno vā | patito brahmahatyādikartā stenād anyaḥ, tasya cauraśabdena saṃgṛhītatāt | atha vā patitād anyaś cauraśabdenocyate | vrātyaḥ patitasāvitrīkaḥ | dāmbhikaḥ khyātilābhādiprayojanadharmānuṣṭhānaḥ | ucchiṣṭabhojī parocchiṣṭabhojanaśīlaḥ | avīrā patiputrarahitā | svarṇakāraḥ prasiddhaḥ | strījitaḥ strīparatantraḥ | grāmayājako 'nekayājakaḥ | śastravikrayī khaḍgādivikrayajīvī | karmāro lohakāraḥ | tantuvāyo vastrasyūtasya kartā, pāṭitavastrasaṃdhāyako vā | śvavṛttavān sevakaḥ | yad vā śunāṃ vṛttaṃ vartanam asti yasmin sa śvavṛtī śvaval lubdhaka ity arthaḥ | sa cāniṣucāry evābhojyānna ity āha gautamaḥ: "mṛgayur aniṣucārī" iti | iṣucāriṇas tu bhojyam ity āha viṣṇuḥ: "na mṛgayor iṣucāriṇaḥ parivarjyam annam" iti | nṛśaṃso ghātakaḥ | rājā bhūpo na tu kṣatriyaḥ | rajako vastrādirāgakartā | kṛtaghna **[239]** upakāranāśakaḥ | vadhajīvī prāṇivadhena yo jīvati | cailadhāvo vastraprakṣālakaḥ | surājīvaḥ surājīvikaḥ | sahopapativeśmā nijabhāryājārasahitagṛhaḥ | somavikrayī somalatāvikrayī | 

	prasaṅgād anyad apy ucyate | bhaviṣyatpurāṇam |

	abhojyaṃ brāhmaṇasyānnaṃ vṛṣalena nimantritam |

	tathaiva vṛṣalasyānnaṃ brāhmaṇena nimantritam ||

paiṭhīnasiḥ: "sāṃvatsaraghāṇṭikagrāmakūṭānnaṃ viṣam | tathā parivittiparividdhānaviddhaprajananavṛṣalīpatididhiṣūpatipunarbhūputrāṇāṃ rudhiram" | sāṃvatsaro nakṣatrajīvī | ghāṇṭiko ghaṇṭāśilpaḥ | tad uktam: "rājñāṃ saṃbodhasamaye ghaṇṭāśilpās tu ghāṇṭikāḥ" | grāmakūṭakaḥ prasiddhaḥ | parivittyādīnāṃ lakṣaṇaṃ śrāddhaprakaraṇe lakṣyate | viddhaprajanano viddhaliṅgaḥ | yamaḥ |

	cakropajīvī gāndharvaḥ kitavas taskaras tathā |

	dhvajī dāropajīvīca śūdrādhyāpakayājakau ||

	kulālaś citrakarmā ca vārdhuṣī carmavikrayī ||

cakropajīvī śākaṭikaḥ | gāndharvo gāyanaḥ | dhvajī madyavikrayī | tathā |

	yathā jalaṃ nirgamaneṣv apeyaṃ nadīgataṃ tat punar eva peyam |

	tathānnapānaṃ vidhipūrvam āgataṃ dvijātipātrāntaritaṃ na duṣyati ||

nirgamanāni rathyodakapravāhāḥ |

	brāhmaṇasya sadāśnīyāt kṣatriyasya tu parvasu |

	prakṛteṣu ca vaiśyasya na śūdrasya kadācana ||

prakṛteṣūtsaveṣu ca |

	tathā rājabhṛtasyānnaṃ caurasyānnaṃ tathaiva ca |

	sūtake mṛtake cānnaṃ svargastham api pātayet ||

	avaliptasya mūrkhasya duṣṭavṛttasya durmateḥ |

	annam aśraddadhānasya yo bhuṅkte bhrūṇahā tu saḥ ||

ātityapurāṇe |

	viṣṇuṃ jāmātaraṃ manyet tasya manyuṃ na kārayet |

	aprajāyāṃ tu kanyāyāṃ nāśnīyāt tasya vai gṛhe ||

	gāndharve caiva rājanyaḥ kuryād vai gamanāgamam || **[240]**

	bra(brā)hamadeyāṃ na vai kanyāṃ datvāśnīyāt kadācana |

	atha bhuñjīta mohād yaḥ pūyāśī narake vaset ||

brāhmādivivāhacatuṣṭayapariṇītā brāhmadeyā | vasiṣṭhaḥ |

	śraddadhānasya bhoktavyaṃ caurasyāpi viśeṣataḥ |

	na tv evaṃ bahuyājyasya yaś copanayate bahūn ||

abhojyam ity anuvṛttāv āpastambaḥ: "yaś ca sarvān varjayeta sarvānnāśī ca" | śaṅkhalikhitau: "bhītāvagītaruditākranditāvākruṣṭakṣutaparibhuktavismitonmattāvadhūtarājapurohitānnāni varjayet" | kadaryādyannabhojane manuḥ prāyaścittam āha |

	bhuktvāto 'nyatamasyānnam amatyā kṣapaṇaṃ tryaham |

	matyā bhuktvācaret kṛcchraṃ reto viṇmūtram eva ca ||

atikṛcchre kṛcchraśabdaḥ, "eṣām annabhojaneṣv atikṛcchraḥ" it śaṅkhavacanāt || 1. 161–164 ||

	**goghrātaṃ śakunocchiṣṭaṃ padā spṛṣṭaṃ ca kāmataḥ || 1.165 ||**

**	piśunānṛtinoś caiva tathā cākrikabandinām |**

**	anarcitaṃ vṛthāmāṃsaṃ keśakīṭasamanvitam || 1.166 ||**

**	śuktaṃ paryuṣitocchiṣṭaṃ śvaspṛṣṭaṃ patitekṣitam |**

**	udakyāspṛṣṭasaṃghuṣṭaṃ paryāyānnaṃ ca varjayet || 167 ||**

goghrātādikam annaṃ vṛthāmāṃsaṃ ca varjayet | śakunaḥ pakṣī | piśuno doṣasūcakaḥ | anṛtī mithyāvādī | cākrikas tailikaḥ | abhiśastapatitacākrikatailika iti bhedasmaraṇāc chākaṭiko vā | vandī stāvakaḥ | anarcitam avajñādattam | vṛthāmāṃsaṃ śrāddhādiprayojanaśūnyaṃ māṃsam | śuktaṃ kālavaśād alam | paryuṣitam anyedyuḥ siddham | ucchiṣṭaṃ bhuktvā(ktā)vaśiṣṭam | saṃghuṣṭaṃ ko bhokṣyata ity abhikruṣṭam | paryāyānnaṃ kramānnaṃ ravidine 'sya somadine 'sya gṛhe bhoktavyam iti | paryācāntam iti pāṭhe paryācāntaṃ bāhulaṅghitam | śvagrahaṇaṃ kākādīnāṃ pradarśanārtham | patitagrahaṇaṃ caṇḍālādīnām | **[241]** bhaviṣyatpurāṇam |

	jātiduṣṭaṃ kriyāduṣṭaṃ kālāśrayavidūṣitam |

	saṃsargāśrayaduṣṭaṃ ca sahṛllekhaṃ svabhāvataḥ ||

jātiduṣṭādīnām udāharaṇāny āha |

	laśunaṃ gṛñjanaṃ caiva palāṇḍuṃ kavakāni ca |

	vārtākanālikālābu upeyāj jātidūṣitam ||

	na bhakṣayet kriyāduṣṭaṃ yaddṛṣṭaṃ patitaiḥ pṛthak |

	kāladuṣṭaṃ ca vijñeyaṃ hy astanaṃ cirasaṃsthitam ||

	dadhi bhakṣyaṃ vikāreṣu madhuvarjaṃ tad iṣyate |

	surālaśunasaṃspṛṣṭaṃ pīyūṣādisamanvitam ||

	saṃsargaduṣṭam etad dhi śudrocchiṣṭavad ācaret |

	śūdrocchiṣṭaṃ tu vijñeyaṃ pūrvaṃ śūdreṣu darśitam ||

	vicikitsā tu hṛdaye yasminn anne prajāyate |

	sahṛllekhaṃ tu vijñeyaṃ purīṣaṃ tu svabhāvataḥ ||

	rasaduṣṭaṃ vikārād dhi rasasyeti nidarśanāt |

	pāyasakṣīrapūpādi tasminn eva dine yathā ||

alābur atra dīrghālābor itaraḥ | dīrghasya śrāddhārhatvāt | adīrghasya jātiduṣṭasya palāṇḍuvan ninditasya śrāddeyatvānupapatteḥ | ata eva,

	alābuṃ grīvakaṃ cāṇuṃ karkarīṃ trapusīṃ tathā |

iti dīrghālāboḥ śrāddhārhatvāt | itarasya ca "pippalīsamukamṛṣabhūstṛṇāsurīsarṣapasurasa-kūṣmāṇḍālābuvārtākapālakyātaṇḍulīyakakusumbhapiṇḍamūlakamahiṣīkṣīrāṇi varjayet" ity aśrāddeyatvam | hārītaḥ |

	palāṇḍuṃ laśunaṃ śuktaṃ niryāsāṃś ceti sarvaśaḥ |

	kudhvanduṃ śvetavārtākaṃ kumbhāṇḍaṃ ca na bhakṣayet ||

kumbhāṇḍo dāḍimasadṛśaḥ phalaviśeṣaḥ | devalaḥ |

	na bījāny upayuñjīta rogāpattim ṛte budhaḥ |

	phalāny eṣām anantāni bījānāṃ hi vināśayet || **[242]**

vasiṣṭhaḥ: "ucchiṣṭam aguror abhojyaṃ svam ucchiṣṭam ucchiṣṭopahataṃ ca" | āpastambaḥ: "aprayatopahatam annam aprayataṃ na tv abhojyam | yasmiṃś cānne keśaḥ syād anyad vāmedhyam amedhyair avamṛṣṭaṃ kīṭo vāmedhyasevī | mūṣakalāṅgaṃ vā padā vopahataṃ sicā vā śunā vāpātreṇa vā dṛṣṭaṃ sicā vohapataṃ dāsyā vā naktam āhṛtaṃ bhuñjānaṃ vā yatra śūdra upaspṛśed anarhadbhir vā samānapaṅktau bhuñjāneṣu vā yatrānutthāyocchiṣṭaṃ prayacched ācāmed vā kutsayitvā vā yatrānnaṃ dadyur manuṣyair avaghrātam anyair vāmedhyaiḥ" | asyārthaḥ — aprayatenāśucinā puruṣeṇa spṛṣṭam annam aśuci bhavati, na punas tad abhojyam | aprayatasyānnasyāgnyadhiśrayaṇamadbhir vā prokṣaṇam, hiraṇyena vā chāgamukhena vā sparśanaṃ prayatatvaṃ karoti | aśuciśūdraspṛṣṭaṃ tv abhojyam eva | mūṣakalā mūṣapurīṣam | mūṣo mūṣakas tadaṅgaṃ vā pucchādi yasmin anne tad abhojyam iti vākyaparisamāptiḥ | sicā vastrāntenopahataṃ dasyā dāsena vā naktam āhṛtam | devalaḥ |

	avalīḍhaṃ śvamārjāradhvāṅkṣakukkuṭamūṣakaiḥ |

	bhojane nopayuñjīta tad amedhyaṃ hi sarvataḥ ||

	viśuddham api cāhāraṃ makṣikākrimijantubhiḥ |

	keśaromanakhair vāpi dūṣitaṃ parivarjayet ||

brahmapurāṇāt |

	ucchiṣṭena tu śūdreṇa saṃspṛṣṭaḥ pariveṣakaḥ |

	dravyahastaś ca yat kiṃcid dadyāt tac ca na bhakṣayet ||

tathā |

	śūdrabhuktāvaśiṣṭaṃ tu nādyād bhāṇḍasthitaṃ tv api |

vasiṣṭhaḥ |

	ghṛtaṃ vā yadi vā tailaṃ vipro nādyān nakhasrutam |

	yamas tad aśuci prāha tulyaṃ gomāṃsabhakṣaṇaiḥ ||

tathā |

	hastadattāś ca ye snehā lavaṇaṃ vyañjanāni ca |

	dātāraṃ nopatiṣṭhanti bhoktkā bhuṅkte tu kilbiṣam ||

	tasmād antaritaṃ deyaṃ varṇenaiva tṛṇena vā |

	pradadyān na tu hastena nāyasena kadācana ||

brahmapurāṇe |

	ekena pāṇinā dattaṃ śūdrād annaṃ na bhakṣayet |

**[243]**	ghṛtaṃ tailaṃ ca lavaṇaṃ pānīyaṃ pāyasaṃ tathā ||

	bhikṣā ca hastadattāpi na grāhyā yatra kutracit ||

śaṅkhalikhitau: "nāpaṇīyam annam aśnīyāt | na dviḥ pakvaṃ na paryuṣitam anyatra rāgacaruṣāḍavadadhiguḍadadhigodhūmayavapiṣṭavikārebhyaḥ" | śaṅkhaḥ |

	apūpāḥ saktavo dhānās takraṃ dadhi ghṛtaṃ madhu |

	etat paṇyeṣu bhoktavyaṃ bhāṇḍalepo na ced bhavet ||

āpastambaḥ |

	dvāv evāśramiṇau bhojyau brahmacāri gṛhī tathā |

	muner annam abhojyaṃ syāt sarveṣāṃ liṅgināṃ tathā ||

	sūtake mṛtake bhuṅkte gṛhīte śaśibhāskare |

	chāyāyāṃ hastino bhuṅkte na bhūyaḥ puruṣo bhavet || 1.165–167||

_śūdraviśeṣānnabhojananiṣedhārtham āha_ |

	**śūdreṣu dāsagopālakulamitrāvasūriṇaḥ |**

**	bhojyānnā nāpitaś caiva yaś cātmānaṃ nivedayet || 1.168 ||**

śūdreṣv iti nirdhāraṇe saptamī | tena śūdrāṇāṃ madhye dāsādayo bhojyānnāḥ | nānye śūdrāḥ | dāsaḥ krītādiḥ | gopālo gavāṃ pātā | kulaṃ svakṣetrakarṣakaḥ | tathā ca devalaḥ |

	svadāso nāpito gopaḥ kumbhakāraḥ kṛṣīvalaḥ |

	brāhmaṇair api bhojyānnāḥ pañcaite śūdrayonaḥ ||

yad vā kulasya mitraṃ kulamitram | kulaṃ vaṃśaḥ | mitraṃ prasiddham | avasūrī saṃbhūya samutthāyitayā sahakarṣakaḥ | nāpitaḥ prasiddhaḥ | yaś ca śūdro 'krīta eva dvijāyātmānaṃ vā vāṅmanaḥkāyakarmabhir nivedayati dadāti | dāsādayo yadīyās tasyaiva te bhojyānnāḥ | hārītaḥ |

	kulamitraṃ kulaputro bhaikṣyadaḥ śiṣyakaḥ suhṛt |

	bhaved yasya sukhaṃ lābhe bhaye trātā ca yo bhavet ||

	ete śūdreṣu bhojyānnā mano yatra vibhāvyate ||

kulaṃ karṣakas tatputraḥ kulaputraḥ | suhṛnmitram | vibhāvyate prasīdati | uktavyatiriktaśūdraviṣaye manur āha |

**[244]**	nādyāc chūdrasya pakvānnaṃ vidvān āśrāddhino dvijaḥ |

	ādadītāmam evāsmād avṛttāv ekarātrikam ||

aśrāddhī śrāddhānarho 'sacchūdra iti yāvat | kānicit pakvānnāny anyeṣāṃ bhojyāni | yathā sumantur āha |

	gorasaṃ caiva saktūṃś ca tailaṃ piṇyākam eva ca |

	apūpān bhakṣayec chūdrād yaś cā (yac cā)nyat payasā kṛtam ||

tathā |

	kaṭu pakvaṃ snehapakvaṃ pāyasaṃ dadhisaktavaḥ |

	etāny aśūdrānnabhujo bhojyāni manur abravīt ||

aśūdrānnabhujo dvijasya | aṅgirāḥ |

	svapātre yac ca vinyastaṃ dugdhaṃ tac chuci nityaśaḥ |

	pātrāntaragataṃ grāhyaṃ śūdrāt svagṛham āgatam ||

	śūdraveśmani vipreṇa kṣīraṃ vā yadi vā dadhi |

	nivṛttena na bhoktavyaṃ śūdrānnaṃ tad api smṛtam ||

nivṛttena śūdrānnabhojanān nivṛttenety arthaḥ | viṣṇupurāṇe |

	saṃprokṣya vidvān gṛhṇīyāc chūdrānnaṃ gṛham āgatam |

śaṅkhaḥ |

	gṛhāśvarathabhūmyarthe gavārthe ca viśeṣataḥ |

	śrotriyeṇāpi bhoktavyaṃ śūdrānnaṃ tu yamo 'bravīt ||

dakṣaḥ |

	śūdrānnarasapuṣṭāṅgas tv adhīyāno 'pi nityaśaḥ |

	juhvan vāpi japan vāpi gatim iṣṭāṃ na vindati ||

vasiṣṭhaḥ |

	śūdrānnenodarasthena maithunaṃ yo 'dhigacchati |

	yasyānnaṃ tasya te putrā annāc chukraṃ pravartate ||

hārītaḥ |

	śūdrānnen tu bhuktena jaṭharasthena yo mṛtaḥ |

	sa vai kharatvam uṣṭratvaṃ śūdratvam upagacchati ||

aṅgirāḥ |

	ṣaṇmāsān yo dvijo bhuṅkte śūdrasyānnaṃ vigarhitam |

	sa ca jīvan bhavec chūdro mṛtaḥ śvā cābhijāyate ||

evaṃ ca sati yaḥ śūdrānnabhojanānugrahaḥ sa āpadviṣaya eva jñeyaḥ || 1.168 ||

_paryuṣitaṃ na bhoktavyam ity asyāpavadam āha_ |

	**annaṃ paryuṣitaṃ bhojyaṃ snehāktaṃ cirasaṃbhṛtam |**

**	asnehā api godhūmayavagorasavikriyāḥ || 1.169 ||**

**[245]**

annaṃ ghṛtādisnehāktaṃ sac cirakālasaṃsthitaṃ paryuṣitaṃ ca bhojyam | godhūmādivikārā asnehā api paryuṣitā bhojyāḥ | yamaḥ |

	śuktāni hi dvijo 'nnāni na bhuñjīta kadācana |

	prakṣālitāni nirdoṣāny āpaddharmo yadā bhavet ||

	masūramāṣasaṃyuktaṃ tathā paryuṣitaṃ ca yat |

	tat tu prakṣālitaṃ kṛtvā bhuñjīta hy abhidhāritam ||

tathā |

	apūpāś ca karambhāś ca dhānāvaṭakasaktavaḥ |

	śākaṃ māṃsaṃ ca yūṣaṃ ca sūpaṃ kṛsaram eva ca ||

	yavāgūr yāvakaṃ caiva yac cānyat snehasaṃyutam |

	sarvaṃ paryuṣitaṃ bhojyaṃ śuktaṃ cet parivarjayet ||

	guḍādidravyasaṃyuktaṃ varjyaṃ paryuṣitaṃ dadhi |

	tathaiva pānakādīni madhvājyaracitāni ca ||

	rājamāṣāḥ sthūlamudgās tathā vṛṣayavāśakau |

	masūrāḥ śatapuṣpāś ca kusumbhaṃ śrīniketanam |

	sasyāny etāny abhakṣyāṇi na ca deyāni kasyacit || iti |

brahmapurāṇe masūrasyāpy abhakṣyatvena nirdeśaḥ | tataś ca śrāddhe kalāyavanmasūrabhakṣaṇe na vikalpaḥ | devalaḥ |

	nāśnīyāt pāyasaṃ naktaṃ bhuktaṃ cen na svapen niśi |

	na kṣīram utsṛjet prāptaṃ pavitraṃ hi payaḥ smṛtam ||

tathā |

	dadhi bhakṣyaṃ śuktam api yac caivaṃ dadhisaṃbhavam |

	kandamūlaphalaiḥ puṣpaiḥ śastaiḥ śuktāsavaṃ tu yat ||

	avikāri bhaven medhyam abhakṣyaṃ tadvikārakṛt |

"kandamūlaphalaiḥ puṣpaiḥ" ityādiḥ | ayam arthaḥ — yac chuktaṃ kandādibhiḥ kṛtaṃ satpānaṃ tad yadi mohādivikārakaraṃ na bhavati tadā bhakṣaṇīyam | smṛtyantaram |

	saphalā kumbhikā yasya gṛhe bhavati nityaśaḥ |

	tasmāt tu kāñcikā grāhyā netarasmāt kadācana ||

tathā |

	na bhakṣayed dāranālaṃ phalamūlavivarjitam || 1.169 ||

_kiṃ ca_ |

**[246]**

	**saṃdhinyanirdaśāvatsāgopayaḥ parivarjayet |**

**	auṣṭram aikaśaphaṃ straiṇam āraṇyakam athāvikam || 1.170 ||**

saṃdhinī vṛṣṭabhopagatā | anirdaśā prasavaprabhṛtyanirgatadaśarātrā | avatsā mṛtavatsā | āsāṃ gavāṃ pratyekaṃ payo varjayet | auṣṭram uṣṭtrikāyāḥ | aikaśapham ekaśapāyā vaḍavādeḥ | striṇaṃ striyāḥ | āraṇyakam āraṇyānām eṇyādīnām | āvikam avyāḥ | payo varjayed iti pratyekam abhisaṃbadhyate | vasiṣṭhaḥ: "gomahiṣyajānām anirdaśānāṃ payaḥ" | varjyam iti śeṣaḥ | manuḥ |

	āraṇyānāṃ ca sarveṣāṃ mṛgāṇāṃ mahiṣīṃ vinā |

payo varjyam iti śeṣaḥ | straiṇam iti strīgrahaṇam ajetaradvistanīnām upalakṣaṇārtham | tathā ca śaṅkhaḥ: "sarvāsāṃ dvistanīnāṃ kṣīram abhojyam ajāvarjyam" iti | kṣīravarjane tadvikārasyāpi varjanaṃ veditavyam | yata āha śaṅkhaḥ |

	kṣīrāṇi yāny abhakṣyāṇi tadvikārāśane budhaḥ |

	saptarātraṃ vrataṃ kuryāt prayatnena samāhitaḥ ||

vrataṃ gomūtrayāvakam | hārītaḥ: "syandinī vṛṣasyantī tasyāḥ payo na pibed ṛtumad bhavati" | gautamaḥ: "syandinīyamasūsaṃdhinīnāṃ ca" | kṣīraṃ na pibed iti śeṣaḥ | syandinī svataḥsravatkṣīrā | yamasūryamalavatsā | baudhāyanaḥ: "kṣīram apeyaṃ vivatsāyā anyavatsāyāś ca" | brahmapurāṇāt |

	ghṛtāt phenaṃ ghṛtān maṇḍaṃ peyūṣam atha cārdragoḥ |

	saguḍaṃ maricāktaṃ tu tathā paryuṣitaṃ dadhi ||

	śīrṇaṃ takram apeyaṃ ca naṣṭāsvādaṃ ca phenavat |

	pramādād bhikṣitair ebhir vane pakṣavrataṃ caret ||

peyūṣaṃ navaprasūtākṣīram | tac ca yāvad ārdratānuvartate | ārdratā sarajaskatā | śīrṇaṃ sphuṭitam | āpastambaḥ |

	kṣatriyaś caiva vṛttastho vaiśyaḥ śūdro 'tha vā punaḥ |

	yaḥ pibet kāpilaṃ kṣīraṃ na tato 'nyo 'sty apuṇyakṛt || **[247]**

bhaviṣyatpurāṇāt |

	kāpilaṃ yaḥ pibec chūdro narake sa vipacyate |

	hutaśeṣaṃ pibed vipra vipraḥ syād anyathā paśuḥ ||

brahmapurāṇāt |

	api prathānasamaye rātrau na prāśayed dadhi |

	madhuparkapradānaṃ ca varjayitvā tu kāmataḥ || 1.170 ||

_api ca_ |

	**devatārthaṃ haviḥ śugrulohitān vraścanāṃs tathā |**

**	anupākṛtamāṃsāni viḍjāni kavakāni ca || 1.171 ||**

devatārthaṃ naivedyaṃ haviścarupuroḍāśādi prāg ghomād devatārthaṃ havis taddhavanārtham āttaṃ vā | śigruḥ saubhāñjanakaḥ | lohitā lohitavarṇā vṛkṣaniryāsāḥ | vraścanā vṛkṣacchedaprabhavā niryāsā alohitā api | tathā ca manuḥ |

	lohitān vṛkṣaniryāsān vraścanaprabhavāṃs tathā | iti |

anupākṛtamāṃsāni devādyarthatvenānupākṛtānām asaṃkalpitānāṃ paśvādīnāṃ māṃsāni | viḍjāni viṣṭhāyāṃ jātāni taṇḍulīyakādīni | kavakāni caityasaṃnibhāni | etāni pratyekaṃ varjayet | baudhāyanaḥ |

	amedhyabhūsthā ye vṛkṣā uptāḥ puṣpaphalopagāḥ |

	teṣāṃ naiva praduṣyanti puṣpāṇi ca phalāni ca ||

anena cārthād vṛkṣavyatirikāny amedhyabhūprarūḍhāni varjayed iti pratipāditaṃ bhavati || 1.171 ||

_kiṃ ca_ |

	**kravyādapakṣidātyūhaśukapratudaṭiṭṭibhān |**

**	sārasaikaśaphān haṃsān sarvāṃś ca grāmavāsinaḥ || 1.172 ||**

**	koyaṣṭiplavacakrāhvabalākābakaviṣkirān |**

kravyam adanti ye pakṣiṇas te gṛdhrādyāḥ kravyādapakṣiṇaḥ | kravyam āmamāṃsam | dātyūhaś cātakaḥ | pratudya bhakṣayantīti pratudāḥ śyenādyāḥ | ekaśaphā aśvādyāḥ | grāmavāsinaḥ pārāvatādayaḥ | koyaṣṭiḥ kovakaḥ (?) | plavenaiva vartanam asyeti plavaḥ pāriplavādiḥ | vikīrya vikīrya bhakṣayantīti viṣkirāḥ | dātyūhādaya ekaśaphavarjāḥ sarve pakṣiviseṣāḥ | ekaśaphāś cāśvādayas tadbhakṣaṇaṃ varjayet | atra grāmyāśvādayaḥ sapta | **[248]** tathā ca paiṭhīnasiḥ: "gaur avir ajo 'śvo 'śvataro gardabho manuṣyaś ceti sapta grāmyāḥ paśavaḥ" | atrāpy avir bhakṣaṇīyaḥ | tathā ca hārītaḥ: "grāmyāraṇyānāṃ paśūnām aśnanti | avyajameṣamahiṣahariṇakhaḍgaruruvṛṣabhaṛśyanyaṅkumahāraṇyavāsinaś ca varāhāṃs tathā śaśakaśalyakamedhāgodhākūrmatittirimayūravārdhrīṇasalāvakakukarakapiñjalān saśalkāṃś ca matsyānyayo(tho)papannān bhakṣayet" | bahuśākhaśṛṅgo mṛga ṛśyaḥ, mṛduśṛṅga eṇa iti prasiddhaḥ | nyaṅkuḥ saṃbarasadṛśaḥ śṛṅgarahitaḥ || 1.172 ||

_api ca_ |

	**vṛthākṛsarasaṃyāvapāyasāpūpaśaṣkulīḥ || 1.173 ||**

pitṛdevaprayojanarahitaṃ kṛsarādikaṃ varjayet | tilamudgamiśrita odanaḥ kṛsaram | saṃyāvo godhūmakaṇā ghṛtakṣīrapakvāḥ | godhūmavikārāḥ snehapakvāḥ śaṣkulyaḥ | prasiddham anyat | kevalātmārthapākapratiṣedhenaiva vṛthākṛsarādivarjane siddhe teṣāṃ pṛthagupādānaṃ tadbhakṣaṇe prāyaścittaviśeṣaprāptyartham || 1.173 ||

_kiṃ ca_ |

	**kalaviṅkaṃ sakākolaṃ kuraraṃ rajjudālakam |**

**	jālapādān khañjarīṭān ajñātāṃś ca mṛgadvijān || 1.174 ||**

**	cāṣāṃś ca raktapādāṃś ca saunaṃ vallūram eva ca |**

**	matsyāṃś ca **

kalaviṅko gṛhacaṭako nigadeṣūktaḥ | tasya grāmavāsiniṣedhe saty ubhayacaratvāt punar grahaṇam | kākolo droṇakākaḥ, "droṇakokilaḥ" iti nigamāt | rajjvādīn dalayatīti rajjudālako vṛkṣakuṭṭakaḥ | jālapādā haṃsādivyatirekeṇājñātā mṛgadvijajātāḥ | atrāpi kalaviṅkādayo jñātamṛgavyatiriktāḥ pakṣiviśeṣāḥ | saunaṃ sūnāgataṃ māṃsam, vallūraṃ śuṣkamāṃsam | saunavallūre bhakṣyāṇām api mṛgādīnāṃ varjanīye | matsyāḥ prasiddhās tān varjayet || 1.174 ||

**[149]**

_varjanīyatayoktānāṃ [bhakṣaṇe] prāyaścittam āha_ |

		**kāmato jagdhvā sopavāsas tryahaṃ vaset || 1.175 ||**

saṃdhinīkṣīrādīnāṃ matsyāntānāṃ madhye 'nyatamaṃ kāmato jagdhvā bhakṣayitvā trirātram upavaset | akāmatas tv ekāham "śeṣeṣūpavased ahaḥ" iti manusmaraṇāt || 1.175 ||

_kiṃ ca_ |

	**palāṇḍuṃ viḍvarāhaṃ ca chatrākaṃ grāmakukkuṭam |**

**	laśunaṃ gṛñjanaṃ caiva jagdhvā cāndrāyaṇaṃ caret || 1.176 ||**

palāṇḍuḥ kandaviśeṣaḥ | viḍvarāho grāmasūkaraḥ | chatrākaṃ chatrasadṛśam | grāmakukkuṭalaśune prasiddhe | gṛñjanaṃ kandaviśeṣaḥ | gartenaka ity udīcyāṃ prasiddhaḥ | etāni kāmataḥ sakṛd bhakṣayityvā cāndrāyaṇaṃ caret | manus tv eṣāṃ kāmato bhakṣaṇābhyāse pātityam āha |

	chatrākaṃ viṣvarāhaṃ ca luśunaṃ grāmakukkuṭam |

	palāṇḍuṃ gṛñjanaṃ caiva matyā jagdhvā pated dvijaḥ || iti |

tataś ca surāpānaprāyaścittaprāptiḥ | amatipūrve tv abhyāse sa evāha |

	amatyaitāni ṣaḍ jagdhvā kṛcchraṃ sāntapanaṃ caret |

	yaticāndrāyaṇaṃ cāpi śeṣeṣūpavased ahaḥ || iti |

amatipūrve sakṛdbhakṣaṇe śaṅkha āha: "laśunapalāṇḍugṛñjanaviḍvarāhagrāmakukkuṭakumbhīkabhakṣaṇe dvādaśarātraṃ payaḥ pibet" iti | sakṛdbhakṣaṇe brahmapurāṇam |

	laśunaṃ gṛñjanaṃ caiva palāṇḍuś ca parārikā |

	kanyā parārikā cānyā dīrghapatraṃ tad ucyate ||

	alambhsā ca tuṣṭaiś ca (?) kṛtanāmā mahauṣadham |

	gṛñjanaṃ yavaneṣṭaṃ ca śaśaṃsūryavanāś ca tat ||

	sṛsakaṃ ca sanāśākaṃ tumburaṃ ca gareṭakam |

	atha pūyanakaṃ nāma lavatarkā ca dāruṇā ||

	trayodaśaitās tasyāpi jātayaś cātigarhitāḥ |

	piṇḍopamaṃ tu khukkhaṇḍaṃ kavakaṃ caityasaṃnibham ||

	chatrākaṃ chatrasadṛśaṃ trayaṃ bhūmisamudbhavam |

**[250]**	nānāvidhāḥ śākhino ye chatrākaṃ ca tadudbhavam ||

	śastracchedeṣu vṛkṣāṇāṃ yaś codbhavati kutracit |

	tvakparyanteṣu ca raso lohitāny aṅkurāṇi ca ||

	palāṇḍupramukhair ebhiḥ pramādād bhakṣitair api |

	cāndrāyaṇaṃ cared vipraḥ kṛcchraṃ sāntapanaṃ tathā ||

	vanavāsavrataṃ māsaṃ cared vā susamāhitaḥ||

asamarthādiviṣayo vikalpaḥ | smṛtyantaram |

	haraṇḍuś ca palāṇḍuś ca lavatarkaḥ parārikā |

	gṛñjanaṃ yavaneṣṭaś ca palāṇḍor daśa jātayaḥ || 1.176 ||

	**bhakṣyāḥ pañcanakhāḥ sedhāgodhākacchapaśallakāḥ |**

**	śaśaś ca matsyeṣv api hi siṃhatuṇḍakarohitāḥ || 1.177 ||**

**	tathā pāṭhīnarājīvasaśalkāś ca dvijātibhiḥ |**

sedhādayaḥ śaśantāḥ pañcanakhās tathā matsyeṣ madhe siṃhatuṇḍakādayo matsyaviśeṣāḥ dvijātibhir bhakṣyāḥ | sāmānyataḥ pravṛtto 'yaṃ pañcanakhabhakṣaṇaniṣedho matsyabhakṣaṇaniṣedhaś ca na teṣu vidyata ity arthaḥ | sedhādīnāṃ prasiddham eva pañcanakhatvam anūdyate 'nyeṣāṃ pañcanakhānāṃ māṃsam abhakṣyam iti jñāpanārtham | sedhā śvāvit | sa ca śvabhakṣako vyāghraviśeṣaḥ | sedhā vallīsadṛśaḥ prāṇiviśeṣaḥ | śaśakacchapau prasiddhau | śallakaḥ śalalī | dvijātigrahaṇam upalakṣaṇārtham | tathā ca devalaḥ |

	uktam etat tu sarveṣāṃ bhakṣyābhakṣyam aśeṣataḥ |

	varṇānāṃ sānulomānāṃ sastrīṇāṃ ca viśeṣataḥ || iti |

vasiṣṭhaḥ: "śvāvicchalyakaśaśakacchapagodhāḥ pañcanakhānāṃ bhakṣyāḥ | anuṣṭraḥ paśūnām anyatodantāś ca matsyānāṃ cāceṭagavayaśiśumāranakrakulīrā vikṛtarūpāḥ sravaśīrṣāś ca gauragavayaśarabhājāś cānudiṣṭās tathā dhenvanaḍuhāvapannadantāḥ" ityādi | avapannadantā ity antam abhikṣya ity pratipadaṃ saṃbandhanīyam | bhakṣyau dhenvanaḍuhau medhyau vājasi(sa)neyakair vijñāyete | khaḍge tu vavadante 'grāmyasūkare ca khaḍge tu vivadante bhakṣyābhakṣyatayāto vikalpaḥ | sa ca vyavasthitaḥ | śrāddhe bhakṣyo nānyatra | agrāmyasūkaro 'raṇyasūkaraḥ || 1.177 ||

**[251]**	**ataḥ śṛṇudhvaṃ māṃsasya vidhiṃ bhakṣaṇavarjite || 1.178 ||**

**	prāṇātyaye tathā śrāddhe prokṣite dvijakāmyayā ||**

**	devān pitṝn samabhyarcya khādan māṃsaṃ na doṣabhāk || 1.179 ||**

uktaṃ māṃsānāṃ bhakṣaṇaṃ varjanaṃ cātaḥ paraṃ vidhinimittaṃ vakṣyamāṇaṃ śṛṇudhvam | tatra prāṇātyayādi māṃśabhakṣaṇe nimittaṃ śābdaṃ varjite tu tadabhāva ārtham | prāṇātyayo vyādhinimitto'nnābhāvanimittaś ca | tathā ca manuḥ |

	niyuktas tu yathānyāyaṃ yo māṃsaṃ nātti mānavaḥ |

	sa pretya paśutāṃ yāti saṃbhavānekaviṃśatim ||

niyukto nimantrito daive śrāddhe vā | tathā ca yamaḥ |

	āmantritas tu yaḥ śrāddhe daive vā māṃsam utsṛjet |

	yāvanti paśuromāṇi tāvan narakam ṛcchati ||

prokṣitaśabdena nirvartitapaśuyāgamāṃsam upalakṣyate | tataś ca paśuyāga iḍārūpamāṃsa ṛtvigyajamānaiḥ kārya eva | dvijakāmyayā dvijecchayā | yaṃ prati dvijās tvayā māṃsaṃ bhakṣaṇīyam itīcchanti sa bhakṣayed ity arthaḥ | devapitṛbhyo dattasya māṃsasya śeṣam aśeṣam aśnīyāt | eṣu nimitteṣu khādan māṃsaṃ na doṣabhāg bhavati || 1.178–179 ||

_varjanavidhim āha_ |

	**vaset sa narake ghore dināni paśuromabhiḥ |**

**	saṃmitāni durācāro yo hanty avidhinā paśūn || 1.180 ||**

avidhinoktanimittavyatirekeṇa yo durācāro māṃsaṃ khādituṃ paśuṃ hanti sa paśuromasaṃmitāni dināni narake vaset | anena ca paśuvadhasya pratiṣiddhasya narakavāsaṃ prati nimittatā bodhyate | yathā "yo 'pagurātai śatena yātayāt" ityādinā brāhmaṇaṃ pratyavagūraṇasya yātanāyāś ca sādhyasādhanasaṃbandhaḥ | tena nedam arthavādamātraṃ kiṃ tu vivakṣitasvarthaṃ vacanam | atra manuḥ |

	anumantā viśasitā nihantā krayavikrayī |

	saṃskartā copahartā ca khādakaś ceti ghātakāḥ || **[252]**

yamaḥ |

	yas tu khādati māṃsāni prāṇināṃ jīvitaiṣiṇām |

	hatānāṃ ca mṛtānāṃ ca yathā hantā tathaiva saḥ ||

tathā |

	dhanena copabhogena vadhabandhena vāpy atha |

	trividhas tu vadho jñeyo bhoktā tatrātiricyate ||

atha mahābhārate |

	caturo vārṣikān māsān yo māṃsaṃ nātti mānavaḥ |

	catvāri bhadrāny āpnoti kīrtim āyur yaśo balam ||

tathā |

	kaumudaṃ tu viśeṣeṇa śuklaṃ pakṣaṃ narādhipa |

	varjayen madhu māṃsāni dharmo hy atra vidhīyate ||

yamaḥ |

	yajuṣā saṃskṛtaṃ māṃsam bhakṣayet tu yathāvidhi |

	na bhakṣayed vṛthāmāṃsaṃ pṛṣṭhamāṃsaṃ vivarjayet ||

pṛṣṭhamāṃsaṃ pṛṣṭhasaṃdhimāṃsam | brahmapurāṇe |

	paśoś ca māryamāṇasya māṃsaṃ na grāhayed dvijaḥ |

	pṛṣṭhamāṃsaṃ garbhaśayyāṃ śuṣkamāṃsam athāpi vā ||

nityam abhojyā ity anuvṛttau gautamaḥ: "ubhayatodantā alomānaḥ keśina ekaśaphāḥ kalaviṅkaplavacaktravākahaṃsāḥ" | keśī camarī || 1.180 ||

_idānīṃ vihitavyatiriktamāṃsabhakṣaṇavarjanasya phalam āha_ |

	**sarvān kāmān avāpnoti hayamedhaphalaṃ tathā |**

**	gṛhe 'pi nivasan vipro munir māṃsavivarjanāt || 1.181 ||**

gṛhastho 'pi san māṃsavivarjanān munitulyo bhavati | tāpaso bhavatīty arthaḥ | sarvān kāmān aśvamedhphalaṃ ca prāpnoti | avāpnotīti vartamānā vibhkaktir vidhivibhaktitvena pariṇāmayitavyā yathā rātrisatre || 1.181 ||

**iti śrīvidhyādharavaṃśaprabhavaśeīśilāhāranarendrajīmūtavāhanānvayaprabhūta-**

**śrīmadaparādityadevaviracite yājñavalkīyadharmaśāstranibandhe**

**[bhojyābhojya] bhakṣyābhakṣyaprakaraṇam || 6 ||**

**atha saṭīkayājñavalkyasmṛtau**

**dravyaśuddhiprakaraṇam (7)**

adhunā dravyaśuddhyupāyavidhiprakaraṇam ārabhate | dravyasya doṣāpagamaḥ śuddhiḥ | **[153]** apetadoṣaṃ hi dravyaṃ śuddham ity ucyate | śāstreṇa ca kākādisaṃpṛktaṃ dravyaṃ prakṣālanāc chudhyatīti kathyate | tena tatrāpi kākādisamparkajanitadoṣāpagama eva śuddhiśabdena vācyaḥ | na ca pratyakṣagamyo doṣa iti śuddhividhānānyathānupapattyā kākādiyogāt ko 'pi dravye doṣo bhavatīti parikalpyate | tadapagamopāyo nānāvidhaḥ prokṣaṇaprakṣālanādiḥ śāstreṇa vidhīyata iti | aśuddhena dravyeṇa na saṃvyavahāraḥ puruṣeṇa sādhyaḥ kiṃ tu śodhitenaiveti śuddhividhibalād eva kalpyate | tac ca karpaṭakapālādinā dravyakhaṇḍenāpi yadi vyavahārasiddhir asti tadā tad api yathāvidhi śodhyam | evaṃ ca yacchāstrakārair ucyate prokṣaṇādinā dravyaṃ śucitām iyāt prayataṃ bhavati śudhyatītyādi, tatra tatra puruṣavyāpāra eva lākṣaṇiko vidheyaḥ, puruṣas tathā kuryād yathā dravyaṃ śuci syād ity arthaḥ | aśuddhena dravyeṇa saṃvyavahārataḥ puruṣasyāśucitā vihitakarmakartṛtvayogyatvapratibandharūpā pratyavāyāntarahetubhūtā ca jāyate | tasyāś ca pratyavāyakaratām āha manuḥ |

	loṣṭamardī tṛṇacchedī nakhakhādī ca yo naraḥ |

	sa vināśaṃ vrajaty āśu sūcako 'śucir eva ca || iti |

tatra dvividhā śuddhiḥ — śarīraśuddhir bāhyadravyaśuddhiś ca | tatra bāhyadravyaśuddhiṃ tāvad āha |

	**sauvarṇarājatābjānām ūrdhvapātragrahāśmanām |**

**	śākarajjumūlaphalavāsovidalacarmaṇām || 1.182 ||**

**	pātrāṇāṃ camasānāṃ ca vāriṇā śuddhir iṣyate |**

**	carusruksruvasasnehapātrāṇy uṣṇena vāriṇā || 1.183 ||**

suvarṇasya vikāraḥ sauvarṇaḥ, rajatasya vikāro rājatam | abjaṃ śaṅkhaśuktyādi | ūrdhvapātraṃ māhāvīrādi | grahā aindravāyavādipātrāṇi | aśmānaḥ pāṣānāḥ | vidalaṃ veṇudalam | pātrāṇi bṛsyādīni sneharahitāni | camasā ūrdhvapātravyatiriktāni dāravāṇi somapātrāṇi | prasiddham anyat | eṣāṃ vāriṇā śuddhiḥ śaucam iṣyate | prakṣālanarūpā ceyaṃ śuddhiḥ, prokṣaṇarūpā tu sphyādipātraviṣayatvena pṛthag eva vakṣyati | carur mṛnmayaṃ bhāṇḍam | srug juhvādiḥ | sruvaḥ prasiddhaḥ | etadādīni sasnehāny ājyaliptāny uṣṇena vāriṇā prkṣālanāc chudhyanti | ucchiṣṭādinaraspṛṣṭānāṃ caiṣāṃ śuddhiḥ | yad āha devalaḥ |

**[254]**	ucchiṣṭāśucisaṃspṛṣṭam adravaṃ śudhyate 'mbhasā |

	sadravaṃ cābhiśudhyeta snehagandhavivarjitam || iti |

aśucir atrotsṛṣṭamūtrādir na tu kākādiḥ | yataḥ kākamukhasaṃspṛṣṭapātrasya śuddhyantaram āha śaṅkhaḥ: "kṛṇaśakunimukhāvamṛṣṭaṃ nirlikhec chvāpadamukhāvamṛṣṭaṃ pātraṃ na tat prayuñjīta" iti | sauvarṇāder alepasyaiṣā śuddhiḥ | tathā ca manuḥ |

	nirlepaṃ kāñcanaṃ bhāṇḍam adbhir eva viśudhyati |

	abjam aśmamayaṃ caiva rājataṃ cānupaskṛtam ||
