anupaskṛtaṃ tāmrādinā yan na saṃspṛṣṭam | taijasānāṃ mūtrādyupaghāte baudhāyana āha: "taijasānāṃ mūtrapurīṣaśukrāsṛkkuṇapavāsitānām āvartanam alpasaṃsarge tu parilekhanam | sparśamātropaghāte triḥsaptakṛtvo bhasmanā parimārjanam | ataijasānām evaṃbhūtānām utsargaḥ" | āvartanam agnisaṃyogena dravīkaraṇam | atra hārītokto viśeṣaḥ: "adbhiḥ kāñcanarajataśaṅkhaśuktīnāṃ tadguṇavarjasnehavaivarṇyopahatānāṃ yavagodhūmakalāyamāṣamasūramudgagomayacūrṇair dhāvanam | amlalavaṇābhyāṃ tāmrāṇām | bhasmanā kāṃsyānām | ṣāṇatailasikatāgharṣaṇaiḥ kārṣṇāyasānām | śilāvadharṣaṇamārjanair maṇimayānām" | yavādicūrṇāni tulyārthatvād vikalpante | udakaṃ tu sarvaiḥ śodhanadravyaiḥ samuccīyate | lohataikṣṇyasādhanaṃ ṣāṇam | āpastambaḥ |

	gavāghrātāni kāṃsyāni śūdrocchiṣṭāni yāni ca |

	śudhyanti daśabhiḥ kṣāraiḥ śvakākopahatāni ca ||

kṣāro bhasma | svalpakālopaghātaviṣayam etat | śaṅkhaḥ |

	sūtikocchiṣṭabhāṇdasya surāmadyahatasya ca |

	triḥ saptamārjanāc chuddhir na tu kāṃsyasya tāpanam ||

kāṃsyavyatiriktānāṃ taijasānāṃ sūtikocchiṣṭādike svalpakālopaghāte yavacūrṇādibhir ekaviṃśatikṛtvo mārjanād eva śuddhir na tu kāṃsyasya tāpanam | arthāt kāṃsyavyatiriktānāṃ tāpanam api kāryam iti gamyate | **[255]** tathā |

	brahmakṣatraviśāṃ caiva sakṛtsaṃmārjanāc chuciḥ |

dvijocchiṣṭayuktaṃ taijasaṃ sakṛtsaṃmārjanāc chudhyatīty arthaḥ |

	caturthena tu yad bhuktaṃ caturbhis tatra mārjanam |

	agnau prakṣipya gṛhṇīyād dhastau prakṣālya yatnataḥ |

	gośṛṅgeṇa tu saṃspṛṣṭaṃ tat pātraṃ śucitām iyāt ||

kāṃsyavyatiriktataijasapātraviṣayam idam | manuḥ |

	taijasānāṃ maṇīnāṃ ca sarvasyāśmamayasya ca |

	bhasmanādbhir mṛdā caiva śuddhir uktā manīṣibhiḥ ||

taijasāni haimādīni | tad uktam |

	hema tāmraṃ ca rajataṃ kāṃsyāyastrapusīsakāḥ |

	ete ca taijasāḥ proktā dhātavas taijasodbhavāḥ || iti |

śaṅkhaḥ |

	uṣṇodakena kāṃsyasya sīsasya trapuṇas tathā |

	kṣāreṇa śuddhiṃ kāṃśyasya lohasya ca vinirdiśet ||

	lohānāṃ dāhanāc chuddhir bhasmanā gomayena vā |

	dahanāt khananād vāpi śailānām ambhasāpi vā ||

	kāṣṭhānāṃ takṣaṇāc chuddhir mṛdgomayajalair api ||

mahati doṣe dahanaṃ khananaṃ ca dvitīyam alpadoṣe | baudhāyanaḥ: "taijasānāṃ pātrāṇāṃ gośakṛdbhasmabhiḥ parimārjanam anyatamena vā" | uśanā: "suvarṇarajatatāmratrapusīsakāṃsyānām adbhir eva bhasmasaṃyuktābhis taijasānāṃ cocchiṣṭānāṃ bhasmanā triḥ prakṣālanam | kanakamaṇirajataśaṅkhaśuktyupalānāṃ vajravidalarajjucarmaṇāṃ cādbhiḥ śaucam | mṛtpātraśastrāṇām agnāv uttāpanam" | kāśyapaḥ: "sikatābhir dantaśṛṅgaśaṅkhaśuktimaṇīnām" | yamaḥ |

	rajatasya suvarṇasya tāmrasya trapuṇas tathā |

	rītyayaḥkāṃsyasīsānāṃ bhasmanā śaucam iṣyate ||

ṛṣyaśṛṅgaḥ |

	muktāphalapravālānāṃ śuddhiḥ prakṣālanena tu |

	abjānāṃ caiva bhāṇḍānāṃ sarvasyāśmamayasya ca ||

viṣṇuḥ: "tāmrarītirapusīsamayānām amlodakena" | smṛtyantaram |

	bhasmanā śudhyate kāṃsyaṃ surayā yan na lipyate |

	surāmūtrapurīṣais tu śudhyate tāpalekhanaiḥ ||

**[256]**	tāmram amlena śudhyet tu na ced āmiṣalepitam |

	āmiṣeṇa tu yal liptaṃ punardāhena śudhyati ||

ādipurāṇāt |

	suvarṇarūpyaśaṅkhāśmaśuktiratnamayāni ca |

	kāṃsyāyastāmraraityāni trapusīsamayāni ca ||

	nirlepāni viśudhyanti kevalena jalena tu |

	śūdrocchiṣṭāni śudhyanti tridhā kṣārāmlavāribhiḥ ||

kṣārādidravyatritvāt tridhātvam | mārjanaṃ tu daśakṛtva eva | vacanāntaravaśāt |

	sūtikāśavaviṇmūtrarajasvalahatāni ca |

	prakṣeptavyāni tāny agnau yad yad yāvat sahed api ||

yad dravyaṃ yāvantam agniprakṣepaṃ sahate yāvatāgniprakṣepeṇa na naśyati tāvantaṃ kuryād ity arthaḥ | alpopaghātaviṣayam etat | śātātapaḥ |

	suvarṇaṃ rajataṃ tāmraṃ trapu kṛṣṇāyasaṃ tathā |

	rītikāsīsalohāni śudhyanty aśmapragharṣaṇāt ||

viṣṇuḥ: "viṇmūtraretaḥśavaraktaliptam āvartanollekhanatāpanair vā | triḥsaptakṛtvaḥ parimārjanena bhasmādinā śudhyati taijasaṃ hi" | taijasānāṃ retoviṇmūtrāsṛkkuṇapādibhiś caṇḍālasūtikodakyāpatitādibhiś ca ciram upahatānām āvartanam | tadalpakālopahatānāṃ parilekhanaṃ tato 'py alpakālopahatānāṃ pratāpanam | sparśamātropahatānām ekaviṃśatikṛtvo bhasmādibhir mārjanaṃ pratimārjane(naṃ) ca prakṣālanam | aṅgirāḥ |

	gaṇḍūṣaṃ padaśaucaṃ ca yaḥ kuryāt kāṃsyabhājane |

	ṣaṇmāsaṃ bhuvi nikṣipya punaś cākāram ādiśet ||

śātātapaḥ |

	gavāghrāteṣu kāṃsyeṣu śūdrocchiṣṭeṣu vā punaḥ |

	daśabhir bhasmabhiḥ śuddhiḥ śvakākopahateṣu ca ||

hārītaḥ |

	saṃhatānāṃ tu pātrāṇāṃ yady ekam upahanyate |

	tasyaiva śodhanaṃ proktaṃ na tu tatspṛṣṭinām api ||

śaṅkhaḥ |

	malaṃ saṃyogajaṃ tajjaṃ yasya yenopahanyate |

	tasya tacchoṣaṇaṃ proktaṃ sāmānyaṃ dravyaśuddhikṛt ||

yasya śodhyasya svabhāvajaṃ saṃyogajaṃ vā malaṃ yena bhasmādinā dravyeṇopahanyate tasya tacchodhakaṃ bhavatīty arthaḥ | **[257]** baudhāyanaḥ: "dārumayānāṃ pātrāṇām ucchiṣṭasamanvārabdhānām avalekhanam | ucchiṣṭalepopahatānām avatakṣaṇaṃ mūtrapurīṣaretaḥprabhṛtibhir utsargaḥ" | śūdrādyucchiṣṭasamanvārabdhānām ity arthaḥ | avalekhanaṃ śastrādinā gharṣaṇam | yamaḥ |

	yadi mūtrapurīṣābhyāṃ retasā rudhireṇa vā |

	cailaṃ samupahanyeta adbhiḥ prakṣālayet tu tat ||

	yady ambhasā na śudhyet tu vastraṃ copahataṃ dṛḍham |

	chedanaṃ tasya dāho vā yanmātram upahanyate ||

pracetāḥ: "cailānām upahatānām utsvedanaṃ gandhalepāpanayanaṃ tanmātracchedanaṃ vā" | purīṣādiliptavastraviṣayam etat | vyāsaḥ |

	vastraṃ mṛdambhasā śudhyed rajjuvaidalam eva ca |

	rajjvādikaṃ cātiduṣṭaṃ tyājyaṃ tanmātram eva ca ||

vaidalaṃ veṇuvetranaḍādimayaṃ śūrpādi | brahmapurāṇam |

	pratyahaṃ kṣālayed vastraṃ daive pitrye ca karmaṇi |

	śavaviṇmūtraśukrais tu dūṣitaṃ ca mṛdambubhiḥ ||

	śodhyādau śodhanīyaṃ ca gomūtrakṣāravāribhiḥ |

	rajjuvalkalapātrāṇāṃ camarālābucarmaṇām ||

	kṛtvā śaucaṃ tataḥ śuddhir govālair gharṣaṇaṃ tataḥ |

	kauśeyāvikayor deyaṃ rajatāktaṃjalaṃ laghu ||

	suvarnāktaṃ tathā dadyāt kṣaumāṇāṃ cātha vāsasām ||

kṛtvā śaucaṃ ni(cami)tyam anuvartate | aṅgirāḥ |

	śaucaṃ mahārgharomāṇāṃ vāyvagnyarkenduraśmibhiḥ |

	retaḥspṛṣṭaṃ śavaspṛṣṭam āvikaṃ na praduṣyati ||

āvikasyāpi mahārghatvaṃ viśeṣaṇam | bodhāyanaḥ |

	ātmaśayyāsanaṃ vastraṃ jāyāpatyaṃ kamaṇḍaluḥ |

	śucīny ātmana etāni pareṣām aśucīni ca ||

hārītaḥ: "yānaśayanāny aparihāryāṇy eke manyate | tan na varṇaviśeṣāc chuklamalinasaṃsargadarśanāt pāpasaṃsargayogāc ca tasmāt pṛthakśaucāc chreyāṃsaḥ" iti | asyārthaḥ — patitādyupahatāni tathādhovarṇopahatāny uttamavarṇair yānaśayanādīny **[258]** aparihāryāṇīti pūrvapakṣam abhidhāya tan netyādinā siddhāntitam | dharmaśāstreṣu varṇānām uttarādharabhāvena viśeṣadarśanāt | tathā pātakopapātakakāribhir malinais tadrahitānāṃ śuklānāṃ tulyaśayyādiyogena saṃsargasya prāyaścittanimittatayābhidhānād akṛtainso 'pi malinasaṃsarge pāpotpattidarśanāt | yathā vyādhitasaṃsarge nīrogasyāpi rogādayo dṛśyante tadvad atrāpi | tasmāt pṛthakśayyādivaśena pṛthakśaucatvam śreya iti | punar hārītaḥ: "svānupapattau śucyantardhāya samāmananti saṃsparse sacailaṃ snānam evaṃ hy āha | āsanaṃ śayanaṃ yānam antardhāya samācaret" | asyārthaḥ — svakīyaśayyādyalābhe kambalādinā śuddhena tad antardhāyopayoktavyam | tataḥ patitādeḥ śayyādisparśe sacailaṃ snānam iti | śaucādhikāre śaṅkhalikhitau: "sarveṣām āpo mṛdariṣṭeṅgudabilvataṇḍulasarṣapakalkakṣāragomūtragomayādīni śaucadravyāṇi | ahatānāṃ prokṣaṇm ity eke" | ahataṃ yantranirmuktam | vāyupurāṇāt |

	ariṣṭaiś ca tathā bilvair iṅgudaiś carmaṇām api |

	vaidalānāṃ ca sarveṣāṃ carmavac chaucam iṣyate ||

tathā |

	tathā carmāsthidārūṇāṃ śṛṅgāṇāṃ cāvalekhanam |

	maṇivajrapravālānāṃ muktāśaṅkhopalasya ca ||

	siddhārthakānāṃ kalkena tilakalkena vā punaḥ |

	syāc chaucaṃ sarvavarṇānām āvikānāṃ ca sarvaśaḥ ||

siddhārthakā gaurasarṣapāḥ | kalko jalamiśraṃ cūrṇam | smṛtyantaram |

	nyagrodhodumbarāśvatthāḥ plakṣaś caiva caturthakaḥ |

	jambvāmrāmalakāś caiva ity ete carmaśodhakāḥ ||

viṣṇuḥ: "maṇimayam aśmamayam abjaṃ saptarātraṃ mahīnikhananena mūtrapurīṣādyupahatānām etat | śṛṅgadantāsthimayaṃ takṣaṇena dāravaṃ mṛmayaṃ ca jahyāt | tathā kārpāsikānāṃ ca bhasmanā samudāhṛtam" | yamaḥ |

	kṛṣṃājinānāṃ bilvaiś ca bālānāṃ mṛdbhir ambhasā |

	gomūtreṇāsthidantānāṃ kṣaumāṇāṃ gaurasarṣapaiḥ || **[259]**

baudhāyanaḥ: "kṛṣājinānāṃ bilvataṇḍulaiḥ" | paiṭhīnasiḥ: "kṛṣṇājinānāṃ gaurasarṣapai rauravabastājinānāṃ bilvataṇḍulaiḥ" | kāśyapaḥ: "tṛṇakāṣṭharajjumuñjajatucarmaveṇuvidalaphalapatravalkalādīnāṃ cailavac chaucam | mṛddārucarmaṇām atyantopahatānāṃ tyāgaḥ | asaṃskṛtāyāṃ bhūmau nyastānāṃ prakṣālanam | parokṣāhṛtānām abhyukṣaṇam | evaṃ kṣudrasamidhām asaṃskṛtāmedhyādyupahatānām ekapuruṣoddhāryāṇām" || 1.183 ||

	**sphyaśūrpājinadhānyānāṃ musalolūkhalānasām |**

**	prokṣaṇaṃ saṃhatānāṃ ca bahūnāṃ dhānyavāsasām || 1.184 ||**

spyādīnām ano'ntānāṃ yajñāṅgabhūtānām aśucispṛṣṭānāṃ prokṣaṇam eva śuddhiḥ | tathā yajñāṅgabhāvam antareṇāpi bahūnāṃ rāśīkṛtānāṃ dhānyavāsasām aśucispṛṣṭānāṃ prokṣaṇam eva śuddhiḥ | yac carmaṇāṃ prakṣālanam uktaṃ tac caṇḍālādispṛṣṭānām idam | śūdrādispṛṣṭānāṃ bahutvena cānekapuruṣoddhāryatvaṃ lakṣyate | ata eva baudhāyano 'nekapuruṣoddhāryāṇām alpataram aśucitvaṃ darsayati: "saṃhatānāṃ kāṣṭhādīnāṃ prakṣālyāvaśoṣaṇaṃ caṇḍālādisparśe puruṣavāhyād arvāk | ūrdhvaṃ tv anekapuruṣoddhārye dāruśile bhūmisame" iti | laugākṣiḥ |

	caṇḍālādiparāmṛṣṭaṃ prokṣaṇād bahu śudhyati |

	alpaṃ prakṣālayed dhānyaṃ taṇḍulaṃ tu parityajet ||

sātiśayabahutvaviṣayam etat | atra dhānyaṃ satuṣaṃ sasyamātraṃ taṇḍulapratiyogitvāt | taṇḍulādīnāṃ ca tyāgo 'tyalpānām | baudhāyanaḥ |

	vrīhayaḥ prokṣaṇād adbhiḥ śākamūlaphalāni ca |

	tanmātrasyāpahārād vā nistuṣīkaraṇena vā ||

caṇḍālādisparśe 'nekapuruṣahāryāṇāṃ vrīhīṇāṃ prokṣaṇam | mūtrādisaṃsarge tanmātrāpahāraḥ | aśucipāṃsvādidravyasaṃyoge nistuṣīkaraṇam | viṣṇuḥ: "asiddhasyānnasya yanmātram upahanyate tanmātram utsṛjya śeṣasya khaṇḍanaprakṣālane kuryāt" | alpadravyaviṣayam etat | "prokṣaṇaparyagnikaraṇāvagāhanair vrīhiyavagodhūmānāṃ vimarśanaprokṣaṇaiḥ phalīkṛtānāṃ nigharṣaṇadalanaprokṣaṇaiḥ śamīdhānyānām" | **[260]** ayam arthaḥ — anekapuruṣoddhāryāṇāṃ vrīhiyavagodhūmānāṃ yathākramaṃ prokṣaṇaparyagnikaraṇāvagāhanaiḥ śuddhiḥ | avagāhanaṃ prakṣālanam | vrīhyāditaṇḍulānāṃ phalīkṛtānām alpānāṃ vimarśanena | anekapuruṣoddhāryāṇāṃ tu prokṣaṇena | khaṇḍanena śuklīkaraṇaṃ phalīkaraṇam | karābhyāṃ gharṣaṇaṃ vimarśanam | śamīdhyānyānāṃ kośīdhānyānāṃ mudgādīnām anekapuruṣoddhāryāṇāṃ nigharṣaṇena | tato 'lpānāṃ dalanena | anekapuruṣoddhāryāṇāṃ tu prokṣaṇena | vimarśanam eva vigharṣaṇam | yat tu "taṇḍulāṃs tu parityajet" iti tad alpaparimāṇaviṣayam | ādipurāṇāt |

	gṛhadāhe samutpanne vipanne paśumānuṣe |

	abhojyas tadgato vrīhir dhātudravyasya saṃgrahaḥ ||

	mṛnmayenāvaruddhānām adhobhuvi ca tiṣṭhatām |

	yavamāṣatilādīnāṃ na doṣaṃ manur abravīt ||

	tataḥ saṃkramamāṇāgnau sthāne sthāne ca dahyate |

	na ca prāṇivadho yatra kevalaṃ gṛhadīpanam ||

	tatra dravyāṇi sarvāṇi gṛhṇīyād avicārayan ||

ṣaṭtriṃśanmatāt |

	śayanāsanayānāni dravyaṃ ca bahu saṃhatam |

	caṇḍālādibhir apy etat spṛṣṭaṃ saṃprokṣaṇāc chuciḥ ||

	tūlikām upadhānaṃ ca puṣparaktāmbaraṃ tathā |

	śoṣayitvātape kiṃcit karaiḥ saṃmārjayet punaḥ ||

	paścāc ca vāriṇābhyukṣya viniyuñjīta karmaṇi |

	tāny apy atimaliṣṭḥāni anyaiḥ śodhyāni śodhanaiḥ ||

upadhānam ucchīrṣakam | kusumbhapuṣpādinā raktaṃ puṣparaktam | tac cāmbaraṃ puṣparaktāmbaram | śaṅkhaḥ: "śayanāsanayānānāṃ saṃhatavac chaucam" || 1.184 ||

	**takṣaṇaṃ dāruśṛṅgāsthnāṃ govālaiḥ phalasaṃbhuvām |**

dāruprabhṛtīnāṃ mūtrādyupahatānāṃ mṛdādibhir lepagandhāpanayanāśaktau takṣaṇam upahatāvayavāpanayanaṃ śuddhiḥ | asthigrahaṇaṃ śaṅkhadantāder upalakṣaṇam | tathā ca manuḥ |

	kṣaumavac chaṅkhaśṛṅgāṇām asthidantamayasya ca |

	śuddhir vijānatā kāryā gomūtreṇodakena ca || **[261]**

asthimayam aśvapārśvādi | phalasaṃbhuvāṃ bilvanārīkenālābuprabhṛtiphalamayānāṃ govālair gharṣaṇaṃ śuddhiḥ | gopucchāgraromāṇi govālāḥ | yamaḥ |

	alābudārupātrāṇāṃ vaidalānāṃ tathaiva ca |

	atyantopahatānāṃ ca parityāgo vidhīyate ||

	**mārjanaṃ yajñapātrāṇāṃ pāṇinā yajñakarmaṇi || 1.185 ||**

yajñasādhanībhūtānāṃ dārvādimayānāṃ pātrāṇāṃ yathāvidhi prokṣaṇapradhāvanatakṣaṇarūpāṃ śuddhiṃ kṛtvā dakṣiṇena pāṇinā saṃsargaś ca kāryaḥ | ayaṃ ca viśeṣo yajñkarmāṇi kriyamāṇa eva || 1.185 ||

	**soṣair udakagomūtraiḥ śudhyaty āvikakauśikam |**

**	saśrīphalair aṃśupaṭṭaṃ sāriṣṭaiḥ kutapaṃ tathā || 1.186 ||**

**	sagaurasarṣapaiḥ kṣaumaṃ punaḥpākena mṛnmayam |**

ūṣaḥ kṣāramṛttikā | ūṣamṛttikāsahitair udakagomūtraiḥ prakṣālyamānam āvikam ūrṇāmayaṃ kauśeyaṃ ca śudhyati | kauśikaṃ kośodbhavaṃ trasrīmayam ity arthaḥ | udakagomutrair api bahuvacanaṃ doṣānighāte 'pi bahukṛtvo 'pi kṣālanaprāptyartham | uktaprakāreṇāpetadoṣasya punaḥ kevalodakena dhāvanārthaṃ ca | saśrīphalaiḥ sabilvair udakagomūtrair aṃśupaṭṭaṃ netrapaṭṭam | ariṣṭaṃ nimbaṃ tatsahitair udakagomūtraiḥ kutapaṃ pārvatīyacchāgaromamayaṃ kambalavasanam | ariṣṭaṃ phenilaphalam | gaurasarṣapasahitair udakagomūtraiḥ kṣaumam atasīmayaṃ vastram | mṛnmayaṃ tu bhāṇḍaṃ punaḥpākena | śudhyatīti pratyekam abhisaṃbadhyate | caṇḍālādisparśe tu parityāgaḥ | tathā ca smṛtyantaram |

	caṇḍālādair upaspṛṣṭaṃ dhānyaṃ vastram athāpi vā |

	prakṣālanena śudhyet tu parityāgān mahīmayam || iti |

udakagomūtrayoḥ kāryabhedāt samuccayaḥ | purīṣādyupahatānāṃ vastrāṇām iyaṃ śuddhiḥ | anyeṣāṃ tu prokṣaṇādiḥ | devalaḥ |

	ūrṇākauśeyakutapāḥ kṣaumapaṭṭadukūlajāḥ |

	alpaśaucā bhavanty ete śoṣaṇaprokṣaṇādibhiḥ ||

	tān evāmedhyasaṃyuktān kṣālayec chodhanaiḥ svakaiḥ || **[262]**

hārītaḥ: "sarvavāsasāṃ plāvenena śuddhiḥ" | sarveṣām āvikakauśeyādīnām | malena liptānām iyaṃ śuddhiḥ | aṅgirāḥ: "udaśvidvalmīkamṛtsarṣapaiś corṇāmayānām | snehasaktukulmāṣonmardanair gurūṇām ūrṇāmayānām" | udaśvit takram | ūrṇā meṣaromāṇi | viṣṇuḥ: "padmākṣair mṛgaromikāṇāṃ tathā pustakānām abhyukṣaṇam" | ṣaṭtriṃśanmatāt |

	kusumbhakuṅkumai raktaṃ tathā lākṣārasena ca |

	prokṣaṇenaiva śudhyet tu caṇḍālasparśane tathā ||

idaṃ ca yadi prakṣālane saty atyantarāganāśas tadā veditavyam | hārītaḥ: "kṣāroṣābhyāṃ kārpāsaśaṇamayānāṃ putrajīvakāriṣṭaiḥ kṣaumavarorṇānāṃ putrajīvakodaśvidbhyām ajinānāṃ cailavac carmaṇāṃ śuddhiḥ | dṛtīnāṃ rañjanam" | dṛtiś carmamayam udakādibhāṇḍam | udakena samuccayaḥ sarveṣāṃ śodhanadravyāṇām | śaṅkhaḥ: "cailānāṃ mṛdbhasmagomūtrakṣārodakaiḥ | cailavad dhānyānāṃ pakṣacāmaracarmatṛṇavālavalkavetrajānāṃ ca" | gautamaḥ: "cailavad rajjuvidalacarmaṇām utsargo vā" iti | utsargas tyāga upahatabhāgasya | āpastambaḥ |

	snānaṃ dānaṃ tapo homaḥ pitṛyajñaś ca tarpaṇam |

	pañca tasya vṛthā yajñā nīlavastrasya dhāraṇāt ||

	mṛte bhartari yā tu strī nīlavastraṃ vidhārayet |

	tāvad bhartā vaset tasyā narake nātra saṃśayaḥ ||

	strīṇāṃ krīḍārthasaṃyoge śayanīye ca duṣyati ||

brahmapurāṇe |

	vastraṃ viṇmūtraśukrais tu dūṣitaṃ ca mṛdambubhiḥ |

	śodhyādau śodhanīyaṃ ca gomūtrakṣāravāribhiḥ ||

	rajjuvalkalapātrāṇāṃ camasālābucarmaṇām |

	kṛtvā śaucaṃ tataḥ śuddhir govālair gharṣaṇaṃ punaḥ ||

kāśyapaḥ: "tṛṇakāṣṛarajjubhūrjaśaṇakṣaumacīracarmaveṇuvidalapatravalkaladīnāṃ cailavc chaucam" | **[263]** manuḥ |

	madyair mūtrapurīṣair vā śleṣmapūyāsruśoṇitaiḥ |

	saṃspṛṣṭaṃ naiva śudhyet tu punaḥpākena mṛnmayam ||

uśanā: "mṛnmayānām ucchiṣṭaliptānāṃ mārjanam ucchiṣṭaspṛṣṭānāṃ prokṣaṇam" || 1.186 ||

	**kāruhastaḥ śuciḥ paṇyaṃ bhaikṣaṃ yoṣinmukhaṃ tathā || 1.187 ||**

kāruḥ śilpī rajakatantuvāyādiḥ | taddhastakṛtaṃ dravyaṃ śucīty arthaḥ | ayaṃ cāśucitvāpavādaḥ | tenāvarajātīyānām api kārūṇāṃ śilpakriyayā dravyam utpādayatāṃ saṃskurvatāṃ vā pratyavāyahetubhāvaḥ prasakto 'nena nivāryate | tena rajakasevakādibhiḥ saṃkṛtānāṃ vastrādīnāṃ kuvindasūpakārādibhiś cotpādyamānānāṃ dravyāṇāṃ śucitvam eveti vākyatātparyam | tataś ca yenānnādinā dravyeṇa śilpisṛṣṭena vinā dravyotpattisaṃskārau na bhavataḥ, tad api śudhyaty eva yathā vastrotpattau khaliḥ | ata eva śaṅkhaḥ: "kāruhastaḥ śucis tathākarāt taddravyāṇi prokṣitāni" iti | ākaro dravyotpattisthānam | taddravyāṇi cākaradravyāṇi turīvemakhaliprabhṛtīni | paiṭhīnasir viśeṣam āha |

	ākarāḥ śucayaḥ sarve varjayitvā surākaram | iti |

paṇyaṃ vikreyadravyam | tac ca prasāritam eva śuci | tathā ca manuḥ: "paṇyaṃ yac ca prasāritam" iti | tasya cānekapaṇyagrāhakapuruṣasaṃsargādinimitto 'śucibhāvo 'nenāpodyate | bhaikṣaṃ bhikṣāsamūhaḥ | tac ca yatibrahmacātigatam eva śuci | tad āha manuḥ |

	brahmacārigataṃ bhaikṣaṃ nityaṃ medhyam iti sthitiḥ |

brahmacārīti vihitiabhikṣāvṛttipuruṣopalakṣaṇārtham | bhikṣāvṛttyadhikāriṇa āha manuḥ |

	sāṃtānikaṃ yakṣyamāṇam adhvagaṃ sārvavedasam |

	gurvarthapitṛmātrarthasvādhyāyārthyupatāpinaḥ ||

	navaitān snātakān vidyād brāhmaṇān dharmabhaikṣukān ||

sāṃtānikaḥ saṃtānaprayojanaḥ | sārvavedaso dattasarvasvaḥ | upatāpī rogī | anye prasiddhāḥ | yāvataivopaghātena rathyāprasarpaṇādikena vinā bhaikṣaṃ na sidhyati, tanmātrasyāpavādo 'yam | ata eva tadatiriktopaghāte śuddhim āha vasiṣṭhaḥ |

**[264]**	carann abhyavahāryeṣu ucchiṣṭaṃ yadi saṃspṛśet |

	bhūmau nidhāya tad dravyam ācamya pracaret punaḥ || iti |

yasyopahatasyācanāc chuddhis tad ihocchiṣṭaśabdenocyate | abhyavahāryaśabdāc ca bhaiṣamātraviṣayam etat | kiṃ tu pariveṣaṇādiviṣayam api | yat tu manunoktam,

	ucchiṣṭena tu saṃspṛṣṭo dravyahastaḥ kathaṃcana |

	anidhāyaiva tad dravyam ācāntaḥ śucitām iyāt ||

iti, tad vastrādyaparadravyaviṣayam | yoṣinmukhaṃ tathā śucīty arthaḥ | rativiṣayam etat | yac chaṅkhaḥ,

	nārīṇāṃ caiva vatsānāṃ śakunīnāṃ śunāṃ mukham |

	ratau prasravaṇe vṛkṣe mṛgayāyām sadā śuci || iti

yathāsaṃkhyam anvayaḥ | vṛkṣe vṛkṣasthitaphalapātane sakunīnāṃ śakunā(nyā)dīnāṃ mukhaṃ śuci | tad ucchiṣṭam api phalaṃ bhoktavyam ity arthaḥ || 1.187 ||

	**bhūśuddhir mārjanād dāhāt kālād gokramaṇāt tathā |**

**	sekād ullekhanāl lepād gṛhaṃ mārjanalepanāt || 1.188 ||**

bhūśuddhihetavo mārjanādayo vyastāḥ samastāś ca | yathopaghātaṃ mārjanaṃ śalākāhastakena pāṃśvādyapanayaḥ | dāhas tṛṇakāṣṭhādes tatra dahanam | kālo gandārdratādyapanayanaparyantaḥ | gokramaṇaṃ gobhir ākramaṇam | gavāṃ tatra nivasanam iti yāvat | tad uktaṃ manunā: "gavāṃ ca parivāsena bhūmiḥ sudhyati" iti | seko jalasya pañcagavyasya vā prakṣepaḥ | ullekhanaṃ khananam, duṣṭabhāgāpanayanaṃ ca | lepanaṃ gomayena sodakena | gṛhaṃ tu śvādispṛṣṭaṃ mārjanāl lepanāc ca | śudhyatīti śeṣaḥ | gṛhasya bhuvo 'nanyatvena tacchuddhividhānenaiva śuddhatvasiddhau pṛthagvacanam upaghātābhāve 'pi tasya mārjanaṃ lepanaṃ ca pratyahaṃ kāryam eva, anyathā tad aśuddhaṃ syād iti jñāpanārtham | devalaḥ |

	yatra prasūyate nārī mriyate dahyate 'pi vā |

	caṇḍālādhyuṣitaṃ yac ca yatrāriṣṭādisaṃgatiḥ ||

	evaṃ kaśmalabhūyiṣṭhā bhūr amedhyā prakīrtitā |

	śvasūkarakharoṣṭrādyaiḥ saṃspṛṣṭā duṣṭatāṃ vrajet ||

	aṅgāradhūmakeśāsthibhasmādair malinā bhavet || **[265]**

evam amedhyaduṣṭamalinasaṃjñā nirdiśya bhūmer vyavasthayā śuddhim āha |

	khananād dahanāc caiva upalepanadhāvanāt |

	parjanyavarṣanāc caiva śaucaṃ pañcavidhaṃ smṛtam ||

	pañcadhā vā caturdhā vā bhūr amedhyā viśodhyate ||

ūnasaṃkhyāpakṣe 'ntyāvalopaḥ | śmaśānabhuvaḥ pañcabhiḥ śuddhiḥ | tad anyasyā amedhyāyā varṣaṇavarjitaiś caturbhiḥ |

	duṣṭā dvidhā tridhā vāpi śodhyate malinaikadhā |

cirakālaṃ duṣṭāyā upalepanāntais tribhir alpaduṣṭāyā ullekhanadāhābhyām | cirakālaṃ malināyā ullekhanenaiva | yamaḥ |

	khananāt pūraṇād dāhād abhivarṣaṇalepanāt |

	gobhir ākramaṇāt kālād bhūmiḥ śudhyati saptabhiḥ ||

pūraṇaṃ khātāyā upari mṛda upavāpaḥ prakṣepa iti yāvat | tathā |

	arathyā vasudhā medhyā grāmamadhye kvacit kvacit |

	sarvatra vasudhā medhyā yatra lopo na dṛśyate ||

baudhāyanaḥ: "ghanāyā upaghāte bhūmer upalepanam | suṣirāyāḥ karṣaṇam | klinnāyā medhyam āhṛtya pracchādanam" | medhyāṃ mṛdam āhṛtya pracchādayed ity arthaḥ | tathā |

	gocarmamātram abbindur goḥ śodhayati pātitaḥ |

	samūḍham asamūḍhaṃ vā yatra lepo na dṛśyate ||

abbindur udakabindur goḥ pṛthivyā yāvati bhūbhāga ekādaśa gāva upaviśanti tāvad gocarma tanmātraṃ śodhayati | saṃvartaḥ |

	gṛhaśuddhiṃ pravakṣyāmi antaḥsthaśavadūṣaṇe |

	protsṛjya mṛmayaṃ bhāṇḍaṃ siddham annaṃ tathaiva ca ||

	gṛhād apāsya tat sarvaṃ gomayenopalepayet |

	gomayenopalipyātha chāgenāghrāpayed budhaḥ ||

	brāhmaṇair mantrapūtaiś ca hiraṇyakuśavāriṇā |

	sarvam abhyukṣayed veśma tataḥ śudhyaty asaṃśayam ||

baudhāyanaḥ: "udbaddhaśavopaghāte veśmano bhittitakṣaṇaṃ sūryaraśmyanupraveśo 'gnijvālābhimarśanaṃ vā" | **[266]** marīciḥ |

	gṛheṣv ajātisaṃveśe śuddhiḥ syād upalepanāt |

	saṃvāso yadi jāyeta dāhatāpau vinirdiśet ||

	dhānyāni sarvabījāni guḍādirasa eva ca |

	kusumbhakārpāsam atho śudhyed vāryagniśodhanāt ||

ajātiś caṇḍālādiḥ | saṃvāsaś cirasaṃvasanam | [dāho] dīpanaṃ jvalanam | vāryagniśodhanam | vāriṇābhyukṣaṇenāgninā paryagnikaraṇeneti draṣṭavyam | baudhāyanaḥ: "anekapuruṣoddhārye dāruśile bhūmisame iṣṭakāś ca śaṅkulīkṛtāḥ | sudhādipratibaddhāḥ | etāni bhūmisamāni" | caṇḍālādisparśe bhūmiśuddhivad eṣāṃ śuddhiḥ kāryety arthaḥ || 1.188 ||

	**goghrāte 'nne tathā keśamakṣikākīṭadūṣite |**

**	salilaṃ bhasma mṛd vāpi prakṣeptavyaṃ viśuddhaye || 1.189 ||**

gavā prayatnata upāttagandhe tathā keśādisaṃyogadūṣite samuddhṛtopahatabhāge 'nne salilādīnām ekaṃ śuddhaye prakṣipet | makṣikāśabdenātra nīlamakṣikocyate | tathā ca baudhāyanaḥ: "atha havirdoṣān vyākhyasyāmaḥ | yathaitan nīlamakṣikāśātikāmatkuṇāś cailaśiraso yūtiketi" | āśātikā makṣikā yā viṣṭhākrimihetuḥ | kīṭo 'trāmedhyasarpī | tathā ca āpastambaḥ: "yasmiṃś cānekaśaḥ syād anyad vā medhyam amedhyair avamṛṣṭaṃ kīṭo vāmedhyasarpī" iti | yat tu śātātapavacanam,

	dantadhāvanam aṅgulyā pratyakṣalavaṇaṃ tathā |

	mṛttikābhakṣaṇaṃ caiva gomāṃsāśanavat smṛtam ||

iti, tad rogaprāptakevalamṛdbhakṣaṇaviṣayam | yat tu gautamenoktam: "nityam abhojyaṃ keśkīṭāvapannam" iti, tad akṛtasalilādiprakṣepaviṣayam | keśagrahaṇaṃ nakhader upalakṣaṇam | tathā ca baudhāyanaḥ: "keśakīṭanakharomākhupurīṣāṇy anne dṛṣṭvā tanmātram annaṃ parityajyādbhiḥ saṃprokṣya bhasmanā saṃspṛṣṭasya punaḥ praśastavacasānugṛhṇīyād oṃ bhūr buvaḥ svar om ity upariṣṭāad dhyātvā punar eva bhuñjīta" | yamaḥ |

	makṣikākeśam anne tu patitaṃ yadi dṛśyate |

**[267]**	mūṣakasya purīṣaṃ vā kṣutaṃ yac cāvadhūnitam ||

	bhasmanā spṛṣṭam aśnīyād abhyukṣya salilena vā |

	avakṣutaṃ keśapataṅgakīṭair udakyayā vā patitaiś ca dṛṣṭam |

	alātabhasmāmbuhiraṇyabhāgaiḥ saṃspṛṣṭam annaṃ manur āha bhojyam ||

avadhūtaṃ yadupari vastrāvadhūnanaṃ kṛtam | avakṣutaṃ yadupari kṣavayuḥ kriyate | śātātapaḥ |

	keśakīṭayutāghrātaṃ makṣikopahataṃ ca yat |

	klībābhiśastapatitaiḥ sūtikodakyanāstikaiḥ ||

	dṛṣṭaṃ vā syād yad annaṃ tu tasya niṣkṛtir ucyate |

	abhyukṣya kiṃcid uddhṛtya tad bhuñjītāviśeṣataḥ ||

	bhasmanā vāpi saṃspṛśya saṃspṛśed udakena vā |

	suvarṇarajatābhyāṃ vā bhojyaṃ ghrātam ajena vā ||

keśakīṭayutaṃ vāghrātaṃ vā gavādināpi veti vigrahaḥ | hārītaḥ: "aniṣṭagandhopaghrātaśravaṇadarśane keśakīṭapipīlikādibhir annādyasyopaghātena kāñcanarajatabhasmatāmravaiḍū(dū)ryagovālājinadarbhāṇām anyatamenādbhiḥ saṃspṛṣṭamantraprokṣaṇaparyagnikaraṇam ādityadarśanāt pūtaṃ bhavati" | baudhāyanaḥ: "siddhahaviṣāṃ mahatāṃ ca vāyasaprabhṛtyupahatānāṃ taddeśapiṇḍam uddhṛtya pavamānaḥ sva(suva)rjana ityetenābhyukṣaṇam | madhūdake payovikāre ca pātrāt pātrāntaranayanena śaucam | evaṃ tailasarpiṣī | ucchiṣṭasamanvārabdhe tūdake 'vadhāyopayojayet" | parāśaraḥ |

	śṛtaṃ droṇādhikasyānnaṃ śvakākair upaghātitam |

	atyājyaṃ tasya śuddhyarthaṃ brāhmaṇebhyo nivedayet ||

	kartavyaṃ vacanaṃ teṣām annasaṃskārakarmaṇi |

	śvakākādyavalīḍhaṃ tu tyaktvā lālāsamanvitam ||

	gāyatryaṣṭasahasreṇa mantrapūtena vāriṇā |

	bhojyaṃ tat prokṣitaṃ vipraiḥ paryagnikṛtam eva ca ||

jamadagniḥ |

	śṛtānnaṃ droṇamātrasya śvakākādyupghātitam |

	grāsam uddhṛtyāgniyogāt prokṣaṇāt tatra śodhanam ||

**[268]**	annam aikāhikaṃ pakvaṃ śvakādādyupaghātitam |

	keśakīṭāvapannaṃ ca tad apy evaṃ viśudhyati ||

	krītasyāpi vinirdiṣṭam evam eva manīṣibhiḥ |

	na dviḥ pakvaṃ paryuṣitaṃ śukādy evaṃ kadācana ||

droṇaṃ pañcāśadadhikaṃ palaśatadvayam | aikāhikānnaśuddhir alpadhanapuruṣaviṣayā | parāśaraḥ |

	kākaśvādyupalīḍhaṃ tu droṇānnaṃ na vivarjayet |

	grāsam uddhṛtya tanmātraṃ yat tu lālākṛtaṃ bhavet ||

	homodakena vābhyukṣed rājatenāmbunātha vā |

	agnijvālpasaṃsparśāt suvarṇamadhusarpiṣām ||

	viprāṇāṃ mantraghoṣeṇa pūtaṃ bhojyaṃ ca tad bhavet |

	śvavāyasagavāśvādair jagdham annaṃ tu tad bhavet ||

	sneho vā goraso vāpi tatra śuddhiḥ kathaṃ bhavet |

	annaṃ parityajet tatra snehasya pacanena tu ||

	aśvatthalatayā śuddhir gorasasya vidhīyate ||

aikāhikānnāpekṣayālpānnaviṣayam etat | snehagorasayor droṣād alpayoḥ pākādiśuddhiḥ | baudhāyanaḥ: "tvakkeśanakhākhupirīṣāṇi dṛṣṭvā taddeśapiṇḍānnam uddhṛtyādbhir abhyukṣya bhasmanāvakīryābhighārya punar abhiprokṣya vācā praśastaṃ saṃvādya bhuñjīta" || 1.189 ||

	**trapusīsakatāmrāṇāṃ kṣārāmlodakavāribhiḥ |**

**	bhasmādbhiḥ kāṃśyalohānāṃ śuddhiḥ plāvo dravasya ca || 1.190 ||**

goghrātakeśāidūṣitānāṃ trapuprabhṛtīnāṃ kṣārodakāmlodakābhyāṃ kevalavāriṇā ca kṣālanaṃ śuddhiḥ | kāṃsyalohānāṃ tu bhasmādbhiḥ | upaghātānusāreṇa kṣārāmlodakayor vikalpasamuccayau | kevalaṃ tu vāri samuccīyate | evaṃ sarvatra dravyaśuddhau | kṣāro bhasma | kāṃsyasya gavāghrātādyupaghātavato bhasmamārjane saṃkhyāviśeṣam āha āpastambaḥ |

	gavāghrātāni kāṃsyāni śūdrocchiṣṭāni yatnataḥ |

	śudhyanti daśabhiḥ kṣāraiḥ śvakākopahatāni ca || **[269]**

dravasya kṣīrāder goghrātādyupahatasya plāvo 'dbhis tadādhāradhāṇḍasya pūraṇaṃ bahiravasekaparyantam | tathā ca brahmāṇḍapurāṇam |

	dravadravyāṇi bhūrīṇi pariplāvyāni cāmbhasā |

	sasyāni vrīhayaś caiva śākamūlaphalāni ca ||

	tyaktvā tu dūṣitaṃ bhāgaṃ plāvyāny atha jalena ca ||

eṣā śuddhir gorasasyaiva | tathā ca śaṅkhaḥ |

	śrapaṇaṃ ghṛtatailānāṃ plāvanaṃ gorasasya tu |

	bhāṇḍāni plāvayed adhbhiḥ śākamūlaphalāni ca ||

	siddham annaṃ tathā sarpiḥ kṣīraṃ ca dadhi cāmbu ca |

	eteṣām avalīḍhānāṃ tejasā śuddhir iṣyate ||

	kākamārjāranakulasarpamūṣakapakṣibhiḥ |

	saṃskṛtaṃ tu yadā hy annam avalihyeta kenacit ||

	suvarṇavarṇatāmrolkair govālai rajatena vā |

	spṛṣṭam ekatareṇāpi bhojyaṃ ghrātam ajena vā ||

tathā: "ghṛtadadhipayastakrāṇām ākarabhāṇḍasthitānām doṣaḥ" | tathā |

	āghāradoṣe tu nayet pātrāt pātrāntaraṃ dravam |

	ghṛtaṃ tu pāyasaṃ kṣīraṃ tathaivekṣuraso guḍaḥ ||

	śūdrabhāṇḍasthitaṃ takraṃ tathā madhu na duṣyati ||

tejasā śuddhiḥ paryagnikaraṇam | eṣā ca śuddhiḥ sarpiṣi pākena samuccīyate | kṣīrādiṣu plāvanena | suvarṇavarṇatvaṃ tāmrasya viśeṣaṇam | iyaṃ ca śuddhiḥ keśādidoṣam uddhṛtya kāryā | duṣṭadravyāṇām utpavanādiśuddhyantaram āha laugākṣiḥ |

	payodadhivikārādi śuci pātrāntarasthitam |

	plāvanotpavanābhyāṃ ca paryagnikaraṇena ca ||

utpavanaṃ vastrādinā gālanam | yamaḥ |

	āmamāsaṃ ghṛtaṃ kṣaudraṃ snehāś ca phalasaṃbhavāḥ |

	mlecchabhāṇḍasthitā dūṣyā niṣkrāntāḥ śucayaḥ smṛtāḥ ||

tathā |

	devadroṇyāṃ vivāheṣu yajñeṣu prakṛteṣu ca |

**[270]**	kākaiḥ śvabhiś ca saṃspṛṣṭam annaṃ tan na vivarjayet |

	tanmātraṃ annam uddhṛtya śeṣaṃ saṃskāram arhati ||

devadroṇī devayātrā | tanmātram upahatamātram | devadroṇīgrahaṇaṃ bahvannopalakṣaṇartham | prasaṅgād anugrahāntarāṇy apy ucyante |

	tīrthe vivāhe yātrāyāṃ saṃgrāme deśaviplave |

	nagaragrāmadāhe ca spṛṣṭāspṛṣṭir na duṣyati ||

tīrthādisādhyakarmamātrānugraho 'yam | śātātapaḥ |

	gokule kanduśālāyāṃ tailayantrekṣuyantrayoḥ |

	amīmāṃsyāni śaucāni strīṣu bālāntareṣu ca ||

vṛddhaśātātapaḥ |

	tāpanaṃ ghṛtatailānāṃ plavanaṃ gorasasya ca |

	tanmātram uddhṛtaṃ śudhyet kaṭhinaṃ tu payo dadhi ||

	avilīnaṃ tathā sarpir vilīnaṃ tapanena tu || 1.190 ||

	**amedhyāktasya mṛttoyaiḥ śuddhir gandhāpakarṣaṇāt |**

amedhyenāktasya liptasya dravyasya mṛttoyair amedhyagandhāpakarṣaṇe sati śuddhir bhavati | śuddhyantaravidhāv apy etat kartavyam | gandhagrahaṇāt snehalepayor grahaṇam | ata eva devalaḥ |

	pralepasnehagandhānām aśuddhau vyapakarṣaṇam |

	śaucalakṣaṇam ity uktaṃ mṛdambhogomayādibhiḥ ||

amedhyam āha smṛtyantaram |

	dūṣitaṃ varjitaṃ duṣṭaṃ kaśmalaṃ ceti liṅginām |

	caturvidham amedhyaṃ ca sarvaṃ vyakyāsyate punaḥ ||

	śucy apy aśucisaṃspṛṣṭaṃ dravyaṃ dūṣitam ucyate |

	abhakṣyabhojyapeyāni varjitāni parcakṣate ||

	tyaktaḥ patitacaṇḍālau grāmasūkarakukkuṭau |

	śvā ca nityaṃ vivarjyāḥ syuḥ ṣad ete dharmataḥ samāḥ ||

	sravaṇaḥ sūtakī sūtī mattonmattarajasvalāḥ |

**[271]**	mṛtabandhuduṣṭaś ca varjyā hy aṣṭau svakālataḥ ||

	svedāsrubindavaḥ pheno nirastaṃ nakharoma ca |

	ārdraṃ carmāsṛg ity etad duṣṭam āhur manīṣiṇaḥ ||

	mānuṣāsthi śavo viṣṭhā retomūtrārtavāni ca |

	kuṇapaṃ pūyam ity etat kaśmalaṃ cety udāhṛtam ||

	dūṣitaiḥ prokṣitenāpi śuddhis tūktā vidhānataḥ |

	duṣṭair mārjanasaṃskāraiḥ kaśmalaiḥ sarvathā bhavet ||

devalaś ca |

	mānuṣāsthi śavaṃ viṣṭhā retomutrārtavaṃ vasā |

	svedāsru dūṣikā śleṣmā madyaṃ cāmedhyam ucyate |\

manuḥ |

	vasā śukram asṛṅ majjā mūtraṃ viṭ karṇaviṭ nakhāḥ |

	śleṣmāstru dūṣikā svedo dvādaśaite nṛṇāṃ malāḥ ||

karṇaviṭ karṇamalaḥ | eṣāṃ ca dehāc cyutānām evāmedhyateti sa evāha: "dehāc caiva malāś cyutāḥ" iti | yas tu bhasmādibhiḥ saha mṛdo vikalpa uktaḥ so 'medhyāktavyatiriktaviṣayaḥ | atra kātyayanokto viśeṣaḥ |

	prāṇinām api śaucārthe jalena prāṅ mṛdā tataḥ |

	tac ca mūtrapurīṣākte kāryam anyatra vāriṇā ||

mūtrapurīṣagrahaṇaṃ sakalaśārīramalopalakṣaṇārtham | tathā ca manuḥ |

	viṇmūtrotsargaśuddhyarthaṃ mṛdvāry ādeyam arthavat |

	daihikānāṃ malānāṃ ca śuddhiṣu dvādaśasv api ||

arthavad iti gandhalepakṣayakaram ity arthaḥ | atra karṇaviṭprabhṛtiṣūttareṣu ṣaṭsu maleṣu mṛdgrahaṇaṃ vaikalpikam,

	ādadīta mṛdo 'paś ca ṣatsu pūrveṣu śuddhaye |

	uttareṣu tu ṣaṭsv adbhiḥ kevalābhir viśudhyati ||

iti smṛtyantaravacanāt | śuddhivikalpasya vyavasthām āha baudhāyanaḥ |

	deśaṃ kālaṃ tathātmānaṃ dravyam dravyaprayojanam |

	upapattim avasthāṃ ca jñātvā śaucaṃ samācaret ||

	**vākśastam ambunirṇiktam ajñātaṃ ca sadā śuci || 1.191 ||**

**[272]**

vākśastādi sadā śuci | śuddham idam iti brāhmaṇair abhihitaṃ vākśatam | ambunā prokṣitaṃ prakṣālitaṃ vāmbubhir nirṇiktam, yad upahatam iti na vijñātaṃ tad ajñātaṃ tatra śuddhiḥ | yatra śuddhiviśeṣo na vihitas tatraitat || 1.191 ||

	**śuci gotṛptikṛt toyaṃ prakṛtisthaṃ mahīgatam |**

gotṛptikṛd gos tṛṣṇāṃ śamayituṃ samartham | prakṛtisthaṃ svābhāvikarūparasagandham | mahīgataṃ bhuvi sthitaṃ ca yat toyaṃ tac chuci śuddham | manuḥ |

	āpaḥ śuddhā bhūmigatā vaitṛṣṇyaṃ yāsu gor bhavet |

	avyāptāś ced amedhyena gandhavarṇarasānvitāḥ ||

devalaḥ |

	avigandhā rasopetā nirmalāḥ pṛthivīgatāḥ |

	akṣīṇāś caiva gopānād āpaḥ śuddhikarāḥ smṛtāḥ ||

	uddhṛtā vā praśastāḥ syuḥ śuddhaiḥ pātrair yathāvidhi |

	ekarātroṣitās tās tu tyajed apaḥ samuddhṛtāḥ ||

tathā |

	akṣobhyāṇi taḍākāni nadīvāpīsarāṃsi ca |

	caṇḍālādyaśucisparśe tīrthataḥ parivarjayet ||

	akṣobhyāṇām apām nāsti prasrutānāṃ ca dūṣaṇam |

	stokānām uddhṛtānāṃ ca doṣair duṣṭatvam ucyate ||

tīrtham avataraṇamārgaḥ |

bṛhaspatiḥ |

	mṛtapañcanakhāt kūpād atyantopahatāt tathā |

	apaḥ samuddharet sarvāḥ śeṣaṃ vastreṇa śodhayet ||

	vahniprajvālanaṃ krtvā kūpe pakveṣṭakācite |

	pañcagavyaṃ nyaset pascān navatoyasamudbhave ||

hārītaḥ |

	vāpīkūpataḍākeṣu mānuṣaṃ śīryate yadi |

	asthicarmavinirmuktaṃ dūṣitaṃ śvakharādibhiḥ |

	uddhṛtya taj jalaṃ sarvaṃ śodhanaṃ parimārjanam ||

devalaḥ |

	śvasṛgālakharoṣṭraiś ca kravyādbhiś ca jugupsitam |

	uddhared udakaṃ sarvaṃ pañca piṇḍān mṛdas tathā || **[273]**

āpastambaḥ |

	upānacchleṣmaviṇmūtrastrīrajo madyam eva ca |

	ebhir vidūṣite kūpe kumbhānāṃ ṣaṣṭim uddharet ||

viṣṇuḥ |

	jalāśayeṣv athālayeṣu sthāvareṣu mahītale |

	kūpavat kathitā śuddhir mahatsu ca na dūṣaṇam ||

	bhūmiṣṭham udakaṃ puṇyaṃ vaiṛṣṇyaṃ yatra gor bhavet |

	avyāptaṃ ced amedhyena tadvad eva śilāgatam ||

	somasūryāṃśupātena mārutasparśanena ca |

	gavāṃ mūtrapurīṣeṇa śudhyanty āpa iti smṛtam ||

svalpataropaghātaviṣayam etat | yamaḥ |

	prapāsv araṇye ghaṭagaṃ ca kūpe droṇyāṃ jalaṃ kośagatās tathāpaḥ |

	ṛte 'pi śūdrāt tad apeyam āhur āpadgataḥ kāṅkṣitavat pibet tu ||

asyārthaḥ — yady api śūdravyatiriktavarṇasaṃbandhi prapādi tathāpi tadgatajalam anāpady apeyam | āpadi tu peyam eva | prapā jalasatraśālāḥ | tāś ced araṇyagā gṛhād anyatrety arthaḥ | ghaṭagaṃ ghaṭastham | droṇī aśmādimayī sarvārthajalapātrī | kośo dṛtiḥ | manuḥ |

	ajā gāvo mahiṣyaś ca brāhmaṇyaś ca prasūtikāḥ |

	daśarātreṇa śudhyanti bhūmiṣṭhaṃ ca navodakam ||

brahmapurāṇe |

	navakhātajalaṃ gāvo brāhmaṇyaś chāgayonayaḥ |

	śudhyanti divasair eva daśabhir nātra saṃśayaḥ ||

kātyāyanaḥ |

	apo niśi na gṛhṇīyād gṛhṇann api kadācana |

	vivṛtyāgnim upary āsāṃ dhāmnodhāmna itīrayan ||

āpadi rātrau yadi gṛhṇīyād agnim upari dhārayan dāhmodhāmna iti mantraṃ paṭhan gṛhṇīyāt | śātātapaḥ |

	antyair api kṛte kūpe setau vāpyādike tathā |

	tatra snātvā ca pītvā ca prāyaścittaṃ na vidyate ||

yamaḥ |

	caṇḍālabhāṇḍasaṃspṛṣṭaṃ pītvā kūpagataṃ jalam |

	gomūtrayāvakāhāras trirātreṇaiva śudhyati ||

tathā |

	**mārgaṃ māṃsaṃ śvacaṇḍālakravyādādinipātitam || 1.192 ||**

śvādibhir nipātitasya mṛgāder māṃsaṃ tathā syāc chucīty arthaḥ | kravyādā vyāghrādayaḥ || 1.192 ||

**[274]**

	**raśmir agnir ajaś chāyā gaur aśvavasudhānilāḥ |**

**	vipruṣo makṣikā sparśe vatsaḥ prasravaṇe śuciḥ || 1.193 ||**

raśmiḥ sūryādiprabhā | ajaś chāgaḥ | raja iti vā padacchedaḥ | tathāgnī raja iti pāṭhaḥ kāryaḥ | prasiddham anyat | chāyā niṣiddhavyatiriktā | vasudhā ca śmaśānādivyatiriktā | vipruṣaḥ susūkṣmā jalakaṇāḥ | tāsāṃ ca śucijalaprabhavānām api caṇḍālādyaṅgasaṅginā vāyunā nīyamānānām aśucitvāśaṅkāyāṃ śucitvavidhir ayam | raśmyādisparśe tu śucir iti vākyārthaḥ | makṣikāgrahaṇam avarjanīyasparśānāṃ daṃśamaśakādīnām upalakṣaṇārtham | tathā vatsaḥ prasravaṇa ūdhaḥsthakṣīrasya stanāt pratyānayane śuciḥ | yamaḥ |

	āsanaṃ śayanaṃ yānaṃ strīmukhaṃ kutapaṃ kṣuram |

	na dūṣayanti vidvāṃso yajñeṣu camasaṃ tathā ||

	gaur aśvo vipruṣaś chāyā makṣikāḥ śalabhāḥ śukāḥ |

	ajo hastīraṇacchatraṃ raśmayaś candrasūryayoḥ ||

	bhūmir agnī rajo vāyur āpo dadhi ghṛtaṃ payaḥ |

	sarvāṇy etāni śuddhāni sparśe medhyāni nityaśaḥ ||

śaṅkhaḥ: "dhūmāgnirajāṃsi vāyuvīritāni suddhāni" | brahmapurāṇe |

	svadārāṇāṃ ratau vaktraṃ śiśoś ca prasave śuci |

devalaḥ |

	ajāśvā mukhato medhyā gāvo medhyās tu pṛṣṭhataḥ |

	taravaḥ puṣpitā medhyā brāhmaṇāś caiva sarvataḥ ||

śivadharmottare |

	vipro gaur makṣikā svedaḥ chāyāgniḥ sūryaraśmayaḥ |

	rajo bhūr vāyur āpaś ca medhyāni sparśane sadā ||

tathā |

	snātaś ca vipraś cāsnātaś chāgagomakṣikās tathā |

	duṣṭabhūmeś ca saṃlagnās teṣāṃ sūryāṃśumārutāḥ ||

	caṇḍālapatitacchāyā sparśe duṣṭā tu no bhavet ||

tathā |

	śuddhau viprasya dvau pādau mārjārasya tu sarvadā ||

tathā |

	grāmayājī parvakāro bhṛtakādhyāpakas tathā |

	vikrīṇāti ca yo vedaṃ tīrthayajñatapāṃsi ca ||

**[275]**	ayājyayājī bhṛtako nityaṃ śūdropadeśakṛt |

	anyadoṣais tu rahitaḥ pūjyaḥ syād vedapāragaḥ ||

anyadoṣāḥ surāpānadayaḥ | tathā |

	caṇḍālapatitacchāyā sparśe duṣṭā tu no bhavet |

	bhasma kṣaudraṃ suvarṇaṃ sadarbhāḥ kutapās tilāḥ ||

patitacaṇḍālayor gopucchparimitadeśād viprakṛṣṭadeśasthayoś chāyānugraho 'yam |

	apāmārgaśirīṣārkāḥ padmāny āmalakā maṇiḥ |

	mālyāni sarṣapā dūrvāḥ sadā bhadrāḥ priyaṅgavaḥ ||

	akṣatāḥsikatā lājā haridrā candanaṃ yavāḥ |

	palāśakhadirāśvatthatulasīdhātakīvaṭāḥ ||

	etāny āhuḥ pavitrāṇi brahmajñā havyakavyayoḥ |

	pauṣṭikāni malaghnāni śodhanāni ca dehinām ||

	teṣv āpo gośakṛn mṛc ca pavitrāṇi viśeṣataḥ |

	aprāptavyavahāraś ca dūto dāronmukho vratī ||

	makṣikāḥ satataṃ dhānā bhūmis toyaṃ hutāśanaḥ |

	ātmaśayyāsanaṃ yānaṃ jāyāpatyaṃ kamaṇḍaluḥ ||

tathā |

	ajāvigomahiṣyaś ca na duṣyanti kadācana |

	akaśmalaiḥ samiddho 'gnir durmanuṣyair adūṣitaḥ ||

	sarveṣām apy aśaucānāṃ samarthaḥ śodhanāya saḥ |

	dravyāṇām agnidagdhānāṃ medhyatvam upajāyate ||

	jvālābhiḥ spṛṣṭamātrāṇāṃ śucitvaṃ niyataṃ bhavet |

	agner vṛṣalabhuktasya grahaṇaṃ nāsty anāpadi ||

	śvapākavṛṣalau bhoktuṃ brāhmaṇāgniṃ tu nārhataḥ |

	vṛṣalāgner amedhyāgneḥ sūtakāgneś ca karhicit ||

	patitāgneś citāgneś ca śiṣṭair grahaṇaṃ smṛtam ||

aprāptavyavahāro bālaḥ | vṛṣalaś caṇḍālaḥ | brahmapurāṇe |

	grāmād daṇḍaśataṃ muktvā (?) nagarāc ca caturguṇam |

	bhūmiḥ sarvatra śuddhānyā yatra lepo na dēśyate ||. **[276]**

caturviṃśatyaṅgulo hastaḥ | hastacatuṣṭayaṃ daṇḍaḥ || 1.193 ||

	**ajāśvaṃ mukhato medhyaṃ na gaur na narajā malāḥ |**

ajā aśvāś cety ubhayaṃ mukhato mukhapradeśe medhyaṃ śuddham | gaur mukhapradeśe medhyā na bhavati | naraśarīrajā vasāśukrādayo malāḥ svarūpeṇaivāmedhyāḥ | bṛhaspatiḥ |

	pādau śucī brāhmaṇānām ajāśvasya mukhaṃ śuci |

	gavāṃ pṛṣṭhāni medhyāni sarvagātrāṇi yoṣitām ||

yamaḥ |

	pṛṣṭhato gaur ajaḥ skandhe sarvato 'śvaḥ śucis tathā |

	goḥ purīṣaṃ ca mūtraṃ ca sarvaṃ medhyam iti sthitiḥ ||

pṛṣṭhaśabdo 'tra mukhavyatiriktaviṣayaḥ | yad āha baudhāyanaḥ |

	mukhavarjaṃ tu gaur medhyā mārjāraś caṅkrame śuciḥ ||

ajāśvayor mukhaṃ saṃyogād dravyāntaraśodhakatvena medhyam ucyate | sparśamedhyatā tu tayoḥ sarvāṅgaviṣayaiva ||

	**panthānas tu viśudhyanti somasūryāṃśumārutaiḥ || 1.194 ||**

caṇḍālādispṛṣṭā api panthānaḥ somasūryaraśmibhir mārutena ca spṛṣṭāḥ śucayo bhavanti || 1.194 ||

	**mukhajā vipruṣo medhyās tathācamanabindavaḥ |**

**	śmaśru cāsyagataṃ dantasaktaṃ tyaktvā tataḥ śuciḥ || 1.195 ||**

mukhajā vipruṣo lālāyāḥ sūkṣmāḥ kaṇās tā amedhyā na bhavanti | tathācamanabindavaḥ | āsyagataṃ ca śmaśru nāmedhyam | dantasaktaṃ dantalagnaṃ yat kiṃcit tat tyaktvā pumāñ śuciḥ| vasiṣṭhaḥ: "na mukhyā vipruṣa ucchiṣṭaṃ kurvanti | na ced aṅge nipatanti" | manuḥ |

	spṛśanti bandavaḥ padau ya ācāmayataḥ parān |

	bhaumikais te samā jñeyā na tair aprayato bhavet ||

āpastambaḥ: "na śmaśrubhir ucchiṣṭo bhavati | antarāsye sadbhir yāvan na hastenopaspṛśati | ya āsyād bindavaḥ patanta upalabhyante teṣv ācamanaṃ vihitam | ye bhūmau na teṣv āca(cā)med ity eke" | vasiṣṭhaḥ: "na śmaśrugato lepaḥ" iti | **[277]** ucchiṣṭaṃ karotīti śeṣaḥ | tathā |

	dantavad dantasakteṣu yac cāpy antarmukhe bhavet |

	ācāntasyāvaśiṣṭaṃ syān nigirann eva tac chuciḥ ||

ācamananivṛttyartha evakāraḥ | gautamaḥ: "dantaśliṣṭeṣu dantavad anyatra jihvābhimarśanāt prāk cyuter ity eke | cyuteṣv āsrāvavad vidyān nigirann eva tac chuciḥ" | tataś ca dantasaktasya tyāganigaraṇayor vikalpaḥ | āsrāvo mukhodakam | śaṅkhaḥ: "dantavad dantalagneṣu rasavarjam anyatra jihvābhimarśanāt" | rasavarjaṃ rasopalambhavarjam ity arthaḥ | devalaḥ |

	bhojane dantalagnāni nirhṛtyācamanaṃ caret |

	dantalagnam asaṃhāryaṃ lepaṃ manyeta dantavat ||

	na tatra bahuśaḥ kuryād yatnam uddharaṇe punaḥ |

	bhaved aśaucam atyarthaṃ tṛṇavedhād vraṇe kṛte ||

bhojanānantaraṃ dantalagnaṃ tyaktvācāmed bhojanād anyatra neti vyavasthā | bhojanānantaram api yad dantalagnam aśakyoddharaṇaṃ na taduddharṇe punaḥ punar yatitavyam | yatas tṛṇeṣīkayā dantamūle raktasrāvād aśaucabhūyastvam | atriḥ |

	madhuparke ca some ca apsu prāṇāhutīṣu ca |

	nocchiṣṭasya bhaved doṣas tv atreś ca vacanaṃ yathā ||

madhuparkādiṣūcchiṣṭasya | mantrocāraviṣayam etat | ācamanaṃ tu somād anyatra kāryam eva | "na somenocchiṣṭā bhavanti" iti śrutis tannivartikā | ṣaṭtriṃśanmate |

	tāmbūle ca phale caiva bhuktasnehāvaśiṣṭake |

	dantalagnasya saṃsparśe nocchiṣṭas tu bhaven naraḥ ||

	tvagbhiḥ pattrair mūlapuṣpais tṛṇakāṣṭhamayais tathā |

	sugandhibhis tathā dravyair nocchiṣṭas tu bhaved dvijaḥ || 1.195 ||

	**snātvā pītvā kṣute supte bhukte rathyāpasarpaṇe |**

**	ācāntaḥ punar ācāmed vāso viparidhāya ca || 1.196 ||**

snānādiṣu kṛteṣu dvir ācāmet | panthānaś ca viśudhyantīti yad uktaṃ tac caṇḍālādispṛṣṭānāṃ teṣāṃ spraṣṭuḥ snānādinivṛttyartham | atra tu rathyāprasarpaṇamātre **[278]** dvirācamanaṃ vidhīyata ity avirodhaḥ | vāsoviparidhānaṃ punar adhovastranibandhanam | tathā ca baudhāyanaḥ: "nīvīṃ visrasya paridhāyāpa upaspṛśet" iti | nīvī paridhānagranthiḥ | āpastambaḥ: "bhokṣyamāṇas tu prayato 'pi dvir ācāmet" | precetāḥ: "mūtrapurīṣotsarganiṣṭhyūtaśuktavākyābhidhāne punar upaspṛśet" | śuktam anṛtam | paiṭhīnasiḥ: "kāsaśvāsāgame catvāraśmaśānākrāntāv ācāntaḥ punar ācāmet" | catu(tva)raś catuṣpathaḥ | ṣaṭtriṃśanmatāt |

	home bhojanakāle ca saṃdhyayor ubhayos tathā |

	ācāntaḥ punar ācāmed anyatra tu sakṛt sakṛt ||

ācāntaḥ punar ācāmed ity anuvṛttau vasiṣṭhaḥ: "oṣṭhau ca saṃspṛśya yatrālomakau" | viṣṇuḥ: "kṣutvā bhuktvā suptvā bhojanādhyayanepsuḥ pītvā niṣṭhīvya vāso viparidhāya rathyām ākramya kṛtamūtrapurīṣaḥ pañcanakhāsthyasnehaṃ spṛṣṭvā vācāmec caṇḍālamlecchasaṃbhāṣaṇe ca nābher adhastāt prabāhuṣu ca kāyikair malaiḥ surābhir madyair vopahato mṛttoyais tadaṅgaṃ prakṣālyātandritaḥ śudhyet" | ācamyeti śeṣaḥ | prabāhuḥ karāgram | vākyāntarapratipannadvirācamananimittabhāvaiḥ svāpādibhiḥ sāhacaryād etāny api dvirācamananimittāni | vyāsaḥ |

	ācāntaḥ punar ācāmej japahomārjaneṣu ca |

japādiṣu kāryeṣv ity arthaḥ | āpastambaḥ: "svapne kṣavathau śiṅghāṇikāsrvālambhe lohitasya keśānām agner gavāṃ brāhmaṇasya striyāś cālambhe mahāpathaṃ ca gatvāmedhyaṃ copaspṛśyāprayataṃ manuṣyaṃ nīvīṃ ca paridhāyopaspṛśet | ārdraṃ vā śakṛd oṣadhīr būmiṃ vā" | kṣavathuḥ kṣutam | śiṅghāṇikā nāsā tasyā alomakapradeśālambhe | asru netrajalam | śakṛd gośakṛt | tathā ca baudhāyanaḥ: "nīvīṃ visrasya paridhāyāp upaspṛśet | ārdraṃ tṛṇaṃ gomayaṃ bhūmiṃ vā spṛśet" iti | upasparśanam ācamanam | **[279]** vasiṣṭhaḥ: "ruditvācāntaḥ punar ācamet" | brahmāṇḍapurānāt |

	niṣṭhīvane tathābhyaṅge bhuktvā viparidhāya va |

	ucchiṣṭānāṃ ca saṃsparśe tathā pādāvasecane ||

	ucchiṣṭasya ca saṃbhāṣād aśucyupahastasya ca |

	saṃdeheṣu ca sarveṣu śikhāmokṣe tathaiva ca ||

	vinā yajñopavītena nityam eva tv upaspṛśet ||

vinā yajñopavītenāvasthānam ācamananimittam |

	uṣṭrasyāvaśasaṃsparśe darśane cāntyavāsinām |

	jihvā caiva saṃspṛśya dantasaktam upaspṛśet ||

avaśasaṃsparśaḥ pramādasaṃsparśaḥ | śakyaparihāraṃ dantasaktaṃ jihvayā spṛṣṭvopaspṛsed ity arthaḥ | mārkaṇḍeyapurāṇe |

	devārcanādikāryāṇi tathā gurvabhivādanam |

	kurvīta samyag ācamya tadvad annabhujikriyām ||

hārītaḥ: "strīśūdrocchiṣṭābhibhāṣaṇe mūtrapurīṣotsargadarśane | devatām abhigantukāma āca(cā)met" | ṣaṭtriṃśanmatāt |

	mānuṣāsthi vasāṃ viṣṭhām ārtavaṃ mūtraretasī |

	majjānaṃ śoṇitaṃ spṛṣṭvā parasya snānam ācaret ||

	svāny etāni tu saṃspṛśya prakṣālyācamya śudhyati |

	uttīryodakam ācāmed avatīrya tathaiva ca ||

hārītaḥ: "suṣupsur ācāmet |

	rajakaś carmakṛc caiva vyādhajājopajīvinau |

	nirṇejakaḥ saunikaś ca naṭaḥ śaulūṣakas tathā |

	cakrī dhvajī vadhyaghātī grāmyakukkuṭasūkarau ||

	ebhir yad aṅgaṃ spṛṣṭaṃ syāc chirovarjaṃ dvijātiṣu |

	toyena kṣālanaṃ kṛtvā ācāntaḥ prayatā matāḥ ||

rajako vastrādīnāṃ rāgakartā | nirṇajakaś cailadhāvakaḥ | naṭo jātiviśeṣaḥ | anaṭo 'pi raṅgāvataraṇajīvī śaulūṣaḥ | padmapurāṇāt |

	japahomapradāneṣu pitṛpiṇḍodakeṣu ca |

	samāpteṣv ācamed vipraḥ sarvavastuṣu cavaṇe ||

**[280]**	varṇatrayasya saṃsparśād ācamya prayato bhavet |

	saṃsparśe pratilomānāṃ kriyātyāgo vidhīyate ||

	kārukāṇāṃ ca saṃsparśe dvijasyācamanakriyā |

	sparśe tu pratilomānāṃ prāṇāyāmo 'dhiko bhavet ||

karmaprayogakāla etat |

	vipro vipreṇa saṃspṛṣṭa ucchiṣṭena kathaṃcana |

	ācamyaiva tu śuddhaḥ syād āpastambo 'bravīn muniḥ ||

smṛtyantaram |

	cared ācamanaṃ sparśe tatprāptipāpake dvijaḥ |

	varṇānāṃ na brāhmaṇānāṃ pavitraṃ paramaṃ hi te || iti |

prajāpatiḥ |

	upakrame viśiṣṭasya karmaṇaḥ prayato 'pi san |

	kṛtvā ca pitṛkarmāṇi sakṛd ācamya śudhyati ||

viśiṣṭaṃ vihitam | śātātapaḥ |

	aśuciṃ saṃspṛśed anya eka eva sa duṣyati |

	utsṛṣṭo 'nyo na duṣtet tu sarvadravyeṣv ayaṃ vidhiḥ ||

parāśaraḥ |

	kṣute niṣṭhīvane caiva dantocchiṣṭe tathānṛte |

	patitānāṃ ca saṃbhāṣe dakṣiṇe śravaṇaṃ spṛśet ||

vṛddhaśātātapaḥ |

	vātakarmaṇi niṣṭhīvya dantotsarge tathā kṣute |

	patitasya ca saṃlāpe dakṣiṇaṃ śravaṇam spṛśet ||

vihitānuṣṭhānakālād anyatraitat | caturviṃśatimatāt |

	ikṣūny ambu phalaṃ mūlaṃ tāmbūlaṃ paya auṣadham |

	bhakṣayitvāpi kartavyāḥ snānadānodakakriyāḥ ||

smṛtyantaram |

	drākṣādīni phalānīkṣūn payo mūlaṃ ghṛtaṃ dadhi |

	tāmbūlam auṣadhaṃ patraṃ havir bhuktvāpi nācamet || 1.196 ||

	**rathyākardamatoyāni spṛṣṭāny antyaśvavāyasaiḥ |**

**	mārutenaiva śudhyanti pakveṣṭakacitāni ca || 1.197 ||**

rathyāgatāḥ kardamāḥ | tathā toyāni | pakveṣṭakābhiś citāni gṛhādīni antyādispṛṣṭāni mārutenaiva śudhyanti | rathyā mārgaḥ | kardamaḥ paṅkaḥ | antyaś caṇḍālādiḥ | prasiddham anyat | **[281]**

vyāsaḥ |

	rathyākardamatoyāni nāvaḥ pathitṛṇāni ca |

	mārutenaiva śudhyanti pakveṣṭakacitāni ca ||

śaṅkhaḥ |

	rathyākardamatoyena ṣṭhīvanādyena vā tv atha |

	nābher ūrdhvaṃ naraḥ spṛṣṭaḥ sadyaḥ snānena śudhyati ||

yamaḥ |

	sakardamaṃ tu varṣāsu praviśya grāmasaṃkaram |

	jaṅghayor mṛttikās tisraḥ pādayor dviguṇāḥ smṛtāḥ ||

etac ca vākyadvayaṃ yatra kardame vyavasthitam amedhyaṃ rūpato gandhataś ca nopalabhyate tadviṣayam iti || 1.197 ||

**iti śrīvidyādharavaṃśaprabhavaśrīśilāhāranarendrajīmūtavāhanānvayaprasūta-**

**śrīmadaparādityadevaviracite yājñavalkīyadharmaśāstranibandhe 'parārke**

**dravyaśuddhiprakaraṇaṃ samāptam || 7 ||**

**atha saṭīkāyājñavalkyasmṛtau**

**dānaprakaraṇam (8)**

_ato 'nantaraṃ dānaprakaraṇavidhiḥ | pātrāya goprabhṛti dātavyam iti vidhāsyati | tadarthaṃ pātrastutaye brāhmaṇānām eva pātratvāt tatpraśaṃsām āha |_

	**tapas taptvā 'sṛjad brahmā brāhmaṇān vedaguptaye |**

**	tṛptyarthaṃ pitṛdevānāṃ dharmasaṃrakṣaṇāya ca || 1.198 ||**

brahmā tapas taptvā vedasaṃrakṣaṇāya devānāṃ pitṝṇāṃ ca tṛptyarthaṃ dharmapālanāya ca brāhmaṇān sasarja | atas te viśiṣṭakāraṇodbhavatvād ananyasādhyavedaguptyādiprayojanavattvāc ca praśastāḥ | tapaḥ sarvendriyajayaḥ || 1.198 ||

_kiṃ ca_ |

	**sarvasya prabhavo viprāḥ śrutādhyayanaśīlinaḥ |**

sarvasya pṛthvīgatasya vastunaḥ śrutādhyayanaśīlino brāhmaṇāḥ prabhavaḥ svāminaḥ | tathā ca manuḥ |

	brāhmaṇo jāyamāno vai pṛthivyām adhijāyate |

	īśvaraḥ sarvabhūtānāṃ dharmakośasya guptaye ||

**[282]**	sarvaṃ svaṃ brāhmaṇasyedaṃ yat kiṃcij jagatīgatam |

	śreṣṭhenābhijanenedaṃ sarvaṃ vai brāhmaṇo 'rhati || iti |

śrutaṃ gurutaḥ sāṅgopāṅgaśrutismṛtivākyārthāvadhāraṇam | adhyayanaṃ śrutyādipāṭhaḥ | śrutādhyayane śīlayanti samyag ācarantīty evaṃsvabhāvāḥ śrutādhyayanaśīlinaḥ | "śālinaḥ" iti pāṭhe tābhyāṃ ślāghamānāḥ ||

	**tebhyaḥ kriyāparāḥ śreṣṭhās tebhyo 'py adhyātmavittamāḥ || 1.199 ||**

tebhyaḥ śrutādhyayanamātropakṣīṇavyāpārebhyaḥ kriyāparā dharmānuṣṭhānapradhānāḥ | kriyāśabdo 'trādharmavarjanārtho 'pi | arthād eṣāṃ śrutādhyayanasiddhir na hi tadrahitāḥ kriyāparā bhavanti | tebhyaḥ kevaladharmibhyo brahmavidaḥ praśastatamāḥ || 1.199 ||

_evaṃ brāhmaṇān praśasya pātralakṣaṇam āha |_

	**na vidyayā kevalayā tapasā vāpi pātratā |**

**	yatra vṛttam ime cobhe tad dhi pātraṃ prakīrtitam || 1.200 ||**

vidyā svadharmabrahmaviṣayaṃ jñānaṃ tayā kevalayā taporahitayā tapasā vā svadharmānuṣṭhānarūpeṇa vidyārahitena pātratā na bhavati | yato yatra brāhmaṇe vṛttam ācāralakṣaṇam asti vidyātapasī ca staḥ, tatpātraṃ maharṣibhiḥ prakīrtitam | dātāraṃ pāpāt tārayatīti pātram | ata eva manuḥ |

	dānaṃ dharmaṃ niṣeveta nityam aiṣṭikapauṣṭikam |

	parituṣṭena bhāvena pātram āsādya śaktitaḥ ||

	yat kiṃcid api dātavyaṃ yācitenānasūyatā |

	utpatsyate hi tat pātraṃ yat tārayati sarvataḥ ||

vasiṣṭhaḥ |

	svādhyāyāḍhyaṃ yonimantaṃ praśāntaṃ vaitānasthaṃ pāpabhīruṃ bahujñam | 

	strīṣu kṣāntaṃ dhārmikaṃ gośaraṇyaṃ vrataiḥ klāntaṃ tādṛśaṃ pātram āhuḥ | 

yonimān kulīnaḥ |

	ye kṣāntadāntāḥ śrutapūrṇakarṇā jitendriyāḥ prāṇivadhān nivṛttāḥ |

	pratigrahe saṃkucitā gṛhasthās te brāhmaṇās tārayituṃ samarthāḥ ||

dāne vyāsaḥ |

	mātāpitṛṣu yad dattaṃ bhrātṛsvasṛsutāsu ca |

	jāyātmajeṣu yad dattaṃ so 'nindyaḥ svargasaṃkramaḥ ||

	pituḥ śataguṇaṃ dānaṃ sahasraṃ mātur ucyate |

	anantaṃ duhitur dānaṃ sodare dattam akṣayam || iti | **[283]**

vacanaprāmānyān mātṛprabhṛtibhyo vidyāhīnebhyo 'pi vakṣyamāṇaṃ gobhūtaprabhṛti dātavyam avaśyam | tathā ca manuḥ |

	śaktaḥ parajane dātā svajane duḥkhajīvini |

	madhvāpāto viṣāsvādaḥ sa dharmapratirūpakaḥ ||

	bhṛtyānām uparodhena yaḥ karoty aurdhvadaihikam |

	tad bhavaty asukhodarkaṃ jīvato 'sya mṛtasya ca ||

aurdhvadaihikam āmuṣmikaphalaṃ karma | udarko 'ntaḥ | dakṣaḥ |

	dayām uddiśya yad dānam apātrebhyo 'pi dīyate |

	dīnāndhakṛpaṇebhyaś ca tad ānantyāya kalpate ||

śātātapaḥ |

	saṃnikṛṣṭam adhīyānaṃ vyatikrāmati yo dvijaḥ |

	bhojane caiva dāne ca sa hanyāt saptamaṃ kulam ||

bhaviṣyatpurāṇam |

	yas tv āsannam atikramya brāhmaṇaṃ patitād ṛte |

	dūrasthaṃ bhojayen mūḍho guṇāḍhyaṃ narakaṃ vrajet ||

	tasmān nātikramet prājño brāhmaṇān prātiveśmikān |

	saṃbandhinas tathā sarvān dauhitraṃ viṭpatiṃ tathā ||

	bhāgineyaṃ viśeṣeṇa tathā bandhūn gṛhādhipa |

	nātikrāmen naras tv etān mūrkhān api ca gopate ||

	atikramya mahāraudraṃ rauravaṃ narakaṃ vrajet ||

prātiveśmikaḥ samīpagṛhavartī | viṭpatir jāmātā | mahābhārate |

	tadbhaktās tadhanā rājaṃs tadgṛhāś tadvyapāśrayāḥ |

	arthinaś ca bhavanty arthe teṣu dattaṃ mahāphalam ||

arthī dhanaviṣaya ity arthaḥ |

	kṛtasarvasvaharaṇā nirdoṣāḥ prabhaviṣṇubhiḥ |

	spṛhayanti suguptānāṃ teṣu dattaṃ mahāphalam ||

prabhaviṣnubhir balibhiḥ kṛtasarvasvaharaṇā ity arthaḥ |

	hṛtasvā hṛtadārāś ca ye viprā deśaviplave |

	arthārtham upagacchanti teṣu dattaṃ mahāphalam ||

	tapasvinas taponityās tathā bhikṣavarāś ca ye |

**[284]**	arthinaḥ kecid icchanti teṣu dattaṃ mahāphalam ||

dakṣaḥ |

	vyasanāpdṛṇārthaṃ ca kuṭumbārthaṃ ca yācate |

	evam anviṣya dātavyaṃ sarvadāneṣv ayaṃ vidhiḥ ||

	śīlaṃ saṃvāsato jñeyaṃ śaucaṃ saṃvyavahārataḥ |

	prajñā saṃkathayā jñeyā tribhiḥ pātraṃ parīkṣyate ||

saṃvartaḥ |

	śrotriyāya daridrāya arthine ca viśeṣataḥ |

	yad dānaṃ dīyate tasmai tad dānaṃ śubhakārakam ||

devalaḥ |

	mātraś ca brāhmaṇaś caiva śrotriyaś ca tataḥ param |

	anūcānas tathā bhrūṇa ṛṣikalpa ṛṣir muniḥ ||

	ity ete 'ṣṭau samuddiṣṭā brāhmaṇāḥ prathamaṃ śrutau ||

	tebhyaḥ paraḥ paraḥ śreṣṭho vidyāvṛtto viśeṣataḥ |

	brāhmaṇānāṃ kule jāto jātimātro yadā bhavet ||

	anapetaḥ kriyāhīno mātra ity abhidhīyate |

	ekoddeśam atikramya vedasyādānavān ṛjuḥ ||

	sa brāhmaṇa iti prokto nibhṛtaṃ satravān ghṛṇī |

	ekāṃ śākhāṃ sakalpāṃ ca ṣaḍbhir aṅgair adhītya ca ||

	ṣaṭkarmanirato vipraḥ śrotriyo nāma dharmavit |

	vedavedāṅgatattvajñaḥ śuddhātmā pāpavarjitaḥ ||

	śeṣaṃ śrotriyavat prāptaḥ so 'nūcāna iti smṛtaḥ ||

seṣaṃ lakṣaṇaṃ ṣaṭkarmaniratatvaṃ śrotriyasyeva yaḥ prāptaḥ so 'nūcāna ity arthaḥ |

	anūcānaguṇopeto yajñasvāhyāyayantritaḥ |

	bhrūṇa ity ucyate prājñaiḥ śeṣabhojī jitendriyaḥ ||

śeṣaṃ bhṛtyādibhuktaśeṣam |

	laukikaṃ vaidikaṃ caiva sarvaṃ jñānam avāpya yaḥ |

	āśramastho vaśī nityam ṛiṣikalpa iti smṛtaḥ ||

	ūrdhvaretās tapasy ugro niyatāśī tv asaṃśayī |

	śāpānugrahayoḥ śaktaḥ satyasaṃdho bhaved ṛṣiḥ ||

	nivṛttaḥ sarvatattvajñaḥ kāmakrodhavivarjitaḥ |

	dhyānastho niṣkriyo dāntas tulyamṛtkāñcano muniḥ ||

	evam anvayavidyābhyāṃ vṛttena ca smucchritaḥ |

	triśuklā nāma viprendrāḥ pūjyante savanādiṣu ||

anvayādīni trīṇi śuklāni śuddhāni yeṣāṃ te triśuklāḥ | savanaṃ somayāgaḥ | vasiṣṭhaḥ |

	yaṃ na santaṃ na cāsantaṃ nāśrutaṃ na bahuśrutam |

	na suvṛttaṃ na durvṛttaṃ veda kaścit sa brāhmaṇaḥ ||

	yogas tapo dayā dānaṃ satyaṃ śaucaṃ śrutaṃ ghṛṇā |

	vidyā vijñānam āstikyam etad brāhmaṇalakṣaṇam ||

tathā |

	kiṃcid vedamayaṃ pātraṃ kiṃcit pātraṃ tapomayam |

	pātrāṇām adhikaṃ pātraṃ śūdrānnaṃ yasya nodare || 1.200 ||

_idānīṃ deyadravyeṇa pātreṇa viśiṣṭadānavidhim apātre dānaniṣedhaṃ cāha_ |

	**gobhūtilahiraṇyādi pātre dātavyam arcitam |**

**	nāpātre viduṣā kiṃcid ātmanaḥ śreya icchatā || 1.201 ||**

pratyekaṃ goprabhṛtidravyam ātmanaḥ śreyaḥ priyaṃ svargādikam icchatārcayitvā pātrāya pradeyam | ādiśabdena śastrāntaroktam annādideyaṃ saṃgṛhṇāti | apātradānāt pratyavāyodayaṃ viduṣā jānatā kiṃcid apy apātrāya na deyam | pātrāya dātavyam itividhisāmarthyād evāpātre na deyam iti  niṣedhe siddhe pṛthaṅniṣedham ārabhamāṇo mukhyapātrāsaṃbhave pratiṣiddhavarjasya pātratāstīti jñāpayati | atra cāpātraśabdo na pātrād anyad apātram āha kiṃ tu pātraviruddham | yasya ca pātratvaṃ pratiṣiddhaṃ tat tadviruddham | yebhyo na deyaṃ tān āha manuḥ |

	na vāry api prayacchet tu baiḍālavratike dvije |

	na bakavratike pāpe nāvedavidi dharmavit ||

	triṣv apy eteṣu dattaṃ hi vidhināpy arjitaṃ dhanam |

	dātur bhavaty anarthāya paratrādatur eva ca ||

anarthaḥ pratyavāyaḥ |

	yaḥ kāraṇaṃ puraskṛtya vratacaryā niṣevate |

	pāpaṃ vratena saṃchādya baiḍālaṃ nāma tad vratam ||

kāraṇaṃ dharmam ity arthaḥ | vrataṃ prāyaścittam |

	pratigṛhyāśramaṃ yas tu sthitvā tatra na tiṣṭhati |

	āśramasya viropena baiḍālaṃ nāma tad vratam ||

**[286]**	avratānām amantrāṇāṃ jātimātropajīvinām |

	teṣāṃ pratigrahād doṣo na śilā tārayec chilām ||

	apaviddhāgnihotrasya guror vipriyakāriṇaḥ |

	draviṇaṃ naiva dātavyaṃ satataṃ pāpakāriṇaḥ ||

	na pratigraham arhanti vṛṣalādhyāpakā dvijāḥ |

	śūdrasyādhyāpanād vipraḥ pataty atra na saṃśayaḥ ||

vasiṣṭhaḥ |

	upakrandati dātāraṃ gaur aśvaḥ kāñcanaṃ mahī |

	aśrotriyasya viprasya hastau dṛṣṭvā nirākṛteḥ ||

dakṣaḥ |

	dhūrte chadmani malle ca kuvidye kitave śaṭhe |

	cāṭacāraṇacaureṣu dattaṃ bhavati niṣphalam ||

vyāsaḥ |

	ūṣare vāpite bījaṃ yac ca bhasmani hūyate |

	kriyāhīneṣu yad dattaṃ na ca tat pretya no iha ||

vṛddhamanuḥ |

	pātrabhūto 'pi yo vipraḥ pratigṛhya pratigraham |

	asatsu viniyuñjīta tasmai deyaṃ na kiṃcana ||

	saṃcayaṃ kurute yaś ca pratigṛhya samantataḥ |

	dharmārthaṃ nopayuṅkte ca na taṃ taskaram arcayet ||

yamaḥ |

	yasya vedaś ca vedī c vicchidyete tripauruṣam |

	sa vai durbrāhmaṇo nāma yaś caiva vṛṣalīpatiḥ ||

vasiṣṭhaḥ |

	udakyānvāsate yeṣāṃ ye ca kecid anagnayaḥ |

	kulaṃ cāśrotriyaṃ yeṣāṃ sarve te śūdradharmiṇaḥ ||

manuḥ |

	samam abrāhmaṇe dānaṃ dviguṇaṃ brāhmaṇabruve |

	sahasraguṇam ācārye anantaṃ vedapārage ||

samaṃ yāvad dhanaṃ tāvat tasya phalam ity arthaḥ | śātātapaḥ |

	neṣṭaṃ devalake dattam apratiṣṭhaṃ ca vārduṣau |

	yac ca nirṇejake dattaṃ niṣphalāśaṃ vidhīyate ||

	yaś ca liṅgyucitāṃ vṛttim aliṅgebhyaḥ prayacchati |

	ghorāyāṃ brahmahatyāyāṃ pacyate nātra saṃśayaḥ ||

	abrāhmaṇāś ca ṣaṭ proktā ṛṣiḥ śātātapo 'bravīt |

	ādyo rājāśrayas teṣāṃ dvitīyaḥ krayavikrayī ||

**[287]**	tṛtīyo bahuyājyaḥ syāc caturtho grāmayājakaḥ |

	pañcamas tu bhṛtas teṣāṃ grāmasya nagarasya ca ||

	anāgatāṃ tu yaḥ pūrvāṃ sādityāṃ caiva paścimām |

	nopāsīta dvijaḥ saṃdhyāṃ sa ṣaṣṭho 'brāhmaṇaḥ smṛtaḥ ||

vyāsaḥ |

	brahmabījasamutpanno mantrasaṃskāravarjitaḥ |

	jātimātropajīvī ca bhaved abrāhmaṇaḥ sa tu ||

	garbhādhānādibhir yuktas tathopanayanena ca |

	na karmakṛn na cādhīte sa bhaved brāhmaṇabruvaḥ ||

yat tu bṛhaspatinoktam:

	śūdre samaguṇaṃ dānaṃ vaiśye taddviguṇaṃ smṛtam |

	kṣatriye triguṇaṃ dānaṃ brāhmaṇe ṣaḍguṇaṃ smṛtam ||

iti, tad annadānaviṣayam, "kṛtānnam itare" iti gautamavacanāt | kṛtānnaṃ pakvānnam | itare kṣatriyādayaḥ | manuḥ |

	anarhate yad dadāti na dadāti yad arhate |

	arhānarhāparijñānād dhanād dharmāc ca hīyate || iti |

atra sāmānyato gavādinā deyena pātre dānena viśiṣṭaṃ dānaṃ vihitaṃ tatra dānaśabdārthaṃ tasya cāvāntaraviśeṣān āha devalaḥ |

	arthānām udite pātre śraddayā pratipādanam |

	dānam ity abhinirdiṣṭaṃ vyākhyānaṃ tasya vakṣyate ||

arthā deyadravyāṇi teṣāṃ pratipādanaṃ nāma pātraṃ prati svasvābhibhāvāpādanaparyantas tyāgaḥ |

	dvihetu ṣaḍadhiṣṭhānaṃ ṣaḍaṅgaṃ ṣaḍvipākayuk |

	catuṣprakāraṃ trividhaṃ trināśaṃ dānam ucyate ||

tatra dvihetukatvam āha |

	nālpatvaṃ vā bahutvaṃ vā dānasyābhyudayāvaham |

	śraddhā śaktiś ca dānānāṃ ṣaḍetāni pracakṣate ||

	pātrebhyo dīyate nityaṃ vṛddhikṣayakarau hi tau ||

eko vāśabda ivārthe dvitīyaḥ samuccaye | yathā nālpatvaṃ dānābhyudayasya kāraṇaṃ tathā na bahutvam api kiṃ tu śraddhāśaktī | śaktir audāryam apaścāttāpaś ca | ṣaḍadhiṣṭhānatvam āha |

**[288]**	dharmam arthaṃ kāmaṃ ca vrīḍāharṣabhayāni ca |

	adhiṣṭhānāni dānānāṃ ṣaḍ etāni pracakṣate ||

	pātrebhyo dīyante dānam anapekṣya prayojanam |

	kevalaṃ tyāgabuddhyā yad dharmadānaṃ tad ucyate ||

	proyojanam anapekṣyaiva prasaṅgād yat pradīyate |

	tad arthadānam ity āhur vaidikaṃ phalahetukam ||

	strīpānamṛgayākṣāṇāṃ prasaṅgād yad pradīyate 

	anarheṣu ca rāgeṇa kāmadānaṃ tad ucyate ||

	saṃsadi vrīḍayāśrutya yo 'rtho 'rthibhyaḥ prayācitaḥ |

	pradīyate cet tad dānaṃ vrīḍādānam iti smṛtam ||

	dṛṣṭvā priyāṇi śrutvā ca harṣavad yat pradīyate |

	harṣadānam iti prāhur dānaṃ tad dharmacintakāḥ ||

	akrośān arthahiṃsānāṃ pratīkārāya yad bhayāt |

	dīyate tāpakartṛbhyo bhayādānaṃ (?) tad ucyate ||

ṣaḍaṅgatvam āha |

	dātā pratigrahītā ca śraddhā daivaṃ ca dharmayuk |

	deśakālau ca dānānām aṅgāny etāni ṣaḍ viduḥ ||

	apāparogī dharmātmā ditsur avyasanaḥ śuciḥ |

	anindyājīvakarmā ca ṣaḍbhir dātā praśasyate ||

	triśuklaḥ kṛśavṛttiś ca ghṛṇāluḥ sakalendriyaḥ |

	vimukto yonidoṣebhyo brāhmaṇaḥ pātram ucyate ||

triśulko vyākhyātaḥ |

	saumukhādyabhisaṃprītir arthināṃ darśane sadā |

	satkṛtiś cānasūyā ca tadā śraddheti kīrtyate ||

	aparābādham akleśaṃ svayaṃ yenārjitaṃ dhanam |

	svalpaṃ vā vipulaṃ vāpi deyam ity abhidhīyate ||

	yady atra durlabhaṃ dravyaṃ yasmin kāle 'pi vā punaḥ |

	dānādau deśakālau tau syātāṃ śreṣṭhau na cānyathā ||

	avasthādeśakalānāṃ pātradātroś ca saṃpadā |

	hīnaṃ vāpi bhaec chreṣṭhaṃ śreṣṭhaṃ vāpy anyathā bhavet || **[289]**

ṣaḍvipākatvam āha |

	duṣphalaṃ niṣphalaṃ hīnaṃ tulyaṃ vipulam akṣayam |

	ṣaḍvipākayug uddiṣṭaṃ ṣaḍ etāni vipākataḥ ||

	nāstikas tena hiṃsrebhyo 'varāya patitāya ca |

	piśunabhrūṇahartṛbhyāṃ pradattaṃ duṣphalaṃ bhavet ||

avaraḥ kṣatriyādiḥ |

	mahad apy aphalaṃ dānaṃ śaddhayā parivarjitaḥ |

	parabādhakaraṃ dānaṃ param apy ūnatāṃ vrajet ||

	yathoktam api yad dattaṃ cittena kaluṣeṇa tu |

	tat tu saṃkalpadoṣeṇa dānaṃ tulyaphalaṃ bhavet ||

	yathoktaiḥ sakalaiḥ ṣaḍbhir dānaṃ syād vipulodayam |

udayaḥ phalam |

	anukrośavaśād dattaṃ dānam akṣayatāṃ vrajet ||

anuśrośo dayā | dīyata iti dānaṃ gavādi | dhruvādicatuṣprakāram āha |

	dhruvam ājasrikaṃ kāmyaṃ naimittikam iti kramāt |

	vaidiko dānamārgo 'yaṃ caturdhā varṇyate dvijaiḥ ||

	prapārāmataḍākādi sarvakāmaphalaṃ dhruvam |

	tad ājasrikam ity āhur dīyate yad dine dine ||

	apatyavijayaiśvaryastrībālārthaṃ yad iṣyate |

	icchāsaṃsthaṃ tu tad dānaṃ kāmyam ity abhidhīyate ||

	kālāpekṣaṃ kriyāpekṣam arthāpekṣam iti smṛtam |

	tridhā naimittikaṃ proktaṃ sahomaṃ homavarjitam ||

trividhatvam āha |

	navottamāni catvāri madhyamāni vidhānataḥ |

	adhamānīti śeṣāṇi trividhatvam idaṃ viduḥ ||

	annaṃ dadhi madhu trāṇaṃ gobhūrukmāśvahastinaḥ |

	dānāny uttamadānāni uttamadravyadānataḥ ||

	vidyā cācchādanavāsaparibhogauṣadhāni ca |

	dānāni madhyamānīti madhyamadravyadānataḥ ||

	upānatpreṅkhayānāni chatrapātrāsanāni ca |

	dīpakṣṭhaphalādīni caramaṃ bahuvārṣikam ||

**[290]**	bahutvād arthajātānāṃ saṃkhyāseṣeṣu neṣyate |

	adhamāny avaśiṣṭāni sarvanānāy ato viduḥ ||

vināśitvam āha |

	iṣṭaṃ dattam adhītaṃ vā praṇaśyaty anukīrtanāt |

	ślādhānuśocanābhyāṃ ca bhagnatejo vipadyate ||

	tasmād ātmakṛtaṃ puṇyaṃ na vṛthā parikīrtayet |

	uktavantam iti prāhus tam evaṃ kṛtavedanam ||

	evaṃ sarvaguṇopetam uktadoṣair vivarjitam |

	kāmadhugdhenuvaddānaṃ phalaty ātmepsitaṃ phalam ||

	iha kīrtiṃ ca dānākhyāṃ sphītān bhogāṃs triviṣṭape |

	dānaśraddhāṃ tṛtīye ca janmani prasavottame ||

	anyāyādhigatāṃ dattvā sakalāṃ pṛthivīm api |

	śraddhāvarjam apātrāya na kāṃcid bhūtim āpnuyāt ||

	pradāya śākamuṣṭiṃ vā śraddhābhaktisamudyatām |

	mahate pātrabhūtāya sarvābhyudayam āpnuyāt ||

manuḥ |

	śraddhayeṣṭaṃ ca pūrtaṃ ca nityaṃ kuryāt prayatnataḥ |

	śraddhākṛte hy akṣaye te bhavataḥ svāgatair dhanaiḥ ||

mahābhāratam |

	ekāgnikarma havanaṃ tretāyāṃ yac ca hūyate |

	antarvedyāṃ ca yad dānam ity abhidhīyate ||

	vāpīkūpataḍākāni devatāyatanāni ca |

	annapradānam ārāmaḥ pūrtam ity abhidhīyate ||

nāradaḥ |

	ātithyaṃ vaiśvadevaś ca iṣṭam ity abhidhīyate |

	puṣkariṇyas tathā vāpyo devatāyatanāni ca ||

	annapradānam ārāmaḥ pūram ity abhidhīyate |

	dvādaśyāṃ caiva yad dānaṃ pūrtam ity abhidhīyate ||

anena cādiśabdena yajñadakṣiṇādānād dānāntaraṃ gṛhyate |

	iṣṭāpūrtau dvijātīnāṃ dharmaḥ sāmānya ucyate |

	adhikārī bhavec chūdraḥ pūrte dharme na vaidike ||

manuḥ |

	yo 'rcitaṃ pratigṛhṇāti dadāty arcitam eva tu |

	tāv ubhau gacchataḥ svargaṃ narakaṃ ca viparyaye || **[291]**

yamaḥ |

	dānaṃ hi bahumānād yo guṇavadbhyaḥ prayacchati |

	sa tu pretya dhanaṃ labdhvā putrapautraiḥ sahāśnute ||

bahumāna ādaraḥ |

	paraṃ cānupahanyeha dānaṃ datvā vicakṣaṇaḥ |

	sukhodayaṃ sukhodarkaṃ pretya vai labhate dhanam ||

āpastambaḥ: "sarvāṇy udakapūrvāṇi dānāni" || 1.201 ||

_na kevalam apātrāya na deyaṃ kiṃ tu tena na pratigrāhyam apīty āha |_

	**vidyātapobhyāṃ hīnena naiva grāhyāḥ pratigrahaḥ |**

**	gṛhṇan pradātāram adho nayaty ātmānam eva ca || 1.202 ||**

vidyātapobhyāṃ hīnena pātralakṣaṇarahitena | pratigṛhyata iti pratigrahaḥ | sa na grāhyaḥ | yato vidyādirahitaḥ pratigṛhṇan dātāram ātmānaṃ ca narakaṃ nayati || 1.202 ||

	**dātavyaṃ pratyahaṃ pātre nimitteṣu viśeṣataḥ |**

**	yācitenāpi dātavyaṃ śraddhāpūtaṃ ca śaktitaḥ || 1.203 ||**

pratyaham anuditaṃ pātre dātavyam | nimitteṣu saṃkrāntyādiṣu tu viśeṣata ādareṇa dātavyam | yācitena dātavyam apiśabdād ayācitena ca | tatrāyācitadānaṃ praśastatamam | tathā ca śātātapaḥ |

	abhigamya tu yad dānaṃ yat tu dānam ayācitam |

	vidyate sāgarasyāntas tasyānto naiva dṛśyate ||

tathā |

	gatvā yad dīyate dānaṃ tad anantaphalaṃ smṛtam | |

	 sahsraguṇam āhūte yācite tu tadardhakam ||

pātre śraddhāpūtaṃ śaktita iti ca prativākyaṃ saṃbadhyate | dānanimittaṃ kālaḥ kriyārtha ity uktaṃ devalena: "kālāpekṣaṃ kriyāpekṣam" ityādinā | tatra kālo vidhīyate pratyaham ityādināharmātram | anena ca rātrir vyudasyate | nimitteṣv ity anena kālaviśeṣā ayanādayo nirdiśyante | tathā ca śātātapaḥ |

	ayanādau sadā deyaṃ dravyam iṣṭaṃ gṛhe tu yat |

	ṣaḍaśītimukhe caiva vimukhe candrasūryayoḥ ||

vimokṣe vartamānayor na tu muktayor ity arthaḥ, "uparāge tu tatkālam" iti vasiṣṭhavacanāt | vyāsaḥ |

	saṃkrāntau yāti dattāni havyakavyāni dātṛbhiḥ |

	tāni nityaṃ dadāty arkaḥ punar janmani janmani ||

	śatam indukṣaye dānaṃ sahasraṃ tu dinakṣaye |

	viṣuve śatasāhsraṃ vyatīpāte tv anantakam ||

saṃvartaḥ |

	ayaneṣu ca yad dattaṃ ṣaḍaśītimukheṣu ca |

	candrasūryoparāge vā dattaṃ bhavati cākṣayam ||

indukṣaye 'māvasyāyām |

	ekasmin sāvane tv ahni tithīnāṃ tritayaṃ yadā |

	tadā dinakṣayaḥ proktas tatra sāhasrikaṃ phalam ||

vasiṣṭhaḥ | 

	mṛgakarkaṭasaṃkrāntī dve tūdagdakṣiṇāyane | 

mṛgo makaraḥ |

	viṣuve ca tulāmeṣe tayor madhye tato 'parāḥ |

	vṛṣavṛścikakumbheṣu siṃhe caiva yadā raviḥ ||

	etad viṣṇupadaṃ nāma viṣuvādadhikaṃ phalam |

	kanyāyāṃ mithune mīne dhanuṣy api raver gatiḥ ||

	ṣaḍaśītimukhī proktā ṣaḍaśītiguṇā phalaiḥ |

	atītānāgate puṇye dve tūdagdakṣiṇāyane |

	uparāge tu tatkālam atīte cottarāyaṇe ||

parvakālas tu sarvasaṃkrāntiṣu prāg ūrdhvaṃ ca bhavati | ata eva vasiṣṭhenaiva vyavasthoktā |

	triṃśatkarkaṭake nāḍyo makare viṃśatiḥ smṛtāḥ |

	vartamāne tulameṣe nāḍyas tūbhayato daśa || iti |

atra vartamāna ubhatata iti ca sarvair eva karkaṭādibhiḥ saṃbadhyate, sākāṅkṣatvāviśeṣāt | tadviśeṣe caikasya pāṭhasaṃnidhir nānvayaniyāmako 'varjanīyatvenānyathāsiddhatvāt |

	ṣaḍaśītyāṃ vyatītāyāṃ ṣaṣṭir uktās tu nāḍikāḥ |

phalabhūyastvābhiprāyam etat | ata eva ṣaḍaśītimukhe 'pi pūrvam api parvakālam āha |

	viṣṇupadyāṃ dhanurmīnanṛyukkanyāsu vai yadā |

	pūrvottaragatai rātrau yadā saṃkramaṇaṃ bhavet ||

**[293]**	pūrvottarāgatai rātrau bhāgaiḥ saṃkramaṇaṃ bhavet |

	pūrvāhṇe pañca nāḍyas tu puṇyāḥ proktā manīṣibhiḥ ||

	aparāhṇe tu pañcaiva śraute smārte ca karmaṇi || iti |

anena ṣaḍaśītyāṃ saṃkrāntyāṃ pūrvarātrer bhāvinyām aparāhṇe saṃkrāntikāryaṃ kartavyam ity ucyate | nṛyug mithunarāśiḥ |

	puṇyākhyā viṣṇupadyāṃ ca prāk paścād api ṣoḍaśa |

	ahni saṃkramaṇe puṇyam ahaḥ kṛtsnaṃ prakīrtitam ||

	rātrau saṃkramaṇe proktaṃ dinārdhaṃ snānadānayoḥ |

	ardharātrād adhas tasmin madhyāhnasyopari kriyā ||

	ūrdhvaṃ saṃkramaṇe cordhvam udayāt praharadvayam |

	pūrṇe ced ardharātre tu yadā saṃkramate raviḥ ||

	prāhur dinadvayaṃ puṇyaṃ muktvā makarakarkaṭau ||

atra ceyaṃ vyavasthā — pūrvarātrasaṃkramaṇe pūrvasyāhna uttarārdhe snānādikaṃ kāryam aparatra saṃkramaṇe tūttarasyāhnaḥ pūrvāhṇe | yat tu vacanam,

	rāhudarśanasaṃkrāntivivāhātyayavṛddhiṣu |

	snānadānādikaṃ kuryān niśi kāmyavrateṣu ca ||

iti, tan makarakarkaṭasaṃkrāntiviṣayam, "muktvā makarakarkaṭau" iti vacanāt | anena vacanenāyanadvaya eva rātrau snānādy anugṛhyate | "rātrau snānaṃ na kurvīta" iti neṣedhaḥ saṃkrāntyantare bhavaty eva | yat tu,

	triṃśatkarkaṭake puṇyaṃ makare viṃśatis tathā |

	bhaviṣyaddakṣiṇe puṇyam atīte cottarāyaṇe ||

iti, tat puṇyātiśayapratipādanārtham | na punar niyamārtham | ata eva,

	madhye viṣuvati dānaṃ viṣṇupade dakṣiṇāyane cādau |

	ṣaḍaśītimukhe 'tīte tathodagayane ca bhūriphalam ||

iti smaranti | ata eve tenāviśeṣeṇoktam |

	saṃkrāntisamayaḥ sūkṣmo durjñeyo 'pi mitekṣaṇaiḥ |

	tadyogād apy adhaś cordhvaṃ triṃśan nāḍyaḥ pavitritāḥ ||

**[294]**	āsannasaṃkramaṃ puṇyaṃ dinārdhaṃ snānadānayoḥ |

	rātrau saṃkramaṇe bhānor viṣuvaty ayane dine ||

	yā yāḥ saṃnihitā nāḍyas tās tāḥ puṇyatamāḥ smṛtāḥ ||

evaṃ cayam arthaḥ siddho bhavati — atītatvaṃ saṃkrānter anāgatatvaṃ vānādṛtya yatra dinārdhe 'tītānāgatā vā saṃkrāntiḥ pratyāsannā bhavati tatra snānadānādikaṃ karyam iti | atha prakṛtam ucyate — kriyāpi hiṃsādiḥ prāyaścittirūpasya dānasya nimittaṃ bhavati | yathoktaṃ manunā,

	dhanaṃ vā jīvanāyālaṃ gṛhaṃ vā sapricchadam |

	sarvasvaṃ vā vedavide brāhmaṇayopapadayet ||

ityādi prāyaścittaprakaraṇe | artho 'pi dānanimittaṃ bhavati | yathoktaṃ mahābhārate |

	ekāṃ gāṃ daśagur dadyād daśa dadyāt tu gośatī |

	śataṃ sahasragur dadyāt sarve tulaphalāḥ smṛtāḥ || iti |

yācitenāpi dātavyam ity uktam | tatra yebhyo 'vaśyaṃ dātavyaṃ tān āha manuḥ |

	sāṃtānikaṃ yakṣyamāṇam adhvagaṃ sārvavedasam |

	gurvarthipitṛmātrarthisvādhyāyārthyupatāpinaḥ ||

	na vai tān snātakān vidyād brāhmaṇān dharmabhaikṣukān |

	niḥsvebhyo deyam etebhyo dānaṃ vidyāviśeṣataḥ ||

	etebhyo hi dvijāgryebhyo deyam annaṃ sadakṣiṇam |

	itarebhyo bahirvedi kṛtānnaṃ bhuvi dīyate || iti |

sāṃtāniko yaḥ saṃtānāya kanyām udvoḍhum icchati | yakṣyamāṇaḥ somayāgaṃ kariṣyamāṇaḥ | adhvago dharmāya pracalitaḥ | sārvavedasaḥ kṛtaviśvajidyāgaḥ | guror artho gurvarthas tadarthī | evaṃ pitrarthī mātrarthī svādhyāyārthī upatāpī rogī ca | te sarve snātakāḥ samāvṛttatvāt | dharmabhikṣukāḥ, vihitabhikṣākāritvāt | brāhmaṇaśabdāt kṣatriyādinivṛttiḥ | dakiṣṇāśabdenātra gavādidravyam evocyate | na tu ṛtvikparikriyo 'saṃbhavatvāt | itare kṣatriyādayaḥ | bahirvedi krator anyatrety arthaḥ | bairvedīti deyam annaṃ sadakṣiṇam ity anena saṃbadhyate, "bahirvedi bhikṣaṃāṇebhya" it gautamavacanāt | kṛtānnaṃ pakvānnam || 1.203 ||

**[1.204]**

_godānetikartavyatām āha_ |

	**hemaśṛṅgī śaphai raupyaiḥ suśīlā vastrasaṃyutā |**

**	sakāṃsyapātrā dātavyā kṣīriṇī gauḥ sadakṣiṇā || 1.204 ||**

hemayukta śṛṅge yasyāḥ sā hemaśṛṅgī | raupymayaiḥ khurair viśiṣṭā | suśīlā sādhvī | vastrasaṃyutā vastrācchāditā | kāṃsyapātrasahitā | kṣīriṇī bahukṣīrā | sadakṣiṇā suvarṇadakṣiṇāsahitā gaur dātavyā | skandapurāṇe |

	yo naro gāṃ pracchet tu savatsāṃ kāṃsyadohanam |

	hemaśṛṅgīṃ raupakhurāṃ dukūlakṣaumavāsitām ||

	śayyāstaraṇasaṃpannāṃ bahupuṣpaphalair yutām |

	brāhmaṇaṃ pūjayitvā tu gandhamālyair alaṃkṛtām ||

	devair adhyāsitāṃ tāṃ tu sarvair hastadvayena tu |

	mṛdubandhena badhnīyād antaḥślakṣṇena rajjunā ||

	kuśān suvarṇabījāni tilān siddhārthakāṃs tathā |

	pradadyāt tāṃ tato adbhiś ca mantreṇānena suvrata ||

	sarvadevamayīṃ dogdhrīṃ sarvalokamayīṃ tathā |

	sarvalokanimittāṃ gāṃ sarvadevanamaskṛtām ||

	prayacchāmi mahāsattvām akṣayāya śubhām iti |


    oṃ hrīṃ namo bhagavati brahmamātar viṣṇubhagini rudradaivate sarvapāpapramocini svarūpaṃ smara iḍe iḍānte havye cāndre ghṛtimati sarasvati suśrute ehy ehi huṃ kuru kuṃ kuru sarvalokamaye ehy āgacchāgaccha svāhā | it dhenukarṇajapaḥ |

	pratigrahītā dātā ca tāv ubhau svargagāminau(ṇau) |

	yadi smārayate pūrvaṃ karṇena dvijasattama || iti |

matsyapurāṇe |

	evaṃ datvā tu gāṃ tāṃ tu yatra yatra prajāyate |

	tatra tatra gatā sā tu jantuṃ tārayate balāt |

	svargalokaṃ naro gatvā ramate ca yathāmaraḥ ||

**[296]**	sa tayā mānuṣe jāto gosahasrī mahābalaḥ |

	rūpavān dhanavāṃś caiva bahuputraś ca jāyate ||

dukūlaṃ patrorṇam | kṣaumam atasīvalkalamayaṃ vastram | vāsitācchāditā | devair adhyāsitetyādis tasyāḥ stutiḥ | hastadvayena badhnīyād ity arthaḥ | rajjunā rajjvety arthaḥ | mahābhārate |

	dvijātim abhisaṃpūjya śvaḥkālyam abhivādya ca |

	pradānārthe 'bhiyuñjīta rohiṇīṃ niyatavrataḥ |

	āhvānaṃ ca prayuñjīta samaṅgā bahuleti ca ||

brahmapurāṇe |

	gāṃ dadyād vedapūrṇāya viprāya gṛhamedhine |

	svarṇālaṃkṛtaśṛṅgīṃ tāṃ vastraghaṇṭāvibhūṣitām ||

	kāṃsyopadohanāṃ rājan narakāt sapta pūruṣān |

	sadakṣiṇāṃ dadad gāṃ tāṃ mokṣayan svargam āpnuyāt ||

mahābhārate |

	vṛttiglāne sīdati cātimātraṃ kṛṣyarthaṃ vā homahetoḥ prasūtyām |

	gurvarthaṃ vā vaṃśasaṃvṛddhaye vā dhenuṃ dadyād eva kālo viśiṣṭaḥ ||

aṅgirāḥ |

	gaur ekasmau pradātavyā śrotriyāya viseṣataḥ |

	sā ha tārayate sarvān sapta sapta ca sapta ca ||

nandipurāṇe |

	apātre sā tu gaur dattā dātāraṃ narakaṃ nayet |

	kulaikaviṃśatyā yuktaṃ grahītāraṃ ca pātayet ||

	pātreṣv ādhyātmikā mukhyā viśuddhāś cāgnihotriṇaḥ |

	devatāś ca tathā mukhyā godāne hy etad uttamam ||

mahābhārate |

	na godānāt paraṃ kiṃcid vidyate vasudhādhipa |

	gaur hi nyāyāgatā dattā sā hi tārayate kulam ||

	yāni kāni na durgāṇi duṣkṛtāni kṛtāni ca |

	taranti caiva pāpmānaṃ ye dhenuṃ dadati prabho ||

	tisro rātrīr abhyupoṣyātha bhūmau tṛptā gāvas tarpitebhyaḥ pradeyāḥ |

	vatsaiḥ prītāḥ suvrataiḥ sopacārās tryahaṃ datvā gorasair vartitavyam ||

jābālaḥ |

	homārtham agnotrasya yo gāṃ dadyād ayācitām |

	trir vittapūrṇā pṛthivī dattā tena na saṃśayaḥ || 1.204 ||

_adhunā phalam āha |_

**[297]**	**dātāsyāḥ svargam āpnoti vatsarān romasaṃmitān |**

asyā gor uktaprakārāyā dātasyā eva yāvanti romāṇi tāvato vatsarān svargam āpnoti labhate ||

_guṇāt phalātiśayam āha |_

**	kapilā cet tārayati bhūya āsaptamaṃ kulam || 1.205 ||**

uktaprakārā gauḥ kapilā ced dīyate tadāsau dātuḥ sapta puruṣān narakāt tārayati | bhūyaḥśabdāt dātāraṃ pūrvoktena phalena yojayati | sarṃvartaḥ |

	daśadhenupradānena tulyaikā kapilā matā ||

bṛhaspatiḥ |

	hemaśṛṅgīṃ raupyakhurāṃ vastrakāṃsyājyasaṃyutām |

	savatsāṃ kapilāṃ datvā sapta vaṃśyān samuddharet ||

ādipurāṇe |

	kapilāṃ ye prayacchanti cailacchannāṃ svalaṃkṛtām |

	svarṇaśṛṅgīṃ raupyakhurāṃ mukhālāṅgūlaśobhitām ||

	śvetavastraparicchannāṃ ghaṇṭāsvanaravair yutām |

	sahasraṃ yo gavāṃ dadyāt kapilāṃ vāpi suvrata ||

	samām eva purā prāha brahmā brahmavidāṃ vara |

	yāvanti romakūpāṇi kapilāṅge bhavanti hi ||

	tāvatkoṭisahasrāṇi varṣāṇāṃ divi modate |

	kṛṣṇāṃ gāṃ dadate yas tu paṭacchannāṃ svalaṃkṛtām ||

	vidhivac ca dvijātibhyo yamalokaṃ na paśyati |

	āyur ārogyam aiśvaryaṃ dātā kāmān samāpnuyāt ||

	suvarṇaśṭṅgābharaṇā tathā raupyakhurā śubhā |

	paṭacchannā śubhā caiva dātavyā varayogine(ṇe) ||

	yaś ca dadyāt tu gāṃ śvetāṃ tasya puṇyaphalaṃ śṛṇu |

	janmaprabhṛti yat pāpaṃ mātṛkaṃ paitṛkaṃ ca yat ||

	hastoddhṛtajalasyeva tatkṣaṇād eva naśyati |

	gāṃ dadānīha ity eva vācā pūyeta sarvaśaḥ || **[298]**

mahābhārate |

	samānavatsāṃ kapilāṃ dhenuṃ datvā payasvinīm |

	suvratāṃ vastrasaṃpannāṃ brahmaloke mahīyate ||

samānavatsā sarūpavatsā | suvratā suśīlā |

	rohiṇīṃ tulyavatsāṃ tu dhenuṃ datvā payasvinīm |

	suvratāṃ vastrasaṃchannāṃ brahmaloke mahīyate || \
	samānavatsāṃ śvetāṃ tu dhenuṃ datvā payasvinīm |

	suvratāṃ vastrasaṃvītām indraloke mahīyate ||

	samānavatsāṃ śabalāṃ dhenuṃ datvā payasvinīm |

	suvratāṃ vastrasaṃchannāṃ somaloke mahīyate ||

	vātareṇusavarṇāṃ tu savatsāṃ kāmadohinīm |

	pradāya vastrasaṃpannāṃ vāyuloke mahīyate ||

	gavāṃ pucchaṃ gṛhītvā tu susuvarṇena pāṇinā |

	gṛhastho vedavid vipro vācayet tat pratigraham ||

	bhogamokṣapradā śvetā prasūtā pāpanāśinī |

	kṛṣṇā svargapradā jñeyā gaurī ca kulavardhinī ||

	raktā rūpapradā jñeyā pītā dāridryaghātinī |

	putrapradā kṛṣṇaśārī nīlā dharmapravardhinī ||

	kapilā sarvapāpaghnī nānāvarṇā ca mokṣadā || iti |

iti godānam || 1.205 ||

_ubhayamukhīdānaṃ setikartavyatāphalaviśeṣaṃ prati sādhanatvenāha | _

	**savatsāromatulyāni yugānu ubhayatomukhī |**

**	dātāsyāḥ svargam āpnoti pūrveṇa vidhinā dadat || 1.206 ||**

vatsena saha varteta iti savatsā tasyā romāṇi savatsāromāṇi tais tulyāni tulyasaṃkhyākāni yugāny ubhayatomukhī ardhaprasūtā gaur datur āsaptamaṃ kulaṃ tārayati | pūrvoketikartavyatayā dadat prayacchaṃs tāvanty eva yugāni svargam āpnoti | yugaṃ devamānena catvāri varṣasahasrāṇi || 1.206 ||

**[299]**

	**yāvad vatsasya dvau pādau mukhaṃ yonyāṃ pradṛśyate |**

**	tāvad gauḥ pṛthivī jñeyā yāvad garbhaṃ na muñcati || 1.207 ||**

yāvad vatsasya jāyamānasya dvau pādau mukhaṃ ca yonyāṃ prajanane dṛśyate tāvad asau gauḥ pṛthivī jñeyāgarbhavomodanāt | tataś ca taddānād dātuḥ pṛthivīdānaphalāvāptir bhavati | ubhayaśirasaṃ dadyād ity anuvṛttau cyavanaḥ |


    tasyāḥ pradānakālaḥ prasavakālo nānyaṃ kālaṃ pratīkṣate | vyatīpātaviṣuvāyanaṣaḍaśīti-mukhaviṣṇupradādyā grahaṇāntāḥ sarva eva puṇyakālāḥ | tadaiva yatra snāte brāhmaṇaṃ śreyāṃsaṃ śrutaśīlasatyaśaucavṛttajātiguṇādair guṇair upetaṃ vijñātaṃ mahatā kālena praṇipatya brūyāt | aham atīvārto bhīto 'smād agādhād apārāt saṃsārārṇavāt samuttārayāmi daśāvarān daśāparān ātmānaṃ ca svāmin bhavantaṃ dānapātram āsādya madanugrahabuddhyā nārthalipsayā gṛhyatām iti dātā tam anumantrayet | tvaṃ mahīm avaniṃ viśvadhenām iti [RV 3.6.16] japati | niṣkrānte 'gnim upasamādhāya devān pitṝn nadīḥ parvatān vanaspatīn udadhīn nāgān oṣadhīs tarpayet svaiḥ svair mantraiḥ | teṣāṃ mantrapadāni bhavanti |


    	ye devāso divyekādaśa stha pṛthivyāṃ madhyekādaśa stha |


    	apsukṣito mahi naikādaśa stha te devā yajñam imaṃ juṣadhvam ||


    [RV 2.2.4] iti devānām |


    	uśantas tvā havāmaha uśantaḥ samidhīmahi |


    	uśannuśata āvaha pitṝn haviṣe attave ||


    iti pitṝṇām |


    	imaṃ me gaṅge yamune sarasvati śutudri stomaṃ sacatā paruṣṇyā |


    	asiknyā marudvṛdhe vitastayārjīkīye śṛṇuhyā suṣomayā ||


    [RV 8.3.8] iti nadīnām |


    	adribhiḥ suto matibhiś ca no hitaḥ prarocayan rodasī mātarā śuciḥ |


    	romāny avyā samayā vi dhāvati madhordhārā pinvamānā dive dive || **[300]**


    [RV 7.2.33] iti parvatānām |


    	vanaspate śatavalśo vi roha sahasravalśā vi vayaṃ ruhema |


    	yaṃ tvām ayaṃ svadhitas tejamānaḥ praṇināya mahate saubhagāya ||


    [RV 6.1.4] iti vanaspatīnām |


    	samudrajyeṣṭhāḥ salilasya madhyāt punānā yanty aniviśamānāḥ |


    	indro yā vajro vṛṣabho rarāda tā āpo devīr iha mām avantu ||


    [RV 5.4.16] iti samudrāṇām |


    	ahir iva bhogaiḥ paryeti bāhuṃ jyāyā hetiṃ paribādhamānaḥ |


    	hastaghno viśvā vayunāni vidvān pumān pumāṃsaṃ pari pātu viśvataḥ ||


    [RV 5.1.21] iti nāgānām |


    	madhu vātā ṛtāyate madhu kṣaranti sindhavaḥ |


    	mādhvīr naḥ santv oṣadhīḥ ||


    [RV 1.6.18] ity oṣadhīnām |


    iti devādīnām oṣadhiparyantānāṃ mantrāḥ | tad anu pārthivībhiḥ pṛthvīṃ tarpayet | 


    	īḍe dyāvāpṛthivī pūrvacittaye 'gniṃ gharmaṃ surucaṃ yāmann iṣṭaye |


    	yābhirbhare kāram aṃśāya jinvathastābhirūṣu ūtibhir aśvinā gatam ||


    [RV 1.7.33]


    	mahī dyauḥ pṛthivī ca na imaṃ yajñaṃ mimikṣatām |


    	pipṛtāṃ no bharīmabhiḥ || [RV 1.2.6]


    	ūrvī pṛthvī bahule dūre ante upa bruve namasā yajñe asmin |


    	dadhāte ye subhage supratūtīṃ dhyāvā rakṣataṃ pṛthivī no abhyāt ||


    [RV 2.5.6]


    	gaurīr mimāya salilāni takṣaty ekapadī dvipadī sā catuṣpadī |


    	aṣṭāpadī navapadī babhūvuṣī sahasrākṣarā parame vyoman ||


    [RV 2.3.22] ityādibhiś caturaśītyājyāhutīr juhoti | brāhmaṇān bhojayet |


    	svasti no mimītām aśvinā bhagaḥ svasti devy aditir anarvaṇaḥ|


    	svasti pūṣā asuro dadhātu naḥ svasti dyāvāpṛthivī sucetunā ||


    [RV 4.3.7]. **[301]**


    ityādisvastyayanaṃ vācayīta | athāsya vyuṣṭim udāharanti — abhakṣyabhakṣaṇam apeyapānaṃ brahmaghnaṃ mātṛghnaṃ pitṛghnaṃ sadya eva punāty upādhyāyīṃ svasutāṃ svāmibhāryāṃ mātaraṃ mātṛṣvasāraṃ pitṛṣvasāraṃ mātulānīṃ bhaginīṃ bhāgineyīṃ śiṣyajāyām anyām apy agamyāṃ gatvobhayaśirasaṃ saparikarāṃ brāhmaṇāya dadyāt | parikaraḥ syāt suvarṇarūpyaratnāni kṣetrāṇi dhānyāni vastrāṇi rasā lavaṇādyāś candanādyā gandhās tadardham ardhaṃ vā sarvasvaṃ vā saha tayā brāhmaṇāya dadyān mahāpātakavimuktaye" iti |

matyapurāṇe |

	matsya uvāca |

	rukmaśṛṅgīṃ raupyakhurāṃ muktālāṅgūlaśobhitām |

	kāṃsyopadohanāṃ rājan savatsāṃ dvijapuṃgave ||

	prasūyamānāṃ gāṃ datvā mahat puṇyaphalaṃ labhet |

	yāvat vatso yonigato yāvad garbhaṃ na muñcati ||

	tāvad gauḥ pṛthivī jñeyā saśailavanakānanā |

	caturantā bhaved dattā pṛthivī nātra saṃśayaḥ ||

	yāvanti dhenuromāṇi vatsasya ca narādhipa |

	tāvatsaṃkhyān yugagaṇān devaloke mahīyate ||

	pitṝn pitāmāhāṃś caiva tathaiva prapitāmahān |

	uddhariṣyaty asaṃdehaṃ narakād bhūridakṣiṇaḥ ||

	ghṛtakṣīravahāḥ kalyā dadhipāyasakardamāḥ |

	yatra tatra gatasyāsya bhavantīpsitakāmadāḥ ||

	golokaḥ sulabhas tasya brahmalokaś ca pārthiva ||

	striyaś ca taṃ candrasamānavaktrāḥ prataptajāmbūnadatulyavarṇāḥ |

	mahānitambastanavṛttamadhyāḥ sevanty ajasraṃ nalinābhanetrāḥ ||

varāhapurāṇe |

	suvarṇaśṛṅgī yaḥ kṛtvā raupayuktāṃ khureṣv atho |

	brāhmaṇasya kare datvā suvarṇaṃ raupyam eva vā ||

	kapilāyās tadā pucchaṃ brāhmaṇasya kare nyaset |

	udakaṃ ca kare datvā vācayec chuddhayānvitaḥ ||

**[302]**	sasamudraguhā tena saśailavanakānanā |

	ratnapūrṇā bhaved dattā pṛthivī nātra saṃśayaḥ ||

	pṛthivīdānatulyena dānenānena mānavaḥ |

	tāritair yāti pitṛbhir viṣṇyākhyaṃ yat paraṃ padam ||

	brahasvahārako goghno bhrūṇahā pākabhedakaḥ |

	mahāpātakayukto 'pi vañcako brahmadūṣakaḥ ||

	nindako brāhmaṇānāṃ ca teṣāṃ karmābhidūṣakaḥ |

	evaṃ pātakayukto 'pi gavāṃ dānena śudhyati ||

	yaś cobhayamukhīṃ dadyāt prabhūtakanakāvṛtām |

	tad dinaṃ pāyasāhāraḥ payasā vātivāhayet ||

	suvarṇasya sahasreṇa tadardhenāpi bhāmini |

	tasyāpy ardhaṃ śataṃ vātha pañcāśac ca tato 'rdhakam ||

	yathāśakti pradātavyaṃ vittaśāṭhyavivarjitam |

	imāṃ gṛhāṇobhayamukhīṃ bhavāṃs trātā mamāstu vai ||

	mama vaṃśaviśuddhiḥ syāt sadā svastikaro bhava |

	irāvatī dhenumatīti japtvā devasyonā tadanantaram ||

	pratigṛhṇāmi tāṃ dhenuṃ kuṭumbārthe viśeṣataḥ |

	svastir bhavatu te nityaṃ bhadraṃ cānte namo namaḥ ||

	dyaus te pratidadāmi pṛthivīṃ te prati gṛhṇāmi |

	ka idaṃ kasmā adād iti ca vasuṃdhare |

	visṛjed brāhmaṇaṃ dadhi gāṃ ca tasya gṛhaṃ nayet ||

iti ubhayamukhīdānam |

	**yathākathaṃcid datvā gāṃ dhenuṃ vādhenum eva vā |**

**	arogām aparikliṣṭāṃ dātā svarge mahīyate || 1.208 ||**

yathākathaṃcid yāvat pūrvoktaprakāravatīṃ gāṃ dhenum adhenuṃ vā rogarahitām aparikliṣṭāṃ datvā svarge mahīyate pūjyate | dhenur navaprasūtā | adhenur anavaprasūtā | aparikliṣṭākṛśā | atra mahābhārate |

	na kṛśām apavatsāṃ vā vandhyāṃ rogānvitāṃ tathā |

	na vyaṅgāṃ na pariśrāntāṃ dadyād gāṃ brāhmaṇāya vai ||

tathā |

	pītodakāṃ jagdhatṛṇāṃ dugdhadohāṃ nirindriyām |

	unmattām aṅgahīnāṃ ca mṛtavatsāṃ mahāśanām ||

	keśacailapurīṣāsthikravyādāṃ syandinīṃ khalām |

	punarnavāṃ yamalasūṃ nityaṃ pragalitastanīm ||

	na dadyād brāhmaṇebhyaś ca sadoṣaṃ vṛṣaṃ tathā ||

pītodakatvajagdhatṛṇatvādinā vṛddhatvam upalakṣyate | khalā duḥśīlā | ekasyāpi godānādikarmaṇaḥ kvacic chāstre bahuphalaṃ kathyate kvacic cālpaṃ taddātur deyasya pātrasya deśakālayoś ca guṇabhūyastvālpatvābhyāṃ vyavasthāpanīyam | tad āha manuḥ |

	pātrasya ca viśeṣeṇa śraddadhānatayāpi ca |

	alpaṃ vā bahu vā pretya dānasyāvāpyate phalam || iti |

dhenudānavidhiprasaṅgena guḍadhenyādividhaya udāhriyante | tatra matsyapurāṇam |

	guḍadhenuvidhānasya yad rūpam iha yat phalam |

	tad idānīṃ pravakṣyāmi sarvapāpapraṇāśanam ||

	kṛṣṇājinaṃ caturhastaṃ prāggrīvaṃ vinyased bhuvi |

	gomayenopaliptāyāṃ darbhān āstīrya yatnataḥ ||

hasto 'ratniḥ |

	laghveṇakājinaṃ tadvad vatsasya parikalpayet |

	prāṅmukhīṃ kalpayed dhenum udakpādāṃ savatsakām ||

prāṅmukhī prākśirāḥ | vatso 'pi tathaiva |

	uttamā guḍadhenuḥ syāt sadā bhāracatuṣṭayam |

	vatsaṃ bhāreṇa kurvīta bhārābhyāṃ madhyamā smṛtā ||

	ardhabhāreṇa vatsaḥ syāt kathitā bhārakeṇa tu |

	caturthāṃśena vatsaḥ syād gṛhavittānusārataḥ ||

phalaśataṃ tulā tulānāṃ viṃśatir bhāraḥ | tad uktam |

	tulā striyāṃ palaśataṃ bhāraḥ syād viṃśatis tulāḥ |

	dhenuvatsau ghṛtāsyau tau sitasūtrāmbarāvṛtau ||

**[304]**	śuktikarṇāv ikṣūpādau śuktimuktāphalekṣaṇau |

	sitasūtraśirālau tau sitakambalakambalau ||

	tāmraguḍakapṛṣṭhau tau sitacāmararomakau |

	vidrumabhrūyugopetau navanītastanānvitau ||

	kṣaumapucchau kāṃsyadohāv indranīlakatārakau |

tārake cakṣurmadhyabhāgau |

	suvarṇaśṛṅgābharaṇau khurau raupyamayair yutau ||

	nānāphalayutau dantau ghrāṇagandhakaraṇḍakau |

	ity evaṃ racayitvā tau dhūpadīpais tathārcayet ||

	yā lakṣmīḥ sarvabhūtānāṃ yā ca deveṣv avasthitā |

	dhenurūpeṇa sā devī mama pāpaṃ vyapohatu ||

	viṣṇor vakṣasi yā lakṣmīḥ svāhā yā ca vibhāvasau |

	candrārkaśakraśaktir yā dhenurūpāstu sā śriye ||

	caturmukhasya yā lakṣmīr yā lakṣmīr dhanadasya ca |

	lakṣmīr yā lokapālānāṃ sā dhenur varadāstu me ||

	svadhā yā pitṛmukhyānāṃ(ṇāṃ) svāhā yajñabhujāṃ ca yā |

	sarvapāpaharā dhenus tasmāc chāntiṃ (?) prayaccha me ||

	evam āmantrya tāṃ dhenuṃ brāhmaṇāya nivedayet |

	vidhānam etad dhenūnāṃ sarvāsām iha paṭhyate ||
