	yās tu pāpavināśinyaḥ paṭhyante daśa dhenavaḥ |

	tāsāṃ svarūpaṃ vakṣyāmi nāmāni ca narādhipa ||

	prathamā guḍadhenuḥ syāt tiladhenus tathā parā |

	ghṛtadhenus tṛtīyā ca caturthī jaladhenukā ||

	kṣīradhenuś ca vikhyātā madhudhenus tathā parā |

	saptamī śarkarādhenur dadhidhenus tathāṣṭamī ||

	rasadhenuś ca navamī daśamī syāt svarūpataḥ |

	kumbhāḥ syur dravadhenūnām itarāsāṃ tu rāśayaḥ ||

kumbho dvādaśapalādhikāni phalaśatāni pañca | tad uktam |

**[305]**	paladvayaṃ tu prasṛtaṃ dviguṇaṃ kuḍavaṃ matam |

	caturbhiḥ kuṣavaiḥ prasthaḥ prasthāś catvāra āḍhakaḥ ||

	āḍhakais taiś caturbhis tu droṇas tu kathito budhaiḥ |

	kumbho droṇadvayaṃ śūrpaḥ khārī droṇās tu ṣoḍaśa ||

	suvarṇadhenum apy atra kecid icchanti mānavāḥ |

	navanītena ratnaiś ca tathānye 'pi maharṣayaḥ ||

	etad eva vidhānaṃ syād ete copaskarāḥ smṛtāḥ |

	mantrāvāhanasaṃyuktāḥ sarvāḥ parvaṇi parvaṇi ||

	yathāśraddhaṃ pradātavyā bhuktimuktiphalapradāḥ |

	guḍadhenuprasaṅgena sarvās tava mayoditāḥ ||

	aśeṣayajñaphaladāḥ sarvāḥ papaharāḥ śubhāḥ |

	ayane viṣuve puṇye vyatīpāte ca vā punaḥ ||

	guḍadhenvādayo deyā uparāgādiparvasu ||

iti guṇadhenuḥ |

atha tiladhenuḥ | viṣṇudharmottare vasiṣṭhaḥ |

	tiladhenuṃ pravakṣyāmi keśavaprīṇanāya yā |

	dattā bhavati yaś cāsyā narendra vidhir uttamaḥ ||

	yāṃ datvā brahmahā goghnaḥ pitṛghno gurutalpagaḥ |

	agāradāhī garadaḥ sarvapāparato 'pi vā ||

	mahāpātakayukto vā yukto yaś copapātakaiḥ |

	pramucyate 'khilaiḥ pāpair viṣṇulokaṃ ca gacchati ||

	upalipte mahīpṛṣṭhe vastrājinasamāvṛte |

	dhenuṃ tilamayīṃ kṛtvā sarvaratnair alaṃkṛtām ||

	svarṇaśṛṅgīṃ raupyakhurāṃ gandhaghrāṇavatīṃ śubhām |

	miṣṭānnajihvāṃ kurvīta guṇāsyāṃ sūtrakambalām ||

	ikṣupādāṃ tāmrapṛṣṭhāṃ kuryān muktāphalekṣaṇām |

	praśastapatraśravaṇāṃ phaladantavatīṃ śubhām ||

	sragdāmapucchāṃ kurvīta navanītastanānvitām |

	phalair manoharair bhakṣyair maṇimuktāphalānvitām ||

**[306]**	tiladroṇena kurvīta āḍhakena tu vatsakam |

	śubhavastrayugacchannāṃ cārucchatrasamanvitām ||

	īdṛksaṃsthānasaṃpannāṃ kṛtvā śraddhāsamanvitaḥ |

	kāṃsyopadohanāṃ dadyāt keśavaḥ prīyatām iti ||

	samyag uccārya vidhinā datvaitena narādhipa |

	sarvapāpavinirmuktaḥ pitaraṃ sapitāmaham ||

	prapitāmahaṃ tathā pūrvapuruṣāṇāṃ catuṣṭayam |

	ātmānaṃ tanayaṃ pautraṃ prapautraṃ tadadhas trayam ||

	tārayaty avanīpāla tiladhenuprado naraḥ |

	yaś ca gṛhṇāti vidhivat tasyāpy evaṃvidhaṃ phalam ||

	caturdaśa tathā ye ca dadataś cānumodataḥ |

	dīyamānāṃ prapaśyanti tiladhenuṃ ca ye narāḥ ||

	te 'py aśeṣāghanirmuktāḥ prayānti paramāṃ gatim |

	praśāntāya suśīlāya tathāmatsariṇe budhaḥ ||

	tiladhenuṃ naro dadyād vedapūrṇāya dharmiṇe |

	trirātraṃ yas tilāhāras tiladhenuṃ prayacchati ||

	datvaikarātraṃ sa naras tilān atti narādhipa |

	dānād viśuddhapāpasya tasya puṇyavato nṛpa ||

	cāndrāyaṇād apy adhikaṃ śastaṃ tat tilabhakṣaṇam || iti |

tiladhenoḥ padmapurāṇoktaḥ parimāṇaviśeṣaḥ |

	ṣoḍaśāḍhakamayī dhenuś caturbhir vatsako bhavet ||

bhaviṣyottare |

	vinītāśva uvāca |

	vidhānaṃ caiva dhenūnāṃ tac chṛṇuṣva narādhipa |

	tāsāṃ vidhānaṃ vakṣyāmi viśeṣaś cāpi yādṛśaḥ ||

	anulipte mahīpṛṣṭhe kṣṇājinakuśottare |

	vastraprastaraṇaṃ kṛtvā dhenuṃ tatropakalpayet ||

	udaṅmukhīṃ savatsāṃā tu sthāpayitvā vicakṣaṇaḥ |

	prasthaiḥ ṣoḍaśabhir dhenuś caturbhir vatsako bhavet ||

	ikṣudaṇḍamayāḥ pādā dantāḥ phalamayāḥ smṛtāḥ |

	jihvā piṣṭamayī tasyā ghrāṇaṃ gandhamayaṃ smṛtam ||

**[307]**	guḍena vadanaṃ kṛtvā netre caiva tu mauktike |

	praśastapatraśravaṇā pṛṣṭhaṃ tāmramayaṃ smṛtam ||

	pucchaṃ śaṇamayaṃ tasyāḥ kṣudramauktikaromikām |

	śvetaiś ca kambalai rājan kambalaṃ caiva kalpayet ||

	phalānāṃ vividhākārāṃ kaṇṭhikāṃ caiva kalpayet |

	stanāś ca navanītena sarvālaṃkārabhūṣitām ||

	svarṇaśṛṅgīṃ raupyakṣurāṃ pañcaratnasamanvitām |

	darbhair ācchādayitvā ca vastraiś ca tadanantaram ||

	ācchādayitvā rājendra candanena kcircitām (?) |

	puṇyaiś ca pūjayitvā tu dhūpagandhaiś ca pūjitām ||

	tādṛśīṃ kalpayitvā tu pātrabhūte dvijottame |

	suvratāya suśīlāya viśeṣeṇāhitāgnaye ||

	vedavedāṅgaviduṣe sādhuvṛttāya dhīmate |

	īdṛśāya pradātavyā tiladhenur narādhipa ||

	mantreṇānena rājendra pūjyā stutyā ca sarvataḥ |

	oṃ yā lakṣmīḥ sarvabhūtānāṃ yā ca deveṣv avasthitā ||

	dhenurūpeṇa sā devī mama pāpaṃ vyapohatu |

	dehasthā yā ca rudrāṇī śaṃkarasya sadā priyā ||

	tena rūpeṇa sā devī mama śāntiṃ prayacchatu |

	viṣṇor vakṣasi yā lakṣmīḥ svāhā yā ca vibhāvasoḥ ||

	candrārakśakraśaktir yā dhenurūpāstu sā śriye |

	caturmukhasya yā lakṣmīr yā lakṣmīr dhanadasya ca ||

	lakṣmīr yā lokapālānāṃ sā dhenur varadāstu me |

	svadhā yā pitṛmukhyānāṃ(ṇāṃ) svāhā yajñabhujām api ||

	sarvapāpaharā dhenus tasmāc chantiṃ prayaccha me |

	annaṃ me jāyatāṃ sadyaḥ pānaṃ sarvarasās tathā ||

	kāmān saṃpādayāsmākaṃ tiladheno dvijārpite |

iti dānamantraḥ|

	evaṃ cāmantrya tāṃ dhenuṃ brāhmaṇāya nivedayet |

	evam uccārayitvā tu dadyāt tasya ca dakṣiṇām ||

**[308]**	suvarṇaṃ vācayitvāgre yathāśakti pradāpayet |

	na vittaśāṭhyaṃ kurvīta ātmano vibhave sati ||

atha pratigrahītṛmantraḥ |

	pratigṛhṇāmi devi tvāṃ kuṭumbārthe viśeṣataḥ |

	bharasva kāmair māṃ sarvais tiladheno namo 'stu te ||

iti tiladhenuḥ |

atha ghṛtadhenudānam | viṣṇudharmeṣu vasiṣṭhaḥ |

	tilālābhe tathā dadyād ghṛtadhenuṃ yatavrataḥ |

	yena bhūpa vidhānena tad ihaikamanāḥ śṛṣu ||

	vāsudevaṃ jagannāthaṃ ghṛtakṣīrābhiṣecanāt |

	saṃpūjya pūrvavat puṣpair gandhadhūpādibhir naraḥ ||

	ahorātroṣito nāmnā abhiṣicya ghṛtārciṣam |

	gavyasya sarpiṣaḥ kumbhaṃ puṣpamālyadiśobhitam ||

	kāṃsyāpdhānasaṃyuktaṃ sitavastrayugena(ṇa) ca |

	hiraṇyagarbhasahitaṃ maṇividrumamauktikaiḥ ||

garbho madhyam, madhyavartinā hiraṇyena sahitaṃ maṇyādibhiś ca sahitaṃ kumbham ity arthaḥ |

	ikṣuyugmamayān pādān khurān rūpyamayāṃs tathā |

	sauvarṇe cakṣiṇī kuryāc chṛṅge cāgurukāṣṭhaje ||

	saptadānyamaye pārśve patroṇaṃ navakambalam |

	kuryād agurukarpūrair ghrāṇaṃ phalamayān stanān ||

	tadvac charkarayā jihvāṃ guḍakṣīramayaṃ mukham |

	kṣaumasūtreṇa lāṅgulaṃ romāṇi sitasarṣapaiḥ ||

	tāmrapātramayaṃ pṛṣṭhaṃ kuryāc chraddhāsamanvitaḥ |

	īdṛksvarūpāṃ saṃkalpya ghṛtadhenuṃ narādhipa ||

**[309]**	tadvat kalpanayā dhenor ghṛtavatsaṃ prakalpayet ||

dhenvāś caturthabhāgena vatsaḥ kāryaḥ, anyatra tathādṛṣṭatvāt |

	tāṃ ca vipraṃ mahābhāgaṃ manasaiva ghṛtārciṣam |

	kalpayitvā tatas tasmai prayataḥ pratipādayet ||

	etāṃ mamopakārāya gṛhṇīṣva tvaṃ dvijottama |

	prīyatāṃ mama deveśo ghṛtārciḥ puruṣottamaḥ ||

	ity udāhṛtya viprāya dadyād dhenuṃ narādhipa |

	ghṛtaratnasuvarṇānāṃ samyakkalpanayā kṛtām ||

	datvaikarātraṃ sthitvā tu ghṛtāhāro narādhipa |

	mucyate sarvapāpebhyas tathā dānaphalaṃ śṛṇu ||

	ghṛtakṣīravahā nadyo yatra pāyasakardamāḥ |

	teṣu lokeṣu sarveṣu supuṇyeṣūpajāyate ||

	pitur ūrdhvaṃ nayet sapta puruṣāṃs tasya ye 'py adhaḥ |

	tāṃs teṣu nṛpa lokeṣu sa nayatyastakalmaṣaḥ ||

	sakāmānām iyaṃ vyuṣṭiḥ kathitā nṛpasattama |

	viṣṇulokaṃ narā yānti niṣkāmā ghṛtadhenudāḥ ||

iti ghṛtadhenuḥ |

atha jaladhenuḥ | viṣṇudharmeṣu vasiṣṭhaḥ |

	jaladhenuṃ pravakṣyāmi prīyate dattayā yayā |

	devadevo hṛṣīkeśaḥ sarvadaḥ sarvabhāvanaḥ ||

	jalakumbhaṃ naravyāghra suvarṇarajatānvitam |

	ratnagarbham aśeṣais tu grāmyair dhānyaiḥ samanvitam ||

	sitavastrayugacchanaṃ dūrvāpallavaśobhitam |

	kuṣṭhamāṃsīpurośīravālakāmakair yutam ||

	priyaṅgupātrasahitaṃ sitayajñopavītinam |

	sopānatkaṃ ca sacchatraṃ darbhaviṣṭarasaṃsthitam ||

	caturbhiḥ saṃbhṛtaṃ bhūpa tilapātraiś caturdiśam |

**[310]**	sthagitaṃ dadhipātreṇa ghṛtakṣaudravatā mukhe ||

	upoṣitaḥ samabhyarcya vāsudevaṃ jaleśvaram |

	puṣpadhūpopahārais tu yathāvibhavam ādṛtaḥ ||

	saṃkalpya jaladhenuṃ ca kumbhaṃ tam abhipūjya ca |

	pūjayed vatsakaṃ tadvat kṛtaṃ jalamayaṃ tataḥ ||

	evaṃ saṃpūjya govindaṃ jaladhenuṃ savatsakam |

	sitavastradharaḥ śānto vītarāgo vimatsaraḥ||

	dadyād dvijāya rājendra prītyarthaṃ jalaśāyinaḥ |

	jalaśāyī jagadyoniḥ prīyatāṃ mama keśavaḥ ||

	yo coccārya bhūnātha viprāya pratipādayet |

	apakvānnāśinā stheyam ahorātram ataḥ param ||

	anena vidhinā datvā jaladhenuṃ narādhipa |

	sarvāhlādān avāpnoti ye divyā ye ca mānuṣāḥ ||

	śarīrārogyam ābādhapraśamaḥ sārvakālikaḥ |

	nṛṇāṃ bhavati dattāyāṃ jaladhenvāṃ na saṃśayaḥ ||

iti jaladhenuvidhānam |

atha lavaṇadhenuvidhānam

	yudhiṣṭhira uvāca |

	kṛṣṇa kṛṣṇa mahābāho sarvaśāstraviśārada |

	kathayasveha dānānām uttamaṃ yat prakīrtitam ||

	yena dattena dānāni sarvāṇy eva bhavanty uta |

	sarvakāmaprasiddhiś ca sarvapāpakṣayo bhavet ||

	prāyaścittaṃ viśuddhiś ca tan me kathaya suvrata ||

	śrīkṛṣṇa ucāva |

	śṛṇu rājan pravakṣyāmi dānānām uttamottamam |

	khyātaṃ lavaṇadhenvākhyaṃ sarvakāmapradaṃ nṛṇām ||

	yad datvā brahmahā goghnaḥ pitṛghno gurutalpagaḥ |

	viśvāsaghātī krūrātmā sarvapāparato 'pi vā ||

	mucyate nātra saṃdehaḥ śivalokaṃ ca gacchati |

	śubhagodhanasaṃpanno dīrghāyur aparājitaḥ ||

**[311]**	jāyate puruṣo loke sarvakāmasamanvitaḥ |

	vidhiṃ vakṣyāmi rājendra lavaṇasyeha kalpanām ||

	gomayenopalipyet tu darbhasaṃstarasaṃsthitam |

	āvikaṃ carma vinyasya pūrvāśābhimukhasthitam ||

	vastreṇācchāditaṃ kṛtvā dhenuṃ kurvīta buddhimān |

	āḍhakenaiva kurvīta bahuvitto 'lpavittavān ||

	svarṇaśṛṅgīṃ raupyakhurām ikṣupādāṃ phalastanīm |

	kāryā śarkarayā jihvā gandhaghrāṇavatīṃ tathā ||

	samudrodaraje śuktī karṇau tasyāḥ prakalpayet |

	śṛṅge candanakāṣṭhābhyāṃ yavān āsye pradāpayet ||

	tilān pārṣṇiṣu kurvīta godhūmāṃś caiva śaktitaḥ |

	evaṃ vai sapta dhānyāni yathālābhaṃ prakalpayet ||

	kambalaṃ paṭṭasūtreṇa grīvāyāṃ chatrikāṃ tathā |

	pṛṣṭe vai tāmrapātraṃ tu apāne guḍapiṇḍikām ||

	lāṅgūle karpaṭaṃ dadyād daśāḥ kṣīrapradeśataḥ |

	yonipradeśe tu madhu sarvatas tu phalānvitām ||

	evaṃ samyak paristhāpya rasasasyamayīṃ daśām |

	sthāpayed vatsakaṃ cāpi caturbhāgena(ṇa) mānavaḥ ||

	evaṃ dhenuṃ samabhyarcya mālyavastravibhūṣaṇaiḥ |

	snātvā devārcanaṃ kṛtvā brāhmaṇān abhipūjya ca ||

	datvā sadakṣiṇāṃ gāṃ tu putrabhāryāsamanvitaḥ |

	brāhmaṇāya suśīlāya vṛttayuktāya vai nṛpa ||

	saubhāgyaṃ paramā buddhir ārogyaṃ sarvasaṃpadaḥ |

	nṛṇāṃ bhavati datvā tu rasadhenuṃ na saṃśayaḥ ||

	svarge ca niyato vāso yāvad ābhūtasaṃplavam ||

	patrorṇakambalagalāṃ lavanāḍhakena kṛtvā phalastanavatīm avicarma pṛṣṭhe |

	datvā dvijāya vidhivad rasadhenum enām loke gavāṃ sakalasaukhyayuto vaset tu ||

iti bhaviṣyottare lavaṇadhenuvidhiḥ |

**[312]**

atha śarkarādhenor vidhānam |

	vinītāśva uvāca |

	tadvac ca śarkarādhenuṃ śṛṇu rājan yathārthataḥ |

	anulipte mahīpṛṣṭhe kṛṣṇājinakuśottare ||

	dhenuḥ śarkarayā rājan sadā bhāracatuṣṭayam |

	uttamā kathyate sadbhiś caturthāṃśena vatsakam ||

	tadardhaṃ madhyamā proktā caturthāṃśena kanyasā(sī) |

	tadvad vatsaṃ prakurvīta caturthāṃśena mānavaḥ ||

	atha kuryād aṣṭaśataiś caturthāṃśena vatsakam |

	svaśaktyā kārayed dhenuṃ yathātmānaṃna pīḍayet ||

	sarvabījāni saṃsthāpya caturdikṣu samantataḥ |

	sauvarṇamukhaśṛṅgāṇi mauktikānayanāni ca ||

	guḍena ca mukhaṃ kāryaṃ jihvā piṣṭamayī tathā |

	kambalaṃ paṭṭasūtreṇa ghaṇṭābharaṇasaṃyutā ||

	ikṣupādā raupyakhurā navanītamayastanī |

	praśastapatraśravaṇā sitacāmarabhūṣitā ||

	pañcaratnasamāyuktā darbharomasamanvitā |

	kāṃsyopadohanā samyag gandhapuṣpaiḥ samanvitā ||

	īdṛgvidhānasaṃyuktā vastrair ācchāditopari |

	gandhapuṣpair alaṃkṛtya brāhmaṇāya nivedayet ||

	śrotriyāya daridrāya sādhuvṛttāya dhīmate |

	vedavedāṅgaviduṣe viśeṣeṇāgnihotriṇe ||

	anasūyave pradātavyā na matsarayutāya vai |

	ayane viṣuve caiva vyatīpāte tu ṣaṇmukhe ||

	eṣu kāleṣu puṇyeṣu yadṛcchāyāpi dāpayet ||

ṣaṇmukhaṃ ṣaḍaśītimukham | yadṛcchāyā yadṛcchayā yādṛgicchayety arthaḥ | ārṣo dīrghaḥ \

**[313]**	satpātraṃ tu dvijaṃ dṛṣṭvā svāgataṃ śrotriyaṃ gṛhe |

	tādṛśāya pradātavyā pucchadeśe nivedayet ||

	pūrvāmukhaḥ sthito dātā atha vāpi hy udaṅmukhaḥ |

	dhenuṃ pūrvāmukhīṃ kṛtvā vatsaṃ tūttarato nyaset ||

	dānakāle tu ye mantrās tān paṭhitvā samarpayet |

	ācchādya daivataṃ vipraṃ mudrikākarṇaveṣṭakaiḥ ||

	svaśaktyā dakṣiṇāṃ dadyād vittaśāṭhyavivarjitaḥ |

	haste ca dakṣiṇāṃ dadyād gandhapuṣpaṃ sacandanam ||

	dhenuṃ samarpayet tasya mukhaṃ ca na vilokayet |

	ekāhaṃ śarkarāhāro brāhmaṇās tridinaṃ vaset ||

	sarvapāpaharā dhenuḥ sarvakāmapradāyinī |

	sarvakāmaprasiddhas tu jāyate nātra saṃśayaḥ ||

	dīyamānāṃ prapaśyanti te 'pi yānti parāṃ gatim |

	ya idaṃ śṛṇuyād bhaktyā paṭhate vāpi mānavaḥ ||

	mucyate sarvapapebhyo viṣṇulokaṃ ca gacchati ||

iti bhaviṣottare dānadharmeṣu śarkarādhenuvidhiḥ \

atha mahādānāni |

matsyapurāṇe |

	ṛṣaya ūcuḥ |

	nyāyenārjanam. arthānāṃ vardhanaṃ cābhirakṣaṇam |

	satpātrapratipattiś ca sarvaśāstreṣu paṭhyate ||

	kṛtakṛtyo bhavet kena manasvī dhanavān budhaḥ |

	mahādānena dattena tāta vistaraśo vada ||

	sūta uvāca |

	dānadharmeṣu yac coktaṃ viṣṇunā prabhaviṣṇunā |

	tad ahaṃ sampravakṣyāmi mahādānam anuttamam ||

	sarvapāpakṣayakaraṃ nṛṇāṃ duḥsvapnanāśanam |

	yat tu ṣoḍaśadhā proktaṃ vāsudevena bhūtale ||

	puṇyaṃ pavitram āyuṣyaṃ sarvapāpaharaṃ śubham |

	pūjitaṃ devatābhiś ca brahmaviṣnuharādibhiḥ ||

**[314]**	ādyaṃ tu sarvadānānāṃ tulāpuruṣasaṃjñakam |

	hiraṇyagarbhadānaṃ ca brahmāṇḍaṃ tadanantaram ||

	kalpapādapadānaṃ ca gosahasraṃ ca pañcamam |

	hiraṇyakāmadhenuś ca hiraṇyāśvas tathaiva ca ||

	hiraṇyāśvarathas tadvad dhemahastirathas tathā |

	pañcalāṅgalikaṃ tadvad dharādānaṃ tathaiva ca ||

	dvādaśaṃ viṣṇucakraṃ ca tataḥ kalpalatātmakam |

	saptasāgaradānaṃ ca ratnadhenus tathaiva ca ||

	mahābhūtaghaṭas tadvat ṣoḍaśaṃ parikīrtitam |

	sarvāṇy etāni kṛtavān purā śambarasūdanaḥ ||

	vāsudevo 'tha bhagavān ambarīṣo 'tha bhārgavaḥ |

	kārtavīryārjuno rāmaḥ prahrādaḥ pṛthur eva ca ||

	kuryur anye mahīpālāḥ kānicid bharatādayaḥ |

	yasmād vighnasahasrāṇi mahādānāni bhūtale ||

	eṣām anyatamaṃ kāryaṃ vāsudevaprasādataḥ |

	na śakyam anyathā kartum api śakreṇa bhūtale ||

	tasmād ārādhya govindam umāpativināyakau |

	mahādāne mukhaṃ kuryād vipraiś caivānumoditaḥ ||

	etad evāha manave parituṣṭo janārdanaḥ |

	yathā tad atra vakṣyāmi śṛṇudhvam ṛṣisattamāḥ ||

	manur uvāca |

	mahādānāni yānīha pavitrāṇi śubhāni ca |

	rahasyāni pradeyāni tāni me kathayācyuta ||

	matsya uvāca |

	noktāni yāni divyāni mahādānāni ṣoḍaśa |

	tāni te saṃpravakṣyāmi yathāvad anupūrvaśaḥ ||

	tulāpuruṣayogo 'yaṃ yeṣām ādau vidhīyate |

	ayane viṣuve puṇye vyatīpāte dinakṣaye ||

	yugādiṣūparāgeṣu tathā manvantarādiṣu |

	saṃkrāntau vaidhṛtidine caturdaśyaṣṭamīṣu ca ||

	sitapañcadaśīparvadvādaśīṣv aṣṭakāsu ca |

	yajñotsavavivāheṣu duḥsvapnādbhutadarśane ||

**[315]**	dravyabrāhmaṇalābhe vā śraddhā vā yatra jāyate |

	tīrthe vāyatane goṣṭhe kūpārāmasaritsu ca ||

	gṛhe vātha vane vāpi taḍāke nijhare tathā |

	mahādānāni deyāni saṃsārabhayabhīruṇā ||

	anityaṃ jīvitaṃ yasmād vasu cātīva cañcalam |

	keśeṣv iva gṛhītas tan mṛtyunā dharmam ācaret ||

	puṇyāṃ tithiṃ samāsādya kṛtvā brāhmaṇavācanam |

	ṣoḍaśāratnimātraṃ tu daśa dvādaśa vā karān ||

	maṇḍalaṃ kārayed vidvāṃś caturbhadrānanaṃ budhaḥ |

	saptahastā bhaved vedī madhye pañcakarātha vā ||

	tanmadhye toraṇaṃ kuryāt sāradārumayaṃ budhaḥ ||

toraṇam idaṃ tulādhāraṇārtham |

	kuryād daṇḍāni catvāri caturdikṣu vicakṣaṇaḥ |

	sumekhalāyoniyutāni dvāri saṃpūrṇakuṇḍāni saviṣṭarāṇi |

	hastapramāṇāni tilājyadhūpapuṣpopahārāṇi suśobhanāni ||

	pūrvottare hastamitātha vedī grahādideveśvarapūjanāya |

	tatrārcanaṃ brahmaśivācyutānāṃ sūryasya kāryaṃ phalamālyavastraiḥ ||

	lokeśavarṇāḥ paritaḥ patākā madhye dhvajaḥ kiṃkiṇikāyutaḥ syāt |

	dvāreṣu kāryāṇi ca toraṇāni catvary api kṣīravanaspatīnām ||

	dvāreṣu kumbhadvayam atra kāryaṃ sugandhadhūpāmbararatnayuktam |

	śākeṅgudīcandanadevadāruśrīparṇabilvaiḥ priyakāñcanottham ||

	stambhadvayaṃ hastayugāvakhātaṃ kṛtvā dṛḍhaṃ pañcakarocchritaṃ ca |

	tadantaraṃ hastacatuṣṭayaṃ syād athottarāṅgaṃ ca tadaṅgam eva ||

tadaṅgaṃ stambhavṛkṣajātimat |

	samānajātiś ca tulāvalambyā haimena madhye putuṣeṇa yuktā |

	dairghyeṇa sā hastacatuṣṭayaṃ tu pṛthutvam asyās tu daśāṅgulāni ||

	tulā suvarṇābaraṇā tu kāryā salohapāśadvayaśṛṅkhalābhiḥ |

**[316]**	yutā suvarṇena ca ratnamālā vibhūṣitā mālyavilepanāḍyā ||

	cakraṃ likhed vārijagarbhayuktaṃ nānārajobhir bhuvi puṣpakīrṇam |

	vitānakaṃ copari pañcavarṇaṃ saṃsthāpayet puṣpaphalopaśobham ||

	atha dvijā vedavidaś ca kāryāḥ surūpaveśānvayaśīlayuktāḥ |

	vidhānadakṣāḥ paṭavo 'nukūlā ye cāryadeśaprabhavā dvijendrāḥ ||

	guruś ca vedārthavidāryadeśasamudbhavaḥ śīlakulābhirūpaḥ |

	kāryaḥ purāṇābhirato 'tidakṣaḥ prasannagambhīrasarasvatīkaḥ ||

	sitāmbaraḥ kuṇḍalahemasūtrakeyūrakaṇṭhābharaṇābhirāmaḥ |

	pūrveṇa ṛgvedayutau ca śastau yajurvidau dakṣiṇataś ca kāryau ||

	sthāpyau dvijau sāmavidau ca paścād ātharvaṇāv uttarataś ca kāryau |

	vināyakādigrahalokapālavasvaṣṭakādityamarudgaṇānām ||

	brahmācyuteśārkavanaspatibhyaḥ svamantrato homacatuṣṭayaṃ syāt |

	japyāni sūktāni tathaiva caiṣām anukrameṇaiva yathāsvarūpam ||

	homāvasāne kṛtatūryanādo gurur gṛhītvā balipuṣpadhūpam |

	āvāhayel lokapatīn krameṇa mantrair amībhir yajamānayuktaḥ ||

	oṃ ehy ehi sarvāmarasiddhasādhyair abhiṣṭuto vajradharaḥ sureśaḥ |

	saṃvījyamāno 'psarasāṃ gaṇena rakṣādhvaraṃ no bhavan namas te ||

	oṃ indrāya namaḥ |

	oṃ ehy ehi sarvāmara havyavāha munipravīrair abhito 'bhujuṣṭaḥ |

	tejovatīlokagaṇena sārdhaṃ mamādhvaraṃ rakṣa kave namas te ||

	oṃ agnaye namaḥ |

	oṃ ehy ehi vaivasvata dharmarāja sarvāmarair arcitadivyamūrte |

	śubhāśubhānandasuvāmadhīśa śivāya naḥ pāhi sakhaṃ namas te ||

	oṃ yamāya namaḥ |

	oṃ ehy ehi rakṣogaṇanāyakas tvaṃ viśālavetālapiśācasaṃghaiḥ |

	mamādhvaraṃ pāhi śubhādhinātha lokeśvaras tvaṃ bhagavan namas te ||

**[317]**	oṃ nirṛtaye namaḥ |

	oṃ ehy ehi pāthogaṇavāridhīnāṃ gaṇena parjanya mahāpsarobhiḥ |	

	vidyādharendrāmaragīyamānaḥ pāhi tvam asmān bhagavan namas te ||

	oṃ varuṇāya namaḥ |

	oṃ ehy ehi yajñaṃ mama rakṣaṇāya mṛgādhirūḍhaḥ saha siddhasaṃghaiḥ |

	prāṇādhipaḥ kālakaveḥ sahāyo gṛhāṇa pūjāṃ bhagavan namas te ||

	oṃ vāyave namaḥ |

	oṃ ehy ehi yajñeśvara yajñarakṣāṃ vidhatsva nakṣatragaṇena sārdham |

	sarvauṣadhībhiḥ pitṛbhiḥ sahaiva gṛhāṇa pūjāṃ bhagavan namas te ||

	oṃ somāya namaḥ |

	oṃ ehy ehi viśveśvara nas triśūlin kapālakhatvāṅgavareṇa sārdham |

	lokeśa bhūteśvara yajñasiddhyai gṛhāṇa pūjāṃ bhagavan namas te ||

	oṃ īśānāya namaḥ |

	oṃ ehy ehi pātāladhārāmarendra nāgāṅganākiṃnaragīyamānaḥ |

	rakṣogaṇenāmaralokasārdham ananta rakṣodhvaram asmadīyam ||

	oṃ anantāya namaḥ |

	oṃ ehy ehi viśvādhipate munīndra lokena sārdhaṃ pitṛdevatābhiḥ |

	viśādhvaraṃ naḥ satataṃ śivāya pitāmahas tvaṃ bhagavan namas te ||

	oṃ brahmaṇe namaḥ |

	trailokye yāni bhūtāni sthāvarāṇi carāṇi ca |

	brahmaviṣṇusuraiḥ sārdhaṃ rakṣāṃ kurvantu tāni me ||

	devadānavagandharvā yakṣarākṣasapannagāḥ |

	ṛṣayo manavo gāvo devā mātara eva ca ||

	sarve mamādhvare rakṣāṃ prakurvantu mudānvitāḥ |

	ity āvāhya surān dadyād ṛtvigbhyo hemabhūṣaṇam ||

	kuṇḍalāni ca haimāni sūtrāṇi kaṭakāni ca |

	tathāṅgulīpavitrāṇi vāsāṃsi śayanāni ca ||

	dviguṇaṃ gurave dadyād bhūṣaṇācchādanādikam |

	japeyuḥ śāntikādhyāyaṃ jāpakāḥ sarvatodiśam || **[318]**

śāntikādhyāyam "śaṃ na indrāgnī" iti sūktam |

	upoṣitāś ca te sarve kṛtvaivam adhivāsanam |

	ādāv ante ca madhye ca kuryād brāhmaṇavācanam ||

	tato maṅgalaśabdena snāpito vedapuṃgavaiḥ |

	triḥ pradakṣiṇam āvṛtya gṛhītakusumāñjaliḥ ||

	śuklamālyāmbaradharas tāṃ tulām anumantrayet |

	namas te sarvadevānāṃ śakti tvaṃ satyam āsthitā ||

	sākṣibhūtā jagaddhātrī nirmitā viśvayoninā |

	ekataḥ sarvasatyāni tathānṛtaśatāni ca ||

	dharmādharmakṛtāṃ madhye sthāpitāsi jagaddhite |

	tvaṃ tule sarvabhūtānāṃ pramāṇam iha kīrtitā ||

	māṃ tolayantī saṃsārād uddharasva namo 'stu te |

	yo 'sau tatrādhipo devaḥ puruṣaḥ pañcaviṃśakaḥ ||

	sa eṣo 'dhiṣṭhito devi tvayi tasmān namo namaḥ |

	oṃ namo namas te govinda tulāpuruṣasaṃjñaka ||

	tvaṃ hare tārayasvāsmāṃs tv asmāt saṃsārakardamāt |

	puṇyaṃ kālaṃ samāsādya kṛtvaivam adhivāsanam ||

	punaḥ pradakṣiṇaṃ kṛtvā tulāṃ tāṃ prāruhed budhaḥ |

	sakhaḍgacarmakavacī sarvābharaṇabhūṣitaḥ ||

	dharmarājam athādhāya somasūtreṇa saṃyutam |

	karābhyāṃ baddhamuṣṭibhyām āste paśyan harer mukham ||

	tato 'pare tulābhāge nyaseyur dvijapuṃkavāḥ |

	samād abhyadhikaṃ yāvat kāñcanaṃ cātinirmalam ||

	puṣṭikāmas tu kurvīta bhūmisaṃsthaṃ nareśvara |

	kṣaṇamātraṃ tataḥ sthitvā punar evam udīrayet ||

	oṃ namas te sarvabhūtānāṃ sākṣibhūte sanātane |

	pitāmahena devi tvaṃ nirmitā parameṣṭhinā ||

	tvayā ghṛtaṃ jagat sarvaṃ mahat sthāvarajaṅgamam |

	sarvabhūtātmabhūtasthe namas te viśvadhāriṇi ||

**[319]**	tato 'vatīrya gurave pūrvam ardhaṃ nivedayet |

	ṛtvigbhyaḥ param ardhaṃ tu dadyād udakapūrvakam ||

	gurave grāmaratnāni ṛtvigbhyaś ca nivedayet |

	prāpya teṣām anujñāṃ ca tathānyebhyo 'pi dāpayet ||

	dīnānāthaviśiṣṭādīn pūjayed brāhmaṇaiḥ saha |

	na ciraṃ ghārayed gehe hema saṃprokṣitaṃ budhaḥ ||

	tiṣṭhadbhayāvahaṃ yasmāc chokavyādhikaraṃ nṛṇām |

	śīghraṃ parasvīkaraṇāc chreyaḥ prāpnoti puṣkalam ||

	anena vidhinā yas tu tulāpuruṣam ācaret |

	pratilokādhipasthāne pratimanvantaraṃ vaset ||

	vimānenārkavarṇena kiṃkiṇījālamālinā |

	pūjyamāno 'psarobhiś ca tato viṣṇupuraṃ vrajet ||

	kalpakoṭiśataṃ yāvat tasmiṃl loke mahīyate ||

	karmakṣayād ih punar bhuvi rājarājabhūpālamaulimaṇirañjitapādapīṭhaḥ |

	śraddhānvito bhavati yajñasahasrayājī dīpapratāpajitasarvamahīpalokaḥ ||

	yo dīyamānam api paśyati bhaktiyukto lokāntare smarati vācayatīha loke |

	yo vā śṛṇoti paṭhatīndusamānarūpaṃ prāpnoti dhāma sa puraṃdaradevajuṣṭam ||

iti tulāpuruṣadānam |

atra bhaviṣyottarīyā viśeṣāḥ |

	tanmadhye kārayed vediṃ hastamātrocchritāṃ śubhām |

	caturdvāreṣu saṃsthāpyāḥ kumbhāḥ syuḥ pallavānanāḥ ||

	pañcaratnasamāyuktāḥsaptadhānyopari sthitāḥ |

pañcaratnāni |

	kanakaṃ hīrakaṃ nīlaṃ padmarāgaṃ ca mauktikam || iti 

saptadhānyāni grāmyāṇi āraṇyāni grāmyāraṇyāni vā |

	vrīhayo yavagodhūmā ubhau ca tilasarṣapau |

	ikṣuḥ priyaṅgavaś caiva grāmyā oṣadhayaḥ smṛtāḥ ||

	veṇuśyāmākanīvārajartilāś ca gavedhukāḥ |

	āraṇyajā markaṭikāḥ sapta gandutikottamāḥ ||

**[320]**	aṇavo rājamāṣāś ca māṣā mudgāś ca kodravāḥ |

	kuhīnakāḥ sahīnāś ca saptaite dvyantarāḥ smṛtāḥ || iti |

tathā |

	atraiva kecid icchanti ṛṣayaḥ ṣoḍaśartvijaḥ |

	āghārāv ājyabhāgau tu pūrvaṃ hutvā dvijottamaḥ ||

	praṇavādisvanāmnā ca svāhānte homa ucyate ||

tathā |

	anenaiva vidhānena kecid raupyamayaṃ punaḥ |

	karpūreṇa tathecchanti kecid brāhmaṇapuṃgavāḥ ||

	tathā sitatṛtīyāyāṃ nāryaḥ saubhāgyadarpitāḥ |

	kuṅkumena prayacchanti lavaṇena guḍena ca ||

	tatra mantrā na homā vā evam eva pradāpayet ||

iti tulādāne viśeṣaḥ |

	athātaḥ saṃpravakṣyāmi mahādānam uttamam |

	nāmnā hiraṇyagarbhākhyaṃ mahapātakanāśanam ||

	puṇyaṃ dinam athāsādya tulāpuruṣadānavat |

	ṛtvigmaṇḍapasaṃbhārabhūṣaṇācchādanādikam ||

	kuryād upoṣitas tadval lokeśāvāhanaṃ budhaḥ |

	puṇyāhavācanaṃ kṛtvā tadvat kṛtvādhivāsanam ||

	brāhmaṇair ānayet kuṇḍaṃ tapanīyam ayaṃ śubham |

	dvāsaptatyaṅgulocchrāyaṃ hemapaṅkajagarbhavat ||

	tribhāgahīnavistāraṃ praśastaṃ murajākṛti |

	daśāntāni saratnāni dātraṃ sūcī tathaiva ca ||

	hemanālaṃ sapiṭakaṃ bahir ādityasaṃyutam |

	athaivāvaraṇaṃ nābher upavītaṃ ca kāñcanam ||

	pārśvataḥ sthāpayet tadvad dhemadaṇḍaṃ kamaṇḍalum |

	padmākāraṃ pidhānaṃ syāt samantād aṅgulādhikam ||

	muktāvalīsamopetaṃ padmarāgadalānvitam |

	tiladroṇopari gataṃ vedimadhye tato 'rcayet ||

	tato maṅgalaśabdena brahmaghoṣaraveṇa ca |

**[321]**	sarvauṣadhyudakasthānaṃ snapitaṃ vedapāragaiḥ ||

	śuklamālyāmbaradharaiḥ sarvābharaṇabhūṣitaḥ|

	ida(ma)m uccārayen mantraṃ gṛhītakusumāñjaliḥ ||

	namo hiraṇyagarbhāya hiraṇyakavacāya ca |

	saptalokasurādhyakṣa jagaddhātre namo namaḥ ||

	bhūrlokapramukhā lokās tava gharbhe vyavasthitāḥ |

	brahmādayas tathā devā namas te viśvadhāriṇe ||

	namas te bhuvanādhāra namaste bhuvanāśraya |

	namo hiraṇyagarbhāya garbhe yasya pitāmahaḥ||

	yatas tvam eva bhūtātmā bhūte bhūte vyavasthitaḥ ||

	tasmān mām uddharāśeṣaduḥkhasaṃsārasāgarāt |

	evam āmantrya tanmadhyam āviśyāsta udaṅmukhaḥ ||

	muṣṭibhyāṃ parisaṃgṛhya dharmarājacaturmukhau ||

	jānumadhye śiraḥ kṛtvā tiṣṭhed ucchvāsapañcakam |

	garbhādhānaṃ puṃsavanaṃ sīmantonnayanaṃ tathā ||

	kuryur hiraṇyagarbhasya tatas te dvijapuṃgavāḥ |

	gīramaṅgalaghoṣeṇa gurur utthāpayet tataḥ ||

	jātakarmādikāḥ kuryuḥ kriyāḥ ṣoḍaśa cāparāḥ |

	sūcyādikaṃ ca gurave datvā mantram imaṃ paṭhet ||

	oṃ namo hiraṇyagarbhāya viśvagarbhāya vai namaḥ |

	carācarasya jagato gṛhabhūtāya vai namaḥ ||

	mātrāhaṃ janitaḥ pūrvaṃ martyadharmāmarottama |

	tvadgarbhasaṃbhavo deva divyadeho bhavāmy aham ||

	caturbhiḥ kalaśair bhūyas tatas te dvijapuṃgavāḥ |

	snānaṃ kuryuḥ prasannāṅgāḥ sarvābharaṇabhūṣitāḥ ||

	devasya tveti mantreṇa sthitasya kanakāsane |

	adya jātasya te 'ṅgāni abhiprekṣyāmahe vayam ||

	divyenānena vapuṣā ciraṃ jīva sukhī bhava |

**[322]**	tato hiraṇyagarbhaṃ taṃ tebhyo dadyād vicakṣaṇaḥ ||

	te pūjyāḥ sarvabhāvena bahavo vā tadājñayā |

	tatropakaraṇaṃ sarvaṃ gurave vinivedayet ||

	pādukopānahacchatraṃ cāmarāsanabhājanam |

	grāmaṃ vā viṣayaṃ vāpi yad anyad dayitaṃ bhavet ||

	anena vidhinā yas tu puṇye 'hni vinivedayet |

	hiraṇyagarbhadānaṃ sa brahmaloke mahīyate ||

	pureṣu lokapālānāṃ praimanvantaraṃ vaset |

	kalpakoṭiśataṃ yāvad brahmaloke mahīyate ||

	kalikaluṣavimuktaḥ pūjitaḥ siddhasaṃghair amalacamaramālāvījyamāno 'psarobhiḥ |

	pitṛśatam atha bandhūn putrapautraprapautrān api narakanimagnāṃs tārayed eka eva ||

iti mātsye hiraṇyagarbhadānavidhiḥ |

	matsya uvāca |

	athātaḥ saṃpravakṣyāmi brahmāṇḍābhidham uttamam |

	yac chreṣṭhaṃ sarvadānānāṃ mahāpātakanāśanam ||

	puṇyaṃ dinam athāsādya tulāpuruṣadānavat |

	ṛtvigmaṇḍalasaṃbhārabhūṣaṇācchādanāni ca ||

	lokeśāvāhanaṃ tadvad adhivāsanakaṃ tathā |

	kuryād viṃśapalād ūrdhvam ā sahasrāc ca śaktataḥ ||

	śakaladvayasaṃyuktaṃ brahmāṇḍaṃ kāñcanaṃ budhaḥ |

	diggajāṣṭakasaṃyuktaṃ ṣaḍvedāṅgasamanvitam ||

	lokapālāṣṭakopetaṃ madhyasthitacaturmukham |

	śivācyutārkaśikharam umālakṣmīsamanvitam ||

	vasvādityamarudgarbhaṃ mahāratnasamanvitam |

	vitaster aṅgulaśataṃ yāvadāyāmavistaram ||

	kauśeyavastrasaṃyuktaṃ tiladroṇopari nyaset |

	tathāṣṭādaśa dhānyāni samantāt parikalpayet || **[323]**

	śyāmākadhānyayavamudgatilāṇumāṣagodhūmakodravakulatthasatīnaśimbaiḥ |

	aṣṭādaśaṃ caṇakalāyamayoṣṭarājamāṣapriyaṅgusahitaṃ ca masūram āhuḥ ||

	pūrveṇānantasaṃyuktaṃ pradyumnaṃ pūrvadakṣiṇe |

	prakṛtiṃ dakṣiṇe deśe saṃkarṣaṇam ataḥ param ||

	paścime caturo vedān aniruddham ataḥ param |

	agnim uttarato hemavāsudevam ataḥ param ||

	samantād guḍapīṭhasthān arcayet kāñcanān budhaḥ |

	sthāpayed vastrasaṃvītān pūrṇakumbhān daśaiva tu ||

	daśaiva dhenavo deyāḥ sahemā varadohanāḥ |

	pādukopānahacchatracāmarāsanadarpaṇaiḥ ||

	bhakṣyabhojyānnadīpekṣuphalamālyānulepanaiḥ |

	homādhivāsanānte tu snāpito vedapuṃgavaiḥ ||

	oṃ namo 'stu viśveśvara viśvadhāma jagatsavitre bhagavan namas te |

	saptarṣilokāmarabhūtaleśa garbheṇa sārdhaṃ vitarābhirakṣām ||

	ye duḥkhitās te sukhino bhavantu prayāntu pāpāni carācarāṇām |

	tvaddānaśastrāhatapātakānāṃ brahmāṇḍa doṣāḥ pralayaṃ prayāntu ||

	devaṃ praṇamyāmaraviśvagarbhaṃ dadyād dvijebhyo daśadhā vibhajya |

	bhāgadvayaṃ tatra guroḥ prakalpya samaṃ bhajec cheṣam ataḥ krameṇa ||

	svalpeṣu homaṃ gurur eka eva kuryād athaikāgnividhānayuktyā |

	sa eva saṃpūjyatamo 'lpavittair yathoktavastrābharaṇādikena ||

	itthaṃ ya etad akhilaṃ puruṣo 'nukuryād brahmāṇḍadānam adhigamya mahad vimānam |

	nirdhūtakalmaṣaviśuddhatanur murārer ānandakṛtpadam upaiti mahāpsarobhiḥ ||

	saṃtārayet pitṛpitāmahaputrapautrabandhupriyātithikalatraśatāṣṭakaṃ saḥ |

	brahmāṇḍadānaśakalīkṛtapātakaugham ānandayec ca jananīkulam apy aśeṣam ||

iti mātsye brahmāṇḍadānavidhiḥ |

atra bhaviṣyottarīyā viśeṣāḥ | **[324]**

	brahmāṇḍaṃ kāñcanaṃ kṛtvā sarvalakṣaṇasaṃyutam |

	devāsurair manuṣyaiś ca gandharvoragarākṣasaiḥ ||

	saṃyuktaṃ ca nadībhiś ca samudraiḥ parvatais tathā |

	vimānaśatakoṭībhir bhūṣitaṃ ca sarovaraiḥ ||

tathā |

	tasyāṅge kalpayed rājan bhuvanāni caturdaśa |

tathā |

	kalaśa(śakala)dvayasaṃyuktaṃ ghaṭākāraṃ susaṃhatam |

tathā |

	puṣpamaṇḍapikāṃ kṛtvā tatra saṃsthāpayed budhaḥ |

	tiladroṇoparigataṃ kuṅkumakṣodacarcitam ||

	vāsoyugmena saṃchādya dhūpagandhādivāsitam |

	aṣṭādaśaiva dhānyāni droṇamātrāṇy athāharet ||

	gṛhe vā maṇḍape vāpi sthāpayet taṃ vicakṣaṇaḥ |

tathā |

	brahmaviṣṇuśivānāṃ ca tannāmnā juhuyāt tilān |

	ayutaṃ homayet pañcān mahāvyāhṛtibhir nṛpa ||

	rudrajāpaś ca kartavyas tasyaivānantaraṃ budhaiḥ |

	tataḥ parvasamīpe tu snātaḥ śuklāmbaraḥ śuciḥ ||

	brahmāṇaṃ pūjayed bhaktyā gṛhītasukumāñjaliḥ (?) |

	namo jagatpratiṣṭhāya viśvadhāmne namo 'stu te ||

	vāṅmayāntarnimagnāya brahmāṇḍe śubhakṛd bhava |

	brahmāṇḍodaravartīni yāni sattvāni kānicit ||

	tāni sarvāṇi me puṣṭiṃ prayacchantv atulāṃ tathā |

	brahmā viṣṇuś ca rudraś ca lokapālās tathā grahāḥ ||

	nakṣatrāṇi tathā nāgā ṛṣayo marutas tathā |

	sarve bhavantu me prītāḥ sapta janmāntarāṇi ca ||

	ity uccārya tato dadyād brahmāṇḍaṃ sarvakāmadam |

	sadakṣiṇaṃ ca tat kṛtvā diksaṃsthān pūjayed dvijān ||

iti bhaviṣyottare viśeṣato brahmāṇḍadānavidhiḥ \

	matsya uvāca |

	kalpapādapadānākhyam ataḥ param anuttamam |

	mahādānaṃ pravakṣyāmi sarvapāpapraṇāśanam ||

**[325]**	puṇyaṃ dinam athāsādya tulāpuruṣadānavat |

	puṇyāhavācanaṃ kṛtvā lokeśāvāhanaṃ tathā ||

	ṛtvigmaṇḍapasaṃskārabhūṣaṇācchādanādikam |

	kāñcanaṃ kārayed vṛkṣaṃ nānāphalasamanvitam ||

	nānāvihagavastrāṇi bhūṣaṇāni ca kārayet |

	śaktitas tripalād ūrdhvam ā sahasrād dhi kārayet ||

	atha taptasuvarṇasya kārayet kalpapādapam |

	guḍaprasthopariṣṭāc ca sitavastrayugāvṛtam ||

	brahmaviṣṇuśivopetaṃ pañcaśākhaṃ sabhāskaram |

	kāmadevam adhastāc ca sakalatraṃ prapūjayet ||

	saṃtānaṃ pūrvatas tadvat turīyāṃśena kalpayet |

	mandāraṃ dakṣiṇe pārśve śriyā sārdhaṃ ghṛtopari ||

	paścime pāribhadraṃ tu savitryā saha jīrake |

	surabhīsaṃyutaṃ tadvat tileṣu harcandanam ||

	tṛtīyāṃśena kurvīta tilena phalasaṃyutam |

	kauśeyavastrasaṃyuktān ikṣumālāsamanvitān ||

	tathāṣṭau pūrṇakalaśān pādukāsanabhājanam |

	dīpakopānahacchatracāmarāsanasaṃyutam ||

	phalamālyayutaṃ tadvad upariṣṭād vitānakam |

	tathāṣṭādaśa dhānyāni samantāt parikalpayet ||

	oṃ namas te kalpavṛkṣāya cintitārthapradāyine |

	viśvaṃbharāya devāya namas te viśvamūrtaye ||

	yasmāt tvam eva viśvātmā brahmā sthānur divākaraḥ |

	mūrtāmūrtaṃ paraṃ bījamataḥ pāhi sanātanam ||

	tvam evāmṛtasarvasvam anantaḥ puruṣo 'vyayaḥ |

	saṃtānādyair upetaḥ san pāhi saṃsārasāgarāt ||

**[326]**	evam āmantrya taṃ dadyād gurave kalpapādapam |

	caturbhyaś cāpi ṛtvigbhyaḥ saṃtānādyān prakalpayet ||

	(svalpeṣv ekāgnivat kuryād gurur evābhipūjitaḥ |

	na vittaśāṭhyaṃ kurvīta na ca vismayavān bhavet ||

	anena vidhinā yas tu mahādānaṃ nivedayet |)

	sarvapāpavinirmuktaḥ so 'śvamedhaphalaṃ labhet ||

	apsarobhiḥ parivṛtaḥ siddhacāraṇakiṃnaraiḥ |

	bhūtān bhavyāṃś ca manujāṃs tārayed romasaṃmitān ||

	stūyamāno divaḥ pṛṣṭhe putrapautraprapautrakān |

	vimānenārkavarṇena viṣṇulokaṃ sa gacchati ||

	divi kalpaśataṃ tiṣṭhed rājarājo bhaven naraḥ |

	nārāyaṇabalopeto nārāyaṇaparāyaṇaḥ ||

	nārāyaṇakathāsakto nārāyaṇaparaṃ vrajet ||

iti mātsye kalpavṛkṣadānavidhiḥ |

asya bhaviṣyottare viśeṣaḥ |

	śrībhagavān uvāca |

	aputraḥ puruṣo yaś ca nārī vā parvatātmane |

	sauvarṇas tena dātavyaḥ kalpavṛkṣo guṇānvitaḥ ||

	kṛttrimaṃ vāpi gṛhṇīyād vṛkṣaṃ vā sthāvarādikam |

	anyajāto 'tha vā putraḥ putratve parikalpayet ||

	tena putravatāṃ loke gacched divi na saṃśayaḥ |

	kalpavṛkṣas tu kartavyaḥ suddhakāñcanasaṃbhavaḥ ||

	bahuśākhaḥ suparṇāṅgo hy anekakusumānvitaḥ |

	mahāskandhaḥ surūpaś ca ratnālaṃkṛtavigrahaḥ ||

	phalāni tasya divyāni sauvarṇāni prakalpayet |

	rājataṃ caiva kurvīta samantāt pīṭham uttamam ||

	pravālāṅkurasaṃpṛktaṃ muktādāmavilambitam |

	catuṣkoṇeṣu kurvīta caturaḥ kāñcanadrumān ||

**[327]**	suvarṇasya pramāṇaṃ tu kathayāmi varānane |

	sahasreṇa tadardhena tasyāpy ardhena vā punaḥ ||

	kārayet kalpavṛkṣaṃ tu sarvakāmasamṛddhaye |

	candrasūryoparāge tu duḥsvapnādbhutadarśane ||

	janmarkṣe viṣuve caiva yugādyāsv atha vā punaḥ |

	nadyās tīre gṛhe vāpi devatāyatane 'pi vā |

	prāgudakpravaṇe deśe maṇḍapaṃ tatra kārayet ||

	daśahastapramāṇena kuṇḍam ekaṃ suśobhanam |

	āgneyyāṃ kārayed rājan mekhalātrayabhūṣitam ||

	tatra ca brāhmaṇā yojyā ṛgyajuḥsāmapāṭhakāḥ |

	upadeṣṭā ca tatraiva dvitīyaḥ pañcamo 'pi vā ||

	sarvābharaṇasaṃpannās tāmrapātravibhūṣitāḥ |

	guḍaprasthopariṣṭāc ca sthāpayet kalpapādapam ||

	brahmaviṣṇuśivopetaṃ pañcaśākhaṃ sabhāskaram |

	kāmadevam adhastāc ca sakalatraṃ prakalpayet ||

	saṃtānaṃ saha gāyatryā pūrvato lavaṇopari |

	mandāraṃ dakṣiṇe pārśve śriyā saha tathā ghṛte ||

	paścime pārijātaṃ ca umayā saha jīrake |

	surabhīsahitaṃ tadvittileṣu haricandanam ||

	kauśeyavastrasaṃyuktān ikṣumālāsamanvitān |

	tathāṣṭau pūrvakalaśān samantāt parikalpayet ||

	agnau praṇayanaṃ kṛtvā adhivāsya tu pādapam |

	homaṃ ca brāhmaṇāḥ kuryuḥ suśuddhenāntarātmanā ||

	āghārāv ājyabhāgau ca pūrvaṃ hutvā vicakṣaṇaḥ |

	talliṅgaiḥ sthāpitān devān homenāpyāyayet tataḥ ||

	mahāvyāhṛtibhiś caiva homaṃ kuryus tataḥ param |

	ayutena bhavet siddhir yajñasya varavarṇini ||

	tataḥ prabhāte cotthāya snātvā śuklāmbaraḥ śuciḥ |

	triḥ pradakṣiṇam āvṛtya mantram etam udīrayet ||

**[328]**	namaste kalpavṛkṣāya cintitārthapradāyaka |

	vṛddhipradāya devāya namas te viśvamūrtaye ||

	yasmāt tvam eva viśvātmā brahmā sthāṇur divākaraḥ |

	mūrtāmūrthaṃ paraṃ bījam ataḥ pāhi sanātanam ||

	evam āmantrya taṃ dadyād gurave kalpapādapam |

	caturbhyaś cātha ṛtvigbhyaḥ saṃtānādīn prakalpayet ||

	anena vidhinā yas tu dānam etat prayacchati |

	tasya puṇyaphalaṃ devi śṛṇuṣva gadato mama ||

	nārī vā puruṣo vāpi sa tāvad bhuvi durlabhaḥ |

	mātṛtaḥ pitṛtaś caiva puruṣān ekaviṃśatim ||

	tārayet kṛtakṛtyaś ca bhavej janmani janmani |

	avasthātritaye yac ca pāpaṃ janmadaśārjitam ||

	tat kṣālayaty asaṃdehaṃ brahmalokaṃ ca gacchati |

	tatra brahmadinaṃ sthitvā punar yāti śivālayam ||

	tatrāpi suciraṃ kālaṃ gamitvā puṇyalokataḥ |

	evamādi vasitvā tu munuṣyo jāyate punaḥ ||

	arogī balavāñ śūro rūpavān subhagas tathā |

	daś janmāni kurute rājyaṃ nihatakaṇṭakaḥ ||

	nārī vā dānam etad dhi datvā caitat phalaṃ labhet |

	etad gauryāḥ samākhyātaṃ bhavena bhavamedinā ||

	mayā ca kathitaṃ sarvaṃ tava pāṇḍukulodvaha ||

	haimaṃ suradrumacatuṣṭayasaṃyutaṃ ca saṃkalpya kalpaviṭapaṃ pratipādayed yaḥ |

	viprāy vedaviduṣe prayato 'hni puṇye prāpnoty analpam avikalpam asāv abhīṣṭam ||

iti bhaviṣyottare kalpavṛkṣadāne viśeṣaḥ |

	matsya ucāca |

	athātaḥ saṃpravakṣyāmi mahādānam anuttamam |

	gosahasrapradānākhyaṃ sarvapāpaharaṃ param ||

	puṇyāṃ tithiṃ samāsādya yugamanvantarādikam |

**[329]**	payovrats trirātraṃ syād ekarātram athāpi vā ||

	lokeśāvāhanaṃ kuryāt tulāpuruṣadānavat |

	puṇyāhavācanaṃ kuryād dhomakāryaṃ tathaiva ca ||

	ṛtvigmaṇḍalasaṃbhārabhūṣaṇācchādanādikam |

	vṛṣaṃ lakṣaṇasaṃyuktaṃ vedimadhye 'dhivāsayet ||

	gosahasrād viniṣkṛṣya gavāṃ daśakam eva ca |

	gosahasraṃ bahiṣkuryād vastramālyavibhūṣitam ||

	suvarṇaśṛṅgābharaṇaṃ raupyapādasamanvitam |

	antaḥ preveśya daśakaṃ vastramālyais tu pūjayet ||

	suvarṇaghaṇṭikopetaṃ hemapaṭṭair alaṃkṛtam |

	kauśeyavastrasaṃvītaṃ gandhamālyasamanvaitam ||

	hemaratnamayaiḥ śṛṅgaiś cāmarair upaśobhitam |

	pādukopānahacchatrabhājanāsanasaṃyutam ||

	gavāṃ daśakamadhye syāt kāñcano nandikeśvaraḥ |

	kauśeyavastrasaṃvīto gandhamālyavibhūṣitaḥ ||

	lavaṇadroṇaśikhare mālekṣuphalasaṃyutaḥ |

	kuryāt palaśatād ūrdhvaṃ sarvam etad asaṃśayam ||

	śaktitaḥ palasāhasraṃ tritayaṃ yāvad eva tu |

	gośate 'pi daśāṃśena sarvam etat samācaret ||

	puṇyakālaṃ samāśādya gītamaṅgalaniḥsvanaiḥ |

	sarvauṣadhyudakasnānaiḥ snāpito vedapuṃgavaiḥ ||

	imam uccārayen mantraṃ gṛhītakusumāñjaliḥ |

	oṃ namo viśvamūrtibhyo viśvamātṛbhya eva ca ||

	viśvādhivāsinībhyaś ca rohiṇībhyo namo namaḥ |

	gavām aṅgeṣu tiṣṭhanti bhuvanāny ekaviṃśatiḥ ||

	brahmādayas tathā devā rohiṇyaḥ pāntu mātaraḥ |

	gāvo mamāgrataḥ santu gāvaḥ pṛṣṭhata eva hi ||

	gāvaḥ śirasi me nityaṃ gavāṃ madhye vasāmy aham |

	yasmāt tvaṃ vṛṣarūpeṇa dharma eva sanātanaḥ ||

**[330]**	aṣṭamūrter adhiṣṭhānam ataḥ pāhi sanātanam |

	ity āmantrya tato dadyād gurave nandikeśvaram ||

	sarvopakaraṇopetaṃ goyugaṃ ca vicakṣaṇaḥ |

	ṛtvigbhyo dhenum ekaikāṃ daśānāṃ vinivedayet ||

	daśa pañcātha vā dadyād anyebhyas tadanujñayā |

	naikā bahubhyo dātavyā yato doṣakaro bhavet ||

	bahvyaś caikasya dātavyāḥ śrīmatārogyavṛddhaye |

	payovrataḥ punas tiṣṭhed ekāhaṃ gosahasradaḥ ||

	śrāvayec chṛṇuyād vāpi mahādānānukīrtanam |

	tad dinaṃ brahmacārī syād ya icched vipulāṃ śriyam ||

	anena vidhinā yas tu gosahasraprado bhavet |

	sarvapāpavinirmuktaḥ siddhacāraṇasevitaḥ ||

	vimānenārkavarṇena kiṅkiṇījālamālinā |

	sarveṣāṃ lokapālānāṃ loke saṃpūjyate 'maraiḥ ||

	pratimanvantaraṃ tiṣṭhet putrapautrasamanvitaḥ |

	sapta lokān atikramya tataḥ śivapuraṃ vrajet ||

	śatam ekottaraṃ tadvat pitṝṇāṃ tārayed budhaḥ |

	mātāmahānāṃ tadvac ca putrapautrasamanvitaḥ ||

	yāvat kalpaśataṃ tiṣṭhed rājarājo bhavet punaḥ |

	aśvamedhaśataṃ kuryāc chivadhyānaparāyaṇaḥ ||

	vaiṣṇavaṃ lokam āsthāya tato mucyeta bandhanāt |

	pitaraś cābhinandanti gosahasrapradaṃ śubham ||

	api syāt sa kule 'smākaṃ putro dauhitra eva vā |

	gosahasraprado bhūtvā narakād uddhariṣyati ||

	tasya karmakaro vā syād api draṣṭā tathaiva ca |

	saṃsārasāgarād asmād yo 'smān saṃtārayiṣyati ||

iti mātsye gosahasradānavidhiḥ |

	matsya uvāca |

	athātaḥ saṃpravakṣyāmi kāmadhenuvidhiṃ param |

	sarvakāmapradaṃ nṝṇāṃ mahāpātakanāśanam ||

**[331]**	lokeśāvāhanaṃ tadvad dhomaḥ kāryo vicakṣaṇaiḥ |

	tulāpuruṣavat kuryāt kuṇḍamaṇḍapavedikām ||

	svalpeṣv ekāgnivat kuryād gurur eva samāhitaḥ |

	kāñcanasyātiśuddhasya dhenuṃ vatsaṃ ca kārayet ||

	uttamā palasāhasrā tadardhena tu madhyamā |

	kanīyasī tadardhena kāmadhenuḥ prakīrtitā ||

	śaktitas tripalād ūrdhvam aśakto 'pi hi kārayet |

	vedyāṃ kṛṣṇājinaṃ nyasya guḍaprasthasamanvitām ||

	nyeased upari tāṃ dhenuṃ mahāratnair alaṃkṛtām |

	kumbhāṣṭakaphalopetāṃ nānāphalasamanvitām ||

	tathāṣṭādaśa dhānyāni samantāt parikalpayet |

	ikṣudaṇḍāṣṭakaṃ tadvac nānāphalasamanvitm ||

	bhājanaṃ cāmaraṃ tadvat tāmradohanakaṃ tathā |

	kauśeyavastradvayasaṃprayuktā dīpātapatrābharaṇābhirāmā |

	sacāmarā kuṇḍalinī saghaṇṭā galartikā pādukaraupyapādā ||

galartikā galabhūṣaṇam |

	rasaiś ca sarvaiḥ parito 'bhijuṣṭā haridrayā puṣpaphalair anekaiḥ |

	ajājikustuṃburuśarkarābhir vitānakaṃ copari pañcavarṇam ||

	snātas tato maṅgalavedaghoṣaiḥ pradakṣiṇīkṛtya sapuṣpahastaḥ |

	āvāhayet tāṃ guruṇoktamantrair dvijāya dadyād atha darbhapāṇiḥ ||

	tvaṃ sarvadevagaṇamandirasaṅgabhūtā viśveśvaratripathagodadhiparvatānām |

	tvaddānaśastraśakalīkṛtapātakaughaḥ prāpto 'smi nirvṛtim atīva parāṃ namāmi ||

	loke yathepsitaphalārthavidhāyinīṃ tvām āsādya ko hia bhavaduḥkham upaiti martyaḥ |

	saṃsāraduḥkhaśamanāya dadasva kāmaṃ tvāṃ kāmadhenur iti devagaṇā vadanti ||

	āmantrya rūpakulaśīlaguṇānvitāya viprāya yaḥ kanakadhenum imāṃ pradadyāt |

	prāpnoti dhāma sa puraṃdaradevajuṣṭaṃ kanyāgaṇaiḥ parivṛtaḥ padam indumauleḥ ||

iti mātsya kāmadhenupradānavidhiḥ |

	matsya uvāca |

	athātaḥ saṃpravakṣyāmi hiraṇyāśvavidhiṃ śubham |

	yasya pradānād bhuvane anantaṃ phalam aśnute ||

**[332]**	puṇyāṃ tithiṃ samāsādya kuryād brāhmaṇavācanam |

	lokeśāvāhanaṃ tadvat tulāpuruṣadānavat ||

	ṛtvigmaṇḍapasaṃbhārabhūṣaṇācchādanādikam |

	alpeṣv ekāgnivat kuryād dhemavājimakhaṃ budhaḥ ||

	sthāpayed vedimadhye tu kārṣṇājinatilopari |

	kauśeyavastrasaṃvītaṃ kārayed dhemavājinam ||

	śaktitas tripalād ūrdhvam āsahasrapalaṃ budhaḥ |

	pādukopāhanacchatracāmarāsanabhājanaiḥ ||

	pūrṇakumbhāṣṭakopetaṃ mālyekṣuphalasaṃyutam |

	śayyāṃ sopaskarāṃ tadvad dhemamārtaṇḍasaṃyutām ||

	tataḥ sarvauṣadhisnānasnāpitaṃ vedapuṃgavaiḥ |

	imam uccārayen mantraṃ gṛhītakusumāñjaliḥ ||

	namas te deva deveśa vedāharaṇalampaṭa |

	vājirūpeṇa mām asmāt pāhi saṃsārasāgarāt ||

	tvam eva saptadhā bhūtvā chandorūpeṇa bhāskaram |

	yasmād bramayase lokān ataḥ pāhi sanātana ||

	evam uccārya gurave tam aśvaṃ vinivedayet |

	datvā pāpakṣayād bhānor lokam abhyeti śāśvatam ||

	gobhir vibhavataḥ sarvān ṛtvijaś cābhipūjayet |

	sarvadhānyopakaraṇaṃ gurave vinivedayet ||

	sarvaṃ śayyādikaṃ datvā bhuñjīta tilam eva ca |

	purāṇaśravaṇaṃ tadvat kārayed bhojanādikam ||

	imaṃ hiraṇyāśvavidhiṃ karoti yaḥ saṃpūjyamāno divi devatendraiḥ |

	vimuktapāpaḥ sa puraṃ murārer āpnoti siddhari abhipūjitaḥ san ||

iti mātsye hiraṇyāśvadānam |

	matsya uvāca |

	athātaḥ saṃpravakṣyāmi mahādānam anuttamam |

	puṇyam aśvarathaṃ nāma mahāpātakanāśanam ||

	puṇyaṃ dinam athāsādya kṛtvā brāhmaṇavācanam |

	lokeśāvāhanaṃ kuryāt tulāpuruṣadānavat ||

**[333]**	ṛtvigmaṇḍapasaṃbhārabhūṣaṇācchādanādikam |

	kṛṣṇājine tilān kṛtvā kāñcanaṃ kārayed ratham ||

	saptāśvaṃ caturaśvaṃ vā catuścakraṃ sukūbaram |

	aindranīlena kumbhena dhvajarūpeṇa saṃyutam ||

	lokapālāṣṭakopetaṃ padmarāgadalānvitam |

	catvāraḥ pūrṇakalaśā dhānyāny aṣṭādaśaiva tu ||

	kauśeyavastrasaṃyuktam upariṣṭād vitānakam |

	mālyekṣuphalasaṃyuktaṃ puruṣeṇa samanvitam ||

	yo yadbhaktaḥ pumān kuryāt sa tannāmnyādhivāsanam |

	chatracāmarakauśeyavastropānahapādukāḥ ||

	gobhir vibhavataḥ sārdhaṃ dadyāc ca śayanāsanam |

	ā bhārāt tripalād ūrdhvaṃ śaktitaḥ kārayed budhaḥ ||

	aṣṭābhir atha saṃyuktaṃ caturbhir vātha vājibhiḥ |

	dvābhyām atha yutaṃ dadyād dhemasiṃhadhvajānvitam ||

	cakrarakṣāv ubhau tadvat turagasthāvathāśvinau |

	puṇyakālam athāsādya pūrvavat snāpito dvijaiḥ ||

	triḥ pradakṣiṇam āvṛtya gṛhītakusumāñjaliḥ |

	śuklamālyāmbaro dadyād imaṃ mantram udīrayet ||

	oṃ namo namaḥ pāpavināśanāya vedātmane vedaturaṃgamāya |

	dhāmnām adhīśāya bhavābhavāya pāpaughadāvānala dehi śāntim ||

	vasvaṣṭakādityamarudgaṇānāṃ tvam eva dhātā paramaṃ nidhānam |

	yatas tato me hṛdayaṃ prayātu dharmaikatānatvamaghaughanāśāt ||

	iti turagarathapradānam evaṃ bhavabhayasūdanam atra yaḥ karoti |

	sa kaluṣapaṭalair vimuktadehaḥ paramam upaiti padaṃ pinākapāṇeḥ ||

	dedīpyamānavapuṣā vijitaprabhāvam ākramya maṇḍalam akhaṇḍam acaṇḍabhānoḥ |

	siddhāṅganānayanaṣaṭpadapīyamānavaktrāmbujo 'mbujabhavena ciraṃ sahāste ||

	iti paṭhati śṛṇoti vā ya itthaṃ kanakaturaṅgarathapradānam asmin |

	na sa narakapuraṃ prayāti jātu narakaripor bhavanaṃ prayāti bhūyaḥ ||

**[334]**

iti mātsye hiraṇyāśvarathadānam |

	matsya uvāca |

	athātaḥ saṃpravakṣyāmi hemahastirathaṃ śubham |

	yasya pradānāc ca harer bhavanaṃ yāti mānavaḥ ||

	puṇyāṃ tithiṃ samāsādya tulāpuruṣadānavat |

	vipravācanakaṃ kuryāl lokeśāvāhanaṃ budhaḥ ||

	ṛtvigmaṇḍalasaṃbhārabhūṣaṇācchādanādikam |

	atrāpy upoṣitas tadvat brāhmaṇaiḥ saha bhojanam ||

	kuryāt puṣparathākāraṃ kāñcanaṃ maṇimaṇḍitam |

	valabhībhir vicitrābhiś catuścakrasamanvitam ||

	lokapālāṣṭakopetaṃ brahmārkaśivasaṃyutam |

	madhye nārāyaṇopetaṃ lakṣmīpuṣṭisamanvitam ||

	kṛṣṇājine tiladroṇaṃ kṛtvā saṃsthāpayed ratham |

	tathāṣṭādaśa dhānyāni bhājanāsanacandanaiḥ ||

	dīpakopanahacchatradarpaṇaṃ pādukānvitam |

	dhvaje tu garuḍaṃ kuryāt kūbarāgre vināyakam ||

	nānāphalasamāyuktam upariṣṭād vitānakam |

	kauśeyakaṃ pañcavarṇam amlānakusumānvitam ||

	caturbhiḥ kalaśaiḥ sārdhaṃ gobhir aṣṭābhir anvitam |

	caturbhir hemamātaṅgair muktādāmavibhūṣitam ||

	svarūpataḥ karibhyāṃ ca yuktaṃ kṛtvā nivedayet |

	kuryāt pañcapalād ūrdhvam ā bhārād api śaktitaḥ ||

	tato maṅgalaśabdena snapito vedapuṃgavaiḥ |

	triḥ pradakṣiṇam āvṛtya gṛhītakusmāñjaliḥ ||

	imam uccārayen mantraṃ brāhmaṇebhyo nivedayet |

	namo namaḥ śaṃkarapadmajārkalokeśavidyādharavāsudevaiḥ |

	tvaṃ sevyase vedapurāṇayajñais tejomaya syandana pāhi tasmāt ||

	yat tatpadaṃ param guhyataraṃ murārer ānandahetu guṇarūpavimuktam antaḥ |

	yogaikamānasadṛśo munayaḥ samādhau paśyanti tat tvam asi nātha rathe 'dhirūḍhaḥ ||

	yasmāt tvam eva bhavasāgarasaṃplutānām ānandabhāṇḍabhṛtamanthanayānapātram ? |

**[335]**	tasmād aghaughaśamanena kuru prasādaṃ cāmīkarebharathamādhavasaṃpradānam ||

	itthaṃ praṇamya kanakebharathapradānaṃ yaḥ kārayet sakalapāpavimuktadehaḥ |

	vidyādharāmaramunīndragaṇābhujuṣṭaṃ prāpnoti tatpadam atīndriyam indumauleḥ ||

	kṛtaduritavitānāṃs tūllasadvahnijālavyatikarakṛtadāhodvegabhājo 'pi bandhūn |

	nayati ca pitṛpautrān rauravād apy aśeṣān kṛtagajarathadānaḥ śāśvataṃ sadma viṣṇoḥ ||

iti mātsye hastirathadānam |

	matsya uvāca |

	athātaḥ saṃpravakṣyāmi mahādānam anuttamam |

	pañcalāṅgalakaṃ nāma mahāpātakanāśanam ||

	puṇyāṃ tithiṃ samāsādya yugādigrahaṇādikām |

	bhūmidānaṃ naro dadyāt pañcalāṅgalakānvitam ||

	kharvaṭaṃ kheṭakaṃ vāpi grāmaṃ vā sasyaśālinam |

	nirvartanaśataṃ vāpi tadardhaṃ vāpi śaktitaḥ ||

	suradārumayān kṛtvā halān pañca vicakṣaṇaḥ |

	sarvopakaraṇair yuktāṃs tathā tān pañca kāñcanān ||

	vṛṣalakṣaṇasaṃyuktān daśaiva ca duraṃdharān |

	suvarṇaśṛṅgābharaṇān muktālāṅgūlaśobhitān ||

	raupyapādāgratilakān raktakauśeyabhūṣaṇān |

	sragdāmacandanayutāñ śālāyām adhivāsayet ||

	parjanyādityarudrebhyaḥ payasā nirvapec carūn |

	etasminn eva kuṇḍe tu gurur yasmai nivedayet ||

	palāśasamidhas tadvad ājyaṃ kṛṣṇatilāṃś tathā |

	tulāpuruṣavat kuryāl lokeśāvāhanaṃ budhaḥ ||

	tato maṅgalaśabdena śuklamālyāmbaro 'tha saḥ |

	āhūya dvijadāṃpatyaṃ hemasūtrāṅgulīyakaiḥ ||

	kauśeyavastrakaṭakair maṇibhiś cābhipūjayet |

	śayyāṃ sopaskarāṃ tadvad dhenum ekāṃ payasvinīm ||

	tathāṣṭādaśa dānyāni samantād adhivāsayet |

	tataḥ pradakṣiṇaṃ kṛtvā gṛhītakusumāñjaliḥ ||

**[336]**	imam uccārayen mantram atha saṃvinivedayet |

	yasmād devagaṇāḥ sarve sthāvarāṇi carāṇi ca ||

	dhuraṃdharāṅge tiṣṭhanti tasmād bhaktiḥ śivāśtu me |

	yasmāc ca bhūmidānasya kalāṃ nārhanti ṣoḍaśīm ||

	dānāny anyāni me bhaktir dharma eva dṛḍhā bhavet |

	daṇḍena saptahastena triṃśad daṇḍā nivartanam ||

	tribhāgahīnaṃ gocarmamānam āha prajāpatiḥ |

	mānenānena yo dadyān nivartanaśataṃ budhaḥ ||

	vidhinānena tasyāśu kṣīyate pāpasaṃhatiḥ |

	tadardham atha vā dadyād api gocarmamātrakam ||

	bhavanasthānamātraṃ so 'pi pāpaiḥ pramucyate |

	yāvanti lāṅgalakamārgamukhāni bhūmes tāsāṃ pater duhituraṅgajaromakāṇi |

	tāvanti śaṃkarapure sa samāni tiṣṭhed bhūmipradānam iha yaḥ kurute manuṣyaḥ ||

	gandharvakiṃnarasurāsurasiddhasaṃghair ādhūtacāmaram upetya mahad vimānam |

	saṃpūjyate pitṛpitāmahabandhuyuktaḥ śaṃbhoḥ puraṃ vrajati cāmaranāyakaḥ san ||

	nendratvam apy adhigataṃ kṣayam abhyupaiti gobhūmilāṅgaladhuraṃdharasaṃpradānāt |

	tasmād aghaughapaṭalakṣayakāri bhūmer dānaṃ vidheyam atibhūtibhavābhavāya ||

iti mātsye pañcalāṅgalakapradānam |

	matsya uvāca |

	athātaḥ saṃpravakṣyāmi dharādānam anuttamam |

	pāpakṣayakaraṃ nṝṇām amaṅgalyavināśanam ||

	kārayet pṛthivīṃ haimīṃ jambudvīpānukāriṇīm |

	maryādāparvatamayīṃ madhye merusamanvitām ||

	lokapālāṣṭakopetāṃ navavarṣasamāyutām |

	nadīnadaśatopetāṃ saptasāgaraveṣṭitām ||

	mahāratnasamākīrṇāṃ vasurudrārkasaṃyutām |

	hemnaḥ palasahasreṇa tadardhenātha śaktitaḥ ||

	śatatrayeṇa vā kuryād dviśatena śatena vā |

	kuryāt pañcapalād ūrdhvam aśakto 'pi vicakṣaṇaḥ ||

**[337]**	tulāpuruṣavat kuryāl lokeśāvāhanaṃ budhaḥ |

	ṛtvigmaṇḍalasaṃbhārabhūṣaṇācchādanādikam ||

	vedyāṃ kṛṣṇājinaṃ kṛtvā tilān upari vinyaset |

	tathāṣṭādaśa dhānyāni rasāṃś ca lavaṇādikān ||

	tathāṣṭau pūrṇakalaśān samantāt parikalpayet |

	vitānakaṃ ca kauśeyaṃ phalāni vividhāni ca ||

	tathāṃśukāni ramyāṇi śrīkhaṇḍaśakalāni ca |

	ity evaṃ racayitvā tām adhivāsanapūrvakam ||

	śuklamālyāmbaradharaḥ śuklābharaṇabhūṣitaḥ |

	pradakṣiṇaṃ tataḥ kṛtvā gṛhītakusumāñjaliḥ ||

	puṇyakālam athāsādya mantrān etān udāharet |

	oṃ namas te sarvadevānāṃ tvam eva bhavanaṃ yataḥ ||

	dhātrī ca sarvabhūtānām ataḥ pāhi vasuṃdhare |

	vasūn dhārayate yasmād vasudhā tena nirmalā ||

	vasuṃdharā tato jātā tasmāt pāhi bhayād alam |

	caturmukho 'pi no gacched yasmād antaṃ tavācale ||

	anantāyai namas tasmāt pāhi saṃsārakardamāt |

	tvam eva lakṣmīr govinde śive gaurīti saṃsthitā ||

	gāyatrī brahmaṇaḥ pārśve jyotsnā candre ravau prabhā |

	buddhir bṛhaspatau khyātā medhā muniṣu saṃsthitā ||

	viśvaṃ vyāpya sthitā yasmāt tato viśvaṃbharā matā |

	sthitir dhṛtiḥ kṣamā kṣoṇī pṛthvī vasumatī rasā |

	etābhir mūrtibhiḥ pāhi devi saṃsārasāgarāt ||

	evam uccārya tāṃ devīṃ brāhmaṇebhyo nivedayet |

	dharārdhaṃ vā caturbhāgaṃ gurave pratipādayet ||

	śeṣaṃ caivātha ṛtvigbhyaḥ praṇipatya visarjayet |

	anena vidhinā yas tu dadyād dhemadharāṃ budhaḥ ||

	puṇyakāle tu saṃprāpte sa padaṃ yāti vaiṣṇavam |

	vimānenārkavarṇena kiṅkiṇījālamālinā ||

**[338]**	nārāyaṇapuraṃ gatvā kalpatrayam atho vaset |

	pitṛpautraprapautrāṃś ca tārayed ekaviṃśatiḥ(tim) ||

	iti paṭhati ya itthaṃ yaḥ śṛṇoti prasaṅgād api kaluṣavitānair yuktadehaḥ samantāt |

	divam amaravadhūbhir yāti sa pārthyamānaḥ padam amarasahasraiḥ sevitaṃ candramaulaiḥ ||

iti mātsye haimapṛthvīdānam |

	matsya uvāca |

	athātaḥ saṃpravakṣyāmi mahādānam anuttamam |

	viśvacakram iti khyātaṃ mahāpātakanāśanam ||

	tapanīyasya śuddhasya viśvacakraṃ ca kārayet |

	śreṣṭhaṃ palasahasreṇa tadardhena tu madhyamam ||

	tasyārdhena kaniṣṭhaṃ syād viśvacakram udāhṛtam |

	anyad viṃśapalād ūrdhvam aśakto 'pi nivedayet ||

	ṣoḍaśāraṃ tataś cakraṃ bhūṣaṇair aṣṭadhāvṛtam |

	nābhipadme sthitaṃ viṣṇuṃ yogārūḍhaṃ caturbhujam ||

	śaṅkhapadmau ca pārśve tu devyaṣṭakasamāvṛtam |

	dvitīyāvaraṇe tadvat pūrvato jalaśāyinam ||

	atrir bhṛgur vasiṣṭhaś ca brahmā kaśyapa eva ca |

	matsyaḥ kūrmo varāhaś ca narasiṃho 'tha vāmanaḥ ||

	rāmo rāmaś ca kṛṣṇaś ca buddhaḥ kalkīti ca kramāt |

	tṛtīyāvaraṇe gaurī mātṛbhir vasubhir vṛtā ||

	caturthe dvādaśādityā vedāś catvāra eva ca |

	pañcame pañca bhūtāni rudrāś caikādaśaiva tu ||

	lokapālāṣṭakaṃ ṣaṣṭhe diṅmātaṅgāṃs tathaiva ca |

	saptame 'strāṇi sarvāṇi maṅgalyāni ca kārayet ||

	antarāntarato devān vinyased aṣṭame punaḥ |

	tulāpuruṣavat sarvaṃ samantāt parikalpayet ||

	ṛtvigmaṇḍalasaṃbhārabhūṣaṇācchādanādikam |

	viśvacakraṃ tataḥ kuryāt kṛṣṇājinatilopari ||

	tathāṣṭādaśa dhānyāni rasāś ca lavaṇādayaḥ |

**[339]**	pūrṇakumbhāṣṭakaṃ caiva vastrāṇi vividhāni ca ||

	mālyekṣuphalaratnāni vitānaṃ caiva kalpayet |

	tato maṅgalaśabdena snātaḥ śuklāmbaro gṛhī ||

	homādhivāsanānte tu gṛhītakusumāñjaliḥ |

	imam uccārayen mantraṃ triḥ kṛtvātha pradakṣiṇam ||

	namo viśvamāyāyeti viśvacakrātmane namaḥ |

	paramānandarūpī tvaṃ pāhi naḥ pāpakardamāt ||

	tejomayam idaṃ yasmāt sadā paśyanti yoginaḥ |

	tad idaṃ triguṇātītaṃ viśvacakraṃ namāmy aham ||

	vāsudeve sthitaṃ cakraṃ cakramadhye ca mādhavaḥ |

	anyonyādhārarūpeṇa praṇamāmi sthitāv iha ||

	cakraṃ. viśvamayaṃ yasmāt sarvapāpaharaṃ hareḥ |

	āyudhaṃ cāpi vāsaś ca bhavād uddhara mām ataḥ ||

	ity āmantrya ca yo dadyād viśvacakram amatsaraḥ |

	vimuktaḥ sarvapāpebhyo viṣṇuloke mahīyate ||

	vaikuṇṭhalokam āsādya caturbāhuḥ sanātanaḥ |

	sevyate 'psarasāṃ saṃghair vaset kalpaśatatrayam ||

	praṇamed vā svayaṃ kṛtvā viśvacakraṃ dine dine |

	tasyāyur vardhate nityaṃ lakṣmīś ca vipulā bhavet ||

	iti sakalajagatsurādhivāsaṃ vitarati yas tapanīyaṣoḍaśāram |

	haribhavanam upāgataḥ sa siddhaiś ciram abhigamya nasyate śirobhiḥ ||

	asudarśanatāṃ prayāti śatror madanasudarśanatāṃ ca kāminīnām |

	sa sudarśanakeśavānurūpaḥ kanakasudarśanadānadagdhapāpaḥ ||

	kṛtaguruduritāriṣoḍaśārapravitaraṇapravarākṛtir murāreḥ |

	abhibhavati bhavodbhavāni bhittvā bhavam abhito bhavane bhayāni bhūyaḥ ||

iti mātsya viśvacakradānam |

	matsya ucāca |

	athātaḥ saṃpravakṣyāmi mahādānam anuttamam |

	mahākalpalatā nāma pātakāvalināśanam ||

**[340]**	puṇyāṃ tithiṃ samāsādya kṛtvā brāhmaṇavācanam |

	ṛtvigmaṇḍalasaṃsārabhūṣaṇācchādanādikam ||

	tulāpuruṣavat kuryāl lokeśāvāhanādikam |

	cāmīkaramayīḥ kuryād daśa kalpalatāḥ śubhāḥ ||

	nānāpuṣpaphalopetā nānāṃśukavibhūṣitāḥ |

	vidyādharasuvarṇānāṃ mithunair upaśobhitāḥ ||

	hārānāditsubhiḥ siddhaiḥ phalāni ca vihaṃgamaiḥ |

	lokapālānukāriṇyaḥ kartavyās tāsu devatāḥ ||

	brāhmīm anantaśaktiṃ tāṃ lavaṇasyopari nyaset |

	adhastāl latayor madhye padmaśaṅkhakare śubhe ||

	ibhāsanasthā ca guḍe pūrvataḥ kuliśāyudhā |

	ajenāvasthitāgneyī sruvapāṇirathānale ||

	yābhyāṃ mahiṣam ārūḍhā daṇḍinī taṇḍulopari |

	ghṛtena nairṛtī sthāpyā sakhaḍgā dakṣiṇāpare ||

	vāruṇī vāruṇe kṣīre ūṣasthā nāgapāśinī |

	patākinī ca vāyavye mṛgasthā śarkaropari ||

	saumyā tileṣu saṃsthāpyā śaṅkhinī nidhisaṃsthitā |

	māheśvarī vṛṣagatā navanīte triśūlinī ||

	mālinyo varadās tadvat kartavyā bālakānvitāḥ |

	śaktyā pañcapalād ūrdhvam ā sahasrāt prakalpayet ||

	sarvāsām upariṣṭāc ca pañcavarṇaṃ vitānakam |

	dhenavo daśa kumbhāś ca vastrayugmāni(ṇi) caive hi ||

	saṃnyased dve ca gurave ṛtvigbhyo 'nyās tathaiva ca |

	tato maṅgalaśabdena snātaḥ śukāmbaro budhaḥ ||

	triḥ pradakṣiṇam āvṛtya mantrāṃś caitān udāharet |

	namo namaḥ pāpavināśinībhyo brahmāṇḍalokeśvarapālinībhyaḥ |

	āśaṃsitādhikyaphalapradābhyo digbhyas tathā kalpalatāvadhūbhyaḥ ||

	iti sakaladigaṅganāpradānaṃ bhavabhavasūdanakāri yaḥ karoti |

**[341]**	abhimataphalade sa nāgaloke vasati pitāmahavatsarāṇi viṃśat ||

	pitṛśatam api tārayed bhavābdher guruduritaughavidhātaśuddhadehaḥ |

	suravaravanitāsahasrasaṃghaiḥ parivṛtam ambujasaṃbhavābhinandyam ||

	iti vidhānam idaṃ sadigaṅganākanakakalpalatāvinivedane |

	paṭhati yaḥ smaratīha tathekṣate sa padam eti puraṃdarasevitam ||

iti mātsye kalpalatādānam |

	matsya uvāca |

	athātaḥ saṃpravakṣyāmi mahāpātaknāśanam |

	saptasāgarakaṃ nāma sarvapāpapraṇāśanam ||

	puṇyaṃ dinaṃ samāsādya kṛtvā brāhmaṇavācanam |

	tulāpuruṣavat kuryāl lokeśāvāhanaṃ budhaḥ ||

	ṛtvigmaṇḍalasaṃbhārabhūṣaṇācchādanādikam |

	kāreyet sapta kuṇḍāni kāñcanāni vicakṣaṇaḥ ||

	prādeśamātrāṇi tathāratnimātrāṇi vā punaḥ |

	kuryāt saptapalād ūrdhvam ā sahasrāc ca śaktitaḥ ||

	saṃsthāpyāni ca sarvāṇi pūrṇāni ca tilopari |

	prathamaṃ pūrayet kuṇḍaṃ lavaṇena vicakṣaṇaḥ ||

	dvitīyaṃ payasā tadvat tṛtīyaṃ sarpiṣā punaḥ |

	caturthaṃ ca guḍenaiva dadhnā pañcamam eva ca ||

	ṣaṣṭhaṃ śarkarayā tadvat saptamaṃ tīrthavāriṇā |

	snāpayel lavaṇasyāntar brahmāṇaṃ kāñcanaṃ śubham ||

	keśavaṃ kṣīramadhye tu ghṛtamadhye maheśvaram |

	bhāskaraṃ guḍamadhye tu dadhimadhye 'marādhipam ||

	śarkarāyāṃ nyasel lakṣmīṃ jalamadhye tu pārvatīm |

	sarveṣu sarvaratnāni dhānyāni ca samantataḥ ||

	tulāpuruṣavac cheṣam atrāpi parikalpayet |

	tato vāruṇahomānte snāpito vedapuṃgavaiḥ ||

	triḥ pradakṣiṇam āvṛtya mantrān etān udāharet |

	namo vaḥ sarvasindhūnām ādhārebhyaḥ sanātanāḥ ||

	jantūnāṃ sthānadebhyaś ca samudrebhyo namo namaḥ |

**[342]**	kṣīrodakājyadadhimādhavalāvaṇekṣusārāmṛtena bhuvanatrayajīvasāṃghān |

	ānandayanti vasubhiś ca yato bhavantas tasmān mamāpy aghavighātam alaṃ diśantu ||

	yasmāt samastabhuvaneṣu bhavanta eva tīrthāmarāsurasugandhimaṇipratānam |

	pāpakṣayādhvaravilepanabhūṣaṇāya lokasya bibhrati tato 'stu mamāpi lakṣmīḥ ||

	iti dadāti rasāmarasaṃyutān suciravismayavān iha sāgarān |

	amalakāñcanaratnacayān asau padam upaiti harer amarārcitam ||

	sakalapāpavighātavirājitaṃ pitṛpitāmahaputraśatatrayam |

	narakalokasamākulam apy alaṃ jhagi(ṭi)ti netum asau śivamandiram ||

iti mātsya saptasāgaradānam |

	matsya uvāca |

	athātaḥ saṃpravakṣyāmi mahādānam anuttamam |

	ratnadhenur iti khyātaṃ golokaphaladaṃ nṛṇām ||

	puṇyāṃ tithiṃ samāsādya tulāpuruṣadānavat |

	lokeśāvāhanaṃ kṛtvā ratnadhenuṃ prakalpayet ||

	bhūmau kṛṣṇājinaṃ kṛtvā lavaṇadroṇasaṃyutam |

	dhenuṃ ratnamayīṃ kuryāt saṃkalpavidhipūrvakam ||

	sthāpayet padmarāgāṇām ekāśītiṃ mukhe budhaḥ |

	puṣparāgaśataṃ tadvad ghoṇāyāṃ parikalpayet ||

	lalāṭe haimatilakaṃ muktāphalaśataṃ dṛśoḥ |

	bhrūyuge vidrumaśataṃ śuktī karṇadvayaṃ smṛtam ||

	kāñcanāni ca śṛṅgāṇi śiro vajraśatātmakam |

	grīvāyāṃ netrapuṭakaṃ gomedakaśatātmakam ||

	indranīlaśataṃ pṛṣṭhe vaiḍū(dū)ryaśatapārśvakau |

	sphaṭikaṃ codare tadvat saugandhikaśatān (t) kaṭiḥ ||

	khurā hemamayāḥ kāryāḥ pucchaṃ muktāvalīmayam |

	sūryakāntendukāntānāṃ prāṇe karpūracandanam ||

	kauṅkumāni ca romāṇi nābhiṃ raupyāṃ ca kalpayet |

	gārutmataśataṃ tadvad apāne parikalpayet ||

	athānyāni ca ratnāni sthāpayet sarvasaṃdhiṣu |

	kuryāc charkarayā jihvāṃ gomayaṃ ca guḍātmakam ||

**[343]**	gomūtram ājyena tathā dadhidugdhaṃ svarūpataḥ |

	pucchāgre camaraṃ dadyāt samīpe tāmradohanam ||

	kuṇḍalāni ca haimāni bhūṣaṇāni svaśaktitaḥ |

	kārayed evam evaṃ tu caturthāṃśena vatsakam ||

	tathā dhānyāni sarvāṇi pādāś cekṣumayāḥ śubhāḥ |

	nānā phalāni sarvāṇi pañcavarṇaṃ vitānakam ||

	evaṃ viracanāṃ kṛtvā tadvad dhomādikaṃ param |

	ṛtvigbhyo dakṣiṇāṃ datvā dhenum āmantrayet tataḥ ||

	guḍadhenuvad āvāhya imaṃ codāharet tataḥ |

	tvāṃ sarvadevagaṇadhāma yataḥ paṭhanti rudrendrasomakamalāsanavāsudevāḥ |

	tasmāt samastabhuvanatrayadevayukte māṃ pāhi devi bhavasāgarapīḍyamānam ||

	āmantrya cettham abhitaḥ parivṛtya bhaktyā dadyād dvijāya gurave jalapūrvakaṃ tām |

	yaḥ puṇyam āpya dinam atra kṛtopavāsaḥ pāpaiḥ sa muktatanur eti padaṃ murāreḥ ||

	iti sakalavidhijño ratnadhenupradānaṃ vitarati sa vimānaṃ prāpya dedīpyamānam |

	sakalakaluṣamukto bandhubhiḥ putrapautraiḥ saha madanasarūpaḥ sthānam abhyeti śaṃbhoḥ ||

iti mātsye ratnadhenuvidhānam |

	matsya uvāca |

	athātaḥ saṃpravakṣyāmi mahādānam anuttamam |

	mahābhūtaghaṭaṃ nāma mahāpātakanāśanam ||

	puṇyāṃ tithim athāsādya kṛtvā brāhmaṇavācanam |

	ṛtvigmaṇḍapasaṃbhārabhūṣaṇācchādanādikam ||

	tulāpuruṣavat kāryaṃ lokeśāvāhanādikam |

	kārayet kāñcanaṃ kumbhaṃ mahāratnacitaṃ śubham ||

	prādeśād aṅgulaśataṃ yāvat kuryāt pramāṇataḥ |

	kṣīrājyapūritaṃ tac ca kalpavṛkṣasamanvitam ||

	padmāsanagatāṃs tadvad brahmaviṣṇumaheśvarān |

	varāheṇoddhṛtāṃ tadvat kuryād bhūmiṃ saparvatām ||

	varuṇaṃ cāsanagataṃ kāñcanaṃ makaropari |

	hutāśanaṃ meṣagataṃ vāyuṃ mṛgakṛtāsanam ||

	tathākāśādhipaṃ kuryān mūṣakasthaṃ vināyakam |

	vinyased ghaṭamadhye tān vedapañcakasaṃyutān ||

**[344]**	ṛgvedasyākṣasūtraṃ syād yajurvedasya paṅkajam |

	sāmavedasya vīṇā syād dhenuṃ dhakṣiṇato nyaset ||

	atharvavedasya punaḥ sruksruvau kamalaṃ kare |

	purāṇavedo varadaḥ sākṣasūtrakamaṇḍaluḥ ||

	paritaḥ sarvadhānyāni cāmarāsanadarpaṇam |

	pādukopānahacchatradīpapkā bhūṣaṇāni ca ||

	śayyātha jalakumbhaś ca pañcavarṇaṃ vitānakam |

	snātvādhivāsanānte tu mantram etad (m) udīrayet ||

	namo vaḥ sarvadevānām ādhārebhyaś carācare |

	mahābhūtādidevebhyaḥ śāntir astu śivaṃ mama ||

	yasmān na kiṃcid apy asti mahābhūtair vinā kṛtam |

	brahmāṇḍe sarvabhūtānāṃ tasmāc chrīr akṣayāstu me ||

	ity uccārya mahābhūtaghaṭaṃ yo vinivedayet |

	sarvapāpavinirmuktaḥ prayāti paramāṃ gatim ||

	vimānenārkavarṇena pitṛbandhusamanvitaḥ |

	stūyamāno varastrībhiḥ padam abhyeti vaiṣṇavam ||

	ṣoḍaśaitāni ya kuryān mahādānāni mānavaḥ |

	na tasya punar āvṛttir iha loke 'bhijāyate ||

	iti paṭhati ya itthaṃ vāsudevasya pārśve sasutapitṛkalatraḥ saṃśṛṇotīha samyak |

	puraripubhavane vai mandire cārkalakṣmyor amarapuravadhūbhir modate so'pi kalpam ||

iti mātsya mahābhūtaghaṭadānam |

atha parvatadānāni |

matsyapurāṇe |

	umāpatir uvāca

	merupradānaṃ vakṣyāmi daśadhā munisattama |

	yatpradānān naro lokān āpnoti surapūjitān ||

	purāṇeṣu ca vedeṣu kṛteṣv eṣu yad aśnute |

	tasmād vidhānaṃ vakṣyāmi parvatānām anukramāt ||

	prathamo dhānyaśailaḥ syād dvitīyo lavanācalaḥ |

	guḍācalas tṛtīyas tu caturtho hemaparvataḥ ||

	pañcamas tilaśailaḥ syāt ṣaṣṭhaḥ kārpāsaparvataḥ |

	saptamo ghṛtaśailaḥ syād ratnaśailas tathāṣṭamaḥ ||

**[345]**	rājato namas tadvad daśamaḥ śarkarācalaḥ |

	vakṣye vidhānam eteṣāṃ yathāvad anupūrvaśaḥ ||

	ayane viṣuve puṇye vyatīpāte dinakṣaye |

	kṛṣṇapakṣe tṛtīyāyām uparāge śaśikṣaye ||

	vivāhotsavayajñeṣu dvādaśyām atha vā punaḥ |

	śuklāyāṃ pañcadaśyāṃ vā puṇyarkṣe vā vidhānataḥ ||

	dhānyaśailādayo deyā yathāśāstraṃ vidhānataḥ |

	tīrthe vāyatane vāpi goṣṭhe vā saṃgame 'pi vā ||

	maṇḍalaṃ kārayed bhaktyā caturaśram udaṅmukham |

	prāgudakpravaṇaṃ tadvat prāṅmukhaṃ vā vidhānataḥ ||

	gomayenopaliptāyāṃ bhūmāv āstīrya vā kuśān |

	tanmadhye parvataṃ kuryād viṣkambhaiḥ parvatair yutam ||

	dhānyadroṇasahasreṇa bhaved girir ihottamaḥ |

	madhyamaḥ pañcaśatikaḥ kaniṣṭhaḥ syāt tibhiḥ śataiḥ \\

	merur mahāvrīhimayas tu madhye suvarṇavṛkṣatrayasaṃyutaḥ syāt |

	pūrveṇa muktāphalavajrayukto yāmyena gomedakapuṣparāgaiḥ ||

	paścāc ca gārutmatanīlaratnaiḥ saumyena vaiḍū(dū)ryasarojanālaiḥ |

	śrīkhaṇḍakhaṇḍair abhitaḥ pravālalatānvitaiḥ śuktiśilātalaḥ syāt ||

	brahmā ca viṣṇur bhagavān purārir divākaro 'py atra hiraṇmayaḥ syāt |

	mūrdhni vyavasthānam amatsareṇa kāryaṃ suvarṇena tathā dvijaughaiḥ ||

	catvāri śṛṅgāṇi ca rājatāni nitambabhāgeṣv api rājataḥ syāt |

	tathekṣuvaṃśāvṛtakandaraś ca ghṛtodakaprasravaṇaś ca dikṣu ||

	śuklāmbarāṇy ambudharāvalī syāt pūrveṇa pītāni ca dakṣiṇena |

	vāsāṃsi paścād atha karburāṇi raktāni caivottarato ghanālī ||

	raupyān mahendrapramukhāṃs tathāṣṭau saṃsthāpya lokādhipatīn krameṇa |

	nānāphalālī ca samantataḥ syān manoramaṃ mālyavilepanaṃ ca ||

	vitānakaṃ copari pañcavarṇam amlānapuṣpābharaṇaṃ sitaṃ ca |

	itthaṃ nivedyāmaraśailam agryaṃ taṃ kāñcanenātivirājamānam ||

**[346]**	tatas tu viṣkambhagirīn krameṇa turīyabhāgeṇa caturdiśaṃ ca |

	saṃsthāpayet puṣpavilepanāḍhyān manoramān vastragaṇāvṛtāṃś ca ||

	yuktaṃ yavaiḥ karabhabhadrakadambacihnaṃ kāmena kāñcanamayena virājamānam |

	taṃ kārayet kusumavastravilepanāḍhyaṃ kṣīrāruṇodasarasā ca vanena caiva ||

	raupyeṇa śuktighaṭitena virājamānaṃ yāmyena gandhamadano 'tra niveśanīyaḥ |

	godhūmasaṃcayamayaḥ kaladhautajo vā haimena yakṣapatinā ghṛtamānasena ||

	vastraiś ca rājatavanena ca saṃyutaḥ syāt paścāc ca mainākatilācalaṃ ca |

	sugandhadhūpena vilepanena puṣpotkarair maṇḍitavigrahābham ||

	sauvarṇapippalahiraṇmayasaṃprayuktam ākārayed rajatapuṣpavanena tadvat |

	vastrānvitaṃ dadhisitodasaras tathāgre saṃsthāpya taṃ vipulaśailam athottareṇa ||

	śailaṃ svapārśvam api dhātumayaṃ suvastraṃ vinyāsabhūṣitamahākṛtisaṃniveśam |

	puṣpaiś ca hemavaṭapādapaśekharaṃ tam ākārayet kanakadhenuvirājamānam ||

	sākṣīkabhadrasurasāvasanena tadvad raupyeṇa bhāsuravatā ca yutaṃ vihāya |

	homaṃ caturbhir atha vedapurāṇavidbhir mānyair anindyacaritākṛtibhir dvijendraiḥ ||

	pūrveṇa hastimukhavac ca vidhāya kuṇḍaṃ kāryas tilair yavaghṛtena samitkuśaiś ca |

	rātrau ca jāgaram anuddhatagītatūryair āvāhanaṃ ca kathayāmi śiloccayānām ||

	tvaṃ sarvadevagaṇadhāmanidhe viruddham asmadgṛheṣv amaraparvata nāśayāśu |

	tvam eva bhagavān īśo brahmā viṣṇur divākaraḥ |

	mūrtāmūrtaṃ paraṃ bījam ataḥ pāhi sanātanaḥ ||

	yasmāt tvaṃ lokapālānāṃ viśvamūrteś ca mandiram |

	rudrādityavasūnāṃ ca tasmāc chāntiṃ prayaccha me ||

	yasmād aśūnyam amarair nārībhiś ca śiras tava |

	tasmān mām uddharāśeṣaduḥkhasaṃsārasāgarāt ||

	evam abhyarcitaṃ meruṃ mandaraṃ cābhipūjayet |

	yasmāc caitrarathena tvaṃ bhadrāśvavariṣeṇa ca ||

	śobhase mandara kṣipram atas tuṣṭikaro bhava |

	yasmāc cūḍāmaṇir jambudvīpe tvaṃ gandhamādana ||

	gandharvavanaśobhāvān ataḥ kīrtir dṛḍhāstu me |

	yasmāt tvaṃ ketumālena vaibhrājena vanena ca ||

	hiraṇmayaiś ca śikharais tasmāt puṣṭir dhruvāstu me |

	uttaraiḥ kurubhir yasmāt sāvitreṇa vanena ca ||

	supārśva rājase nityam ataḥ śrīrakṣayāstu me |

	evam āmantrya tān sarvān prabhāte vimale punaḥ ||

	snātvātha gurave dadyān madhyamaṃ parvatottamam |

	viṣkambhaparvatān paścād ṛtvigbhyaḥ kramaśo mune ||

	gāś ca dadyāc caturviṃśad atha vā daśa nārada |

	śaktitaḥ sapta vāṣṭau vā pañca dadyād aśaktimān ||

	ekāṃ vā gurave dadyāt kapilāṃ ca payasvinīm |

	parvatānām aśeṣāṇām eṣa eva vidhiḥ smṛtaḥ ||

	ta eva pūjane viprās ta evopaskarāḥ smṛtāḥ |

	grahaṇaṃ lokapālānāṃ brahmādīnāṃ ca sarvadā ||

	svamantreṇaiva sarveṣu homaḥ śaileṣu paṭhyate |

	upavāsī bhaven nityam aśaktau naktam iṣyate ||

	vidhānaṃ sarvaśailānāṃ kramaśaḥ śṛṇu nārada |

	dānakāleṣu ye mantrāḥ parvateṣu ca yat phalam ||

	annaṃ brahma yataḥ proktam annaṃ prāṇāḥ prakīrtitāḥ |

	annād bhavanti bhūtāni jagad annena vartate ||

	annam eva yato lakṣmīr annam eva janārdanaḥ |

	dhānyaparvatarūpeṇa pāhi tasmān nagottama ||

	anena vidhinā yas tu dadyād dhānyamayaṃ girim |

	manvantaraśataṃ sāgraṃ devaloke mahīyate ||

	apsarogaṇagandharvair ākīrṇena virājatā |

	vimānena divaḥ pṛṣṭham āyāti ṛṣisevitaḥ ||

	karmakṣaye rājarājyam āpnotīha na saṃśayaḥ ||

iti dhānyaparvatadānam |

**[348]**

	matsya uvāca |

	athātaḥ saṃpravakṣyāmi lavaṇācalam uttamam |

	yatpradānān naro lokān āpnoti śivasaṃmatān ||

	uttamaḥ ṣoḍaśadroṇaḥ kartavyo lavaṇācalaḥ |

	madhyamaḥ syāt tadardhena caturbhir avamaḥ smṛtaḥ ||

	vittahīno yathā śaktyā dronād ūrdhvaṃ tu kārayet |

	caturthāṃśena viṣkambhaparvatān kārayet pṛthak ||

	vidhānaṃ pūrvavat kuryād brahmādīnāṃ ca sarvadā |

	tadvad dhemamayān sarvāṃl lokapālān niveśayet ||

	sarāṃsi kāmadevādīṃs tadvac cātra niveśayet |

	kuryāj jāgaram atrāpi dānamantrān nibodha me ||

	saubhāgyarasasaṃbhūto yato 'yaṃ lavaṇācalaḥ |

	tadātmakatvena ca māṃ pāhi pāpān nagottama ||

	yasmād annarasāḥ sarve notkaṭā lavaṇaṃ vinā |

	priyaṃ ca śivayor nityaṃ tasmāc chāntiṃ prayaccha me ||

	viṣṇudehasamudbhūtaṃ yasmād ārogyavardhanam |

	tasmāt parvatarūpeṇa pāhi saṃsārasāgarāt ||

	anena vidhinā yas tu dadyāl lavaṇaparvatam |

	umāloke vaset kalpaṃ tato yāti parāṃ gatim ||

iti lavaṇaparvatadānam |

	athātaḥ saṃpravakṣyāmi guḍaparvatam uttamam |

	yatpradānān naraḥ śrīmān svargam āpnoti pūjitaḥ ||

	uttamo daśabhir bhārair madhyamaḥ pañcabhir mataḥ |

	tribhir bhāraiḥ kaniṣṭhaḥ syāt tadardhenālpavittavān ||

	tadvad āmantraṇaṃ pūjā hemavṛkṣasurārcanam ||

	viṣkambhaparvatāṃs tadval lokapālādhivāsanam |

	dhānyaparvatavat kuryād imaṃ mantram udīrayet ||

	yathā deveṣu viśvātmā pravaro 'yaṃ janārdanaḥ |

	sāmavedas tu vedānāṃ mahādevas tu yoginām ||

	praṇavaḥ sarvamantrāṇāṃ nārīṇāṃ pārvatī yathā |

**[349]**	tathā rasānāṃ pravaraḥ sadaivekṣuraso mataḥ ||

	mama tasmāt parāṃ lakṣmīṃ dadasva guḍaparvata |

	surāsurāṇāṃ sarveṣāṃ nāgayakṣarkṣapakṣiṇām ||

	nivāsaś cāpi pārvatyās tasmān māṃ pāhi sarvadā ||

	anena vidhinā yas tu dadyād guḍamayaṃ girim |

	pūjyamānaḥ sa gandharvair gaurīloke mahīyate ||

	punaḥ kalpaśatānte tu saptadvīpādhipo bhavet |

	āyurārogyasaṃpannaḥ śatrubhiś ca parājitaḥ ||

iti guḍaparvatadānam |

	athātaḥ saṃpravakṣyāmi hiraṇyācalam uttamam |

	yasya pradānād bhavanaṃ vairiñcaṃ yāti mānavaḥ ||

	uttamaḥ palasāhasro madhyamaḥ pañcabhiḥ śataiḥ |

	tadardhenāvaras tadvad alpavitto 'pi śaktitaḥ ||

	dadyād ekapalād ūrdhvaṃ yathā śaktyā vimatsaraḥ |

	dhānyaparvatavat sarvaṃ vadadhyān munipuṃgava ||

	viṣkambhaśailāṃs tadvac ca kṛtvā mantram udīrayet |

	namas te brahmabījāya brahmagarbhāya vai namaḥ ||

	yasmād anantaphaladas tasmāt pāhi śiloccaya |

	yadmād agner apatyaṃ tvaṃ yasmād ulbaṃ jagatpateḥ ||

	hemaparvatarūpeṇa tasmāt pāhi namo namaḥ |

	anena vidhinā yas tu dadyāt kanakaparvatam ||

	sa yāti paramaṃ sthānaṃ brāhmamānandakāram (?) |

	tatra kalpaśataṃ tiṣṭhet tato yāti parāṃ gatim ||

iti suvarṇaparvatadānam |

	athātaḥ saṃpravakṣyāmi tilaśailaṃ vidhānataḥ |

	yat pradānān naro yāti viṣṇulokam anuttamam ||

	uttamo daśabhir droṇair madhyamaḥ pañcabhir mataḥ |

	tribhiḥ kaniṣṭho viprendra tilaśailaḥ prakīrtitaḥ ||

**[350]**	pūrvavac cāparaṃ sarvaṃ viṣkambhaparvatādikam |

	dānamantraṃ pravakṣyāmi yathāvan munipuṃgava ||

	yasmān madhuvadhe viṣṇor dehasvedasamudbhavāḥ |

	tilā mudgāś ca māṣāś ca tasmāc chaṃ no bhavatv iha ||

	havyakavyeṣu yasmāc ca tilair evābhirakṣaṇam |

	bhavād uddhara śailendra tilācala namo 'stu te ||

	ity āmantrya ca yo dadyāt tilācalam anuttamam |

	sa vaiṣṇavapadaṃ yāti punarāvṛttidurlabham ||

	dīrghāyuṣyam avāpnoti iha cāmutra mānavaḥ |

	pitṛbhir devagandharvaiḥ pūjyamāno divaṃ vrajet ||

iti tilaparvatadānam |

	kārpāsaparvatas tadvad viṃśadbhārair ihottamaḥ |

	daśabhir madhyamaḥ proktaḥ kaniṣṭhaḥ pañcabhir mataḥ ||

	bhāreṇālpadhano dadyād vittaśāṭhyavivarjitaḥ |

	dhānaparvatavat sarvam āsādya munipuṃgava ||

	prabhātāyāṃ tu śarvaryāṃ dadyād idam udīrayet |

	tvam evāvaraṇaṃ yasmāl lokānām iha sarvadā ||

	karpāsācala tasmāt tvam aghaughadhvaṃsano bhava |

	evaṃ kārpāsaśailendraṃ yo dadyāt parvasaṃnidhau ||

	rudraloke vaset kalpaṃ tato rājā bhaved iha ||

iti kārpāsaparvatadānam |

	athātaḥ saṃpravakṣyāmi ghṛtācalam anuttamam |

	tejomṛtamayaṃ divyaṃ mahāpātakanāśanam ||

	viṃśatyā ghṛtakumbhānām uttamaḥ syād ghṛtācalaḥ |

	daśabhir madhyamaḥ proktaḥ pañcabhis tv avaraḥ smṛtaḥ ||

	alpavitto 'pi yaḥ kuryād dvābhyām iha vidhānataḥ |

	viṣkambhaparvatāṃs tadvac caturbhāgena kalpayet ||

	śālitaṇḍulapātrāṇi kumbhopari niveśayet |

	kārayet saṃhatān uccān yathāśobhaṃ vidhānataḥ ||

**[351]**	veṣṭayec chuklavāsobhir ikṣudaṇḍaphalādibhiḥ |

	dhānyaparvatavac cheṣaṃ vidhānam iha paṭhyate ||

	adhivāsanapūrvaṃ tu tadvad dhomasurārcanam |

	prabhātāyāṃ vibhāvaryāṃ gurave tu nivedayet ||

	viṣkambhaparvatāṃs tadvad ṛtvigbhyaḥ śāntamānasaḥ |

	saṃyogād ghṛtam utpannaṃ yasmād amṛtatejasoḥ ||

	tasmād ghṛtārcirviśvātmā prīyatāṃ mama śaṃkaraḥ |

	yasmāt tejomayaṃ brahma ghṛte tac ca vyavasthitam ||

	ghṛtaparvatarūpeṇa tasmān naḥ pāhi bhūdhara |

	anena vidhinā dadyād ghṛtaparvatam uttamam ||

	mahāpātakayukto 'pi lokam āyāti śaṃkaram |

	haṃsasārasayuktena kiṃkiṇījālamālinā ||

	vimānenāpsarobhiś ca siddhavidyādharair vṛtaḥ |

	viharet pitṛbhiḥ sārdhaṃ yāvad ābhūmisaṃplavam ||

iti ghṛtaparvatadānam |

	athātaḥ saṃpravakṣyāmi ratnācalam anuttamam |

	muktāphalasahasreṇa parvataḥ syād anuttamaḥ ||

	madhyamaḥ pañcaśatiko dviśatenāvaraḥ smṛtaḥ |

	caturthāṃśena viṣkambhaparvatāḥ syuḥ samantataḥ ||

	pūrveṇa vajragomedair dakṣiṇenendranīlakaiḥ |

	puṣparāgayutaiḥ kāryo vidvadbhir gandhamādanaḥ ||

	vaiḍū(dū)ryavidrumaiḥ paścāt saṃmiśro vipulācalaḥ |

	padmarāgaiḥ sasauvarṇair uttareṇa ca vinyaset ||

	dhānyaparvatavat sarvatrāpi parikalpayet |

	tadvad āvāhanaṃ kṛtvā vṛkṣān vedāṃś ca kāñcanān ||

	pūjayet puṣpapānīyaiḥ prabhāte syād visarjanam |

	pūrvavad guruṛtvigbhya imān mantrān udīrayet ||

	yathā devagaṇāḥ sarve sarvaratneṣv avasthitāḥ |

	tvaṃ hi ratnamayo nityam ataḥ pāhi mahācala ||

**[352]**	yasmād ratnapradānena tuṣṭiṃ prakurute hariḥ |

	sadānandaprasādena tasmān naḥ pāhi bhūdhara ||

	anena vidhinā yas tu dadyād ratnamahāgirim |

	sa yāti vaiṣṇavaṃ lokam amareśvarapūjitaḥ ||

	yāvatkalpaśataṃ sāgraṃ vasitveha narādhipaḥ |

	rūpārogyaguṇopetaḥ saptadvīpādhipo bhavet ||

	brahmahatyādikaṃ kiṃcid yad atrāmutra vā kṛtam |

	tat sarvaṃ nāśam āyāti girir vajrahato yathā ||

iti ratnaparvatadānam |

	athātaḥ saṃpravakṣyāmi rūpyācalam anuttamam |

	yatpradānān naro yāti somalokaṃ narādhipa ||

	daśabhiḥ palasāhasrair uttamo rajatācalaḥ |

	pañcabhir madhyamaḥ proktas tadardhenāvaraḥ smṛtaḥ ||

	aśakto viṃśater ūrdhvaṃ kārayec chaktitaḥ sadā |

	viṣkambhaparvatāṃs tadvat turīyāṃśena kārayet ||

	pūrvavad rājatān kuryān mandarādīn vidhānataḥ |

	kaladhautamayāṃs tadval lokeśān arcayed budhaḥ ||

	brahmaviṣṇvarkavān kāryo nitambo 'tra hiraṇmayaḥ |

	rājataṃ syād yad anyeṣāṃ sarvaṃ tad iha kāñcanam ||

	śeṣaṃ ca pūrvavat kuryād dhomajāgaraṇādikam |

	dadyāt tadvat prabhāte tu gurave raupyaparvatam ||

	viṣkambhaśailān ṛtvigbhyaḥ prājyavastravibhūṣaṇān |

	imaṃ mantraṃ paṭhan dadyād darbhapāṇir vimatsaraḥ ||

	pitṝṇāṃ vallabhaṃ yasmād dharīndrāṇāṃ śivasya ca |

	rajataṃ pāhi tasmān naḥ śokasaṃsārasāgarāt ||

	itthaṃ nivedya yo dadyād rajatācalam uttamam |

	gavāyutasahasrasya phalam āpnoti mānavaḥ ||

	somaloke sa gandharvaiḥ kiṃnarāpsarasāṃ gaṇaiḥ |

	pūjyamāno vased vidvān yāvad ābhūtasaṃplavam ||

iti rajataparvatadānam |

**[353]**	athātaḥ saṃpravakṣyāmi śarkarācalam uttamam |

	yasya pradānād viṣṇvarkarudrās tuṣyanti sarvadā ||

	aṣṭabhiḥ śarkarābhārair uttamaḥ syān mahācalaḥ |

	caturbhir madhyamaḥ prokto bhārābhyām avaro mataḥ ||

	bhāreṇa vārdhabhāreṇa kuryād yaḥ svalpavittavān |

	viṣkambhaparvatān kuryāt turīyāṃśena mānavaḥ ||

	dhānyaparvatavat sarvam āsādyāmarasaṃyutam |

	meror upari tat tadvat sthāpyaṃ hematarutrayam ||

	mandāraḥ pārijātaś ca tṛtīyaḥ kalpapādapaḥ |

	etad vṛkṣatrayaṃ mūrdhni sarveṣv api niveśayet ||

	haricandanasaṃtānau pūrvapaścimabhāgayoḥ |

	niveśyau sarvaśaileṣu viśeṣāc charkarācale ||

	mandāre kāmadevas tu pratyagvaktraḥ sadā bhavet |

	gandhamādanaśṛṅge ca dhanadaḥ syād udaṅmukhaḥ ||

	prāṅmukho vedamūrtiś ca haṃsaḥ syād vipulācalaḥ |

	haimī supārśvasurabhī dakṣiṇābhimukhī bhavet ||

	dhānyaparvatavat sarvam āvāhanamakhādikam |

	kṛtvātha gurave dadyān madhyamaṃ parvatottamam ||

	ṛtvigbhyaś caturaḥ śailān imān mantrān udīrayet |

	saubhāgyāmṛtasāro 'yaṃ paramaḥ śarkarācalaḥ ||

	tasmād ānandakarī tvaṃ bhava śailendra sarvadā |

	amṛtaṃ pibatāṃ ye tu nipetur bhuvi śīkarāḥ ||

	devānāṃ tatsamuttho 'yaṃ pāhi naḥ śarkarācalaḥ |

	manobhavadhanur madhyād udgatā śarkarā yataḥ ||

	tanmayo 'pi mahāśaila pāhi saṃsārasāgarāt |

	yo dadyāc charkarāśailam anena vidhinā tataḥ ||

	sarvapāpavinirmuktaḥ sa yāti śivamandiram |

	candrādityāgnisaṃkāśam adhiruhyānujīvibhiḥ ||

	sahaiva yānam ātiṣṭhet sa tu viṣṇuprabho divam |

	tataḥ kalpaśatānte tu saptadvīpādhipo bhavet ||

**[354]**	āyurārogyasaṃpanno yāvajjanmārbudatrayam |

	bhojanaṃ śaiktitaḥ kuryāt sarvaśaileṣv amatsaraḥ ||

	sarvatra kṣāralavaṇam aśnīyāt tadanujñayā |

	parvatopaskarān sarvān prāpayed brāhmaṇālaye ||

	paśyed amūn mānadhano hi bhaktyā spṛśen manuṣyair iha dīyamānān |

	śṛṇoti bhaktvyātha matiṃ dadāti vikalmaṣaḥ so 'pi divaṃ prayāti ||

iti śarkarācaladānam |

atha kṛṣṇājinadānaṃ vicāryate | tatra viṣṇuḥ |


    atha vaiśākhyāṃ paurṇamāsyāṃ kṛṣṇājinaṃ sakhuraṃ suvarṇaśṛṅgaṃ rūpyakhuraṃ muktālāṅgūlabhūṣitaṃ kṛtvāvikavastre prasārayet | tatra tilaiḥ pracchādayet | suvarṇanābhaṃ ca kuryād ahatena vāsasor yugalena pracchādayet | sarvaratnagandhaiś cālaṃ kuryāt | catasṛṣu dikṣu catvāri taijasāni pātrāṇi kṣīradadhimadhusarpiḥpūrṇāni nidhāyāhitāgnaye brāhmaṇāyālaṃkṛtāya vāsoyugena pracchāditāya dadyāt | atha gāthā bhavanti |

	yas tu kṛṣṇājinaṃ dadyāt sakhuraṃ śṛṅgasaṃyutam |

	tilaiḥ pracchādya vāsobhiḥ sarvaratnair alaṃkṛtam ||

	sasamudraguhā tena saśailavanakānanā |

	caturantā bhaved dattā pṛthivī nātra saṃśayaḥ ||

	kṛṣṇājine tilān kṛtvā hiraṇyaṃ madhusarpiṣī |

	dadāti yas tu viprāya sa saṃtarati duṣkṛtam || iti |

yamagāthāsu |

	gobhūhiraṇyasaṃyuktamārgam ekaṃ dadāti yaḥ |

	hitvā duṣkṛtakarmāṇi sāyujyaṃ brahmaṇo vrajet ||

	gobhiś catasṛbhir yuktaṃ tathā bhūmisamanvitam |

	pratigrahasamarthāya viduṣe brahmacāriṇe ||

matsyapurāṇe |

	matsya uvāca |

	vaiśākhī paurṇamāsī ca grahaṇaṃ candrasūryayoḥ |

	paurṇamāsī tathā māghī āṣāḍhī kārtikī tathā ||

	turāyaṇaṃ tu dvādaśyāṃ tasyāṃ dattaṃ mahāphalam |

	āhitāgnir dvijo yaś ca tad deyaṃ kasya pārthiva ||

**[355]**	yathā yena vidhānena tan me nigadataḥ śṛṇu |

	gomayenopalipte tu śucau deśe narādhipa ||

	ādāv eva samāstīrya śobhanaṃ vastram āvikam |

	tataḥ saśṛṅgaṃ sakhuram āvike kṛṣṇamārgaṇam ||

	kartavyaṃ rūpyaśṛṅgaṃ tadrūpyadantaṃ tathaiva ca |

	lāṅgūlaṃ vidrumaṃ caiva netrayor mauktikaṃ tathā ||

	tilair ātmasamaṃ kṛtvā vāsasācchādayed budhaḥ |

	suvarṇanābhaṃ tat kuryād alaṃkuryād viśeṣataḥ ||

	gandhair annair yathāśaktyā tasya dikṣu ca vinyaset |

	dhātupātrāṇi catvāri dikṣu dadyād yathākramam ||

	hiraṇmayeṣu pātreṣu pūrvādikrameṇa tu |

	ghṛtaṃ kṣīraṃ dadhi kṣaudram evaṃ datvā yathāvidhi ||

	campakasya tathā śākhām avraṇaṃ kumbham eva ca |

	vādyopasthāpanaṃ kṛtvā śubhavitto niveśayet ||

	jīrṇavastreṇa pītena sarvāṅgāni ca mārjayet |

	dhātumayāni pātrāṇi pādeṣv asya pradāpayet ||

	yāni kāmyāni pāpāni mayā loke kṛtāni vai |

	lohapātrapradānena praṇaśyantu mamāśu vai ||

	tilapūrṇaṃ tu taṃ kṛtvā vāmapāde niveśayet |

	yāni pāpāny akāmyāni kāmotthāni kṛtāni ca ||

	kāṃsyapātrapradānena tāni naśyantu me sadā |

	madhupūrṇaṃ tu taṃ kṛtvā pāde vai dakṣiṇe nyaset ||

	parāpavādapaiśunyāt pṛṣṭhamāṃsasya bhakṣaṇāt |

	tatrotthitaṃ ca me pāpaṃ tāmrapātrāt praśaśyatu ||

	kanyānṛtaṃ gavāṃ caiva paradārapragharṣaṇam |

	rūpyapātrapradānād dhi kṣipraṃ nāśaṃ prayātu me ||

	ūrdhvapādau tv imau kāryau tāmrasya rajatasya ca |

	janmajanmasahasreṣu kṛtaṃ pāpaṃ kubuddhinā ||

**[356]**	suvarṇapātradānena nāśayāśu janārdana |

	hema muktā vidrumaṃ ca dāḍimaṃ bījapūrakam ||

	praśastapātre śravaṇe khuraśṛṅgāṭakāni ca |

	evaṃ kṛtvā yathoktena sarvaśākaphalāni ca ||

	tatpratigrahavid vidvān āhitāgnir dvijottamaḥ |

	snāto vastrayugacchannaḥ svaśaktyā vāpy alaṃkṛtaḥ |

	pratigrahaś ca tasyoktaḥ pucchadeśe mahīpate ||

	suvarṇanābhakaṃ dadyāt prīyatāṃ vṛṣabhadhvajaḥ |

	anena vidhinā datvā yathāvakṛṣṇamārgaṇam ||

	na spṛśyaḥ sa dvijo rājṃś citiyūpasamo hi saḥ |

	dāne ca śraddadhāne ca dūrataḥ parivarjayet ||

	svagṛhān preṣya taṃ vipraṃ maṇḍale snānam ācaret |

	pūrṇakumbhena rājendra śākhāyāṃ caṇakasya ca ||

	kṛtvā cācāryakalaśaṃ mantreṇānena mūrdhani |

	āpyāyatāṃ samudras tvām ṛco japyās tu ṣoḍaśa ||

	ahate vāsasī kṛtvā cācāntaḥ śucitām iyāt |

	tadvat susaṃhitaṃ kumbhaṃ nītvotkṣipya catuṣpathe ||

	kṛtenānena yā vyuṣṭir na sā kratuśatair api |

	vaktuṃ ca nṛpatiśreṣṭha tathāpy uddeśataḥ śṛṇu ||

	samagrabhūmidānasya phalaṃ prāpnoty asaṃśayam |

	sarvāṃś ca lokāñ jayati kāmacārī vihaṃgamaḥ ||

	ābhūtasaṃplavaṃ yāvatsvargaṃ prāpnoty asaṃśayam |

	na pitā putramaraṇaṃ viyogaṃ bhāyayā saha ||

	dhanadeśaparityāgaṃ na caivehāpnuyāt kvacit ||

iti kṛṣṇājinadānavidhiḥ |

atha kālapuruṣadānam |

	śrīkṛṣṇa uvāca |

	puṇyaṃ dinam athāsādya bhūmibhāge same śubhe |

	caturdaśyāṃ caturthyāṃ vā viṣṭyāṃ vā pāṇdunandana ||

**[357]**	pumān kṛṣṇatilaiḥ kāryo rūpyadantaḥ suvarṇadṛk |

	khaḍgodyatakaro dīrgho japākusumamaṇḍitaḥ ||

	raktāmbaradharaḥ sragvī śaṅkhamālāvibhūṣitaḥ |

	tīkṣṇāsiputryā bandhanaṃ prabhāvitakaṭītaṭaḥ ||

	upānadyugayukto 'pi kṛṣṇakambalapārśvagaḥ |

	gṛhītasāṃsapiṇḍaś ca vāme karatale tu saḥ ||

	evaṃvidhaṃ tu taṃ kṛtvā gṛhītakusumāñjaliḥ |

	yajamānaḥ prasannātmā imaṃ mantram udīrayet ||

	saṃpūjya gandhakusumair vaivedyaṃ vinivedya ca |

	sarvaṃ kālayase yasmāt kālas tenaiva codyase ||

	brahmaviṣṇuśivādīnāṃ tvam asādhyo 'si suvrata |

	pūjitas tvaṃ mayā bhaktyā pārthitaś ca mayā sukham ||

	yad yujyate tava vibho tat kuruṣva namo namaḥ |

	evaṃ saṃpūjayitvā taṃ brāhmaṇāya nivedayet ||

	brāhmaṇaḥ prathamaṃ pūjyo vāsobhir bhūṣaṇais tathā |

	dakṣiṇāṃ śaktito datvā praṇipatya visarjayet ||

	anena vidhinā yas tu dānam etat prayacchati |

	apasṛtyubhayaṃ tasya na ca vyādhikṛtaṃ bhavet ||

	bhavaty avyāharaiśvaryaḥ sarvabādhāvivarjitaḥ |

	dehānte sūryabhavanaṃ bhittvā yāti parāṃ gatim ||

	puṇyakṣayād ihābhyetya rājā bhavati dhārmikaḥ |

	yajñayājī śriyā yuktaḥ putrapautrasamanvitaḥ ||

	saṃpūjya kālapuruṣaṃ vidhivad dvijāya datvā śubhāśubhaphalodayahetubhūtam |

	rogāmayaiḥ sakalarogamayaiḥ śrīre dehī na moham upagacchati tatprabhāvāt ||

iti bhaviṣyottare kālapuruṣadānavidhānam |

atha tithidānāni | tatra viṣṇuḥ |


    mārgaśīrṣaśuklapañcadaśyāṃ mṛgaśirasā yuktāyāṃ cūrṇitalavaṇasya suvarṇanābhaṃ prastham ekaṃ brāhmaṇāya pratipādayet | anena karmaṇā rūpasaubhāgyaṃ **[358]** jāyate | pauṣī cet puṣyayuktā syāt tasyāṃ gaurasarṣapakalkenotsāditaśarīro gavyaghṛtakumbhenābhiṣiktaḥ sarvauṣadhībhiḥ sarvagandhaiḥ sarvabījaiś ca snāto ghṛtena ca bhagavantaṃ vāsudevaṃ snāpayitvā puṣpadhūpadīpagandhanaivedyādibhiś cābhyarcya vaiṣṇavaiḥ sūktair bārhaspatyaiś ca mantraiḥ pāvakaṃ hutvā susuvarṇena ghṛtena brāhmaṇaṃ svasti vācayet | vāsoyugaṃ ca kartre dadyāt | anena karmaṇā puṣyate | māghī maghāyuktā cet syāt tasyāṃ tilaiḥ śrāddhaṃ kṛtvā pūto bhavati | phālgunī phalgunena yuktā cet syāt tasyāṃ brāhmaṇāya susaṃskṛtaṃ svāstīrṇaṃ śayanaṃ nivedya bhāryāṃ manojñāṃ pakṣavatīṃ rūpavatīṃ draviṇavatīṃ cāpnoti nary apy evaṃvidhaṃ bhartāram | caitrī citrāyuktā cet syāt tasyāṃ brāhmaṇāya citravastradānena saubhāgyam āpnoti | vaiśākhyāṃ paurṇamāsyāṃ brāhmaṇānāṃ saptakaṃ kṣaudrayuktais tilaiḥ saṃtarpya dharmarājaṃ prīṇayitvā pāpebhyaḥ pūto bhavati | jyaiṣṭhī jyeṣṭhāyuktā cet syāt tasyāṃ chatropanatpradānena nagarādhipatyam āpnoti | āṣāḍhyām āṣāḍāyuktāyām annapānadānena tad evākṣayyam āpnoti | śrāvaṇyāṃ śraṇayuktāyāṃ jaladhenuṃ sānnāṃ vāsoyugācchāditāṃ datvā svargalokam āpnoti | proṣṭhapadyā tadyuktāyāṃ godānena sarvapāpavinirmukto bhavati | āśvayujyām aśvinīgate candramasi ghṛtapūrṇabhājanaṃ suvarṇayutaṃ viprāya datvā dīpāgnir bhavati | kārtikī cet kṛttikāyuktā syāt tasyāṃ sitam ukṣāṇam anyavarṇaṃ vā śaśāṅkodaye sarvasasyaratnagandopetaṃ dīpamadhye brāhmaṇāya dadyāt | kāntārabhayaṃ na paśyati | vaiśākhamāsatṛtīyāyām upoṣito 'kṣatair vāsudevam abhyarcya tān eva hutvā datvā sarvaṃ yac ca tasminn ahani prayacchati tad akṣayyam āpnoti | pauṣyām atītāyāṃ kṛṣṇapakṣadvādaśyāṃ sopavāsas tilaiḥ snātas tilodakaṃ datvā tilair vāsudevam abhyarcya tān eva hutvā bhuktvā ca sarvapāpebhyaḥ pūto bhavati | māghyāṃ samatītāyāṃ kṛṣṇadvādaśīṃ saśravaṇāṃ prāpya vāsudevāgrato mahāvartidvayena dīpadvayaṃ dadyāt | dakṣiṇapārśve mahārajanaraktena samagreṇa vāsasā ghṛtatulām aṣṭādhikāṃ datvā vāmapārśve tilatailatulāṃ sāṣṭāṃ datvā śvetena samagreṇa vāsasaitat kṛtvā yasmin rāṣṭre 'bhijāyate
