yasmin deśe yasmin kule ca tatrojjvalo bhavati || **[359]**

yamaḥ |

	vaiśākhyāṃ paurṇamāsyāṃ tu brāhmaṇān sapta pañca vā |

	kṣaudrayuktais tilaiḥ kṛṣṇair vārcayed yadi vetaraiḥ ||

	prīyatāṃ dharmarājeti yad vā manasi vartate |

	yāvajjīvaṃ kṛtaṃ pāpaṃ tatkṣaṇād eva naśyati ||

tathā |

	vaiśākhyām eva vidhivad brāhmaṇān bhojayed daśa |

	trirātram uṣitaḥ snātvā kṛsaraṃ prayataḥ śuciḥ ||

	gaurān yadi vā kṛṣṇāṃs tilān kṣaudreṇa saṃyutān |

	datvā daśasu vipreṣu tān eva svasti vācayet ||

	prīyatāṃ dharmarājeti pitṝn devāṃś ca tarpayet |

	yāvajjīvaṃ kṛtaṃ pāpaṃ tatkṣaṇād eva muñcati ||

	ayutāyutaṃ ca tiṣṭhet svargaloke na saṃśayaḥ |

	mām eva ca na paśyet tu na ca pāpena lipyate ||

jābālaḥ |

	śṛtānnam udakumbhaṃ tu vaiśākhyāṃ ca viśeṣataḥ |

	nirdiśya dharmarājāya godānaphalam āpnuyāt ||

	suvarṇatilayuktais tu brāhmaṇān sapta pañca vā |

	tarpayed udapātrais tu brahmahatyāṃ vyapohati ||

mahābhārate |

	vaiśākhyāṃ paurṇamāsyāṃ tu tilān dadyād dvijātiṣu |

	tilā bhakṣayitavyāś ca sadā cālabhanaṃ ca taiḥ ||

	kāryaṃ satatam icchadbhiḥ śreyaḥ sarvātmanā gṛhe |

anādiṣṭaprāyaścittam āha saṃvartaḥ |

	māghamāse tu saṃprāpte paurṇamāsyām upoṣitaḥ |

	brāhmaṇebhyas tilān datvā sarvapāpaiḥ pramucyate ||

atra dānaṃ paurṇamāsyāṃ vidhīyate pradhānatvāt tataś cārthāc caturdaśyām upavāsaḥ |

	upavāsarato bhūtvā paurṇamāsyāṃ tu kārtike |

	hiraṇyam annaṃ vastraṃ ca datvā tarati duṣkṛtam ||

yamaḥ |

	kārtikasya tamisre tu madhāsu navamītithau |

	ahorātroṣito bhūtvā dharmarājāya bhojayet ||

	vidhivad brāhmaṇān bhaktyā svargaloke mahīyate |

	tilān kṛṣṇājine kṛtvā hiraṇyaṃ madhusarpiṣī ||

**[360]**	datvā tu brāhmaṇāyāśu sarvaṃ tarati duṣkṛtam |

	dhenuṃ datvobhayamukhīṃ bhūdānaphalam āpnuyāt ||

	māghāndhakāradvādaśyāṃ tilair hutvā hutāśanam |

	tilān datvā dvijātibhyaḥ sarvapāpaiḥ pramucyate ||

	ādityavāre viprāya sahiraṇyaṃ sadaiva tu |

	yaḥ prayacchaty apūpaṃ ca tasya tuṣyati vai yamaḥ ||

skandapurāṇe |

	tilapātrāṇi yo dadyād viprebhyaḥ śuddhamānasaḥ |

	amāvasyāṃ tu saṃprāpya kṛṣṇānāṃ tu samāhitaḥ ||

	pitṝṃś ca tarpayitvā tu akṣayaṃ narapuṃgavaḥ |

	pitṛlokaṃ samāpnoti ciraṃ ca sukham edhate ||

atha nakṣatradānāni |

tatra viṣṇuḥ |


    pratimāsaṃ revatīgate candramasi madhughṛtayutaṃ paramānnaṃ brāhmaṇān bhojayitvā rūpabhāg bhavati |

	māsi māsi ca revatyāṃ brāhmaṇān gṛtapāyasaiḥ |

	sadakṣiṇaṃ bhojayitvā rūpabhāg abhijāyate ||

bhaviṣyottare | 

	śrīkṛṣṇa uvāca |

	nakṣatrayoge yad yasmin deyaṃ bhavati bhārata |

	tat te 'haṃ saṃpravakṣyāmi sarvapātakanāśanam ||

	kṛttikāsu mahābhāga pāyasena sasarpiṣā |

	saṃtarpya brāhmaṇān sādhūṃl lokān āpnoti cākṣayān ||

	rohiṇyāṃ pāṇḍavaśreṣṭha māṃsair annena sarpiṣā |

	payo 'nnadānaṃ dātavyam ānṛṇyārthaṃ dvijātaye ||

	dogdhrīṃ datvā savatsāṃ tu nakṣatre somadaivate |

	datvā divyavimānasthaḥ svargam āpnoty anuttamam ||

	ārdrāyāṃ kṛsaraṃ datvā tailasiddhaṃ samāhitaḥ |

	naras tarati durgāṇi sarvāṇy eva narottama ||

	pūpān punarvasau datvā tilapūrṇān supācitān |

	yaśasvī rūpasaṃpanno bahvanno jāyate kule ||

**[361]**	puṇye ca kāñcanaṃ datvā kṛtaṃ cākṛtam eva ca |

	anālokeṣu lokeṣu somavat sa virājate ||

	aśleṣāsu tathā raupyaṃ yaḥ surūpaṃ prayacchati |

	sa sarvabhayanirmuktaḥ śāstravān abhijāyate ||

	madhāsu tilapūrṇāni vardhamānāni mānavaḥ |

	pradāya paśumāṃś caiva putravāṃś cābhijāyate ||

	phalgunīparvasamaye vaḍavāṃ dvijapuṃgave |

	datvā puṇyakṛtāṃ lokān prāpnoti surasevitān ||

	uttarāphalgunīyoge datvā sauvarṇapaṅkajam |

	sūryalokam avāpnoti sarvabādhāvivarjitaḥ ||

	haste tu hastinaṃ datvā kāñcanaṃ śaktitaḥ kṛtam |

	prayāti śakrasadanaṃ varavāraṇadhūrgataḥ ||

	citrāsu vṛṣabhaṃ datvā puṇyagandhāṃś ca bhārata |

	caraty apsarasāṃ loke modate nandane vane ||

	svātiṣv atha dhanaṃ datvā yadabhīṣṭam ihātmanaḥ |

	prāpnoti suśubhāṃl lokān iha loke mahad yaśaḥ ||

	viśākhāsu mahārāja dhuraṃdharavibhūṣitam |

	sopāsaṅgaṃ ca śakaṭaṃ dhānyavastrādisaṃyutam ||

	datvā prīṇāti sa pitṝn pretya cānantyam aśnute |

	na ca durgāṇy avāpnoti rauravādīni mānavaḥ ||

	datvā yatheṣṭaṃ viprebhyo gatim iṣṭāṃ sa vindati |

	kambalān anurādhāsu datvā prāvaraṇāni ca ||

	svarge varṣaśataṃ sāgram āste suragaṇair vṛtaḥ |

	kālaśākaṃ ca viprebhyo datvā martyaḥ samūlakam ||

	jyeṣṭhāsu jyeṣṭhatām eti gatim iṣṭāṃ ca vindati |

	mūle mūlaphalaṃ datvā brāhmaṇebhyaḥ samāhitaḥ ||

	pitṝn prīṇayate sarvān gatim āpnoty anuttamām |

	atha pūrvāsv āṣāḍhāsu dadhipātrāṇi mānavaḥ ||

**[362]**	kulavṛttena saṃpanne brāhmaṇe vedapārage |

	pradāya jāyate pretya kule sa bahugodhane ||

	putrapautraiḥ parivṛtaḥ paśumān dhanavāṃs tathā |

	udamanthaṃ sasarpiṣkaṃ prabhūtamadhuphāṇitam ||

	datvottarāsv āṣāḍhāsu sarvān kāmān avāpnuyāt |

	dugdhaṃ tv abhijitā yoge datvā ghṛtamadhuplutam ||

	darmavidbhyo manīṣibhyo svarge vasati puṇyabhāk |

	śravaṇe pustakaṃ śreṣṭhaṃ pradadātīha yo naraḥ ||

	svecchayā yāti yānena sarvāṃl lokān asaṃvṛtān |

	goyugaṃ ca dhaniṣṭhāsu datvā viprāya mānavaḥ ||

	sarvān rasān avāpnoti yatra yatreha jāyate |

	tathā śatabhiṣāyoge datvā śagurucandanam ||

	prāpnoty apsarasāṃ lokān pretya gandhāṃś ca śobhanān |

	pūrvabhadrapadāyoge (?) rājamāṣān pradāpayet ||

	sarvabhakṣyaphalopetaḥ sa vai pretya sukhī bhavet |

	aurabhram uttarāyoge savastraṃ yaḥ prayacchati ||

	ptiṝn prīṇāti sakalān pretya cānantyam aśnute |

	kāṃsyopadohanāṃ dhenuṃ revatyāṃ yaḥ prayacchati ||

	sā pretya kāmān ādāya dātāram upatiṣṭhati |

	ratham aśvasamāyuktaṃ datvāśvinyāṃ narottamaḥ ||

	hastyaśvarathasaṃpanne varcasvī jāyate kule |

	bharaṇīṣu dvijātibhyas tiladhenuṃ pradāya vai ||

	gāḥ suprasūtāḥ prāpnoti naraḥ pretya yaśas tathā |

	ity eṣa dakṣiṇoddeśaḥ prokto nakṣatrayogataḥ ||

	devakyā nāradeneha mayā ca kathitas tava |

	sarvapāpapraśamanaḥ sarvopadravanāśanaḥ ||

	na cātra kālaniyamo na nakṣatrakramas tathā |

	vittaṃ śraddhā ca rājendra kāraṇaṃ cātra kathyate ||

	yady atra te bhagavatā kamalāsanasya putreṇa dānam uditaṃ prasamīkṣya vedān |

	tad yo dadāti vibhave sati sādhuvṛtte kiṃ tena pārtha na kṛtaṃ bhavatīha loke ||

iti bhaviṣyottare nakṣatradānavidhiḥ |

atha māsadānāni

viṣṇuḥ |


    āśvinaṃ sakalaṃ māsaṃ brāhmaṇebhyaḥ pratyahaṃ ghṛtaṃ pradāyāśvinau prīṇayitvā rūpabhāg bhavati | asminn eva māsi pratyahaṃ gorasair brāhmaṇān bhojayitvārogyabhāg bhavati | māghe māsy agniṃ pratyahaṃ tilair hutvā saghṛtaṃ kulmāṣaṃ brāhmaṇān bhojayitvā ca dīptāgnitvam āpnoti |

tathā |

	ghṛtam āśvayuje māsi nityaṃ dadyād dvijātaye |

	prīṇayitvāśvinau devau rūpabhāg abhijāyate ||

	tilapradaḥ prajām iṣṭāṃ puruṣaḥ khalu vindati |

	māghe māsi viśeṣeṇa tat tamisre viśeṣataḥ ||

yamaḥ |

	kṛsaraṃ bhojayitvā tu svaśaktyā śiśire dvijān |

	dīptāgnitvam avāpnoti svargalokaṃ ca gacchati ||

	māsi māsi ca revatyāṃ brāhmaṇān ghṛtapāyasam |

	sadakṣiṇaṃ bhojayitvā rūpabhāg abhijāyate ||

ādityapurāṇe |

	jyeṣṭhe māsi tilān datvā paurṇamāsyāṃ viśeṣataḥ |

	aśvamedhasya yat puṇyaṃ tat prāpnoti na saṃśayaḥ ||

devīpurāṇe |

	dhenuṃ tilamayīṃ māghyāṃ dadyād yaś cottarāyaṇa (?) |

	vicitrāṇi ca vastrāṇi caitre dadyād dvijottamaḥ ||

	vaiśākhe yavagodhūmāñ jyeṣṭhe toyabhṛtān ghaṭān |

	āṣāḍhe candanaṃ deyaṃ sakarpūraṃ mahāphalam ||

	navanītaṃ nabhomāsi chatraṃ proṣṭhapade matam |

	guḍaśarkaravarṇāḍhyāṃl laḍḍukān āśvine mune ||

	dīpadānaṃ mahāpuṇyaṃ kārtike yaḥ prayacchati |

	sarvān kāmān avāpnoti kramān mārgādyudāhṛtān ||

	dhenuṃ pauṣe ghṛtamayīṃ māghe tilamayīṃ tathā |

	jyeṣṭhe toyamayīṃ dadyād ghṛtavatsāṃ mahāphalām ||

	surūpāṃ śrāvaṇe dadyād gāṃ mahāphaladāyikām |

	sarvahemamayaiḥ śṛṅgai raupyapādā udāhṛtāḥ ||

	kāṃsyapātrāḥ saghaṇṭās tu kiṅkiṇībhiḥ suśobhitāḥ |

	sayugāḥ sasrajo vatsā datvyā vidhinā mune ||

**[364]**	devībrahmeśasūryān vā viṣṇuṃ vātha yathāvidhi |

	svabhāvavṛttasaṃpanne pūjayitvā dvijottame ||

	dātavyālaṃkṛtā dhenuḥ kāmakrodhavivarjite |

	ayācake sadācāre vinīte vinayānvite ||

	gopradānāl labhet kāmān sve sve loke manoramān |

tathā |

	āṣāḍhe toyadhenuḥ syād dhenur bhādrapade sadā |

	māghe tu tiladhenuḥ syād yāṃ datvā labhate hitam ||

	māghe māsi tilān yas tu brāhmaṇebhyaḥ prayacchati |

	sarvasattvasamākīrṇaṃ narakaṃ na sa paśyati ||

yamaḥ |

	mahāpātakasaṃghātaḥ kāmato vāpy akāmataḥ |

	śuddhiṃ tasya pravakṣyāmi svargasādhanam eva ca ||

	śuklaiḥ kṛṣṇais tathā labdhair dvātriṃśadaṅgulocchritaḥ |

	rāśis tilaiḥ same deśe kartavyaḥ puruṣāyataḥ ||

	pratimāṣṭāṅgulotkṣepyā sauvarṇīṃ vibhave sati |

	kṣaudreṇa payasā dadhnā ghṛtenāpūrayed ghaṭān ||

	yathāvibhavavistāraṃ brāhmaṇe śrotriye 'rthini |

	dadyān māghe 'tha vaiśākhe viṣuve cottarāyaṇe ||

	yāvajjīvaṃ kṛtaṃ pāpaṃ tatkṣaṇād eva naśyati |

vāmanapurāṇe |

	māghe māsi tilā deyās tiladhenuś ca dānava |

	idhmendhanādayaś caiva mādhavaprīṇanāya vai ||

	phālgune vrīhayo gāvo vastraṃ kṛṣṇājinānvitam |

	govindaprīṇanārthāya dātavyaṃ puruṣarṣabha ||

	caitre vicitravastrāṇi śayanāny āsanāni ca |

	viṣṇoḥ prītyartham etāni deyāni brāhmaṇeṣv atha ||

	gandhāś ca mālyāni tathā vaiśākhe surabhīṇi ca |

	deyāni dvijamukhyebhyo madhusūdanatuṣṭaye ||

	udakumbhāmbudhenuṃ ca tālavṛntaṃ sacandanam |

	trivikramasya prītyarthaṃ dātavyaṃ sādhubhiḥ sadā ||

	upānadyugalaṃ chatraṃ lavanāmalakāni ca |

	āṣāḍhe vāmanaprītyai dātavyāni tu bhaktitaḥ ||

**[365]**	ghṛtaṃ ca kṣīrakumbhāś ca ghṛtadhenus tathaiva ca |

	śrāvaṇe śrīdharaprītyai dātavyāni vipaścite ||

	māsi bhādrapade dadyāt pāyasaṃ madhusarpiṣī |

	hṛṣīkeśaprīṇanāya lavaṇaṃ suguḍaudanam ||

	tilās turaṅgavṛṣabhadadhitāmrarasādikam |

	prītyarthaṃ padmanābhasya deyam āśvayuje naraiḥ ||

	rajataṃ kanakaṃ dīpā maṇimuktāphalādikam |

	dāmodarasya prītyarthaṃ pradadyāt kārtike naraḥ ||

	kharoṣṭrāśvatarā nāgāḥ śakaṭokṣam ajāvikam |

	dātavyaṃ keśavaprītyai māsi mārgaśire naraiḥ ||

	prāsādanagarādīni gṛhaprāvaraṇāni ca |

	nārāyaṇasya tuṣṭyarthaṃ pauṣe deyāni yatnataḥ ||

	dāsīdāsasamalaṃkāram annaṃ ṣaḍrasasaṃyutam |

	puruṣottamatuṣṭyarthaṃ pauṣe deyāni yatnataḥ ||

	atha vā caturthapādaḥ pradeyaṃ sārvakāmikam |

	yad yad iṣṭatamaṃ kiṃcid yac cāpy asti śubhaṃ gṛhe ||

	tat tad dhi deyaṃ prītyarthaṃ devadevasya cakriṇaḥ || iti || 1.208 ||

_gopradānaprasaṅgād dānāny uktāni, prakṛtam ucyate |_

	**śrāntasaṃvāhanaṃ rogiparicaryā surārcanam |**

**	pādaśaucaṃ dvijocchiṣṭamārjanaṃ gopradānavat || 1.209 ||**

śrāntasaṃvāhanādikaṃ pratyekaṃ godānena phalataḥ samaṃ bhavati | śrāntaḥ khinnas tasya saṃvāhanaṃ śramāpanayanam | rogiparicaryā cikitsādi | prasiddham anyat | pādaśaucadvijocchiṣṭamārjane samottamavarṣaviṣaye | yamaḥ |

	devamālyāpanayanaṃ devāgārasamūhanam |

	snāpanaṃ sarvadevānāṃ gopradānasamaṃ matam ||

nandipurāṇe |

	dharmārthakāmakokṣāṇām ārogyaṃ sādhanaṃ yataḥ |

	atas tv ārogyadānena naro bhavati sarvadaḥ ||

**[366]**	ārogyaśālāṃ kurute mahauṣadhiparicchadām |

	vidagdhavaidyasaṃyuktāṃ ghṛtānnamadhusaṃyutām ||

	vaidyas tu śāstravit prājño dṛṣṭauṣadhiparamparaḥ |

	oṣadhīmūlaparṇajñaḥ samuddharaṇakālavit ||

	rasavīryavipākajñaḥ śālimāṃsauṣadhīgaṇe |

	yogavid dehināṃ dehaṃ yo dhiyā praviśed budhaḥ ||

	dhātupathyāmayajñaś ca nidānavid atandritaḥ |

	vyādhīnāṃ pūrvaliṅgajñas taduttaravidhānavit ||

	deśakālavidhānajñaś cikitsāsāmayavit tathā |

	aṣṭāṅgāyurvedavettā muṣṭiyogavidhānavit ||

	evaṃvidhaḥ śubho vaidyo bhaved yatrābhiyojitaḥ |

	ārogyaśālām evaṃ tu kuryād yo dharmasaṃśrayaḥ ||

	sa pumān dhārmiko loke sa kṛtārthaḥ sa śuddhimān |

	samyag ārogyaśālāyām auṣadhaiḥ snehapācanaiḥ ||

	vyādhitaṃ nīrujīkṛtya apy ekaṃ karuṇāyutaḥ |

	prayāti brahmasadanaṃ kulasaptakasaṃyutaḥ ||

	āḍhyo vittānusāreṇa daridraḥ phalabhāg bhavet |

	daridrasya kutaḥ śālā ārogyāya bhiṣak tathā ||

	api mūlena kenāpi candanādyair athāpi vā |

	svasthīkṛte labhen martye pūrvoktaṃ lokam avyayam ||

	vātapittakaphādyānāṃ cayāpacayabhedinām |

	yas tu svaslpābhyupāyena mokṣayed vyādhipīḍitān ||

	so 'pi yāti śubhāṃl lokān avāpyān yajñayājibhiḥ |


    śalyaṃ śālakyaṃ kāyacikitsā bhūtavidyā kaumāraprabhṛtyam aśvatantraṃ rasāyanatantraṃ vājīkaraṇatantram |

iti suśrutoktāny aṣṭāṅgāny āyurvedasya | ity ārogyadānam || 1.209 ||

**[367]**

_kiṃ ca_ |

	**bhūdīpānnāśvavastrāmbhastilasarpiḥpratiśrayān |**

**	naiveśikasvarṇadhuryān datvā svarge mahīyate || 1.210 ||**

bhūmidīpādidānena svargam āpnotīti vākyārthaḥ | bhūś ca sasyavatī phalapradā vā deyā | taddvāreṇaiva tadgurutvam |

	bhūmiṃ sasyavatīṃ śreṣṭhāṃ datvā svarge mahīyate |

iti saṃvartaḥ | pāpakṣayārtham api bhavati | yathāha bṛhaspatiḥ |

	yat kiṃcit kurute pāpaṃ janmaprabhṛti mānavaḥ |

	api gocarmamātreṇa bhūmidānena śudhyati ||

	saptahastena daṇḍena triṃśad daṇḍā nivartanam |

	daśa tān eva gocarma datvā svarge mahīyate ||

carmamātragopradānenāpi svargaprāptiḥ | "divyaṃ varṣaśataṃ yāvad bhūmidaḥ svargam āpnoti | dviyaṃ varṣaśataṃ sārdhaṃ tathā" iti, tad dvaiguṇyāditāratamyād iti | yat punar manunoktam "bhūmido bhūmim āpnoti" iti, tat svargacyutābhiprāyeṇa nyūnātmadānābhiprāyeṇa vā | taddānasya vaiśvarūpyāt | ata eva |

	suvarṇaṃ rajataṃ tāmraṃ maṇimuktāvasūni ca |

	sarvam etad bhaved dattaṃ vasudhāṃ yaḥ prayacchati || iti |

na ca sakalavasudhābhiprāyeṇocyate | tasyā aśakyatvāt | evaṃ pradīpādidāne 'pi pātraviśeṣād āvṛttau vā svargaprāptiḥ |

	pātrasya hi viśeṣeṇa śraddadhānatayāpi ca |

	alpaṃ vā bahu vā pretya dānasyāpnoti tatphalam ||

iti vacanāt | anyathā —

	vāridas tṛptim āpnoti sukham akṣayyam annadaḥ |

	tilapradaḥ prajām iṣṭāṃ dīpadaś cakṣur uttamam ||

	vāsodaś candrasālokyaṃ sūryasālokyam aśvadaḥ | iti |

vastrādiviśeṣāc ca phalaviśeṣo dvitrādisaṃkhyātaś ca | kṣīṇavṛtter āyātasyāsmin bhavane sthīyatām iti pratiśrayaḥ | niveśārthaṃ kanyāpi dīyata iti naiveśikam | **[368]** ata eva |

	mātāpitṛvihīnaṃ tu saṃskārodvāhanādibhiḥ |

	yaḥ sthāpayati tasyeha puṇyasaṃkhyā na vidyate || iti |

	na tacchreyo 'gnihotreṇa nāśvamedhena nānyathā |

	yacchreyaḥ prāpyate pretya vipreṇa shāpitena tu || iti |

sthāpitena bhavanādidānena pratiṣṭhāpitenety arthaḥ | dakṣaḥ | "suvarṇam eva svarṇam asya ca deśakālapātrasuvarṇaparimāṇāc ca phalaviśeṣaḥ" | tathā |

	uccā divi dakṣiṇāvanto asthur ye aśvadāḥ saha te sūryeṇa |

	hiraṇyadā amṛtatvaṃ bhajante vāsodāḥ soma pra tiranta āyuḥ ||

ity amṛtatvaṃ muktir darśitā | tathā: "svarṇadhuryān dartvā svarge mahīyate" iti | gargaḥ |

	bhūmido bhūmim āpnoti dīrgham āyur hiraṇyadaḥ |

	gṛhado 'gryāṇi veśmāni rūpyado rūpam uttamam || iti |

etac ca suvarṇadāne 'pi veditavyam | alaṃkāre tu phalaviśeṣaḥ |

	alaṃkṛtas tv alaṃkāraṃ datvā svarge mahīyate | iti |

dhuram arhatīti dhuryaḥ | 

	anaḍuhaḥ śriyaṃ puṣṭāṃ godo bradhnasya viṣṭapam | iti |

atrāpi pātrādideśakālaviśeṣād dvitrādiviśeṣāc ca phalaviśeṣaḥ | viṣṇudharmeṣu |

	bhagavān uvāca |

	chatrapradānena gṛhaṃ variṣṭhaṃ rathaṃ tathopānahasaṃpradānāt |

	dhuryapradānena gavāṃ tathaiva lokān avāpnoti puraṃdarasya ||

	svarīyam apy āha hiraṇyadānaṃ tathā variṣṭhaṃ kanakapradānam |

	naiveśikaṃ sarvaguṇopapannaṃ prayacchate yaḥ puruṣo dvijāya ||

	svādhyāyacāritryaguṇānvitāya tasyāpi lokāḥ pravarā bhavanti |

	yo brahmadeyāṃ pradadāti kanyāṃ bhūmipradānaṃ ca karoti vipre ||

	vastrānnadānaṃ ca tathā viśiṣṭaṃ sa śakralokaṃ labhate durāpam |

	bhūdānena samaṃ dānaṃ na bhūtaṃ na bhaviṣyati |

	iti dharmavidaḥ prāhus tan me nigadataḥ śṛṇu ||

**[639]**	ṣaṣṭiṃ varṣasahasrāṇi svarge vasati bhūmidaḥ |

	ācchettā cānumantā ca tāny eva narake vaset ||

	dānānām ati sarveṣāṃ bhūmidānam ihocyate |

	acalā hy akṣayā bhūmiḥ sarvān kāmān prayacchati ||

	bhūmidaḥ svargam āruhya śāśvatīr edhate samāḥ |

	punarjanma ca saṃprāpya bhaved bhūmipatir dhruvam ||

	yathā bhūmiḥ sadā devī dātāraṃ kurute patim |

	evaṃ sadakṣiṇā dattā kurute gaur janādhipam ||

	api pāpakṛtaṃ prāpya pratigṛhṇīta bhūmidam |

	mahīṃ dadat pavitraḥ syāt puṇyā hi jagatī yataḥ ||

	nāma vai priyadatteti guhyam etat sanātanam |

	tadāsyāḥ satataṃ prītyai kīrtanīyaṃ prayacchatā ||

	yat kiṃcit kurute pāpaṃ puruṣo vṛttikarṣitaḥ |

	api gocarmamātreṇa bhūmidānena śudhyati ||

	suvarṇaṃ rajataṃ tāmraṃ maṇimuktāvasūni ca |

	sarvān etān mahāprājña dadāti vasudhāṃ dadat ||

	phālakṛṣṭāṃ mahīṃ dattvā sodakāṃ ca phalānvitām |

	sodakaṃ vāpi śaraṇaṃ prāpnoti paramaṃ padam ||

	ratnopakīrṇāṃ vasudhāṃ yo dadāti dvijātaye |

	vimuktaḥ kilbiṣaiḥ sarvaiḥ svargaloke mahīyate ||

	ikṣubhiḥ sahitāṃ bhūmiṃ yavagodhūmaśālibhiḥ |

	ye prayacchanti viprebhyo nopasarpanti te yamam ||

	sarvakāmadughāṃ bhūmiṃ sarvasasyasamanvitām |

	yo dadāti dvijendrāya brahmalokaṃ sa gacchati ||

	bhūmidānaṃ naraḥ kuryān mucyate sarvato bhayāt |

	na bhūpa bhūmidānād dhi dānam anyad viśiṣyate ||

	puṇyāṃ sarvarasāṃ bhūmiṃ yo dadāti nararṣabhaḥ |

	na tasya lokāḥ kṣīyante bhūmidasya mahātmanaḥ ||

	kṛśāya kṛśabhṛtyāya vṛttikṣīṇāya sīdate |

	bhūmiṃ vṛttikarīṃ dattvā satrī bhavati mānavaḥ ||

**[370]**	āsphoṭayanti pitaraḥ pravalganti pitāmahāḥ |

	bhūmido 'smatkule jātaḥ so 'smān saṃtārayiṣyati ||

ādityapurāṇe |

	ya etāṃ dakṣiṇāṃ dadyāt pṛthivīṃ pṛthivīpatiḥ |

	punaś ca jananaṃ prāpya bhavet sa pṛthivīpatiḥ ||

	yathā dānaṃ tathā bhoga iti dharmeṣu niścayaḥ |

	saṃgrāme vā tanuṃ jahyād dadyād vā pṛthivīm imām ||

	ity etāṃ kṣattrabandhūnāṃ vadanti paramāśiṣam |

	api pāpakṛtāṃ rājñāṃ pratigṛhṇanti sādhavaḥ ||

	pṛthivīṃ nānyad icchanti pāvanaṃ hy etad uttamam |

	nāmāsyāḥ priyadatteti guhyaṃ devyāḥ sanātanam ||

	dānaṃ vāpy atha vā jñānaṃ nāmno 'syāḥ paramaṃ priyam |

	yas tu gocarmamātrāṃ vai prayacchanti vasuṃdharām ||

	vimuktaḥ sarvapāpebhyo viṣṇulokaṃ sa gacchati |

	ṣaṣṭiṃ varṣasahasrāṇi svarge vasati bhūmidaḥ ||

	ācchettā cānumantā ca tāny eva narake vaset |

	svadattāṃ paradattāṃ vā yo hareta vasuṃdharām ||

	śvaviṣṭhāyāṃ kṛmir bhūtvā pitṛbhiḥ saha majjati ||

matsyapurāṇe |

	yat kiṃcit kurute pāpaṃ puruṣo vṛttikarṣitaḥ |

	api gocarmamātreṇa bhūmidānena śudhyati ||

	suvarṇānāṃ sahasreṇa labhed dattena yat phalam |

	gocarmabhūmimātreṇa tatphalaṃ tu vidhīyate ||

mahābhārate |

	na coṣarāṃ na nirdagdhāṃ mahīṃ dadyāt kathaṃcana |

	na śmaśānaparītāṃ ca na ca pāpaniveśitām ||

iti bhūmidānam |

dīpadāne saṃvartaḥ |

	devāgāre dvijānāṃ vā dīpaṃ datvā catuṣpathe |

	medhāvī jñānasaṃpannaś cakṣuṣmāṃś ca sadā bhavet ||

viṣṇudharmeṣu (?) |

	uccaiḥ pradīpam ākāśe yo dadyāt kārtike naraḥ |

	sa sarvaṃ kulam uddhṛtya viṣṇulokam avāpnuyāt || **[371]**

kārtikanirṇayaś ca bhaviṣyottare boddhavyaḥ | tad yathā |

	viṣṇor āyatane ye tu sahasraṃ paridīpakān |

	prajvālayanty anudinaṃ divārātram anirvṛtāḥ |

	tāmisram āśvayukpakṣaṃ śuklapakṣaṃ tu kārtikam || iti |

dīpadāne mantraḥ |

	dāmodarāya nabhasi tulāyāṃ lolayā saha |

	pradīpaṃ te prayacchāmi namo 'nantāya vedhase || iti |

tathā |

	yadā yadā naraśreṣṭha puṇyakālaḥ prapadyate |

	saṃkrāntisūryagrahaṇe candre parvaṇi vaidhṛte ||

	uttare tv ayane prāpte dakṣiṇe tv ayane tathā |

	ekādaśyāṃ śuklapakṣe caturdaśyāṃ dinakṣaye ||

	saptamyām atha ṣaṣṭhyāṃ vā snātvā vrataparo naraḥ |

	bhavadbhūmidevebhyaḥ prayacchet prayato gaṇe ||

	ghṛtakumbhe ca vastreṇa prajvalantaṃ pradīpakam ||

gaṇe samudāye vartamāna ity arthaḥ | tathā |

	sūryāya raktavastreṇa pūrṇavarti ghṛtena tām |

	catuṣprasthaiḥ prajvalantīṃ mantreṇānena dāpayet ||

	tad viṣṇor iti mantreṇa vartiṃ dadyāt sadaiva hi |

	pītavastreṇa kṛṣṇāya śvetavastreṇa śūline ||

	kausumbhaghṛtavastreṇa gaurīm uddiśya dāpayet |

	lākṣāraktena durgāyai pūrṇavartiṃ prabodhayet ||

	netrapaṭṭena madhunā gṛtena madhukūpake |

	arcite ca site caive lalitāyai prabodhayet ||

	mantreṇānena rājendra taṃ niśāmayya vaidikān |

	ā te vatso mano yamat paramāc cit sadhasthāt |

	agne tvāṃ kāmayā girā ||

	ṛtāvānaṃ vaiśvānaram ṛtasya jyotiṣaspatim |

	ajasraṃ dharmam īmahe ||

**[372]**	divi pṛṣṭhe arocanāgnir vaiśvānaro matān |

	jyotiṣā bādhate tamaḥ ||

	kāmo bhūtasya bhavyasya samrāḍ eko virājati | ity anto mantraḥ |

	evam etena vidhinā ye prayacchanti dīpakam |

	vistīrṇe vipule pātre ghṛtakumbhaṃ niveśitam ||

	yānti te brahmasadanaṃ vimānenārkatejasā |

	tiṣṭhanti dyotamānās te yāvad ābhūmisaṃplavam ||

	ghṛtena dīpo dātavyo rājaṃs tailena vā punaḥ |

	vasāmajjādibhir dīpo na tu deyaḥ kathaṃcana ||

	dīpatailena kartavyaṃ na tu karma vijānatā |

	nirvāpaṇaṃ ca dīpasya hiṃsanaṃ ca vigarhitam ||

	yaḥ kuryāt tena karmāṇi syād asau puṣpitekṣaṇaḥ |

	dīpahartā bhaved andhaḥ kāṇo nirvāpako bhavet ||

	padmasūtrotthitāṃ vartiṃ gandhatailena dīpakam |

	nīrogaḥ subhagaś caiva datvā bhavati mānavaḥ ||

	prajvālya devadevasya karpūreṇa tu dīpakam |

	aśvamedham avāpnoti kulaṃ caiva samuddharet ||

iti dīpadānam |

athāśvadānam |

devīpurāṇe |

	aśvaṃ vā yadi vā yugyaṃ śobhane vātha pāduke |

	dadāti yaḥ pradānaṃ vai brāhmaṇebhyaḥ susaṃyataḥ ||

	tasya divyāni yānāni rathadhvajapatākinaḥ |

	duṣṭaḥ panthā na caiveha bhavaty eva kadācana ||

skandapurāṇe |

	aśvaṃ yas tu praccheta hemacitraṃ sulakṣaṇam |

	sa tena karmaṇā devi gāndharvaṃ lokam aśnute ||

annadāne saṃvartaḥ |

	annadas tu sukhī śrīmān sutṛptaḥ sarvakarmasu |

mahābhārate | **[373]**

	nārada uvāva |

	nānnadānāt paraṃ dānaṃ kiṃcid asti nareśvara |

	annena dhāryate kṛtsnaṃ carācaram idaṃ jagat ||

	annaṃ vai prāṇināṃ prāṇā ity uvāca prajāpatiḥ |

	tasmād annaprado rājan prāṇadaḥ procyate budhaiḥ ||

	annadaḥ paśumāṃl loke dhanavān rūpavān api |

	āyuṣmān balavāṃś caiva sukhī ca pretya jāyate ||

	nityaṃ dadāti yaś cānnam atithibhyaḥ samāhitaḥ |

	sa yāti brahmasālokyam evam āha parāśaraḥ ||

	annena sadṛśaṃ dānaṃ na bhūtaṃ na bhaviṣyati |

	tasmād annaṃ viśeṣeṇa dātum icchanti sādhavaḥ ||

	kṛtvāpi sumahat pāpaṃ yaḥ paścād annado bhavet |

	vimuktaḥ sarvapāpebhyaḥ svargalokaṃ sa gacchati ||

	āśaṃsantīha pitaraḥ suvṛṣṭim iva karṣakāḥ |

	asmākam iha putro vā pautro vānnaṃ pradāsyati ||

	yo dadyād aparikliṣṭam annam adhvani vartine |

	śrāntāyādṛṣṭapūrvāya sa puṇyāṃ gatim āpnuyāt ||

	na pṛcched gotracaraṇaṃ na svādhyāyaṃ śrutaṃ tathā |

	yācito brāhmaṇenānnaṃ dadyād evāvicārayan ||

	durvṛttaḥ sādhuvṛtto vā mūrkho vā yadi paṇḍitaḥ |

	yaḥ prāpto vaisvadevānte so 'tithiḥ svargasaṃkramaḥ ||

	adṛṣṭaṃ dṛṣṭapūrvaṃ vāmitraṃ vā suhṛdaṃ tathā |

	brāhmaṇaṃ bhojayen nityaṃ śāntaṃ śīlasamanvitam ||

	yasya hy annam upāśnāti brāhmaṇānāṃ śataṃ satām |

	hṛṣṭena manasā dattaṃ na sa tiryaggatir bhavet ||

	bhojayitvā daśa śataṃ naro vedavidāṃ nṛpa |

	nyāyavid dharmaviduṣāṃ smṛtibhāṣyavidāṃ tathā ||

	na yāti narakaṃ ghoraṃ saṃsāraṃ ca na sevate |

	brāhmaṇānāṃ sahasrāṇi daśa bhojyāni bhārata ||

	naro 'dhrmāt pramucyeta pāpeṣv api rataḥ sadā | **[374]**

bṛhaspatiḥ |

	annadānaṃ guṇakaraṃ sarvadānādhikaṃ smṛtam |

	annāt prāṇaprajananaṃ nṝṇāṃ saṃjāyate sadā ||

	prāṇāpyāyanamātraṃ tu yo viprāya prayacchati |

	durbhikṣe tu viśeṣeṇa sa labhetākṣayāṃ divam ||

	hemaratnāmbarayuto 'bhuñjāno mriyate naraḥ |

	aśnan vināpy alaṃkāraṃ jīrṇavastro 'pi jīvati ||

	tasmāt pradadyād viprebhyaḥ saṃskṛtānnaṃ sadakṣiṇam |

	teneha kīrtim āpnoti svargaṃ cānantakaṃ tathā ||

ādityapurāṇe |

	annadānāt paraṃ nāsti na bhūtaṃ na bhaviṣyati |

	putraṃ prajāṃ paśūn medhāṃ striyaḥ kāmāṃś ca sarvaśaḥ ||

	sarvaṃ cānnapradānena labhate nātra saṃśayaḥ |

	ādareṇa tu bhaktyā ca yad annam upadīyate ||

	tat prīṇayati gātrāṇi nāmṛtaṃ mānavarjitam |

	durlabhas tu mudā dātā mudā bhoktā ca durlabhaḥ ||

	mudā dātā ca bhoktā ca tāv ubhau svargagāminau(ṇau) |

	yo dadyād apriyeṇānnaṃ yaś cānnaṃ nābhinandati ||

	tāv ubhau narake magnau vasetāṃ śaradāṃ śatam |

viṣṇudharmottare |

	dānānām uttamaṃ dānaṃ vastradānaṃ prakīrtitam |

	vāso hi sarvadai(de)vatyaṃ sarvasāyujyam aśnute ||

	vastradātā suveśaḥ syād rūpadraviṇasaṃyutaḥ |

	nīlīraktaṃ tathā śīrṇaṃ na deyaṃ brāhmaṇasya tu ||

	deyaṃ na cāpy upahataṃ bahupuṇyam abhīpsatā |

	datvā kārpāsikaṃ vastraṃ svargaloke mahīyate ||

	datvā saromam api tat tato daśaguṇaṃ labhet |

	āvikaṃ vasanaṃ datvā bhṛgūṇāṃ lokam āpnuyāt ||

	chāgaṃ datvā cāṅgirasaṃ kṣaumaṃ datvā bṛhaspateḥ |

	vasūnāṃ lokam āpnoti kuśakauśeyavāsasī ||

	kṛmijaṃ ca tathā datvā somaloke mahīyate |

	agniṣṭomam avāpnoti datvaiva mṛgalomikam ||

**[375]**	datvā valkalajaṃ vāso vasūnāṃ lokam āpnuyāt |

	vastrapradānāt tejasvī sarveṣāṃ priyadarśanaḥ ||

	bhavet saṃbhogavāṃś caiva strīṇāṃ caiva manoharaḥ ||

iti vastradānam |

athodakadānam |

saṃvartaḥ |

	vāridas tṛptim atulāṃ vitṛṣṇaḥ sarvavastuṣu |

bhaviṣyottare |

	śrīkṛṣṇa uvāca |

	atīte phālgune māsi prāpte caitramahotsave |

	puṇye 'hni viprakathite grahacandrabalānvite ||

	taḍākaṃ kārayed vidvān dhanacchāyaṃ manoramam |

	purasya madhye hy ath vā kāntāre toyavarjite ||

	devatāyatane vāpi citravṛkṣatale 'pi vā |

	suśītalataraṃ ramyaṃ vicitrāsanasaṃyutam ||

	kārayen maṇḍalaṃ divyaṃ śītātapasahaṃ dṛḍham |

	tanmadhye sthāpayed bhavyān maṇīn kumbhāṃś ca śobhanān ||

	akālamūlān kavakān vastreṇāveṣṭitānanān |

	brāhmaṇaḥ śīlasaṃpanno bhṛtiṃ datvā yathocitām ||

	prapāpālaḥ prakartavyo bahuputraparicchadaḥ |

	pānīyapānam aśrānto yaḥ kārayati mānavān ||

	evaṃvidhāṃ prapāṃ kṛtvā śubhe 'hni vidhipūrvakam |

	yathāśaktyā naraśreṣṭhaḥ prārambhe bhojayed dvijān ||

	tataś cotsarjayed vidvān mantreṇānena mānavaḥ |

	prapeyaṃ sarvasāmānyā bhūtebhyaḥ pratipāditā ||

	asyāḥ pradānāt pitaras tṛpyantu ca pitāmahāḥ |

	anivāryaṃ tato deyaṃ jalaṃ sāmacatuṣṭayam ||

	tripakṣaṃ vā mahārāja jīvānāṃ jīvanaṃ param |

	gandhāḍhyaṃ sarasaṃ śītaṃ śobhane bhājane sthitam ||

**[376]**	pradadyād apratihataṃ śraddhāvān avalokayan |

	pratyahaṃ kārayet tasya bhojanaṃ śaktito dvije ||

	anena vidhinā yas tu grīṣme śoṣavināśanam |

	pānīyam uttamaṃ dadyāt tasya puṇyaphalaṃ śṛṇu ||

	kapilāśatadānasya samyagdattasya yat phalam |

	tat puṇyaphalam āpnoti sarvadevais tu pūjitaḥ ||

	pūrṇacandrapratīkāśaṃ vimānaṃ so 'dhiruhya vai |

	yāti devendrabhavanaṃ pūjyamāno 'psarogaṇaiḥ ||

	triṃśatkoṭyo hi varṣāṇāṃ yakṣagandarvasevitaḥ |

	puṇyakṣayād ihāgatya caturvedo dvijo bhavet ||

	tataḥ param idaṃ yāti punarāvṛttir durlabham |

	prapāṃ dātum aśaktena viśeṣād dharmam īpsunā ||

	pratyahaṃ dharmaghaṭakaḥ karpaṭāveṣṭitānanaḥ |

	brāhmaṇasya gṛhe deyaḥ śītāmalajalaḥ śuciḥ ||

	tasya vodyāpanaṃ kāryaṃ māsi māsi narādhipa |

	maṇḍakāveṣṭikābhiś ca pakvānnaiḥ sarvakāmikaiḥ ||

	uddiśya śaṃkaraṃ viṣṇuṃ brahmāṇaṃ vāsavaṃ tathā |

	salilaṃ prokṣayitvā tu mantreṇānena mānavaḥ ||

	eṣa dharmaghaṭo datto brahmaviṣṇuśivātmakaḥ |

	asya prasādāt(dānāt) sakalā mama santu manorathāḥ ||

	dharmaghaṭadānamantraḥ |

	anena vidhinā yas tu dharmakumbhaṃ prayacchati |

	prapādānaphalaṃ so 'pi prāpnotīha na saṃśayaḥ ||

	dharmakumbhapradāne 'pi aśakto yaḥ pumān bhavet |

	tenāśvatthataror mūlaṃ nityaṃ sevyaṃ yatātmanā ||

	aśvattharūpī bhagavān prīyatāṃ me janārdanaḥ |

	ity uccārya namaskṛtya pratyahaṃ pāpanāśanam ||

	yaḥ karoti taror mūle sekaṃ māsacatuṣṭayam |

	so 'pi tatphalam āpnoti śrutir eṣā sanātanī ||

**[377]	**spṛṣṭā suśītasalilā klamanāśinī ca prāpte parasya pathi pānthasamūhabhūmau |

	yasya prapā bhavati sarvajanasya bhogyā dharmān naraḥ sa khalu jīvati jīvaloke ||

iti bhaviṣyottare prapādānavidhiḥ \

mahābhārate |

	tilā nityaṃ pradātavyā yathāśakti dvijātibhiḥ |

	nityadānāt sarvakāmāṃs tilā nirvartayanty uta ||

	ghṛtapradānena tathā dīrghaṃ vindati jīvitam |

	datvā pratiśrayaṃ loke tathā datvaiva cābhayam ||

	tathā datvā kṣitiṃ vipro brahmaloke mahīyate |

naiveśikadāne kālikāpurāṇam |

	kārayitvā tathodvāhaṃ śrotriyāṇāṃ kuleṣu ca |

	vedavicchīlavṛtteṣu dvijeṣv ekādaśasv atha ||

	tato gṛhāṇi ramyāṇi kuryād ekādaśaiva tu |

	kārayitvā tu dhānyais tu vividhaiś caiva pūjayet ||

	dāsīgomahiṣīś cāpi śayanāsanapādukāḥ |

	bhājanāni vicitrāṇi tāmramṛnmayakāni ca ||

	pātrāṇi bhojanārthaṃ ca kṛtsnaṃ copaskaraṃ ca yat |

	lohaṃ ca kāñcanaṃ caiva vastrāṇi tu viśeṣataḥ ||

	saṃbhṛtyaivaṃ susaṃbhāraṃ tadgṛheṣu niyojayet |

	yojayec caiva vṛttyarthaṃ śaktito vā śataṃ śatam ||

	pṛthak pṛthag lāṅgalānāṃ nirvartanaśatāny api |

	viṣayaṃ kharvaṭaṃ kheṭaṃ grāmārthaṃ grāmam eva vā ||

	yojayet somamūrtiṃ ca cintya teṣu dvijeṣu vai |

	ekādaśaiva tās tatra dampatyoḥ pratimātmakāḥ ||

	vicintya parayā bhaktyā tadgṛheṣu niveśayet |

	grāhayed agnihotrāṇi praviśyaitad dvijottamān ||

	vidhipūrvaṃ yathānyāyyam ātmanaḥ śreyase naraḥ |

	aduṣṭakulajānāṃ ca vidhir eṣa ciraṃtanaḥ ||

	śivaśaktyor vibhāktānāṃ dvijānāṃ kārayet sadā |

	yaś ca preṣyān nijān mūḍho yojayed dhavyakavyayoḥ ||

**[378]**	na bhavet phalaṃ tasya daivikīṃ śrutir dhruvā |

	yajñadānavratādyaṃ ca tīrthayātrādikaṃ ca yat ||

	yas tv evaṃ kārayej jantus tena sarvam anuṣṭhitam |

	sa yāty arkasamānābhaṃ vimānaṃ ratnamālinam ||

	āruhya tatpadaṃ puṇyaṃ surastrībhir alaṃkṛtam |

	vinānaiś cāparair divyaiḥ sahasraiḥ parivāritam ||

	sarvalokagatān bhogān bhuktvā tasmin prapadyate |

	jñātvā svavittasāmarthyād ekaṃ codvāhayed dvijam ||

	tenāpy āpnoti tat sthānaṃ śivabhakto naro dhruvam |

	sthānena sthānasaṃprāptir vidhivat tena jāyate ||

dakṣaḥ |

	mātāpitṛvihīnaṃ tu saṃskārodvāhanādibhiḥ |

	yaḥ sthāpayati tasyeha puṇyasaṃkhyā na vidyate ||

ādityapurāṇe |

	bhūmipālaṃ cyutaṃ rājyād yas tu saṃsthāpayed dvijaḥ |

	tasya vāso munīndreha nākapṛṣṭhe na saṃśayaḥ ||

hiraṇyadāne bhārgavarāmaṃ prati visiṣṭhavākyāni |

	sarvaratnāni nirmathya tejorāśiṃ samutthitam |

	suvarṇam ebhyo viprendra ratnaṃ paramam uttamam ||

	etasmāt kāraṇād devā gandharvoragarākṣasāḥ |

	manuṣyāś ca piśācāś ca prayatā dhārayanti tat ||

	mukuṭair aṅgadayutair alaṃkāraiḥ pṛthagvidhaiḥ |

	suvarṇe vighṛte tatra virājati bhṛgūttama ||

	tasmāt sarvapavitrebhyaḥ pavitraṃ paramaṃ smṛtam |

	pṛthivīṃ gāṃ ca datveha tathānyad api kiṃcana ||

	viśiṣyate suvarṇasya dānaṃ paramakaṃ vibho |

	akṣayaṃ pāvanaṃ caiva suvarṇam iti kathyate ||

	prayaccha dvijamukhyebhyaḥ pāvanaṃ hy etad uttamam |

	suvarṇam eva sarvatra dakṣiṇāsu vidhīyate ||

**[379]**	suvarṇaṃ ye prayacchanti varṇadās te bhavanty uta |

	agnir hi devatāḥ sarvāḥ suvarṇaṃ ca tadātmakam ||

	tasmāt suvarṇaṃ dadato dattāḥ syuḥ sarvadevatāḥ ||

nandipurāṇe |

	kṛṣṇalāḥ pañca māṣās tu māṣaiḥ ṣoḍaśabhiḥ smṛtam |

	suvarṇam ekaṃ taddānād dātā svargam avāpnuyāt ||

tathā |

	tasmāt sarvātmanā pātre dadyāt kanakadakṣiṇām |

	apātre pātayed dattaṃ suvarṇaṃ narakārṇave ||

iti suvarṇadānam |

atha bhaviṣyottare vṛṣabhadānam |

	kṛṣṇa uvāca |

	vṛṣadānaphalaṃ puṇyaṃ śṛṇuṣva kathayāmi te |

	pavitraṃ pāvanaṃ caiva sarvadānottamaṃ tathā ||

	daśadhenusamo 'naḍvān ekaś caiva dhuraṃdharaḥ |

	daśadhenupradānād dhi sa evaiko viśiṣyate ||

	voḍhā caraṃś ca puṣṭāṅgo hy arogaḥ pāṇḍunandana |

	yuvā bhadraḥ suśīlaś ca sarvadoṣavivarjitaḥ ||

	trātā bhavati saṃsāre nātra kāryā vicāraṇā |

	alaṃkṛtya vṛṣaṃ śāntaṃ puṇye 'hni samupasthite ||

	raupyalāṅgalasaṃyuktaṃ brāhmaṇāya nivedayet |

	mantreṇānena rājendra taṃ śṛṇuṣva vadāmi te ||

	dharmas tvaṃ vṛṣarūpeṇa jagadānandakārakaḥ |

	aṣṭamūrter adhiṣṭhānam ataḥ pāhi sanātana ||

	datvainaṃ dakṣiṇāyuktaṃ praṇipatya visarjayet |

	saptajanmakṛtaṃ pāpaṃ vāṅmanaḥkāyakarmaṇā ||

	tat sarvaṃ vilayaṃ yāti godānena kṛtena vai |

	dānaṃ vṛṣabhasaṃyuktaṃ dīpyamānaṃ suśobhitam ||

	āruhya kāmagaṃ divyaṃ svarlokam adhirohati |

	yāvanti tasya romāṇi govṛṣasya mahīpate ||

	tāvad varṣasahasrāṇi gavāṃ loke mahīyate |

	golokād avatīrṇaś ca iha loke dvijo bhavet ||

**380]**	yajñayājī mahātejāḥ sarvabrāhmaṇapūjitaḥ |

	yathoktas te mahārāja deyo yasya vṛṣottamaḥ ||

	tad apy ahaṃ te vakṣyāmi pātraṃ prāṇapradaṃ nṛṇām ||

	ye kṣāntadāntāḥ śrutapūrṇakarṇā jitendriyāḥ prāṇivadhān nivṛttāḥ |

	pratigrahe saṃkucitā gṛhashās te brāhmaṇās tārayituṃ samarthāḥ ||

	tejasvinaṃ bharasahaṃ dṛḍhakandharaṃ ca yacchanti ye vṛṣam aśeṣaguṇopapannam |

	dattena yad bhavati godaśakena puṇyaṃ satyaṃ bhavanti bhuvi tatphalabhāginas te ||

iti bhaviṣyottare vṛṣadānam || 1.210 ||

_kiṃ ca |_

	**gṛhadhānyābhayopānacchatramālyānulepanam |**

**	yānaṃ vṛkṣaṃ priyaṃ śayyāṃ datvātyantaṃ sukhī bhavet || 1.211 ||**

gṛhādidātātyantam atiśayen sukhī bhavet | matsyapurāṇe gṛhadānam |

	matsya uvāca |

	pakveṣṭakā(ka)citaṃ kṛtvā śailajaṃ vāpi dārujam |

	mṛnmayaṃ vāpi kartavyaṃ śubhalakṣaṇasaṃyutam ||

	prabhūtabalipuṣpāḍhyaṃ dhenvā caiva samanvitam |

	arjunaiḥ saralaiḥ śākair anyaiś caiva manoharaiḥ ||

	tiniśaiḥ sarjavṛkṣaiś ca kadambaiḥ saha vañjulaiḥ |

	śubhasthānasamutpannair vāstulakṣaṇasaṃyutam ||

	sthāpanaṃ ca yathānyāyaṃ bhūmeś caiva suśobhanam |

	mārjanaṃ siñcanaṃ caiva śāstātīyena kārayet ||

śāntātīyena saṃ na indrāgnī iti sūktena |

	maṅgalāny upahārāś ca vāstuvidyoditās tathā |

	devatāpañcakaṃ tatra catvāriṃśatsamanvitam ||

	pūjayitvā yathānyāyaṃ tato dadyād gṛhaṃ gṛhī |

	ayane viṣuve puṇye vyatīpāte dinakṣaye ||

	yugādiṣūparāge ca tathā manvantarādiṣu |

	saṃkrāntau vaidhṛtidine paurṇamāsyaṣṭamīṣu ca ||

	yajñotsavavivāheṣu duḥsvapnānāṃ ca darśane |

	dravyabrāhmaṇasaṃpattau śraddhā vā yatra jāyate ||

**[381]**	gṛhadānaṃ tato deyaṃ saṃsārabhayabhīruṇā |

	anityaṃ jīvitaṃ yasmāl lakṣmīś cātīva cañcalā ||

	etaj jñātvā tu kartavyam aiśānyāṃ hastasaṃmitam |

	caturasraṃ samaṃ kuṇḍaṃ mekhalāyonibhūṣitam ||

	pūrvottare hastamitā ca vedī grahādideveśvarapūjanāya |

	tatrārcanaṃ brahmaśivācyutānāṃ sūryasya kāryaṃ phalapuṣpagandhaiḥ ||

	dvāreṣu kāryāṇi ca toraṇāni patrair api kṣīravanaspatīnām |

	madhye tu saṃsthāpya ca pūrṇakumbhaṃ sraggandhadhūpāmbararatnayuktam ||

	gṛhyoktena vidhānena hutvā cāgnimukhaṃ tataḥ |

	gavyena payasā divyaṃ sthālīpākacaruṃ śrapet ||

	tataś ca vai taṃ carukaṃ juhoti madhyasthitābhyo gṛhadevatābhyaḥ |

	baliṃ ca samyagvidhisaṃprayogāt kṣīreṇa dhārāṃ paritas tu dadyāt ||

	brahmāṇaṃ da(dī)kṣayet pūrvaṃ parituṣṭaṃ kṣamāpayet |

	śayyāṃ tu dakṣiṇo bhāge sopadhānāṃ sadīpakām ||

	sitavastrais tu saṃchannāṃ lakṣmīnārāyaṇānvitām |

	sitāmbaraṃ kuṇḍalahemabhūṣitaṃ keyūrakaṇṭhābharaṇābhirāmam |

	patnīsametaṃ ca kare gṛhītvā dātā paṭhen mantram imaṃ gṛhasthaḥ ||

	ehy ehi nārāyaṇa divyarūpa sarvāmarair arcitapādapadma |

	śubhāśubhānāṃ jagatām adhīśa lakṣmīyutas tvaṃ hi gṛhaṃ gṛhāṇa ||

	namaḥ kaustubhanāthāya hiraṇyakavacāya ca |

	kṣīrodārṇavasuptāya jagaddhātre namo namaḥ ||

	namo hiraṇyagarbhāya viśvagarbhāya vai namaḥ |

	carācarasya jagato gṛhabhūtāya vai namaḥ ||

	bhūlokapramukhā lokās tava dehe vyavasthitāḥ |

	nandanti yāvat kalpāntaṃ tathāsmin bhavane gṛhī ||

	tvatprasādena deveśa putraiḥ pautrair yuto dvijaḥ |

	pañcayajñakriyāyukto vased ācandratārakam ||

	evam uktvā tu deveśaṃ sapatnīkaṃ dvijottamam |

	tilaprasthoparisthāyāṃ śayyāyām upaveśya ca ||

**[382]**	vaded idaṃ tato vākyaṃ sarvadhānyayutaṃ gṛham |

	sarvopaskarasaṃyuktaṃ gṛhaṃ gṛhṇa dvijottama ||

	tatropakaraṇaṃ sarvaṃ dampatyos tu nivedayet |

	pādukopānahacchatrabhūṣaṇāsanabhājanam ||

	saṃpannaṃ cāpy asaṃpannaṃ gṛhopaskarabhūṣaṇam |

	sarvaṃ saṃpūrṇam evāstu tvatprasādāj janārdana ||

	anena vidhinā yas tu pakveṣṭaṃ vinivedayet |

	kalpakoṭiśataṃ yāvad brahmaloke mahīyate ||

	śailajaṃ dārujaṃ vāpi yo dadyād vidhipūrvakam |

	vaset kṣīrārṇave ramye nārāyaṇasamīpataḥ ||

	mṛnmayaṃ caiva yo dadyād gṛhaṃ sopaskarānvitam |

	putreṣu lokapālānāṃ pretyāmanvantaraṃ vaset ||

	kalikaluṣavimuktaḥ pūjitaḥ siddhasaṃghair amaracamaramālāvījyamāno 'psarobhiḥ |

	pitṛśatam api bandhūn putrapautraprapautrān api narakanimagnāṃs tārayed eka eva ||

	divyān bhogāṃs tato bhuktvā rājarājo bhaved bhuvi |

	nārāyaṇabalopeto nārāyaṇaparāyaṇaḥ ||

	nārāyaṇakathāsakto jīved varṣaśataṃ sukhī |

	devatāpañcakaṃ tatra catvāriṃśat samanvitam || iti |

atrāyaṃ vidhiḥ |

	ekāśītipadaṃ kṛtvā reṇubhiḥ kanakena ca |

	paścāl limpec cānulimpet sūtreṇāloḍya sarvataḥ ||

	daśa pūrvāyatā rekhā daśa caivodagāyatāḥ |

	sarvavāstuvibhāgeṣu vijñeyā navakā nava ||

	ekāśītipadaṃ kṛtvā vāstuvit sarvavāstuṣu |

	padasthān pūjayed devāṃs triṃśat pañcadaśaiva tu ||

	dvātriṃśad bāhyataḥ pūjyāḥ sūkṣmāś cāntas trayodaśa |

	nāmatas tān pravakṣyāmi sthānāni ca nibodhata ||

	īśānakoṇādi surān pūjayet padikān nava |

	śikhī caivātha parjanyo jayantaḥ kuliśāyudhaḥ ||

**[383]**	śūnyaḥ satyo bhṛśaś caiva ākāśe vāyur eva ca |

	pūṣātha vitathaś caiva gṛhakṣatayamāv ubhau ||

	gandharvo bhṛṅgarājaś ca mṛgaḥ pitṛgaṇas tathā |

	dauvāriko 'tha sugrīvaḥ puṣpadanto jalādhipaḥ ||

	asuraḥ śeṣapāpau ca rogo 'hir mukhya eva ca |

	bhallāṭaḥ somasūryau ca aditiś ca ditis tathā ||

	bahir dvātriṃśad ete tu tadantaś caturaḥ śṛṇu |

	īśānādicatuṣkoṇasaṃsthitān pūjayed budhaḥ ||

	āpaś caivātha sāvitro jayo rudras tathaiva ca |

	madhye navapade brahmā tasyāṣṭau ca samīpagān ||

	sarvān ekāntarān vidyāt pūrvādyān nāmataḥ śṛṇu |

	aryamā svitā caiva vivasvān vibudhādhipaḥ ||

	mitro 'tha rājayakṣmā ca tathā pṛthvīdharaḥ kramāt |

	aṣṭamas tv āpavatsas tu parito brahmaṇaḥ smṛtāḥ ||

	āpaś caipāvatsaś ca parjanyo 'gnir ditis tathā |

	padikānāṃ tu vargo 'yam evaṃ koṇeṣv aśeṣataḥ ||

	tanmadhye tu bahirviśad dvipadās te tu sarvadā |

	aryamā ca vivasvāṃś ca mitraḥ pṛthvīdharas tathā ||

	brahmaṇaḥ parito dikṣu tripadās te tu sarvataḥ ||

atraivaṃ prayogaḥ — gṛhamadhye samāṃ caturasrāṃ bhūmiṃ kṛtvā tatra sudhāliptāni daśa sūtrāṇi samāntarālāni pātayet tathaivottarāyatāni | evam ekāśītipadāni saṃpadyante | tatreśānakoṇage pade śikhī pūjyas tasya dakṣiṇato 'nantare parjanyaḥ | tadanantare dakṣiṇe pade svapaścimenaikīkṛte jayantaḥ | evaṃ taddakṣiṇa indraḥ | taddakṣiṇe śūnyaḥ | evaṃ taddakṣiṇe satyaḥ | evaṃ tddakṣiṇe bhṛśaḥ | tato dakṣiṇa ekasminn eva koṣṭha ākāśaḥ | taddakṣiṇe āgneyakoṇagṛha ekasminn eva koṣṭhe vāyuḥ | tataḥ paścime pūṣā | tataḥ paścime vitathaḥ | evaṃ tathā paścime gṛhakṣataḥ | tataḥ paścime gandharvaḥ | **[384]** evaṃ tataḥ paścime bhṛṅgarājaḥ | tatah paścime ekasminn eva mṛgaḥ | nairṛtakoṇa ekasminn eva pitṛgaṇaḥ | tata uttara ekasminn eva dauvārikaḥ | tata uttare sugrīvaḥ | viyavaduttare varuṇaḥ | evaṃ taduttare puṣpadantaḥ | evaṃ taduttare varuṇaḥ | evaṃ taduttare 'suraḥ | evaṃ taduttare śeṣaḥ | taduttare ekasminn eva pāpaḥ | vāyavyakoṇe rogaḥ | tataḥ pūrvasminn ahiḥ | tataḥ pūrvasmin mukhyaḥ evaṃ tatpūrvasmin bhallāṭaḥ | evaṃ tatpūrvasmin somaḥ | evaṃ tatpūrvasmin sūryaḥ | evaṃ tatpūrvasminn aditiḥ | ekasminn eva ditiḥ | madhye navasu padeṣv ekīkṛteṣu brahmā | tatpūrvasmin dakṣiṇottarābhyām ekīkṛte 'ryamā | tasya dakṣiṇata ekasmin savitā | tatpaścime padatraya ekīkṛte vivasvān | tataḥ paścima ekasminn eva vibudhādhipaḥ | tata uttare padatraya ekīkṛte mitraḥ | tata uttara ekasminn eva rājayakṣmā | tataḥ pūrvasmin padatraya ekīkṛte pṛthvīdharaḥ | tataḥ pūrvasminn evāpavatsaḥ | parjanyāt paścima ekasminn eva pada āpaḥ | ākāśāt paścima ekasminn eva sāvitraḥ | dauvārikāt pūrvasminn ekasmiñ jayaḥ | pāpāt pūrvasminn ekasmin rudra iti | bṛhaspatiḥ |

	rasānnnopaskarān gehaṃ viprebhyo yaḥ prayacchati |

	tasya na kṣīyate vaṃśaḥ svargam āpnoty anantakam || iti |

iti gṛhadānam |

viṣṇudharmottare |

	dhānyānām uttamaṃ dhānyaṃ kathitaṃ dvijapuṃgavaiḥ |

	dhānyebhyo 'pi paraṃ dhānyaṃ raktaśāliḥ prakīrtitaḥ ||

	raktaśāliḥ naro datvā sūryaloke mahīyate |

	tathā godhūmadānena vasūnāṃ lokam āpnuyāt ||

	priyo bhavati lokasya priyaṅguṃ yaḥ prayacchati |

	dadāti yas tu śyāmakaṃ tasya prīyanti devatāḥ ||

	anyeṣāṃ śūkadhānyānāṃ pradānanirato naraḥ |

	svargalokam avāpnoti nātra kāryā vicāraṇā ||

	mudgadaḥ śakralokaṃ tu yamalokaṃ tu māṣadaḥ |

	yatheṣṭalokam āpnoti tathā vipras tilapradaḥ ||

**[385]**	mayoṣṭakānāṃ dānena lokaṃ vai nairṛtaṃ vrajet |

	satīnacaṇake datvā lokaṃ vāruṇam āpnuyāt ||

	vāyavyaṃ ca masūrāṇi rājamāṣāṇi dhānadam |

	anyeṣāṃ śiṣṭadhānyānāṃ pradānāt svargam āpnuyāt ||

	ikṣumṛdvīkayor dānāt paraṃ saubhāgyam āpnuyāt ||

iti dhānadānam |

athābhayadānam |

tatra viṣṇuḥ: "annapradānādhikam abhayadānam | etatpradānenābhīṣṭalokam āpadyate" | saṃvartaḥ |

	bhūtābhayapradānena sarvān kāmān avāpnuyāt |

	dīrtham āyuś ca labhate sadā ca sumanā bhavet ||

nandīpurāṇe |

	mahatāṃ sūkṣmadehānāṃ tathā ca vyādhitātmanām |

	hiṃsrāṇāṃ saumyamūrtīnāṃ sarvadā hy abhayāt sukham ||

	varam ekasya sattvasya jīvitābhayarakṣaṇam |

	na tu viprasahasrasya gosahasraṃ sadakṣiṇam ||

mārkaṇḍeyapurāṇe |

	dhik tasya jīvitaṃ puṃsaḥ śaraṇārthinam āturam |

	yo nārtam anugṛhṇāti vairipakṣam api dhruvam ||

	yajñadānatapāṃsīha paratra ca na bhūtaye |

	bhavanti tasya yasyārtaparitrāṇe na mānasam ||

mahābhārate |

	lobhād dveṣād bhayād vāpi yas tyajec charaṇāgatam |

	brahmahatyāsamaṃ tasya pāpam āhur manīṣiṇaḥ ||

tathā |

	prāṇināṃ vadhyamānaṃ hi yaḥ śaktaḥ samupekṣate |

	sa yāti narakaṃ ghoram iti prāhur manīṣiṇaḥ ||

	catuḥsāgaraparyantāṃ yo dadyāt pṛthivīm imām |

	sattvebhyo 'thābhayaṃ yaś ca tayor abhayado 'dhikaḥ || iti |

rāmāyaṇe |

	vinaṣṭaḥ paśyato yasya rakṣituḥ śaraṇāgataḥ |

	ādāya sukṛtaṃ tasmāt sarvaṃ gacchaty arakṣitaḥ ||

manuḥ |

	yat kiṃcid api dātavyaṃ yācitenānasūyataḥ |

	utpatsyate hi tat pātraṃ yat tārayati sarvataḥ ||

	vāridas tṛptim āpnoti sukham akṣayam annadaḥ |

	tilapradaḥ prajām iṣṭāṃ dīpadaś cakṣur uttamam ||

**[386]**	bhūmidaḥ svargam āpnoti dīrgham āyur hiraṇyadaḥ |

	gṛhado 'gryāṇi veśmāni rūpyado rūpam uttamam ||

	vāsodaś candrasālokyam aśvisālokyam aśvadaḥ |

	anaḍuddaḥ śriyaṃ puṣṭāṃ godo bradhnasya viṣṭapam ||

	yānaśayyāprado bhāryām aiśvaryam abhayapradaḥ |

	dhānyadaḥ śāśvataṃ saukhyaṃ brahmado brahma śāśvatam || iti |

saṃvartaḥ |

	pādukopānahau chatraṃ śayanāny āsanāni ca |

	vividhāni ca ratnāni datvā dravyapatir bhavet ||

viṣṇuḥ: "chatradānena ca svargam āpnoti | upānahāṃ pradānenāśvatarayuktaṃ ratham" | mahābhārate |

	upānahau prayatnād yo brāhmaṇāya prayacchati |

	mandare kaṇṭakān sarvān viṣamān saṃtariṣyati ||

	śakaṭaṃ damyasaṃyuktaṃ dattaṃ bhavati caiva hi |

tathā |

	chatrado gṛham āpnoti gṛhado nagaraṃ tathā |

	upānahāṃ pradānena ratham āpnoty anuttamam ||

bṛhaspatiḥ |

	asipatravanaṃ mārgaṃ kṣuradhārāsamanvitam |

	tīkṣṇātapaṃ ca tarati chatropānatprado naraḥ ||

devīpurāṇe |

	annadānāśvagovastraraupyacchatrāsanāni ca |

	pretaloke praśastāni dānāny aṣṭau viśeṣataḥ ||

	kṣīraṃ dadhi ghṛtaṃ vāpi madhu tailaṃ guḍaṃ tathā |

	yaḥ prayacchati viprebhyo sa yamaṃ nopasarpati ||

śayyādāne viṣṇudharmottareṣu |

	śayyādānena cāpnoti bhāryāṃ brāhmaṇasattamaḥ |

	datvā dvijāya śayanaṃ svāstīrṇaṃ sottaracchadam ||

	kule mahati saṃbhūtāṃ rūpadraviṇasaṃyutām |

	tathā pakṣavatīṃ bhāryāṃ prāpnoti vaśagāṃ tathā ||

	anenaiva ca dānena bhāryā patim āpnuyāt ||

tathā |

	vitānakapradānena sarvapāpaiḥ pramucyate |

	chatadaś ca tathā vipro nātra kāryā vicāraṇā ||

**[387]**	chatraṃ śataśalākaṃ tu datvaivātapavāraṇam |

	sarvapāpavinirmuktaḥ svargaloke mahīyate ||

	yāmyaṃ mārgaṃ tathā yāti sukhena dvijasattama |

	upānahau tathā datvā ślakṣṇe snehasamanvite ||

	ratham aśvatarīyuktaṃ tridivaṃ pratipadyate |

	sarvapāpavinirmukto yāmyaṃ mārgaṃ sukhaṃ vrajet ||

	mālyadaḥ śriyam āpnoti phaladaḥ saphalāḥ kriyāḥ |

	anulepanadānena sarvatāpaiḥ pramucyate ||

tathā |

	naraś candanadānena rūpavān abhijāyate |

	saubhāgyakārakaṃ proktaṃ pradānaṃ kuṅkumasya ca ||

	tathā karpūradānena sarvān kāmān avāpnuyāt |

	mṛganābhipradānena yaśasā bhuvi rājate ||

vāyupurāṇe |

	candanānāṃ pradātāraḥ śaṅkhānāṃ mauktikasya ca |

	pāpakartṝn api pitṝṃs tārayanti yathā śrutiḥ ||

vṛkṣadānaṃ mahābhārate |

	puṣpopagaṃ vātha phalopagaṃ vā yaḥ pādapaṃ lambayate dvijāya |

	sa strīsamṛddhaṃ bahuratnapūrṇaṃ prāpnoty ayatnopagataṃ gṛhaṃ vai ||

yamaḥ |

	devatāpuṣpadānena jāyate śrīsamanvitaḥ |

	ūrdhvaṃ gatim avāpnoti yaś ca dhūpaprado naraḥ ||

	garbhauṣadham athābhyaṅgaṃ mākṣikaṃ lavaṇaṃ tathā |

	yaḥ prayacchati viprāya saubhāgyaṃ tu sa vindati ||

	annapradānād āpnoti yān kāmān manasepsitān |

	pānīyasya pradānena tṛptiṃ vindati śāśvatīm ||

viṣṇuḥ |

	yad yad iṣṭatamaṃ loke yac casya dayitaṃ gṛhe |

	tat tad guṇavate dayeṃ tad evākṣayam icchatā ||

bhaviṣyottare śayyādānam |

	śrīkṛṣṇa uvāca |

	śayyādānaṃ pravakṣyāmi tava pāṇḍukulodvaha |

	yāṃ datvā sukhabhāgī syād iha loke paratra ca ||

	anityaṃ jīvitaṃ yasmāt paścāt ko 'nyaḥ pradāsyati |

	tāvat sa bandhuḥ sa pitā yāvaj jīvati bhārata ||

**[388]**	mṛto mṛta it jñātvā kṣaṇāt sneho nivartate |

	tasmād yatnena dātavyaṃ svayaṃ bhojyaphalādikam ||

	ātmaiva hy ātmano bandhur iti saṃcintya cetasā |

	ātmaiva yadi nātmānaṃ dānadharmaiḥ prapūjayet ||

	ko 'nyo hitakaras tasmād yaḥ paścāt pūjayiṣyati |

	tasmāc chayyāṃ samāsādya sāradārumayīṃ dṛḍhām ||

	sudantapatraracanāṃ hemapaṭṭair alaṃkṛtām |

	haṃsatūlīparicchannāṃ śubhagaṇḍopadhānakām ||

	pracchādanapaṭīyuktāṃ dhūpagandhādhivāsitām |

	tasyāṃ saṃsthāpayed dhaimaṃ hariṃ lakṣmyā samanvitam ||

	tacchīrṣake ghṛtayutaṃ kalaśaṃ parikalpayet |

	vijñeyaḥ pāṇḍava sadā sa nidrākalaśo budhaiḥ ||

	tāmbūlakuṅkumakṣodakarpūrāgurucandanam |

	dīpakopānahacchatracāmarāsanabhājanam ||

	pārśveṣu sthāpayed bhaktyā sapta dhānyāni caiva hi |

	śayanasthasya bhavati yad anyad upakārakam ||

	śṛṅgārakaravādyaṃ ca pañcavarṇavitānakam |

	śayyām evaṃvidhāṃ kṛtvā brāhmaṇāyopapādayet ||

	sapatnīkāya viprāya puṇye 'hni vidhipūrvakam |

	yathā na kṛṣṇa bhavataḥ śūnyā sāgarajā tathā ||

	śayyā mamāpy aśūnyāstu tathā janmani janmani |

	datvaivaṃ talpam amalaṃ praṇipatya visarjayet ||

	ekādaśe(śā)he 'pi tathā vidhir eṣa prakīrtitaḥ |

	dadāti yadi dharmārthaṃ bāndhavo bāndhave mṛte ||

	viśeṣaṃ cātra rājendra kathyamānaṃ niśāmaya |

	tenopabhuktaṃ yad vastu kiṃcit pūrvaṃ gṛhe satā ||

	tadgātralagnaṃ ca tathā vastravāhanabhājanam |

	yad yad iṣṭaṃ ca tasyāsīt tat sarvaṃ parikalpayet ||

**[389]**	tathaiva puruṣaṃ haimaṃ tasyāṃ saṃsthāpayet tadā |

	pūjayitvā pradātavyā mṛtaśayyā yathoditā |

	svarge puraṃdaragṛhe sūryaputrālaye tathā ||

	sukhaṃ vasaty asau jantuḥ śayyādānaprabhāvataḥ |

	pīḍayanti na taṃ yāmyāḥ puruṣā bhīṣaṇā naram ||

	na dharmeṇa na śītena bādhyate sa naraḥ kvacit |

	api pāpasamāyuktaḥ svargalokaṃ sa gacchati ||

	vimānavaram ārūḍhaḥ sevyamāno 'psarogaṇaiḥ |

	ābhūtasaṃplavaṃ yāvat tiṣṭhet pātakavarjitaḥ ||

	śayyāpradānam amalaṃ tava pāṇḍuputra saṃkīrtitaṃ sakalasaukhyanidhānabhūtam |

	tad yo dadāti vidhivat svayam eva nāke kalpaṃ vikalparahitaḥ sa vibhāti saukhyam ||

iti bhaviṣyottare śayyādānavidhiḥ || 1.211 ||

_kiṃ ca |_

	**sarvadharmamayaṃ brahma pradānebhyo 'dhikaṃ yataḥ |**

**	tad dadat samavāpnoti brahmalokam avicyutaḥ || 1.212 ||**

brahma vedas tadadhyāpayan brahmalokam avicyuto 'napabhraṣṭaḥ prāpnoti | atra hetuḥ — brahmaṇaḥ sarvadharmamayatvenānyebhyaḥ pradeyebhyo 'dhikam | prācurye mayaṭpratyayaḥ | yathā śālimayā magadhāḥ | annamayo yajña iti | abhede vā yathā — ānandamayaṃ brahmeti | abhedaś cātra pramāṇaprameyayor abhedopacāreṇa | bṛhaspatiḥ |

	sahasram eva dhenūnāṃ śataṃ cānuḍuhāṃ samam |

	śatānaḍutsamaṃ yānaṃ daśayānasamo hayaḥ ||

	daśavājosamā kanyā bhūmidānaṃ ca tatsamam |

	bhūmidānāt samaṃ nāsti vidyādānaṃ tato 'dhikam ||

yamaḥ |

	imāṃ pṛthvīṃ ca yo dadyāt sarvaratnopaśobhitām |

	dadyāc chāstraṃ ca viprāṇāṃ tac ca tāni ca tatsamam ||

brahmadānaprasaṅgena vidyāntaradānavidhir ucyate | tatra bhaviṣyottaram |

	vidyādānavidhiṃ vakṣye yāthātathyena te 'dhunā |

	yathātathyaṃ phalaṃ yac ca dattena yadunandana ||

**[390]**	śubhe 'hni viprakathite gomayena suśobhanam |

	kārayen maṇḍalaṃ divyaṃ caturasraṃ samantataḥ ||

	puṣpaprakarasaṃyuktaṃ svastikādisamanvitam |

	pustakaṃ tatra saṃsthāpya gandhapuṣpaiḥ samarcayet ||

	sauvarṇīṃ lekhanī kāryā raupyaṃ ca maṣibhājanam |

	dīpajvālāsamudbhūtakajjalena maṣī bhavet ||

	audumbarāmatrapāṇighṛṣṭabolarasānvitā |

	lekhakaṃ pūjayitvā tu prārabdhaṃ kārayet sudhīḥ ||

	vinītaś cāpramattaś ca tataḥ prabhṛti lekhakaḥ |

	mātrānusvārasaṃyuktaṃ padacchedaiḥ samanvitam ||

	samāni samaśīrṣāṇi vartulāni ghanāni ca |

	mātrāsu pratibaddhāni yo jānāti sa lekhakaḥ ||

	lekhayed akṣarāṇīha tadgatenāntarātmanā |

	granthānāṃ pañcakaṃ vātha daśakaṃ viṃśam eva vā ||

	triṃśaṃ vā catvāriṃśaṃ vā paraṃ pañcāśakaṃ sudhīḥ |

	padavākyapramāṇajño madhurasnigdhabhuk śuciḥ ||

	sāmājikeṣu tṛpteṣu hṛṣṭeṣu ca śanaiḥ śanaiḥ |

	niṣpādayitvā sacchāstraṃ śaivaṃ vāpy atha vaiṣṇavam ||

	niṣpādite punaḥ pūjyo lekhako vastrabhūṣaṇaiḥ |

	saṃpūjayitvā tacchāstraṃ deyam guṇavate tathā ||

	śāstrasaṃbhāvaviduṣe vācake ca priyaṃvade |

	vastrayugmena(ṇa) saṃyuktaṃ pustakaṃ pratipādayet ||

	sāmānyaṃ sarvalokānāṃ sthāpayed atha vā maṭhe |

	anena vidhinā datvā yat phalaṃ prāpnuyān naraḥ ||

	tad ahaṃ te pravakṣyāmi yudhiṣṭhira nibodha me |

	yat phalaṃ tīrthayātrāyāṃ yat puṇyaṃ yajñayājinām ||

	kapilānāṃ sahasreṇa samyag dattena yat phalam |

	tat phalaṃ samavāpnoti pustakaikapradānataḥ ||

**[391]**	purāṇaṃ bhārataṃ vāpi rāmāyaṇam athāpi vā |

	datvā yat phalam āpnoti pārtha tat kena varṇyate ||

	prātar utthāya yaḥ śiṣyān adhyāpayati yatnataḥ |

	vedaśāstraṃ tu paṭhitaṃ kīrtitaṃ sadṛśaṃ kṛtam ||

	upādhyāyasya yo vṛttiṃ datvādhyāpayate dvijān |

	kiṃ na dattaṃ bhavet tena dharmakāmārthadarśitā ||

	chātrāṇāṃ bhojanābhyaṅgaṃ vastraṃ bhikṣām athāpi vā |

	datvā prāpnoti puruṣaḥ sarvvakāmān asaṃśayaḥ ||

	viveko jīvitaṃ dīrghaṃ sarvakāmārthasaṃpadaḥ |

	sarvaṃ tena bhaved dattaṃ chātrāṇāṃ bhojane kṛte ||

	śastraśāstrakalāśilpaṃ yo yam icched upārjitam |

	tasyopakārakaraṇe pārtha kāryaṃ sadā manaḥ ||

	vājapeyasahasrasya samyag iṣṭasya yat phalam |

	tat phalaṃ samavāpnoti vidyādānān na saṃśayaḥ ||

	śivālaye viṣṇugṛhe sūryasya bhavane tathā |

	yaḥ kārayati dharmātmā sadā pustakavācanam ||

	gobhūhiraṇyavāsāṃsi śayanāny āsanāni ca |

	pratyahaṃ tena dattāni bhavanti puruṣarṣabha ||

	dharmādharmau na jānāti vidyāvirahitaḥ pumān |

	tasmāt sarvatra dharmātmā vidyādānarato bhavet ||

	trailokyaṃ catu(tvā)ro varṇāś catvāraś cāśramāḥ pṛthak |

	brahmādyā devatāḥ sarvā vidyādāne pratiṣṭhitāḥ ||

	caturyugāni(ṇi) rājendra ekasaptatisaṃkhyayā |

	kalpaṃ viṣṇupure tiṣṭhan pūjyamānaḥ surottamaiḥ ||

	kṣitiṃ cāgatya kālānte rājā bhavati dhārmikaḥ |

	hastyaśvarathayānāḍhyo dātā bhoktā vimatsarī ||

	rūpasaubhāgyasaṃpanno dīrghāyur nirujo bhavet |

	putrapautraiḥ parivṛto jīvec ca śaradāṃ śatam ||

	dānaṃ viśeṣaphaladaṃ jagatīha nānyadvidyāṃ vihāya vadanābjakṛtādhivāsām |

	gobhūhiraṇyagajavājirathādi sarvaṃ tāṃ yacchatā kim iha pārtha bhaven na dattam ||

**[392]**

iti bhaviṣyottare vidyādānavidhiḥ \

matsyapurāṇe |

	matsya uvāca |

	purāṇaṃ sarvaśāstrāṇāṃ prathamaṃ brahmanā smṛtam |

	anantaraṃ ca vaktrebhyo vedā yasya vinirgatāḥ ||

	purāṇam ekam evāsīt tasmin kālāntare 'pi ca |

	trivargasādhanaṃ puṇyaṃ śatakoṭipravistaram ||

	tadartho 'tra caturlakṣaiḥ saṃkṣepeṇa pradarśitaḥ |

	purāṇāni daśāṣṭau ca sāṃprataṃ tad ihocyate ||

	nāmatas tān pra(ni)vakṣyāmi śṛṇudhvam ṛṣisattamāḥ |

	brahmaṇābhihitaṃ pūrvaṃ yāvanmātraṃ marīcaye ||

	brāhmaṃ taddaśasāhasraṃ purāṇaṃ parikīrtyate |

	likhitvā tac ca yo dadyāj jaladhenusamanvitam ||

	vaiśākhapaurṇamasyāṃ tu brahmaloke mahīyate ||

granthaḥ 10,000 iti brahmapurāṇadānavidhiḥ | (1)

	etad eva yadā padmam abhūd dhairaṇmayaṃ jagat |

	tat kathāntāśrayaṃ tadvat pādmam ity ucyate budhaiḥ ||

	pādmaṃ tat pañcapañcāśatsahasrāṇīha paṭhyate |

	tat purāṇaṃ ca yo dadyāt suvarṇakamalānvitam ||

	jyeṣṭhe māsi tilair yuktaṃ so 'śvamedhaphalaṃ labhet ||

granthaḥ 55,000 iti padmapurāṇadānavidhiḥ | (2)

	vārāhakalpavṛttāntam adhikṛtya parāśaraḥ |

	yat prāha dharmān akhilāṃs tad yuktaṃ vaiṣṇavaṃ viduḥ ||

	tadāṣāḍhe tu yo dadyād ghṛtadhenusamanvitam |

	paurṇamāsyāṃ vipūtātmā sa padaṃ yāti vāruṇam ||

	trayoviṃśatisāhasraṃ tat purāṇaṃ vidur budhāḥ ||

granthaḥ 23,000 iti viṣṇupurāṇadānavidhiḥ | (3)

	śrutakalpaprasaṅgena dharmān vāyur ihābravīt |

	yatra tad vāyavīyaṃ syād rudramāhātmyasaṃyutam ||

	caturviṃśatisāhasraṃ purāṇaṃ tad ihocyate |

	śrāvaṇyāṃ śrāvaṇe māsi guḍadhenusamanvitam ||

**[393]**	yo dadyād dadhisaṃyuktaṃ brāhmaṇāya kuṭumbine |

	śivaloke sa pūtātmā kalpam ekaṃ vasen naraḥ ||

granthaḥ 24,000 iti vāyupurāṇadānavidhiḥ | (4)

	yatrādhikṛtya gāyatrīṃ varṇyate dharmavistaraḥ |

	vṛtrāsuravadhopetaṃ tad bhāgavatam ucyate ||

	likhitvā tac ca yo dadyād dhemasiṃhasamanvitam |

	paurṇamāsyāṃ prauṣṭhapadyāṃ sa yāti paramaṃ padam ||

	aśṭādaśa sahasrāṇi purāṇaṃ tat prakīrtitam |

granthaḥ 18,000 iti bhāgavatapurāṇadānavidhiḥ |

	yatrāha nārado dharmān bṛhatkalpāśrayāṃs tv iha |

	pañcaviṃśatsahasrāṇi nāradīyaṃ tad ucyate ||

	tad iṣe pañcadaśyāṃ tu yo dadyād dhenusaṃyutam |

	paramāṃ siddhim āpnoti punarāvṛttidurlabhām ||

granthaḥ 25,000 iti nāradapurāṇadānam | (6)

	yatrādhikṛtya śakunīn dharmādharmavicāraṇam |

	purāṇaṃ navasāhasraṃ mārkaṇḍeyam ihocyate ||

	parilekhya ca yo dadyāt sauvarṇakarisaṃyutam |

	kārtikyāṃ pauṇḍarīkasya yajñasya phalabhāg bhavet ||

granthaḥ 9,000 iti mārkaṇḍeyadānavidhiḥ | (7)

	yat tad īśānakalpasya vṛttāntam adhikṛtya ca |

	vasiṣṭhāyāgninā proktam āgneyaṃ tat pracakṣate ||

	lekhayitvā ca yo dadyād dhemapadmasamanvitam |

	mārgaśīrṣyāṃ vidhānena tiladhenuyutaṃ tathā |

	tac ca ṣoḍaśasāhasraṃ sarvakratuphalapradam ||

granthaḥ 16,000 ity āgneyapurāṇadānavidhiḥ | (8)

	yatrādhikṛtya māhātmyam ādityasya caturmukhaḥ |

	aghorakalpavṛttāntaprasaṅgena jagatsthitim ||

	manave kathayāmāsa bhūtagrāmasya lakṣaṇam |

	caturdaśa sahasrāṇi tathā pañcaśatāni ca ||

**[394]**	bhaviṣyaccaritaprāyaṃ bhaviṣyat tad ihocyate |

	tat pauṣe māsi yo dadyāt paurṇamāsyāṃ viśeṣataḥ ||

	guḍakumbhasamāyuktam agniṣṭomaphalaṃ labhet |

granthaḥ 14,500 | iti bhaviṣyatpurāṇadānavidhiḥ | (9)

	rathantarasya kalpasya vṛttāntam adhikṛtya ca |

	savarṇir nāradāyāha kṛṣṇamāhātmyam uttamam ||

	yatra brahmavarāhasya caritaṃ varṇyate mahat |

	tad aṣṭādaśasāhasraṃ brahmavaivartam ucyate ||

	purāṇaṃ brahmavaivartaṃ yo dadyān māghamāsi ca |

	paurṇamāsyāṃ ca bhagavan braahmaloke mahīyate ||

granthaḥ 18,000 iti brahmavaivartadānavidhiḥ | (10)

	yatrāgniliṅgamadhyasthaḥ prāha devo maheśvaraḥ |

	dharmārthakāmamokṣārtham āgneyam adhikṛtya ca ||

	kalpaṃ tal laiṅgam ity uktaṃ purāṇaṃ brahmaṇā svayam |

	tad ekādaśasāhasraṃ phālgune yaḥ prayacchati ||

	tiladhenusamāyuktaṃ sa yāti śivasātmyatām ||

granthaḥ 11,000 iti liṅgapurāṇadānavidhiḥ | (11)

	mahāvarāhasya punar māhātmyam adhikṛtya ca |

	viṣṇunābhihitaṃ kṣoṇyai tad varāham ihocyate ||

	mānavasya prasaṅgena kalpasya munisattamāḥ |

	caturviṃśatisāhasraṃ purāṇaṃ tad ihocyate ||

	kāñcanaṃ garuḍaṃ kṛtvā tiladhenusamanvitam |

	paurṇamāsyāṃ ca yo dadyād brāhmaṇāya kuṭumbine ||

	varāhasya pradānena padam āpnoti vaiṣṇavam |

granthaḥ 24,000 iti vārāhapurāṇadānavidhiḥ | (12)

	yatra māheśvaraṃ dharmam adhikṛtya ca ṣaṇmukhaḥ |

	kalpe tān puruṣe vṛttacaritair upaśobhitam ||

	skāndaṃ nāma purāṇaṃ tad ekāśītir nigadyate |

	sahasrāṇi śataṃ caikam iti yatnena paṭhyate ||

**[395]**	paralekhya ca yo dadyād dhemaśūlasamanvitam |

	śaivaṃ padam avāpnoti mīne copagate ravau ||

granthaḥ 81,100 iti skandapurāṇadānavidhiḥ | (13)

	trivikramasya māhātmyam adhikṛtya caturmukhaḥ |

	trivargam abhyadhād yatra vāmanaṃ parikīrtyate ||

	purāṇaṃ daśasāhasraṃ khyātaṃ kalpānugaṃ śivam |

	yac ca tad viṣuve dadyād vaiṣṇavaṃ yāty asau padam ||

granthaḥ 10,000 iti vāmanapurāṇadānavidhiḥ | (14)

	yatra dharmārthakāmānāṃ mokṣasya ca rasātale |

	māhātmyaṃ kathayāmāsa kūrmarūpī janārdanaḥ ||

	indradhyumnaprasaṅgena ṛṣīṇāṃ śakrasaṃnidhau |

	saptadaśa sahasrāṇi lakṣmīkalpānuṣaṅgikam ||

	yo dadyād ayane kaurmaṃ hemakūrmasamanvitam |

	gosahasrapradānasya sa phalaṃ prāpnuyān naraḥ ||

granthaḥ 17,000 iti kūrmapurāṇadānavidhiḥ | (15)

	śrutīnāṃ yatra kalpādau pravṛttyarthaṃ janārdanaḥ |

	matsyarūpī ca manave narasiṃhopavarṇanam ||

	adhikṛtyābravīt sapta saptakalpamunivratam |

	tan mātsyam iti jānīdhvaṃ sahasrāṇi trayodaśa ||

	viṣuve haimamatsyena dhenvā caiva samanvitam |

	yo dadyāt pṛthivī tena dattā bhavati cākhilā ||

granthaḥ 13,000 iti matsyapurāṇadānavidhiḥ | (16)

	yadā ca gāruḍhe kalpe viśvānte paruḍo bhavet |

	adhikṛtyābravīt kṛṣṇo gāruḍaṃ tad ihocyate ||

	tad aṣṭādaśakaṃ ceha sahasrāṇāṃ prapaṭhyate |

	sauvarṇahaṃsasaṃyuktaṃ yo dadāti śubhe 'hani ||

	sa siddhiṃ labhate mukhyāṃ śivaloke ca saṃsthitim ||

granthaḥ 18,000 iti garuḍapurāṇadānavidhiḥ | (17)

**[396]**	brahmā brahmāṇḍamāhātmyam adhikṛtyābravīt punaḥ |

	tac ca dvādaśasāhasraṃ brahmāṇḍaṃ dviśatādhikam ||

	bhaviṣyāṇāṃ ca kalpānāṃ śrūyate yatra vistaraḥ |

	tad brahmāṇḍapurāṇaṃ tu brahmaṇā samudāhṛtam ||

	yo dadyāt tadvyatīpāte patrorṇayugasaṃyutam |

	rājasūyasahasrasya phalaṃ prāpnoti mānavaḥ ||

granthaḥ 12,200 iti brahmāṇḍapurāṇadānavidhiḥ | (18)

iti mātsye vidyādāna |

nandīpurāṇe |

	śāstre yasmāj jagatsarvaṃ saṃśritaṃ ca śubhāśubham |

	tasmāc chāstraṃ prayatnena dātavyaṃ śubhakarmaṇā ||

	vidyāś caturdaśa proktāḥ krameṇa tu yathāsthiti |

	ṣaḍaṅgāś caturo vedā dharmaśāstraṃ purāṇakam ||

	mīmāṃsā tarka iti ca etā vidyāḥ prakīrtitāḥ |

	āyurvedaḥ sāmavedo bahubhedaḥ prakīrtitaḥ ||

	sarvottamā cātmavidyā saṃsārabhayanāśinī |

	sarvaduḥkhāntakaraṇī sarvapāpavināśinī ||

	etā vidyāḥ samākhyātā bahubhedopabhedataḥ |

	kalā vidyās tathā cānyāḥ śilpavidyās tathā parāḥ ||

	sarvā eva mahābhāga sadā sarvārthasādhikāḥ |

	sthitāś ca tāratamyena viśiṣṭaphalasādhikāḥ ||

	ātmavidyā pradhānā tu tathāyurvedasaṃjñitā |

	dharmapraṇayinīretāḥ kalāḥ sarvārthasādhikāḥ ||

	sasyavidyā ca vitatā etā vidyā mahāphalāḥ |

	yathaiko jīvati prāṇī kayāpi kila kutracit ||

	prayacchaty akṣayāṃl lokān vidhinā vāvidhānataḥ |

	śilpavidyāṃ naro datvā vaiṣṇavaṃ lokam āpnuyāt ||

	dharmaśāstraṃ naro datvā svarge kalpatrayaṃ vaset |

	ātmavidyāṃ tu yo dadyāt tasya saṃkhyā na vidyate ||

**[396]**	puṇyasya gadituṃ samyag api varṣaśatāyutaiḥ |

	etāvac chakyate vaktuṃ yat kalpāyutam uttamam ||

	satyaloke vasen martyo yatra brahmā vaset prabhuḥ |

	apy ekaṃ nīrujīkṛtya jantuṃ yādṛśatādṛśam ||

	āyurvedapradānena kiṃ na dattaṃ bhaved bhuvi |

	sasyavedapradānena saṃpannā yasya śālayaḥ ||

	kiṃ nāma na kṛtaṃ tatra puṇyaṃ bhavati śāśvatam |

	mīmāṃsāśāstramāhātmyād buddhvā vai vedanirṇayam ||

	kiṃ na nāma śubhaṃ dattaṃ yajñakarmaprvartanāt |

	ātmavidyā ca paurāṇī dharmaśāstrātmikā ca yā ||

	etad vidyātrayaṃ mukhyaṃ sarvadānakriyāphalaiḥ |

	dharmaśāstraṃ naro buddhvā yat kiṃcid dharmam āśrayet ||

	tasya dharmaṃ daśaguṇaṃ dharmaśāstrapradasya vai |

	purāṇākhānavidvāṃsaḥ pitṛdevārcane ratāḥ ||

	lokān sarvān kāmapūrṇān yānti sarvasubhodayān |

	purāṇavidhyādātāras tv anantaphalabhāginaḥ ||

	ātmavidyāpradātāro narā dharmasamāśrayāḥ |

	na punar yoninirayaṃ praviśanti duratyayam ||

	uttīrṇāḥ sarvapāpebhyaḥ saputrapaśubāndhavāḥ |

	mucyante nirayair ghorair asaṃkhyair yātanātmakaiḥ ||

tathā |

	ślokaṃ prahelikāṃ gāthām athānyad vā subhāṣitam |

	datvā prītikaraṃ yāti lokam apsarasāṃ śubham ||

	yad etat puṇyam ākhyātaṃ vidyādānasya sāṃpratam |

	deśakālavidhiśraddhāpātrayogāt tathāvidham ||

	prāpnoti koṭiguṇitaṃ phalaṃ vidyāprado naraḥ |

	yas tu puṇyaparo martyo jigīṣuḥ kīrtisādhakaḥ ||

	sa vidhānena vai dadyād vidyāṃ vividhakāmadām |

	evaṃ vidyāpradānena sarvakāmaguṇānvitam ||

**[398]**	yatnena pātre dātavyaṃ rahasyaṃ hy etad uttamam |

	uddiśya devatādattaṃ pradānaṃ yatra kutracit ||

	tasyāsamāptapuṇyasya kena puṇyaṃ (?) nirūpyate ||

asamāptaṃ puṇyaṃ yena so 'samāptapuṇyam |

	gurum ārādhya yatnena vidyāvyākhyānapāragam |

	śaktyā bhaktyā praṇāmena dhanaiḥ sarvair guṇais tathā ||

	yathā ghaṭapraticchannā ratnarājā mahāprabhāḥ |

	akiṃcitkaratāṃ prāptās tadvad vidyāś caturdaśa ||

	vinā tu guruṇā samyag bodhakena vipaścitā |

	naiva vidyāphalaprāptir guruṃ tasmāt tu pūjayet ||

	sragdāmabhūṣaṇair nityaṃ yathā devaṃ pinākinam |

	yo guruṃ pūjayen nityaṃ sthitaṃ vā prasthitaṃ ca vā ||

	tatprasādena yasmāt sa prāpnuyāt sarvasaṃpadam |

	tasmād guruṃ prayatnena mahādevavad arcayet ||

	bhaktyā prītyā prayatnena śraddhayā ca sadaiva hi |

	eṣa mātā pitā hy eṣa eṣ eva ca bāndhavaḥ ||

	eṣa cintāmaṇiś caiva eṣa eva ca me suhṛt |

	evaṃ śraddhāparo nityaṃ gurum ārādhayed budhaḥ ||

	ajñānduḥkhaśamanaṃ narakoddhāraṇaṃ tathā |

	kuto mātā pitā vāpi bāndhavo 'pi mahāguṇaḥ ||

	tādṛg abhyudayaṃ kuryād yādṛk kuryād gurur mahat |

	ko 'nyo jñānena duḥkhaughād uddhared bhavabandhaṇāt ||

	samyak śāstrārthaboddhāraṃ mahādevavad arcayet |

	vastumātreṇa yo jñānaṃ śāstrarūpam upanyaset ||

	sa tāvac chivavat pūjyo bhaktyā bhavabhayāpahaḥ |

	yas tu śāstravivakṣākhyaṃ viśeṣārthaṃ prapūjayet ||

	padavākyārthabodhena samyak śāstrapravartanāt |

	pūrvottarārthasaṃgatyā samudāyārthaniścayāt ||

	svaśāstrābhimatā vācaḥ samyag yo vetti tattvataḥ |

	sa tu sākāṇ mahābuddhir bhagavān iha śaṃkaraḥ ||

**[399]**	taṃ bhajet sarvabhāvena bhaktiyogena sarvadā |

	ādityena vinā yadvaj jagadandhaṃ vibhāvyate ||

	guruvākyaṃ vinā sarvaṃ tathaiva hi tamomayam |

	tasmād yathā mahādevaṃ tadvad eva guruṃ sadā ||

	yaḥ paśyati sa puruṣaḥ sarvadharmān avāpnuyāt |

	vidyā ca mukhyaṃ dānānāṃ guruto 'sya vidhiṃ punaḥ ||

	śrutvā vidheyaṃ vidhivac chraddhayā bhāvitātmanā |

	satyāṃ tebhyas tu tām dadyād viśeṣād guṇaśāliṣu ||

	upayogyaṃ ca yad yasya tat tasya pratipādayet |

	surālayeṣu sarveṣu yathāvibhavavistaraiḥ ||

	dātavyās tu prayatnena mahāpuṇyaphalārthibhiḥ |

	datvā tu pustakaṃ tatra pitṝṇāṃ dharmam uddiśet ||

	bāndhavānāṃ ca hṛdyānām anantaṃ phalam icchatā |

	tato datvā vidhānena tāṃ vidyāṃ śivamandire ||

	tataś ca bhojayed viprān rudrabhaktāṃś ca mānavān |

	yathāśakti ca kartavya utsavaḥ sveṣu veśmasu ||

	rājñā ca nagare kāryo grāme grāmādhipais tathā |

	gṛhe gṛhasthaiḥ kartavya utsavo bandhubhiḥ saha ||

	snātair bhuktaiḥ samālabdhaiḥ sragvibhiḥ susamāhitaiḥ |

	pratiyuktais tataḥ śrāvyaṃ śāstraṃ śraddhāsamanvitaiḥ ||

	vācakaṃ dakṣayet tatra yathāvibhavavistaraiḥ |

	guruṃ ca bhaktyā matimān yathāśakti na māyayā ||

	tataḥ puṣpaiś ca dhūpaiś ca śrāvakān saṃprapūjayet |

	vācako brāhmaṇaḥ prājñaḥ śrutaśāstro mahāmahāḥ ||

	abhyastākṣaravinyasto vṛttaśāstraviśāradaḥ |

	śabdārthavit pragalbhaś ca vinīto medhayānvitaḥ ||

	gītajño vākyavic chrāvyasvaro 'nāvilabhāṣakaḥ |

	guruś ca dharmavān prājñaḥ śrutaśāstro vimatsaraḥ ||

**[400]**	vipraḥ prakṛtasaṃśuddhaḥ śrutismṛtimukhaḥ sadā |

	suvṛttas tarkaśāstrajño dharmaśāstraviśāradaḥ ||

	svabhyastaśāstrasaṃdohaḥ prakṛtārthapravartakaḥ |

	nāprakramakṛtavyākhyaḥ paurvāparyārthaviṣṭadhī ||

viṣṭadhīḥ prakṛṣṭavāg ity arthaḥ | paurvāparyaviṣiṣṭadhīr iti pāṭhe paurvāparye viśiṣṭā saviśeṣā saṃbandhaprāpaṇātmikā dhīr yasyeti bhāvaḥ |

	adhyāyasargavicchedavibhaktārthaprayojakaḥ |

	saṃskāraiḥ saṃskṛtāṃ vidyāṃ prākṛtaiḥ prākṛtām api ||

	ālāpamātrair vyākhānair yaś ca śiṣyān prabodhayet |

	deśābhidhānavinyāsair bodhayec cāpi yo guruḥ ||

	sa guruḥ sa pitā mātā sa tu cintāmaṇiḥ smṛtaḥ |

	yaḥ śāstropāyam ākhyāya nakebhyaḥ samuddharet ||

	kas tena sadṛśo loke bāndhavo bhuvi vidyate |

	yasya vāgraśmisaṃdhena naśyate hṛdgataṃ tamaḥ ||

	mahāsaṃsārarajanībhavaṃ śokaṃ mahādyuteḥ |

	nodvijet tasya pāruṣye na ca vai lopya pṛcchataḥ ||

	na cāsya vyādhiduḥkheṣu malānāṃ cāpi śodhane |

	prasādayet tu kupitaṃ duḥkhmagnaṃ samuddharet ||

	rogebhyaś cāpi yatnena pairakṣen na codvijet |

	evaṃ vyākhyāṃ śubhāṃ śrutvā guruvaktrān narottamaḥ ||

	vidheyaṃ cintayed yatnāt paratra hitakāraṇam |

	śṛṇuyāc chraddayā yuktaḥ praṇato 'bhimato guroḥ ||

	bhiṣajāṃ vacanaṃ kāryaṃ gurūṇāṃ ca mahātmanām |

	na tatkṛtaṃ svayaṃ kuryāt te samiddhānalavat viṣaḥ ||

	aprastutakathākṣepaṃ yaḥ kuryād agrato guroḥ |

	sa brahmahatyām āpnoti guruvākeṣv aniścayāt ||

**401]**	yaś ca śrutvānyataḥ śāstraṃ saṃskāraṃ prāpya vā śubham |

	anyasya janayet kīrtiṃ guroḥ sa brahmahā bhavet ||

	vismārayec ca vā mauḍhyād yo 'pi śāstram uttamam |

	sa yāti narakaṃ ghoram akṣayaṃ bhīmadarśanam ||

	yas tu buddhvā naraḥ śāstraṃ kiṃcit kuryāc chubhāśubham |

	bhavec chataguṇaṃ tad vai vijñānaniratasya vai ||

	evaṃ vidhānato vācyaṃ vācakena vipaścitā |

	tapaḥ śamātmakaṃ bhogasvargādiphalasādhakam ||

	śanair vibhodhya vai vācyam adhyātmādi ca yad bhavet |

	kruddhotkiṃ yuddhasaṃkṣobhaṃ (?) dhārāvartena vācayet ||

	sarāgalalitair vākyair vācayed vṛddhasaṃgame |

	nānāvṛttānurūpeṇa lālityena ca vācayet ||

	sargādhyāyasamāptau ca kathāparyanta eva vā |

	praśastapadasaṃyoge kuryād iti virāmaṇam ||

	samāpte vācane 'bhīṣṭaṃ stūye(stuyā)d evaṃ vicakṣaṇaḥ |

	avadhārya jagacchāntim ante śāntyudakaṃ spṛśet ||

	sadehasuśrutaṃ bhūyād astu vyākhyānanityatā |

	lokaḥ pravartatāṃ dharme rājā cāstu jayī sadā ||

	dharmabāndhavasaṃpanno guruś cāstu nirāmayaḥ |

	iti procya yathāyātaṃ gantavyaṃ ca vibhāvya taiḥ ||

	śiṣyaiḥ parasparaṃ śāstraṃ cintanīyaṃ vicakṣaṇaiḥ |

	kathāvastuprasaṅgena nānāvyākhyānubhāvanaiḥ ||

	yuktibhiś ca smared vyākhyāṃ cihnaiś cāpi svayaṃkṛtaiḥ |

	evaṃ dine dine vyākhyāṃ śṛṇuyān niyato naraḥ ||

	samagraśāstraśravaṇena puṃsāṃ śraddhāpradhānaṃ bhavatīha cetaḥ |

	rāgaṃ ca śāstrātmakam abhyupaiti doṣāś ca nāśaṃ nikhilena yānti ||

	yathākathaṃcic chṛṇuyān na śāstram aśaddhayodāhṛtadharmasaṃghaḥ |

**[402]**	tataḥ samāptāv atha śāstrasargaiḥ kathodaye vāpi vinītabuddhiḥ ||

	śaktyārcayed vācakam agryam evaṃ guruṃ ca bhaktyā pitṛvat trikārthī ||

dharmārthakāmās trikaḥ |

	eṣa vidyāpradānasya pradhāno vidhir ucyate |

	anenaiva vidhānena brāhmaṇe śīlaśālini ||

	prabodhayati dhīyukta yuktijñe vedavedini |

	vinyasec ca śubhaṃ śāstraṃ mahāpuṇyajigīṣayā ||

vedavedini labdhaveda ity arthaḥ |

	dhanair vā vipulair dakṣayed guruṃ kṛtvā sutarpitam |

	adhyāpayec chubhāṇ śiṣyān abhijātān sumedhasaḥ ||

	evaṃ vidyāpradānaṃ tu sarvadānottamaṃ smṛtam |

	sarvadā sarvavarṇānāṃ narakaplavam uttamam ||

plava uttāraḥ |

	anena vidhinā datvā vidyāṃ puṇyaparo naraḥ |

	yat phalaṃ tv aśvamedhānāṃ śatasyāśu kṛtasya vai ||

	rājasūyasahasrasya samyag iṣṭasya yat phalam |

	tat phalaṃ labhate martyo vidyādānena bhāgyavān ||

	sarvasasyasusaṃpūrṇāṃ sarvaratnopaśobhitām |

	brāhmaṇebhyo mahīṃ datvā grahaṇe candrasūryayoḥ ||

	yat phalaṃ labhate martyo vidyādānena tat phalam |

	yāvad akṣarasaṃkhyānaṃ vidyate śāstrasaṃśraye ||

	tāvad varṣasahasrāṇi svarge vidyāprado vaset |

	yāyatyaḥ paṅktayas tatra pustake 'kṣarasaṃmitāḥ ||

	tāvato narakāt kulyān uddhṛtya nayate divi |

kulyā vaṃśyāḥ |

	yāvac ca patrasaṃkhyānaṃ vidyate pustake naraḥ |

	tāvad varṣasahasrāṇi sakulo modate divi ||

	yāvac ca pātakaṃ tena kṛtaṃ janmaśatair api |

	tat sarvaṃ naśyate tasya vidyādānena dehinaḥ ||

**[403]**	sa jāto manujo loke sa dhanyaḥ sa ca kīrtimān |

	yo vidyādānasaṃparkaprasaktaḥ puruṣottamaḥ ||

	yathāvibhavato vidyād vidyāṃ śāṭhyavivarjitaḥ |

	yāti puṇyamayāṃl lokān akṣayān bhogabhūṣitān ||

	ye 'pi patramaṣīpātralekhanīsaṃpuṭādikam |

	dadyuḥ śāstrābhiyuktāya te 'pi vidyāpradāyinām ||

	yānti lokāñ śubhān martyāḥ puṇyalokā mahādhiyaḥ |

	iti vidyāpradānasya mahābhāgyaṃ prakīrtitam ||

	śrutvaitat pātakair mukto niyataṃ saptajanmajaiḥ ||

iti nandipurāṇe vidyādānavidhiḥ |

atha matsyapurāṇe kalpadānam |

	kalpānukīrtanaṃ vakṣye sarvapāpapraṇāśanam |

	yasyānukīrtanād eva vīrapuṇyena yujyate ||

	prathamaḥ śvetakalpas tu dvitīyo nīlalohitaḥ |

	vāmadevas trtīyas tu tato rāthantaro 'paraḥ ||

	rauravaḥ pañcamaḥ proktaḥ ṣaṣṭhaḥ prāṇa iti smṛtaḥ |

	saptamas tu bṛhatkalpaḥ kandarpo 'ṣṭama ucyate ||

	satyo 'tha navamaḥ prokta īśāno daśamaḥ smrtaḥ |

	vyāna ekādaśaḥ proktas tathā sārasvato 'paraḥ ||

	trayodaś udānas tu gāruḍo 'tha caturdaśa |

	kaurmaḥ pañcadaśaḥ proktaḥ paurṇamāsī prajāpateḥ ||

	ṣoḍaśo nārasiṃhas tu samānas tu tato 'paraḥ |

	āgneyo 'ṣṭādaśaḥ proktaḥ somakalpas tataḥ paraḥ ||

	mīnakalpa iti proktas tat pumān iti cāparaḥ |

	vaikuṇṭhaś cāparas tasya lakṣmīkalpas tathāparaḥ ||

	caturviṃśas tataḥ proktaḥ sāvitrīkalpasaṃjñitaḥ |

	pañcaviṃśatamo ghoro vārāhas tu tato 'paraḥ ||

	saptaviṃśas tu vairājo gaurīkalpas tataḥ paraḥ |

	māheśvaras tataḥ proktas tripuraṃ yatra ghātitam ||

**[404]**	pitṛkalpas tathānte tu yā kuhūr brahmaṇaḥ smṛtā |

	ity ayaṃ brāhmaṇo māsaḥ sarvapāpapraṇāśanaḥ ||

	ādāv eva hi māhātmyaṃ yasmin yasmin vidhīyate |

	tasya kalpasya tannāma vihitaṃ brahmaṇā purā ||

	yas tu dadyād imān kṛtvā haimān parvaṇi parvaṇi |

	brahmaviṣṇupure kalpaṃ munibhiḥ pūjyate divi ||

	sarvapāpakṣayakaraṃ kalpadānaṃ tato bhavet |

	munirūpāṃs tataḥ kṛtvā dadyāt kalpān vicakṣaṇaḥ ||

iti mātsya kalpadānam |

athādeyāni |

tatra dakṣaḥ |

	sāmānyaṃ yācitaṃ nyastam ādhir dārāś ca taddhanam |

	anvāhitaṃ ca nikṣepaḥ sarvasvaṃ cānvaye sati ||

	āpatsv api na deyāni nava vastūni paṇḍitaiḥ |

	yo dadāti sa mūḍhātmā prāyaścittīyate naraḥ ||

sāmānyaṃ sādhāraṇam | yācitakaṃ parakīyaṃ kāryasiddhyartham ānītam | nyastanikṣiptayor bhedo dvitīyo 'dhyāye vakṣyate | dārāḥ kalatram | taddhanaṃ strīdhanam | anyasmai dātum anyena yad arpitaṃ tad anvāhitam | kātyāyanaḥ |

	vikrayaṃ caiva dānaṃ ca na deyāḥ syur anicchavaḥ |

	dārāḥ putrāś ca sarvasvam ātmanaiva tu yojayet ||

yojayet saṃdhayed ity arthaḥ |

	āpatkāle tu kartavyaṃ dānaṃ vikrayam eva vā |

	anyathā naiva kartavyam iti śāstrasya niścayaḥ ||

śātātapaḥ |

	vedavikrayanirviṣṭaṃ strīṣu yac cārjitaṃ dhanam |

	adeyaṃ pitṛdevebhyo yac ca klībād upāgatam ||

nirviṣṭaṃ prāptam | strīṣu vikrītāsv iti śeṣaḥ | klībān napuṃsakāt | tathā |

	dravyeṇanyāyalabdhena yaḥ karoty aurdhvadaihikam |

	na sa tat phalam āpnoti tasyārthasya durāgamāt ||

yamaḥ |

	suvarṇaṃ rajataṃ tāmraṃ yatibhyo yaḥ prayacchati |

	na sa tat phalam āpnoti tatraiva parivartate ||

**[405]**	pakvam annaṃ gṛhasthasya vānaprasthasya gorasaḥ |

	vṛttiś ca bhaikṣavṛttibhyo na deyaṃ puṇyam icchatā ||

vṛttiḥ kṣetrādikā | bhaikṣavṛttayo brahmacāriparivrājakāḥ |

	na śūdrāya havir dadyāt svasti kṣīraṃ tilān madhu |

	na śūdrāt pratigṛhṇīyāt teṣām anyan nivedayet ||

svatīti na brūyād ity arthaḥ | etac ca prākpraṇāmāt | tathā ca smṛtyantaram |

	apraṇāmagate śūdre na brūyāt svasti kutracit | iti |

teṣāṃ kṣīrādīnāṃ krayārtham anyad dravyaṃ śūdrāya nivedayet | aṅgirāḥ |

	bahubhyo na pradeyāni gaur gṛhaṃ śayanaṃ striyaḥ |

	vibhaktadakṣiṇā hy etā dātāraṃ tārayanti hi ||

vibhaktaḥ pṛthagbhūta eka iti yāvat | tatsaṃbandhinyo dakṣiṇā vibhaktadakṣiṇāḥ | kvacit pāṭhaḥ |

	vibhaktadakṣiṇā hy ete dātāraṃ na bhajanti hi | iti |

tasyārthaḥ — ete pratigrahītāraḥ kṛtadakṣiṇāvibhāgā dātāraṃ na bhajanti dānaphalanimittatayeti |

	ekā hy ekasya dātavyā na bahubhyaḥ kathaṃcana |

	sā tu vikrayam āpannā dahaty āsaptamaṃ kulam ||

ekā gaur dvibahubhyo dattā vikrayam āpadyate | tatrāyaṃ datur doṣaḥ |

	devatānāṃ gurūṇāṃ ca mātāpitros tathaiva ca |

	puṇyaṃ deyaṃ prayatnena nāpuṇyaṃ coditaṃ kvacit ||

pāpaṃ devatayā na kvacid vihitam ity arthaḥ | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">nanu</span> ca puṇyam anyasmai na śakyaṃ dātum anyena saha tasya svasvāmibhāvāpādanāsaṃbhavāt | na ca brahmadānābhayadānavad yathākathaṃcit saṃbandhamātraṃ tad dānam iti vācyam | saṃpradānasya puṇyasya ca saṃbandhamātram aśakyaṃ yataḥ | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">maivam</span> | vacanaprāmāṇyād deyasya pātrasya ca saṃbandhaḥ puṇyaṃ phalaṃ dadāti pātraṃ tat phalaṃ bhuṅkta ity evam ātmā kalpyate | tad anyathānupapattyā dīyamānāt puṇyāt pātre puṇyāntarodayaḥ phalabhogānuguṇaḥ parikalpyate | yat tu nyāyavidbhir uktam — śāstraphalaṃ prayoktarīti | tat prathamapuṇyodayaviṣayam | dvitīyādidharmotpattis tu vacanaprāmāṇyād aprayoktary api kalpyata eveti |

	na kevalaṃ pāpadānam avihitaṃ niṣiddhaṃ ca | tathā ca yamaḥ |

**[406]**	kalmaṣaṃ brāhmaṇo datvā dātā yāty aśubhāṃ gatim |

	vinirmokavinirmuktaḥ pannagendraḥ kṣato yathā ||

nandipurāṇe |

	pāpadaḥ pāpam āpnoti naro lakṣaguṇaṃ sadā |

	puṇyadaḥ puṇyam āpnoti śataśo 'tha sahasraśaḥ ||

	tathā pātraviśeṣeṇa dānaṃ syād uttarottaram |

	gurumātṛpitṛbrahmavādināṃ dīyate tu yat ||

	tal lakṣaguṇitaṃ vidyāt puṇyaṃ vā pāpam eva vā |

śātātapaḥ |

	praśnapūrvaṃ tu yo dadyād brāhmaṇāya pratigraham |

	sa pūrvaṃ narakaṃ yāti brāhmaṇas tadanantaram ||

idaṃ paṭhetyādeśaḥ praśnaḥ |

	mā dadasveti yo brūyād gavāgnibrāhmaṇeṣu ca |

	tiryagyoniśataṃ gatvā brāhmaṇeṣv abhijāyate || 1.212 ||

_idānīm adadato 'pi dānaphalaprāptyupāyam āha_ |

	**pratigrahasamartho 'pi nādatte yaḥ pratigraham |**

**	ye lokā dānaśīlānāṃ tān sa prāpnoti puṣkalān || 1.213 ||**

pratigrahasamartho 'pi pātrabhūto 'pi san yo gobhūhiraṇyādi na pratigṛhṇāti sa gavādidānaśīlānāṃ ye lokās tān puṣkalān avikalān prāpnoti || 1.213 ||

_sarvāpratigrahe prāpte kvacid apavādam āha_ |

	**kuśāḥ śākaṃ payo matsyā gandhāḥ puṣpaṃ dadhi kṣitiḥ |**

**	māṃsaṃ śayyāsanaṃ dhānāḥ pratyākhyeyaṃ na vāri ca || 1.214 ||**

kuśādikaṃ dīyamānaṃ na pratyākhyeyam | bṛṣṭā yavā dhānāḥ | manuḥ |

	śayyāṃ gṛhān kuśān gandhān āpaḥ puṣpaṃ maṇīn dadhi |

	matsyān dhānāḥ payo māṃsaṃ śākaṃ caiva na nirṇudet ||

tathā |

	edhodakaṃ mūlaphalam annam abhyuddhṛtaṃ ca yat |

	sarvataḥ pratigṛhṇīyān madhv athābhayadakṣiṇām ||

abhayadakṣiṇām abhayadānam ity arthaḥ | aṅgirāḥ |

	khalakṣetragataṃ dhānyaṃ vāpīkūpagataṃ jalam |

	abhojyād api tad grāhyaṃ yac ca goṣṭhagataṃ payaḥ ||

**[407]**	vicchinneṣv atha pakṣeṣu haviḥṣv āgrā(gra)yaṇeṣu ca |

	iṣṭiṃ tv adhikṛtāṃ kuryāt sukṛtaṃ ca na lopayet ||

pakṣaśabdena pakṣānte vihitāni karmāṇi lakṣyante | iṣṭiṃ tv adhikṛtāṃ kuryād iti yāgam uddiśya yācetety arthaḥ | na caivaṃ sukṛtaṃ lupyate |

	pakvānnavarjaṃ viprebhyo godānaṃ kṣatriyād api |

	vaiśyāt tu sarvadhānyāni śūdrād grāhyaṃ na kiṃcana ||

abhojyaviprādiviṣayam etat | [yat tu]

	yat tu kṣetragataṃ dhānyaṃ khale vātha gṛhād bahiḥ |

	sarvakālaṃ grahītavyaṃ śūdrebhyo 'py aṅgiromatam ||

	saṃskāraiḥ śudhyati hy evaṃ dhānyaṃ tena śuci smṛtam |

	tasmād āmaṃ grahītavyaṃ mṛtasūtyantareṣv api ||

iti, tad āpadviṣayam || 1.214 ||

	**ayācitāhṛtaṃ grāhyam api duṣkṛtakarmaṇaḥ |**

**	anyatra kulaṭāśaṇḍhapatitebhyas tathā dviṣaḥ || 1.215 ||**

ayācitam aprārthitam ātmānaṃ prati dātum ānītaṃ kulaṭādivarjitasya duṣkṛtakāriṇo 'pi grāhyam | kulaṭā svairiṇī strī | manuḥ |

	āhṛtām udyatāṃ bhikṣāṃ purastād apracoditām |

	mene prajāpatir grāhyam api duṣkṛtakarmaṇaḥ ||

	nāśnanti pitaras tasya daśa varṣāṇi pañca ca |

	na ca havyaṃ vahaty agnir yad tām abhyavapadyate ||

	cikitsakakṛtaghnānāṃ śalyahantus tu vārdhuṣeḥ |

	śaṇḍhasya kulaṭāyāś ca udyatām api varjayet ||

bhikṣāśabdenātra pakvānnam upalakṣyate | yamaḥ |

	cikitsakasya mṛgayor veśyāyāḥ kṛtakasya ca |

	ṣaṇḍhanartakayor eva udyatāṃ parivarjayet ||

vasiṣṭhaḥ |

	śastraṃ viṣaṃ surā cāpratigrāhyāṇi || 1.215 ||

**[408]**

_brāhmaṇasya nimittāntareṇa sarvataḥ pratigraham āha |_

	**devātithyarcanakṛte gurubhṛtyārtham eva ca |**

**	sarvataḥ pratigṛhṇīyād ātmavṛttyartham eva ca || 1.216 ||**

iti dānaprakaraṇam || 8 ||

devārcanādyarthaṃ sarvataḥ kṣatriyādito 'pi gṛhṇīyāt | sakalāvaśyakakarmopalakṣaṇaṃ caitat | ātmavṛttiḥ śarīradhāraṇamātram | na tu tṛptiḥ | yad āha viṣṇuḥ |

	gurūn bhṛtyāṃś cojjihīrṣann arciṣyan devatātithīn |

	sarvataḥ pratigṛhṇīyān na tu tṛpyet svayaṃ tataḥ ||

	eteṣv api ca kāryeṣu samarthaḥ san pratigrahe |

	nādadyāt kulaṭāśaṇḍhapatitebhyas tathā dviṣaḥ ||

aṅgirāḥ |

	gurvartham aitithīnāṃ vā bhṛtyānāṃ ca viśeṣataḥ |

	śūdrānnaṃ pratigṛhṇīyān na tu bhuṅkte svayaṃ tataḥ ||

yamaḥ |

	kūpārāmaprapākārī tathā vṛkṣapraropakaḥ |

	kanyāpradaḥ setukārī svargam āpnoty asaṃśayam ||

	taḍāge yasya pānīyaṃ satataṃ khalu tiṣṭhati |

	svargalokagatis tasya nātra kāryā vicāraṇā ||

	yeṣāṃ taḍāgāni śubhāḥ prapāś cārāmāś ca kūpāś ca pratiśrayāś ca |

	annapradānaṃ madhurā ca vāṇī teṣām ayaṃ caiva paraś ca lokaḥ ||

viśṇuḥ: "atha kūpakartus tatpravṛtte pānīye duṣkṛtārdhaṃ naśyati | tadutsargakṛn nityatṛpto vāruṇaṃ lokam aśnute | nālapradaḥ sadā tṛpto bhavati | vṛkṣaropayitur vṛkṣāḥ paraloke putrā bhavanti | vṛkṣapradasya vṛkṣāḥ pasūnair devān prīṇayanti | phalaiś cātithīṃś chāyayā cābhyāgatān deve varṣaty udakena pitṝn | setukṛt svargam āpnoti" | tathā |

	kūpārāmataḍāgeṣu devatāyataneṣu ca |

	punaḥsaṃskārakartā ca labhate maulikaṃ phalam ||

nandīpurāṇe |

	yo vāpīm atha kūpaṃ vā deśe toyavivarjite |

	khanayet sa naro yāti bindau bindau śataṃ samāḥ ||

	devair ekatvam atulaṃ tṛṣṇākṣudvarjitas tathā |

	taḍāgakartā vasate savarge yugacatuṣṭayam ||

**[409]**	yatra vipro 'tha gaur ekā pāyinī salilaṃ kvacit |

	taḍāgaṃ tādṛśaṃ kṛtvā svarge daś yugān vaset ||

tathā |

	yo vāpīm agnisākṣye ca vidhivat pratipādayet |

	koṇeṣūdakakumbhasthān samudrān arcya śraddhayā ||

	caturaś caturantā tu tena dattā mahī bhavet |

	tatsaṃnidhau dvijān arcya vidhivat pānabhojanaiḥ ||

	sa yāti vāruṇaṃ lokaṃ divyakāmasamanvitam |

matsyapurāṇe: "matsya uvāca —

	śṛṇu rājan mahābāho taḍāgādiṣu yo vidhiḥ |

	prāpya pakṣaṃ śubhaṃ śuklam atīte cottarāyaṇe ||

	puṇye 'hni vipraiḥ kathite kṛtvā brāhmaṇavācanam |

	prāg udakpravaṇe deśe taḍāgasya samīpataḥ ||

	caturhastā śubhā vediś caturaśrā caturmukhī |

	tathā ṣoḍaśahastaḥ syān maṇḍapaś ca caturmukhaḥ ||

	vedyāś ca parito gartā ratnimātrās trimekhalāḥ |

	nava saptātha vā pañca yonivaktrānvitā nṛpa ||

	vitatastimātrā yoniḥ syāt prāksaptāṅguliniḥsṛtā |

	gartāś ca tatra hastāḥ syus triparvocchritamekhalāḥ ||

	sarvataḥ sarvavarṇāḥ syuḥ patākādhvajasaṃyutāḥ |

	aśvatthodumbaraplakṣavaṭaśākhākṛtāni tu ||

	maṇḍapasya pratidiśaṃ dvārāṇy etāni kārayet |

	śubhās tatrāṣṭa hotāro dvārapālās tathāṣṭa vai ||

	aṣṭau tu jāpakāḥ kāryā brāhmaṇā vedapāragāḥ |

	sarvalakṣaṇasaṃpūrṇā mantravanto jitendriyāḥ ||

	kulaśīlasamāyuktāḥ sthāpakāḥ syur dvijottamāḥ |

	pratigarte tu kulaśā yajñopakaraṇāni ca ||

	vyajanaṃ cāmaraṃ śubhraṃ tāmrapātraṃ suvistaram |

	tatas tv anekavarṇāḥ syur balayaḥ pratidaivatam ||

**[410]**	ācāryaḥ prakṣiped bhūmāv anumantrya vicakṣaṇaḥ |

	triratnimātro yūpaḥ syāt kṣīravṛkṣavinirmitaḥ ||

	yajamānapramāṇaṃ vā saṃsthāpyo bhūtim icchatā |

	hemālaṃkāriṇaḥ kāryāḥ pañcaviṃśatiṛtvijaḥ ||

	kuṇḍalāni ca haimāni keyūrakaṭakāni ca |

	tathāṅgulīpavitrāṇi vāsāṃsi vividhāni ca ||

	dakṣayec ca samaṃ sarvān ācāryaṃ dviguṇaṃ punaḥ |

	dadyāc chayanasaṃyuktam ātmanaś cāpi yat priyam ||

	sauvarṇau kūrmamakarau rājatau matsyaḍuṇḍubhau |

	tāmrau kulīramaṇḍūkau vāyasaḥ śiśumārakaḥ ||

	evam āsādya tān sarvān ādāv eva viśāṃpate |

	śuklamālyāmbaradharaḥ śuklamālyānulepanaḥ ||

	sarvauṣadhyudakasnātaḥ snāpito vedapuṃgavaiḥ |

	yajamānaḥ sapatnīkaḥ putrapautrasamanvitaḥ ||

	paścimaṃ dvāram āśritya praviśed yāgamaṇḍapam |

	tato maṅgalaśabdena bherīṇāṃ ninadena ca ||

	rajasā maṇḍalaṃ kuryāt pañcavarṇena tattvavit |

	ṣoḍaśāraṃ tataś cakraṃ padmagarbhaṃ caturmukham ||

	caturaśraṃ ca parito vṛttaṃ madhye suśobhanam |

	vedyāś copari tat kṛtvā grahalokapatiṃs tataḥ ||

	vinyasen mantrataḥ sarvān pratidikṣu vicakṣaṇaḥ |

	jhaṣādīn snapayen madhye vāruṇaṃ mantram āśritaḥ ||

	brahmāṇaṃ ca śivaṃ viṣṇuṃ tatraiva sthāpayed budhaḥ |

	vināyakaṃ ca vinyasya kamalām ambikāṃ tathā ||

	śāntyarthaṃ sarvalokānāṃ bhūtagrāmaṃ nyaset tataḥ |

	puṣpabhakṣaphalair yuktam evaṃ kṛtvādhivāsayet ||

	kumbhāṃś ca ratnagarbhāś ca vāsobhir abhiveṣṭya ca |

	puṣpagandhair alaṃkṛtya dvārapālān samantataḥ ||

	paṭhadhvam iti tān brūyād ācāryas tv abhipūjayet |

	bahvṛcau pūrvataḥ sthāpyau dakṣiṇena yajurvidau ||

**[411]**	sāmagau paścime sthāpyāv uttareṇa tv atharvaṇau |

	udaṅmukho dakṣiṇato yajamāna upāviset ||

	yajadhvam iti tān brūyād dhotṛkān punar eva ca |

	utkṛṣṭamantrajapyena tiṣṭhadhvam iti jāpakān ||

	evam āmantrya tān sarvān paryukṣyāgniṃ ca mantravit |

	juhuyād vāruṇair mantrair ājyaṃ ca samidhas tathā ||

	ṛtvigbhiś caiva hotavyaṃ vāruṇair eva sarvaśaḥ |

	grahebhyo vidhivad dhutvā tathendrāyeśvarāya ca ||

	marudbhyo lokapālebhyo vidhivad viśvakarmaṇe |

	rātrisūktaṃ ca raudraṃ ca pāvamānaṃ sumaṅgalam ||

	japeran pauruṣaṃ sūktaṃ pūrvato bahvṛcaḥ pṛthak |

	śārṅgaṃ raudraṃ ca saumyaṃ ca kūṣmāṇḍaṃ jātavedasam ||

	sauraṃ sūktaṃ japeraṃs te dakṣiṇena yajurvidaḥ |

	vairājaṃ pauruṣaṃ sūktaṃ sauparṇaṃ raudrasaṃhitām ||

	śaiśavaṃ pañcanidhanaṃ gāyatraṃ jyeṣṭhasāma ca |

	vāmadevyaṃ bṛhatsāma rauravaṃ sarathantaram ||

	gavāṃ vrataṃ vikīrṇaṃ ca rakṣoghnaṃ ca yaśas tathā |

	gāyanti sāmagā rājan paścimadvāram āśritāḥ ||

	atharvaṇaś cottarataḥ śāntikaṃ pauṣṭikaṃ tathā |

	japeran manasā devam āśritya varuṇaṃ prabhum ||

	pūrvedyur abhito rātrāv evaṃ kṛtvādhivasanam |

	gajāśvarathāvalmīkasaṅgamahradagokulāt ||

	mṛdam ādāya kumbheṣu prakṣipec catvarāt tathā |

	rocanāṃ ca sasiddhārthāṃ gandhān guggulum eva ca ||

	snapanaṃ tasya kartavyaṃ pañcaratnasamanvitaiḥ |

	pūrvaṃ kartur mahāmantrair evaṃ kṛtvā vidhānataḥ ||

	evaṃ kṣapām atīvāhya vidhiyuktena karmaṇā |

	tatra prabhāte vimale saṃjāte tu śataṃ gavām ||

**[412]**	brāhmaṇebhyaḥ pradātavyam aṣṭāṣaṣṭir athāpi vā |

	pañcāśad vātha ṣaṭtriṃśat pañcaviṃśatir eva ca ||

	tataḥ sāṃvatsaraiḥ prokte śuddhalagne suśobhane |

	vedaśabdaiḥ sagandharvair vādyaiś ca vividhiaḥ śubhaiḥ ||

	kanakālaṃkṛtāṃ kṛtvā jale gām avatārayet |

	sāmagāya ca sā deyā brahmaṇāya viśṃpate ||

	pātrīm ādāya sauvarṇī pañcaratnasamanvitām |

	tato nikṣipya makaraṃ matsyādīṃs tāṃś ca sarvataḥ ||

	bhṛtāṃ caturbhir vipraiś ca vedavedāṅgapāragaiḥ |

	mahānadījalopetāṃ dadhyakṣatavibhūṣitām ||

	uttarābhimukhīṃ nyubjāṃ jalamadhye tu kārayet |

	atharvaṇena sāmnā ca punar mām ety ṛceti ca ||

	āpo hi ṣṭheti mantreṇa kṣiptvāgatya ca maṇḍapam |

	pūjayitvā sadasyāṃ tu baliṃ dadyāt samantataḥ ||

	punar dināni hotavyaṃ catvāri munisattama |

	caturthīkarma kartavyaṃ deyās tatrāpi śaktitaḥ ||

	dakṣiṇā rājaśārdūla varuṇaṃ saṃsmaret tataḥ |

	kṛtvā tu yajñapātrāṇi yajñopakaraṇāni ca ||

	ṛtvigbhyas tu samaṃ datvā maṇḍapaṃ vibhajet punaḥ |

	hemapātrīṃ ca śayyāṃ ca sthāpakāya nivedayet ||

	tataḥ sahasraṃ viprāṇām atha vāṣṭaśataṃ tathā |
