	bhojayeta yathāśakti pañcāśad vātha viṃśatim ||

	evam eva purāṇeṣu taḍāgavidhir ucyate |

	kūpavāpīṣu sarvāsu tathā puṣkariṇīṣu ca ||

	eṣa eva vidhir dṛṣṭaḥ pratiṣṭhāsu tathaiva ca |

	mantratas tu viśeṣaḥ syāt prāsādodyānabhūmiṣu ||

	ayaṃ tv aśaktāv ardhena vidhir dṛṣṭaḥ svayaṃbhuvā |

	svalpeṣv evāgnivat kāryaṃ vittaśāṭhyād ṛte nṛbhiḥ ||

**[413]**	prāvṛṭkālasthitaṃ toyam agniṣṭomasamaṃ smṛtam |

	śaratkālasthitaṃ yat syād amuṣyaphaladāyakam ||

	vājapeyātirātrābhyāṃ hemante śiśire sthitam |

	aśvamedhasamaṃ proktaṃ vasantasamaye sthitam ||

	grīṣme 'pi yat sthitaṃ toyaṃ rājasūyād viśiṣyate |

	etān mahārāja viśeṣadharmān karoti yo 'gryāmalaśuddhabuddhiḥ |

	sa yāti rudrālayam āśupūtaḥ kalpān anekān divi modate ca ||

	anekalokān samahastapādīn bhuktvā parārdhadvayam aṅganābhiḥ |

	sahaiva viṣṇoḥ paramaṃ padaṃ tat prāpnoti tad yogabalena bhūyaḥ ||

parārdhalakṣaṇam uktam |

	ekaṃ daśa śataṃ caiva sahasram ayutaṃ tathā |

	lakṣaṃ ca niyutaṃ caiva koṭir arbudavṛndake ||

	kharvaṃ nikharvaṃ śaṅkhaṃ ca padmaṃ sāgaram eva ca |

	antyaṃ madhyaṃ parārdhaṃ ca krameṇa parikīrtitāḥ ||	

	sthānāny aṣṭādaśaitāni daśabhir gaṇayet pumān |

iti mātsya taḍāgapratiṣṭhāvidhiḥ |

bahvṛcagṛhyapariśiṣṭam |


    athāto vāruṇo vidhiḥ | vāpīkūpataḍāgasetuyajñaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ | puṇye tithikaraṇe śubhe nakṣatre vā prācīṃ diśaṃ gatvā prākpravaṇam udaksamīpe 'gnim upasamādhāya vāruṇaṃ caruṃ śrapayitvājyabhāgāntaṃ kṛtvājyāhutīr juhuyāt | samudrajyeṣṭhā [RV 5.4.16] iti tsṛbhiḥ pratyṛcaṃ tato haviṣāṣṭābhir juhuyāt | tat tvā yāmi brahmaṇā vandamāna vidvān [RV 1.2.15] iti pañca | tvaṃ no agne varuṇasya vidvān [RV 4.1.4] iti dve | imaṃ me varuṇa śrudhi [RV 1.2.19] iti ca | sviṣṭakṛtaṃ ca navamaṃ nava vai prāṇāḥ prāṇā vā āpas tasmād apo navabhir juhoti | mārjanānte dhenum avatārayed avtīryamānām anumantrayetedaṃ salilaṃ pavitraṃ kuruṣva śuddhāḥ pūrā amṛtāḥ santu nityaṃ tārayantī tīrthābhiṣiktaṃ **[414]** lokālokaṃ tarati tīryata iti pucchāgre svayaṃ lagno 'nvārabdha uttīrya āpo asmān mātaraḥ śundhayantu [RV 7.6.24] ity athāparājitāyāṃ diśy utthāpayet | sūyavasād bhagavatī hi bhūyā [RV 2.3.21] iti | hiṃ kṛtaṃ ced dhiṃ kṛṇvatī vasupatnī vasūnām iti | sacelaghaṇṭāṃ kāñcanaśṛṅgīṃ vṛṣabhaprajāṃ raupyakhurāṃ kāṃsyopadohāṃ viprāya dadyād itarāṃ vā śaktyā dakṣiṇāṃ tata utsargaṃ kuryāt | devapitṛmanuṣyāḥ prīyantām iti | yad votsṛjety āha śaunako brāhmaṇān bhojayitvā svastyayanaṃ vācayeta ||

atha vṛkṣavidhiḥ |

tatra matsyapurāṇe |

	pādapānāṃ vidhiṃ vakṣye tathaivodyānabhūmiṣu |

	taḍāgavidhivat sarvam āsādya jagatīśvara ||

	ṛtvigmaṇḍapasaṃbhāram ācāryaś cāpi tadvidhaḥ |

	pūjayed brāhmaṇāṃs tadvad dhemavastrānulepanaiḥ ||

	sarvauṣadhyudakaiḥ siktān piṣṭātakavibhūṣitān |

	vṛkṣān mālyair alaṃkṛtya vāsobhir abhiveṣṭayet ||

	sūcyā sauvarṇayā kāryaṃ tadvad dhemaśalākayā |

	phalāni sapta cāṣṭau vā kāladhautāni kārayet ||

kāladhautāni rūpyamayāṇīty arthaḥ |

	pratyekaṃ sarvavṛkṣāṇāṃ vedyantāny adhivāsayet |

	dhūpo 'tra gugguluḥ śreṣṭhas tāmrapātrair adhiṣṭhitān ||

	sarvadhānyasthitān kṛtvā vastragandhānulepanaiḥ |

	kumbhān sarveṣu vṛkṣeṣu sthāpyitvā nareśvaraḥ ||

	sahiraṇyān aśeṣāṃs tān kṛtvā balinivedanam |

	yathāval lokapālānām indrādīnāṃ vidhānataḥ ||

	vanaspater adhīvāsam evaṃ kāryaṃ dvijātibhiḥ |

	tataḥ śuklāmbaradharāṃ sauvarṇakṛtaśekharām ||

**[415]**	kāṃsyopadohāṃ sauvarṇaśṛṅgābhyām atiśālinīm |

	payasvinīṃ vṛkṣamadhyām utsṛjed gām udaṅmukhīm ||

	tato 'bhiṣekamantreṇa vādyamaṅgalagītakaiḥ |

	ṛjyajuḥsāmamantrair vā vāsuṇair abhitas tadā ||

	tair eva kumbhaiḥ snapanaṃ kuryur brāhmaṇapuṃgavāḥ |

	snātaḥ śuklāmbaradharo yajamāno 'bhipūjayet ||

	gobhir vibhavataḥ sarvān ṛtvijas tān samāhitaḥ |

	hemasūtraiḥ sakaṭakair aṅgulīyapavitrakaiḥ ||

	vāsobhiḥ śayanīyaiś ca tathopaskarapādapaiḥ |

	kṣīrābhiṣecanaṃ dadyur yāvad dinacatuṣṭayam ||

	homaś ca sarpiṣā kāryo yavaiḥ kṛṣṇatilair api |

	palāśasamidhaḥ śastāś caturthe 'hni tathotsavaḥ ||

	dakṣiṇā ca punas tadvad deyā tatrāpi śaktitaḥ |

	yad yad iṣṭatamaṃ tadvat tat tad dadyād amatsaraḥ ||

	ācārye dviguṇaṃ datvā praṇipatya kṣamāpayet |

	anena vidhinā yas tu kuryād vṛkṣotsavaṃ budhaḥ ||

	sarvān kāmān avāpnoti padaṃ cānantyam aśnute |

	yaś caikam api rajendra vṛkṣaṃ saṃsthāpayed budhaḥ ||

	so 'pi svarge vased rājan yāvad indrāyutatrayam |

	bhūtān bhavyāṃś ca manujāṃs tārayed romasaṃmitān ||

	paramāṃ siddhim āpnoti punarāvṛttidurlabhām ||

viṣṇuḥ |

	eṣṭavyā bahavaḥ putrā yady eko 'pi gayāṃ vrajet |

	yajeta vāśvamedhena nīlaṃ vā vṛṣam utsṛjet ||

atha vṛṣotsargavidhiḥ |

kārtikyām āśvayujyāṃ vā tatrādāv eva vṛṣabhaṃ parīkṣeta | jīvavatsāyāḥ payasvinyāḥ putraṃ sarvalakṣaṇopetaṃ nīlaṃ lohitaṃ vā mukhapucchapādasarvaśuklaṃ yūthasyācchādakaṃ tato gavāṃ madhye susamiddham agniṃ paristīrya pauṣṇaṃ caruṃ payasā śrapayitvā pūṣā gā anvetu naḥ | iha raḍir iti ca hutvā vṛṣabham ayaskāras tv aṅkayet | ekasmin pārśve cakreṇāparasmiñ śūlenāṅkitam | **[416]** hiraṇyavarṇā iti catasṛbhiḥ śaṃ no devīr iti ca snāpayet | snātam alaṃkṛtam alaṃkṛtābhiś catasṛbhir vatsatarībhiḥ sārdham ānīya rudrān puruṣasūktaṃ kūṣmāṇḍāṃś ca japet | pitā vatsa iti ca mantraṃ vṛṣabhasya dakṣiṇe karṇe | idaṃ ca,

	vṛṣo hia bhagavān dharmaś catuṣpādaḥ prakīrtitaḥ |

	vṛṇomi tam ahaṃ bhaktyā sa me rakṣatu sarvataḥ ||

etaṃ yuvānaṃ pari vo dadāmi tena krīḍantīś carata priyeṇa (TS 3.3.9) mā hā sma hi prajayā mā tanubhir mā radhāma dviṣate soma rājan ||

	vṛṣaṃ vatsatarīyuktam aiśānyām kārayed diśi |

	hotur vastrayugaṃ dadyāt suvarṇaṃ kāṃsyam eva ca ||

	ayaskārasya dātavyaṃ vetanaṃ manasepsitam |

	bhojanaṃ bahusarpiṣkaṃ brāhmaṇāṃś cātra bhojayet ||

	utsṛṣṭo vṛṣabho yasmin pibaty atha jalāśaye |

	tarpayitvākhilān devān pitṝṃs tasyopatiṣṭhati ||

	śṛṅgeṇollikhate bhūmiṃ yatra kvacana darpitaḥ |

	pitṝṇām annadānaṃ tat prabhūtam upatiṣṭhati ||

brahmāṇḍapurāṇe |

	phalaṃ vṛṣasya vakṣyāmi gadato me nibodhaya |

	vṛṣotsṛṣṭaḥ punāty eva daśa pūrvān daśāparān ||

	yat kiṃcit pibate toyam avatīrṇo nadīṃ vṛṣaḥ |

	vṛṣaspṛṣṭaṃ pitṝṇāṃ tad akṣayaṃ samudāhṛtam ||

	yena yena spṛśet toyaṃ lāṅgūlādibhir antataḥ |

	sarvaṃ tad akṣayaṃ tasya pitḍṇāṃ nātra saṃśayaḥ ||

	śṛṅgaiḥ khuraiś ca yad bhūmim ullikhaty aniśaṃ vṛṣaḥ |

	madhukalyāḥ pitṝṇāṃ tu akṣayā hi bhavanti tāḥ ||

	sahasranalvamātreṇa taḍāgena yathāvidhi |

	tṛptis tu yā pitṝṇāṃ tu sā vṛṣeṇeti kathyate ||

**iti śrīvidyādharavaṃśaprabhavaśrīśilāhāranarendrajīmūtavāhanānvayaprasūta-**

**śrīmadaparādityadevaviracite yājñavalkīyadharmaśāstranibandhe**

**dānaprakaraṇaṃ samāptam || 8 ||**

**atha saṭīkayājñavalkyasmṛtau**

**śrāddhaprakaraṇam | (9)**

_śrāddhaṃ svadhanatyāgarūpatvād dānena sadṛśam iti dānavidhānānantaraṃ buddhistham ato dānaprakaraṇānantaraṃ śrāddhakalpam ārabhate | tatra kālo 'ṅgam apy anupādeya iti svarūpeṇaivādhikārahetuḥ | na hi kālāntare vartamānaḥ kartāṅgabhūtaṃ kālāntaraviśiṣṭaṃ karma śaknuyāt kartum | kiṃ tu tatkāla eveti yuktaṃ kālasyādhikārahetutvam | viṣṇukramādīnāṃ tūpādeyāṅgānāṃ na svarūpam adhikārahetuḥ kiṃ tu tadviṣayā śaktis tasmāt kālasyādhikārahetutvād adhikārāyattatvāc cānuṣṭhānasya śrāddhakālāṃs tāvad āha |_

	**amāvāsyāṣṭakā vṛddhiḥ kṛṣṇapakṣo 'yanadvayam |**

**	dravyabrāhmaṇasaṃpattir viṣuvat sūryasaṃkramaḥ || 1.217 ||**

**	vyatīpāto gajacchāyā grahaṇaṃ candrasūryayoḥ |**

**	śrāddhaṃ prati ruciś caiva śrāddhakālāḥ prakīrtitāḥ || 1.218 ||**

amāvāsyādayaḥ śrāddasyāṅgabhūtāḥ kālā manvādibhiḥ prakīrtitāḥ | atrāmāvāsyā kṛṣṇapakṣasya pañcadaśī tithiḥ | sā ca sanīvālī kuhūś ceti dvividhā |

	dṛṣṭacandrā sinīvālī naṣṭacandrā kuhūs tathā |

tatra sāgnikaiḥ sinīvālyāṃ śrāddhaṃ kāryam itaraiḥ kuhvām | tathā ca vyāsaḥ |

	dṛṣṭacandrā snīvālī kāryā viprais tu sāgnikaiḥ |

	naṣṭacandrā kuhūḥ kāryā śūdrair viprair anagnikaiḥ |

śūdrair anagnikair vipraiś ceti yojyam | yat tu precetasoktam,

	sinīvālī kuhūś caiva śrutyukte pitṛkarmaṇi |

	syātāṃ caite tu madhyāgne śrāddhādi syāt kathaṃ tadā ||

	tithikṣaye sinīvālī tithivṛddhau kuhūr matā |

	sāmye 'pi ca kuhūr jñeyā vedavedāṅgavedibhiḥ || **[418]**

iti, tad yatra kṣaye sinīvālyāṃ pitṛyajño bhavati tadviṣayaṃ grāhyam | yadā tu kuhvāṃ pitṛyajñas tadā sāgnikair api saiva grāhyā | pitṛyajñānantaraṃ hi śrāddhaṃ vihitam | yad āha manuḥ |

	pitṛyajñaṃ tu nirvartya vipraś candrakṣaye 'gnimān |

	piṇḍānvāhāryakaṃ śrāddhaṃ kuryān māsānumāsikam || iti |

vīpsāto nityam amāvāsyāśrāddham iti saṃbadhyate | tathā ca laugākṣiḥ |

	śrāddhaṃ kuryād avaśyaṃ tu pramītapitṛkaḥ svayam |

	indukṣaye māsi māsi vṛddhau pratyabdam eva ca || iti |

etac ca niragnināpi kāryam | tathā ca uśanā |

	kuryād ahar ahaḥ śrāddhaṃ pramītapitṛko dvijaḥ |

	sāgniko 'nagniko vāpi pratimāse tathābdikam || iti |

pramītapitṛka iti vacanāj jīvapitṛkasyāniyamo gamyate | tathā ca hārītaḥ |

	jīve pitari vai putraḥ śrāddhakarma vivarjayet |

	yabhyo vāpi pitā dadyāt tebhya eke pracakṣate ||

tebhya eveti ca pakṣaḥ sāgnikasyaiva | yad āha sumantuḥ|

	na jīvatpitṛkaḥ kuryāc chrāddham agnim ṛte dvijaḥ |

	yebhya eva pitā kuryāt tebhya eva tu sāgnikaḥ ||

atra viśeṣo maitrāyaṇīyapraiśiṣṭāt |

	udvāhe putrajanane pitryeṣṭyāṃ saumike makhe |

	tīrthe brāhmaṇa āyāte ṣaḍ ete jīvataḥ pituḥ ||

jīvatpitṛkasya ṣaḍ ete śrāddhakālā ity arthaḥ | pitryeṣṭiś cāturmāsyeṣu saumike makhe puroḍāśāt piṇḍadānam | atra ca pitṛgrahaṇam upalakṣaṇārtham, yad āha viṣṇuḥ: "pitari jīvati yaḥ śrāddhaṃ kuryāt sa yeṣāṃ pitā kuryāt tebhyaḥ kuryāt | pitāmahe jīvati yeṣāṃ pitāmahaḥ | pitari pitāmahe prapitāmahe ca jīvati naiva kuryāt" iti | evaṃ tāvaj jīvapitṛka itaro vā sāgniḥ sinīvālyāṃ śrāddhaṃ kuryād ity uktam | tatra ye sinīvālīpratiṣedhās te niragniviṣayāḥ piṇḍapitṛyajñāyogyasinīvālīviṣayā vā grāhyāḥ | te tāvad udāhriyante | tatra baudhāyanaḥ |

**[419]**	madhyāhnāt parato yatra caturdaśy eva vartate |

	sinīvālīti sā jñeyā pitṛkārye tu niṣphalā ||

kārṣṇājiniḥ |

	bhūtaviddhām amāvāsyāṃ mohād ajñānato 'pi vā |

	śrāddhakarmāṇi ye kuryus teṣām āyuḥ prahīyate ||

ityādayaḥ | yat tu pracetasoktam,

	nāgaviddhā ca yā ṣaṣṭhī saptamyā ca tathāṣṭamī |

	daśamyekādaśīviddhā trayodaśyā caturdaśī ||

	bhūtaviddhā tv amāvāsyā na grāhyā munipuṃgavaiḥ |

iti, tac chrāddhād anyatra draṣṭavyam | hārītaḥ |

	tulāmakarameṣeṣu kanyāyāṃ mithune tathā |

	bhūtaviddhā tv amāvāsyā pūjyā bhavati yatnataḥ ||

etad api vratopavāsādiviṣayam | baudhāyanaḥ |

	ghaṭikaikāpy amāvāsyā pratipatsu na cet tadā |

	bhūtaviddhāpi kartavyā daive pitrye ca karmaṇi ||

anagnibhir api bhūtaviddhaiva śrāddhe kāryety arthaḥ | ghaṭikaikāpīti karmakālaṃ vyāpnotīty arthaḥ | tenāparāhṇavyāpinī kuhūḥ śrāddhakarmaṇi sarvair eva tyājyā | tathā ca jābālaḥ |

	pratipatsv apy amāvasyā pūrvāhṇavyāpinī yadi |

	pūraviddhaiva sā kāryā pitrye karmaṇi sarvadā ||

amāvāsyāśrāddhasyāvaśyakatvam, asāmarthye ca pratividhiviśeṣam āha hārītaḥ |

	aṣṭakānvaṣṭakābhyudayatīrthapātropapattayaḥ |

	pitṝṇām atireko vai māsiko 'rtho dhruvaḥ smṛtaḥ ||

	api mūlaiḥ phalair vāpi tathāpy udakatarpaṇaiḥ |

	avidyamāne kurvīta na tu prāptaṃ vilaṅghayet || iti |

māsiko 'rthaḥ pārvaṇaṃ śrāddham | atraiva viṣaye devalaḥ |

	yad eva tarpayaty adbhir āhitāgnir dine dine |

	pitryaṃ tenaiva cāpnoti vārṣikādikriyāphalam ||

	piṇḍamātraṃ pradātavyam abhāve dravyaviprayoḥ |

	śrāddhāhani tu saṃprāpte bhaven niraśano 'pi vā || **[420]**

piṇḍadānāsaṃbhave niraśanatvam | tathā |

	pātrābhāve paraṃ kṛtvā pitṛyajñavidhiṃ naraḥ |

	nirdiśyāpy annam uddhṛtya yatra pātraṃ tato gatiḥ ||

pitṛyajñavidhiṃ kṛtvā yatra brāhmaṇas tatra tad annaṃ nītvā brāhmaṇāya dadyād ity arthaḥ | tathā |

	nidhāya vā darbhacāṭūn āsaneṣu samāhitaḥ |

	praiṣānupraiṣasaṃyuktaṃ nidhānaṃ pratipadyate ||

	sarvābhāve kṣiped agnau gave dadyāt tathāpsu vā |

	na tu prāptasya lopo 'sti paitṛkasya viśeṣataḥ ||

	ekenāpi hi vipreṇa ṣaṭpiṇḍaṃ śrāddham ācaret |

	ṣaḍ arghyān dāpayet tatra ṣaḍbhyo dadyāt tathāsanam ||

	pitā bhuṅkte dvijakare mukhe bhuṅkte pitāmahaḥ |

	prapitāmahas tu tālusthaṃ kaṇṭhe mātāmahaḥ smṛtaḥ ||

	evam apy ācarec chrāddhaṃ ṣaḍdaivatyaṃ mahāmune |

	viluptiṃ kārayed yas tu pitṛhā sa prajāyate ||

vṛddho vṛddhapramātāmahaḥ | manuḥ |

	anena vidhinā śrāddhaṃ trirabdasyeva nirvapet |

	hemantagrīṣmavarṣāsu pañcayajñikam anvaham ||

devalaḥ |

	anena vidhinā śrāddhaṃ kuryāt saṃvatsare sakṛt |

	triś catur vā yathā śrāddhaṃ māse māse dine dine ||

vṛddhavasiṣṭhaḥ |

	kiṃcid dadyād aśaktas tu udakumbhādikaṃ dvije |

	tṛṇāni vā gave dadyāt piṇḍān vāpy atha nirvapet ||

	tiladarbhaiḥ pitṝn vāpi tarpayet snānapūrvakam |

	agninā vā dahet kakṣaṃ śrāddhakāle samāgate |

	tasmin vopavased ahni japed vā śrāddhasaṃhitām ||

viṣṇupurāṇe |

	asamartho 'nnadānasya dhānyam āmaṃ svaśaktitaḥ |

	pradāsyati dvijāgryebhyaḥ svalpālpām api dakṣiṇām ||

**[421]**	tatrāpy asāmarthyayutaḥ karāgrāgrasthitāṃs tilān |

	praṇamya dvijamukhyāya kasmaicin nṛpa dāsyati ||

	tilaiḥ saptāṣṭabhir vāpi samavetaṃ jalāñjalim |

	bhaktinamraḥ sumuddiśya bhuvy asmākaṃ pradāsyati ||

	yataḥ kutaścit saṃprāpya gobhyo vāpi gavāhnikam |

	abhāve prayatas tasmāc chraddhāyuktaḥ pradāsyati ||

	sarvābhāve vanaṃ gatvā kakṣamūlapradarśakaḥ |

	sūryādilokapālānām idam uccaiḥ paṭhiṣyati ||

[tad yathā mārkaṇḍeyapurāṇe yoginyā madālasayoktam]

	na me 'sti vittaṃ na dhanaṃ na cānyc chrāddhopayogi svapitṝn nato 'smi |

	tṛpyantu bhaktyā pitaro mayaitau bhujau kṛtau vartmani mārutasya ||

	ity evaṃ pitṛbhir gītaṃ bhāvābhāvaprayojanam |

	yaḥ karoti kṛtaṃ tena śrāddhaṃ bhavati pārthiva ||

smṛtyantaram |

	aṅgāni pitṛyajñasya yadā kartuṃ na śaknuyāt |

	sa tadā vācayed viprān sākalyāt siddhir astv iti ||

pitṛyajñaḥ śrāddham | evam amāvāsyāśrāddhasya nityatvād upāttaduritakṣayo 'karaṇanimittapratyavāyaparihāro vā niyogasiddhir vā prayojanam | brahmajñānasahitasya tu muktiḥ | vakṣyati hi tattvajñānaniṣṭhaḥ śrāddhakṛd vimucyata iti | anyeṣām api nityakarmaṇām etat prayojanam anusaṃdheyam | na ca,

	piṇḍānām aṅgabhūtaṃ hi māsikaṃ śrāddham ucyate |

	paścād idaṃ bhaved yasmāt praśastāmiṣayogataḥ ||

iti bhaviṣyatpurāṇavacanād amāvāsyāśrāddasyāṅgatvam avagamyate | na pṛthakprayojanam asyāstīti vācyam | yataḥ piṇḍānāṃ pitṛyajñasya yo 'ṅgam amāvāsyākhyaḥ kālas tatra bhūtaṃ tadaṅgabhūtam iti tasyārthaḥ | na punaḥ pitṛyajñāṅgatvam, tathā hi sati niragnes tacchrāddham avidheyaṃ syāt |

	aṣṭakā mārgaśīrṣādimāsatrayāparapakṣāṣtamyaḥ | aṣṭakāśabdo yady api karmaviśeṣanāma tathāpi tadaṅgabhūtaṃ kālam iha lakṣayati nānyathā śrāddhakālāḥ prakīrtitā iti yujyate | tatra gṛhyakṛcchaunakaḥ |

	hemantaśiśirayoś caturṇām aparapakṣāṇām aṣṭamīṣv aṣṭakāḥ | **[422]**

iti vadann aṣṭamīcatuṣṭayam aṣṭakāṅgatvenāha | viṣṇus tu trayam evāha: "amāvāsyās tisro 'ṣṭakās tisro 'nvaṣṭakā | māghīproṣṭhapadyūrdhvaṃ kṛṣṇatrayodaśī vrīhiyavapākau ceti | 

	etāni śrāddhakālāni nityāny āha prajāpatiḥ |

	śrāddham eteṣv akurvāṇo narakaṃ pratipadyate" || iti 

ata eva nityatā hy aṣṭakāśrāddhasya sidhyati | brahmapurāṇe punar aṣṭakāś catasraḥ |

	aindryāṃ tu prathamāyāṃ ca śākaiḥ saṃtarpayet pitṝn |

	prājāpatyāṃ dvitīyāyāṃ māṃsaiḥ śuddhaiś ca tarpayet ||

	vaiśvadevyāṃ tṛtīyāyāṃ apūpaiś ca yathākramam |

	varṣāsu medhyaiḥ śākais tu caturthyām eva sarvadā ||

śrāvaṇādayaś catvāro māsā varṣāḥ | mādhyaṃdinaśākhāgṛhye ca madhyāvarṣe sā turīyā śākāṣṭakā | tathā — aindrī vaiśvadevī prājāpatyā pitryeti ca | vṛddhir vivāhādiḥ | vaidikaḥ karmagaṇaḥ putrajanmādiś ca | sā ca nimittatvād anupādeyeti kālatulyatvāc chrāddhakālāḥ prakīrtitā iti kālaśabdena śakyā saṃgrahītum | tataś ca vṛddhiśrāddhaṃ naimittikatvād āvaśyakam | ata eva vṛddhaśātātapaḥ |

	vṛddhau na tarpitā yair vai devatā gṛhamedhibhiḥ |

	taddānaphalaṃ sarvam āsuro vidhir eva saḥ || iti |

kṛṣṇapakṣaḥ prasiddhaḥ | tasya śrāddhakālatvaṃ śrāddhāṅgabhūtāparāhṇāvacchedakapratipadāditithinirūpaṇadvāreṇa | etac cāvaśyakam, "śākenāpy aparapakṣaṃ nātikrāmen māsi māsi vo 'śanam iti śrutiḥ" iti kātyāyanavacanāt | etac cāmāvāsyena śrāddhena vikalpate, "atha śrāddham amāvāsyāyāṃ pitṛbhyo dadyāt pañcamīprabhṛrti vāparapakṣasya" iti gautamavacanāt | na ca pañcamīprabhṛtitvaṃ niyatam | yataḥ sa evāha: "sarvasmin vā" iti | na ca pratyahaṃ śrāddham āśaṅkanīyam | yad āha kātyāyanaḥ: "aparapakṣe śrāddhaṃ kurvītordhvaṃ caturthyāṃ yad ahaḥ saṃpadyate" iti | manus tu,

	kṛṣṇapakṣe daśamyādau varjayitvā caturdaśīm |

	śrāddhe praśastās tithayo yathaitā na tathetarāḥ ||

iti daśamyādipakṣam apy uktavān | **[423]** pratimāsaṃ kṛṣṇapakṣavidhānenaiva proṣṭhapadyā aparapakṣo 'pi prāptaḥ | tathāsya yamena yaḥ pṛthag vidhiḥ kriyate,

	āṣāḍhīm avadhiṃ kṛtvā yaḥ pakṣaḥ pañcamo bhavet |

	tatra śrāddhaṃ prakurvīta kanyāstho 'rko bhaven na vā ||

iti, so 'māvāsyāśrāddhena samuccayārthaḥ | pratyahaṃ tatra śrāddhaprāptyarthaś ca | ata eva brahmapurāṇam |

	aśvayukkṛṣṇapakṣe tu śrāddhaṃ kāryaṃ dine dine |

	tribhāgahīnaṃ pakṣaṃ vā tribhāgaṃ tv ardham eva vā ||

atra paurṇamāsyantamāsābhiprāyeṇa proṣṭhapadyā aparapakṣo 'śvayukkṛṣṇapakṣa  uktaḥ | tribhāgahīnapakṣe 'pi pratyahaṃ śrāddhaṃ kāryam | pakṣam iti dvitīyāvaśādatyantasaṃyogāvagamāt | evam uttaratrāpi: "tribhāgahīne pakṣe pañcamīprabhṛti vāparapakṣasya" iti gautamavacanāt | pañcamīprabhṛtikaraṇapakṣa ādyāś catasras tithayo hīyante caturdaśī ceti tithipañcakahānād bhavati tribhāgahīnaḥ pakṣaḥ | tribhāgapakṣe daśamyām upakramaḥ | caturdaśīparityāgāc ca tribhāgatvam | ardhapakṣe punar aṣṭamyām upakramaḥ | caturdaśīvarjanāc cārdhatvam | vikalpaś cāyaṃ kartṛśaktyapekṣaḥ | malamāsāparapakṣe 'pi proṣṭhapadyā aparapakṣaḥ kadācid bhavati | tannivṛtyartham āha śāṭyāyaniḥ |

	nabhasy asyāpare pakṣe tithiṣoḍaśakaṃ tu yat |

	kanyāgatānvitaṃ cet syāt sa kālaḥ śrāddhakarmavat || iti |

śuklapratipadam antarbhāvya ṣoḍaśasaṃkhyā pūraṇīyā | nabhasyaḥ proṣṭhapadaḥ | kanyāgatānvaye viśeṣam āha kārṣṇājiniḥ |

	ante vā yadi vā madhye yatra kanyāṃ ravir vrajet |

	pakṣaḥ sa pañcamaḥ pūjyaḥ śrāddhaṣoḍaśakaṃ prati || iti |

tena siṃhagate sūrye 'sti śrāddhaṣoḍaśakārambhaḥ | tathā ca jātūkarṇyaḥ |

	āṣāḍhīm avadhiṃ kṛtvā ya pakṣaḥ pañcamo bhavet |

	śrāddhakālaḥ sa vijñeyaḥ kanyāṃ gacchatu vā na vā || iti |

pakṣopakramābhiprāyam etat | kanyāgatānvayena tu pakṣasya bhavitavyam eva, "kanyāgatānvitaṃ cet syāt" it vacanāt | tataś ca proṣṭhapadyāḥ pūrvasminn **[424]** aparasmin vā pakṣe kanyāsaṃkrāntau satyām uttaraḥ pakṣaḥ śrāddhakālaḥ | yat tu brahmāṇḍapurāṇe,

	kanyāgate savitari yāny ahāni tu ṣoḍaśa |

	kratubhis tāni tulyāni tatra dattaṃ mahāphalam ||

tat phalādhikyābhiprāyam | tad āha śāṭyāyaniḥ |

	puṇyaḥ kanyāgatas tāvat puṇyaḥ pakṣaś ca pañcamaḥ |

	kanyāgataḥ pañcamaś ca so 'tyantaṃ puṇya ucyate ||

tataś ca savituḥ kanyāgatatve pṛthakśrāddhakālatvam | ataḥ punar eva kārṣṇājiniḥ |

	kanyāgate savitari pitaro yānti vai sutān |

	tāvat pretapurī śūnyā yāvad vṛścikadarśanam ||

brahmapurāṇam |

	yāvac ca kanyātulayoḥ kramād āste divākaraḥ |

	tāvac chrāddhasya kālaḥ syāc chūnyaṃ pretapuraṃ tadā || iti |

pañcamapakṣaśrāddhaṃ nityam | yad āha jātukarṇyaḥ |

	naiyogiko vidhir hy eṣa pakṣe vai pañcame smṛtaḥ |

	tasmin dattaṃ havirbhūtaṃ pitṝṇām akṣayaṃ bhavet || iti |

naiyogiko naiyamikaḥ | ata eva vyāsaḥ |

	haste varṣāsu kanyāsthe śākenāpi gṛhe vasan |

	pañcamyor antare dadyād ubhayor vaṃśayor ṛṇam ||

ṛṇam avaśyaṃ dayatvāt | ubhayor vaṃśayor mātāpitṛvaṃśayoḥ | pañcamyoḥ kṛṣṇaśuklapakṣapañcamyor ity arthaḥ | atrānukūlyam āha sumantuḥ |

	sūrye kanyāsthite kuryāc chrāddhaṃ yo na gṛhāśramī |

	dhanaṃ putrāḥ kutas tasya pitṛniḥśvāsapīḍanāt ||

	yeyaṃ dīpānvitā rājan khyātā pañcadaśī bhivi |

	tasyāṃ dadyān na ced dattaṃ pitṝṇāṃ vai mahālaye ||

mahālaye kanyāgatapakṣe | yad api smṛtyantaram,

	bandhūnām api sarveṣāṃ śrāddhaṃ kanyāgate ravau |

	nirvaped ānulomyena mṛtāhatithim āśritaḥ ||

iti, tad anapatyabandhuviṣayam | **[425]**

	ayanadvayaṃ makarakarkaṭasaṃkrāntī tadupalakṣitaḥ kālaḥ śrāddhakālaḥ | "sūryasaṃkramaḥ" ity anenaivāyanaparigrahasiddhau pṛthagvacanam ayanaśrāddhasya nityatvaṃ bahuphalatvaṃ vā gamayati | tathā ca jātūkarṇyaḥ |

	grahoparoge (?) svasute ca jāte pitrye maghāyām ayanadvaye ca |

	nityaṃ ca śaṅkhe ca tathaiva padme dattaṃ bhaven niṣkasahasratulyam ||

nityaśabdaśravaṇād uparāgādiśrāddhasāhacaryāc cāyanaśrāddham āvaśyakam | niṣkasahasradānatulyam adhikaphalam | pitrye pitṛkṣayāhani | yad vā pitrye nabhasyāparapakṣe yā maghā tasyām ity arthaḥ |

	śaṅkham āhur amāvāsyāṃ kṣīṇasomāṃ dvijottamāḥ |

	aṣṭakā tu bhavet padmaṃ tatra dattam athākṣayam ||

viṣṇupurāṇe |

	vaiśākhaśuklasya tu yā tṛtīyā navamy asau kārtikaśuklapakṣe |

	nabhasyamāsasya ca kṛṣṇapakṣe trayodaśī pañcadaśī ca māghe ||

	etāś catasras tithayo yugādyā dattaṃ hutaṃ cāśu bhaved anantam |

	upaplavaś candasamo raveś ca tisro 'ṣṭakāyā ayanadvayaṃ ca ||

	pānīyam apy atra tilair vimiśraṃ dadyāt pitṛbhyaḥ prayato manuṣyaḥ |

	śrāddhaṃ kṛtaṃ tena samāḥ sahasraṃ rahasyam etan munayo vadanti ||

pānīyam pay atretivacanād eṣāṃ śrāddhānām āvaśyakatvaviniścayaḥ | kṛṣṇapakṣa iti trayodaśyāḥ pañcadaśyāś ca viśeṣaṇam iti kecit | tan na, śāstrāntare 'nyathādarśanāt | tathā ca brahmapurāṇe |

	vaiśākhaśuklapakṣe tu tṛtīyāyāṃ kṛtaṃ yugam |

	kārtike śuklapakṣe ca tretā ca navame 'hani ||

	atha bhādrapade kṛṣṇatrayodaśyāṃ tu dvāparam |

	māghe tu pūrṇamāsyāṃ tu ghoraṃ kaliyugaṃ tathā ||

	yugārambhās tu tithayo yugādyās tena viśrutāḥ || iti |

etena,

	dve śukle dve tathā kṛṣṇe yugādye parikīrtite |

iti kasyacid vyākhyānaṃ prayākhyātam | yamaḥ |

	āṣāḍhyām atha kārtikyāṃ mādhyāṃ trīn pañca vā dvijān |

	tarpayet pitṛpūrvaṃ tu tad apy akṣayam ucyate ||

gautamaḥ: "śrāvaṇyāgrahāyaṇyoś cānvaṣṭakāsu pitṛbhyo dadyān māghīvaiśākhyoś ca" | **[426]** yat tu viṣṇunoktam: "ādityasaṃkramaṇaṃ viṣuvaddvayaṃ viśeṣeṇāyanadvayaṃ vyatīpāto janmarkṣam abhyudayaś ca |

	etāṃs tu śrāddhakālān vai kāmyān āha prajāpatiḥ |

	śrāddham eteṣu yad dattaṃ tad ānantyāya kalpate" ||

iti, tat pitṛtṛptirūpaphalānantyakāmasya vidhāyakam ity ayanaśrāddhasya nityatāṃ na vihanti | sarvam eva hi śrāddhaṃ pitṛtṛptipradaṃ pitṝṃs tarpayed ityādivacanabalād avagamyate | atha vāyanādiśrāddhasya bhavatu niyatā kāmyatā ca vacanadvayabalād agnihotrādivat | atha vāyanadvayaśabdenaiva makarakarkaṭasaṃkrāntyor abhidhānam | kiṃ tu tābhyāṃ pṛthag eva raver uttarāṃ dakṣiṇāṃ ca diśaṃ prati gamanayoḥ |

	dravyabrāhmaṇasaṃpattir dravyasya śrāddhārhasya brāhmaṇasya vā paṅktipāvanasya saṃpattir lābho yatra kāle sa śrāddhakālaḥ | etac ca naimittikatvād āvaśyakam | yad āha hārītaḥ |

	tīrthadravyopapattau tu na kālam avadhārayet |

	pātraṃ ca brāhmaṇaṃ prāpya sadyaḥ śrāddhaṃ vidhīyate || iti |

tīrthaṃ puṣkarādi | viṣuve meṣe tulāyāṃ ca sūryasya saṃkrāntiḥ | ayanavad asyāpi pṛthagvacane prayojanam | atra pulastyokto viśeṣaḥ |

	ayanadvitaye śrāddhaṃ viṣuvaddvitaye tathā |

	yugādiṣu ca sarvāsu piṇḍanirvapaṇād ṛte || iti |

sūryasaṃkramaḥ sūryasya rāśito rāśyantaragamanam | vyatīpāto yogaviśeṣaḥ pāribhāṣiko vā | tatra vṛddhamanuḥ |

	śravaṇāśvadhaniṣṭhārdrānāgadaivatamastake |

	yadyamā ravivāreṇa vyatīpātaḥ sa ucyate ||

nāgadaivatam āśleṣā | mastake prathamapāde yadi candra ity arthaḥ | varāhapurāṇe |

	śrāddhārham āgataṃ dravyaṃ viśiṣṭam atha vā dvijam |

	śrāddhaṃ kurvīta vijñāya vyatīpāte 'yane tathā ||

	viṣuve caiva saṃprāpte grahaṇe candrasūryayoḥ |

	samasteṣv eva viprendra rāśiṣv arke 'dhigacchati ||

	nakṣatre grahapīḍāsu duṣṭasvapnāvalokane |

	icchāśrāddhāni kurvīta navasasyāgame tathā || **[427]**

gajacchāyā hasticchāyā, tathā ca kāṭhakī śrutiḥ |

	etad dhi devapitṝṇāṃ cāyanaṃ yad dhasticchāyā ||

tathā: "hasticchāyāyāṃ śrāddhaṃ dadyāt" | mahābhārate pitṛgāthā |

	anena sarvalohena varṣāsu niyatavrataḥ |

	hasticchāyāsu vidhivat karṇavyajanavījinam || iti |

śrāddhaṃ dadyād iti śeṣaḥ | karṇavyajanavījitam ity abhidhānāt pratyakṣahasticchāyāviṣayam evaitad vākyam | pāribhāṣikī ca gajacchāyā, sā coktā smṛtyantare |

	yadenduḥ pitṛdai(de)vatye haṃsaś caiva kare sthitaḥ |

	tithir vaiśravaṇīyā ca gajacchāyeti sā smṛtā || iti |

pitṛdai(de)vatyaṃ maghā | haṃsa ādityaḥ | karo hastanakṣatram | vaiśravaṇīyā trayodaśī | etattritayayogo gajacchāyā | grahaṇam uparāgaḥ | atra ca rātryādāv api śrāddham iṣyate | yad āha viṣṇuḥ |

	saṃdhyārātryor na kartavyaṃ śrāddhaṃ khalu vicakṣaṇaiḥ |

	tayor api ca kartavyaṃ yadi syād rāhudarśanam || iti |

matsyapurāṇe |

	candrasūryagrahe caiva maraṇe putrajanmani |

	malamāse 'pi deyaṃ syād dattam akṣayakārakam ||

prasaṅgād grahaṇaviṣayam anyad api kiṃcid ucyate | tatra mārkaṇḍeyaḥ |

	candre vā yadi vā sūrye dṛṣṭe rāhau mahāgrahe |

	akṣayaṃ kathitaṃ puṇyaṃ tatrārke tu viśeṣataḥ ||

dṛṣṭe darśanayogya ity arthaḥ | vyāsaḥ |

	sarvaṃ bhūmisamaṃ dānaṃ sarve brahmasamā dvijāḥ |

	sarvaṃ gaṅgāsamaṃ toyaṃ rāhugraste divākare ||

divākara iti candrasyāpy upalakṣaṇam, yataḥ |

	indor lakṣaguṇaṃ puṇyaṃ raver daśaguṇaṃ tataḥ |

	gaṅgātoye tu saṃprāpte indoḥ koṭī raver daśa ||

	gavāṃ koṭisahasrasya samyag dattasya yat phalam |

	tat phalaṃ jāhnavīsnāne rāhigraste niśākare ||

	divākare punas tadvad daśasaṃkhyam udāhṛtam |

	candrasūryagrahe caiva yo 'vagāheta jāhnavīm ||

**[428]**	sa snātaḥ sarvatīrtheṣu kim artham aṭate mahīm |

	sūryavāre raver grāsaḥ some somagrahas tathā ||

	cūḍāmaṇir iti khyātas tatrānantaṃ phalaṃ bhavet |

	vāreṣv anyeṣu yat puṇyaṃ grahaṇe candrasūryayoḥ ||

	yat puṇyaṃ koṭiguṇitaṃ grāse cūḍāmaṇau smṛtam |

liṅgapurāṇe |

	candrasūryagrahe snāyāt sūtake mṛtake 'pi ca |

	asnāyī mṛtyum āpnoti snāyī pāpaṃ na vindati ||

	sūtake mṛtake caiva na doṣo rāhudarśane |

	tāvad eva bhavec chuddhir yāvan muktir na dṛśyate ||

snānaviṣayam etat | tataś ca samantrakam eva snānaṃ rāhudarśane sūtakādāv api kāryam | tathā |

	trirātraṃ samupoṣyaivaṃ grahaṇe candrasūryayoḥ |

	snātvā datvā ca vidhivan modate brahmaṇā saha ||

	ekarātram upoṣyaivaṃ snātvā datvā ca śaktitaḥ |

	kañcukād iva sarvasya niṣkṛtiḥ pāpakośataḥ ||

kātyāyanaḥ |

	upākarmaṇy athotsarge pretasnāne tathaiva ca |

	candrasūryagrahe caiva rajodoṣo na vidyate ||

devīpurāṇe |

	kārtike grahaṇaṃ śreṣṭhaṃ gaṅgāyamunasaṃgame |

	mārge tu grahaṇaṃ puṇyaṃ devikāyāṃ mahāmune ||

	pauṣe tu narmadā puṇyā māghe saṃnihitā śubhā |

saṃnihitā śubhā narmadā kurukṣetramadhyagety arthaḥ |

	phālgune varuṇā puṇyā caitraṃ puṇyā sarasvatī |

	vaiśākhe tu mahāpuṇyā candrabhāgā sarid varā ||

	jyeṣṭhe tu kauśikī puṇyā āṣāḍhe tāpikā nadī |

	śrāvaṇe sindhunāmā ca proṣṭhe śreṣṭhā ca gaṇḍakī ||

	āśvine sarayūḥ śreṣṭhā bhūyaḥpuṇyā tu narmadā |

	godāvarī mahāpuṇyā candre rāhusamanvite ||

	sūrye ca śaśinā graste tamorūpe mahāmate |

	narmadātoyasaṃsargāt kṛtakṛtyo bhaven naraḥ |

	evaṃ gaṅgāpi draṣṭavyā tadvad devī sarasvatī || **[429]**

matsyapurāṇe |

	gaṅgākanakhale puṇye prayāgaṃ puṣkaraṃ gayā |

	kurukṣetraṃ tathā puṇyaṃ rāhugraste divākare ||

ṛṣyaśṛṅgaḥ |

	rāhugraste yadā sūrye yas tu śrāddhaṃ prakalpayet |

	tenaiva sakalā pṛthvī dattā viprasya vai kare ||

mārkaṇḍeyaḥ |

	candrasya yadi vā bhānor yasminn ahani bhārgava |

	grahaṇaṃ tu bhavet tatra na pūrvaṃ bhojanakriyā ||

	nācaret saṃgrahe (?) tasmiṃs tathaivāstam upāgate |

	yāvat syān nodayas tasya nāśnīyāt tāvad eva tu ||

evaṃ ca sati,

	candrasūryagrahe nādyād adyāt snātvā vimuktayoḥ |

	amuktayor astagayor dṛṣṭvā snātvā pare 'hanit ||

ity atra candrasūryagrahaśabdas taduktam ahorātraṃ lakṣyati | anyathā "na pūrvaṃ bhojanakriyā" iti vākyavirodhaḥ syāt | sarvatrāhani rātau ca bhojanasya pratiṣiddhasya pratiprasavārtham uktam "adyāt snātvā vimuktayoḥ" iti | prasiddham anyat | dṛṣṭvety udayopalakṣaṇārtham, "yāvat syān nodayas tasya" iti vacanāt | tathā |

	grahaṇaṃ ca bhaved indoḥ prathamād adhi yāmataḥ |

	bhuñjītāvartanāt pūrvaṃ paścime prathamād adhi(dhaḥ) ||

prathamayāmād ūrdhvam ity arthaḥ | āvartanaṃ dinamadhyam | paścime tu rātriyāme rātreś caturthaprahare yadi grahaṇaṃ tadā rātrer eva tasyāḥ prathamapraharād adho bhuñjīteti | tathā |

	aparāhṇe tu madhyāhne madhyāhne yadi saṃgave |

	bhuñjīta saṃgave cat syān na pūrvaṃ bhojanakriyā ||

atyantāsamarthaviṣayam etat | samarthasya tu bhojane prāyaścittam uktaṃ kātyāyanena |

	candrasūryagrahe bhuktvā prājāpatyena śudhyati |

	tasminn eva dine bhuktvā trirātreṇaiva śudhyati ||

ṣaṭtriṃśanmatāt |

	sarveṣām eva varṇānāṃ sūtakaṃ rāhudarśane |

	snātvā karmāṇi kurvīta śṛtam annaṃ vivarjayet ||

	navaśrāddhasya yac chiṣṭaṃ grahaparyuṣitaṃ ca yat |

	dampatyor bhuktiśiṣṭaṃ tu bhuktvā cāndrāyaṇaṃ caret ||

	sūryagraho yadā rātau divā candragraho yadi |

	tatra snānaṃ na kurvīta dadyād dānaṃ na ca kvacit ||

yad bhūbhāgavyavasthitānām uparāgo darśanāyogyas tadviṣayam etat | **[430]** devalaḥ |

	yathā snānaṃ ca dānaṃ ca sūryasya grahaṇr divā |

	somasyāpi tathā ratrau snānaṃ dānaṃ vidhīyate ||

yatra graho(sūryo)dayād ūrdhvaṃ grastasya candrasyāstamayas tatra sūryodayāt prāg eva rāhudarśaṇanimittaṃ snānadānādi kāryam | na tu paścād ity arthaḥ | grahaṇanimittaṃ ca śrāddham āvaśyakam | tathā liṅgapurāṇe |

	sarvasvenāpi kartavyaṃ śrāddhaṃ vai rāhudarśane |

	akurvāṇas tu tac chrāddhaṃ paṅke gaur iva sīdati ||

śātātapaḥ |

	āpady anagnau tīrthe ca candrasūryagrahe tathā |

	āmaśrāddhaṃ dvijo dadyāc chūdro dadyāt sadaiva tu ||

	snānaṃ dānaṃ tapaḥ śrāddham anantaṃ rāhudarśane |

	āsurī rātrir anyatra tasmāt tāṃ parivarjayet ||

śrāddhaṃ prati ruciś caiveti | atra rucir icchā | sā ca sadā śrāddhānuṣṭhānaviṣayā bhavati tadaiva śraddhaṃ kuryāt | nimittena ca kālatulyatvāt tasyā aupacārikaṃ śrāddhakālatvam | evaṃ śrāddhaṃ prati kālavidhir uktaḥ | śrāddhasvarūpam āpastambaś cāha: "athaitan manuḥ | śrāddhaśabdakarma provāca prajāniḥśreyasāya tatra pitaro devatā brāhmaṇās tv āhavanīyārthe" iti | anena homātmakaḥ śrāddhaśabdārtho nirūpitaḥ | brāhmaṇā āhavanīyārtha āhavanīyakārye prakṣipyamāṇahavirdhāraṇalakṣaṇe vartante | na cābhuñjānās te tat kāryaṃ kartuṃ śaknuvantīty arthād brāhmaṇabhojanaparyantatā śrāddhasyānenoktā | ata eva vakṣyati |

	tato yathāsukhaṃ vācyaṃ bhuñjīraṃs te 'pi vāgyatāḥ | iti |

ata eva gṛhyakṛc chaunakaḥ: "navāvarāñ śrotriyān bhojayed ayujo vā" ity āha | manur api |

	pitṛśabdenātra yasya yasya mātāmahāder devatātvaṃ śāstrāntareṇa vidhīyate tasya sarvasya parigrahaḥ kriyate | tathā hi sati bahuvacanam upapadyate | pitṛśabdenātrāsapiṇḍīkṛtā **[431]** apy ucyante navaśrāddhādeḥ śrāddhatvasiddhyartham | āmaśrāddhādau ca praṇāḍyā brāhmaṇabhojanaparyantatāyā vidyamānatvān mukhyam eva śrāddhatvam | kiṃ tu pākapariveṣaṇādyaṅgānanuṣṭhānāt tatra gauṇatvoktiḥ | tasmāt siddhaṃ śrāddhasya homātvakatvam | tatra putrāder adhikāras tasya tatra kartṛtvasmaraṇāt | yat kartṛkaṃ hi yat karma sa eva tatrādhikārī yathā rājā rājakartṛke rājasūye | tatra śaṅkhaḥ |

	pituḥ putreṇa kartavyā piṇḍadānodakakriyā |

	putrābhāve tu patnī syāt patnyabhāve tu sodaraḥ || iti |

atra pitṛgrahaṇaṃ pradarśanārtham | tena mātur apy aurdhvadaihikaṃ putreṇa kāryam | yat tu śātātapenoktam,

	anvaṣṭakāsu vṛddhau ca pratisaṃvatsaraṃ tathā |

	atra mātuḥ pṛthakśrāddham anyatra patinā saha ||

iti, tat sapiṇḍīkaraṇād uttarakālaviṣayam | pretatvavimokṣārthaṃ śrāddhajātaṃ sarvam eva mātuḥ pṛthakkāryam | yad āha śaṅkhaḥ |

	anvaṣṭakāṃ tathā mātṛśrāddhaṃ caiva mṛtāhani |

	ekoddiṣṭaṃ tathā bhuktvā strīṣu nānyat pṛthag bhavet || iti |

atra caikoddiṣṭaśabdena pretatvavimocakaṃ sarvam eva śrāddham ucyate ca punar anvaṣṭakādiśrāddhāny ekoddiṣṭāny eva kāryāṇīty ucyate | ata eva viṣṇuḥ: "anvaṣṭakāsu daivapūrvaṃ śākamāṃsāpūpaiḥ śrāddhaṃ kṛtvānvaṣṭakāsv aṣṭakāvad vahnau hutvā daivapūrvam eva mātre pitāmahyai prapitāmahyai ca pūrvavad brāhmaṇān bhojayitvā dakṣiṇābhiś cābhyarcyānuvrajya visarjayet" | ata eva vṛddhiśrāddhe śaṅkhaḥ pārvaṇam eva vidhim āha |

	pitrāditrayapatnīṣu bhojyā mātṝḥ prati dvijāḥ |

	strīṇām eva tu tad yasmān mātṛśrāddham ihocyate || iti |

kecid anyatra patinā saheti vacanaṃ pitrā saha sapiṇḍīkṛtāyāṃ mātarīti vyavasthāpayanti | tatpramāṇatayā ca śātātapīyaṃ vacanaṃ paṭhanti |

	ekamūrtitvam āyāti sapiṇḍīkaraṇe kṛte |

	patnī patipitṝṇāṃ tu tasmād aṃśeṣu bhāginī || iti |

bārhaspatyam api |

	svena bhartrā samaṃ śrāddhaṃ mātā bhuṅkte sudhāsamam |

	pitāmahī ca svenaiva svenaiva prapitāmahī || **[432]**

iti, tad ayuktam | na hy atra vākyadvaye 'pi pitrā saha mātuḥ sapiṇḍanam avabodhyate | yena tadviṣayatve pūrvavākyasyaitat pramāṇaṃ syāt | yat tu sapiṇḍīkaraṇe kṛta ekamūrtitvam ity uktaṃ tat pitrādidai(de)vatye śrāddhe tatpatnīnāṃ sahabhāvalakṣaṇam ekamūrtitvam avabodhayati | na punar abhedalakṣaṇam | na hi yo yena sapiṇḍī kriyate sa tenābhinnas taddai(de)vatye vā śrāddhe sahabhāvena devatātvam anubhavati pramāṇābhāvāt | tasmāt pitāmahyā sapiṇḍīkṛtāyāṃ mātary apy eta vacanam upapadyate | sapiṇḍīkaraṇottarakālam eva pitrādidai(de)vatye mātṝṇāṃ sahabhāvena devatātvam ity etāvanmātravidhiparatvāt tasya | ata eva ṣaṭtriṃśanmate gotrasūtakasāhacaryeṇa bhartrā sahaikapiṇḍatvaṃ nāryāḥ kīrtyate |

	ekatvaṃ sā gatā bhartuḥ piṇḍe gotre 'tha sūtake |

	na pṛthakpiṇḍadānaṃ tu tasmāt patnīṣu vidyate || iti |

tataś ca pitāmahyā pitāmahena vā sapiṇḍīkṛtāyā mātur na pṛthakśrāddham | etac cāniyatam iti gamyate caturviṃśatimatāt |

	kṣayāhaṃ varjayitvaikaṃ strīṇāṃ nāsti pṛthakkriyā |

	kecid icchanti nārīṇāṃ pṛthakśrāddhaṃ maharṣayaḥ || iti |

tataś cānvaṣṭakāditraye strīṇāṃ śrāddhaṃ pṛthag eva | gayāmahālayādau tu pṛthak saha vā svabhartṛbhir iti siddham |

	pituḥ putreṇa kartavyā piṇḍadānodakakriyā |

iti piṇḍadānagrahaṇaṃ sakalaurdhvadaihikopalakṣaṇārtham | putraśabdo yady apy aurase mukhyaḥ kṣetrajādiṣu gauṇas tathāpi "putrābhāve tu patnī syāt" ity atra mukhye gauṇe ca vartate | anyathā gauputrakaraṇe yad uktam,

	piṇḍado 'ṃśaharaś caiṣāṃ pūrvābhāve paraḥ paraḥ |

iti, tad virudhyate | "patnyabhāve tu sodaraḥ" iti sodaragrahaṇaṃ patnyabhāve yo dāyaharas tadupalakṣaṇārtham | tataś ca duhitrādīnāṃ śrāddhadatvam uktaṃ bhavati | atra ca patnīśabdo vivāhayajñasaṃyoginyāṃ bhāryāyāṃ vartate | yat punar āha kātyāyanaḥ |

	aṣṭakāyāṃ patir dadyād aputrāyāṃ na tu kvacit |

	na putrasya pitā caiva nānujasya tathāgrajaḥ || **[433]**

iti, tad aṃśaharatvābhāve pitrāder draṣṭavyam | aṃśaharatve 'pi pitrādir api kuryād eva | baudhāyanaḥ |

	pituḥ putreṇa kartavyaṃ na kurvīta pitā sute |

	atisnehāt tu kartavyaṃ sapiṇḍīkaraṇaṃ tyajet ||

viṣṇuḥ: "yaś cārthaharaḥ sa piṇḍadāyī putraḥ pitṛvittābhāve 'pi piṇḍaṃ dadyāt" | piṇḍaśabdaḥ śrāddhopalakṣaṇārthaḥ | putrasaṃstutā bhrātṛputrasapatnīputrānujabhrātaro riktagrahaṇe 'pi śrāddhaṃ dadyuḥ | tathā ca manuḥ |

	bhrātṝṇām ekajātānām ekaś cet putravān bhavet |

	sarve te tena putreṇa putriṇo manur abravīt ||

	sarvāsām ekapatnīnām ekā cet putriṇī bhavet |

	sarvās tās tena putreṇa prāha putravatīr manuḥ ||

tathā |

	putravat pālayec caināñ jyeṣṭho bhrātā yavīyasaḥ |

tathā |

	mātur agre 'dhijananaṃ dvitīyaṃ mauñjibandhane |

	tatrāsya mātā sāvitrī pitā tv ācārya ucyate ||

viṣṇupurāṇe tv anyathā krama uktaḥ |

	putraḥ pautraḥ prapautro vā tadvad bhātrādisaṃtatiḥ |

	sapiṇḍasaṃtatir vāpi kriyārhā nṛpa jāyate ||

	teṣām abhāve sarveṣāṃ samānodakasaṃtatiḥ |

	mātṛpakṣasya piṇḍena saṃbaddho yo jalena vā ||

	kuladvaye 'pi cotsanne strībhiḥ kāryā kriyā nṛpa |

	tatsaṃghāntargatair vāpi kāryāḥ sarvā matāḥ kriyāḥ ||

	utsannabandho raktād vā kārayed avanīpatiḥ |

	pūrvakriyā madhyamāś ca tathā caivottarāḥ kriyāḥ ||

	triprakārāḥ kriyā hy etās tāsāṃ bhedāñ śṛṇuṣva me |

ā dāhād dhāryāyudhādisparśād antyāś ca(?) yāḥ kriyāḥ piṇḍadānād yā aśaucamadhyabhāvās tāḥ pūrvāḥ | madhyamā māsi māsy ekoddiṣṭasaṃjñakāḥ |

	prete pitṛtvam āpanne sapiṇḍīkaraṇād anu |

	kriyante yāḥ kriyāḥ pitryāḥ procyante tā nṛpottarāḥ ||

**[434]**	pitṛmātṛsapiṇḍais tu samānasalilais tathā |

	tat saṃdhāntargataiś caiva rājñā vā dhanahāriṇā ||

	pūrvakriyās tu kartavyāḥ putrādyair eva cottarāḥ |

	dauhitrair vā naraśreṣṭha kāryās tattanayais tathā ||

	mṛtāhani tu kartavyāḥ strīṇām apy uttarāḥ kriyāḥ |

	pratisaṃvatsaraṃ rājann ekoddiṣṭavidhānataḥ || iti |

smṛtyantaram |

	putro bhrātā tathā śiṣyaḥ sagotrodakabhāginaḥ |

	vihitāḥ piṇḍadāne tu tathā bandhuḥ samāśritaḥ ||

gautamaḥ: "putrābhāve sapiṇḍamātṛsapiṇḍāḥ śiṣyāś ca dadyuḥ | tadabhāva ṛtvigācāryau" iti | dharmaḥ |

	mātulo bhāgineyasya svasrīyo mātulasya ca |

	śvaśurasya guroś caiva sakhyur mātāmahasya ca ||

	eteṣāṃ caiva bhāryābhyaḥ svasur mātuḥ pitus tathā |

	śrāddhadānaṃ tu kartavyaṃ nāmabhis tat tathaiva ca ||

mārkaṇḍeyapurāṇāt |

	putrābhāve sapiṇḍas tu tadabhāve sahodakaḥ |

	mātuḥ sapiṇḍā vā ye syur ye vā mātuḥ sahodakāḥ ||

	sarvābhāve striyaḥ kuryuḥ svabhartṝṇām amantrakam |

	tadabhāve tu nṛpatiḥ kārayet svakuṭumbavat ||

	tajjātīyair naraiḥ samyag dāhādyāḥ sakalāḥ kriyāḥ |

	sarveṣām eva varṇānāṃ bāndhavo nṛpatir yataḥ ||

strīśabdo 'tra bhujiṣyāvarodhanādyapariṇītastrīviṣayaḥ | tataś ca "patnyabhāve tu sodaraḥ" ity anenāvirodhaḥ |

	prītyā śrāddhaṃ tu kartavyaṃ sarveṣāṃ varṇaliṅginām |

	evaṃ kurvan naraḥ samyaṅ mahatīṃ śriyam āpnuyāt ||

liṅgina āśramiṇaḥ | atra viṣaye viśeṣair apavādam āha pāraskaraḥ |

	na brāhmaṇena kartavyaṃ śūdrasyāpy aurdhvadaihikam |

	śūdreṇa vā brāhmaṇasya vinā pāraśavāt kvacit || **[435]**

pāraśavo vinnāyāṃ śūdrāyāṃ brāhmaṇāj jātaḥ | sa ca brāhmaṇyādiputrāntarābhāve 'dhikārī | kārṣṇājiniḥ |

	putraḥ śiṣyo 'tha vā patnī pitā bhrātā snuṣā guruḥ |

	strīhārī dhanahārī ca kuryāt piṇḍodakakriyām ||

brahmapurāṇam |

	brāhmaṇas tv anyavarṇānāṃ na karoti kadācana |

	kāmān mohād bhayāl lobhāt kṛtvā tajjātitāṃ vrajet ||

	putrāḥ kurvanti viprāya kṣatraviṭśūdrayonayaḥ |

	sa tādṛśebhyaḥ putrebhyo na karoti kadācana ||

	svamātā kurute teṣāṃ te 'pi tasyāś ca kurvate ||

smṛtyantaram |

	strīṇām amantrakaṃ śrāddhaṃ tathā śūdrāsutasya ca |

	prāg dvijāter vratādeśāt te 'pi kuryus tathaiva tat ||

atha dvyāmuṣyāyaṇādhikāro nirūpyate | tatra yamaḥ |

	kuryān mātāmahaśrāddhaṃ niyamāt putrikāsutaḥ |

	ubhayor atha saṃbaddhaḥ kuryāt sa ubhayor api ||

dvividhaḥ putrikāputraḥ | eko mātāmahenaiva saṃbaddho 'paraḥ pitṛmātāmahābhyām iti | tatra prathamo mātāmahaśrāddhaṃ niyamena kuryāt pitṛśrāddham icchayā | yas tūbhayasaṃbaddhaḥ sa ubhayor niyamena kuryāt | tatra mātāmahaśrāddham ekoddiṣṭaṃ tripuruṣaṃ veti jijñāsāyāṃ kātyāyana āha |

	mātāmahasyāputrasya śrāddhādi pitṛvad bhavet |

	saṃbandhibāndhavādīnām ekoddiṣṭaṃ tu sarvadā ||

etac ca dauhitramātraviṣayam aviśeṣāt | na tu putrikāputraviṣayam eva | yasya tu putrikāputrasya mātaiva mātāmahena putratayā parigṛhītā taṃ prati manur āha |

	mātuḥ prathamataḥ piṇḍaṃ nirvapet putrikāsutaḥ |

	dvitīyaṃ tu pitus tasyās tṛtīyaṃ tu pituḥ pituḥ ||

yas tu dauhitro na tu putrikāputraḥ kiṃ tu,

	akṛtā vā kṛtā vāpi yaṃ vindet sadṛśāt sutam |

	pautrī pitāmahas tena dadyāt piṇḍaṃ hared dhanam ||

iti manuvacanabalān mātāmahadhanādāyī sa niyamena mātāmahaśrāddhaṃ kuryāt | **[436]** yad āha skandaḥ |

	śrāddhaṃ mātāmahānāṃ tu avaśyaṃ dhanahāriṇā |

	dauhitreṇārthaniṣkṛtyai kartavyaṃ vidhivat sadā||

atropapattim āha |

	malam etan manuṣyāṇāṃ draviṇaṃ yat prakīrtitam |

	tad gṛhṇan malam ādatte durbhida jñāninām api ||

	ṛṣibhis tasya nirdiṣṭā niṣkṛtiḥ pāvanā parā |

	ā dehapatanāt kuryāt tasya piṇḍōdakakriyām || iti |

yas tu dauhitro na putrikāputro na ca mātāmahasya dhanaṃ gṛhṇāti sa tasyāputrasya śrāddhaṃ kurvan niḥśreyasena yujyate | na punar akuvan pratyavāyī syāt | kṣetrajo 'pi dvyāmuṣyāyaṇo yaḥ kṣetrikabījibhyāṃ pitṛbhyāṃ saṃbaddhas taṃ prati devala āha |

	dvyāmuṣyāyaṇakā dadyur dvābhyāṃ piṇḍodake pṛthak |

	dvābhyāṃ deyās tu ṣaṭpiṇḍā eva kurvan na muhyati ||

dvābhyāṃ pitṛvargābhyām ity arthaḥ | evaṃ brāhmaṇabhojane 'pi | atrāsamarthaṃ prati baudhāyana āha |

	dvipituḥ piṇḍadānaṃ syāt piṇḍaḥ piṇḍo dvināmakaḥ |

	dvābhyāṃ deyās trayaḥ piṇḍā evaṃ kurvan na muhyati ||

atra kramaviśeṣam āha ṛṣyaśṛṅgaḥ |

	kṣetrikasya pitus tv ādau dadyāt piṇḍaṃ tathodakam |

	paścāt tu yena ye jātās tebhyo dadyāj jalāñjalim ||

marīciḥ |

	sagotro vānyagotro vā yo bhaved vidhavāsutaḥ |

	piṇḍaṃ śrāddhavidhānaṃ ca kṣetriṇe prāg vinirvapet ||

	bījine ca tataḥ paścāt kṣetrī jīvati cet kvacit |

	bījine dadyur ādau ca mṛte paścāt pradīyate ||

	ubhau yadi mṛtau syātāṃ bījiny ādau tadā dadet (?) |

	kṣetriṇy ādau na dattaṃ ced bījine nopatiṣṭhati ||

nāradaḥ |

	jātā ye tv aniyuktāyām ekena bahubhis tathā |

	arikthabhājas te sarve bījinām eva te sutāḥ ||

	dadyus te bījine piṇḍaṃ mātā cec chulkato hṛtā |

	aśulkopanatāyā te piṇḍadā voḍhur eva te ||

śulkaṃ mūlyam | **[437]** ṛṣyaśṛṅgaḥ |

	strīṇām ādyasya bhartur vai yad gotraṃ tena nirvapet |

	yadi tv akṣatayoniḥ syād anyapakṣasamāśritā ||

	tadgotreṇa tathā deyaṃ piṇḍaṃ śrāddham tathodakam || 1.217–218 ||

_śrāddhasaṃpattihetūna viprāñ ślokatrayeṇāha_ |

	**agryaḥ sarveṣu vedeṣu śrotriyo brahmavid yuvā |**

**	vedārthavij jyeṣṭhasāmā trimadhus trisuparṇakaḥ || 1.219 ||**

**	svasrīyaṛtvigjāmātṛyājyaśvaśuramātulāḥ |**

**	trinā(ṇā)ciketadauhitraśiṣyasaṃbandhibāndhavāḥ || 1.220 ||**

**	jñānaniṣṭhās taponiṣṭhāḥ pañcāgnir brahmacāriṇaḥ |**

**	pitṛmātṛparāś caiva brāhmaṇāḥ śrāddhasaṃpade || 1.221 ||**

agryo mukhyo 'dhyetṝṇām, sarveṣu caturṣu vedeṣu | śrotriyo yathāvidhy ekaśākhādhyāyī | brahmavid aupaniṣadapuruṣavit | yuvā madhyavayāḥ | vedārthavid vedavākyārthavit | jyeṣṭhasāmā jyeṣṭhasāmākhyaṃ vrataṃ kṛtvā jyeṣṭhākhyasāmādhyetā | trimadhvākhyaṃ vrataṃ kṛtvā yas tadākhyam eva vedabhāgam adhīte sa trimadhuḥ | evaṃ trisuparṇaḥ | trinā(ṇā)ciketavratapūrvakaṃ tadākhyavedabhāgādhyāyī trinā(ṇā)ciketaḥ | saṃbandhino vaivāhyāḥ | bāndhavā mātāmahaprabhṛtayaḥ | jñānaniṣṭhā adhyātmavidaḥ | karmaniṣṭhā iti pāṭhe vihitānuṣṭhānaparāḥ | evaṃ taponiṣṭhāḥ | sabhyāvasathyau tretā ceti pañcāgnayas tadvān pañcāgniḥ | brahmacāriṇa ity ekasmin bahuvacanaṃ jātyabhiprāyam | anye prasiddhāḥ | ete brāhmaṇā bhojyamānāḥ śrāddhasya saṃpade samṛddhaye bhavanti | atra manuḥ |

	śrotriyāyaiva deyāni havyakavyāni dātṛbhiḥ |

	arhattamāya viprāya tasmai dattaṃ mahāphalam ||

	ekaikam api vidvāṃsaṃ daive pitrye ca bhojayet |

	puṣkalaṃ phalam āpnoti nāmantrajñān bahūn api ||

	dūrād eva prīkṣeta brāhmaṇaṃ vedapāragam |

	tīrthaṃ taddhavyakavyānāṃ pradāne so 'tithiḥ smṛtaḥ ||

pitṛprabhṛtibahutarapuruṣaprīkṣā dūrāt parīkṣā | tīrthaṃ jalaprāptimārgaḥ | tena **[438]** yathodakaṃ prāpyata evaṃ devapitṛbhis tathāvidhavipramārgeṇa havyakavyāni prāpyante | atithir dātur atyantopakārakaḥ |

	sahasraṃ tu sahasrāṇām anṛcāṃ yatra bhuñjate |

	ekas tān mantravit prītaḥ sarvān arhati dharmataḥ ||

sarvān arhati sa eko 'pi sarvais tulya ity arthaḥ |

	jñānaniṣṭhā dvijāḥ kecit taponiṣṭhās tathā pare |

	tapaḥsvādhyāyaniṣṭhāś ca karmaniṣṭhās tathaiva ca ||

niṣṭhā tātparyam |

	jñānotkṛṣṭeṣu kavyāni pratiṣṭhāpyāni yatnataḥ |

	havyāni ca yathānyāyaṃ sarveṣv eva caturṣv api ||

caturṣu jñānaniṣṭhādiṣv ity arthaḥ |

	vedavidyāvrasnātāñ śrotriyān gṛhamedhinaḥ |

	pūjayed dhavyakavyena viparītāṃs tu varjayet ||

veda eva vidyā vedavidyā | gṛhamedhino gṛhasthāḥ |

	eṣa vai prathamaḥ kalpaḥ pradāne havyakavyayoḥ |

	anukalpas tv ayaṃ jñeyaḥ sadā sadbhir anuṣṭhitaḥ ||

	mātāmahaṃ mātulaṃ vā svasrīyaṃ śvaśuraṃ gurum |

	dauhitraṃ viṭpatiṃ bandhum ṛtvigyajyau ca bhojayet ||

viṭpatir jāmātā |

	vratastham api dauhitraṃ śrāddhe yatnena bhojayet |

	kutapaṃ cāsanaṃ dadyāt tilaiś cāvakiren mahīm ||

	apāvyopahatā paṅktiḥ pāvyate yair dvijottamaiḥ |

	tān nibodhata kārtsyena dvijāgryān paṅktipāvanān ||

	agryāḥ sarveṣu vedeṣu sarvapravacaneṣu ca |

	śrotriyānvayajāś caiva vijñeyāḥ pakṅtipāvanāḥ ||

procyata ebhir vedārtha iti pravacanāni niruktādīni vedāṅgāni |

	trinā(ṇā)ciketaḥ pañcāgnis trisuparṇaḥ ṣaḍaṅgavit |

	brahmadeyānusaṃtāno jyeṣṭhasāmaga eva ca ||

brahmadeyānusaṃtāno brāhmavivāhoḍhāpatyam |

**[439]**	vedārthavit pravaktā ca brahmacārī sahasradaḥ |

	śatāyuś caiva vijñeyo brāhmaṇaḥ paṅktipāvanaḥ ||

pravaktā dharmārtham adhyapakaḥ | sahasrado bahupradaḥ | gautamaḥ: "śrotriyān vāgrūpavayaḥśīlasaṃpannān" — nimantrayetetyanvayaḥ — "yuvabhyo dānaṃ prathamam eke pitṛvat" | pitṛpitāmahaprapitāmahabrāhmaṇā vṛddhavṛddhataravṛddhatamā ity arthaḥ | vasiṣṭhaḥ: "yatīn gṛhasthasādhūn vā pariṇatavayasaḥ sukarmasaṃsthāñ śrotriyān aśiṣyān anantevāsinaḥ | antevāsino naiṣṭhikā[n] brahmacāriṇaḥ śiṣyān api guṇavato bhojayet |

	atha cen mantravid yuktaḥ śārīraiḥ paṅktidūṣaṇaiḥ |

	aduṣṭaṃ taṃ yamaḥ prāha paṅktipāvana eva saḥ ||"

śārīraiḥ śvitrādibhiḥ | yamaḥ |

	pītasomā virajaso dharmajñāḥ śāntabuddhayaḥ |

	vratino niyamasthāś ca ṛtukālābhigāminaḥ ||

virajaso vītarāgāḥ | vratino niyamasthā brahmacāriṇaḥ saṃyatāḥ |

	pañcāgnir apy adhīyāno yajurvedavid eva ca |

	bahvṛco yas trisauparṇas trimadhur vāpi yo bhavet ||

pañcāgnividyā nāma chāndogyopaniṣatpaṭhitavidyā tām adhīyānaḥ | 

	triṇāciketo virajāś chandogo jyeṣṭhasāmagaḥ |

	atharvaśiraso 'dhyetā catvāraḥ paṅktipāvanāḥ ||

virajā nāma mantraviśeṣaḥ | tadadhyayanād virajāḥ | arharvaśirā nāmātharvavedaikadeśaḥ |

	gṛhastho brahmacārī ca yajurvedavid eva ca |

	vedavidyāvratasnātā brāhmaṇāḥ paṅktipāvanāḥ ||

	mantriṇo niyamasthāś ca ye viprāḥ śrutisaṃgatāḥ |

	prāṇihiṃsānivṛttāś ca te dvijāḥ paṅktipāvanāḥ ||

mantriṇo rudrādimantrābhyāsaratāḥ | śrutisaṃgatāḥ śrutyabhimatāḥ | śrutyarthānuṣṭhāyina ity arthaḥ |

**[440]**	satyavantaś ca dhīrāś ca nityadānaratāś ca ye |

	maṅgalācārayuktāś ca te dvijāḥ paṅktipavanāḥ ||

	agnihotraratāḥ śāntāḥ kṣamāvanto 'nasūyakāḥ |

	ye pratigrahaniḥsnehās te dvijāḥ paṅktipāvanāḥ ||

anasūyakāḥ paiśunyarahitāḥ | kārṣṇājiniḥ |

	brahmadeyānusaṃtāno brahmadeyāpradāyakaḥ |

	brahmadeyāpatiś caiva brāhmaṇāḥ paṅktipāvanāḥ ||

	api syāt sa kule jantur bhojayed yas tu yoginam |

	vipraṃ śrāddhe prayatnena tena tṛpyāmahe vayam ||

viṣṇuḥ: "atha paṅktipāvanāḥ | vedāṅgasyāpy ekasya pāragaḥ purāṇetihāsavyākaraṇapārago dharmaśāstrasyāpy ekasya pāragaḥ | tīrthapūto yajñapūtas tapaḥpūtaḥ satyapūto gāyatrījapanirato jāmātā dauhitraś ceti pātraviśeṣeṇa ca yoginaḥ" | brahmāṇḍapurāṇāt |

	ye tu vṛtte sthitā nityaṃ jñānino dhyāninas tathā |

	śikhibhyo dhāturaktebhyas tridaṇḍibhyaś ca dāpayet ||

	alābhe dhyānabhikṣūṇāṃ bhojayed brahmacāriṇam |

	tadalābhe hy udāsīnaṃ gṛhastham api bhojayet ||

dhyānayogād vānaprastho 'tra dhyānaśabdenoktaḥ | bhikṣuḥ pravrajitaḥ | udāsīno rāgādirahitaḥ |

	siddhā hi viprarūpeṇa caranti pṛtivīm imām |

	tasmād atithim āyātaṃ abhigacchet kṛtāñjaliḥ ||

	pūjayed arghyapādyābhyāṃ pādābhyañjanabhojanaiḥ|

	urvīṃ sāgaraparyantāṃ divā yogīśvarāḥ sadā ||

	nānārūpāś caranty ete prajādharmeṇa yoginaḥ |

	tasmād dadyāt sadā śrāddhaṃ viprāyātithaye naraḥ ||

siddhā viditātmatattvāḥ | prajādharmeṇa prākṛtarūpeṇa |

	pipāditāya śrāntāya saṃbuddhāya bubhukṣave |

	tasmai satkṛtya dātavyaṃ yajñasya phalam icchatā ||

saṃbuddhāya vijñānavate |

**[441]**	akḷptānnaṃ ghṛṇiklāntaṃ kṛśavṛttim ayācakam |

	ekāntaśīlaṃ hrīmantaṃ sadā śrāddeṣu bhojayet ||

akḷptānnam akḷptabhojanam | ghṛṇiklāntaṃ sūryātapakhinnam |

	ṣaḍaṅgaviddhyānayogisarvatantrās tathaiva ca |

	yāyāvaraś ca pañcaite vijñeyāḥ paṅktipāvanāḥ ||

sarvatantraḥ śālīnākhyo gṛhasthaḥ | yāyāvaro gṛhasthaviśeṣaḥ |

	śrāddhakalpaṃ paṭhed yas tu sa nityaṃ paṅktipāvanaḥ |

	caturdaśānāṃ vidyānām ekasyā api pāragaḥ ||

	yathāvad vartamānaś ca sarve te paṅktipāvanāḥ |

	ye ca bhāṣyavidaḥ kecid ye ca vyākaraṇe ratāḥ ||

	adhīyānāḥ purāṇaṃ ye dharmaśāstram athāpi vā |

	puṇyeṣu ye ca tīrtheṣu kṛtasnānāḥ kṛtaśramāḥ ||

	makheṣu ye ca sarveṣu bhavanty avabhṛthaplutāḥ |

	ye ca satyavratā nityaṃ svadharmaniratāś ca ye ||

	akrodhanāḥ kṣāntiparās tañ śrāddheṣu nimantrayet |

	pratyāsannam adhīyānaṃ vyatikrāmati yo dvijam ||

	bhojane caiva dāne ca hanyāt tripuruṣaṃ kulam ||

devalaḥ |

	jyeṣṭhāśramaniviṣṭaś ca śatāyur jyeṣṭhasāmagaḥ |

	agnicit somapaś ceti brāhmaṇaḥ paṅktipāvanaḥ ||

jyeṣṭhāśramo gṛhasthāśramaḥ | agnicic chākkarāgnicayanakṛt | cayanāntaragrahaṇe somapa ity anarthakaṃ syāt | matsyapurāṇe |

	yaś ca vyākurute vedaṃ yaś ca mīmāṃsate 'dhvaram |

	sāmasvaravidhijñaś ca paṅktipāvanapāvanāḥ ||

	aṣṭavarṣā tu yā dattā śrutaśīlasamanvite |

	sā gaurī tatsuto gauraḥ paṅktipāvana eva saḥ ||

manuḥ |

	kiṃ brāhmaṇasya pitaraṃ kiṃ vā pṛcchasi mātaram |

	śrutaṃ ced asti vedyaṃ vā tan mātāpitarau smṛtau ||

yamaḥ |

	pañcāgnir vā yajurvedī atharvā brahmaśīrṣakaḥ |

	ātmavic cāṅgavic caiva brahmadeyāsutas tathā ||

yadi yajurvedī pañcāgnividyādhyāyī, ātharvaṇaś ca brahmaśīrṣādhyetā | **[442]** matsyapurāṇāt |

	maṇḍalabrāhmaṇajñā ye ye sūktaṃ pauruṣaṃ viduḥ |

	tāṃs tu dṛṣṭvā naraḥ kṣiptraṃ sarvapāpaiḥ pramucyate ||

yamaḥ |

	sthavirāṃs tapasvino dāntāñ śiṣṭān vā yadi vetarān |

	tān sarvān bhojayec chrāddhe sādhubhiś ca nimantrayet ||

	arjayitvā dhanaṃ pūrvaṃ dāruṇaiḥ kṛṣikarmabhiḥ |

	bhavet sarvātithiḥ paścāt sa rājan ketanakṣamaḥ ||

itarān asthavirān ity arthaḥ | ketanaṃ nimantraṇam | atriḥ |

	ṣaḍbhyas tu puruṣebhyo 'rvāg aśrāddheyās tu gotriṇaḥ |

	ṣaḍbhyas tu parato bhojyāḥ śrāddhe syur gotrajā api ||

asaṃbhave 'pi tribhyaḥ parato bhojyāḥ | yad āha gautamaḥ: "bhojayed ūrdhvaṃ tribhyo guṇavantam" | ṣaḍbhyas tribhya iti sapiṇḍapuruṣasaṃkhyānirdeśaḥ | atriḥ |

	pitā pitāmaho bhrātā putro vātha sapiṇḍakaḥ |

	na parasparam arghyāḥ syur na śrāddhe ṛtvijas tathā ||

	ṛtvikputrādayo 'py ete sakulyā brāhmaṇā dvijāḥ |

	vaiśvadeve niyoktavyā yady ete guṇavattarāḥ ||

	sagotrā na niyoktavyāḥ striyaś caiva viśeṣataḥ |

paṅktipāvana ity anuvṛttau vyāsaḥ |

	mātāpitror yasya vaṃśyāḥ śrotriyā daśa pūruṣāḥ |

	ṛtukālābhigāmī ca dharmapatnīṣu yaḥ sadā ||

chāgaleyaḥ |

	sarvalakṣaṇasaṃyuktair vidyārūpaguṇānvitaiḥ |

	puruṣatrayavikhyātaiḥ sarvaṃ śrāddhaṃ prakalpayet ||

puruṣatrayavikhyātair iti pūrvoktāsaṃbhave | devalaḥ |

	ekāṃ śākhāṃ sakalpāṃ vā ṣaḍbhir aṅgair adhītya yaḥ |

	ṣaṭkarmanirato vipraḥ śrotriyo nāma dharmavit ||

	vedavedāṅgatattvajñaḥ śuddhātmā pāpavarjitaḥ |

	śeṣaṃ śrotriyavat prāptaḥ so 'nūcāna iti smṛtaḥ ||

	anūcānaguṇopeto yajñasvādhyāyamantravit |

	bhrūṇa ity ucyate śiṣṭaiḥ śeṣabhojī jitendriyaḥ ||

	vaidikaṃ laukikaṃ caiva sarvaṃ jñānam avāpya yaḥ |

	āśramastho vaśī nityam ṛṣikalpaḥ sa ucyate ||

**[443]**	ūrdharetās tapasy ugre rato niyatabhug yataḥ |

	śāpānugrahayoḥ śaktaḥ satyasaṃdho bhaved ṛṣiḥ ||

	niyataḥ sarvatattvajñaḥ kāmakrodhavivarjitaḥ |

	dhyānastho niṣkriyo dāntas tulyamṛtkāñcano muniḥ ||

	eṣāṃ paraḥ paraḥ śreṣṭho vidyādyair adhiko 'pi san |

	cīrṇavratā guṇair yuktā bhaveyur ye ca karṣakāḥ ||

	sāvitrījñāḥ kriyāvantas te rājan ketanakṣamāḥ |

	kṣatradharmiṇam apyājau ketayet kulajaṃ dvijam ||

	na tv eva vaṇijaṃ tāta śrāddheṣu parikalpayet ||

vṛddhamanuḥ |

	yaś ca vyākurute vācaṃ yaś ca mīmāṃsate 'dhvaram |

	ātmakaivalyavic caiva paṅktipāvanapāvanaḥ ||

yamaḥ |

	ṛjur ghṛṇī kṣamī dāntaḥ śāntaḥ satyavrataḥ śuciḥ |

	vedajñaḥ sarvaśāstrajña upavāsaparāyaṇaḥ ||

tathā |

	chagogaṃ bhojayec chrāddhe vaiśvadeve ca bahvṛcam |

	puṣṭikarmaṇy athādhvaryaṃ śāntikarmaṇy atharvaṇam ||

āpastambaḥ: "tulyaguṇeṣv api vayovṛddhaḥ śreyān | dravyakṛśaś cecchan" | matsyapurāṇe |

	arthajño vedavin mantrī jñātavaṃśaḥ kulānvitaḥ |

	purāṇavettā sarvajñaḥ svādhyāyajapatatparaḥ ||

	sivabhaktaḥ pitṛparaḥ sūryabhakto 'tha vaiṣṇavaḥ |

	brahmaṇyo yogavic chānto vijitātmātha śīlavān ||

skandapurāṇe |

	kulaśrutābhyāṃ saṃyuktād alubdhas tu viśiṣyate |

	tābhyām api ca viprābhyāṃ ciravāsī viśiṣyate ||

ciravāsī vijñātaśīlo yad vā gurukula cirakliṣṭo bhavatīti tātparyam | āpastambaḥ | "bhojayed brāhmaṇān brahmavido yonigotramantrāntevāsyasaṃbandhān guṇahānyā tu pareṣāṃ samuditaḥ sodaryo 'pi yojayitavyaḥ" | yonigotramantrāntevāsitvenāsaṃbandhān pareṣām asaṃbandhināṃ guṇahīnatvena guṇair yuktaḥ sodaryo 'pi bhojayitavyaḥ | kim uta vyavahitasaṃbandhaḥ || 1.219, 220, 221 ||

_uktaguṇānām api viprāṇāṃ rogitvādinimittena nindyatvaṃ ślokatrayeṇāha |_

	**rogī hīnātiriktāṅgaḥ kāṇaḥ paunarbhavas tathā |**

**	avakīrṇī kuṇḍagolau kunakhī śyāvadantakaḥ || 1.222 ||**

**	bhṛtakādhyāpakaḥ klībaḥ kanyādūṣy abhiśastakaḥ |**

**	mitradhruk piśunaḥ somavikrayī parivindakaḥ || 1.223 ||**

**	mātāpitror guros tyāgī kuṇḍāśī vṛṣalātmajaḥ |**

**	parapūrvāpatiḥ stenaḥ karmaduṣṭāś ca ninditāḥ || 1.224 ||**

rogibprabhṛtayo ninditāḥ śrāddhe varjanīyā ity arthaḥ | rogī dīrgharogī | tathā ca brahmapurāṇam |

	bhoktuṃ śrāddheṣu nārhanti daivopahatacetasaḥ |

	ṣaṇḍho mūkaś ca kunakhī khalvāṭo dantarogavān ||

	śyāvadantaḥ pūtināsaś chinnāṅgaś cādhikāṅguliḥ |

	galarogī ca gaḍumān sphuṭitāṅgaś ca sajvaraḥ ||

	khañjatūparamandāś ca tathānye dīrgharogiṇaḥ |

hīnāṅga ūnāṅgaḥ saṃkhyātaḥ parimāṇato vā | evam atiriktāṅgaḥ | aṅgam aṅgulyādi | kāṇa ekacakṣuḥ | cakṣur nāṅgaṃ kiṃ tv indriyam | ato hīnāṅgāt kāṇasya pṛthaggrahaṇam | punarbhūḥ punarūḍhā tasyāḥ patis tasyāḥ suto vā paunarbhavaḥ | tattvatas tu suta eva | ata eva hārītaḥ |

	svairiṇī ca punarbhūś ca retodhāḥ kāmacāriṇī |

	sarvabhakṣā ca vijñeyāḥ pañcaitāḥ śūdrayonayaḥ ||

	etāsāṃ yāny apatyāni cotpadyante kadācana |

	na tān paṅktiṣu yuñjīta naite paṅktyarhakāḥ smṛtāḥ || iti |

retodhāḥ kuṇḍamātā | kāmacāriṇī anyapuruṣagāminī | sarvabhakṣā surāpī | avakīrṇinam āha devalaḥ |

	gūḍhaliṅgy avakīrṇī syād yaś ca bhagnavratas tathā |

gūḍhaliṅgī daṇḍādikāśramaliṅgarahitaḥ | bhagnavrato viplutabrahmacaryaḥ | **[445]** yamo py āha |

	vratī yaḥ striyam abhyeti so 'vakīrṇī nirucyate |

vratī brahmacārī | kuṇḍagolakāv āha manuḥ |

	paradāreṣu jāyete dvau sutau kuṇḍagolakau |

	jīve bhartari kuṇḍaḥ syān mṛte bhartari golakaḥ ||

kṣetrajasutaviṣayam etat | anyasyābrāhmaṇatvā evāprāptiḥ | kunakhī svabhāvān mṛtanakhaḥ | śyāvadantaḥ svabhāvāt kṛṣṇadantaḥ | bhṛta eva bhṛtako bhṛtakaś cāsāv adhyāpako bhṛtakādhyāpakaḥ | atha vā bhṛtako 'dhyāpako yasya sa bhṛtakādhyāpakaḥ | atra devalaḥ |

	bhṛtakādhyāpako yaś ca bhṛtakādhyāpitaś ca yaḥ |

	tāv ubhau patitau viprau svādhyāyakrayavikrayāt ||

klībaḥ ṣa(pa)ṇḍaḥ | aṅgulyādinā yaḥ kanyāṃ kṣatayoniṃ karoti sa kanyādūṣī kanyādoṣakhāpako vā | aniścitasatyabhāvena pāpakāritayokto 'bhiśastaḥ | mitradhruṅ mitradrohī | piśunaḥ paradoṣasūcakaḥ | somavikrayī somalatāyāḥ somayāgasya vā vikretā | parivindakaḥ parivettā | atra manuḥ |

	dārāgnihotrasaṃyogaṃ kurute yo 'graje sthite |

	parivettā sa vijñeyaḥ parivittiḥ sa pūrvajaḥ ||

śātātapaḥ |

	klībe deśāntarasthe ca patite pravraje tathā |

	yogaśāstrābhiyukte ca na doṣaḥ privedane ||

	pitṛvyaputrān sāpatnān paranārīsutāṃs tathā |

	dārāgnihotrasaṃyoge na doṣaḥ parivedane ||

paranārīsutā dattakādibhrātaraḥ | vasiṣṭhaḥ: "aṣṭau daśa dvādaśa vā varṣāṇi jyeṣṭhaṃ bhrātaram aniviṣṭam apratīkṣamāṇaḥ prāyaścittī bhavati" | aniviṣṭam akṛtavivāhāgnihotram | tatra ślokau bhavataḥ |

	dvādaśaiva tu varṣāṇi jyāyān dharmārthayor gataḥ |

	nyāyyaḥ partīkṣituṃ bhrātā śrūyamāṇaḥ punaḥ punaḥ ||

	unmattaḥ kilbiṣī kuṣṭhī patitaḥ klība eva ca |

	rājayakṣmy āmayāvī nā na nyāyyaḥ syāt pratīkṣitum ||

	khaññavāmanakubjeṣu gadgadeṣu jaḍeṣu ca |

	jātyandhe badhire mūke na doṣaḥ parivedane || **[446]**

vṛddhavasiṣṭhaḥ |

	agrajaś ca yadānagnir ādadyād anujaḥ katham |

	agrajānumataḥ kuryād agnihotraṃ yathāvidhi ||

etac ca dharmādhikāriṇi jyeṣṭhe 'gnyādheyam akurvati draṣṭavyam | nānadhikāriṇi | hārītaḥ |

	sodarāṇāṃ tu sarveṣāṃ parivettā kathaṃ bhavet |

	dārais tu parivedyante nāgnihotreṇa nejyayā ||

vivāhādhikāriṇānumato 'pi nodvahed ity arthaḥ | uśanā |

	pitā pitāmaho yasya agrajo vātha kasyacit |

	tapo'gnihotramantreṣu na doṣaḥ parivedane ||

yasya pitrādayaḥ santi tasya tadanujñātasya tapo'gnihotrādayaḥ parivedanahetavo na bhavantīty arthaḥ | sumantuḥ |

	pitur yasya tu nādhānaṃ kathaṃ putras tu kārayet |

	agnihotre 'dhikāro 'sti śaṅkhasya vacanaṃ yathā ||

anujñātasyeti śeṣaḥ |

	vyasanāsakticitto vā nāstiko 'py atha vāgrajaḥ |

	kanīyān dharmakāmas tu ādhānam atha kārayet ||

vyasanādinānadhikāritvam upalakṣyate | atas tadanumatenaivādhikārī kanīyān ādadhyā(dhyā)t |

	jyeṣṭho bhrātā yadā tiṣṭhed ādhānaṃ naiva kārayet |

	anujñātas tu kurvīta śaṅkhasya vacanaṃ yathā ||

śātātapaḥ |

	nāgnayaḥ parivindanti na vedā na tapāṃsi ca |

	na ca śrāddhaṃ kaniṣṭhasya yā ca kanyā virūpitā ||

anadhikṛte jyeṣṭha iti śeṣaḥ | jyeṣṭhe 'dhikāriṇi śrāddham kurvaty api kaniṣṭhas tu tat kurvan na parividyate | virūpāyāṃ jyeṣṭhāyām anūḍḥāyām api kaniṣṭhāvivāho na doṣāya | yogayājñavalkyaḥ |

	āvasathyam anāhṛtya tretāyāṃ yaḥ pravartate |

	so 'nāhitāgnir bhavati parivettā tathocyate ||

āvasathyādhānam apītarādhānavad bhavatīty āha gārgyaḥ |

**[447]**	sodarye tiṣṭhati jyeṣṭhe na kuryād dārasaṃgraham |

	āvasathyaṃ tathādhānaṃ patitas tu tathā bhavet ||

brahmagarbhaḥ |

	yājanādhyāpanādānair anindyebhyo dhanena ca |

	aupāsanaṃ samādadyā(dhyā)t sve kāle parivedayan ||

prakṛtam ucyate — mātāpitrācāryādīn vinā pātityādinā kāraṇena yas tyajati sa mātrādityāgī | tathā ca manuḥ |

	akāraṇāt parityaktā mātāpitror guros tathā |

gurur atrācāryo na pitā tasya pṛthagupāttatvāt | kuṇḍāśī kuṇḍagolakānnabhojī | tathā ca kuṇḍagolakāv abhidhāyāha manuḥ |

	yas tayor annam aśnāti sa kuṇḍāśy ucyate budhaiḥ |

brahmapurāṇāt |

	catuḥṣaṣṭyā palaiḥ śuddhaiḥ kuṇḍaṃ prasthacatuṣṭayam |

	bhavet tad yas tu nigiret sa kuṇḍāśī pataty adhaḥ ||

dharmahīno vṛṣalaḥ | tad āha manuḥ |

	vṛṣo hi bhagavān dharmas tasya yaḥ kurute tv alam |

	vṛṣalaṃ taṃ vidur devāḥ sarvadharmabahiṣkṛtam ||

tasyātmajo vṛṣalātmajaḥ | atha vā vṛṣalaḥ śūdraḥ sa ātmajo yasya sa vṛṣalātmajaḥ |

	parapūrvā pūrvam anyasmai dattā tasyāḥ patiḥ parapūrvāpatiḥ | stenaś cauraḥ | niṣiddhakarmakāriṇaś ca karmaduṣṭās te coktebhyo 'nye cikitsakadevalakādayaḥ śāstrāntarād avaboddhavyāḥ | atra manuḥ |

	ye stenapatitaklībā ye ca nāstikavṛttayaḥ |

	tān havyakavyayor viprān anarhān manur abravīt ||

nāsti daivam itimatimān nāstikaḥ | nāstikaśāstravyākhyānādinibandhanavṛttimāṃs tadvṛttiḥ | yamaḥ |

	nāśnanti piśune devā nāśnanty anṛtavādini |

	bhāryājitasya nāśnanti yasya copapatir gṛhe ||

	na kharair upayātasya na raktāmbaravāsasaḥ |

**[448]**	dvyaṅgulātītakarṇasya pitaro bhuñjate haviḥ ||

	ya etair lakṣaṇair yuktās tāṃs tu paṅktyā na nirviśet ||

śaṅkhaḥ |

	anadhyāyeṣv adhīyānāḥ śaucācāravivarjitāḥ |

	śūdrānnarasapuṣṭāṅgā brāhmaṇāḥ paṅktidūṣitāḥ ||

yamaḥ |

	caurā vārdhuṣikā duṣṭāḥ parasvānām ca nāśakāḥ |

	cāturāśramyabāhyāś ca vijñeyāḥ paṅktidūṣakāḥ ||

	ye vyapetāḥ svakarmabhyaḥ stenās te parikīrtitāḥ |

	kavyaṃ dadāti yas tebhyas tasya tat pretya naśyati ||

	jñānapūrvaṃ tu ye tebhyaḥ prayacchanty alpamedhasaḥ |

	purīṣaṃ bhuñjate sarve śataṃ varṣāṇy amutra te ||

	tasmād vai dātukāmena daivaṃ śrāddhaṃ ca sarvaśaḥ |

	praśāntebhyaḥ pradātavyaṃ nāśāntebhyaḥ kathaṃcana ||

vāyupurāṇe |

	yas tiṣṭhed vāyubhakṣas tu cāturāśramyabāhyataḥ |

	ayatir mokṣavādī ca ubhau tau paṅktidūṣakau ||

mahābhārate |

	aparijñātapūrvāś ca gaṇapūrvāś ca bhārata |

	putrikāputrapūrvāś ca śrāddhe nārhanti ketanam ||

ketanaṃ nimantraṇam | gaṇapūrvo gaṇaputraḥ | gaṇo gaṇako maṭhabrāhmaṇādir vā | manuḥ |

	na śrāddhe bhojayen mitraṃ dhanaiḥ kāryo 'sya saṃgrahaḥ |

	nāriṃ na mitraṃ yām vidyāt taṃ śrāddhe bhojayed dvijam ||

anyaviprāsaṃbhave sa evāha |

	kāmaṃ śrāddhe arcayen mitraṃ nābhirūpam api tv arim |

	dviṣatā hi havir bhuktaṃ bhavati pretya niṣphalam ||

brahmāṇḍapurāṇāt |

	nānuyogo 'sti vedānāṃ yo 'nuyuṅkte sa pāpakṛt |

	bhoktā vedaphalād bhraśyed dātā dānaphalāt tataḥ ||

anuyogaḥ parīkṣārthaṃ praśnaḥ kiṃ paṭhatīty evaṃrūpaḥ | kaśyapaḥ |

	arīn viśvastahantṝṃś ca vyaṅgān nakṣatrasūcakān |

	varjayed brāhmaṇān etān sarvakarmasu yatnataḥ ||

	kāṇāḥ kuṣṭhāś ca ṣaṇḍhāś ca tv acarmāṇaḥ kacair vinā |

	sarve śrāddhe na yoktavyā miśritā vedapāragaiḥ || **[449]**

acarmāṇaḥ śipiviṣṭāḥ | kacair vinā khalataya ity arthaḥ | mahābhārate |

	avratī kitavaḥ stenaḥ prāṇivikrayiko 'pi vā |

	paścāc cet pītavān somaṃ so 'pi ketanam arhati ||

vratam atra vedavratam | manuḥ |

	yāvato grasate piṇḍān havyakavyeṣv amantravit |

	tāvato grasate pretya dīpāñ śūlarṣṭyayoguḍān ||

śūlam ṛṣṭiś cāyudhaviśeṣaḥ | ayoguḍo lohapiṇḍaḥ | devalaḥ: "kūṭasākṣipuṃśtvopaghātistrījita-setubhedakatālāvadhāraṇaraṅgopajīvividharmapāṭhakanityayācakaprāyaścittanimittadhūrta-sāhasikamṛgayukitavanāstikapiśunaśaṭhavaṇigdharmipaunarbhavātmambharipukkasisamudra-yāyikṛtyābhicāraśūlamelakavaidyabhṛtakakanyādūṣakakṛtaghnakuhikakrūramitradhrugdattāpa-vyayisamayabhedivāgduṣṭaparuṣakāruśilpikahastyārohāśvabandhakāś ceti varjyāḥ" | tālāvadhāraṇas tālavādanājīvī | vidharmapāṭhakāḥ pāṣaṇḍyāgamasya pāṭhakāḥ | pukkasī mṛgavadhajīvī | dattāpavyayī dattāpahartā | aśvabandhako vikrayārtham aśvān yo badhnāti | vasiṣṭhaḥ |

	vidvadbhojyāny avidvāṃso yeṣu rāṣṭreṣu bhuñjate |

	tāny anāvṛṣṭim icchanti mahad vā jāyate bhayam ||

hārītaḥ |

	api vidyākulair yuktā hīnavṛttā narādhamāḥ |

	kṣaudreṣu niratā nityaṃ yātudhānāḥ prakīrtitāḥ ||

kṣaudreṣu parapīḍākareṣu karmasv ity arthaḥ |

	pakṣimīnamṛgaghnā ye sarpakacchapaghātinaḥ |

	nānājantuvadhe saktāḥ protkā durbrāhmaṇā hi te ||

tathā |

	śūdrapreṣyo bhṛto rājñā vṛṣalo grāmayājakaḥ |

	vadhabandhopajīvī ca ṣaḍ ete brahmabandhavaḥ ||

yamaḥ |

	yasya vedaś ca vedī ca vicchidyete tripauruṣam |

	sa vai durbrāhmaṇo nāma yaś ca vai vṛṣalīpatiḥ || **[450]**

uśanā |

	vandhyā tu vṛṣalī jñeyā vṛṣalī tu mṛtaprajā |

	aparā vṛṣalī jñeyā kumārī yā rajasvalā ||

	yas tv enām udvahet kanyāṃ brāhmaṇo jñānadurbalaḥ |

	aśrāddheyam apāṅkteyaṃ taṃ vidyād vṛṣalīpatim ||

	datvānuyogenārthāya patitān manur abravīt |

	vedavikrayiṇo hy ete naitāñ śrāddheṣu bhojayet ||

	asaṃskṛtādhyāpakāś ca bhṛtakādhyāpakāś ca ye |

	tamo viśanti te ghoram iti vaivasvato 'bravīt ||

ata evaite na bhojanīyā ity arthaḥ | manuḥ |

	jaṭilaṃ cānadhīyānaṃ durbālaṃ kitavaṃ tathā |

	yājayanti ca ye pūgāṃs tāṃś ca śrāddhe vivarjayet ||

jaṭilo brahmacārī | durbālaḥ khalatiḥ |

	cikitsakān devalakān māṃsavikrayiṇas tathā |

	vipaṇena ca jīvanti varjyāḥ syur havyakavyayoḥ ||

cikitsako vṛttyarthaṃ na dharmārtham | devalaḥ |

	devakośopajīvī ca nāmnā devalako bhavet |

	apāṅkteyaḥ sa vijñeyaḥ sarvakarmasu sarvadā ||

tathā |

	devārcanarato vipro vittārthī vatsaratrayam |

	asau devalako nāma havyakavyeṣu garhitaḥ ||

vipaṇo vaṇijyā | vipaṇajīvitayā pratiṣiddhasyāpi māṃsavikrayiṇaḥ pṛthakpratiṣedho 'tyantavarjyatvakhyāpanārthaḥ | tenoktaguṇavatāṃ vipaṇajīvinām apy āpady upādeyatvaṃ gamyate | evam anye 'pi sāmānyataḥ pratiṣedhasiddhau viśeṣapratiṣedhā atyantānupādānārthā veditavyāḥ |

	preṣyo grāmasya rājñaś ca kunakhī śyāvadantakaḥ |

	pratiroddhā guroś caiva tyaktāgnir vārdhuṣiś tathā ||

pratiroddhā pratikūlaḥ | tyaktāgniḥ śāstroktatyāgakāraṇam antareṇeti śeṣaḥ | vārdhuṣir niṣiddhavṛddhyupajīvī | niṣedhaś ca yathā |

	samarghaṃ dhanam uddhṛtya mahārghaṃ yaḥ prayacchati |

	sa vai vārdhuṣiko nāma brahmavādiṣu garhitaḥ ||

**[451]**	yakṣmī ca paśupālaś ca parivettā nirākṛtiḥ |

	brahmadviṭ parivittiś ca gaṇābhyantara eva ca ||

yakṣmī rājayakṣmī | nirākṛtim āha devalaḥ |

	adhītya vismṛte vede bhaved vipro nirākṛtiḥ |

kātyāyanas tv anyathā nirākṛtim āha |

	yas tv ādhāyāgnim ālasyād devādīn naibhir iṣṭavān |

	nirākartāmarādīnāṃ sa vijñeyo nirākṛtiḥ ||

brahmadviḍ brāhmaṇadveṣṭā | gaṇābhyantaro gaṇamadhyagaḥ | gaṇo maṭhastho brāhmaṇādiḥ |

	kuśīlavo 'vakīrṇī ca vṛṣalīpatir eva ca |

	paunarbhavaś ca kāṇaś ca yasya caopapatir gṛhe ||

kuśīlavo naṭādiḥ | tathā |

	brāhmair yaunaiś ca saṃbandhaiḥ saṃyogaṃ patitair gataḥ |

asya ca patitāt pṛthagupādānaṃ kṛtaprāyaścittasyānugrahārtham | upapātakasaṃyogyanugrahārthaṃ vā |

	agāradāhī garadaḥ kuṇḍāśī somavikrayī |

	samudrayāyī bandī ca tailikaḥ kūṭakārakaḥ ||

garado viṣadaḥ | bandī maṅgalapāṭhakaḥ | kūṭakārakas tulāder mānasya sākṣyasya vā kūṭasya kartā |

	pitrā vivadamānaś ca kekaro madyapas tathā |

	pāparogy abhiśastaś ca dāmbhiko rasavikrayī ||

kekaro 'py a(dhya)rdhadṛṣṭiḥ | madyaṃ drākṣārasādi na tu surā | tatpātuḥ patitatvenaiva niṣiddhatvāt | pāparogān āha devalaḥ: "unmādas tvagdoṣo rājayakṣmā śvāso madhumeho bhagaṃdaro mahodaram aśmarīty aṣṭau pāparogāḥ" | raso viṣaṃ pārad ikṣurasādir vā |

	dhanuḥśarāṇāṃ kartā ca yaś cāgredidhiṣūpatiḥ |

	mitradhrug dyūtavṛttiś ca putrācāryas tathaiva ca ||

agredidhiṣūm āha devalaḥ |

	jyeṣṭhāyāṃ yady anūḍhāyāṃ kanyāyām uhyate 'nujā |

	sā cāgredidhiṣūr jñeyā pūrvā ca didhiṣūr matā || **[452]**

manus tu didhiṣūpatim anyathāha |

	bhrātur mṛtasya bhāryāyāṃ yo 'nurajyeta kāmataḥ |

	dharmeṇāpi niyuktāyāṃ sa jñeyo didhiṣūpatiḥ || iti |

lakṣaṇābhidhānād eva didhiṣūpatir api varjya iti jñeyam |

	bhrāmarī gaṇḍamālī ca śvitry atho piśunas tathā |

	unmatto 'ndhaś ca varjyāḥ syur vedanindaka eva ca ||

bhrāmary apasmārī | śvitrī śvetatvak |

	hastigo'śvoṣṭradamako nakṣatrair yaś ca jīvati |

	pakṣiṇāṃ poṣako yaś ca yuddhācāryas tathaiva ca ||

	srotasāṃ bhedakaś caiva teṣāṃ cāvaraṇe ratāḥ |

sroto jalapravāhas tasya bhedako vidārakaḥ | āvaraṇaṃ setvādinā nirodhaḥ |

	gṛhasaṃbījako dūto vṛkṣaropaka eva ca |

	śvakrīḍī śyenajīvī ca kanyādūṣaka eva ca ||

gṛhasaṃbījako gṛhasya kartā | dūtaḥ saṃdhivigrahī | vṛkṣaropako mūlārtham |

	hiṃsro vṛṣalavṛttiś ca gaṇānāṃ caiva yājakaḥ |

	ācārahīnaḥ klībaś ca nityayācanakas tathā ||

vṛṣalavṛttir vṛttir yasya sa vṛṣalavṛttiḥ | bahavo militā ekakarmakāriṇo 'tra gaṇāḥ | pratyekaṃ bahūnāṃ yājakaḥ pūgayājakaḥ | tenāpunaruktatā | klībo 'nutsāhī |

	kṛṣijīvī ślīpadī ca sadbhir nindita eva ca |

	aurabhriko māhiṣikaḥ parapūrvāpatis tathā ||

ślīpadaṃ vyādhiviśeṣaḥ | uktavyatirikto 'pi sādhuninditaḥ | aurabhriko meṣajīvī | evaṃ māhiṣiko vyabhicāriṇīsuto vā | yathāha devalaḥ |

	mahiṣīty ucyate bhāryā sā caiṣa vyabhicāriṇī |

	tasyāṃ yo jāyate garbhe sa vai māhiṣikaḥ smṛtaḥ ||

	pretanirhārakaś caiva varjanīyaḥ prayatnataḥ |

pretanirhārako mūlyena, dharmārthaṃ tu na doṣaḥ |

**[453]**	etān viharhitācārān apāṅkteyān dvijādhamān |

	dvijātipravaro viprān ubhayatra vivarjayet ||

ubhayatra daive pitrye ca | gautamaḥ: "na bhojayet stenapatitanāstikatadvṛttivīrahāgredidhiṣū-didhiṣūpatistrīgrāmayājakājapālotsṛṣṭāgnimadyapakucārakūṭasākṣiprātihārikān | upapatir yasya ca saḥ | kuṇḍāśī sīmavikrayī | agāradāhigaradāvakīrṇigaṇapreṣyāgamyāgāmiparivittiparivettṛ-paryāhitaparyādhātṛtyaktātmadurbālakunakhiśyāvadantapaunarbhavakitavājaparājapreṣya-prātirūpikaśūdrāpatinirākṛtikilāsikusīdivaṇikśilpopajīvijyāvāditratālanṛtyagītaśīlān | pitrā vā kāmena vibhaktān | śiṣyāṃś caike sagotrāṃś ca vīrahā brāhmaṇetarapuruṣahā ca" | brahmahā ca patitatvenaiva gṛhītaḥ | patiśabdo 'gredidhiṣūdidhiṣūśabdābhyāṃ pratyekaṃ saṃbadhyate | yājakaśabdaś ca strīgrāmaśabdābhyāṃ pratyekaṃ saṃbadhyate | yājakaśabdaś ca strīgrāmaśabdābhyāṃ pratyekaṃ saṃbadhyate | kucāraḥ kutsitācāraḥ | prātihārika aindrajālikaḥ | upapatiṃ na bhojayet | upapatir yasya sa upapatis taṃ cety arthaḥ | paryāhitaparyādhātārāv āha laugākṣiḥ |

	sodarye tiṣṭhati jyeṣṭhe yo 'gnyādhānaṃ karoti hi |

	tayoḥ paryāhito jyeṣṭhaḥ paryādhātā kaniṣṭhakaḥ ||

tyaktātmā sāhasikaḥ | prātirūpikaḥ kūṭatulādimānavyavahārī, prakārāntareṇa vā pratārakaḥ | kilāsī kuṣṭhī, bhūmihartā vā | kusīdī kutsitavṛddhyupajīvī | jyāśīlo dhanurvidyopajīvī | evaṃ vāditrādiśīlāḥ | sagotrāḥ sapiṇḍāḥ | śaṅkhasikhitau: "anṛtavāk taskaro rājadviṣṭo bhṛtyo vṛkṣaropakavṛttir garado 'gnido māhiṣikaś chāgalikaḥ śūdropādhyāyo bandī ghāṇṭiko devalakaḥ purohito nakṣatrādeśavṛttir brahmapuruṣo 'patyavikrayī kitavaḥ kūṭakārakamānuṣapaśuvikrayiṇaś cety apāṅkteyāḥ" | hārītaḥ: **[454] **"cikitsakavṛṣalapreṣya-kārukakitavaśvakrīḍakaśakunijīvimīnaghātakāveṣṭakapuṃścalivārdhukṣikāhituṇḍikapratyavasita-bhṛtakādhyāpakabhṛtakādhyāpitamelakasūcakāniyāmakakuśīlavādīn daive pitrye ca varjayet" | manuḥ |

	somavikrayiṇe viṣṭhā bhiṣaje pūyaśoṇitam |

	apratiṣṭhaṃ vārdhuṣike naṣṭaṃ devalake bhavet ||

	yatu vāṇijake dattaṃ neha nāmutra tad bhavet |

	bhasmnīva hutaṃ havyaṃ tathā paurnarbhave dvije ||

	itareṣu tv apāṅktyeṣu yathoddiṣṭeṣv asādhuṣu |

	medo'sṛṅmāṃsamajjāsti vadanty annaṃ manīṣiṇaḥ ||

	apāṅktyo yāvataḥ pāṅktyān bhuñjānān anupaśyati |

	tāvatāṃ na phalaṃ tatra dātā prāpnoti bāliśaḥ ||

	yāvataḥ saṃspṛśed aṅgair brāhmaṇāñ śūdrayājakaḥ |

	tāvatāṃ na bhaved dātuḥ phalaṃ dānasya paurtikam ||

	vīkṣyāndho navateḥ kāṇaḥ ṣaṣṭeḥ śvitrī śatasya tu |

	pāparogī sahasrasya dātur nāśayate phalam ||

vīkṣyāndha iti yogyatātra vivakṣitā | tataś ca yatra pradeśe 'vasthitaś cakṣuṣmān viprān bhuñjānān avalokayituṃ kṣamas tatra pradeśe 'vasthito vāndho navater viprāṇāṃ bhojanaphalaṃ nāśayatīty arthaḥ | vāyupurāṇe |

	anāśramī tapas tepe taṃ vipraṃ na nimantrayet |

	aupapattis tathā śākyo nāstiko vedanindakaḥ ||

	dhyāninaṃ ye ca nindanti sarve te paṅktidūṣakāḥ ||

aupapattir aupapattikaḥ śuṣkatārkikaḥ śākyasāhacaryāt | āgamānusāratārkikaḥ praśasta eva |

	vṛthāmuṇḍāś ca jaṭilāḥ sarve kāpaṭikās tathā |

	nirghṛṇān bhinnavṛttāṃś ca sarvāñ śrāddhe vivarjayet ||

	prāha vedān vedabhṛto vedān yaś copajīvati |

	ubhau tau nārhataḥ śrāddhaṃ putrikāpatir eva ca ||

vedabhṛto vedaprāptaye parikrītaḥ | vedopajīvanaṃ vārādhyayanādi |

	vṛthā dārāṃśca yo gacched yājayec cāvṛto 'dhvare |

	nārhatas tāv api śrāddhaṃ dvijo yaś caiva nāstikaḥ ||

**[455]**	ātmārthaṃ yaḥ paced annaṃ na devātithikāraṇāt |

	nārhaty asāv api śrāddhaṃ patito brahmarākṣasaḥ ||

hārītaḥ |

	svakulaṃ pṛṣṭhataḥ kṛtvā yo vai parakulaṃ vrajet |

	tena duścaritenāsau kāṇḍapṛṣṭho na saṃśayaḥ ||

brahmapurāṇe |

	kṛtaghnān nāstikān stabdhān mlecchadeśanivāsinaḥ |

	triśaṅkubarbarān āndhrān bakān draviḍakuṅkuṇān ||

	karṇāṭakāṃś ca bāhlīkān kaliṅgāṃś ca vivarjayet ||

skandapurāṇe |

	īśvara uvāca |

	śrāddhaṃ parīkṣya dātavyam ity eṣā vaidikī śrutiḥ |

	parīkṣaṇāc ca rambhoru ārjavaṃ guṇavattaram ||

	aparīkṣya tu yo dadyāc chrāddham ārjavam āsthitaḥ |

	tasya tuṣyanti pitaro devatāś ca na saṃśayaḥ || 1.222, 223, 224 ||

	**nimantrayeta pūrvedyur brāhmaṇān ātmavāñ śuciḥ |**

śrāddhadināc ca pūrvedyur brāhmaṇān paṅktipāvanān | tadabhāve mātāmahādīn | ātmavān vijitendriyaḥ | śuciḥ prayato nimantrayeta | apratyākhyeyo niyogo nimantraṇam | devalaḥ |

	akruddho nibhṛtaḥ svasthaḥ śraddhāvān atvaraḥ śuciḥ |

	samāhitamanāś cātra kriyāyām asakṛt sadā ||

nibhṛto mandabhāṣī | svasthaḥ prakṛtisthaḥ | samāhitamanās tatparaḥ |

	śvaḥ kartāsmīti niścitya dātā viprān nimantrayet |

	nirāmiṣaṃ sakṛd bhuktvā sarvabhuktajane gṛhe ||

	asaṃbhave paredyur vā brāhmaṇāṃs tān nimantrayet |

	ajñātīn asamānārthān ayugmān ātmaśaktitaḥ ||

asaṃbhave pūrvedyur nimantraṇāsaṃbhave | tadaharnimantraṇapakṣe 'pi pūrvedyus tyaktastrīsaṅgā eva nimantraṇīyāḥ | atra mārkaṇḍeyaḥ |

	nimantrayeta pūrvedyuḥ pūrvoktān dvijasattamān |

	aprāptau taddine vāpi hitvā yoṣitprasaṅginam ||

	bhikṣārtham āgatān viprān kāle saṃyamino yatīn |

	bhojayet praṇipātādyaiḥ prasādya yatamānasaḥ || **[456]**

saṃyamino brahmacāriṇaḥ | pracetāḥ |

	savarṇaṃ preṣayed āptaṃ dvijānām upamantraṇe |

svayaṃnimantraṇāsāmarthya etat |

	kṛtāpasavyaḥ pūrvedyuḥ pūrvān pitṝn nimantrayet |

	bhavadbhiḥ pitṛkāryaṃ naḥ saṃpādyaṃ ca prasīdatha(ta) ||

	savyena vaiśvadevārthaṃ praṇipatya nimantrayet ||

manus tu vaiśvadevikabrāhmaṇānāṃ pūrvaṃ nimantraṇam icchati | yad āha |

	daivādyantaṃ yadīheta pitrādyantaṃ na tad bhavet |

	pitrādyantaṃ tv īhamānaḥ kṣipraṃ naśyati sānvayaḥ || iti |

tataś ca vikalpaḥ | yamaḥ |

	jātikriyāvabodhādyair guṇair yuktān alolupān |

	prārthayeta pradoṣānte bhuktān āśayitān dvijān ||

	sarvāyāsavinirmuktaiḥ kāmakrodhavivarjitaiḥ |

	bhavdbhir bhavitavyaṃ naḥ śvobhūte śrāddhakarmaṇi ||

	te taṃ tathety avighnena yātīyaṃ rajanī yadi |

	yathāśrutaṃ pratīkṣerañ śrāddhakālam atandritaḥ ||

te tatheti brūyur iti śeṣaḥ | matsyapurāṇe |

	dakṣiṇaṃ jānum ālabhya tvaṃ māyādya nimantritaḥ |

	evaṃ nimantrya niyamāñ śrāvayet paitṛkān budhaḥ ||

	akrodhanaiḥ śaucaparaiḥ satataṃ brahmacāribhiḥ |

	bhavitavyaṃ bhavadbhiś ca mayā ca śrāddhakarmaṇi ||

varāhapurāṇe |

	vastraśaucādi kartavyaṃ śvaḥ kartāsmīti jānatā |

	sthānopalepanaṃ bhūmiṃ kṛtvā viprān nimantrayet ||

	dantakāṣṭhaṃ ca visṛjed brahmacārī śucir bhavet ||

	**taiś cāpi saṃyatair bhāvyaṃ manovākkāyakarmabhiḥ || 1.225 ||**

tair nimantritaiḥ saṃyatamanovākkāyavyāpārair bhavitavyam | cakarāt kartrāpi bhavitavyam | manuḥ |

	nimantrito dvijaḥ pitrye niyatātmā bhavet sadā |

	na ca chandāṃsy adhīyīta yasya śrāddhaṃ ca tad bhavet || **[457]**

devalaḥ |

	pūrvaṃ nimantrito 'nyasya yati kuryāt pratigraham |

	bhuktāhāro 'pi vā bhuṅkte sukṛtaṃ tasya naśyati ||

manuḥ |

	ketitas tu yathānyāsaṃ havyakavye dvijottamaḥ |

	kathaṃcid apy atikrāman pāpaḥ sūkaratāṃ vrajet ||

aṅgīkṛtanimantraṇasyaitat | āpastambaḥ: "ārabdhe cābhojanam ā samāpanāt" | yamaḥ |

	ketanaṃ kārayitvāpi yo 'tipātayate dvijaḥ |

	brahmahatyām avāpnoti śūdrayonau ca jāyate ||

nimantrya brāhmaṇam atipatayate 'tikrāmati taṃ na bhojyata iti yāvat |

	āmantritas tu yaḥ śrāddhe tv anyasya kurute kṣaṇam |

	saṃvatsarakrtaṃ puṇyaṃ tasya naśyati durmateḥ ||

	āmantrya brāhmaṇaṃ yas tu yathānyāyaṃ na pūjayet |

	atikṛcchrāsu ghorāsu tiryagyoniṣu jāyate ||

hārītaḥ |

	daive vā yadi vā pitrye nimantrya brāhmaṇaṃ yadi |

	tarpayen na yathānyāyaṃ sa tat tasya phalaṃ haret ||

	prasādād vismṛtaṃ jñātvā prasādyainaṃ prayatnataḥ |

	tarpayitvā viśeṣeṇa sarvaṃ tat phalam āpnuyāt ||

manuḥ |

	nimantritas tu yaḥ śrāddhe vṛṣalyā saha modate |

	dātur yad duṣkṛtaṃ kiṃcit tat sarvaṃ pratipadyate ||

vṛṣalī śūdrā | manuḥ |

	daivapūrvaṃ tu yac chrāddham adaivaṃ vāpi yad bhavet |

	brahmacārī bhavet tatra bhuktvā śrāddham tu naityakam ||

kātyāyanaḥ : "tadahaḥ śucir akrodhano 'tvarito 'pramattaḥ satyavādī syāt | maithunaśramasvādhyāyān varjayet | āvāhanādi vāgyata ā upasparśanāt | āmantritaś caivam" | upasparśanam ācamanaṃ karmaṇo 'nte tatparyantaṃ vācaṃyamaḥ syād ity arthaḥ | vṛddhaśātātapaḥ |

	śuddhyarthaṃ prātar utthāya bhakṣayed dantadhāvanam |

etac ca bhoktur na dātuḥ, "klinnadantaḥ pitṝn yajeta" it śruteḥ | hārītaḥ: "atha śvobhūte dakṣiṇāpravaṇāṃ diśaṃ gatvā dakṣiṇāpraṇatān samūlān **[458]** darbhān āharet | aparigṛhītās cāpaḥ | kṛtaveśvakarmāṇaḥ sastrībālavṛddhāḥ surabhisnātāḥ śucivāsasaḥ syuḥ" | surabhisnātāḥ sugandhitailādidravyasnātāḥ | yamaḥ |

	samūlas tu bhaved darbhaḥ pitṝṇāṃ śrāddhakarmaṇi |

	mūlena lokāñ jayati śakrasya tu mahātmanaḥ ||

	rakṣanti darbhā asurāṃs tilā rakṣanti rākṣasān |

	vedavid rakṣati tv annaṃ yataye dattam akṣayam ||

brahmapurāṇe |

	haritā vai sapiñjūlāḥ snigdhāḥ puṣṭāḥ samantataḥ |

	ratnimātrāḥ pramāṇena pitṛtīrthena saṃskṛtāḥ ||

sapiñjūlā acchinnaprāntāḥ | baddhamuṣṭiḥ karo ratniḥ | saṃskṛtāḥ parāmṛṣṭāḥ | 

	tathā śyāmākanīvāradūrvāś ca samudāhṛtāḥ |

kuśābhāva iti draṣṭavyam | tathā ca viṣṇuḥ: "kuśābhāve kuśasthāne kāśadūrvāś ca dadyāt" | gobhilaḥ: "bahir upamūlalūnaṃ pitṛbhyas teṣām alābhe śūkatṛṇaśarasūryasutanalaṣaṇḍha(ṇḍa)varjaṃ sarvatṛṇāni" | śukatṛṇaṃ śūkadhānyatṛṇam | kātyāyanaḥ |

	haritā yajñiyā darbhāḥ pītakāḥ pañcapajñiyāḥ|

	samūlāḥ pitṛdai(de)vatyāḥ kalmāṣā vaiśvadevikāḥ ||

	piṇḍārthaṃ saṃbhṛtāḥ syur ye tarpaṇārthaṃ tathaiva ca |

	dhṛtaikatas tu viṇmūtre teṣāṃ tyāgo vidhīyate ||

purāṇāt |

	tarpaṇādīna kāryāṇi pitṝṇāṃ yāni kānicit |

	tāni syur dviguṇair darbhaiḥ saṃstarārthaṃ viśeṣataḥ ||

	sapiṇḍīkaraṇaṃ yāvad ṛjudarbhaiḥ pitṛkriyā |

	sapiṇḍīkaraṇād ūrdhvaṃ dviguṇair vidhivad bhavet ||

kuśagrahaṇamantraḥ |

	viriñcinā sahotpanna parameṣṭhin nisargaja |

	nuda pāpāni sarvāṇi bhava svastikaro mama || **[459]**

iti kuśāḥ | atha prokṣaṇam | tatra vṛddhaśātātapaḥ |

	bahir ācamya nadyādau sodakaś ca susaṃyataḥ |

	āharet prokṣaṇaṃ prājño naikajātir na cāvrataḥ ||

	śaivalatṛṇaparṇādyair asaṃskārāmbubhājanaiḥ |

	saikatāvastratoyādyair na kuryāt prokṣaṇaṃ budhaḥ ||

ekajātiḥ śūdraḥ | śaivalādibhir yuktair asaṃskṛtabhājanaiḥ | saikatāntargatair vastrādinirgataiś ca jalair na pokṣayed ity arthaḥ | āpastambaḥ |

	nālikābhinnapātreṇa kāṃśyapātreṇa caiva hi |

	pāṇyaṅgaphalajenāpi kuryān nābhyukṣaṇaṃ budhaḥ ||

nālikā veṇumayī | bhinnapātraṃ yan mṛnmayam | prāṇyaṅgajaṃ śaṅkhaśuktyādi | phalajaṃ nārikelabilvādimayam |

	gṛhe vā samyag ācāntaḥ kṛtvā svarṇodakaṃ budhaḥ |

	nādhovastraikadeśena śuddhyartham ap āharet ||

	yady ānītaṃ tu savyena prokṣayed dakṣiṇena tu |

	āgneyaṃ prathamaṃ proktaṃ viprahastād dvitīyakam ||

	tṛtīyam udakashtānāc caturthaṃ maṇikāt smṛtam ||

agniyuktabhājanastham āgneyam | maṇika udapātram | pracetāḥ |

	saṃgṛhyābhyukṣaṇaṃ yāyāt sopānatko gṛhaṃ prati |

	tad amuktvā gṛhaṃ prāpya ācāmet paricārakāt ||

	abhyukṣaṇodapātraṃ tu na tāvat sthāpyate kvacit |

	yāvan nācamanaṃ dattaṃ prokṣitā na galantikā ||

galantikā vādhdhānī | viṣṇuḥ: "na naktaṃ gṛhītena śrāddhakarma kuryād udakena" | brahmāṇḍapurāṇe |

	durgandhi phenilaṃ varjyaṃ tathā vai palvalodakam |

	nāpnuyād yatra gaus tṛptiṃ naktaṃ yac caiva gṛhyate ||

iti prokṣaṇam | atha vaiśvadevādiḥ | tatra laugākṣiḥ |

	pitrarthaṃ nirvapet pākaṃ vaiśvadevārtham eva ca |

	vaiśvadevaṃ na pitrarthaṃ na dārśaṃ vaiśvadevikam || **[460]**

devayajñārthaṃ vaiśvadevam | darśaśrāddhaṃ dārśam | etac ca śrāddhamātropalakṣaṇārtham | paiṭhīnasiḥ |

	pitṛpākaṃ samuddhṛtya vaisvadevaṃ karoti yaḥ |

	āsuraṃ tad bhavec chrāddhaṃ pitṝṇāṃ nopatiṣṭhati ||

laugākṣiḥ |

	pakṣāntakarma nirvartya vaiśvadevaṃ ca sāgnikaḥ |

	piṇḍayajñaḥ tataḥ kuryāt tato 'nvāhāryakaṃ budhaḥ ||

pakṣāntakarmāgnyanvādhānam | anvāhāryakaṃ darśaśrāddham |

	akṛte vaiśvadeve tu sthālīpākaḥ prakīrtitaḥ |

	anyatra piṇḍayajñāt tu so 'parāhṇe vidhīyate ||

piṇḍayajñasthālīpākāt prāg vaiśvadevaḥ kārya ity arthaḥ | bhaviṣyatpurāṇe tv anyakramaḥ |

	kṛtvā śrāddhaṃ mahābāho brāhmaṇāṃś ca visṛjya ca |

	vaiśvadevādikaṃ karma tataḥ kuryāt narādhipa || iti |

tathā |

	pitṝn saṃtarpya vidhivad baliṃ dadyād vidhānataḥ |

	vaiśvadevaṃ tataḥ kuryāt kṛtvā brāhmaṇavācanam ||

	ye agnidagdhā mantreṇa bhūmau yan nikṣiped budhaḥ |

	jānīhi tad baliṃ vīra śrāddhakarmaṇi nityadā ||

evaṃ vaiśvadevasya trayaḥ kālāḥ | ekaḥ pākāntaro 'paro balidānānantaraḥ śrāddhasamāptyanantaras tṛtīyaḥ | athāparetikartavyatā | tatra purāṇam |

	bhūmiḥ śrāddhe pañcagavyair liptā śodhyā tatholmukaiḥ |

	gauramṛttikayā channā prakīrṇatilasarṣapā ||

uśanā: "gomayodakair bhūmibhājanabhāṇḍaśaucaṃ kuryāt" | devalaḥ |

	tathaiva yantrito dātā prātaḥ snātvā sahāmbaraḥ |

	ārabheta navaiḥ pātrair annārambhaṃ ca bāndhavaiḥ ||

**[461]**	tilān avakiret tatra sarvato vāsayed ajān |

	asuropahataṃ sarvaṃ tilaiḥ śudhyaty ajena ca ||

	tato 'nnaṃ bahusaṃskāraṃ naikavyañjanabhakṣyavat |

	coṣyapeyasamṛddhaṃ ca yathāśakti prakalpayet ||

	tato nivṛte madhyāhne luptalomanakhān dvijān |

	abhigamya yathāmārgaṃ prayacched dantadhāvanam ||

	tailam udvartanaṃ snānaṃ snānīyaṃ ca pṛthagvidham |

	pātrair audumbarair dadyād vaiśvadevakapūrvakam ||

	tataḥ snātvā nivṛttebhyaḥ pratyutthāya kṛtāñjaliḥ |

	pādyam ācamanīyaṃ ca saṃprayacched yathākramam ||

audumbaraṃ tāmram | viśnuḥ |

	snāto 'dhikārī bhavati daive pitrye ca karmaṇi |

	pavitrāṇāṃ tathā japye dāne ca vidhicodite ||

vṛddhavasiṣṭhaḥ |

	japahomopavaseṣu dhautavastraḥ sadā bhavet |

	alaṃkṛtaśucir maunī śrāddhādau vijitendriyaḥ ||

pracetāḥ: "śrāddhakṛc chuklavāsāḥ syāt" | kaṣayaraktapratiṣedham āha baudhāyanaḥ |

	kāṣāyavāsāḥ kurute japahomapratigrahān |

	na tad devagamaṃ bhavati havyakavyeṣv atho haviḥ ||

yogayājñavalkyaḥ |

	jape home tathā dāne daive pitrye ca karmaṇi |

	badhnīyān nāsurīṃ kakṣyāṃ śeṣe kāle yathecchayā ||

	paridhānād bahiḥ kakṣyā nibaddhā hy āsurī bhavet ||

bhṛguḥ |

	nagnaḥ syān malavadvāsā nagnaḥ kaupīnakevalaḥ |

	dvikakṣyo 'nuttarīyaś ca akakṣo 'vastra eva ca ||

	nagnaḥ kāṣāyavāsāḥ syān nagnaś cārdhapaṭaḥ smṛtaḥ ||

śātātapaḥ |

	ekavastro na bhuñjīta na kuryād devatārcanam |

	na cārcayed dvijān nagnaḥ kuryād evaṃvidho naraḥ ||

	savyād aṃsāt paribhraṣṭaṃ kathaṃcid vivṛtāmbaram |

	ekavastraṃ tu taṃ vidyād daive pitrye ca varjayet || **[462]**

vṛddhamanuḥ |

	savyaṃdhautena kartavyāḥ kriyā dharmyā vipaścitā |

	na tu nejakadhautena nāhatena ca karhicit ||

ahatam āha kaśyapaḥ |

	ahataṃ yantranirmuktam uktaṃ vāsaḥ svayaṃbhuvā |

	śastaṃ tan māṅgalikyeṣu tāvat kālaṃ na sarvadā ||

māṅgalikyaṃ vivāhādi | tato 'nyatra sakṛt prakṣālitam ahatam ity āha pracetāḥ |

	īṣaddhautaṃ navaṃ śvetaṃ sadaśaṃ yan na dhāritam |

	ahataṃ tad vijānīyāt sarvakarmasu pāvanam ||

vyāsaḥ |

	acchinnāgraṃ ca yad vastraṃ mṛdā prakṣālitaṃ ca yat |

	ahataṃ dhāturaktaṃ tat pavitram iti vai sthitiḥ ||

śāṭyāyaniḥ |

	tataḥ sūryam upasthāya samyag ācamya ca svayam |

	abhyukṣaṇaṃ samādāya saṃyatātmā gṛhaṃ vrajet ||

	sopānatkaḥ sadarbhaś ca sapātraḥ sadaśottaraḥ ||

sadaśam uttaram uttarīyaṃ yasya sa sadaśottaraḥ | sūryopasthānaṃ brahmayajñādyupalakṣaṇārtham | yogayājñavalkyaḥ |

	tenodakena pātrāṇi prokṣyācamya punar gṛhe |

	pātrād virahitaṃ toyam uddhṛtaṃ savyapāṇinā ||

	na tena prokṣaṇaṃ kuryād vastranirṇejanena ca ||

brahmāṇḍapurāṇe |

	nāprokṣitaṃ spṛśet kiṃcid daive pitrye ca vā punaḥ |

	uttareṇāhared vedyā dakṣiṇena visarjayet ||

vediḥ śrāddhabhūmiḥ | gobhilaḥ |

	dānam ācamanaṃ homaṃ bhojanaṃ devatārcanam |

	prauḍhapādo na kurvīta svādhyāyaṃ pitṛtarpaṇam ||

	āsanārūḍhapādo yo jānvor vā jaṅghayos tathā |

	kṛtāvasikthiko yas tu prauḍhapādaḥ sa ucyate ||

baudhāyanaḥ: "nābher adhaḥ karasparśaṃ karmayukto vivarjayet" | tathā |

	saṃdhyayor ubhayor japye bhojane dantadhāvane |

	pitṛkārye ca daive ca tathā mūtrapurīṣayoḥ ||

	gurūṇāṃ saṃnidhau dāne yoge caiva viseṣataḥ |

	eteṣu maunam ātiṣṭhet svargam āpnoti mānavaḥ || **[463]**

yogayājñavalkyaḥ |

	yadi vāgyamalopaḥ syāj japyādiṣu kathaṃcana |

	vyāhared vaiṣṇavaṃ mantraṃ smared vā viṣṇum avyayam ||

mārkaṇḍeyaḥ |

	ahnaḥ ṣaṭsu muhūrteṣu gateṣu tv atha tān dvijān |
