	pratyekaṃ preṣayet preṣyaṃ snānārthaṃ cāmalodakam ||

	snātaḥ snātān samāhūtān svāgatenārcayet pṛthak |

	sthitān deśe vivikte tu prakīrṇatilabarhiṣi || 1.225 ||

	**aparāhṇe samabhyarcya svāgatenāgatān dvijān |**

**	pavitrapāṇir ācāntān āsaneṣūpaveśayet || 1.226 ||**

**	yugmān daive yathāśakti pitrye 'yugmāṃs tathaiva ca |**

**	pariśrite śucau deśe dakṣiṇāpravaṇe tathā || 1.227 ||**

**	dvau daive prāk tu pitrye trīn udag ekaikam eva vā |**

tān nimantritān āgatān viprān aparāhṇe 'hano 'parabhāge svāgatena svāgatavākyena pūjitān ācāntāñ śucau śuddhe pariśrite kāṇḍapaṭādinā parivṛte dakṣiṇataḥ kramanimne pradeśe daive vaiśvadevike yathāśakti yugmān prāṅmukhān pitrye pitṛkārye yathāśaktyā vā | ayugmān iti pāṭhaḥ | ayugmān udaṅmukhān āsaneṣu pavitrapāṇir upaveśayet | atha vā dvāv eva vaiśvadeve trīn eva pitrye | yad vobhayatraikaikam | dvicaturādisaṃkhyākā yugmāḥ | ekatrapañcakādisaṃkhyākā ayugmāḥ | mahāsaṃkhyāyām asamarthasya cālpasaṃkhyāvidhiḥ | yat tu manunoktam,

	dvau daive pitryakṛtye trīn ekaikam ubhayatra vā |

	bhojayet susamṛddho 'pi na prasajyeta vistare ||

	satkriyāṃ deśakālau ca śaucaṃ brāhmaṇasaṃpadam |

	pañcaitān vistaro hanti tasmān neheta vistaram ||

iti, tan nyūnasaṃkhyāpraśaṃsārthaṃ nādhikasaṃkhyāniṣedhārtham | tathā sati nādhikasaṃkhyā vidhīyate | vidhatte ca gautamaḥ: "navāvarān bhojayed ayujo vā yathotsāham" iti | gṛhyakṛcchaunakaḥ: "athātaḥ pārvaṇe śrāddhe kāmya ābhyudayika ekoddiṣṭe vā **[454]** brāhmaṇāñ śrutaśīlavṛttasaṃannān ekena vā kāle jñāpitān snātān kṛtaśaucāṃs tān udaṅmukhān pitṛvad upaveśya caikaikam ekaikasya dvau dvau trīṃs trīn vā vṛddhau phalabhūyastvaṃ na tv evaikaṃ sarveṣāṃ piṇḍair vyākhyātaṃ kāmam anādye" | asyārthaḥ — pārvaṇādiśrāddhacatuṣṭaye brāhmaṇāñ śrutādiguṇopetān ekena vā śrutādinā guṇena saṃpannān kāle pūrvedyur jñāpitān nimantritān snātān samāvṛttān āplutān vā taddine kṛtapādaśaucān pitṛvat pitṛtulyavayaskān | vṛddhavṛddhataravṛddhatamān ity arthaḥ | pitrādīnām ekaikasya sthāna ekam ekaṃ dvau dvau viprau trīṃs trīn viprān vopaveśyet | viprasaṃkhyayā vṛddhau phalabhūyastvaṃ na tu sarveṣāṃ pitrādīnāṃ sthāna ekaṃ brāhmaṇam upaveśayet | kāmam anādye ādyaṃ tu sapiṇḍīkaraṇaṃ tato 'nyad anādyam | yad vānnam ādyaṃ tadabhāvo 'nādyaṃ yad vānādyam āmam iti | brahmapurāṇe |

	deśakāladhanābhāvād ekaikam ubhayatra vā |

	śeṣān vittānusāreṇa bhojayed anyaveśmani ||

ubhayatra daive pitrye cety arthaḥ | śaṅkhaḥ |

	bhojayed atha vāpy ekaṃ brāhmaṇaṃ paṅktipāvanam |

	daive kṛtvā tu naivedyaṃ paścāt tasya tu nirvapet ||

purāṇāt |

	eka eva yadā vipro dvitīyo nopapadyate |

	pitṝṇāṃ brāhmaṇo yojyo daive tv agniṃ niyojayet ||

vasiṣṭhaḥ |

	api vā bhojayed ekaṃ brāhmaṇaṃ vedapāragam |

	śrutaśīlādisaṃpannaṃ sarvālakṣaṇavarjitam ||

	yady ekaṃ bhojayec chrāddhe daivaṃ tatra kathaṃ bhavet |

	annaṃ pātre samuddhṛtya sarvasya prakṛtasya tu ||

	devatāyatane kṛtvā tataḥ śrāddhaṃ pravartayet |

	prāsyed annaṃ tad agnau tu dadyād vā brahmacāriṇe ||

bṛhaspatiḥ |

	yady ekaṃ bhojayec chrāddhe svalpatvāt prakṛtasya tu |

	stokaṃ stokaṃ samuddhṛtya tebhyo 'nnaṃ nivedayet ||

brāhmaṇatṛptisamarthasyānnasya stokaṃ tṛtīyaṃ bhāgaṃ buddhyā pṛthakkṛtya tebhyaḥ pitrādibhyaḥ pratyekaṃ pradadyād ity arthaḥ | **[465]**

	aparāhṇe samabhyarcyety atra saṃdehaḥ | kiṃ dvidhā vibhaktasyāhṇa uttaro bhāgo 'parāhṇaḥ kiṃ vā pañcadhā vibhaktasya caturtho bhāgo 'parāhṇaḥ | tatra kecid āhuḥ: pañcadhā vibhaktasya caturtho bhāgo 'parāhṇa iti | tathā hi śrutiḥ: "ādityo vai sarva ṛtavaḥ sa yadaivodety atha vasanto yadā saṃgavo 'tha grīṣmo yadā madhaṃdine 'tha varṣā yadāparāhṇo 'tha śarad yadāstamety atha hemantaḥ" iti | smṛtir api, yad āha vyāsaḥ |

	muhūrtatritayaṃ prātas tāvān eva saṃgavaḥ |

	madhyāhnas trimuhūrtaḥ syād aparāhṇas tu tādṛśaḥ ||

	sāyāhnas trimuhūrto 'tha sarvakarmabahiṣkṛtaḥ || iti |

ataś ca śrautādiprayogāt pañcadhā vibhaktasyāhnaś caturtha eva bhāgo 'parāhṇaśabdavācya iti | tad anye nānumanyante | te hi manyante — naivāsmāt prayogād vācyaniyamaḥ śakyo 'vadhārayitum | bhavati hi śrutāv evāhno bhāgāntare 'py aparāhṇaśabdaprayogaḥ | yathā: "pūrvāhṇo vai devānāṃ madhyāhno manuṣyāṇām aprāhṇaḥ pitṝṇām" iti | atra khalu tredhāvibhaktasyāhnas tṛtīyo bhāgo 'parāhṇaśabdavācyaḥ prayujyate | tathā "tasmāt supūrvāhṇa eva pūrvayopasadā pracaritavyaṃ svaparāhṇe parayā" ityādau dinasyāntime muhūrte dvedhā vibhaktasyāhno dvitīye bhāge 'py asti prayogaḥ | yad āha manuḥ |

	yathā caivāparaḥ pakṣaḥ pūrvapakṣād viśiṣyate |

	tathā śrāddhasya pūrvāhṇād aparāhṇo viśiṣyate || iti |

tataḥ pañcadhāvibhaktasyāhnaś caturtha eva bhāge 'parāhṇaśabdaprayogaḥ ity asiddham | tadasiddhau ca na sa evāparāhṇapadavācyaḥ | yadi hi tathā syāt tadā paṅkajaśabdavat kuśalapravīṇādiśabdavad vā yogarūḍhatvādikalpanayāparāhṇe samabhyarcyetyādivākye madhyāhnasāyāhnayor madhagato 'hno bhāga eva vākyārthānvayī syāt | na tv etad asti | tasmād ahno 'paro bhāga ity anayā vyutpattyā yaugika evāyaṃ śabdaḥ | ata eva kutapakālavyāpinyām amāvāsyāyām amāvāsyāśrāddhaṃ kāryam āha jābāliḥ |

	bhūtaviddhā tv amāvāsyā pratipanmiśritā ca yā |

	tayos tu pitṛkṛtye 'pi grāhyāḥ kutapakālikī || iti || **[466]**

	anena ca pārvaṇaṃ śrāddhaṃ kutape kāryaṃ vidhīyate | anyathā kutapavyāpinyā grahaṇavidhir adṛṣṭārthaḥ syāt | tasmād aparāhṇe vihitaṃ śrāddhaṃ kutape kāryam iti vidhiḥ kutapasyāparāhṇāntarbhāvaṃ gamayati | bhavati ca kutapasya dvitīyam ardham aparāhṇamadhyavarti | ahno hi pañcadaśamuhūrtarūpasyāṣṭamo muhūrtaḥ kutapas tena tasya bhavati dvitīyam ardham aparāhṇaḥ | yadi ca sāyāhnāt prāktanaṃ muhūrtatrayam evāparāhṇaḥ syāt tadā grāhyā kutapakālikīti vidhinā kutapo nityavad vihitam aparāhṇaṃ bādhitvā vidheyaḥ | sa cābādhe saty anyāyyaḥ | ata eva kutapvidhānān nāhṇas tṛtīye bhāge 'syāparāhṇaśabdasya vṛttir avasīyate | yad uktaṃ gautamena,

	prārabhya kutape śrāddhaṃ kuryād ārauhiṇād budhaḥ |

	vidhijño vidhim āsthāya rauhiṇaṃ na tu laṅghayet ||

iti, tad api kutapamātravyāpikuhvādiśrāddhaviṣayam | na punaḥ sakalamadhyāhnavyāpiśrāddha-tithāv ekoddiṣṭaviṣayam | tathāhi sati rauhiṇānatikramavidher adṛṣṭaṃ mūlaṃ kalpyaṃ syāt | na tu viṣyāntare | tathā hi aparāhṇāntargatarauhiṇāṃśārabdhe śraddhe śrāddhāṅgabhūtatithikṣaye 'pi prārabdhakarmasamāptir anantaram eva tithyantare 'pi vidhinākṣipyate samāpyate ca | kutapottarārdhārabdhaṃ rauhiṇe śrāddhaṃ vinā puruṣāparādhād iti dṛṣṭamūlaiva rauhiṇānatikramasmṛtiḥ | tasmād ukta eva viṣayo 'sya vākyasya yuktaḥ | yat tu vyāsādibhir madhyaṃdināt parato muhūrtatraye 'parāhṇaśabdaḥ prayujyate | tat tasya bhāgasya śabdāntareṇa vyapadeṣṭum aśakyatvāt | na punas tasyaivāparāhṇapadavyapadeśyatvāt | darśito hi tasya sāyāhne madhyaṃdinottarārthe ca prayogaḥ | nanu ca dvitīyam aharardham aparāhṇas tathāpi yad aparāhṇe vihitaṃ tadahnaḥ pañcadhā vibhaktasya caturtha eva bhāge kāryam | yad āha parāśaraḥ |

	yad yad eteṣu vihitaṃ tat tat kuryād vicakṣaṇaḥ |

asyārthaḥ — yad yat karma snānadānaśrāddhādikaṃ pūrvāhṇādikāleṣu vihitaṃ tad eteṣu prātarādiṣu muhūrtatrayaparimiteṣv ahnaḥ pañcasu bhāgeṣu kāryam iti | tan na, na hy anena vākyenāparāhṇavihitaṃ śrāddham ahnaḥ pañcadhā vibhaktasya caturtha eva bhāge kāryam iti niyamyate | kiṃ tu piṇḍānvāhāryakaṃ śrāddhaṃ madhyaṃdinād uttaratra muhūrtatraye kāryam ity aucityaprāptam anūdyate | tad dhi pitṛyajñaṃ kṛtvā kāryaṃ pitṛyajñaṃ tu nirvartyety atroktam | yata eva nedaṃ niyamakam ata eva darśaśrāddhaprakaraṇe matsyapurāṇam |

**[467]**	ūrdhvaṃ muhūrtāt kutapād yan muhūrtacatuṣṭayam |

	muhūrtapañcakaṃ vāpi svadhāvācanam iṣyate || iti |

etac ca parāśaravākyasyāniyāmakatva eva yujyate | niyāmaktve tu punaḥ kutapasaṃjñakād aṣṭamān muhūrtād uttaro rauhiṇasaṃjñako muhūrtaḥ śrāddhāṅgatvena na śakyate vidhātum | daśamādaya eva hi trayo muhūrtāḥ parāśareṇa niyamyeran na tu navamaḥ | evaṃ tasya niyāmakatve muhūrtapañcakaṃ veti trayodaśasya muhūrtasya sāyāhnāntaḥ pātino 'ṅgatvavidhir anupapannaḥ | asya ca caturthapraharāntaḥpātāc chrāddhāṅgatvaṃ pratiṣidhyate | tathā ca vāyupurāṇam |

	caturthe prahare prāpte yaḥ śrāddhaṃ kurute naraḥ |

	āsuraṃ tad bhavec chrāddhaṃ dātā ca narakaṃ vrajet ||

ata eva vihitapratiṣiddhatvān muhūrtapañcakaṃ veti vikalpa uktaḥ | vyavasthitaś cāyam | yadā prāk caturthāt praharād amāvasyādiśrāddhāṅgatithiḥ samagraśrāddhaprayogasaṃpādanasamarthā bhavati cet pratiṣedhaḥ | no ced vidhiḥ | parāśaravālkyasyāniyamatvam eva sphuṭī karoti vyāghrapāt |

	vidhijñaḥ śraddhayopetaḥ samyak pātraprayojakaḥ |

	rātrer anyatra kurvāṇaḥ śreyaḥ prāpnoty anuttamam || iti |

yata eva dvitīyam ahno 'rdham aparāhṇo 'ta eva bahvṛcabrāhmaṇe śrūyate: "uddhārāhavanīyam ity aparāhṇa āha" iti | ata eva ca āśvalāyanīyasūtram: "utsarge 'parāhṇe gārhapatyaṃ prajvālya" ityādi | sāyaṃkālavihitasyāgnihotrasyāṅgam uddharaṇaṃ sāyam eva kāryam "tatkālaś caiva tadguṇaḥ" iti vacanāt | tena sāyāhna evāyam aparāhṇaśabdaḥ | tasmāt siddhaṃ dvedhā vibhaktasyāhno dvitīyo bhāgo 'parāhṇa iti | tatrāmāvasyāyā anyatra śrāddhakaraṇe prathama evāparāhṇabhāg etat kāryam, vilambe hetvabhāvāt | amāvāsyāyāṃ tu piṇḍānvāhāryakapitṛyajñānurodhena yatrāparāhṇabhāge 'māvāsyāyukte saṃpadyate tatra kāryam | sāṃvatsarādikaṃ tu śrāddhatithiyukte 'parāhṇabhāge yatra kutracit karyam | sā cet sāyāhnamātravyāpinī syāt tadā sāyāhna eva vyāghrapādvacanabalena śrāddhaṃ kāryaṃ na punar udayavyāpinyām aparāhṇaparyantāyām | tathā ca smṛtyantaram |

**[468]**	darśaṃ ca paurṇamāsaṃ ca pituḥ sāṃvatsaraṃ dinam |

	pūrvaviddham akurvāṇo narakaṃ pratipadyate || iti |

śrāddhādāvastagāminīti ca pitur iti ca pradarśanārtham | yat tu grāhyā kutapakālikīti vacanam, tad anagner amāvāsyāśrāddhaṃ prati kālaviśeṣavidhāyakaṃ na punaḥ śrāddhāntaraṃ pratīti mantavyam | śrāddhaviśeṣe 'parāhṇāt kālāntaram āha śātātapaḥ |

	āmaśrāddhaṃ tu pūrvāhṇa ekoddiṣṭaṃ tu madhyataḥ |

	pārvaṇaṃ cāparāhṇe tu prātar vṛddhinimittakam || iti |

atra dvijānām āmaśrāddhaṃ pākāsāmarthye nimitte vidhīyamānatvād anityam | śūdrasya nimittānapekṣaṃ tad bhavatīti nityam | tatra nobhayavidhe tasmin pūrvāhṇavidhir ayaṃ nityānityasaṃyogavirodhāt | tatra dvijānām āmaśrāddhavidhaya udāhriyante | tatra saṃvartaḥ |

	pākābhāve 'dhikāraḥ syād dvijātīnām udāhṛtaḥ |

	apatnīnāṃ mahābāho videśagamanādibhiḥ ||

	sadā caiva tu śūdrāṇām āmaśrāddhaṃ vidur budhāḥ ||

uśanā |

	ātmano deśakālānāṃ viplave samupasthite |

	āmaśrāddhaṃ dvijaiḥ kāryaṃ śūdreṇa tu sadaiva hi ||

pracetāḥ |

	āpady anagnau tīrthe ca candrasūryagrahe tathā |

	āmaśrāddhaṃ dvijaiḥ kāryaṃ śūdraiḥ kāryaṃ sadaiva hi ||

tīrthe pākāsāmarthye sati | candrasūryagrahe bhoktur abhāve |

	strī śūdraḥ svapacaś caiva jātakarmaṇi vāpy atha |

	āmaśrāddhaṃ tadā kuryād vidhinā pārvaṇena tu ||

svpacaḥ svayaṃpacaḥ | jamadagniḥ |

	yāvat syān nāgnisaṃyukta utsannāgir athāpi vā |

	āmaśrāddhaṃ sadā kuryād dhaste 'gnaukaraṇaṃ bhavet ||

hārītaḥ |

	śrāddhavighne dvijātīnām āmaśrāddhaṃ prakīrtitam |

	amāvāsyādi niyataṃ māsasaṃvatsarād ṛte || iti |

māsikaṃ sāṃvatsarikaṃ ca śrāddhaṃ varjayitvā sa vidhir ity arthaḥ | ayaṃ māsikasāṃvatsarikāmaśrāddhaniṣedho grahaṇavyatiriktaviṣayaḥ | candrasūryagrahe sati māsikasāṃvatsarikaśrāddham āmānnenaiva kāryam iti bhāvaḥ | evamādibhir vacanaiḥ **[469]** pākāsāmarthyanimitte 'dhikārabhaṅge saty āmena dravyeṇa śrāddhasya prayogaviśeṣo 'dhikārojjīvanāya vidhīyamāno naimittiko bhavati | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">nanu</span> "śūdraḥ kuryāt sadaiva hi" iti vacanāc chūdratvena nimittena pūrvavad eva prayogaviśeṣo naimittikaḥ kasmān na vidhīyate | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">ucyate</span> — prāptaṃ khalu śūdraṃ satyām aśrāddham iti vidheyam | kiṃ tv anuvādyam | tathā hi pratiṣiddhaṃ brāhmaṇabhojanaṃ śūdrasya | yad āha sumantuḥ |

	na pakvaḥ bhojayed viprān sacchūdro 'pi kadācana |

	bhojayan pratyavāyī syān na ca tasya phalaṃ bhavet ||

	bhojanena hi viprasya yat pāpaṃ syād durātmanaḥ |

	tato 'sau lipyate mūḍho yaḥ śūdro bhojayed dvijān || iti |

na cātra saṃprītyādiprayojanam eva brāhmaṇabhojanaṃ niṣidhyate na tu vaidham iti vācyam | yataḥ "na cāpnoti phalaṃ tasya" it vākyaśeṣo vaidhaviprabhojana eva yujyate | naivāyaṃ niṣedhaḥ śrāddhopādhibhūtaviprabhojanaviṣayo na bhavatīti śakyate vaktuṃ kāraṇābhāvāt | brāhmaṇabhojanapratiṣedhe ca śrāddhādhikāra eva śakyate | tathā hi śrāddhakalpe brāhmaṇanimantraṇādividhidarśanāt | tathā haviḥ pacet, śrāddhadeśaṃ pratyāharet, pariveṣayet, viprān bhojayed ityādividhidarśanāc chrāddhayajñasya brāhmaṇabhojanarūpopādhiparyantatāvasīyate | na copādhisaṃpādanasāmarthyapratibandha upahite bhaveti sāmarthyāpratibandhaḥ | yat tv abhyudite 'ṣṭāv upāṃśuyājasya devatoddeśarahitasyāpi prayojyatvaṃ nyāyavidbhir ucyate, tad yuktam eva | na khalv abhyuditeṣṭer adhikārabuddhir anuṣṭhāpikā | kiṃ tv adhikārabhramaḥ | vihitakālabhrāntyā hi tatra kālāntaraviṣayādhikārabhramo janyate | ata upādhibhūtadevatoddeśasāmarthyavirahe 'py upāṃśuyājānuṣṭhānaṃ nāyuktam | tatra hy adhikārabhrāntipravartitaḥ prayoga eva tasya vikṛtasya samāptinimittam | tena naimittikanimittaprakrāntasyopāṃśuyājaprayogasya devatoddeśarahitasyāpi samāptir vacanasāmarthyāt tatra yujyate | śrāddhe tu nādhikārabhramo 'nuṣṭhānahetuḥ kiṃ tu tadbhaṅgaḥ | ato viprabhojanopahitasya śrāddhātmakapradhānasyānuṣṭhānasāmarthyapratibandhe bhavati śūdrasyādhikārabhaṅgaḥ | na ca vācyam, anadhikṛta eva śrāddhe śūdra iti | yato, 

	bhāryāratiḥ śucir bhṛtyabhartā śrāddhakriyāparaḥ | **[470]**

ityādivacanaiḥ śṛṅgagrāhitayā śūdraṃ prati śrāddhaṃ vihitam | tataś ca śūdrasya sakalopādhisahitaṃ śrāddham astīti tatsaṃnihitam eva vidhiḥ śrāddhaṃ praty api pravartamānaḥ prayuṅkte | tatra brāhmaṇabhojananiṣedhānugrahārthaṃ dvijātikartṛkaśrāddhaḥ (?) śrāddha iti sākṣād brāhmaṇabhojanaṃ na prayuṅkte praṇāḍyā tu rayuṅkta eva | na khalv aparathā śūdraṃ prati pravartamānayor viprabhojanaviṣayor vidhiniṣedhayor avirodhaḥ śakyaḥ saṃpādayitum | śakyate ca pitṝn uddiśya parityaktam āmam annaṃ śūdreṇāpi viprān praty etat tyaktvā yuṣmābhir bhojyam iti prārthanā viprabhojanaṃ praṇāḍyā kartum | evaṃ ca sati śūdrasya nimittānapekṣayā prāptam āmaśrāddhaṃ "śūdraḥ kuryāt sadaiva hi" ityādibhir anūdyate | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">nanu</span> ca dvijānām api haviṣpākabrāhmaṇabhojanāsāmarthye śūdravad āmena śrāddhaprayogo nimittānapekṣaḥ pākābhāve 'dhikāraḥ syād ityādibhir anūdyate | <span style="text-decoration:underline;">satyam</span> | yadi dvijātīnāṃ yathāśrutapākādyaṅgānuṣṭhāne vidhyaucityaprāptasākṣādbrāhmaṇabhojanaviṣayasāmarthaṃ na syāt | tadasāmarthye ca śrāddhātmani pradhāne 'py asāmarthayam | tac cādhikārasya bhaṅge prāpte tadvaj jīvanāyāmadravyasādhyaḥ śrāddhaprayogaviśeṣo naimittiko vidhīyate | tathā ca sati nityaṃ śūdrakartṛkam āmaśrāddham anityaṃ ca divjakartṛkaṃ prati pūrvāhṇo na śakyo 'bhidhātuṃ nityānityasaṃyogavirodhāt | tatra na tāvan nitye sa śakto vidhātum | aupadeśikenāparāhṇena saha vikalpaprasaṅgāt | dvijakartṛkaṃ tv āmaśrāddhaṃ naimittikatvād vikṛtir iti | tatrāparāhṇa ātideśika aupadeśikaḥ pūrvāhṇaḥ | na caupadeśikātideśikayor vikalpas tasmāt tatraiva pūrvāhṇavidhir na śūdrkartṛke 'py āmaśrāddhe | kiṃ tu tatrāparāhṇavidhir eva | ata eva ca yat śātāpapīyam eva vākyam,

	madhyāhnāt parato yas tu kutapaḥ samudāhṛtaḥ |

	āmamātreṇa tatraiva pitṝṇāṃ dattam akṣayam ||

iti, tac chūdraviṣayam | anuvādakaṃ caitat | sādhāraṇāparāhṇopadeśād evāparāhṇasya śūdrāmaśrāddhe 'pi prāptatvāt | tasmāt siddhaṃ śūdrakartṛkam āmaśrāddham aparāhṇa eva kāryam | 

	prasaṅgād āmaśrāddhavidhayaḥ kecil likhyante | yatra vyāsaḥ |

	āmaṃ dadad dhi kaunteya dadyād annaṃ caturguṇam |

	siddhānnena vidhir yaḥ syād āmaśrāddhe 'py asau vidhiḥ ||

	āvāhanādi sarvaṃ syāt piṇḍadānaṃ ca bhārata |

	dadyād yaś ca dvijātibhyaḥ śṛtaṃ vā yadi vāśṛtam ||

**[471]**	tenāgnaukaraṇaṃ kuryāt piṇḍāṃs tenaiva nirvapet |

atra puruṣāhārāpekṣaṃ cāturguṇyam, siddhānnenetyādir atideśo dvijāmaśrāddhaviṣayaḥ | ṣaṭtriṣanmatāt |

	āmaśrāddhaṃ yadā kuryāt piṇḍadānaṃ kathaṃ bhavet |

	gṛhapākāt samuddhṛtya saktubhiḥ pāyasena vā ||

piṇḍadānaṃ bhaved iti śeṣaḥ | tathā |

	āmaśrāddhaṃ yadā kuryād vidhijñaḥ śrāddhadas tathā |

	haste 'gnaukaraṇaṃ kuryād brāhmaṇasya vidhānataḥ ||

āmaśrāddhe ca bhojanaprayuktānāṃ tṛptipraśnādīnāṃ nivṛttiḥ |

	evaṃ kāryaṃ sadā śrāddhaṃ śūdreṇāpy āmam eva ca |

	mantravarjaṃ tu śūdrasya sarvam etad vidhīyate ||

bhaviṣyatpurāṇam |

	dharmepsavaś ca dharmajñā yadi śūdrāḥ prakurvate |

	agnaukaraṇamantraś ca namaskāro vidhīyate ||

āmaśrāddhāsamarthaṃ prati hemaśrāddham āha vyāsaḥ |

	dravyābhāve dvijābhāve pravāse putrajanmani |

	hemaśrāddhaṃ prakurvīta yasya bhāryā rajasvalā ||

dravyam atra bhojyaṃ vivakṣitaṃ dvijaś ca bhoktā | manuḥ |

	śuciṃ deśaṃ viviktaṃ ca gomayenopalepayet |

	dakṣiṇāpravaṇaṃ caiva prayatnenopapādayet ||

vivikto vijanaḥ | śucer api deśasya gomayopalepanaṃ vacanāt saṃskārātiśayāya kāryam | tathā |

	avakāśeṣu cokṣeṣu jalatīreṣu caiva hi |

	vivikteṣu ca tuṣyanti dattena pitaraḥ sadā ||

cokṣāḥ svabhāvaśucayaḥ | yamaḥ |

	parakīyapradeśeṣu pitṝṇāṃ nirvapet tu yaḥ |

	tadbhūmisvāmipitṛbhiḥ śrāddhakarma vihanyate ||

	aṭavyaḥ parvatāḥ puṇyā nadītīrāṇi yāni ca |

	sarvāṇy asvāmikāny āhur na hi teṣu parigrahaḥ ||

	tasmāc chrāddhāni deyāni puṇyeṣv āyataneṣu ca |

	nadītīreṣu tīrtheṣu savbhūmau ca prayatnataḥ ||

	upahvaranikuñjeṣu tathā parvatasānuṣu | **[472 ]**

upahavraṃ parvatanikaṭaḥ | nikuñjao guhā |

	rūkṣaṃ krimihataṃ klinnaṃ saṃkīrṇāniṣṭagandhikam |

	deśaṃ tva aniṣṭaśabdaṃ ca varjayec chrāddhakarmaṇi ||

rūkṣam asnigdham | klinnaṃ sakardamam | aniṣṭaśabdaṃ duḥkhakaraśabdam | śaṅkhaḥ |

	mlecchadeśe tathā rātrau saṃdhyāyāṃ ca viśeṣataḥ |

	na śrāddham ācaret prājño mlecchadeśaṃ na ca vrajet ||

brahmāṇḍapurāṇam |

	uttareṇa manānadyā dakṣiṇena ca kīkaṭam |

	eṣa traiśaṅkavo nāma varjitaḥ śrāddhakarmaṇi ||

	pāraskarāḥ kaliṅgāś ca sindhor uttaram eva ca |

	pranaṣṭaśrāddhakarmāṇo varjyā deśāḥ prayatnataḥ ||

	gogajāśvādipṛṣṭheṣu kṛtrimāyāṃ tathā bhuvi |

	āpatsv api ca kaṣṭāsu na kuryāt pitṛtarpaṇam ||

athāpāsanīyāni | tatra yamaḥ |

	kukkuṭo viḍvarāhaś ca kākaḥ śvātha biḍālakaḥ |

	vṛṣalīpatiś ca vṛṣalaḥ ṣaṇḍho nārī rajasvalā ||

	ete tu śrāddhakāle vai varjanīyāḥ prayatnataḥ |

manuḥ |

	caṇḍālaś ca varāhaś ca kukkuṭaḥ śvā tathaiva ca |

	rajasvalā ca ṣaṇḍhaś ca nekṣerann aśnato dvijān ||

	home pradāne bhojye ca yad ebhir abhivīkṣitam |

	daive karmaṇi pitrye vā yad ebhir abhivīkṣitam ||

	daive karmaṇi pitrye vā tad gacchaty ayathātatham ||

	ghrāṇena sūkaro hanti pakṣapātena kukkuṭaḥ |

	śvā tu dṛṣṭinipātena sparśenāvaravarṇajaḥ ||

avaravarṇajaḥ śūdraḥ 

	khañjo vā yadi vā kāṇo dātuḥ preṣyo 'pi vā bhavet |

	hīnātiriktagātro vā tam apy apanayet tataḥ ||

khañjaḥ kuṇṭhaḥ | devalaḥ |

	bībhatsam aśuciṃ nagnaṃ mattaṃ dhūrtaṃ rajasvalām |

	nīlakāṣāyavasanaṃ chinnakarṇaṃ ca varjayet ||

	śastraṃ kālāyasaṃ sīsaṃ malināmbaravāsasam |

	annaṃ paryuṣitaṃ cāpi śrāddheṣu parivarjayet ||

**[473]**	daive vā yadi vā pitrye surāpy āyatanaṃ spṛśet |

	rajasvalā puṃścalī vā rakṣaḥ saṃgacchate hi tat ||

vyāsaḥ |

	caṇḍālaśvapacau varjyau nirvāpe samupasthite |

	kāṣāyavāsāḥ kuṣṭhī vā patito bhrūṇahāpi vā ||

	saṃkīrṇayonir vipraś ca saṃbandhī patitasya yaḥ |

	varjanīyā budhair ete nirvāpi samupasthite ||

nirvāpaḥ śrāddham | saṃkīrṇayoniḥ kṣetrajādiḥ | upasthitaśabdād upakramaprabhṛty ete varjanīyāḥ | 

	madyapaḥ svairiṇī yā ca parapūrvāpatis tathā |

	naiva śrāddhe 'bhivīkṣerann āvāpāt prabhṛti kvacit ||

āvāpaḥ śrāddhopakramaḥ | brahmāṇḍapurāṇe |

	nagnādayo na paśyeyuḥ śrāddham etat kadācana |

	gacchanty etais tu dṛṣṭena pitaro 'tha pitāmahāḥ ||

	sarveṣām eva bhūtānāṃ trayī saṃvaraṇaṃ yataḥ |

	ye vai tyajanti tāṃ mūḍhās te vai nagnādayaḥ smṛtāḥ ||

	dasyuḥ caiva nṛśaṃsaṃ ca darśane parivarjayet |

	ye cānye pāpakarmāṇaḥ sarvās tān parivarjayet ||

dasyuś cauraḥ | nṛśaṃso niṣṭhuraḥ | vāyuprāṇe |

	vṛthā jaṭī vṛthā muṇḍī vṛthā nagnaś ca yo naraḥ |

	mahāpātakino ye ca te vai nagnādayo narāḥ ||

	annaṃ paceyur ete tu yadi vai havyakavyayoḥ |

	utsraṣṭavyaṃ pradhānārthaṃ saṃskāro vā yadi smṛtaḥ ||

utsraṣṭavyaṃ tyājyam | āpadi tu śrāddhātmakapradhānārthaṃ saṃskāryam | saṃskāraś ca brahmapuṛāṇa uktaḥ |

	haviṣāṃ saṃskṛtānāṃ tu pūrvam evāpavarjanam |

	mṛtsaṃpṛktābhir adbhiś ca prokṣaṇaṃ tu vidhīyate ||

	siddhārthakaiḥ kṛṣṇatilaiḥ kāryaṃ cāpy avakīraṇam |

	gurusūryāgnivastūnāṃ darśanaṃ ca prayatnataḥ ||

śvādyabhivīkṣitānāṃ pakvānāṃ haviṣām avaparjanaṃ tyāgaḥ | pūrvaḥ prathamaḥ | **[478]** āpadi tu mṛtsaṃpṛktābhir adbhir ityādikaṃ saṃskāraṃ kṛtvā havīṃśy upayojyāni | 

	athopādeyāni | tatra brahmapurāṇam |

	yatis tridaṇḍaḥ karuṇā rājataṃ pātram eva ca |

	dauhitraḥ kutapaḥ kālaś chāgaḥ kṛṣṇājinaṃ tathā ||

dinasyāṣṭamo muhūrtaḥ kutapaḥ kalaḥ |

	gaurāḥ kṛṣṇās tathāraṇyās tathaiva trividhās tilāḥ |

	pitṝṇāṃ tṛptaye sṛṣṭā daśaite brahmaṇā svayam ||

	darbhair mantrais tilair hemnā rājatena vinā jalam |

	dattaṃ hanti rakṣāṃsi tasmād dadyān na kevalam ||

darbhādibhir jalena ca vinā yad dattaṃ tad rakṣāṃsi harantīty arthaḥ | darbhamantrādirahitam udakam eva vā dattaṃ harantīry arthaḥ | manuḥ |

	aparāhṇas tathā darbhā vāstusaṃpādanaṃ tilāḥ |

	sṛṣṭir mṛṣṭir dvijāś cāgryāḥ śrāddhakarmasu saṃpadaḥ ||

sṛṣṭiḥ prabhūtatā | mṛṣṭiḥ svādutā |

	trīṇi śrāddhe pavitrāṇi dauhitraḥ kutapas tilāḥ |

	trīṇi cātra praśaṃsanti śaucam akrodham atvarām ||

devalaḥ |

	darbhās tilā gajacchāyā dauhitraṃ madhusarpiṣī |

	kutapo nīlamaṇḍaś ca pavitrāṇīha paitṛke ||

nīlamaṇḍo nīlavṛṣaḥ | smṛtyantaram |

	apatyaṃ duhituś caiva khaḍagapātraṃ tathaiva ca |

	ghṛtaṃ ca kapilāyā gaur dauhitram iti kīrtitam ||

[duhitṛputraḥ śrāddhe dakṣiṇādāv eva pūjyo na tu śrāddhakartṛtāyām | atra nirṇayo manusmṛtau grāhyaḥ | ] vṛddhaśātātapaḥ |

	dauhitraṃ khaḍgaśṛṅgaṃ tu lalāṭaṃ yat tad ucyate |

	tasya śṛṅgasya yat pātraṃ dauhitram iti kīrtitam ||

smṛtyantaam |

	brāhmaṇaḥ kambalo gāvaḥ sūryo 'gnis tithir eva ca |

	tilā darbhāś ca kālaś ca navaite kutapāḥ smṛtāḥ || **[475]**

mātsyāc ca |

	prācīnāvītam udakaṃ tilāḥ savyāṅgam eva ca |

	yavanīvāramudgāś ca śuklapuṣpaghṛtāni ca ||

	vallabhāni praśastān pitṝṇām iha sarvadā ||

āpastambaḥ |

	aṭavyāṃ ye samutpannā akṛṣṭāḥ phalitās tathā |

	te vai śrāddhe pavitrās tu tilās te na tilās tilāḥ ||

grāmyāś tilā na tilakāryakarā bhavantīty arthaḥ | purāṇāt |

	sthūlodumbaravastrāṇi rajataṃ khaḍgam eva ca |

	śrāddhe mahāpavitrāṇi phalāni samidhas tathā ||

vāyupurāṇe |

	kṛṣṇājinasya saṃnidhyaṃ darśanaṃ dānam eva ca |

	rakṣoghnaṃ brahmavarcasyaṃ paśūn putrāṃś ca dāpayet ||

manuḥ |

	vratastham api dauhitraṃ śrāddhe yatnena bhojayet |

	kutapaṃ cāsanaṃ dadyāt tilaiś cāvakiren mahīm ||

kutapo 'tra kambalaḥ | matsyapurāṇam |

	udapātraṃ ca kāṃsyaṃ ca mekṣaṇaṃ ca samit kuśān |

	āhared apasavyena sarvaṃ dakṣiṇataḥ śanaiḥ ||

	evam āsādya tat sarvaṃ bhavanasyāgrato bhuvi |

	gomayenopaliptāyāṃ gomūtreṇa tu maṇḍalam ||

	akṣatābhiḥ sapuṣpābhis tad abhyarcyāpasvyavat |

	viprāṇāṃ kṣālayet pādān abhinandya punaḥ punaḥ ||

smṛtyantaram |

	dakṣiṇāpravaṇaṃ kāryaṃ maṇdaladvayam eva ca |

	uttare 'kṣatasaṃyuktān pūrvāgrān vinyaset kuśān ||

	dakṣiṇe dakṣiṇāgrāṃś ca satilān vinyased dvijaḥ ||

śaṃbhuḥ |

	saṃmārjitopalipte tu dvāri kurvīta maṇḍale |

	udakplavam udīcyaṃ syād dakṣiṇaṃ dakṣināplavam ||

brahmanirukte |

	pādyaṃ caiva tathaivārghyaṃ daivaṃ ādau pradāpayet |

	śaṃ no dvīti mantreṇa pādyaṃ caiva pradāpayet ||

āmbarīṣaḥ sindhudvipa ṛṣiḥ | āpo devatā | gāyatrī chandaḥ | **[476]** yamaḥ |

	pādaprakṣālaṇam kuryāt svayam eva vinītavat |

	tataḥ siddhim iti procya kalpiteṣv āsaneṣu ca ||

	samādhvam iti tān brūyād āsanaṃ saṃspṛśann api |

	brahmodyāś ca kathāḥ kurvan pitṝṇām etad īpsitam ||

pādaprakṣālanānantaraṃ śrāddhasy karmaṇaḥ siddhiṃ bhavanto bruvantv iti brāhmaṇān prati procya samādhvam ity anenāsanaṃ spṛśann upaveśeyed ity arthaḥ | dharmaḥ |

	anvārabhya tato devān upaveśya tataḥ pitṝn |

	samastābhir vyāhṛtibhir āsaneṣūpaveśayet ||

pitṛbrāhmaṇopaveśana eva vyāhṛtayaḥ | manuḥ |

	teṣām ārakṣabhūtaṃ tu pūrvaṃ daivaṃ nivedayet |

	rakṣāṃsi vipralumpanti śrāddham ārakṣavarjitam ||

ārakṣaṇam ārakṣā(kṣāḥ) | smṛtyantaram |

	āsyatām iti tān brūyād āsanaṃ saṃspṛśann api |

	upastīrṇeṣu cāsīran na spṛśeyuḥ parasparam ||

āsyatām ity anena svadhvam ity asya vikalpaḥ | viṣṇuḥ |

	yathābhūyovayaḥkrameṇa kuśottareṣv āsaneṣūpaveśayet |

	vidyātapo'dhikānāṃ vai prathamāsanam iṣyate ||

	prāṅktyānāṃ tu viśiṣṭānāṃ samaṃ gandhādibhojanam ||

hārītaḥ |

	saṃtiṣṭhamāneṣv arhatsu yo 'narho 'grāsanaṃ śrayet |

	gṛhṇāti sa malaṃ paṅkter āyuṣā ca viyujyate ||

	caturṇāṃ duṣkṛtaṃ hanti brāhmaṇo vighnakārakaḥ |

	annasyānnapateḥ paṅktes tathā bhojanakāṅkṣiṇaḥ ||

hantir atra gatyarthaḥ | teṣāṃ nivāryātmanaḥ svīkuruta iti yāvat | gārgyaḥ |

	sparśe sparśe bhavet pāpam ekapaṅktiniyojane |

	hīnavṛttādipaṅktau tu tasmād yuktaṃ vivecanam ||

bṛhaspatiḥ |

	ekapaṅktyupaviṣṭā ye na spṛśanti parasparam |

	bhasmanā kṛtamaryādā na teṣāṃ saṃkaro bhavet ||

	agninā bhasmanā vāpi stambhenāpy udakena vā |

	dvārasaṃkramaṇenāpi paṅktibhedaḥ prakīrtitaḥ || **[477]**

pracetāḥ |

	upamūlaṃ sakṛllūnān kuśāṃs tatropasādayet |

	yavāṃs tilān bṛsīṃ kāṃsyam apaś ca svayam āhṛtāḥ ||

	pārṇarājatatāmrāṇi pātrāṇi syuḥ samin madhu |

	puṣpadhūpasugandhāś ca kṣaumasūtraṃ ca bhekṣaṇam ||

viṣṇuḥ: "kutapaḥ kṛṣṇājinaṃ tilāḥ siddhārthakā akṣatāni ca pavitrāṇi rakṣoghnāni ca" | ata etāny āsecayed ity arthaḥ || 1.226, 227 ||

_mātāmahaśrāddhaṃ praty atideśaṃ vaiśvadevatatravikalpaṃ cāha_ |

	**mātāmahānām apy evaṃ tantraṃ vā vaiśvadevikam || 1.228 ||**

mātāmahānām api śrāddham evaṃ pitṛśrāddhavat kāryam | tatra vaiśvadevikabrāhmaṇabojane pratiśrāddhaṃ bhedena nyāyataḥ prāptau vikalpārtham idaṃ vacanaṃ "tantraṃ vā vaiśvadevikam" iti | sāmarthyādhīnā cātra vyavasthā | ata eva vṛddhavasiṣṭhaḥ |

	śrāddhadvayaṃ kariṣyaṃs tu daśaiva caturo 'pi vā |

	trīn vā nimantrayed viprān ekaṃ vā brahmavādinam ||

tatra, "dvau daive pitṛkṛtye trīn" iti pakṣaṃ vaiśvadevikabhedapakṣaṃ cāśritya daśety uktam | ekaikam eva ceti pakṣe catura iti | atraiva vaiśvadevatantre trīn iti | atyantāpadi tv ekam ity uktam | precetāḥ |

	apasavyaṃ tataḥ kṛtvā japtvā mantraṃtu vaiṣṇavam |

	gāyatrīṃ praṇavaṃ cāpi tataḥ śrāddham upakramet ||

	śrāddhaṃ kariṣya ity evaṃ pṛcched viprān samāhitaḥ |

	kuruṣveti sa tair ukto dadyād darbhāsanāny atha ||

kātyāyanaḥ |

	sarvatra praśneṣu paṅktimūrdhanyaṃ pṛcchati sarvān vā |

brahmapurāṇam |

	upaviśya japed dhīmān gāyatrīṃ tadanujñayā |

	pāpāpahaṃ pāvanīyam aśvamedhaphalaṃ tathā ||

	mantraṃ pakṣyāmy ahaṃ tasmād amṛtaṃ brahmanirmitam |

	devatābhyaḥ pitṛbhyaś ca mahāyogibhya eva ca ||

	namaḥ svadhāyai svāhāyai nityam eva bhavatv iha |

	ādyāvasāne śrāddhasya trirāvartaṃ japet sadā ||

**[478]**	piṇḍanirvapaṇe cāpi japed etat samāhitaḥ |

	paṭhyamānam idaṃ śrutvā śrāddhakāla upasthite ||

	pitaraḥ kṣipram āyānti rākṣasāḥ pradravanti ca ||

brahmāṇḍapurāṇe |

	tatra siddhārthakān bhūmau kṣiped rakṣopanuttaye |

	dikṣu sarvāsu ca tilān mantreṇānena dharmavit ||

	oṃ nihanmi sarvaṃ yad amedhyavad bhaved dhātāś ca sarva 'suradānavā mayā |

	rakṣāṃsi yakṣāḥ sapiśācaguhyakā hatā mayā yātudhānāś ca sarve ||

	etena mantreṇa susaṃyatātmā tilān kṣiped dikṣu yatha vidikṣu ||

nigamaḥ: "apahatā asurā rakṣāṃsīti tilān vikiret" | āsuraṃ yajñaḥ (juḥ) parameṣṭhiprajāpatidṛṣṭam || 1.228 ||

	**pāṇiprakṣālanaṃ datvā viṣṭarārthān kuśān api |**

**	āvāhayed anujñāto viśve devāsa ity ṛcā || 1.229 ||**

pāṇiprakṣālanasādhanaṃ haste jalaṃ datvā haste viṣṭarārthāṃś ca kuśān datvā vaiśvadevikabrāhmaṇair anujñāto "viśve devāsa āgata" ity gāyatryā vaiśvadevyā prajāpatidṛṣṭayā viśvān devān āvāhayet | anujñāta ity vacanād viśvān devān āvāhayiṣya ity anujñāpanam āvāhayeti cānujñānam arthasiddham | atra ca mantrānte purūravārdravanāmāno devā āgaccheti pāraṇe vācyam | śrāddhāntare tu nāmāntarāṇi | yathāha bṛhaspatiḥ |

	iṣṭiśrāddhe kratur dakṣaḥ satyo nāndīmukhe vasuḥ |

	naimittike kālakāmau kāmye ca dhuniro(rilo)canau ||

	purūravārdavaś caiva pāvaṇe samudāhṛtau |

	utpattiṃ nāma caiteṣāṃ na vidur ye dvijātayaḥ ||

	ayam uccāraṇīyas tu ślokaḥ śraddhāsamanvitaiḥ |

	āgacchantu mahābhāgā viśve devā mahābalāḥ ||

	ye yatra vihitāḥ śrāddhe sāvadhānā bhavantu te ||

precetāḥ |

	darbhāś caivāsane dadyān na tu pāṇau kadācana |

	pitṛdevamanuṣyāṇāṃ syāt tuṣṭiḥ śāśvatī tathā ||

**[479]**	daive tu ṛjavo darbhāḥ pradātavyāḥ pṛthak pṛthak |

	dharmo 'sīty atha mantreṇa gṛhṇīyus te ca tān kuśān ||

bṛhaspatiḥ |

	ṛjūn savyena kṛtvā vai daive darbhān pradakṣiṇān |

	dviguṇān apasavyena dadyāt pitrye 'pasavyavat ||

tataś ca daivāsaneṣu yajñopavīty āsanasya dakṣiṇato darbhān dadāti | itaratra tu prācīnāvītī paścimata iti siddham | baudhāyanaḥ |

	pradakṣiṇaṃ tu devānāṃ pitṝṇām apradakṣiṇam |

	devānāṃ sayavā darbhāḥ pitṝṇāṃ dviguṇās tilaiḥ ||

pradakṣiṇam udaksaṃstham apradakṣiṇaṃ prāksaṃstham | dvaiguṇyaṃ darbhāṇāṃ bhaṅgaparyantaṃ kāryam | yad āha śaunakaḥ: "apaḥ pradāya darbhāṃś ca dviguṇān bhugnān āsane pradāya" | śātātapaḥ |

	udaṅmukhas tu devānāṃ pitṝṇāṃ dakṣiṇāmukhaḥ |

	pradadyāt pārvaṇe śrāddhe daivapūrvaṃ vidhānataḥ ||

bṛhaspatiḥ |

	āsane cārghyadāne ca piṇḍadāne 'vanejane |

	saṃbandhagotranāmāni yathārham anukīrtayet ||

katyāyanaḥ |

	dakṣiṇaṃ pātayej jānuṃ devān paricaran sadā |

	pātayed itaraṃ jānuṃ pitṝn paricaran sadā ||

tathāsaneṣu darbhān āstīrya viśvān devān āvāhayiṣya iti pṛcchati | āvāhayety anujñāto viśve devāsa āgatety āvāhya viśve devāḥ śṛṇutemam iti japtvau(pitvau)ṣadhaya ity akṣatāvāpanam || 1.229 ||

	**yavair anvavakīryātha bhājane sapavitrake |**

**	śaṃ no devyā payaḥ kṣiptvā yavo 'sīti yavāṃs tathā || 1.230 ||**

**	yā divyā iti mantreṇa hasteṣv arghyaṃ vinikṣipet |**

āvāhanaṃ kṛtvā dve pavitravatī pātre yavair anvavakīrya pātrayor yavān prakṣipya śaṃ no devīty ṛcā pātradvaye 'paḥ kṣiptvāpsu ca yavo 'sīti yajuṣā yavān prakṣipya "yā divyāḥ" iti mantreṇa vaiśvadevikabrāhmaṇahasteṣv ekapātrastham arghyam ekasya brāhmaṇasya hastayoḥ pātrāntarastham aparasya nikṣipet | pratyarghyadānaṃ mantrāvṛttiḥ | evam apāṃ ca prakṣepe yavānāṃ ca prakṣepe mantrāvṛttiḥ | **[480]** parajāpatiḥ |

	sauvarṇaṃ rājataṃ tāmraṃ khaḍgaṃ maṇimayaṃ tathā |

	yajñiyaṃ camasaṃ vāpi tv arghyārthaṃ pūrayed budhaḥ ||

kātyāyanaḥ |

	anantargarbhiṇaṃ sāgraṃ kauśaṃ dvidalam eva ca |

	prādeśamātraṃ vijñeyaṃ pavitraṃ yatra kutracit ||

yogayājñavalkyaḥ |

	pavitre stha iti mantreṇa dve pavitre ca kārayet |

	antargarbhe kuśacchanne kauśe prādeśasaṃmite ||

yajñapārśvaḥ |

	oṣadhīr antaraṃ kṛtvā aṅguṣṭhāṅguliparvaṇoḥ |

	chindyāt prādeśamātraṃ tu pavitraṃ viṣṇudaivatam ||

	na nakhena na kāṣṭhena na lohena na mṛnmayāt ||

caturviṃśatimatāt |

	dve dve śalāke devānāṃ pātre kṛtvā tv apaḥ kṣipet |

	śaṃ no devyā yavo 'sīti yavān api tataḥ kṣipet ||

	puṣpadhūpādibhiḥ kṛtvā pūjāṃ patreṣu mānavaḥ |

	pitṛpātre viśeṣo 'yaṃ tilo 'sīti tilān kṣipet |

	tisras tisraḥ śalākās tu pitṛpātreṣu pārvaṇe ||

	ekoddiṣṭe śalākaikā nidhāyodakam āharet ||

śalākā darbhāgram | precetāḥ |

	pavitra iti mantreṇa pavitre kārayed budhaḥ |

	te nidhāyārhyapātreṣu śaṃ no devīty apaḥ kṣipet ||

tisṛṣv api śalākāsu pavitre stha iti dvivacanānta eva mantraḥ prayoktavyaḥ | ekasminn api pātre vikalpyamānasuvarṇādidrvayabahutvāt pātreṣv iti bahuvacanam | matsyapurāṇe |

	viśvān devān yavaiḥ puṣpair abhyarcyāsanapūrvakam |

	pūrayet pātrayugmāṃs tu sthāpya darbhapavitrake ||

pracetāḥ |

	ekaikasya tu viprasya arghyaṃ pātre vinikṣipet |

	yavo 'sīti yavān kṣiptvā gandhapuṣpaiḥ supūjitam ||

gārgyaḥ |

	datvā haste pavitraṃ tu kṛtvā pūjāṃ vidhānataḥ |

	yā divyā iti mantreṇa hasteṣv arghyaṃ vinikṣipet ||

precetāḥ |

	pādaprabhṛti mūrdhāntaṃ devānāṃ puṣpapūjanam |

	śiraḥprabhṛti pādāntaṃ namo va iti paitṛke || **[481]**

gārgyaḥ |

	svadheti caiva mantrānte pitṝṇāṃ vacanaṃ yathā |

	svāheti caiva devānāṃ homakarmaṇy udāharet ||

arghyādipradānāni cātra homaśabdenocyante ||

	**datvodakaṃ gandhamālyaṃ dhūpadānaṃ sadīpakam || 1.231 ||**

gandhamālyādidānāni pratyekam udakaṃ datvā kāryāṇi | tathā ca gautamaḥ: "bhikṣādānam appūrvaṃ dadāti caivaṃ dharmyeṣu" iti | āpaḥ pūrvaṃ yasmāt ata appūrvam | atra manuḥ |

	gandhamālyaiḥ surabhibhir arcayed daivapūrvakam |

śaunakaḥ punar ācchādanadānam apy āha: "etasmin kāle gandhamālyadhūpadīpācchādanānāṃ pradānam" | etasmin kāle 'rghyadānād ūrdhvam ity arthaḥ | gandhādimantrāḥ pitṛpūjāyāṃ vakṣyante te 'trāpy avirodhād grāhyāḥ | brahmapurāṇe |

	devān āvāhayiṣye te prāhur āvāhayasva ca |

	viprāṅguṣṭhaṃ gṛhītvā tu viśvān devān samāhvayet ||

	tato mantraṃ japen maunī viśve devāsa āgata |

	dvitīyaṃ ca japen mantraṃ viśve devāḥ śṛṇo(ṇu)ta ca ||

	japet tṛtīyaṃ mantraṃ tu paurāṇaṃ puṇyavardhanam |

	āgacchantu mahābhāgā viśve devā mahābalāḥ ||

	ye yatra vihitāḥ śrāddhe sāvadhānā bhavantu te |

	idaṃ ca vaḥ pādyam arghyaṃ puṣpadhūpavilepanam ||

	ayaṃ dīpaprakāśaś ca viśve devāḥ samarpyate ||

anena ca pādyādidāneṣu mantravidhiḥ kriyate | tataś ca — idaṃ vo viśve devāḥ pādyam idaṃ vo viśve devā arghyam ity evaṃ sarvatra prayojyam | dhūpadīpaprakāśayor ayaṃ va ity mantrādiḥ | evaṃ caiṣāṃ mantrāntarair vikalpaḥ || 1.231 ||

	**apasavyaṃ tataḥ kṛtvā pitṝṇām apradakṣiṇam |**

**	dviguṇāṃs tu kuśān datvā uśantas tv ity ṛcā pitṝn || 1.232 ||**

**	āvāhya tadanujñāto japed āyantu nas tataḥ |**

**	yavārthas tu tilaiḥ kāryaḥ kuryād arghādi pūrvavat || 1.233 ||**

**[482]**

tato vaiśvadevikamā(kā)vāhanādidīpapradānāntapadārthe(rtha) kāṇḍād ūrdhvam apasavyaṃ prācīnāvītaṃ kṛtvāpradakṣiṇaṃ prāksaṃsthaṃ dviguṇān kuśān viṣṭarārthān datvā pitṝn pitāmahān prapitāmahān ity evamādīn uddeśyān pitṝn āvāhayiṣya iti viprān ananujñāpyāvāhayati etair anujñāt uśantas tvety anuṣṭubhā damanadṛṣṭayā pitṛdai(de)vatyayā pitrādīn āvāhyāyantu na iti triṣṭubhaṃ śaṅkhadṛṣṭāṃ pitṛdai(de)vatyām japet | yavakāryaṃ cātra tilaiḥ kartavyam | arghyādi vaiśvadevikavat kuryāt | purāṇāt |

	apasavyaṃ tataḥ kṛtvā tilān ādāya saṃyataḥ |

	pitṝn āvāhayāmīti pṛcched viprān udaṅmukhān ||

	āvāhayed anujñāta uśantas tvety ṛcā pitṝn |

	kṣiptvāpasavyaṃ ca tilān pitṝn dhyāyan samāhitaḥ ||

	japed āyantu na iti mantraṃ samyag aśeṣataḥ |

	rakṣārthaṃ pitṛsatrasya triḥ kṛtvā sarvatodiśam ||

	tilāṃs tu prakṣipen mantraṃ tuccāryāpahatā iti |

	sauvarṇarājatāmbhojamaṇipātrāṇy athāpi vā ||

	arghyārthaṃ saṃskaroty eva śubhapatrapuṭādinā ||

brahmapurāṇe |

	pitṝn āvāhayiṣye 'haṃ śeṣān viprān vadet tataḥ |

	āvāhayasvety uktas taiḥ sāvadhānā bhavantv iti ||

sāvadhānā bhavtv iti kartā brūyāt |

	idaṃ vaḥ pādyam arghyaṃ ca caturthyantaṃ nivedayet |

	pitṝn pitāmahān yakṣye bhojanena yathākramam ||

	prapitāmahāṃś ca sarvāṃś ca tat pitṝṃś cānupūrvaśaḥ |

	uśantas tv eti ca japet pitṝn āvāhayet tataḥ ||

	somadattā barhiṣad astv agniṣvāttāś ca ye pare |

	pitaraḥ puṇyayaśasaḥ sarve 'py āyantu nas tv iti ||

	tatas tilān gṛhe tasmin vikirec cāpradakṣiṇam |

	śraddhayā parayā yukto japed apahatās tv iti ||

	tato yajñiyavṛkṣotthapātreṣu sakuśeṣu ca |

	gṛhītvāpaḥ pavitrāś ca śaṃ no devīṃ japan kṣipet ||

	vikiret teṣu ca tilāṃs tilo 'sīti japan kramāt |

	arghyaiḥ puṣpaiś ca gandhaiś ca tāḥ prapūjyāś ca śāstravat ||

**[483]**	tato vāmena hastena gṛhītvā camasān kramāt |

	pitṛtīrthena tat toyaṃ dakṣiṇena ca pāṇinā ||

	dattadarbhodake haste viprebhyaś ca pṛthak pṛthak |

	dadyān mantraṃ japaṃś cātha yā divyā āpa ity api ||

	amukāmukagotraitat tubhyam astu tilodakam |

	eṣa te 'rgha iti procya tebhyo dadyād yathā svadhā ||

	jalaṃ kṣīraṃ dadhi ghṛtaṃ tilataṇḍulasarṣapān |

	kusāgrāṇi ca puṇyāni datvācāmet tataḥ svayam ||

	idaṃ vaḥ puṣpam ity uktvā puṣpāṇi ca nivedayet |

	ayaṃ vo dhūpa ity uktvā tad agre tu dahet tataḥ ||

	ayaṃ vo dīpa ity uktvā dīpaṃ gṛhyaṃ nivedayet |

	anaṅgalagnaṃ yad vastraṃ vibhave tad yugaṃ śubham ||

	śvetacandanakarpūrakuṅkumāni śubhāni ca |

	vilepanārthaṃ dadyāt tu yad vānyat pitṛvallabham ||

kātyāyanaḥ |

	apasavyavad āsiñcet pitṛpātreṣu pūrvavat |

	tatas tilāṃs tilo 'sīti gandhapuṣpāṇi caiva hi ||

pūrvavac chaṃ no devīr ity anayety arthaḥ | dakṣaḥ |

	datvā haste pavitraṃ tu kṛtvā pūjāṃ ca pādataḥ |

	yā divyā iti mantreṇa hasteṣv arghyaṃ vinikṣipet ||

	haste prādeśamātraṃ tu trivṛd datvā pavitrakam |

	abhyarcya pūrvato 'rghyaṃ vai dadyāt tu pitṛdiṅmukhaḥ ||

ślokagautamaḥ |

	śrasaḥ pādato vāpi samyag abhyarcya saṃyataḥ |

	pūrvavat pṛthag ekaikam ekaikenārghayet kramāt ||

	ekaikaṃ brāhmaṇam ekaikenārghyeṇa pratipūjayet ||

pracetāḥ |

	apradakṣiṇam eteṣām ekaikaṃtu pitṛkramāt |

	saṃbodhya gotranāmabhyām eṣa te 'rgha itīrayet ||

tataś ca yady ekaikasya dvau dvau trīṃs trīn vā viprān upaveśayet tathāpy ekaika eva brāhmaṇo 'rghyo na sarve | ata eva śaunakas trīṇy evārghapātrāṇy āha: "triṣu pātreṣv evaikadravyeṣv anekadravyeṣu vā" iti | **[484]** smṛtyantaram |

	vibhaktibhis tu saṃyuktaṃ dīyate pitṛdaivatam |

	dattam akṣayatāṃ yāti viparītaṃ nirarthakam ||

bahvṛcagṛhyapariśiṣṭe |

	gotraṃ svarāntaṃ sarvatra gotrasyākṣayyakarmaṇi |

	gotras tu tarpaṇe kuryād evaṃ dātā na muhyati ||

	sarvatraiva pitaḥ proktaḥ pitā tarpaṇakarmaṇi |

	akṣayye tu pituḥ kāryaṃ tarpaṇaṃ tṛptim icchatā ||

	śarmann arghyādike kāryaṃ śarmaṇo 'kṣayyakarmaṇi |

	śarmā tu tarpaṇe kuryād evaṃ kurvan na muhyati ||

tataś cāmukagotra pitaramukaśramann etat te 'rghyam iti prayoktavyam | evaṃ pitāmahādiṣv api | tarpaṇe tv amukagotraḥ pitāmukaśarmā tṛpyatv iti prayogaḥ | evaṃ pitāmahādiṣv api | akṣayyodake tv amukagotrasya pitur amukaśarmaṇo 'kṣayyam astv iti prayogaḥ | evaṃ pitāmahādiṣv api || 1.232, 233 ||

	**datvārghyaṃ saṃsravāṃs teṣāṃ pātre kṛtvā vidhānataḥ |**

**	pitṛbhyaḥ sthānam asīti nyubjaṃ pātraṃ karoty adhaḥ || 1.234 ||**

arghyaṃ datvāvaśiṣṭān saṃsravān saṃsrāvapātrasthāñ jalaśeṣān ekasmin pātre kṛtvā yathāvidhi pitṛbhyaḥ sthānam asīti mantreṇa tat pātram adhomukhaṃ karoti | adho bhūmyāṃ na phalakādāv ity arthaḥ | pracetāḥ |

	prathamaṃ pitṛpātre tu sarvān saṃbhṛtya saṃsravān |

	pitṛbhyaḥ sthānam ity uktvā kuryād bhūmāv adhomukham ||

	arghyasaṃsrāvapātraṃ tu śundhantām iti saṃspṛśet |

	pitṛbhyaḥ sthānam asīti nyubjaṃ kuryāt pavitravat ||

	tasyopari kuśaṃ datvā pradadyād daivapūrvakam |

	gandhapuṣpāṇi dhūpaṃ ca pradīpaṃ ca yathākramam ||

anena gandhadānaṃ caivaṃ brāhmaṇeṣu kāryam ity ucyate | tadā puṣpādidānāny api | tataś ca datvodakaṃ gandhamālyam ity atra ya uktaḥ kramas tenāsya vikalpaḥ | kātyāyanaḥ: "ekasmin pitṛpātre saṃsrāvān samavanīya putrakāmo mukham anakti | tathā śundhantāṃ lokāḥ pitṛṣadanā ity ekadeśam avasicya tatra **[485]** nyubjaṃ pātraṃ karoti pitṛṣadanam asīti kuśavatyāṃ bhūmyām adhomukhaṃ kuryāt | tasyopari ca kuśapuṣpagandhadhūpadīpopapavītavāsasāṃ dānāni" | tasya pātrasyopari gandhādidānaṃ kuśasāhacaryāt | anye tu manyante — gandhādidānaṃ pitṛbrāhmaṇebhya ity uktvā kuśadānam eva pātrasyoparīti, kuśaśabdaṃ ca dvitīyāntaṃ paṭhanti | ślokakātyāyanaḥ |

	arghyaṃ svadhā yā ity uktvā saṃsrāvān abhimantrayet |

	ye devā iti mantreṇa putrakāmo mukhaṃ spṛśet ||

yamaḥ |

	paitṛkaṃ prathamaṃ pātraṃ tasmin paitāmahaṃ nyaset |

	prapitāmahaṃ tato nyasya noddharen na ca cālayet ||

	spṛṣṭam uddhṛtam anyatra nītam udghāṭitaṃ tathā |

	pātraṃ dṛṣṭvā vrajanty āśu pitaraḥ praśapanti ca ||

matsyapurāṇāt |

	yā dviyety arghyam utsṛjya dadyād gandhādikaṃ tataḥ |

	vastrottaraṃ cānupūrvaṃ datvā saṃsravam āditaḥ ||

	pitṛpātre nidhāyātha nyubjam uttarato nyaset ||

asyārthaḥ — "yā divyāḥ" ity arghaṃ(ghyaṃ) datvā pitṛpātre saṃsrāvam arghyāvaśeṣam ādita ādau kṛtvā nidhāyānantaraṃ śrāddhadeśād uttarato nyubjaṃ tan nyaset | tato gandhādi vastraparyantaṃ dadyād iti | viṣṇuḥ: "candanakuṅkumakarpūrāṇy anulepanāya" | mārkaṇḍeyaḥ |

	candanāgurukarpūrakuṅkumāni pradāpayet |

	aśvamedham avāpnoti pitṝṇām anulepanāt ||

vyāsaḥ |

	vipavitrakaro gandhair gandhadvāreti pūjayet |

	dhūpaṃ ca dhūr asīty uktvā dīpo(pa) jyotir idaṃ ca te ||

tatra — "gandhadvārām" ity anuṣṭubhaṃ strīdai(de)vatyāṃ viśve devā apaśyan | "dhūr asi" iti dhūpadai(de)vatyaṃ yajuḥ parameṣṭhī prājāpatyo 'paśyat | vṛddhaśātātapaḥ |

	pavitraṃ tu kare kṛtvā yaḥ samālabhate dvijam |

	rākṣasaṃ tad bhavec chrāddhaṃ nirāśaiḥ pitṛbhir gataiḥ ||

gandhaiś carcanaṃ samālambhanam | devalaḥ |

	yajñopavītaṃ viprāṇāṃ skandhān naivāvatārayet |

	gandhādipūjāsiddhyarthaṃ daive pitrye ca karmaṇi || **[486]**

śaṅkhaḥ |

	upavītaṃ kaṭau kṛtvā kuryād gātrānulepanam |

	ekavāsāś ca yo 'śnīyān nirāśāḥ pitaro gatāḥ ||

vṛddhamanuḥ |

	vinopavītaṃ no kuryād gandhaiḥ śrāddhe 'nulepanam |

	niyuktaś ca śikhāvarjaṃ mālyaṃ śirasi veṣṭayet ||

mārkaṇḍeyaḥ |

	jātyāś ca sarvā dātavyāḥ mallikāḥ śvetayūthikāḥ |

brahmāṇḍapurāṇe |

	śuklāḥ sumanasaḥ śreṣṭhās tathā padmopalāni ca |

	gandharūpopapannāni yāni cānyāni kṛtsnaśaḥ ||

	japādi kusumaṃ bhāṇḍī rūṣikāḥ sakuraṇḍikāḥ |

	puṣpāṇi varjanīyāni śrāddhakarmaṇi nityaśaḥ ||

śaṅkhaḥ |

	ugragandhīny agandhīni caityavṛkṣodbhavāni ca |

	puṣpāṇi varjanīyāni raktavarṇāni yāni ca ||

	jalodbhavāni devāni raktāny api viśeṣataḥ ||

caityavṛkṣaḥ śmaśānavṛkṣaḥ | varjayed ity anuvṛttau viṣṇuḥ: "ugragandhīni kaṇṭakijāni raktāni ca puṣpāṇi | tathā sitāni sugandhīni kaṇṭakijātāny api jalajāni raktāny api dadyāt | puṣpavatīr it puṣpam" | oṣadhīḥ pratimodadhvam ity asyā madhye pratīkam etat | brahmapurāṇe |

	candanāguruṇī cobhe tathaivośīrapadmakam |

	turuṣkaṃ gugguluṃ caiva ghṛtāktaṃ yugapad dahet ||

	ghṛtaṃ na kevalaṃ dadyād duṣṭaṃ vā tṛṇaguggulum ||

śaṅkhaḥ |

	dhūpārthe gugguluṃ dadyād ghṛtayuktaṃ madhūtkaṭam |

purāṇāt |

	vanaspatiraso divyo gandhāḍhyaḥ sumanoharaḥ |

	āhvānaṃ sarvadevānāṃ dhūpo 'yaṃ pratigṛhyatām ||

śātātapaḥ |

	hastavātāhataṃ dhūpaṃ ye pibanti dvijottamāḥ |

	vṛthā bhavati tac chrāddhaṃ tasmāt tat parivarjayet ||

devalaḥ |

	puṣpavatītimantreṇa dadyāt puṣpāṇy atandritaḥ |

	idaṃ jyotir iti jyotiḥ sujyotir iti te 'pi ca || **[487]**

kratuḥ |

	lalāṭe puṇḍraṃ dṛṣṭvā skande(ndhe) mālāṃ tathaiva ca |

	nirāśāḥ pitaro yānti dṛṣṭvā ca vṛṣalīpatim ||

puṇḍrakaṃ cātra vṛttaṃ niṣiddhaṃ nordhvam | marīciḥ |

	ghṛtād vā tilatailād vā nānyad dādyāt tu dīpakam ||

atriḥ |

	yuvaṃ vasrāṇīty anena dadyād vāsāṃsi śaktitaḥ ||

vāyupurāṇāt |

	vāso hi sarvadai(de)vatyaṃ sarvadevair abhiṣṭutam |

	vastrābhāve kriyā na syād yajñadānādikā kvacit ||

	tasmād vastrāṇi deyāni śrāddhakāle viśeṣataḥ |

	dadad vai tāni cāpnoti yajñadānatapāṃsi ca ||

tathā|

	ācchādanaṃ tu yo dadyād ahataṃ śrāddhakarmaṇi |

	āyuḥ prākāmyam aiśvaryaṃ rūpaṃ ca labhate śubham ||

	kauśeyaṃ kṣaumakārpāsaṃ dugū(kū)lam ahataṃ tathā |

	śrāddheṣv etāni yo dadyāt kāmān āpnoti puṣkalān ||

śātātapaḥ: "yuvā suvāsā iti vāso dadyāt tadabhāve yajñopavītakam" || tathā |

	loke śreṣṭhatamaṃ sarvam ātmanaś cāpi yat priyam |

	sarvaṃ pitṝṇāṃ dātavyaṃ tad evākṣayam icchatā ||

vāyupurāṇe |

	śrāddheṣūpānahau dadyād brāhmaṇebhyo viśeṣataḥ |

	divyaṃ sa labhate cakṣur vājiyuktān rathāṃs tathā ||

	yajñopavītaṃ yo dadyāc chrāddhakāle tu dharmavit |

	pāvanaṃ sarvaviprāṇāṃ brahmadānasya tat phalam ||

	kṛtaṃ vipreṇa yo dadyāc chrāddhakāle kamaṇḍalum |

	dhenuṃ sa labhate divyāṃ ghaṭopabhṛtadohanām ||

	tūlapūrṇe tu yo dadyāt pāduke śrāddhakarmaṇi |

	śobhanaṃ labhate yānaṃ pādayoḥ sukham eva ca ||

	vyajanaṃ tālavṛntaṃ ca datvā viprāya satkṛtam |

	prāpnuyāt sparśayuktāni sugandhīni mṛdūni ca ||

	śreṣṭhaṃ chatraṃ ca yo dadyāt puṣpamālāvibhūṣitam |

	prāsādo hy uttamo bhūtvā gacchantam anugacchati ||

**[488]**	dadyāt pavitraṃ yogibhyo gantur dhāraṇam ambhasaḥ |

	atha niṣkasahasrasya phalam āpnoti mānavaḥ ||

tathā |

	lavaṇena supūrṇāni śrāddhe pātrāṇi dāpayet |

	rasās tam upatiṣṭhanti bhakṣyaṃ saubhāgyam eva ca ||

	pātraṃ vai taijasaṃ dadyān manojñaṃ śrāddhabhojane |

	pātraṃ bhavati kāmānāṃ vidyānāṃ ca dhanasya ca ||

	rājataṃ kāñcanaṃ caiva dadyāc chrāddheṣu yaḥ pumān |

	datvā sa labhate dātā prākāmyaṃ dhanam eva ca ||

purāṇāt |

	rājataṃ rājatāktaṃ vā pitṝṇāṃ pātram eva ca |

	rajatasya kathā vāpi darśanaṃ dānam eva ca ||

	anantam akṣayaṃ svargyaṃ rājataṃ dānam ucyate |

	pitṝn etena dānena satputrās tārayanty uta ||

manuḥ |

	rājatair bhājanair eṣām api vā rājatānvitaiḥ |

	vāry api śraddhayā dattam akaṣayāyopakalpate ||

vṛddhaśātātapaḥ |

	pātre tu mṛnmaye yas tu śrāddhe vai bhojayet pitṝn |

	annadātā purodhāś ca bhoktā ca narakaṃ vrajet ||

atriḥ |

	bhojane haimaraupyāṇi daive pitrye yathākramam |

	na mṛnmayāni kurvīta bhojane daivapitryayoḥ ||

	pālāśebhyo vinā na syuḥ parṇapātrāṇi bhojane ||

viṣṇuḥ: "taijasāni pātrāṇi dadyād viśeṣato rājatāni | ghṛtādidāne taijasāni pātrāṇi phalgupātrāṇi vā" | phalgur vṛkṣaviśeṣaḥ | matsyapurāṇāt |

	akṛtvā bhasmamaryādāṃ yaḥ kuryāt paṅktibhojanam |

	āsuraṃ tad bhavec chrāddhaṃ pitṝṇāṃ nopatiṣṭhati ||

brahmapurāṇe |

	maṇḍalāni ca kāryāṇi naivāraiś cūrṇikaiḥ subhaiḥ |

	gauramṛttikayā vāpi praṇītenātha bhasmanā ||

	pāṣāṇacūrṇasaṃkīrṇād āhṛtaṃ tatra varjayet ||

brahmāṇdapurāṇe |

	prakṣālya hastapātrādi paścād adbhir vidhānavit |

	prakṣālanaṃ darbhais tilair miśraṃ kṣipec chucau || **[489]**

viṣṇuḥ |

	mantrahīnaṃ kriyāhīnaṃ saṃpaddhīnaṃ dvijottamāḥ |

	śrāddhaṃ saṃpūrṇatāṃ yātu prasādād bhavatāṃ mama || iti || 1.234 ||

	**agnau kariṣya ādāya pṛcchaty annaṃ ghṛtaplutam |**

**	kuruṣvety abhyanujñāto hutvāgnau pitṛyajñavat || 1.235 ||**

**	hutaśeṣaṃ pradadyāt tu bhājaneṣu samāhitaḥ |**

**	yathālābhopapanneṣu raupyeṣu tu viśeṣataḥ || 1.236 ||**

bahutarājyasiktam annam upādāyāgnau kariṣya ity anena mantreṇa śrāddhabhoktṝn anjujñāpya kuruṣvety anena tair anujñātaḥ svasūtroktapiṇḍapitṛyajñahomakalpena tadannaikadeśam agnau hutvā hutaśeṣaṃ brāhmaṇabhojanabhājaneṣu raupyamayeṣu tadasaṃbhave pratiṣiddhavarjaṃ yathālābopapanneṣu samāhitas tanmanāḥ prakṣipet | raupyapātranirdeśāt pitṛbrāhmaṇabhājaneṣv eva hutaśeṣapradānam icchatīti gamyate | atrānujñānavacanaṃ sarvair eva brāhmaṇair yugapad vācyam ity āha manuḥ |

	agnau kuryād anujñāto brāhmaṇo brāhmaṇaiḥ saha ||

brāhmaṇḍapurāṇe |

	āhṛtya dakṣiṇāgniṃ tu homārthaṃ vai prayatnataḥ |

	agnaye kavyavāhāya svadhā nama iti bruvan ||

	somāya ca pitṛmate svadhā nama iti bruvan |

	yamāyāṅgirasāṃ patye svadhā nama iti bruvan ||

	ity ete homamantrās tu trayāṇām anupūrvaśaḥ |

	dakṣiṇato 'gnaye nityaṃ somāyottaratas tathā ||

	etayor antare nityaṃ juhuyād vai vivasvate |

	bahuśuṣkendhane cāgnau susamiddhe viśeṣataḥ ||

	vidhūme lelihāne ca hotavyaṃ karmasiddhaye |

	aprabuddhe sadhūme vā juhuyād yo hutāśane ||

	yajamāno bhaved andhaḥ so 'mutreti hi naḥ śrutam |

	antar nidhāya samidhaṃ juhuyāt kavyavāhanam ||

	palāśaphalgunyaghrodhaplakṣāśvatthavikaṅkatāḥ |

	udumbaras tathā bilvaś candanaṃ yajñiyāś ca ye ||

**[490]**	saralo devadāruś ca sālaś ca khadiraś ca ha |

	samidarthe praśastāḥ syur ete vṛkṣā viśeṣataḥ ||

	grāhyāḥ kaṇṭakinaś caiva yajñiyā ye ca kecana |

	pūjitāḥ samidarthe ye pitṝṇāṃ vacanaṃ yathā ||

	śleṣmāntako raktamālaḥ kapitthaḥ śa(śā)lmalis tathā |

	nīpo vibhītakaś caiva śrāddhakarmaṇi garhitāḥ ||

	cirabilvas tathā ṭaṅkas tindukāmrātakau tathā |

	bilvakaḥ kovidāraś ca ete śrāddhe vigarhitāḥ ||

	nivāsaś caiva kīṭānāṃ garhitāḥ syur ayajñiyāḥ |

	gulmāṃś ca veṣṭitān yāṃś ca balībhiś ca samantataḥ ||

	śakunānāṃ nivāsāṃś ca varjayed dvijasattamaḥ |

	anyāṃś caivaṃvidhān sarvān varjayed vā ayajñiyān ||

	puṣpāṇāṃ ca phalānāṃ ca bhakṣāṇāṃ ca prayatnataḥ |

	agram uddhṛtya sarveṣāṃ juhuyāj jātavedase ||

mārkaṇḍeyaḥ |

	āhitāgniś ca juhuyād dakṣiṇāgnau samāhitaḥ |

	anāhitāgniś caupasade agnyabhāve tathāpsu vā ||

aupasado gṛhyāgniḥ | āhitāgner dakṣiṇāgnividhānam aupasadābhāve veditavyam | aupasade tu sati tatraiva | tathā ca vāyupurāṇam |

	āhṛtya dakṣiṇāgniṃ tu homārthaṃ vai prayatnataḥ |

	agnyarthaṃ laukikaṃ vāpi juhuyāt karmasiddhaye ||

atra vākye 'gniśabdaḥ prakṛte 'gnau vartate | śrāddhaprayogavidhau ca gṛhyo 'gniḥ prakṛtaḥ śrāddhaprayogasya gṛhyaśāstravidheyatvāt | gṛhyāgnyadhikāreṇa ca gṛhyaśāstrāṇāṃ pravṛttir iti tadabhāva eva tatkārye dakṣiṇāgnilaukikāgnyor vidhir yujyate tatsadbhāve tu tenaiva svakāryasiddhau kim agnyantaravidhānena | yo 'pi dharmaśāstreṣu purāṇeṣu ca śrāddhaprayogavidhiḥ sa gṛhyoktād abhinnaḥ pratyabhijñānāt tena dharmaśāstreṣv api gṛhya evāgniḥ prakṛtaḥ | ato 'gnyartham ity atrāgniśabdo gṛhyaparaḥ prakṛtatvād iti yuktam | yat punar anāhitāgniś caupasada iti vacanaṃ tad dakṣiṇāgnāv agnaukaraṇavidhānād anāhitāgneḥ śrāddhānadhikārāśaṅkānirākaraṇārtham | **[491]** tataś cānāhitāgniś caupasade kuryād eva na na (?) kuryāt | na tv anāhitāgnir evaupasada iti tasyārthaḥ | anagnis tu viprakare 'gnaukaraṇahomaṃ kuryād ity āha manuḥ |

	agnyabhāve tu viprasya pāṇāv evopapādayet |

yat tu jātūkarṇyenoktam,

	agnyabhāve tu viprasya haste dadyāt tu dakṣiṇe |

	agnyabhāvaḥ smṛtas tāvad yāvad bhāryāṃ na vindati ||

iti, tad bhāryāvedanāt prāṅ niyatāgnyabhāvo na punas tataḥ prāg evāgnyabhāva ity abhiprāyaḥ(yeṇa) | labdhabhāryo 'pi prāg dāyavibhāgād anagniḥ saṃbhavati | pāṇāv evopapadayed ity evaśabdo laukikam agniṃ vyudasyati yataḥ sa evāha |

	na paitṛyajñiyo homo laukiko 'gnau vidhīyate |

matsyapurāṇe |

	agnyabhāve tu viprasya pāṇāv atha jale 'pi vā |

	ajakarṇe 'śvakarṇe vā goṣṭhe vātha śivāntike ||

śaṅkhaḥ |

	ajasya dakṣiṇe karṇe pāṇau viprasya dakṣiṇe |

	apsu caiva kuśastambe agniṃ kātyāyano 'bravīt ||

	rajate ca suvarṇe ca nityaṃ vasati pāvakaḥ ||

kātyāyanaḥ |

	pitrye yaḥ paṅktimūrdhanyas tasya pāṇāv anagnikaḥ |

	hutvā mantravad anyeṣāṃ tūṣṇīṃ pātreṣu nikṣipet ||

	mātāmahasya bhede 'pi kuryāt tantre ca sāgnikaḥ ||

mātāmahasya yo brāhmaṇas tasya pāṇau vaiśvadevikatantre bhede ca pṛthag agnaukaraṇaṃ kāryam ity arthaḥ | vāyupurāṇe |

	daive hy anagnikaḥ kuryāc cheṣaṃ pitrye nivedayet |

	na hi smṛtāḥ śeṣabhājo viśve devāḥ purāṇagaiḥ ||

yamaḥ |

	daivaviprakare 'nagniḥ kṛtvāgnaukaraṇaṃ dvijaḥ |

	hutvā pitṛbhyaḥ śeṣāt tu piṇḍārthaṃ sthāpayet punaḥ ||

vāyupurāṇam |

	vaiśvadeve yadaikasmin bhaveyur dvyādayo dvijāḥ |

	tadaikapāṇau dātavyaṃ syād vidhir vihatas tadā ||

asyārthaḥ — yadaikasmiñ śrāddhe vaiśvadevike karye dvau catvāraḥ ṣaḍ ity evaṃ dvyādayo viprāḥ syus tadaikasya haste home kṛte kṛto vidhir ato na viprāntarahaste kārya iti | vaiśvadevikahaste homo 'nagner vaikalpikaḥ | yadā ca haste homas **[492]** tadā bhavatsv evāgnaukaraṇam iti brāhmaṇānujñānam | tatheri ca prativacanam | tad āha śaunakaḥ: "anagniś ced ājyaṃ gṛhītvā bhavatsv evāgnaukaraṇam iti pūrvavat tathāstv iti" | yamaḥ |

	hutvāgnau ca tataḥ paścād vidhinānena mantravit |

	svadhety evaṃ haviḥśeṣam ādāya prasamīkṣya ca ||

homāvaśiṣṭaṃ svadhety anena mantreṇa prasamīkṣyālokyādāya pitṛbhyo datvā piṇḍārtham avaśeṣayet || 1.235, 236 ||

	**datvānnaṃ pṛthivī pātram iti pātrānumantraṇam |**

**	kṛtvedaṃ viṣṇur ity anne dvijāṅguṣṭhaṃ niveśayet || 1.237 ||**

hutaśeṣād anyad bhojanārtham upakḷptam annaṃ vicitraṃ tad devebhyaḥ pitṛbhyaś ca datvā saṃkalpya pṛthivī te pātram iti pātrānumantraṇaṃ kṛtvā "idaṃ viṣṇur vi cakrame" iti gāyatryā medhātithidṛṣṭayā viṣṇudai(de)vatyayā dvijāṅguṣṭhaṃ tasminn anne niveśayet | śaunakaḥ |

	pākaṃ sarvam upānīya saṃvedya ca pṛthak pṛthak |

	vidhinā daivapūrvaṃ tu pariveṣaṇam ārabhet ||

saṃvedya bhoktṝṇāṃ saṃviditaṃ kṛtvety arthaḥ | uśanā |

	hutaśeṣaṃ pitṛbhyaś ca datvānnaṃ pariveṣayet |

	haviṣyaṃ madhumāṃsāni pāyasāpūpam eva ca ||

śaṅkhaḥ |

	uṣṇam annaṃ dvijātibhyaḥ śraddhayā vinivedayet |

	anyatra phalapuṣpebhyaḥ pānakebhyaś ca paṇḍitaḥ ||

phalādy anuṣṇaṃ deyam ity arthaḥ | dharmaḥ |

	pariveṣaṇam iṣṭaṃ syād bhāryayā pitṛtṛptaye |

	phalasyānantatā proktā svayaṃ ca pariveṣaṇe ||

hutaśeṣaṃ pradāya svayaṃ ca pariveṣaṇaṃ kāryam iti vihitam | śaunakas tu pariveṣaṇottarakālaṃ hutaśeṣapradānam āha: "annam anne mṛṣṭaṃ dattaṃ samṛdhnukam" iti | hutāvaśiṣṭam annaṃ bhājane pūrvaṃ datte bhojanārthe 'nne dattaṃ samṛdhnukam ṛddhikaraṃ bhavatīty arthaḥ | manuḥ |

	pāṇibhyām upasaṃgṛhya svayam annasya vardhitam |

	viprāntike pitṝn dyāyañ śanakair upanikṣipet || **[493]**

tataś ca viprabhojanapradeśāt pradeśāntare 'nnasya vardhitaṃ hastābhyām upasaṃgṛhya viprasaṃnidhau pitrādīn dhyāyañ śanakaiḥ sthāpayet svayam eva | ekaikasya bhoktur bhojanārtham upakalpito bhāgo 'nnasya vardhitam | tathā |

	ubhayor hastayor muktaṃ yad annam upanīyate |

	tad vipralumpanty asurāḥ sahasā duṣṭacetasaḥ ||

	guṇāṃś ca sūpaśākādyān payo dadhi ghṛtaṃ madhu |

	vinyaset prayataḥ samyag bhūmāv eva samāhitaḥ ||

guṇā vyañjanādikāni tāni ca sūpaśākādiśabdair nirdiṣṭāni tāni ca bhūmisthiteṣu bhājaneṣu deyāni | nāmarya(trā)disthiteṣu | vṛddhaśātātapaḥ |

	āyasena tu pātreṇa yad annam upanīyate |

	bhoktā viṣṭhāsamaṃ bhuṅkte dātā tu narakaṃ vrajet ||

tathā |

	hastadattās tu ye snehā lavaṇavyañjanādayaḥ |

	dātāraṃ nopatiṣṭhanti bhoktā bhuñjīta kilbiṣam ||

	sauvarṇarājatābhyāṃ vā khaḍgenaudumbareṇa vā |

	dattam akṣayatāṃ yāti phalgupātreṇa vā punaḥ ||

audumbaraṃ tāmramayam | yamaḥ |

	mākṣikaṃ phāṇitaṃ śākaṃ gorasaṃ lavaṇaṃ tathā |

	hastadattāni bhuktvā tu kṛcchraṃ sāntapanaṃ caret ||

viṣṇuḥ: "na pratyakṣaṃ lavaṇaṃ dadyāt" | vāyupurāṇe |

	saindhavaṃ lavaṇaṃ caiva tathā mānasasaṃbhavam |

	pavitre parame hy ete pratyakṣe 'pi ca nityaśaḥ ||

hārītaḥ |

	paṅktyāṃ vai copaviṣṭebhyaḥ samaṃ gandhādi bhojanam |

	na paṅktyāṃ viṣamaṃ dadyān na yācen na ca dāpayet ||

	yācako dāpako dātā sarve nirayagāminaḥ(ṇaḥ) ||

kārṣṇājiniḥ |

	apasavyena kartavyaṃ pitryaṃ kṛtyaṃ viśeṣataḥ |

	annadānād ṛte sarvam evaṃ mātāmaheṣv api ||

	apasavyena yas tv annaṃ brāhmaṇebhyaḥ prayacchati |

	viṣṭhām. aśnanti pitaras te ca sarve dvijātayaḥ ||

	yat tu śrāddhaṃ kriyāduṣṭam ajñānapariveṣitam |

	tasmin bhuktvācaret kṛcchraṃ cāndrāyaṇam athāpi vā || **[494]**

apasavyam atra prācīnāvītam | yamaḥ |

	yāvad dhaviṣyaṃ bhavati yāvat sṛṣṭaṃ pradīyate |

	tāvad aśnanti pitaro yāvan nāha dadāmy aham ||

	yat kiṃcit pacyate gehe bhakṣyaṃ vā bhojyam eva vā |

	na bhoktavyaṃ pitṝṇāṃ syād anivedya kathaṃcana ||

purāṇāt |

	nāpavitreṇa hastena naikena na vinā kuśam |

	nāyase nāyasenaiva śrāddhe tu pariveṣayet ||

āyase bhājana āyasena darvyādinā na dadyād ity arthaḥ |

	tasmād antaritaṃ deyaṃ parṇenātha tṛṇena ca |

paiṭhīnasiḥ: "pṛthivī te pātraṃ dyaur apidhānaṃ brāhmaṇasya mukhe 'mṛtaṃ juhomi svadhā | idaṃ viṣṇur vi cakrama ity anenāṅguṣṭham anne codake cāvadharya vyāhṛtipūrvāṃ gāyatrīṃ japtvā svadateti brūyāt" | yamaḥ |

	aṅguṣṭhamātro bhagavān viṣṇuḥ paryaṭate mahīm |

	rākṣasānāṃ vadhārthāya ko me 'dya prahariṣyati ||

	tasmāc chrāddheṣu sarveṣu aṅguṣṭhagrahaṇaṃ smṛtam |

	niraṅguṣṭhaṃ ca yac chrāddhaṃ bahirjānu ca yat kṛtam ||

	bahirjānu ca yad bhuktaṃ sarvam evāsuraṃ bhavet |

	viṣṇo havyaṃ ca kavyaṃ ca brūyād rakṣeti ca kramāt ||

	vāriṣv agrapradatteṣu tam aṅguṣṭhaṃ niveśayet ||

kātyāyanaḥ: "vaiṣṇavyā vā yajuṣā vāṅguṣṭham anne 'vagāhyāpahatā iti tilān prakīryoṣṇaṃ sviṣṭam annaṃ dadyāt" | idaṃ viṣṇur vi cakrama it vaiṣṇavī, viṣṇo havyam iti yajuḥ | dadyād devebhyaḥ pitṛbhyaś ceti śeṣaḥ | viṣṇuḥ: "namo viśvebhyo devebhya ity annam ādau prāṅmukhayor nivedayet | pitre pitāmahāya ca nāmagotrābhyām udaṅmukheṣu" | uktavākyebhyaḥ pūrvam aṅguṣṭhaniveśanaṃ paścād annasaṃkalpa iti kramaḥ pratīyate | atra prāṅmukhayor udaṅmukheṣv iti saptamyā brāhmaṇānām āhavanīyārthatvaṃ pratipadyate | viśvebhyo devebhyaḥ pitra ityādikayā caturthyā viśveṣāṃ devānāṃ pitrādeś ca devatātvaṃ tena yad āpastambena: "athaitan manuḥ śrāddhaśabdaṃ karma provāca" ityādinā śrāddham uktaṃ tad etan nivedanādiśabdenocyate | **[495]** brahmapurāṇe |

	tato madhughṛtāktaṃ tu soṣṇam annaṃ tilānvitam |

	gṛhītvā devatīrthena praṇavenaiva tat punaḥ ||

	etad vo 'nnam itīty uktvā viśvān devāṃś ca saṃyajet ||

asyārthaḥ — vaiśvadevikabrāhmaṇabhojanārthaṃ madhughṛtābhyām abhyaktenānnena pūrṇapātraṃ satilodakena hastāgreṇa gṛhītvom ity etad vo viśve devā amukanāmāno 'nnam iti nivedayed iti |

	pitṛbhyaś ca tato dadyād annam āmantraṇena tu |

	amukāmukagotraitat tubhyam annaṃ svadhā namaḥ ||

	atha datvā samagraṃ tu kulāntaṃ bhojanaṃ kramāt |

	viśvebhyaś cātha devebhyaḥ kuryāc ca pratipādanam ||

	dvijāṅguṣṭhaṃ gṛhītvā tu paṭhan mantraṃ ca vāgyataḥ |

	pṛthvī te pātram ity annam amṛtaṃ cintayet paṭhan ||

	viṣṇo havyam idaṃ rakṣa madīyam iti kīrtayan |

	ekaikasyātha viprasya gṛhītvāṅguṣṭham ādarāt ||

	amukāmukagotraitat tubhyam annaṃ svadhā namaḥ |

	tilayuktaṃ ca pānīyaṃ sakuśaṃ teṣu cāgrataḥ ||

	vikiret pitṛbhṛtyebhyo japann apahatā iti |

	tebhyo dadyād apośānaṃ bhavantaḥ prāśayantv iti ||

asmād vākyād aṅguṣṭhaniveśanaṃ paścāt pūrvam annasaṃkalpa iti gamyate | tataś cāṅguṣṭhaviveśanānnasaṃkalpayoḥ paurvāparye vikalpaḥ | atriḥ |

	asaṃkalpitam annādyaṃ pāṇibhyāṃ yad upaspṛśet |

	abhojyaṃ tad bhaved dattaṃ pitṝṇāṃ nopatiṣṭhate ||

devādibhyo 'nnapradānaṃ saṃkalpaḥ |

	apośānakare vipre saṃkalpaṃ yaḥ samācaret |

	tad annam asurair bhuktaṃ pitṝṇāṃ nopatiṣṭhati ||

	hastena saktam annadyam idam annam udīrayet |

	svadheti ca tataḥ kuryāt svasattāvinivartanam ||

**[496]**	gotrasaṃbandhanāmāni idam annam iti svadhā |

	pitṛkramād udīryeti svasattāṃ vinivartayet ||

svasattāvinivartanāya na mameti mānasaḥ saṃkalpaḥ kāryaḥ | tataś cāmukagotrapitar amukaitat te 'nnaṃ svadhā nama ity uccārya na mameti manasā saṃkalpayet | evaṃ pitāmahādāv api | yadā tu bahūnāṃ pitrādīnām ekaika eva brāhmaṇo bhojyate tadā yāvantaḥ pitaras tāvato 'nnabhāgān budhyā kṛtvāikaikaṃ bhāgaṃ pitrādibhyaḥ saṃkalpayet | tathā |

	datte vāpy atha vādatte bhūmau yo nikṣiped balim |

	tad annaṃ viphalaṃ yāti nirāśaiḥ pitṛbhir gataiḥ ||

bharadvājaḥ |

	pitṝṇām annam ādāya baliṃ yas tu prayacchati |

	steyena brāhmaṇas tena sa sarvasteyakṛd bhavet || 1.237 ||

	**savyāhṛtikāṃ gāyatrīṃ madhu vātā iti tryṛcam |**

**	japtvā yathāsukhaṃ vācyaṃ bhuñjīraṃs te 'pi vāgyatāḥ || 1.238 ||**

tisṛbhir vyāhṛtibhiḥ sahitāṃ gāyatrīṃ madhuvātā iti ca tryṛcaṃ rāhugaṇagautamadṛṣṭaṃ gāyatraṃ vaiśvadevaṃ japitvā yathāsukhaṃ juṣadhvam iti viprān prati vācyam | te ca viprā vācaṃyamā bhuñjīran | pracetāḥ |

	apośānaṃ pradāyātha sāvitrīṃ trir japed atha |

	madhu vāta(tā) iti tryṛcaṃ madhv ity etat trikaṃ tathā ||

madhv iti trir uccārayed ity arthaḥ | laghuyamaḥ |

	annaṃ madhumayaṃ kṛtvā madhu vāteti mantritam |

	agnihīnaṃ kriyāhīnaṃ mantrahīnaṃ ca yad bhavet ||

	sarvam acchidram ity uktvā tato yatnena bhojayet ||

madhumayaṃ pracuramadhukam ity arthaḥ | acchidrabhāṣaṇaṃ ca prāg evāpośānadānāt kāryaṃ na paścāt | tad āha pracetāḥ |

	apośānakarāgrāṇām acchidrasya ca bhāṣaṇāt |

	nirāśāḥ pitaro yānti devaiḥ saha na saṃśayaḥ ||

vyāsaḥ |

	juṣadhvam iti te coktāḥ samyagvidhṛtabhānanāḥ |

	kṛtamaunāḥ samaśnīyur apośānād anantaram || **[497]**

śaṅkhalikhitau: "nāgrāsanasthaḥ pūrvam aśnīyān nābhyadhikaṃ dadyān na pratigṛhṇīyāt" | baudhāyanaḥ |

	juṣeti prathamaṃ brūyād bhuktānte brāhmaṇeṣu ca |

	mantrakarmaviparyāsād acchidraṃ jāyatām iti ||

bahvṛcagṛhyapariśiṣṭam |

	yac ca pāṇitale dattaṃ yc cānnam upakalpitam |

	ekībhāvena bhoktavyaṃ pṛthagbhāvo na vidyate ||

pāṇitale dattam ity agnaukaraṇānnam ity arthaḥ | tac cānnaṃ saṃkalpāt pūrvaṃ pṛthak sthāpyaṃ tato bhojanārthenānnena miśraṇīyam | manuḥ |

	na ca dvijātayo brūyur dātrā pṛṣṭān havirguṇān |

	yāvad ūṣmā bhavaty anne yāvad aśnanti vāgyatāḥ ||

	tāvad aśnanti pitaro yāvan noktā havirguṇāḥ ||

pracetāḥ |

	pītvāpośānam aśnīyāt pātre dattam agarhitam |

	sarvendriyāṇāṃ cāpalyaṃ pādapāṇyos tathaiva ca ||

	dantacchedaṃ hastapānaṃ varjayec cātibhojanam ||

pānādikaṃ hastena na pibet | śaṅkhalikhitau: "brāhmaṇā annaṃ guṇadoṣair nābhivadeyuḥ | nānṛtaṃ brūyuḥ | anyonyaṃ na praśaṃseyuḥ | annapānaṃ na prabhūtam iti na brūyuḥ | anyatra hastasaṃjñāyā yāvad bhūmau yāvat praśastaṃ yāvat soṣma tāvad aśnanti pitaro hy anyatra phalammūlapānakebhyaḥ" | phalādīnāṃ soṣmatā na kāryety arthaḥ | yamaḥ |

	yaś ca pāṇitale bhuṅkte yaś ca vāyuṃ samutsṛjet |

	na tasya pitaro 'śnanti yaś caivāgre praśaṃsati ||

varāhapurāṇe |

	yācate yadi dātāraṃ brāhmaṇo jñānavarjitaḥ |

	pitaras tasya tuṣyanti dātur bhoktur na saṃśayaḥ ||

hārītaḥ |

	uddhṛtya pāṇiṃ vihasan sakrodho vismayānvitaḥ |

	śrāddhakāle tu yad bhuṅkte na tat prīṇāti vai pitṝn ||

vṛddhaśātātapaḥ |

	āsane pādam āropya yad bhuṅkte ca dvijottamaḥ |

	hanti daivaṃ ca pitryaṃ ca tad annaṃ ca prajāḥ paśūn ||

devalaḥ |

	yo 'prasannamanā bhuṅkte sopānatko 'pi vā punaḥ |

	pralāpaśīlaḥ kruddho vā sa vipraḥ pitṛdūṣakaḥ || **[498]**

yamaḥ |

	yas tu bhuktvā punar bhuṅkte yaś ca tailābhighāritam |

	rajasvalābhir yad dṛṣṭaṃ tad vai rakṣāṃsi gacchati ||

rajasvalādibhir iti vyākhyeyaṃ bahuvacanam |

	niroṃkāreṇa yad bhuktaṃ pariviṣṭaṃ samanyunā |

	durātmanā ca yad bhuktaṃ tad vai rakṣāṃsi gacchati ||

niroṃkāreṇety oṃkārādikaṃ bhojanamantram antareṇety arthaḥ |

	vidhihīnam asṛṣṭānnaṃ mantrahīnam adakṣiṇam |

	aśraddhayā hutaṃ dattaṃ tad vai rakṣāṃsi gacchati ||

	niyuktaś caiva yaḥ śrāddhe yat kiṃcit parivarjayet |

	pitaras tasya taṃ māsaṃ nairāśyaṃ pratipedire ||

vasiṣṭhaḥ |

	ubhayoḥ śākhayor muktaṃ pitṛbhyo 'nnaṃ niveditam |

	tadantaraṃ pratīkṣante hy asurā duṣṭacetasaḥ ||

	tasmād aśūnyaṃ hastena tiṣṭhed ucchoṣaṇād dvijaḥ ||

tathā |

	niyuktas tu tathā śrāddhe daive vā māṃsam utsṛjet |

	yāvanti paśuromāṇi tāvan narakam ṛcchati ||

varāhapurāṇe |

	uddhared yadi pātraṃ tu brāhmaṇo jñānadurbalaḥ |

	haranti rākṣasās tasya bhuñjāno 'nnaṃ vasuṃdhare ||

śātātapaḥ |

	arghabhukte tu yo vipras tasmin pātre jalaṃ pibet |

	yad bhuktaṃ tat pitṝṇāṃ tu śeṣaṃ vidyād athāsuram ||

	hastaṃ prakṣālya yaś cāpaḥ pibed bhuktvā dvijaḥ sadā |

	tad annam asurair bhuktaṃ nirāśāḥ pitaro gatāḥ ||

manuḥ |

	śrāddhaṃ bhuktvā ya ucchiṣṭaṃ vṛṣalāya prayacchati |

	sa mūḍho narakaṃ yāti kālasūtram avākśirāḥ ||

śātātapaḥ |

	bhagnapṛṣṭhas tu yo bhuṅkte bahirjānus tathaiva ca |

	haste vakti cājasraṃ sa jñeyaḥ pitṛghātakaḥ ||

	na spṛśed vāmahastena bhuñjāno 'nnaṃ kadācana |

	na pādau na śiro bastiṃ na padā bhājanaṃ spṛśet || **[499]**

baudhāyanaḥ |

	pādena pādam ākramya yo bhuṅkte 'nāpadi dvijaḥ |

	naivāsau bhojyate śrāddhe nirāśāḥ pitaro gatāḥ ||

brahmāṇḍapurāṇe |

	śūdrāya cānupetāya śrāddhocchiṣṭaṃ na dāpayet |

	yo dadyād rāgasaṃmohān na tad gacchati vai pitṝn ||

	tasmān na deyam ucchiṣṭam annādyaṃ śrāddhakarmaṇi |

	anyatra dadhisarpirbhyāṃ śiṣyāya ca sutāya ca ||

	harṣayed brāhmaṇāṃs tuṣṭo bhojayec cāśanaṃ śanaiḥ |

	annādyenāsakṛc caitān guṇaiś ca paricodayet ||

paricodayet pravartayet | nigamaḥ |

	apekṣitaṃ na yo dadyāc chrāddhārthaṃ parikalpitam |

	adhaḥ kṛcchrāsu ghorāsu tiryagyoniṣu jāyate ||

	māṃsāpūpaphalekṣvādi dantacchedaṃ na bhakṣayet |

	grāsaśeṣaṃ na pātre syāt pītaśeṣaṃ tu no pibet ||

atriḥ |

	huṃkāreṇāpi yo brūyād dhastād vātha guṇān vadet |

	bhūtalāc coddharet pātraṃ muñjed dhastena vā pibet ||

	prauḍhapādo bahiṣkakṣo bahirjānukaro 'tha vā |

	aṅguṣṭhena vināśnāti mukhaśabdena vā punaḥ ||

	pītvāvaśiṣṭatoyādi punar uddhṛtya vā pibet |

	khāditārdhaṃ punaḥ khāden modakādi phalādi vā ||

	mukhena vā dhamed annaṃ niṣṭhīved bhājane 'pi vā |

	ittham aśnan dvijaḥ śrāddhaṃ hatvā gacchaty adhogatim ||

	ghṛtaṃ vā yadi vā tailaṃ vipro nādyān nakhacyutam |

	yamas tad aśuci prāha tulyaṃ gomāṃsabhakṣaṇaiḥ ||

śātātapaḥ |

	atyuṣṇaṃ satilaṃ sarvam anivāritam adrutam |

	alolupo jitakrodho bhuñjītānnaṃ mitaṃ hitam ||

kārṣṇājiniḥ |

	kuryād athāpariśrānto dambhāhaṃkāravarjitaḥ |

	krodhaṃ mohaṃ tathā lobhaṃ varjayec chrāddhakarmaṇi ||

kuryād bhojanam ity anvayaḥ | **[500]**

manuḥ |

	brāhmaṇaṃ bhukṣukaṃ vāpi bhojanārtham upāgatam |

	brāhmaṇair abhyanujñātaḥ śaktitaḥ pratipūjayet ||

yamaḥ |

	bhikṣuko brahmacārī vā bhojanārtham upāgataḥ |

	upaviṣṭeṣu tu prāptaḥ kāmaṃ tam api bhojayet || 1.238 ||

	**annam iṣṭaṃ haviṣyaṃ ca dadyād akrodhano 'tvaraḥ |**

annaṃ pāyasādi brāhmaṇānām abhīṣṭaṃ tac ca havirbhāgārhaṃ krodhatvarārahito dadyāt | śaṅkhaḥ |

	agnaukaraṇaśeṣeṇa yad annam abhighārayet |

	tasmiṃs tu prāśite dadyād yad anyat prakṛtaṃ bhavet ||

śaṅkhalikhitau: "tatas tilair māṃsaiḥ śākaiḥ sūpaiḥ kṛsarapāyasāpūpair lājair bhakṣaiḥ pānair madhunā ghṛtena dadhnā payasā ca prabhūtamiṣṭato 'nnaṃ dadyād anasūyaḥ" | yamaḥ |

	tato viṣa(śa)dam ānīya bhojayet prayato dvijān |

	annaṃ sūpaṃ ghṛtaṃ śākaṃ māṃsaṃ dadhi payo madhu ||

	sarvam etat samānīya praṇayet yathāsukham |

	yad yad roceta viprebhyas tat tad dadyād amatsarī ||

nārāyaṇaḥ |

	yad dhavyaṃ yat pavitraṃ ca yat pitryaṃ yat sukhāvaham |

	dvijātibhyaḥ savarṇāyā nāryā hastena dīyate ||

	hṛdayaṃ yad annam uṣṇaṃ yat tad uṣṇam iha śasyate ||

manuḥ |

	havir yac cirarātrāya yac cānantyāya kalpate |

	pitṛbhyo vidhivad dattaṃ tat pravakṣyāmy aśeṣataḥ ||

	tilair vrīhiyavair māṣair adbhir mūlaphalena vā |

	dattena māsaṃ prīyante vidhivat pitaro nṛṇām ||

viṣṇuḥ: "tilair vrīhiyavair māṣair adbhir mūlaphalaiḥ śākaiḥ priyaṅgunīvārair godhūmaiś ca māsaṃ prīyante | ekādaśaurabhreṇājena saṃvatsaraṃ tu payasā tadvikārair vā" | manuḥ |

	munyannāni payaḥ somaṃ māṃsaṃ yac cānupaskṛtam |

	akṣāralavaṇaṃ caiva prakṛtyā havir ucyate ||

anupakṛtaṃ kāryāntarārthatvenāpakvam | **[501]** bṛhaspatiḥ |

	saṃskṛtaṃ vyañjanāḍhyaṃ ca payomadhughṛtānvitam |

	śraddhayā dīyate yasmāc chrāddhaṃ tena nigadyate ||

āpastambaḥ: "naiyamikaṃ tu yac chrāddhaṃ snehavad eva dadyāt | sarpir māṃsam iti prathamakalpābhāve tailaṃ śākam iti" | kārṣṇājiniḥ |

	yad iṣṭaṃ jīvataś cāsīd dadyāt tat tasya yatnataḥ ||

yamaḥ |

	kṛcchraṃ dvādaśarātreṇa mucyate karmaṇas tataḥ |

	tasmād vidvān naiva dadyān nāpi yāceta dāpayet ||

vṛddhaśātātapas tv anyathāha |

	apekṣitaṃ yācitavyaṃ śrāddhārtham upakalpitam |

	na yācate dvijo mūḍhaḥ sa bhavet pitṛghātakaḥ ||

	apekṣitaṃ yo na dadyāc chrāddhārtham upakalpitam |

	kṛpaṇo mandabuddhis tu na sa śrāddhaphalaṃ labhet || iti |

tac ca śrāddhārtham upakalpitaṃ yācitavyaṃ dātavyaṃ ca | anupakalpitaṃ tu na yācyaṃ nāpi deyam iti vyavasthā ||

	**ā tṛptes tu pavitrāṇi japtvā pūrvajapaṃ tathā || 1.239 ||**

**	annam ādāya tṛptāḥ stha śeṣaṃ caivānumānya ca |**

**	tad annaṃ prakired bhūmau dadyāc cāpaḥ sakṛt sakṛt || 2.240 ||**

brāhmaṇatṛptiṃ yāvat pavitrāṇi sūktāni yajūṃṣi sāmāni ca japitvā yad yad annaṃ viprair upabhuktaṃ tatas tata ekadeśaṃ kvacit pātre kṛtvopādāya pūrvaṃ japaṃ japitvā tṛptāḥ stheti viprān āmantrya taiś ca tṛptāḥ sma iti pratyuktaḥ śeṣam annaṃ yathā netuṃ manyante tathoktvā tatpātrastham annaṃ bhūmau prakiret | tato viprebhyaḥ sakṛt sakṛd apo dadyāt | vyāhṛtayaḥ sāvitrī "madhu vātā ṛtāyate" iti tryṛcaś ca pūrvajapaḥ sa yajñopavītinā kāryaḥ | yad āha jamadagniḥ |

	apasavyena kartavyaṃ sarvaṃ śrāddhaṃ yathāvidhi |

	sūktaṃ stotraṃ japaṃ muktvā viprāṇāṃ ca visarjanam || iti |

kātyāyanaḥ: "aśnatsu japed vyāhṛtipūrvāṃ gāyatrīṃ sapraṇavāṃ sakṛt trir vā rakṣoghnīḥ pitṛmantrān puruṣasūktam apratiratham anyāni ca pavitrāṇi" | **[502]** kṛṇuṣva pāja [RV 3.4.23] ityādyā rakṣoghnāḥ | pitṛmantrā udīratām avara [RV 7.6.17] ityādayaḥ | baudhāyanaḥ |

	rakṣoghnāni ca sāmāni svadhāvanti yajūṃṣi ca |

	madhvṛco 'tha pavitrāṇi śrāvayed āśayāñ śanaiḥ ||

manuḥ |

	svādhyāyaṃ śrāvayet pitrye dharmaśāstrāṇi caiva hi |

	ākhyānānītihāsāṃś ca purāṇāni khilāni ca ||

	brahmaviṣṇvarkarudrāṇāṃ stotrāṇi vividhāni ca |

	indreśasomayuktāni pāvamānīś ca śaktitaḥ ||

	bṛhadrathantaraṃ tadvaj jyeṣṭhasāma ca rauravam |

	tathaiva śāntikādhyāyaṃ madhubrāhmaṇam eva ca ||

	maṇḍalabrāhmaṇaṃ tadvat prītikāri ca yat punaḥ |

	viprāṇām ātmanaś caiva tat sarvaṃ samudīrayet ||

viṣṇupurāṇe |

	rakṣoghnamantrapaṭhanaṃ bhūmer āstaraṇaṃ tilaiḥ |

	kṛtvā dhyeyāś ca pitaras ta eva dvijasattamāḥ ||

	pitā pitāmahaś caiva tathaiva prapitāmahaḥ |

	mama tṛptiṃ prayāntv agryāṃ vipradeheṣu saṃsthitāḥ ||

	pitā pitāmahaś caiva tathaiva praptāmahaḥ |

	mama tṛptiṃ prayāntv agnihomāpyāyitamūrtayaḥ ||

	pitā pitāmahaś caiva tathaiva praptāmahaḥ |

	tṛptiṃ prayāntu piṇḍena mayā dattena bhūtale ||

	pitā pitāmahaś caiva tathaiva prapitāmahaḥ |

	tṛptiṃ prayāntu me bhaktyā yan mayaitad udīritam ||

	mātāmahas tṛptim upaitu tasya tathā pitā tasya pitā ca yo 'nyaḥ |

	viśve ca devāḥ paramāṃ prayāntu tṛptiṃ praṇaśyantu ca yātudhānāḥ ||

	yajñeśvaro yajñasamastakavyabhoktāvyayātvā harir īśvaro 'tra |

	tat saṃnidhānād apayāntu sadyo rakṣāṃsy aśeṣāṇy asurāś ca sarve ||

vāyupurāṇe |

	saptārciṣaṃ pravakṣyāmi sarvakāmapradaṃ śubham |

	svargāpavargasopānaṃ pitṝṇāṃ ca vimuktaya ||

**[503]**	amūrtīnāṃ samūrtīnāṃ pitṝṇāṃ dīptatejasām |

	namasyāmi sadā teṣāṃ dhyāyināṃ yogacakṣuḍām ||

	indrādīnāṃ janetāro dakṣamārīcayos tathā |

	saptarṣīṇāṃ tathānyeṣāṃ tān namasyāmi kāmadān ||

	manvādīnāṃ janetāraḥ sūryācandamasos tathā |

	tān namasyāmi sarvān vai pitṝn apsuṣadas tathā ||

	nakṣatrāṇāṃ grahāṇāṃ ca vāyvagnyoś ca pitṝn atha |

	dyāvāpṛthivyoś ca sadā namasyāmi kṛtāñjaliḥ ||

	devarṣīṇāṃ janetāraḥ sarvadevanamaskṛtāḥ |

	bhrātaraḥ sarvabhūtānāṃ tān namasye pitāmahān ||

	prajāpateḥ kaśyapāya somāya varuṇāya ca |

	yogīśvarebhyaś ca sadā namasyāmi kṛtāñjaliḥ ||

	namo gaṇebhyaḥ saptabhyas tathā lokeṣu saptasu |

	svayaṃbhuve namasyāmi brahmaṇe yogacakṣuṣe ||

	ity etad uktaṃ saptārcir brahmarṣigaṇapūjitam |

	pavitraṃ paramaṃ hy etac chrīmad rakṣovināśanam || iti |

śeṣānujñāpane viśeṣam āha śaunakaḥ: "tṛptāñ jñātvā madhumatīḥ śrāvayed akṣannamīmadanteti ca saṃpannaṃ pṛṣṭvā yad yad annam upabhuktaṃ tataḥ sthālīpākena saha piṇḍārtham uddhṛtya śeṣaṃ nivedayed abhimate 'numate vā" iti | asyārthaḥ — śrāddhe bhoktṝṃs tāṃs tṛptān viditvā madhu vātā ṛtāyata iti tryṛcam akṣannamīmadanta iti caikām ṛcaṃ rāhūgaṇagautamadṛṣṭām indradai(de)vatyāṃ paṅktiṃ japitvā saṃpannam iti brāhmaṇān pṛṣṭvā saṃpannam iti taiḥ pratyukta yad yad annaṃ tair brāhmaṇair bhuktaṃ tatas tataḥ sthālīpākād annād ekadeśaṃ piṇḍārthaṃ pātrāntare piṇḍapitṛyajñasthālīpākena sahoddhṛtya brāhmaṇān anujñāpayaty avaśiṣṭam annaṃ kiṃ kriyatām iti | tatas tasminn anne brāhmaṇair abhimate svīkṛte vipragṛhaṃ prati tat prāpaṇiyam | atha jñātibhiḥ sahopabhujyatām ity anumanyante tadā tathaiva kuryād iti | **[504]** manuḥ |

	tato bhuktavatāṃ teṣām annaśeṣaṃ nivedayet |

	yathā brūyus tathā kuryād anujñātas tu tair dvijaiḥ ||

mārkaṇḍeyaḥ |

	praṣṭavyā brāhmaṇā bhaktyā bhūniviṣṭena jānunā |

	tṛptā bhavantaḥ saṃpannaṃ bhavatāṃ kaścid eva tu ||

manuḥ |

	sārvavarṇikam annādyaṃ saṃnīyāplāvya vāriṇā |

	samutsṛjed bhuktavatām agrato vikiren bhuvi ||

saṃnayanam ekatra pātre grahaṇam |

	asaṃskṛtapramītānāṃ tyāgināṃ kulayoṣitām |

	ucchiṣṭaṃ bhāgadheyaṃ syād darbheṣu vikiraś ca yaḥ ||

	ucchoṣaṇaṃ bhūmigatam ajihmasyāśaṭhasya ca |

	dāsavargasya tat pitryaṃ bhāgadheyaṃ pracakṣate ||

bhāgadheyaṃ bhāgaḥ | tataś cānupanītapramītāṃś ca svakulotpannāñ jantūṃs tathā kulayoṣitprabhṛtīnām atyājyānāṃ ye tyāginas tāṃś coddiśya viprabhojanapātrastham annaṃ darbheṣu ca yo vikiras tad ubhayaṃ pṛthak pṛthak tyājyam ity arthaḥ siddho bhavati | yaś ca (yac ca) bhūmigataṃ viprocchiṣṭaṃ tad ajihmāyāśaṭhāya mṛtāya dāsavargāya saṃkalpanīyam | vasiṣṭhas tu |

	ucchoṣaṇaṃ bhūmigataṃ vikiraṃ lepamodakam |

	anupreteṣu visṛjed aprajānām anāyuṣām || iti |

preteṣu pitrādiṣi ye 'nupretā anumṛtā ye ca svakule 'prajaso 'lpāyuṣaś ca tān uddiśyocchoṣaṇādi dadyāt | tathā |

	prāk saṃskārāt pramītānāṃ sapreṣyāṇām iti śrutiḥ |

	bhāgadheyaṃ manuḥ prāha ucchiṣṭocchoṣaṇe ubhe ||

pātragatam ucchiṣṭam | bhūmigatam ucchoṣaṇam | tataś cāsaṃskṛtapramītebhyaḥ sapreṣyebhya iti coddeśaḥ kārya iti siddhaṃ bhavati | vaiśvadevikabrāhmaṇavikire gobhiloktamantraḥ |

	asomapāś ca ye devā yajñabhāgavivarjitāḥ |

	teṣām annaṃ pradāsyāmi vikiraṃ vaiśadevikam ||

pitryabrāhmaṇasaṃbandhivikiraviṣaye bṛhaspatiḥ |

	upaspṛṣṭodakānāṃ tu brāhmaṇānāṃ tadagrataḥ |

	sodakaṃ vikired annaṃ mantram enam udāharet ||

**[505]**	anagnidagdhā ye jīvā ye 'pi dagdhāḥ kule mama |

	bhūmau dattena tṛpyantu tṛptā yāntu parāṃ gatim ||

iti bṛhaspatimate vikira ācamanānantaram | anyamate tu prāg evācamanāt | kātyāyanaḥ punar etaṃ mantram āha |

	ye agnidagdhā ye anagnidagdhā jīvā jātāḥ kule mama |

	bhūmau dattena tṛpyantu yāntu parāṃ gatim || iti |

mārkaṇḍeyaḥ |

	nnaṃ satṛṇam abhyukṣya māmekṣeṣṭheti mantrataḥ |

	udaṅmukhānāṃ viprāṇāṃ purataḥ sodakaṃ tataḥ ||

	annaṃ tu vikired bhaktyā bhṛtyabhāgas tu sa smṛtaḥ ||

atrānnavikire mantraḥ | na tu prokṣaṇe | tṛṇam atra darbhāḥ, "darbheṣu vikiraś ca yaḥ" iti vacanāt | marīciḥ |

	śrāddheṣu vikiraṃ datvā yo nācāmen matibhramāt |

	pitaras tasya ṣaṇmāsān bhavaty ucchiṣṭabhojinaḥ || 1.239, 240 ||

	**sarvam annam upādāya satilaṃ dakṣiṇāmukhaḥ |**

**	ucchiṣṭasaṃnidhau piṇḍān dadyād dhi pitṛyajñavat || 1.241 ||**

prakṛtaṃ sarvaprakāram annaṃ stokaśaḥ stokaśaḥ kvacit pātra upādāyoddhṛtya piṇḍapitṛyajñavidhānena cānnamayān piṇḍān dadyāt | satilaṃ dakṣiṇāmukha iti pitṛyajñād viśeṣaḥ | ucchiṣṭasaṃnidhau nāgnisaṃnidhāv ity arthaḥ | atriḥ |

	pitṝṇām āsanasthānām agratas triṣv aratniṣu |

	ucchiṣṭasaṃnidhānaṃ tan nocchiṣṭāsanasaṃnidhau ||

jātūkarṇyaḥ |

	vyāmamātraṃ samuddhṛtya piṇḍāṃs tatra pradāpayet |

	yatropaspṛśatāṃ vāpi prāpnuvanti na bindavaḥ ||

bhāskarasmṛtau |

	viprāṇāṃ bāhumātreṇa piṇḍadānaṃ vidhīyate ||

manuḥ |

	upalipte sucau deśe sthānaṃ kurvīta saikatam |

	maṇḍalaṃ caturaśraṃ vā dakṣiṇāvanataṃ mahat ||

	ekadarbheṇa tanmadhyam ullikhet triś ca taṃ tyajet |

	tasmin sthāne tato darbhān ekamūlaśikhān bahūn |

	dakṣiṇāgrān udakpādān sarvāṃs tān stṛṇuyāt samam || **[506]**

kātyāyanaḥ: "tṛptāñ jñātvānnaṃ prakīrya sakṛt sakṛd apo datvā pūrvavad gāyatrīṃ japtvā madhumatīr madhu madhv iti ca tṛptāḥ stheti pṛcchati | tṛptāḥ sma ity anujñātaḥ śeṣam annam anujñāpya sarvam annam ekata uddhṛtyocchiṣṭasamīpe darbheṣu trīn piṇḍān avanijya dadyād ācānteṣv ity eke" | brahmāṇḍapurāṇe |

	savyottarābhyāṃ pāṇibhyāṃ kuryād ullekhanaṃ dvijaḥ |

	pragharṣaṇaṃ tataḥ kuryāc chrāddhakarmaṇy atandritaḥ ||

	khaṇḍanaṃ peṣaṇaṃ caiva tathaivollekhanaṃ budhaḥ |

	sakṛd eva pitṝṇāṃ syād devānāṃ ca trir ucyate ||

ullekhanaṃ piṇḍanirvapaṇapradeśe lekhākaraṇam | vāyupurāṇāt |

	sakṛd evāstared darbhān piṇḍārthaṃ dakṣiṇāmukhaḥ |

	prāg dakṣiṇāgrān prayato dadyāt piṇḍān anantaram ||

tathā |

	madhusarpistilayutāṃs trīn piṇḍān nirvaped budhaḥ |

	jānu kṛtvā tathā savyaṃ bhūmau pitṛparāyaṇaḥ ||

jātūkarṇyaḥ |

	upamūlaṃ samāstīrya darbhān ucchiṣṭasaṃnidhau |

	kṛtvāvanejanaṃ dadyāt trīn piṇḍāṃs tu yathāvidhi ||

sumantuḥ |

	śrāddhasevanakāle tu pāṇinaikena dīyate |

	tarpaṇe tūbhayaṃ kuryād eṣa eva vidhiḥ smṛtaḥ || iti |

bṛhaspatiḥ |

	sarvasmāt prakṛtādannāt (?) piṇḍān madhutilānvitān |

	pitṛmātāmahādīnāṃ dadyād gṛhyavidhānataḥ ||

marīciḥ |

	pātrāṇāṃ khaḍgapātreṇa piṇḍadānaṃ vidhīyate |

	rājatodumbarābhyāṃ vā hastenaivātha vā punaḥ ||

udumbaraṃ tāmramayam | pāraskaraḥ |

	arghadāne 'tha saṃkalpe piṇḍadāne tathākṣaye |

	gotrasaṃbandhanāmāni yathāvat pratipādayet ||

gṛhyakṛt: "yadi nāmāni na vidyāt svadhā pitṛbhyaḥ pṛthivīsadbhya iti prathamaṃ piṇḍaṃ nindyāt | svadhā pitṛbhyo 'ntarikṣaṣadbhya iti dvitīyam | svadhā pitṛbhyo diviṣadbhya iti tṛtīyam" | **[507]** viṣṇudharmottare |

	piṇḍanirvapaṇaṃ kāryaṃ kuśābhāve vicakṣaṇaiḥ |

	kāśeṣu rājan dūrvāsu pavitre te pare smṛte ||

vyāsaḥ |

	brūyāc chrāddheṣu sāvitrīṃ piṇḍe piṇḍe samāhitaḥ |

	somāyeti ca vaktavyaṃ tathā pitṛmateti ca ||

marīciḥ |

	ārdrāmalakamātrāṃs tu piṇḍān kurvīta pārvaṇe |

	ekoddiṣṭe bilvamātraṃ piṇḍam ekaṃ tu nirvapet ||

	navaśrāddhe sthūlataraṃ tasmād api tu nirvapet ||

	navaśrāddhe sthūlataraṃ tasmād api tu nirvapet |

	tasmād api sthūlataram aśauce prativāsaram ||

manuḥ |

	nyupya piṇḍān pitṛbhyas tu prayato vidhipūrvakam |

	teṣu piṇḍeṣu taṃ hastaṃ nirmṛjyāl lepabhāginām ||

lepabhāgina āha matsyapurāṇam |

	lepabhājaś caturthādyāḥ pitrādyāḥ piṇḍabhāginaḥ |

	piṇḍadaḥ saptamas teṣāṃ sāpiṇḍyaṃ sāptapauruṣam ||

viṣṇuḥ: "atra pitaro mādayadhvam iti darbhamūle karāvagharṣaṇam" | vyāghraḥ |

	darbhamūleṣu nirmṛjyād dhastalepaṃ samāhitaḥ |

	adbhiḥ prakṣālya tat pātraṃ pratipiṇḍaṃ tu pūrvavat ||

	kṛtvāvanejanaṃ kuryāt piṇḍapātram adhomukham ||

manuḥ |

	ācamyodak parāvṛtya trir āyamya śanair asūn |

	ṣaḍṛtūṃś ca namaskuryāt pitṝn eva ca mantravit ||

brahmāṇḍapurāṇāt |

	kṛṣṇāc caiva tilāt tailaṃ yatnāt suparirakṣitam |

	bilvapātreṇa dātavyaṃ pitṛbhyo 'bhyañjanaṃ budhaiḥ ||

tilād iti jātyabhiprāyam ekavacanam | tathā |

	apasavyaṃ pitṛbhyas tu dadyād añjanam uttamam |

	nāmāny uccārya sarveṣāṃ vastrārthaṃ sūtram eva ca ||

	kṣaumasūtraṃ navaṃ dadyād diśet kārpāsakaṃ tathā |

	pattorṇaṃ paṭṭasūtraṃ ca kauśeyaṃ ca visarjayet ||

kṣaumam atasīprabhavam | pattorṇaṃ dhautakauśeyam | paṭṭasūtraṃ prasiddham | kauśeyaṃ trasarīsūtram | **[508]** śaṅkhaḥ |

	ūrṇāsūtraṃ pradātavyaṃ kārpāsam atha vā navam |

	daśāṃ vivarjayet prājño yady apy ahatavastrajā ||

āśvalāyanaḥ: "vāso dadyād daśām ūrṇāstukāṃ vā" iti | tataś ca vihitapratiṣiddhatvā daśāyā vikalpaḥ | vyāghraḥ |

	gandhapuṣpādi dhūpaṃ ca dīpaṃ ca vinivedayet |

	etad vaḥ pitaro vāso daśā dadyāt pṛthak pṛthak ||

bṛhaspatiḥ |

	dhūpadīpair mālyagandhais tathā vastrāñ janādinā |

	samabhyarcyodapātraṃ tu teṣām upari nikṣipet ||

brahmapurāṇāt |

	madhu vājyaṃ jalaṃ cārghaṃ puṣpaṃ dhūpaṃ vilepanam |

	baliṃ dadyāc ca vidhivat piṇḍo 'ṣṭāṅgo bhaved yathā ||

purāṇāt |

	yat kiṃcit pacyate gehe bhakṣyaṃ bhojyam agarhitam |

	anivedya na bhoktavyaṃ piṇḍamūle kathaṃcana ||

viṣṇuḥ: "piṇḍānāṃ vikiraṃ kṛtvārghapuṣpadhūpānulepanānnādyabhakṣyabhojyaṃ nivedayet | udapātraṃ madhughṛtatilaiḥ saṃyuktaṃ ca" | manuḥ |

	avijighrec ca tān piṇḍān yathā nyuptān samāhitaḥ || 1.241|

	**mātāmahānām apy evaṃ dadyād ācamanaṃ tataḥ |**

mātāmahānām apy evaṃ pitṛvat piṇḍadānaṃ kuryāt | tato brāhmaṇān ācāmayet | viṣnuḥ: "udaṅmukheṣv ācamanaṃ datvā tataḥ prāṅmukheṣu dadyāt" | tataś ca suprokṣitam iti śrāddhadeśaṃ prokṣya darbhapāṇiḥ sarvaṃ kuryāt | nārāyaṇaḥ |

	acālayitvā tat pātraṃ svasti kurvanti ye dvijāḥ |

	tad annam asurair bhuktaṃ nirāśaiḥ pitṛbhir gataiḥ ||

bṛhaspatiḥ |

	bhājaneṣu tu tiṣṭhatsu svasti kurvanti ye dvijāḥ |

	nirāśāḥ pitaras teṣāṃ śaptvā yānti yathāgatam ||

jātūkarṇyaḥ |

	pātrāṇi cālayec chrāddhe svayaṃ śiṣyo 'tha vā sutaḥ |

	na strībhir na ca bālena na sajātyā kadācana ||

	**svastivācyaṃ tataḥ kuryād akṣayyodakam eva ca || 1.142 ||**

**	datvā tu dakṣiṇāṃ śaktyā svadhākāram udāharet |**

**[509]**	**vācyatām ity anujñātaḥ prakṛtebhyaḥ svadhocyatām || 1.243 ||**

**	**

**	brūyur astu svadhety ukte bhūmau siñcet tato jalam |**

tato viprācamād ūrdhvaṃ svastivācanaṃ kuryāt | svasti bhavanto bruvantv iti viprān vācayed ity arthaḥ | taiś ca svastīty ukte 'kṣayyodakaṃ kuryāt | ṣaṣṭhyantagotrasaṃbandhanāmānantaram akṣayyam astv ity uktvā vigrahas teṣu jalaṃ niṣiñced ity arthaḥ | tato yathāśakti dakṣiṇāṃ datvā svadhākāraṃ kārayet svadhāṃ vācayiṣya iti viprān anujñāpayed ity arthaḥ | taiś ca vācyatām ity anujñātaḥ prakṛtebhyaḥ pitrādibhyaḥ svadhocyatām iti viprānujñāpane kṛte 'stu svadheti tair ukte bhūmau jalaṃ siñcet | śātātapaḥ |

	abhipretārthasiddhyartham iṣṭakāmāṃs tu vācayet |

	dīrghāḥ sūryahayā nadyo viṣṇos trīṇi padāni ca ||

	evam eṣāṃ praṇāmena dīrgham āyur avāpnuyāt |

	apāṃ madhye sthitā devāḥ sarvam apsu pratiṣthitam ||

	brāhmaṇasya kare nyastāḥ śivā āpo bhavantu naḥ |

	lakṣmīr vasati puṣpeṣu lakṣmīr vasati puṣkare ||

	lakṣmīr vaset sadā some saumanasyaṃ sadāstu me |

	akṣataṃ cāstu me puṇyaṃ śāntiḥ puṣṭir dhṛtis tu me ||

	yad yac chreyaskaraṃ loke tat tad astu sadā mama |

	dakṣiṇāyāṃ tu sarvatra bahu deyaṃ tathāstu naḥ ||

	evam astv iti tair vācyaṃ mūrdhnā grāhyaṃ tu tena tat ||

brahmapurāṇāt |

	ācānteṣūdakaṃ dadyāt puṣpāṇi sayavāni ca |

	yavo 'sīti paṭhan mantraṃ śraddhābhaktisamanvitaḥ ||

	dadyāt tathākṣayyajalaṃ tilājyamadhusaṃyutam |

	sapavitrān kuśān bhūmāv āstīrya satilāṃs tathā ||

brahmāṇḍapurāṇāt |

	sauvarṇaraupyapātrāṇi manojñāni śubhāni ca |

	hastyaśvarathayānāni samṛddhāni gṛhāṇi ca ||

	upānatpādukāchatracāmarāṇy ajināni ca |

	yajñeṣu dakṣiṇā puṇyā seti saṃcintayet sadā ||

yā yajñadakṣiṇā saiveyam iti buddhiḥ kāryety arthaḥ | **[510]**

	daridro 'pi yathāśakti dadyād vipreṣu dakṣiṇām |

tathā |

	loke śreṣṭhatamaṃ sarvaṃ manasaś cāpi yat priyam |

	sarvaṃ pitṝṇāṃ dātavyaṃ teṣām evākṣayārthinā ||

	anantam akṣayyaṃ svargyaṃ rājataṃ dānam ucyate |

	pitṝṇāṃ tena dānena satputrās tārayanty uta ||

mārkaṇḍeyaḥ |

	api syāt sa kule 'smākaṃ kaścit puruṣasattamaḥ |

	prasūyamānāṃ yo dhenuṃ dadyād brāhmaṇapuṃgave ||

	api syāt sa kule 'smākaṃ dadyāt kṛṣṇājinaṃ ca yaḥ |

	suvarṇaśṛṅgaṃ sakhuraṃ vidhinā mānavottamaḥ ||

pāraskaraḥ |

	ekapaṅktyupaviṣṭānāṃ viprāṇāṃ śrāddhakarmaṇi |

	bhakṣyaṃ bhojyaṃ samaṃ deyaṃ dakṣiṇā tv anusārataḥ ||

pātrānusārata ity arthaḥ | vṛddhagautamaḥ |

	dakṣiṇāṃ pitṛdevebhyo dadyāt pūrvaṃ tato dvayoḥ |

pitaro devā yeṣāṃ te pitṛdevāḥ pitṛdevatyāḥ śrāddhabhoktāra ity arthaḥ | tebhyaḥ pūrvaṃ dakṣiṇāṃ dadyāt tato dvayor vaiśvadevikaviprayor ity arthaḥ | dvayor iti caturthyarthe saptamī | tataś ca brāhmaṇebhya eva dakṣiṇā deyā na pitrādibhyaḥ | tathā ca devalaḥ |

	ācāntebhyo dvijebhyaś ca prayacched atha dakṣiṇām |

	hiraṇyaratnabhogānām anyeṣāṃ ca svaśaktitaḥ ||

evaṃ ca sati dakṣiṇāśabdasāmañjasyaṃ bhavati | yac ca vākyam "pitṛbhyo dakṣiṇā deyā" iti tat pitṛdevatyabrāhmaṇasaṃbandhaparam | anyathā brāhmaṇānāṃ dakṣiṇāsvāmyaṃ na syāt | jamadagniḥ |

	sarvaṃ karmāpasavyena dakṣiṇādānavarjanam |
