apasavyaṃ tatrāpi bhagavān matsyo mene | kātyāyanaḥ: "svadhāvācanīyān sapavitrān kuśān āstīrya svadhāṃ vācayiṣya iti pṛcchati vācyatām ity ukte pitṛbhyaḥ pitāmahebhyaḥ prapitāmahebhyaḥ svadhocyatām ity anujñāpitair viprair astu svadhety ucyamāna ūrjaṃ vahantīty apo niṣiñcet sapavitreṣu kuśeṣu" || 1.242, 243 ||

	**viśve devāś ca prīyantāṃ vipraiś cokta idaṃ japet || 1.244 ||**

**[511]**

**	dātāro no 'bhivardhantāṃ vedāḥ saṃtatir eva ca |**

**	śraddhā ca no mā vyagamad bahu deyaṃ ca no 'stv iti || 1. 245 ||**

viśve devāḥ prīyantām iti kartrā vipraiś cokte dātāro no 'bhivardhantām iti ślokaṃ japet | purāṇāt |

	savyavad divyatīrthena yavodakam atho dadat |

	viśve devāś ca yajñe 'smin prīyantām ity udāharet ||

matsyapurāṇe |

	tataḥ svadhāvācanakaṃ viśve(śva)deveṣu codakam |

	datvāśiṣo 'pi gṛhṇīyād dvijebhyaḥ prākmukho budhaḥ ||

	aghorāḥ pitaraḥ santu santv ity ukte punar dvijaiḥ |

	gotraṃ tathā vardhatāṃ nas tathety uktaś ca taiḥ punaḥ ||

	dātāro no 'bhivardhantāṃ vedāḥ saṃtatir eva ca |

	śraddhā ca no mā vyagamad bahu deyaṃ ca no 'stv iti ||

	etāḥ satyāśiṣaḥ santu santv ity uktaś ca taiḥ punaḥ ||

atra baudhāyanena "dātāro no 'bhivardhantām" iti ślokānantaram,

	annaṃ ca no bahu bhaved atithīṃś ca labhemahi |

	yācitāraś ca naḥ santu mā ca yāciṣma kaṃcana ||

iti mantra āmnātaḥ || 1.244, 245 ||

	**ity uktvā tu priyā vācaḥ praṇipatya visarjayet |**

**	vāje vāja iti prītaḥ pitṛpūrvaṃ visarjanam || 1.246 ||**

iti pūrvoktaṃ mantram uktvā brāhmaṇānāṃ priyā vācaś coktvā tāṃś ca namaskṛtya prītaḥ san "vāje vāje" ity anayā triṣṭubhā vasiṣṭhadṛṣṭayā pipradevatyayā visarjayet | atra pitṛvisrajanaṃ pūrvam | atra matsyapurāṇam |

	tatas tān agrataḥ sthitvā pratigṛhyodapātrakam |

	vāje vāja iti japan kuśāgreṇa visarjayet ||

vipravisarjanaṃ copavītinā kāryam, "upavīryo svadheti visṛjed astu svadheti visṛjet | asstu svadheti vā" iti śaunakavacanāt | pratibrāhmaṇaṃ mantrāvṛttiḥ | kuśāgrasparśarūpavisargasya sarvavipraviṣayasya yugapat kartum aśakyatvāt | **[512]** bṛhaspatiḥ |

	adya me saphalaṃ janma bhavatpādābhivandanāt |

	adya me vaṃśajāḥ sarve gatās te 'nugrahād divam ||

	atra śākādidānena kleśitā ye mayedṛśāḥ |

	tatkleśajātaṃ cittena vismṛtya kṣantum arhatha || 1.246 ||

	**yasmiṃs te saṃsravāḥ pūrvam arghyapātre niveśitāḥ |**

**	pitṛpātraṃ tad uttānaṃ kṛtvā viprān visarjayet || 1.247 ||**

yasminn arghyapātre 'rghyasaṃsrāvāḥ pūrvaṃ sthāpitās tat pātraṃ pūrvam uttānaṃ kāryaṃ tataḥ prāg uktaṃ vipravisarjanaṃ kāryam | yeṣāṃ gṛhe pitṛpātram uttānam eva pātrāntareṇa pihitaṃ sthāpanīyam eveti vihitaṃ tanmatam āśritya dakṣiṇādānānantaram uktaṃ brāhmāṇḍapurāṇe |

	tataḥ saṃsrāvapātrebhyo jalam ādāya cārpitam |

	ūrjaṃ vahantīś ca japan piṇḍāṃś cāpy avasiñcati || 1.247 ||

	**pradakṣiṇam anuvrajya bhuñjīta pitṛsevitam |**

**	brahmacārī bhavet tāṃ tu rajanīṃ brāhmaṇaiḥ saha || 1.248 ||**

tān viprān pradakṣiṇīkṛtya gacchato 'nugamya pitṛsevitaṃ śrāddhāvaśiṣṭam evānnaṃ bhuñjīta | śrāddhakartā bhoktāraś ca tāṃ rātriṃ brahmacāriṇo bhaveyuḥ | matsyapurāṇāt |

	bahiḥ pradakṣiṇaṃ kuryāt padāny aṣṭāv anuvrajet |

	bandhuvargeṇa sahitaḥ putrabhāryāsamanvitaḥ ||

	nivṛtya praṇipatyātha paryukṣyāgniṃ sa mantravit |

	vaiśvadevaṃ prakurvīta naityakaṃ balim eva ca ||

bahir gṛhād bahir ity arthaḥ | kātyāyanaḥ: "vāje vāje iti visṛjyāmāvājasya ity anuvrajya pradakṣiṇīkṛtya praviśet" | manuḥ |

	prakṣālya hastāv ācamya jñātiprāyaṃ prakalpayet |

	jñātibhyaḥ śaktito datvā bāndhavān api pūjayet ||

	tato gṛhabaliṃ kuryād iti dharmo vyavasthitaḥ || **[413]**

jñātayaḥ pitṛpakṣyāḥ | bāndhavā mātṛpakṣyāḥ | gṛhabaliśabdena sakalam eva vaiśvadevādi karmopalakṣyate | purāṇāt |

	tato visarjayed viprān praṇipatya ca bhaktitaḥ |

	ādvāram anugacchec ca āgacchec cānumoditaḥ ||

mārkaṇḍeyaḥ |

	tato nityakriyāṃ kuryād bhojayec ca tathātithim |

	nityakriyāṃ pitṝṇāṃ ca kecid icchanti mānavāḥ ||

	pitṝṇāṃ na tathaivānye śeṣaṃ pūrvavad ācaret |

	pṛthakpākena cety anye kecit pūrvaṃ tu pūrvavat ||

	tatas tad annaṃ bhuñjīta saha bhṛtyādibhir naraḥ ||

nityakriyā vaiśvadevādiḥ | smṛtyantaram |

	ātithyarahitaṃ śrāddham āsuraṃ sati saṃbhave |

	dehi dehīti vaktavye bhoktur doṣo 'nyathā bhavet ||

devalaḥ |

	nirvartya pitṛmedhaṃ tu dīpaṃ pracchādya pāṇinā |

	ācamya pāṇī prakṣālya jñātīñ śeṣeṇa toṣayet ||

brahmapurāṇe |

	bhaginyo bāndhavāḥ pūjyāḥ śrāddheṣu ca sadaiva hi ||

tathā |

	bandimāgadhasūtāś ca tauryatrikavidas tathā |

	alabdhalābhāḥ śrāddheṣu nāśayanti mahad yaśaḥ ||

	tasmāt te 'pi vibhoktavyāḥ sakalaṃ ca vibhajya ca ||

gītanṛttavādyāni tauryatrikam | devalaḥ |

	śrāddhaṃ datvā tu yo vipro na bhuṅkte 'tha kadācana |

	devā havir na gṛhṇanti kavyāni pitaras tathā ||

āpastambaḥ: "sarvataḥ samavadāyottareṇa yajuṣā grāsārdhaparārdhaṃ prāśnāti" | etat saṃkalpitaikādaśyādyupavāsaviṣayaṃ bhojanavirodhirogaviṣayaṃ ca | "prāṇe niviṣṭo 'mṛtaṃ juhomi brahmaṇi ma ātmāmṛtatvāya" ity uttaraṃ yajuḥ | tataś ca "bhuñjīta pitṛsevitam" ity anena bhojanaṃ kartavyam eveti niyamyate | tatrāmiṣādi pitṛsevitam apy aupavasathye 'hany agnimatā na bhakṣyam | "amāṣam amāṃsaṃ vrataṃ vratayīta" iti śruteḥ | anagnis tu bhakṣayed eva | yat punaḥ,

	āsaptamaṃ kulaṃ hanti śiro'bhyaṅge caturdaśī |

	māṃsāśane pañcadaśī kāmadharme tathāṣṭamī || **[514]**

ityādi pañcadaśyāṃ māṃsavarjanaṃ tad rāgaprāptaṃ māṃsabakṣaṇaṃ vārayati | na vaidham | pitṛsevitabhojanavidhiś ca sakṛdbhakṣaṇamātreṇaiva caritārtho bhavatīti tadabhyāso rāgīya eva | viṣṇupurāṇe |

	śrāddhe niyukto bhuktvā vā bhojayitvā niyojya ca |

	vyavāyī retaso garbhe majjayaty ātmanaḥ pitṝn ||

vyavāyo maithunam | śātātapaḥ |

	śrāddhaṃ kṛtvā pare śrāddhe bhuñjate ye tu jihmalāḥ |

	patanti pitaras teṣāṃ luptapiṇḍodakakriyāḥ ||

tathā |

	punarbhojanam adhvānaṃ bhārādhyayanamaithunam |

	dānaṃ pratigrahaṃ homaṃ śrāddhaṃ bhuktvāṣṭa varjayet ||

yamaḥ |

	daśakṛtvaḥ pibec cāpo gāyatryā śrāddhabhug dvijaḥ |

	tataḥ saṃdhyām upāsīta japec ca juhuyād api ||

atra sakṛn mantraḥ, kāryāviśeṣāt | yatra hi mantrakāryaṃ śiṣyate tatra karmavṛttau mantro 'py āvartate | yathā nirvāpyājyagrahaṇadhūpacchedanamantrāḥ | tair hi nirvāpādisaṃskāryaṃ dravyaṃ prakāśyate | tadbhedād yuktā mantrāvṛttiḥ | matsyapurāṇe |

	punarbhojanam adhvānaṃ dyūtam āyāsamaithunam |

	svādhyāyaṃ kalahaṃ caiva divā svapnaṃca sarvadā ||

brahmapurāṇe |

	astāste ca tataḥ sūrye viprapātrāṇi cāmbhasi |

	nikṣipet prayato bhūtvā sarvāṇy adhomukhāni ca ||

	dvitīye 'hani sarvaṃ ca bhāṇḍaprakṣālanaṃ tathā || 1.248 ||

_sarveṣāṃ śrāddhānāṃ prakṛtibhūtaṃ pārvaṇaṃ śrāddhaṃ vidhāyedānīṃ tadvikṛtyātmakam ābhyudayikaṃ śrāddhaṃ vidhātum āha |_

	**evaṃ pradakṣiṇaṃ kṛtvā vṛddhau nāndīmukhān pitṝn |**

**	yajeta dadhikarkandhumiśrāḥ piṇḍā yavaiḥ kriyāḥ || 1.249 ||**

vṛddhau vivāhādau nāndīmukhasaṃjñakān pitṝn evaṃ pārvaṇoktaśrāddhaprakāreṇa yajeta | pradakṣiṇaṃ kṛtvā pradakṣiṇaṃ kurvann ity arthaḥ | atra paurvāparyam avivakṣitam | saṃmīlya hasatītivat | atrāparo viśeṣaḥ karkandhumiśrāḥ piṇḍā yavaiś ca tilaiś ca kāryāḥ kriyā iti | karkandhu badaram | **[515]** atra viṣṇupurāṇam |

	kanyāputravivāheṣu praveśe navaveśmani |

	nāmakarmaṇi bālānāṃ cūḍākarmādike tathā ||

	sīmantonnayane caiva putrādimukhadarśane |

	nāndīmukhaṃ pitṛgaṇaṃ pūjayet prayato gṛhī ||

	yugmāṃs tu prāṅmukhān viprān bhojayen manujeśvara ||

matsyapurāṇam |

	utsavānandasaṃtāne yajñodvāhādimaṅgale |

	mātaraḥ prathamaṃ pūjyāḥ pitaras tadanantaram ||

	tato mātāmahāḥ pūjyā viśve devās tathaiva ca ||

śātātapaḥ |

	nāniṣṭvā tu pitṝñ śrāddhe karma vaidikam ācaret |

	tisro 'pi mātaraḥ pūrvaṃ pūjanīyāḥ prayatnataḥ ||

	akṛtvā mātṛyāgaṃ tu yaḥ śrāddhaṃ pariveṣayet |

	tasya krodhasamāviṣṭā hiṃsāṃ kurvanti mātaraḥ ||

brahmapurāṇe |

	karmaṇy athābhyudayike maṅgalyavati śobhane |

	janmany athopanayane vivāhe putrakasya ca ||

	pitṝn nāndīmukhān nāma tarpayed vidhipūrvakam ||

śātātapaḥ |

	mātṛśrāddhaṃ tu pūrvaṃ syāt pitṝṇāṃ tadanantaram |

	tato mātāmahānāṃ ca vṛddhau śrāddhatrayaṃ smṛtam ||

bhāskaraḥ |

	niṣekakāle some ca sīmantonnayane tathā |

	jñeyaṃ puṃsavane śrāddhaṃ karmāṅgaṃ vṛddhivat kṛtam ||

kātyāyanaḥ |

	vivāhādiḥ karmagaṇo ya ukto garbhādhānaṃ yasya śuśruma cānte |

	vivāhādāv ekam evātra kuryāc chrāddhaṃ nādau karmaṇaḥ karmaṇaḥ syāt ||

	ādhāne homayoś caiva vaiśvadeve tathaiva ca |

	balikarmaṇi darśe ca paurṇamāse tathaiva ca |

	navayajñe ca yajñajñā vadanty evaṃ manīṣiṇaḥ ||

	evam eva bhavec chrāddham eteṣu na pṛthak prthak |

	nāṣṭakāsu bhavec chrāddhaṃ na śrāddhe śrāddham iṣyate ||

purāṇāt |

	vaiśvadevavihīnaṃ tat kecid icchanti mānavāḥ |

	yugmās tatra dvijāḥ kāryās te pūjyāś ca pradakṣiṇam || **[516]**

vṛddhavasiṣṭhaḥ |

	pūrvedyur mātṛkaṃ śrāddhaṃ karmāhe paitṛkaṃ tathā |

	uttaredyuḥ prakurvīta mātāmahagaṇasya tu ||

vṛddhaśātātapaḥ |

	pṛthag dineṣv aśaktāś ced ekasminn eva vāsare |

	śrāddhatrayaṃ prakurvanti tantraṃ vā vaiśvadevikam ||

śātātapaḥ |

	pūrvāhṇe mātṛkaṃ śrāddhaṃ madhyāhne paitṛkaṃ smṛtam |

	tato mātāmahānāṃ tu vṛddhau śrāddhatrayaṃ smṛtam ||

vasiṣṭhaḥ |

	śrāddhatrayaṃ prakurvīta tantraṃ vā vaiśvadevikam |

	mātṛbhyaḥ kalpayet pūrvaṃ pitṛbhyas tadanantaram ||

	tato mātāmahānāṃ tu piṇḍān dadyāt krameṇa tu ||

kātyāyanaḥ |

	asakṛd yāni karmāṇi kriyeran karmakāribhiḥ |

	atiprayogaṃ naitāḥ syur mātaraḥ śrāddham eva ca ||

	gaṇaśaḥ kriyamāṇeṣu mātṛbhyaḥ pūjanaṃ sakṛt |

	sakṛd eva bhavec chrāddham ādau na pṛthagādiṣu ||

etac ca sarva eva pratyuddhāraḥ putrajanmanā vyākhyāta ity etadviṣayam | asya cāyam arthaḥ — sarva eva patitasya kṛtaprāyaścittasya pratyuddhāro jñātiparigrahaḥ putrajanmanā vyākhyātaḥ | putre jāte ye tasya jātakarmādayaḥ saṃskārās te sarve 'py asya kāryā iti | evaṃ ca jātakarmādīnāṃ saṃskārāṇāṃ yugapatkaraṇād gaṇaśaḥ kriyamāṇatvam |

	svapitṛbhyaḥ pitā dadyāt sutasaṃskārakāraṇāt |

	piṇḍān odvāhanāt teṣāṃ tasyābhāve tu tatkramāt ||

piṇḍān abhyudayaśrāddhe teṣāṃ putrāṇām odvāhanād ā vivāhāt pitā svapitṛbhyo dadyāt | tasya pitur abhāve tatkramāt | atra kramaśabdena pitur anantaro bhrātrādir lakṣyate | putravivāhe pituḥ śrāddhādikāraḥ kanyāputravivāheṣv ity anenokto voḍhur api pṛthagadhikāro nāniṣṭvā tu pitṝñ śrāddham ity anenoktas tena putravivāhe pitrā putreṇa ca vṛddhiśrāddhaṃ pṛthak kāryam | putreṇa ca,

	yebhya eva pitā dadyāt tebhyo dadyāt suto 'gnimān |

iti vidhim āśritya kartavyam | atra cāgnimadgrahaṇam adhikārimātropalakṣaṇārtham | ata eva samāvartane brahmacāriṇā jīvatpitṛkeṇa pitāmahādibhyaḥ śrāddhaṃ pradīyate | vṛddhavasiṣṭhaḥ |

**[517]**	mātṛśrāddhe tu viprāṇām alābhe pūjayed api |

	patiputrānvitā bhavyā yoṣito 'ṣṭau mudānvitāḥ ||

caturviṃśatimatāt |

	athābhyudayike prāpte devatāsthāpanaṃ smṛtam |

	jātidharmakulaśreṇilokānāṃ vṛddhikāraṇam ||

	tisraḥ pūjyāḥ pitus tisraḥ pūjyā mātāmahī tathā |

	ity etā mātaraḥ proktāḥ pitṛmātṛṣvasāṣṭamī ||

mātā pitāmahī prapitāmahīti tisraḥ pitṛpakṣe | mātāmahī mātuḥ pitāmahī mātuḥ prapitāmahīti tisro mātṛvarge | tathā mātṛṣvasā pitṛṣvasā cety aṣṭau mātaraḥ |

	brahmāṇyādyās tathā sapta durgākṣetragaṇādhipān |

	vṛddhyādau pūjayitvā tu paścān nāndīmukhān pitṝn ||

	mātṛpūrvān pitṝn pūjya tato mātāmahān api |

	mātāmahīs tataḥ kecid yugmā bhojyā dvijātayaḥ ||

kātyāyanaḥ |

	karmādiṣu tu sarveṣu mātaraḥ sagaṇādhipāḥ |

	pūjanīyāḥ prayatnena pūjitāḥ pūjayanti tāḥ ||

	pratimāsu ca śubhrāsu likhitā vā paṭādiṣū |

	api vākṣatapuñjeṣu naivedyaiś ca pṛthagvidhaiḥ ||

	kuḍyalagnā vasor dhārāḥ pañca dhārā ghṛtena tu |

	kārayet sapta dhārā vā nātinīcā na cocchritāḥ ||

	āyuṣyāṇi ca śāntyarthaṃ japtvā tatra samāhitaḥ ||

	*_additonal verses given in the edition_

	[lalitā ca umā gaurī ambikā salilāśrayā |

	bhagāhī ca bhagākṣī ca dhārāḥ sapta prakīrtitāḥ ||

	anumatiś ca rākā ca sinīvālī kuhūs tathā |

	dhātrī sarveśvarī caiva hy annaiśvarī tathaiva ca ||

	etās tu devatā nityaṃ bhaktagolakadevatāḥ |

	pūjyā hy akṣoṭaśākhāyām ekāntavāsinī sadā ||

	mṛttikāgolake pūjyo mahāgaṇapatir vibhuḥ |

	pañcāmṛtaṃ ghṛtābhyaktaṃ madhumāṃsaṃ dvitīyakam || iti | ]

āyuṣyāṇi ānobhadrīyādīni | mātaras tu |

	brahmāṇī caiva māheśī kaumārī vaiṣṇavī kramāt |

	vārāhī nārasiṃhy aindrī saptaitā mātaro matāḥ ||

yad vā |

	gaurī padmā śacī medhā sāvitrī vijayā jayā |

	devasenā svadhā svāhā mātaro lokamātaraḥ ||

**[518]**	dhṛtiḥ puṣṭis tathā tuṣṭir ātmadevatayā saha |

	apo 'rghyaṃ gandhapuṣpaṃ ca dhūpaṃ dīpaṃ nivedayet ||

brahmapurāṇāt |

	pūrvāhṇe daivike kāryaṃ śrāddham abhyudayārthinā |

	savyena copavītena ṛjudarbhaiś ca dhīmatā ||

savyaṃ pradakṣiṇam | tathā |

	yugmāṃs tu bhojayed vṛddhau brāhmaṇān niyataḥ śuciḥ |

	nāndīmukhās tu pitaras tṛpyantām iti vācayet ||

atriḥ |

	pūrvāhṇe vai bhaved vṛddhir vinā janmanimittakam |

	putrajanmani kurvīta śrāddhaṃ tātkālikaṃ budhaḥ ||

kātyāyanaḥ: "ābhyudayike pradakṣiṇam upacāraḥ pitryamantravarjaṃ japa ṛjavo darbhā yavais tilārthaḥ saṃpannam iti tṛptipraśno dadhibadarākṣatmiśrāḥ piṇḍāḥ nāndīmukhān pitṝn āvāhayiṣya iti pṛcchati | nāndīmukhāḥ pitaraḥ prīyantām ity akṣayyasthāne | nāndīmukhān pitṝn vācayiṣya iti pṛcchati | nāndīmukhāḥ pitaraḥ pitāmahāḥ prapitāmahāḥ prīyantām iti svadhāṃ prayuñjīta | yugmān āśayet" | tathā |

	ataḥ paraṃ pravakṣyāmi viśeṣa iha yo bhavet |

	prātar āmantritān viprān yugmān ubhayatas tathā ||

	upaveśya kuśān dadyād ṛjunaiva hi pāṇinā || iti |

prātar upaveśyety anvayaḥ | āmantraṇaṃ pūrvedyur eva | tathā |

	nipāto na hi savyasya jānuno vidyate kvacit |

	sadā paricared bhaktyā pitṝn apy atra devavat ||

	pitṛbhya iti datteṣu upaveśya kuśeṣu tān |

	gotranāmabhir āmantrya pitṝn arghyaṃ pradāpayet ||

	nātrāpasavyakaraṇaṃ na pitryaṃ tīrtham iṣyate |

	pātrāṇāṃ pūraṇādīni daive naiva hi kārayet ||

	jyeṣṭhottarakarān yugmān karāgrāgrapavitrakān |

	kṛtvārghyaṃ saṃpradātavyaṃ naikaikasyātra dīyate ||

dvayor dvayor brāhmaṇayor hastau melayitvārghyadānaṃ kāryam | tatra jyeṣṭhasya viprasya hasta uttaraḥ kāryaḥ | **[519]** tathā |

	madhu madhv iti yas tatra trir japo 'śitum icchatām |

	gāyatryanantaraṃ so 'tra madhumantravivarjitaḥ ||

	na cāśnatsu japed atra kadācit pitṛsaṃhitām |

	anya eva japaḥ kāryaḥ somasāmādikaḥ śubhaḥ ||

	yas tasya prakaro 'nnasya tilamān yavamāṃs tathā |

	ucchiṣṭasaṃnidhau so 'tra tṛpteṣu viparītakaḥ ||

	saṃpannam iti tṛptāḥ stha praśnasthāne vidhīyate |

	susaṃpannam iti prokte śeṣam annaṃ nivedayet ||

	prāgagreṣu tu darbheṣu ādyam āmantrya pūrvavat |

	apaḥ kṣipen mūladeśe 'vanenidhveti nistilāḥ ||

ādyaḥ pāṅktimūrdhanyo vipraḥ |

	dvitīye ca tṛtīye ca madhyadeśāgradeśayoḥ |

	mātāmahaprabhṛtīṃs tu eteṣām eva vāmataḥ ||

	sarvasmād annam uddhṛtya vyañjanair upasicya ca |

	saṃyojyākṣatakarkandhudadhibhiḥ prāṅmukhas tataḥ ||

	avanejanavat piṇḍān datvā bilvapramāṇakān |

	tatpātrakṣālanenātha punar apy avanejayet ||

	uttarottardānena piṇḍānām uttarottaraḥ |

	bhaved adhaś ca karaṇād adharaḥ śrāddhakarmasu ||

	tasmāt sarveṣu śrāddheṣu vṛddhimatsv itareṣu ca |

	mūlamadhyāgradeśeṣu īṣatsaktāṃś ca nirvapet ||

	gandhādīni kṣipet tūṣṇīṃ tata ācāmayed dvijān |

	anyatrāpy eṣa eva syād yavādirahito vidhiḥ ||

	dakṣiṇāpravaṇe deśe dakṣiṇābhimukhasya ca |

	dakṣiṇāgreṣu darbheṣu eṣo 'nyatra vidhiḥ smṛtaḥ ||

	athāgrabhūmim āsiñcet samyak prokṣitam astv iti |

	śivā āpaḥ santv iti ca yugmān evodakena ca ||

	saumanasyam astv iti ca puṣpadānam anantaram |

	akṣataṃ cāriṣṭaṃ cāstv ity akṣatān pratipādayet ||

**[520]**	akṣayyodakadānaṃ ca arghyadānavad iṣyate |

	ṣaṣṭhyaiva nityaṃ tat kuryān na caturthyā kadācana ||

	prārthanāsu pratiprokte sarvāsv eva dvijottamaiḥ |

	pavitrāntarhitān piṇḍān siñced uttānapātrakṛt ||

	yugmān eva svastivācya aṅguṣṭhagrahaṇaṃ sadā |

	kṛtvā dhuryasya viprasya praṇamyānuvrajet tataḥ ||

dhuryaḥ paṅktimūrdhanyaḥ | āśvalāyanagṛhyapariśiṣṭam: "ābhyudayike yugmā brāhmaṇā amūlā darbhāḥ prāṅmukhebhya udaṅmukho dadyāt | udaṅmukhebhyo vā prāṅmukhaḥ | dvau darbhau pavitre sopayāmāni pātrāṇi catvāri śaṃ no devīr ity abhimantritāsu yavān āvapati | yavo 'si somadaivatyo gosavo devanirmitaḥ | pratnavadbhiḥ prabhus tuṣṭyā nāndīmukhāṃl lokān prīṇayāhi naḥ svāheti pitaraḥ prīyantām ity eṣāṃ pratigrahaṇaṃ visarjanaṃ ca | evam uttarayoḥ pitṛpitāmahayor nityaṃ cāgnaukaraṇam | svāhākāreṇa homaś ca | ato devā avantu na ity aṅguṣṭhagrahaḥ | idaṃ viṣṇur vi cakrama ity atra pāvamānīḥ śaṃvatīr aindrīr apratirathaṃ ca śrāvayet | bhuktvā ca yeṣu piṇḍadānam āśayān gomayenopalipya teṣu prāgagrān kuśān āstīryālaṃkṛtya pṛthag ājyamiśraguḍaudano haviḥ sarvatra tasyārdhena dve dve ājyāhutīr juhuyāt | nāndīmukhāḥ pitaraḥ prīyantām iti visṛjet | pradakṣiṇam upacāraḥ | yavais tilārthaḥ sarvaṃ dvir dviḥ" iti | bhaviṣyatpurāṇam |

	piṇḍanirvapaṇaṃ kuryān na vā kuryān narādhipaḥ |

	vṛddhiśrāddhe mahābāho loke dharmam apekṣate ||

iti nāndīmukhaśrāddhavidhānam || 1.249 ||

_athaikoddiṣṭaprayogavidhim āha_ | **[521]**

	**ekoddiṣṭaṃ daivahīnam ekārghaikapavitrakam |**

**	āvāhanāgnaukaraṇarahitaṃ hy apasavyavat || 1.250 ||**

**	upatiṣṭhatām ity akṣayyasthāne vipravisarjane |**

**	abhiramyatām iti vaded brūyus te 'bhiratāḥ sma ha || 1.251 ||**

ekam uddiśya yat kriyate śrāddhaṃ tad ekoddiṣṭam | tad daivahīnaṃ viśve(śva)devarahitam | tatraikam arghyaṃ pavitram apy ekam āvāhanamantreṇāgnaukaraṇena ca rahitam | yat pārvaṇe yajñopavītavat karma tad ihāpasavyavat kāryam | apasavyaṃ prācīnāvītam | "upatiṣṭhatām" iti mantraḥ prakṛtasyākṣayyam astv iti mantrasya kārye prayojyo vipravisarjane 'bhiramyatām iti vadet | na tu "vāje vāje" iti | viprāś cābhiratāḥ sma iti pratibrūyuḥ | ekasyaikoddeśasya bahuvipraniyojanapakṣe bahuvacanam | kātyāyanaḥ: "athaikoddiṣṭam ekam arghyam ekaṃ pavitrakam ekaḥ piṇḍo nāvāhanaṃ nāgnaukaraṇaṃ nātra viśve devāḥ svadhitam iti tṛptipraśnaḥ susvadhitam ity anujñānam | upatiṣṭhatām ity akṣayasthāne 'bhiramyatām iti visargo 'bhiratāḥ sma ity apare" | śātātapaḥ |

	ekoddiṣṭaṃ tu yac chrāddhaṃ naimittikam ihocyate |

	tad apy adaivaṃ kartavyam ayugmān āśayed dvijān ||

ekoddiṣṭam uktaṃ tac ca trividham | navaṃ miśraṃ purāṇaṃ ca | tatraikādaśāhāntaṃ navam | tadūrdhvam ā saṃvatsarān miśram | tata uttaraṃ purāṇam | tatra navamiśraviṣayā vidhayas tāvad ucyante | tatra vyāghraḥ |

	ekādaśe caturthe ca māsi māsi ca vatsaram |

	pratisaṃvatsaraṃ caivam ekoddiṣṭaṃ mṛtāhani ||


        * addition in mss: "pratisaṃvatsaraṃ caivam ity anena caturthavatsare śuddhaśrāddhaṃ tripauruṣaṃ vidheyam it gamyate"

kātyāyanaḥ |

	śrāddham agnimataḥ kāryaṃ dāhād ekādaśe 'hani |

	dhruvāṇi tu prakurvīta pramītāhani sarvadā ||

traipakṣikād ūrdhvāni dhruvāṇi | ata evāha jātūkarṇyaḥ |

	ūrdhvaṃ tripakṣād yac chrāddhaṃ mṛtāhany eva tad bhavet |

	adhas tu kārayed dāhād āhitāgner dvijanmanaḥ || iti | **[522]**

tathā |

	dvādaś pratimāsyāni ādyaṃ ṣāṇmāsike tathā |

	sapiṇḍīkaraṇaṃ caivam ity etac chrāddhaṣoḍaśam ||

ṣāṇmāsike ity anena vihitayoḥ śrāddhayor nirūpaṇārtham āha |

	ekāhena tu ṣaṇmāsā yadā syur api vā tribhiḥ |

	nyūnaḥ saṃvatsaraś caivaṃ syātāṃ ṣāṇmāsike tadā ||

ekenāhnā tribhir vāhobhir yadā ṣaṇmāsā nyūnāḥ syuḥ saṃvatsaraś ca tāvatsaṃkhyayā nyūno 'sti tadā ṣāṇmāsike śrāddhe kārye ity arthaḥ | bhaviṣyatpurāṇe |

	akṛtvā ṣoḍaśaitāni kṛtvā varṣaśatāyutam |

	na mucyate tu pretatvād yathāha bhagavāñ śivaḥ ||

	arvāg abdāt pramītasya tasya māsās tryodaśa |

	śrāddhaṃ tasyāpi kartavyaṃ pratimāsaṃ tu vatsaram ||

tathā |

	mṛtāhani tu dātavyaṃ pretāya sukham icchatā |

	mṛtāhani tu dattena mucyate karmaṇo 'śubhāt ||

	asthisaṃcayane śrāddhaṃ tripakṣe māsikāni tu |

	riktayoś ca tathā tithyoḥ pretaśrāddhāni ṣoḍaśa ||

riktayos tithyor ekenāhnā nyūne ṣaṣṭhe dvādaśe ca māsa ity arthaḥ | tathā ca paiṭhīnasiḥ |

	ṣāṇmāsikābdike śrāddhe syātāṃ pūrvedyur eva te |

	māsikāni svakīye tu divase dvādaśe 'pi ca ||

tathā |

	sapiṇḍīkaraṇād arvāk kuryāc chrāddhāni ṣoḍaśa |

	ekoddiṣṭavidhānena kuryāt sarvāṇi tāni tu ||

	pretasaṃskārakarmāṇi yāni śrāddhāni ṣoḍaśa |

	yathākāle tu kāryāṇi nānyathā mucyate tataḥ ||

anenedam ucyate — sapiṇḍīkaraṇe dvādaśāhādau kṛte 'pi māsikāni pratimāsam eva kāryāṇīti | tāni ca yady apy ekoddiṣṭāni pretatvavimocanārthāni ca tathāpi tāni mantravanti na punar navaśrāddhavad amantrakāni | yad āha paiṭhīnasiḥ |

	navaśrāddham atikramya mṛtāhani tu māsikam |

	pretam uddiśya mantrais tu vatsaraṃ nirvapet sutaḥ || **[523]**

atikramya samapyety arthaḥ | brahmapurāṇe |

	nṝṇāṃ tu tyaktadehānāṃ śrāddhāḥ ṣoḍaśa sarvadā |

	caturthe pañcame caiva navamaikādaśe tathā ||

	tato dvādaśabhir māsaiḥ śrāddhā dvādaśasaṃkhyayā |

	kartavyāḥ śrutitaś caiṣāṃ tatra viprāṃś ca tarpayet ||

asmāc ca pūrṇe māsi māsikaṃ kāryam iti gamyate | śaṅkhaḥ |

	ādyaṃ śrāddham aśuddho 'pi kuryād ekādaśe 'hani |

	kartus tātkālikī śuddhir aśuddhaḥ punar eva saḥ ||

paiṭhīnasiḥ |

	sadyaḥśauce 'pi dātavyaṃ pretasyaikādaśe 'hani |

	sa eva divasas tasya śrāddhaśayyāsamādhiṣu ||

[*apiśabdo 'trāśauce saty apīti gamayati]

matsyapurāṇam |

	ekādaśe 'hani tathā viprān ekādaśaiva tu |

	putrādiḥ sūtakānte tu bhojayed ayujo dvijān ||

	dvitīye 'hni punas tadvad ekoddiṣṭaṃ samācaret ||

[*sūtakānta iti brāhmaṇasyaiva tadviṣayam (?) | kṣatriyavaiśyaśūdrāṇāṃ tu |]

vṛddhavasiṣṭhaḥ |

	saptame ca tṛtīye ca prathame navame tathā |

	ekādaśe 'hni yac chrāddhaṃ tat sāmānyam udāhṛtam ||

caturṇāṃ varṇānāṃ sāmānyam ity arthaḥ | tarhy aśaucakālasya dattas tilāñjalir ity āśaṅkyāha sa eva |

	caturṇām api varṇānāṃ sūtakaṃ tu pṛthak pṛthak ||

sūtakam aśaucam ity arthaḥ | eṣāṃ madhye navaśrāddhāny āha yamaḥ |

	caturthe pañcame caiva navamaikādaśe tathā |

	yad atra dīyate jantor navaśrāddhaṃ tad ucyate ||

tathā |

	yasya saṃcayanād arvāg āhitāgner dvijanmanaḥ |

	ayugmān bhojayed viprāṃs tan navaśrāddham ucyate ||

atriḥ |

	pretārthaṃ sūtakānte tu brāhmaṇān bhojayed daśa |

	navaśrāddhanimittaṃ tu ekam ekādaśe 'hani || **[524]**

evaṃ ca saty aikādaśāhikān navaśrāddhād āśaucāntakāryaṃ brāhmaṇabhojanaṃ karmāntaram | vyāsaḥ |

	prathame saptame caiva navamaikādaśe tathā |

	yat tu vai dīyate jantos tan navaśrāddham ucyate ||

bahvṛcagṛhyapariśiṣṭe: "navaśrāddhaṃ saha dadyuḥ" na punaḥ pratyekam ity arthaḥ | navaśrāddhagrahaṇaṃ pradarśanārtham | ata eva pracetāḥ |

	ekādaśyādyāḥ kramaśo jyeṣṭhasya vidhivat kriyāḥ |

	kuryur naikaikaśaḥ śrāddham ābdikaṃ tu pṛthak pṛthak ||

	arvāk saṃvatsarāt sarve tu kuryuḥ śrāddhaṃ sametya vai |

	saṃvatsare vyatīte tu kuryuḥ śrāddhaṃ pṛthak pṛthak ||

uśanā |

	navaśrāddhaṃ sapiṇḍatvaṃ śrāddhāny api ca ṣoḍaśa |

	ekenaiva hi kāryāṇi saṃvibhaktadhanair api ||

ekena jyeṣṭhenety arthaḥ | śātātapaḥ |

	ekādaśe 'hni yac chrāddhaṃ mātāpitros tu dīyate |

	tat sametais tu kartavyaṃ pūrvaṃ caiva pṛthak pṛthak ||

pūrvaṃ purāṇam ābdikādikam | marīciḥ |

	sarvair anumataṃ kṛtvā jyeṣṭhenaiva tu yat kṛtam |

	dhanena cāvibhaktena sarvair eva kṛtaṃ bhavet ||

vyāghraḥ |

	pretasya pretakāryāṇi akṛtvā dhanahārakaḥ |

	varṇānāṃ yad vadhe proktaṃ tad vrataṃ prayataś caret ||

tathā |

	deyāni veśmaśuddhyarthaṃ navaśrāddhāni yatnataḥ |

	tataḥ pretaviśuddhyarthaṃ mṛtāhani tu vatsaram ||

gṛhaviśuddhyartham iti gṛhe praviṣṭayamakiṃkaratṛptyartham | 

	śauce tu sūtakaṃ cet syān niśāśeṣe tathaiva ca |

	navaśrāddhāni deyāni yathākālaṃ yathākramam ||

	yasyaitāni na dīyanta ekoddiṣṭāni ṣoḍaśa |

	piśācatvaṃ sthiraṃ tasya dattaiḥ śrāddhaśatair api ||

vṛddhavasiṣṭhaḥ |

	alabdhvā tu navaśrāddhaṃ pretatvāc ca na mucyate |

	arvāk tu dvādaśāhasya labdhvā tarati duṣkṛtam || **[525]**

bhaviṣyatpurāṇe |

	navaśrāddhaṃ tripakṣaṃ ca ṣāṇmāsaṃ māsikāni ca |

	na karoti suto yasya tasyāghaḥ pitaro gatāḥ ||

vyāsaḥ |

	dvādaśāhe tripakṣe ca ṣāṇmāse māsike 'bdike |

	śrāddhāni ṣoḍaśaitāni saṃsmṛtāni manīṣibhiḥ ||

	ṣānmāsikābdike śrāddhe syātāṃ pūrvedyur eva te ||

āśvalāyanapariśiṣṭam |

	navaśrāddhaṃ daśāhāni navamiśraṃ tu ṣaḍṛtūn |

	ataḥ paraṃ purāṇaṃ syāt trividhaṃ śrāddham ucyate ||

na cānenaikādaśāhikasya navaśrāddhatvaṃ vyāvartyate | vacanāntarais tadbhāvasya vihitatvāt | bhaviṣyatpurāṇe |

	navaśrāddhādiśrāddhāni yasya vai na kṛtāni saḥ |

	nādhikārī bhavet tatra māsaṣāṇmāsikābdike ||

śaunakagṛhyapariśiṣṭāt |

	pretaśrāddheṣu sarveṣu na svadhā nābhiramyatām |

	svasty astu visṛjed evaṃ sakṛt praṇavavarjitam ||

	ekoddiṣṭasya piṇḍe tu anuśabdo na yujyate |

	pitṛśabdaṃ na kurvīta pitṛhā copajāyate ||

sapiṇḍīkaraṇāt prāktanaikoddiṣṭaviṣayam etat | bahvṛcagṛhyapariśiṣṭe |

	asagotraḥ sagotro vā yadi strī yadi vā pumān |

	prathame 'hani yo dadyāt sadaśāhaṃ samāpayet ||

	anūdakam adhūpaṃ ca gandhamālyavivarjitam |

	navaśrāddham amantraṃ ca piṇḍodakavivarjitam ||

anūdakam anarghyam | piṇḍodakam avanejanam | varāhapurāṇe |

	śvaḥ kariṣya iti jñātvā brāhmaṇāmantraṇakriyā |

	gato 'si divyalokaṃ tvaṃ kṛtāntavihitāt pathaḥ ||

	manasā vāyubhūtena vipre tvāhaṃ niyojaye |

	pūjayiṣyāmi bhogais tvām evaṃ vipraṃ nimantrayet ||

	astaṃ gate tathāditye gatvā vipraniveśanam |

	datvā tu pādyaṃ vidhivan namaskṛtya dvijottamam ||

**[526]**	pādau prakṣālya tailena pretasya hitakāmyayā |

	prabhātāyāṃ ca śarvaryām udite ca divākare ||

	kārayitvā śmaśrukarma nakhacchedas tataḥ param |

	snāpanābhyañjanaṃ dadyād viprāya vidhipūrvakam ||

	gṛhṇīyād bhūmibhāgaṃ ca sthaṇḍilaṃ tadanantaram |

	nipānadeśaṃ saṃgṛhya kartavyaṃ sthaṇḍilaṃ mahat ||

	nadīkūle nivāse vā pretabhūmiṃ vinirdiśet |

	akṛtvā bhūmibhāgaṃ tu nirgataṃ ye na kurvate ||

	tad adhvani jagad bhadre tad ucchiṣṭaṃ kṛtaṃ bhavet |

	na devāḥ pitaras tasya gṛhṇantīha kadācana ||

	patanti niraye ghore tenocchiṣṭena sundari |

	satailaṃ snapanaṃ kṛtvā gatvā caiva mahānadīm ||

	tīrthāni manasā dhyātvā taiḥ svam abhyukṣayed budhaḥ |

	evaṃ śuddhiṃ tataḥ kṛtvā brāhmaṇaṃ śīghram ānayet ||

	ānītaṃ ca dvijaṃ dṛṣṭvā kartavyā svāgatakriyā |

	arghyaṃ pādyaṃ tataḥ kṛtvā hṛṣṭatuṣṭena mādhavi ||

	āsanaṃ copakalpeta mantreṇa vidhipūrvakam ||

tathā |

	upaveśyāsane bhadre chatraṃ tatra prakalpayet ||

āvaraṇārthaṃ chatraṃ tad brāhmaṇāya pradīyate |

	paścād upānahau dadyāt pādasparśakare śubhe |

	saṃtaptavālukāṃ bhūmim asikaṇṭakitāṃ tathā ||

	saṃtārayati durgāṇi pretaṃ dadad upānahau |

	tilopacāraṃ kṛtvā tu viprasya niyatātmavān ||

	nāmagotram udāhṛtya pretāya tadanantaram |

	śīghram āhvānayed bhūmiṃ darbhahasto 'tha bhūtale ||

mantraḥ |

	imaṃ lokaṃ parityajya gato 'si paramāṃ gatim |

	evam āhvāya taṃ gandhapuṣpadhūpān samarpayet ||

devalaḥ |

	ekoddiṣṭeṣu sarveṣu brāhmaṇebhyaḥ samutsṛjet |

	tataḥ kāmaṃ tu bhuñjīta svayaṃ maṅgalabhojane || **[527]**

ekoddiṣṭeṣu sarveṣv iti navaśrāddhābhiprāyam | tatrāvaśiṣṭam annaṃ bhoktṛbhya eva deyam | maṅgalabhojanaṃ sāṃvatsarikaikoddiṣṭāvaśiṣṭam | ata eva aṅgirāḥ |

	navaśrāddheṣu yac chiṣṭaṃ grahaparyuṣitaṃ ca yat |

	dampatyor bhuktaśiṣṭaṃ ca tan na bhuñjīta karhicit ||

bṛhaspatiḥ |

	caturthe 'hani viprebhyo deyam annaṃ hi bāndavaiḥ |

	gāvaḥ savarṇaṃ vittaṃ ca pretam uddiśya śaktitaḥ ||

caturthe 'sthisaṃcayanāha (?) ity arthaḥ |

	yad iṣṭaṃ jīvataś cāsīt tad dadyāt tasya yatnataḥ |

tasya jīvata ity anvayaḥ | satyavrataḥ: "prātar utthāya pretabrāhmaṇān ekādaśāmantryāparāhṇe nānābhakṣyānnarasavinyāsair ekaikam uddiśya vidhivat piṇḍadānam | vāso hiraṇyadāsyupānacchatrodakumbhadakṣiṇāḥ | guṇavati pātre śayyāpradānaṃ tataḥ svastyayanādi dharmāḥ pravartante daśamyām atītāyām ekaikaṃ tam uddiśya bhojayet | teṣām evaikasmai guṇavate śayyā" | viṣṇuḥ: "dvādaśāhaṃ śrāddhaṃ kṛtvā trayodaśe 'hni vā kuryāt" | vyāsaḥ |

	putraḥ patnī ca vapanaṃ kuryād ante yathāvidhi |

	piṇḍadānocito 'nyo 'pi kuryād itthaṃ samāhitaḥ ||

tathā |

	aśaucāntadine kṣauraṃ jananyāṃ ca gurau tathā |

saṃsthitāyāṃ jananyāṃ gurau saṃsthita ity arthaḥ | smṛtyantaram |

	nandāyāṃ bārgavadine caturdaśyāṃ tripuṣkare |

	navaśraddhaṃ na kurvīta gṛhī putradhanakṣayāt ||

	ekādaśyāṃ tu nandāyāṃ sinīvālyāṃ bhṛgor dine |

	nabhasyasya caturdaśyāṃ kṛttikāsu tripuṣkare ||

yo nandāyāṃ niṣedhaḥ sa ekādaśyām eva | śukre 'māvāsyāyām eva | caturdaśyāṃ bhādrapadacaturdaśyām eva | tripuṣkare kṛttikāsv eva | **[528]** baudhānayaḥ: "saṃvatsaraṃ pretapatnī madhumāṃsalavaṇāni varjayet | adhaḥ śayīta ṣaṇmāsān iti maudgalyaḥ" | abrāhmaṇīviṣayam etat | brāhmaṇī tu sarvakālam eva madhvāi varjayet | pracetāḥ |

	pretāyānnaṃ sadā deyam abdaṃ vṛttividhānataḥ |

	ekoddiṣṭavidhānena sarvaiḥ putraiḥ prayatnataḥ ||

	ninīyāśmani pūrvaṃ tu tataḥ śrāddhaṃ prakalpayet |

	paścāt tu ninayet pūrvaṃ tasminn eva yathāvidhi ||

hārītaḥ: "nāśiṣaḥ pratigṛhṇanti nānnaṃ vikiren na svadhāṃ ninayet | pitṛmantravarjam aśnatsu japaḥ |

	pradadyād dakṣiṇāṃ tebhyaḥ sarvebhyaś cānupūrvaśaḥ |

	yathāśakti pradadyāc ca gobhūhemādikaṃ tathā ||

navāni bhāṇḍāni yeṣv annaṃ saṃskriyate yeṣu bhujyate tāni bhuktavadbhyo dadyāt" | tathā |

	nāgnaukaraṇamantrāś ca ekaṃ cātra tilodakam |

prāksapiṇḍīkaraṇānta eva svastīty uktvā naveṣu visargaḥ |

	anuddiśya hi pretāya sarvaṃ tatraiva dīyate || 1.250, 251 ||

_atha sapiṇḍīkaraṇam āha_ |

	**gandhodakatilair yuktaṃ kuryāt pātracatuṣṭayam |**

**	arghyārthāṃ pitṛpātreṣu pretapātraṃ prasecayet || 1.252 ||**

**	ye samānā iti dvābhyāṃ śeṣaṃ pūrvavad ācaret |**

**	etat sapiṇḍīkaraṇam ekoddiṣṭaṃ striyā api || 1.253 ||**

gandhaiś candanādibhir udakena tilaiś ca yuktaṃ pātracatuṣṭayaṃ pretādibhyo 'rghyaṃ dātuṃ kuryāt | tatra pretāyārghyaṃ datvā tatpātrasthaṃ jalaṃ pitāmahādipātreṣu triṣu "ye samānāḥ" iti dvābhyām anuṣṭubbhyāṃ prajāpatidṛṣṭābhyāṃ yathākramaṃ pitṛjīvadevatābhyāṃ prasiñcet | śeṣaṃ tu karma brāhmaṇanimantraṇādi pārvaṇavad ācaret | etaduktaprakāraṃ pitāmahādidai(de)vatyaṃ pārvaṇaṃ pretadai(de)vatyaṃ caikoddiṣṭaṃ śrāddhaṃ sapiṇḍīkaraṇasaṃjñakaṃ veditavyam | striyā api caitat kāryaṃ na punaḥ puruṣasyaiva | atra bhaviṣyatpurāṇam | **[529]**

	pātrāṇi kṛtvā catvāri pūrayitvā (?) tilāmbubhiḥ |

	triṣv ekaṃ pitṛpātreṣu prasiñcen nāmagotrataḥ ||

śaunakaḥ: "atha sapiṇḍīkaraṇaṃ catvāry udakapātrāṇi | ekaṃ pretasya trīṇītareṣāṃ prathamaṃ pātraṃ triṣu pātreṣu niyojayet | samānīva (?) ākūtir ity evam eva prathamaṃ piṇḍaṃ triṣu niyojayet | madhumatībhiḥ saṃgacchatīti dvābhyām eva caturtho 'nujñāpito bhavati" iti | brahmapurāṇam |

	caturbhyaś cārghyapātrebhya ekaṃ vāmena pāṇinā |

	gṛhītvā dakṣiṇenaiva pāṇinā ca tilodakam ||

	saṃsṛjatu tvā pṛthivī ye samānā iti smaran |

	pretaviprasya haste tu caturbhāgaṃ jalaṃ kṣipet ||

	tataḥ pitāmahādibhyas tan mantraiś ca pṛthak pṛthak |

	ye samānā iti dvābhyāṃ taj jalaṃ tu samarpayet ||

	arghyaṃ tenaiva vidhinā pretapātrāc ca pūrvavat |

	tebhyaś cārghyaṃ nivedyaiva paścāc ca svayam ācamet ||

pitāmahādibhya iti vacanāt pretaśabdenācirātīta ucyate | na tu prapitāmahasya piteti gamyate |

	atha tenaiva vidhinā darbhamūle 'vanejanam |

	pitur datvā tu piṇḍaṃ tu dadyād bhaktyā tu pūrvavat ||

	kṛtvā piṇḍam athāṣṭāṅgaṃ dhyātvā tu vasubhāsvaram |

	suvarṇarūpyadarbhaiś ca tasmin piṇḍe tatas tridhā ||

	kṛtvā pitāmahādibhyo vidhivac caitam arpayet |

	saṃsṛjatu tvā pṛthivī vāyur agniḥ prajāpatiḥ ||

	etaṃ mantraṃ japed bhaktyā samānāvartam eva ca |

	ye samānā iti dvābhyāṃ pitṛbhyaḥ pretam arpayet |

	suvartulāṃs tatas tāṃs trīn piṇḍān kṛtvā prapūjayet ||

	arghapuṣpais tathā dhūpair dīpamālyānulepanaiḥ |

	mukhyaṃ tu pitaraṃ kṛtvā punas tva anyān yathākramam || **[530]**

atra ca pituḥ pātraṃ piṇḍaṃ ca mukhyaṃ prathamaṃ kuryāt | tathā pitari pretaśabdaḥ prayukta iti gamyate | pituḥ pātrapiṇḍau pitāmahādīnāṃ pātreṣu piṇḍeṣu prakṣeptavyāv iti pratīyate | tataś ca yaiḥ kaiścid ucyate pitur yaḥ prapitāmahas tadīyau pātrapiṇḍau tridhā kṛtvā pitrādipātrapiṇḍeṣu nikṣeptavyāv iti | tad etad vacanaviruddhatvād upekṣaṇīyam | śātātapavacanavirodhaś ca | tathā hi |

	pretānām iha sraveṣāṃ ye mantraiś ca niyojitāḥ |

	kṛtārthās te hi saṃvṛttāḥ sapiṇḍīkaraṇe kṛte ||

	pretatvāc ceha nistīrṇāḥ prāptāḥ pitṛgaṇaṃ tu te || iti |

prapitāmaha idānīṃ kriyamāṇāt sapiṇḍīkaraṇāt pitṛtvaṃ [na] pratipadyate kiṃ tu pūrvam evāsau tathā saṃpannas tasmāt pitur eva pretatvavimuktipūrvikā pitṛtvaprāptiḥ sapiṇḍīparaṇasādhyā | pitṛtvaprāpteś ca prayojanam uktaṃ viṣṇupurāṇe |

	tataḥ pitṛtvam āpanne tasmin prete mahīpate |

	śrāddhadharmair aśeṣais tu tatpūrvān arcayet pitṝn ||

na ca caturthapuruṣapramukhānāṃ(ṇāṃ) pitṝṇāṃ śrāddheṣv arcanādhikāro 'sti tatparebhyo 'nadhikārāt | "na caturthaṃ piṇḍaṃ gacchati" ityādiniṣedhebhyaḥ | viṣṇuḥ |

	arvāk sapiṇḍīkaraṇāt preto bhavati vai mṛtaḥ |

	pretalokaṃ gatasyānnaṃ sodakumbhaṃ prayacchata ||

	pitṛlokaṃ gatasyāsya śrāddhaṃ śraddhāsamanvitam |

	pitṛlokaṃ gatasyāpi tasmāc chrāddhaṃ prayacchata ||

ityādivacanārthaparyālocanavaśād gamyate — mṛtasya prāk sapiṇḍīkaraṇāt ko 'py avasthāviśeṣaḥ pretaśabdapravṛttinimitto bhavatīti | sapiṇḍīkarṇād ūrdhvaṃ tajjanyaḥ pitṛśabdapravṛttinimittabhūtaḥ ko 'py atiśayas tatra jāta iti | yat punaḥ śātātapenoktam,

	nirupya caturaḥ piṇḍān piṇḍadaḥ pratināmataḥ |

	ye samānā iti dvābhyām ādyaṃ tu vibhajet tridhā ||

iti, yat tu (yac ca) laugākṣivacanam: "caturthaṃ piṇḍam utsṛjya traidhaṃ kṛtvā piṇḍeṣu nidadyāt" **[531]** iti, tad ubhayam apy acirātītapitrādipiṇḍaviṣayam eva | tasya piṇḍasya pitāmahādipiṇḍatrayāt prāg ūrdhvaṃ vā pradānaṃ vihitam | tatra yadā pūrvaṃ dīpyate tadāsāv ādyaḥ | yadordhvaṃ tadāsāv eva caturthaḥ | tataś ca "ādyaṃ tu vibhajet tridhā," "caturthaṃ piṇḍam utsṛjya traidhaṃ kṛtvā" ityādivākyāni tadviṣayāṇy eva | tatrāpi cirātītasya pūrvaṃ piṇḍodaya ity abhiprāyeṇātra mukhyaṃ tu pitaraṃ kṛtvetyādi purāṇavacanaṃ pramāṇam | ata eva viṣṇuḥ: "saṃvatsarānte pretāya tatpitre tatpitāmahāya tatprapitāmahāya ca brāhmaṇān devapūrvān bhojayet" ity uktavān | śātātapas tu pretapiṇḍasya paścāt pradeyatām āha |

	sapiṇḍīkaraṇaṃ śrāddhaṃ devapūrvaṃ niyojayet |

	pitṝn evāśayet tatra punaḥ pretaṃ ca nirdiśet || iti |

uśanasā ca,

	sapiṇḍīkaraṇe viprān bhojayet pārvaṇe yathā |

	pṛthak ca kalpayed annam ekoddiṣṭavidhānataḥ ||

ity uktam | purāṇe 'pi |

	śrāddhadvayam atikramya kurvīta sahapiṇḍatām |

	tayos tripuruṣaṃ pūrvam ekoddiṣṭaṃ tataḥ param ||

pitāmahāditrayadai(de)vatyaṃ tripuruṣam | acirādītadai(de)vatyam ekoddiṣṭam | atha sapiṇḍīkaraṇe 'dhikārī nirūpyate | tatra purāṇam |

	putra eva sapiṇḍatvaṃ pitror eva samācaret |

	aurasaḥ kṣetrajo vāpi dharma eva sanātanaḥ ||

eṣa mukhyaḥ śāstrārthaḥ | putrāsaṃbhave 'nyeṣām apy asty adhikāraḥ | ata eva paiṭhīnasiḥ |

	bhrātā vā bhrātṛputro vā sapiṇḍaḥ śiṣya eva vā |

	sapiṇḍīkaraṇaṃ kuryāt putrahīne mṛte sati ||

	sarvabandhuvihīnasya patnī kuryāt sapiṇḍanam |

	ṛtvijaṃ kārayed vāpi purohitam athāpi vā ||

yat tu sumantunoktam,

	sarvabandhuvihīnasya patnī kuryād aninditā |

	atha vā śiṣyasabrahmaṛtvigbhṛtyapurohitaiḥ ||

	kārayeta kriyāḥ sarvāḥ sapiṇḍīkaraṇam vinā |

	sapiṇḍīkaraṇaṃ putraiḥ kāryaṃ nānyaiś ca niścitam || **[532]**

iti, tat pravāsādivaśāt sapiṇḍīkaraṇāsamarthe putre sati veditavyam | sāmarthyalābhe sati tu kālātyaye 'pi putreṇaiva kāryam | tad uktaṃ vāyupurāṇe |

	śrāddhāni ṣoḍaśāpādya vidadhīta sapiṇḍatām |

	pituḥ putro vidhānajña iti paurāṇikā viduḥ ||

	śrāddhāni ṣoḍaśādatvā kuryān na tu sapiṇḍatām |

	proṣitāvasite putraḥ kālād aticirād api ||

proṣitāvasite pravāsāvasāne putro 'ticārād api kālād yat sapiṇḍatvaṃ kuryāt tat ṣoḍaśa śrāddhāny adatvā na kuryāt kiṃ tu datvaivety arthaḥ | yadi tāni bhrātrādinā dattāni tadā sapiṇḍatvam eva kuryāt | tathā |

	ajñānād atha vā mohān na kṛtā cet sapiṇḍatā |

	tatrāpi vidhivat kāryā kālād aticirād api ||

ajñānamohau sakalāsāmarthyopalakṣaṇārthau | sumantuḥ |

	sutaḥ sapiṇḍīkaraṇaṃ na kuryād yadi mohitaḥ |

	yāvaj jīvati duḥkhārto mṛto narakam āpnuyāt ||

sutagrahaṇam adhikārimātropalakṣaṇārtham | paiṭhīnasiḥ |

	navaśrāddhaṃ sapiṇḍatvaṃ śrāddhāny api ca ṣoḍaśa |

	ekenaiva tu kāryāṇi saṃvibhaktadhaneṣv api ||

	vibhaktais tu pṛthak kāryaṃ pratisaṃvatsarādikam |

	ekenaivāvibhakteṣu kṛte sarvais tu tat kṛtam ||

kātyāyanaḥ |

	pitāmahaḥ pituḥ paścāt pañcatvaṃ yadi gacchati |

	pautreṇaikādaśāhādi kartavyaṃ śrāddhaṣoḍaśam ||

	na tatpautreṇa kartavyaṃ putravāṃś cet pitāmahaḥ |

	pituḥ sapiṇḍatāṃ kṛtvā kuryān māsānumāsikam ||

	asaṃskṛtau na saṃskāryau pūrvau pautraprapautrakaiḥ |

	pitaraṃ tatra saṃskuryād iti kātyāyano 'bravīt ||

	pāpiṣṭham api śuddhena śuddhaṃ pāpakṛtāpi vā |

	pitāmahena pitaraṃ saṃskuryād iti niścayaḥ ||

asaṃskṛtāv asapiṇḍitau pitāmahaprapitāmahau pautreṇa prapautreṇa ca na **[533]** saṃskāryau na sapiṇḍanīyāv ity arthaḥ | etac ca pratyāsanne sapiṇḍīkaraṇakartari sati draṣṭavyam | asati tu pautrādiḥ kuryād eva sapiṇḍatvāt | pāpiṣṭham api śuddheneti patitādivyatiriktaviṣayam | tathā ca sapiṇḍīkaraṇānuvṛttau baijavāpaḥ: "abhiśaptapatitabhrūṇaghnān strīr abhicāriṇīr nātidiśet | atideśaḥ sapiṇḍanam | gautamaḥ: "pāpakarmiṇo na saṃsṛjeran striyaś cābhicāriṇīḥ" | atha patitān ity adhikṛtyāha vṛddhayājñavalkyaḥ |

	sarpaviprahatānāṃ ca śṛṅgidaṃṣṭrisarīsṛpaiḥ |

	ātmanas tyāgināṃ caiva śrāddham eṣāṃ na kārayet ||

[*śrāddham aurdhvadaihikādi]

chāgaleyaḥ |

	caṇḍālād udakāt sarpād brāhmaṇād vaidyutād api |

	daṃṣṭribhyaś ca paśubhyaś ca maraṇaṃ pāpakarmiṇām ||

	udakaṃ piṇḍadānaṃ ca pretebhyo yat pradīyate |

	nopatiṣṭhati tat sarvam antarikṣe vinaśyati ||

tarhi pretatvavimokṣa udapiṇḍadānādiprāptau copāyam āha |

	nārāyaṇabaliḥ kāryo lokagarhābhayān naraiḥ |

	tatas tebhyo 'pi dātavyam annam evaṃ sadakṣiṇam ||

tata iti nārāyaṇabalikaraṇād anantaram ity arthaḥ | vṛddhayājñavalkyaḥ |

	nārāyaṇaṃ samuddiśya śivaṃ vā yat pradīyate |

	tasya śuddhāv ahṃ caiva tad bhaven na tad anyathā ||

saṃgrahāt |

	pretam uddiśya yat kāryaṃ kuryān nārāyaṇāya tat |

	śivāya vodakaśrāddhapiṇḍanirvapaṇādikam ||

yamaḥ |

	caṇḍālais tu hatā ye ca śṛṅgidaṃṣṭrisarīsṛpaiḥ |

	śrāddham eṣāṃ na kartavyaṃ brahmadaṇḍahatāś ca ye ||

	mahāpātakināṃ caiva tathā caivātmaghātinām |

	udakaṃ piṇḍadānaṃ ca śrāddhaṃ caiva tu yat kṛtam ||

	nopatiṣṭhati tat sarvaṃ rākṣasair vipralupyate || **[534]**

smṛtyantaram |

	vidyudgonṛpaviprāmbuśṛṅgidaṃṣṭryagnighātitāḥ |

	vṛthotpannamahāklībavratino nodabhājanāḥ ||

udabhājanā arghyodakasaṃsargabhājanā ity arthaḥ | tathā |

	brāhmaṇādihate tāte patite saṅgavarjite |

	vyutkramāc ca mṛte deyaṃ yebhya eva dadāty asau ||

saṅgavarjito bhikṣuḥ | smṛtyantarāt |

	svecchayā maraṇaṃ vipra śṛṅgidaṃṣṭrisarīsṛpaiḥ |

	antyāntyajaviṣodbandhair ātmanā caiva tāḍanaiḥ ||

	saṃpūrṇasarvagātrāṇāṃ viṣād ākarṣato 'tha vā |

	jalāgniśvabhrapātaiś ca nirāhārādibhis tathā ||

	yeṣām eva bhavet te vai kathitāḥ pāpakarmaṇi |

	pāṣaṇḍam āśritāś caiva mahāpātakinas tathā ||

	striyaś ca vyabhicāriṇya ārūḍhapatitās tathā |

	na teṣāṃ snānasaṃskāro na śrāddhaṃ na sapiṇḍanam ||

	śrāddhāni ṣoḍaśoktāni nānyāny api bhavanti hi ||

nirāhāratvam atra roṣavaśāt pāpipadakāraṃ na punar dāridryabhāvāt | ārūḍhapatitā daśadinābhyantara eva mṛtā yoṣitaḥ |

	vaitānaṃ prakṣipet toye gṛhyāgniṃ ca catuṣpathe |

	pātrāṇi dāhayed agnau yajamāne vṛthā mṛte ||

sāgnike pāpakarmaṇīti pāṭhaḥ |

	pūrṇe saṃvatsare teṣām atha kāryaṃ dayālubhiḥ |

	ekādaśīṃ samāsādya śuklapakṣasya vai tithim ||

	viṣṇuṃ yamaṃ ca saṃpūjya gandhapuṣpādibhis tathā |

	daśa piṇḍān ghṛtābhyaktān darbheṣu madhusaṃyutān ||

	yajñopavītī satilān dyāyan viṣṇuṃ yamaṃ tathā |

	dakṣiṇābhimukhas tūṣṇīm ekaikaṃ nirvapet tu tam ||

	uddhṛtya niyataḥ piṇḍāṃs tīrthādyambhasi nikṣipet |

	kṣipaṃs tān kīrtayen nāma gotraṃ tu mṛtakasya tu ||

	punar abhyarcayed viṣṇuṃ yamaṃ kusumacandanaiḥ |

	dhūpadīpaiś ca naivedyair bhakṣyabhojyasamanvitaiḥ ||

**[535]**	tataś copavased ahni viprāṃś caiva nimantrayet |

	kulavidyātapoyuktān rūpaśīlasamanvitān ||

	nava saptātha vā pañca svasāmarthyānusārataḥ |

	apare 'hani saṃprāpte madhyāhne susamāhitaḥ ||

	viṣṇor abhyarcanaṃ kṛtvā viprāṃs tān upaveśayet |

	udaṅmukhān yathājyeṣṭhaṃ pitṛrūpam anusmaran ||

	mano niveśya viṣṇau ca sarvaṃ kuryād atandritaḥ |

	āvāhanādi yat proktaṃ daivapūrvaṃ tu tad bhavet ||

	tṛpāñ jñātvā tato viprāṃs tṛptiṃ pṛṣṭvā yathāvidhi |

	haviṣyavyañjanenaiva tilādisahitena ca ||

	evaṃ piṇḍān pradadyād vai daivaṃ rūpam anusmaran |

	prathamaṃ viṣṇave dadyād brahmaṇe ca śivāya ca ||

	yamāya saparivārāya caturthaṃ piṇḍam utsṛjet |

	mṛtaṃ saṃkīrtya manasā gotrapūrvaṃ tataḥ param ||

	viṣṇor nāma gṛhītvaivaṃ pañcamaṃ pūrvavat kṣipet |

	viprān ācāmayitvā tu dakṣiṇābhiḥ samarcayet ||

	ekaṃ vṛddhatamaṃ vipraṃ hiraṇyena prapūjayet |

	gavā vastreṇa bhūmyā ca pretasya manasā smaran ||

	tatas tilāmbho viprās tu hastair darbhasamanvitaiḥ |

	kṣipeyur gotram uddiśya nāma buddhau niveśya ca ||

	bahir gatvā tilāmbhas tu tasmai dadyāt samāhitaḥ |

	mitrabandhujanaiḥ sārdhaṃ paścād bhuñjīta vāgyataḥ ||

	evaṃ viṣṇumate sthitvā yo dadyād ātmaghātine |

	samuddharati taṃ kṣipraṃ nātra kāryā vicāraṇā ||

vāyupurāṇe |

	śuklapakṣe tu dvādaśyāṃ kuryāc chrāddhaṃ tu vatsaram |

	dvādaśāhani vā kuryāc chukle ca prathame 'hani ||

smṛtyantaram |

	yadaiva śudhyati preto nārāyaṇabalau kṛte |

	tadaiva pāpanirmuktaḥ kriyārho jāyate tu saḥ ||

	tadaiva smaraṇaṃ tasya yasminn ahani śudhyati |

	sutair annapradānena viṣṇoḥ saṃsamaraṇakramāt ||

**[536]**	yo dadāti kriyāpiṇḍaṃ tasmai pretāya vai sutaḥ |

	tasyaivāśaucam uddiṣṭaṃ tryaham eva na saṃśayaḥ ||

	viṣṇuśrāddhasamāptau tu trayodaśyāṃ dinatrayam |

	āśaucaṃ piṇḍadaḥ kuryān na tu tadbandhugotrajāḥ ||

evaṃ ca pratiṣiddhaśrāddhānāṃ madhye keṣāṃcid ātmaghātakādīnāṃ nārāyaṇabalir uktaḥ | tatra ye vidhita ātmānaṃ ghātayanti teṣāṃ na śrāddhapratiṣedho nāpi nārāyaṇabalividhiḥ | vidhiniṣedhavirodhato 'pratiṣiddhasya cāpratyavāyakaratvāt | pratyavāyakaraṇasya maraṇasya śrāddhapratiṣedhādinimittatā | tathā ca brahmagarbhaḥ |

	yo jīvituṃ na śaknoti mahāvyādhyupapīḍitaḥ |

	so 'gnyudakamahāyātrāṃ kurvan nāmutra duṣyati ||

vivasvān |

	sarvendriyaviraktasya vṛddhasya kṛtakarmaṇaḥ |

	vyādhitasyecchayā tīrthe maraṇaṃ tapaso 'dhikam ||

tathā gārgyo 'pi gṛhastham adhikṛtyāha |

	mahāprasthānagamanaṃ jvalanāmbupraveśanam |

	bhṛguprapatanaṃ caiva vṛthā necchet tu jīvitam ||

bhṛguḥ parvatakaṭakaḥ | vṛthā dharmānuṣṭhānaśūnyam | manus tu vānaprastham adhikṛtyāha |

	aparājitāṃ cāsthāya vrajed diśam ajihmagaḥ |

	ā nipātāc charīrasya yukto vāryanilāśanaḥ ||

aparājitā pūrvottareśānadik tām ā śarīrapātād akuṭilaṃ jalam anilaṃ vā bhakṣayan samāhito vrajet |

	āsāṃ maharṣicaryāṇāṃ tyaktvānyatamayā tanum |

	vītaśokabhayo vipro brahmabhūyāya kalpate ||

nāgasarpahataṃ prati kāryaviśeṣa uktaḥ smṛtyantare |

	pramādād icchayā vāpi nāgād vā sarpato mṛtaḥ |

	pakṣayor ubhayor nāgān pañcamīṣu prapūjayet ||

	kuryāt piṣṭamayīṃ lekhāṃ nāgapratikṛtiṃ bhuvi |

	arcayet tāṃ sitaiḥ puṣpaiḥ sugandhaiś candanena tu ||

	pradadyād dhūpadīpau ca taṇḍulāṃś ca sitān kṣipet |

	āmam iṣṭaṃ tathaivānnaṃ kṣīraṃ ca vinivedayet ||

**[537]**	upasthāya vaded evaṃ muñca muñcāmukaṃ tv iha |

	madhuraṃ tad dine dadyād evam abdaṃ samācaret ||

	sauvarṇaṃ śaktito nāgaṃ tato dadyād dvijanmane |

	gāṃ savatsāṃ tato dadyād ity ājñā gāruḍī tathā ||

	yathāvibhāgaṃ karmāṇi nāgārthaṃ yatnato naraḥ |

	dvijān vimokṣayitvā tu suprītāḥ santu pannagāḥ ||

ṣaṭtriṃśanmatāt |

	pituḥ putreṇa kartavyaṃ na kurvīta pitā sute |

	atisnehena kurvīta sapiṇḍīkaraṇaṃ vinā ||

brahmapurāṇe |

	mṛte pitari yasyātha vidyate ca pitāmahaḥ |

	tena devās trayaḥ piṇḍāḥ prapitāmahapūrvakāḥ ||

	tebhyas tu paitṛkaṃ piṇḍo niyoktavyas tu pūrvavat |

	mātary atha mṛtāyāṃ ca vidyate ca pitāmahī ||

	prapitāmahīpūrvakaṃ tu kāryas tatrāpy ayam vidhiḥ ||

yat tu,

	vytkramāñ ca mṛtānāṃ tu naiva kāryā sapiṇḍatā ||

iti vacanam, tan mātāpitṛvyatiriktapretaviṣayam | chandogapariśiṣṭe kātyāyanaḥ |

	na yoṣidbhyaḥ pṛthag dadyād avasānadinād ṛte |

	savabhartṛpiṇḍamātrābhyas tṛptir āsāṃ yataḥ smṛtā ||

tathā |

	pitāmahaḥ pituḥ paścāt pañcatvaṃ yadi gacchati |

	pautreṇaikādaśāhādi kartavyaṃ śrāddhaṣoḍaśam ||

	naitat pautreṇa kartavyaṃ putravāṃś cet pitāmahaḥ |

	pituḥ sapiṇḍatāṃ kṛtvā kuryān māsānumāsikam ||

	asaṃskṛtau na saṃskāryau pūrvau pautraprapautrakaiḥ |

	pitaraṃ tatra saṃskuryād iti kātyāyano 'bravīt ||

	pāpiṣṭham api śuddhena śuddhaṃ pāpakṛtāpi vā |

	pitāmahena pitaraṃ saṃskuryād iti niścayaḥ ||

pūrvau pitāmahau yatra kenāpi nimittenāsaṃkṛtāv akṛtasapiṇḍīkaraṇau tatrāpi tābhyāṃ saha pitaraṃ saṃskuryāt sapiṇḍayed ity arthaḥ | vājasaneyayajñavārśvaḥ | **[538]**

	homāntaḥ pitṛyajñaḥ syāj jīve pitari jānataḥ |

	pitaraṃ bhojayitvā vā piṇḍau nipṛṇuyāt parau ||

	yebhyaḥ piṇḍaṃ pitā dadyāt tebhyaḥ putro'pi dāpayet |

	jīve pitari no dadyād ity eṣā naigamī śrutiḥ ||

	jīvet pitāmaho yasya pitā cāntarito bhavet |

	pitur ekasya dātavyam evam āhur manīṣiṇaḥ ||

	yasya pramītau dvau syātāṃ jīvec ca prapitāmahaḥ |

	piṇḍau nipṛṇuyāt pūrvau bhojayet prapitāmaham ||

ṣaṭtriṃśanmatāt |

	pitrā śrāddhaṃ na kartavyaṃ putrāṇāṃ ca kathaṃcana |

	bhrātrā tu naiva kartavyaṃ bhrātṝṇāṃ ca yavīyasām ||

vṛddhavasiṣṭhaḥ |

	yatīnāṃ tu na saṃsargaḥ kartavyo 'tra sutaiḥ sadā |

	tridaṇḍagrahaṇād eva pretatvaṃ nopapadyate ||

daṇḍāpūpikānyāyenaitan mantavyam | yasya pretatvaṃ nāsti tasya maraṇe 'śaucaśaṅkaiva keti | prajāpatiḥ |

	sapiṇḍīkaraṇaṃ na syād yatīnāṃ caiva sarvadā |

	ahany ekādaśe prāpte pārvaṇam tu vidhīyate ||

bṛhaspatiḥ |

	navaśrāddhaṃ yater na syāt sapiṇḍīkaraṇaṃ tathā |

	ahany ekādaśe prāpte kuryāt tasya tu pārvaṇam ||

atra navaśrāddhagrahaṇam aśeṣapretatvavimuktyarthakarmopalakṣaṇārtham | tathā ca śātātapaḥ |

	ekoddiṣṭaṃ jalaṃ piṇḍam aśaucaṃ pretasatkriyām |

	na kuryāt pārvaṇād anyad brahmībhūtāya bhikṣave ||

brahmībhūto brahmāham asmīty upāsakaḥ | atha kālāḥ | tatra bhaviṣyatpurāṇam |

	sapiṇḍīkaraṇaṃ kuryād yajamāno hy anagnimān |

	anāhitāgneḥ pretasya pūrṇe 'bde bhatarṣabha ||

	niragniḥ sahapiṇḍatvaṃ pitur mātuś ca dharmataḥ |

	pūrṇe saṃvatsare kuryād vṛddhir vā yad ahar bhavet || **[539]**

kartur uddeśyasya ca niragnitve nimitte kālo 'tra niyamyate tasya karmāṅgatvena vidheyatvāt | yat tu kāle karma vidhīyate na karmaṇi kāla iti nyāyavidvacanaṃ tad anupādeyatvābhiprāyam | na punar avidheyatvaparam | tathā sati tasyāṅgatvaṃ na syāt | na hy avihitam aṅgaṃ bhavatīti | vṛddhir abhyudayaḥ | uśanā |

	pituḥ sapiṇḍīkaraṇaṃ vārṣike mṛtavatsare |

	ādhānādyupasaṃprāptāv etat prāg api vatsarāt ||

laghuhārītaḥ |

	bhrātā vā bhrātṛputro vā sapiṇḍaḥ śiṣya eva vā |

	sahapiṇḍakriyāṃ kṛtvā kuryād abhyudayaṃ tataḥ ||

sumantuḥ |

	anagnis tu yadā vīra bhavet kuryāt tadā gṛhī |

	pretaś ced agnimāṃs tu syāt tripakṣe vai sapiṇḍanam ||

atrāpi pūrvavat kālaniyamaḥ | anagnir yadā gṛhī bhaved ity anvayaḥ | śrāddhakartā gṛhī | tathā |

	yajamānāgnimān rājan pretaś cānagnimān bhavet |

	dvādaśāhe bhavet kāryaṃ sapiṇḍakaraṇaṃ sutaiḥ ||

jābāliḥ |

	sapiṇḍīkaraṇaṃ kuryāt pūrve darśe 'gnimān sutaḥ |

	parato daśarātrasya pūrṇe 'bde tu tathā paraḥ ||

daśarātragrahaṇam aśaucakālopalakṣaṇārtham | kātyāyanaḥ |

	ekādaśāhaṃ nirvartya pūrvaṃ darśād yathāvidhi |

	prakurvītāgnimān vipro mātāpitroḥ sapiṇḍanam ||

hārītaḥ |

	yā tu pūrvam amāvasyā mṛtāhād daśamād bhavet |

	sapiṇḍīkaraṇaṃ tasyāṃ kuryād evaṃ suto 'gnimān ||

	nāsapiṇḍy agnimān putraḥ pitṛyajñaṃ samācaret |

	na pārvaṇaṃ nābhyudayaṃ kurvan na labhate phalam ||

asti hi putrikāputrasya pārvaṇaśrāddhe mātur devatātvam,

	mātuḥ prathamataḥ piṇḍaṃ nirvapet putrikāsutaḥ |

ityādivacanāt | itarasyāpi mātā pārvaṇaśrāddhādau pitṛvat tṛptim upaitīti gamyate | uktaṃ hi |

	svena bhartrā samaṃ śrāddhaṃ mātā bhuṅkte svadhāsamam |

	pitāmahī ca svenaiva svenaiva prapitāmahī || iti **[540]**

na cānuddeśyamānāyās tat saṃbhavatīti sāpy uddeśyā | uddeśe ca sā sahabhāvenaiva niviśate na mukhyatvena | tenotpattiśiṣṭe 'pi pitrādidevatātve strīṇām api devatātvam aviruddham | tataś ca prāg darśān mātur api sapiṇḍīkaraṇavidhānaṃ yujyate | evaṃ śrāddheṣu sapatnīkāḥ pitṛpitāmahaprapitāmahā uddeś¥ā ity api siddham | sapiṇḍīkaraṇaṃ kartavyam ity anuvṛttau viṣṇuḥ: "mantravarjaṃ hi śūdrāṇāṃ dvādaśe 'hni" | amāvāsyāśrāddhakātiśūdraviṣayam etat | vacanabalād aśaucamadhy eva śrāddhakaraṇam | evaṃ ca sāgnikasya kartuḥ sapiṇḍīkaraṇakālās traya uktā bhavanti | dvādaśāhaḥ | tathāśaucāntaprathamadarśayor madhye kim apy ahaḥ | tathāśaucānantaraṃ prathamo darśa iti | anagnes tu catvāraḥ kālāḥ | yad āha gobhilaḥ: "pūrṇe saṃvatsare ṣaṇmāse tripakṣe vā yad ahar vā vṛddhir āpadyeta" | paiṭhīnasiḥ |

	sapiṇḍīkaraṇaṃ putraḥ pituḥ kurvīta yo 'gnimān |

	anagnes tu kriyā nānyā ekoddiṣṭād ṛte kvacit ||

etad anagneḥ saṃvatsarānte sapiṇḍīkaraṇaṃ kariṣyataḥ prathamasaṃvatsaravartiśrāddhviṣayam | vṛddhavasiṣṭhaḥ |

	śrāddhāni ṣoḍaśādattvā naiva kuryāt sapiṇḍanam |

	taddhānau tu kṛte pretaḥ pitṛtvaṃ na prapadyate ||

etad api pūrveṇa samānaviṣayam | viṣayāntare tu laugākṣir āha |

	yasya saṃvatsarād arvāk sapiṇḍīkaraṇaṃ bhavet |

	māsikaṃ codakumbhaṃ ca deyaṃ tasyāpi vatsaram || iti |

yat hārītenoktam: "mukhyaṃ śrāddhaṃ māsi māsi aparyāptāvṛttaṃ prati dvādaśāhena vā bhojyā ekāhe dvādaśāpi vā" iti, tad asamarthaviṣayam | apakṛṣyety anuvṛttāv āha uśanā |

	vṛddhiśrāddhavihīnas tu pretaśrāddhāni yaś caret |

	sa śrāddhī narake ghore pitṛbhiḥ saha pacyate ||

anupajātāyāṃ vṛddhau yaḥ pretaśrāddhān apakarṣed ity arthaḥ | samarthaviṣayaṃ caitat | śāṭyāyaniḥ |

	pretaśrāddhāni sarvāṇi sapiṇḍīkaraṇaṃ tathā |

	apakṛṣyāpi kurvīta kartuṃ nāndīmukhaṃ dvijaḥ || **[541]**

atha mātṛsapiṇḍīkaraṇam | tatra vṛddhaśātātapaḥ |

	mātuḥ sapiṇḍīkaraṇaṃ kathaṃ kāryaṃ sutair bhavet |

	pitāmahyā sahaivāsyāḥ sapiṇḍīkaraṇaṃ smṛtam ||

gārgyaḥ |

	patyaivaikena kartavyaṃ sapiṇḍīkaraṇaṃ striyāḥ |

	sā mṛtāpi hi tenaikyaṃ gatā mantrāhutivrataiḥ ||

sumantuḥ |

	pitā pitāmahe yojyaḥ pūrṇe saṃvatsare sutaiḥ |

	mātā mātāmahe tadvad ity āha bhagavāñ śivaḥ ||

yamaḥ |

	jīvatpitā pitāmahyā mātuḥ kuryāt sapiṇḍanam |

	pramītapitṛkaḥ pitrā tatpitrā putrikāsutaḥ ||

tatpitrā mātuḥ pitrety arthaḥ | pituḥ pitāmahyāś cābhāve vyavasthām āha śātātapaḥ |

	mṛtā yānugatā nāthaṃ sā tena saha piṇḍatām |

	arhati svargavāsaṃ ca yāvad ābhūmisaṃplavam || iti |

evaṃ ca saty anvārūḍhaviṣaye jīvantyām ajīvantyāṃ vā pitāmahyāṃ pitraiva saha mātuḥ sapiṇḍanaṃ kāryam | anyadā tu tatpitrā pitāmahyā veti siddham | yadi punaḥ prete pitari tenaiva sapiṇḍanaṃ syāt tadānvārūḍhaviṣayaṃ vacanam anarthakaṃ bhavet | tasya tv anvārūḍhā bhartraiva saha sapiṇḍanīyeti niyāmakatvenārthavattve sati pramītapitṛkaḥ pitretivacanaṃ na niyamaparaṃ śakyate vaktum ity aniyamasiddhiḥ | yat tu,

	mṛte pitari mātus tu na kuryāt sahapiṇḍatām |

	pitur eva sapiṇḍatve tasyā api kṛtaṃ bhavet ||

iti, tac cet samūlaṃ syāt tadāpadviṣayatayā neyam | laghuhārītaḥ |

	putreṇaiva tu kartavyaṃ sapiṇḍīkaraṇaṃ striyāḥ |

	puruṣasya punas tv anye bhrātṛputrādayo 'pi ye ||

mārkaṇḍeyapurāṇam |

	strīṇām apy evam evaitad ekoddiṣṭam udāhṛtam |

	sapiṇḍīkaraṇaṃ tāsāṃ putrābhāve na vidyate ||

bhartur abhāva etat | yad āha paiṭhīnasiḥ |

	aputrāyāṃ mṛtāyāṃ tu patiḥ kuryāt sapiṇḍanam |

	śvaśrvādibhiḥ sahaivāsyāḥ sapiṇḍīkaraṇam bhavet || **[542]**

śātātapaḥ |

	tanmātrā ca pitāmahyā tacchvaśrvā tu sapiṇḍanam |

	āsurādivivāheṣu vinnānāṃ yoṣitāṃ smṛtam ||

tanmātrā mātur mātrety arthaḥ | pitāmahī ca mātur eva | atha mātur gotranirṇayaḥ | tatra bṛhaspatiḥ |

	bhartur gotreṇa nāmnā ca mātuḥ kuryāt sapiṇḍanam |

	tūṣṇīṃ dampatipiṇḍābhyāṃ kuśaur antarayan pitṝn ||

antarayaṃs tirodadhānaḥ | śātātapaḥ |

	kuryād gotreṇa dauhitro mātulenāvanejanam |

	piṇḍanirvapaṇaṃ caiva mātur mātāmahasya ca ||

avanejanaṃ jaladānam | yad āha laugākṣiḥ |

	mātāmahasya gotreṇa mātuḥ piṇḍodakakriyām |

	kurvīta putrikāputra evam āha prajāpatiḥ ||

mārkaṇḍeyaḥ |

	brāhmādiṣu vivāheṣu yā tūḍhā kanyakā bhavet |

	bhartṛgotreṇa kartavyās tasyāḥ piṇḍodakakriyāḥ ||

	āsurādivivāheṣu pitṛgotreṇa dharmavit ||

mātuḥ pitṛgotreṇety arthaḥ | vyāsaḥ |

	patyā sahaikatā tāvad yāvat putro na jāyate |

	putrikāyāḥ sutotpattau tasyaikatvaṃ nivartate || 1.252, 253 ||

	**arvāk sapiṇḍīkaraṇaṃ yasya saṃvatsarād bhavet |**

**	tasyāpy annaṃ sodakumbhaṃ dadyād varṣaṃ dvijanmane || 1.254 ||**

saṃvatsarād arvāg iti saṃbandhaḥ | varṣam ity atyantasaṃyoge dvitīyā | yasyāpi pretasya saṃvatsarapūrteḥ pūrvam eva dvādaśāhādau sapiṇḍīkaraṇaṃ bhavet, tasyāpi saṃvatsaraṃ yāvat sodakumbham annaṃ dvije dadyāt | tasyeti ṣaṣṭhī caturthyarthe dvijanmana iti caturthī samyak saṃpradānārthā | dadyāt saṃvatsaraṃ dvija iti pāṭhe saptamī yathārthā, śrāddhe brāhmaṇasyāhavanīyārthatvāt | saṃvatsaram iti cātyantasaṃyoge dvitīyā | ataḥ saṃvatsaraṃ yāvat pratyaham annaṃ deyam | tathā ca āpastambaḥ |

	yasya saṃvatsarād arvāk sapiṇḍīkaraṇaṃ kṛtam |

	abdam ambughaṭaṃ dadyāt pratyahaṃ tv annasaṃyutam || **[543]**

yal laghuhārīta āha |

	sapiṇḍīkaraṇe vṛtte pṛthaktvaṃ nopapadyate |

	pṛthaktve tu kṛte paścāt punaḥ kāryā sapiṇḍatā ||

śātātapaḥ |

	sapiṇḍīkaraṇād ūrdhvaṃ yatra yatra pradīyate |

	tatra pārvaṇavac chrāddhaṃ jñeyam abhyudayād ṛte || iti |

tasyāyam apavādaḥ | tasyāpy annaṃ sodakumbham ity ekavacanaśravaṇāt | apiśabdāt saṃvatsarānte sapiṇḍīkaraṇe 'py etat kāryam || 1.254 ||

_aparam apy apavādam āha_ |

	**mṛtāhani tu kartavyaṃ pratimāsaṃ tu vatsaram |**

**	pratisaṃvatsaraṃ caivamādyam ekādaśe 'hani || 1.255 ||**

yan mṛtāhani saṃvatsaraṃ yāvat pratimāsaṃ yac ca tatraivāhani prativarṣaṃ yac cādyaṃ yac caikādaśe 'hani śrāddhaṃ tad evaṃ kāryam | ekoddiṣṭavidhānenety arthaḥ | ādyaśabdena navaśrāddhāny ucyante | māsikānām ābdikasya caikoddiṣṭatvaṃ na nityaṃ pārvaṇavadbhāvasyāpi vidhānāt | yad āha jātūkarṇyaḥ |

	pituḥ pitṛgaṇasthasya kuryāt pārvaṇavat sutaḥ |

	pratyabdaṃ pratimāsaṃ ca vidhir jñeyaḥ sanātanaḥ ||

pitṛgaṇasthaḥ sapiṇḍitaḥ | tatra māsikeṣu [na] vyavasthitavikalpo vyavasthākapābhāvāt | ata evāha kātyāyanaḥ |

	sapiṇḍīkaraṇād ūrdhvaṃ na dadyāt pratimāsikam |

	ekoddiṣṭavidhānena dadyād ity āha śaunakaḥ || \
atraikoddiṣṭavidhānena māsikaṃ dadyād ity ekaḥ kalpa uktaḥ | na dadyād ity aparaḥ | sāṃvatsarikaśrāddhe tu vyavasthitavikalpaḥ | tatra kṣetrajaurasaputrikāputrāṇām agnimattvaṃ pārvaṇavattve vyavasthāpakam | tathā śrāddhoddeśyasyāmāvāsyāyāṃ pretapakṣe vā mṛtatvaṃ yatitvaṃ vā yena kenacit kriyamāṇasya śrāddhasya pārvaṇavattvavyavasthāpakam | śastrahataśrāddhasya kṛṣṇacaturdaśyāṃ kriyamāṇatvaṃ sarvam eva kartāraṃ pratyekoddiṣṭatvavyavasthāpakam | tathā kartur uddeśyasya vānagnitvaṃ tathāgnimato 'pi kartur aurasakṣetrajaputrikāputravyatiriktatvam ekoddiṣṭatvavyavasthāpakam | mṛtāhikād anyat saṃkrāntyuparāgamahālayādikālavihitaṃ tatraikoddiṣṭatayā vidhir eva nāstīti tat pārvaṇavad eva kāryam | etāṃ ca vyavasthām āhur munayaḥ | tatra tāvaj jātūkarṇyaḥ |

**[544]**	pratyabdaṃ pārvaṇenaiva vidhinā kṣetrajaurasau |

	kuryātām itare kuryur ekoddiṣṭaṃ sutā daśa ||

kārṣṇājiniḥ |

	agnipradhānaṃ pārvaṇenaiva vidhinā kṣetrajaurasau |

	kuryātām itare kuryur ekoddiṣṭaṃ sutā daśa ||

kārṣṇājiniḥ |

	agnipradhānaṃ sarveṣām anuṣṭhānaṃ gṛhāśrame |

	tad yogāt kṛtasāhāyyaḥ sarvatrārhati pārvaṇam ||

	niragner aurasasyoktam ekoddiṣṭaṃ mṛtāhani |

	pratyabdaṃ pārvaṇaṃ sāgner anyeṣāṃ na tu pārvaṇam ||

yat tu smṛtyantaram,

	bahvagnayas tu ye viprā ye caikāgnaya eva ca |

	teṣāṃ sapiṇḍanād ūrdhvam ekoddiṣṭaṃ na pārvaṇam ||

iti, tat kṣetrajādivyatiriktaviṣayam | aputrakaśrāddhaviṣayaṃ vā | putrikāputro 'py auravasat kuryāt tatsamatvāt | tathā ca vyāsaḥ |

	mukhya eva sutaḥ kuryāt sapiṇḍīkaraṇaṃ pituḥ |

	aurasas tu suto mukhyas tatsamaḥ putrikāsutaḥ ||

śaṅkhaḥ |

	amāvāsyākṣayo yasya pretapakṣe 'tha vā yadi |

	sapiṇḍīkaraṇād ūrdhvaṃ tasyoktaḥ pārvaṇo vidhiḥ ||

pretapakṣo bhādrapadāparapakṣaḥ | śātātapaḥ |

	ekoddiṣṭaṃ jalaṃ piṇḍam aśaucaṃ pretasatkriyām |

	na kuryāt pārvaṇād anyad brahmībhūtāya bhikṣave ||

gargaḥ |

	caturdaśyāṃ tu yac chrāddhaṃ sapiṇḍīkaraṇe kṛte |

	tad ekoddiṣṭavidhinā kartavyaṃ śastraghātine ||

tathā |

	sapiṇḍīkaraṇād ūrdhvam mṛte kṛṣṇacaturdaśīm |

	pratisaṃvatsarād anyad ekoddiṣṭaṃ na pārvaṇam ||

prajāpatiḥ |

	saṃkrāntāv uparāge ca parvotsavamahālaye |

	nivaped atra piṇḍāṃs trīn ekatas tu kṣaye 'hani ||

kātyāyanaḥ |

	yāni pañcadaśādīni aputrasyetarāṇy api |

	ekasyaivātra dātavyam aputrāyāś ca sarvadā ||

āpastambaḥ |

	aputrā ye mṛtāḥ kecit striyo vā puruṣāś ca ye |

	teṣām api ca deyaṃ syād ekoddiṣṭaṃ na pārvaṇam ||

atha mṛtāhāparijñānaviṣayāṇi vākyāny ucyante | tatra bṛhaspatiḥ |

**[545]**	na jñāyate mṛtāhaś cet pramīte proṣite sati |

	māsaś cet prativijñātas tad darśe syān mṛtāhani ||

mṛtāhe yat kāryaṃ tad vijñātamāsāmāvāsyāyāṃ kāṛyam ity arthaḥ |

	yadā māso na vijñāto vijñātaṃ dinam eva tu |

	tadā mārgaśiromāsi māghe vā taddinaṃ bhavet ||

	dinamāsau na vijñātau maraṇasya yadā punaḥ |

	prasthānadinamāsau tu grāhyau pūrvoktayā diśā || iti |

atra tithau dinaśabdaḥ | pūrvoktayā diśety asyāyam arthaḥ — proṣitamaraṇe māsaparijñāne mṛtatithijñānābhāve sati parijñātamāsāmāvāsyāyāṃ tasya mṛtāhakālaḥ | tathā mṛtatithiparijñāne māsajñānābhāve sati tadā mārgaśiromāsi māghamāse vā tasyāṃ parijñātāyāṃ tithau tasya mṛtāhakālaḥ | tathaiva mṛtatithimāsāparijñāne prasthānadinamāsau grāhyau yasyāṃ tithau māse vā prasthānaṃ kṛtaṃ tatraiva tasya mṛtāhakālas tatrāpy abhāve mṛtavārtāśravaṇadine mṛtāhakāla iti bhāvaḥ | pracetāḥ: "aparijñāte mṛtāhe 'māvāsyāyāṃ śravaṇadivase vā" | jātūkarṇyaḥ |

	pitari proṣite yasya na vārtā naiva vāgatiḥ |

	ūrdhvaṃ pañcadaśād varṣāt kṛtvā tatpratirūpakam ||

	kuryāt tasya ca saṃskāraṃ yathoktavidhinā tataḥ |

	tadādīny eva sarvāṇi śeṣakarmāṇi saṃcaret ||

smṛtyantaram |

	na labhyate śarīraṃ cel labhyante 'sthīni cet tadā |

	ghṛtena tāni saṃsicya saṃskuryād vidhinā mṛtam ||

	dagdhāny asthīni saṃprāpya kṣīreṇāplāvya tāni tu |

	teṣām api na lābhaś cet palāśānāṃ śatatrayam ||

	dvāṣaṣṭyadhikam ādāya kuryāt tatpratirūpakam |

	tatra dvātriṃśatiṃ(taṃ) mūrdhni kaṇṭhe ṣaṣṭiṃ tataḥ param ||

	vakṣasy aśītiṃ jaghane viṃśatiṃ viṃśatidvayam |

	bāhvor daśāṅgulīṣv atra muṣkayoḥ ṣaṭ ca sādhane ||

	catvāry ūrudvaye ṣaṣṭiṃ viṃśatiṃ jānunos tataḥ |

	viṃśatiṃ jaṅghayoḥ paścād daś pādāṅgulīṣu ca ||

**[546]**	nyaset palāśavṛttānām ūrṇāsūtreṇa veṣṭayet |

	lepayed yavapiṣṭena saṃskuryād vidhivat tataḥ ||

	kṣiped udakadhārāṃ tu saṃskārānte sumantataḥ ||

vṛddhamanuḥ |

	jīvan yadi sa āgacched ghṛtakuṇḍe nimajjya tam |

	uddhṛtya snāpayitvāsya jātakarmādi kārayet ||

	vratacaryā dvādaśāhaṃ trirātram atha vāsya tu |

	snātvodvaheta tāṃ bhāryām anyāṃ vā tadabhāvataḥ ||

	agnīn ādhāya vidhivad vrātyastomena vā yajet |

	tathaindrāgneyapaśunā giriṃ gatvā sa tatra tu ||

	iṣṭim āyuṣmatīṃ kuryād īpsitāṃś ca kratūṃs tataḥ ||

āyuṣmatīm iṣṭim āyuṣkāmeṣṭim ity arthaḥ | māsikam ābdikaṃ ca mṛtāhe kāryam ity uktam | tatrāhaḥśabdenāhorātra upalakṣyate | sa ca trividhaḥ — sāvanaḥ saura aindavaś ceti | tad uktaṃ brahmasiddhānte |

	sāvanaṃ syād ahorātram udayād udayo ravaḥ |

	sauras triṃśas tu rāśyaṃśas tithisaṃbhogam aindavam ||

meṣāsirāśes triṃśam aṃśaṃ yāvatā kālena ravir bhuṅkte tāvān kālaḥ sauro 'horātraḥ | aindavas tu pratipadāditithiparimitaḥ | sa eva mṛtāhanīty atra vivakṣitaḥ | tad uktam |

	māsapakṣatithispṛṣṭe yo yasmin mriyate 'hani |

	pratyabdaṃ ca tathābhūtaṃ kṣayāhaṃ tasya taṃ viduḥ ||

māso 'pi pūrvavat trividha eva | tad uktaṃ brahmasiddhānta eva |

	darśād darśaṃ cāndras triṃśaddivasas tu sāvano māsaḥ |

	ravisaṃkrāntikacihnaḥ sauro māso 'bhigadyate tajjñaiḥ ||

tathā |

	cāndraḥ śuklādidarśāntaḥ sāvanas triṃśatā dinaiḥ |

	ekarāśau ravir yāvat kālaṃ māsaḥ sa bhāskaraḥ ||

māsaś cāndra eva pitṛkārye grāhyaḥ | smaranti hi |

	vivāhādau smṛtaḥ sauro yajñādau sāvanaḥ smṛtaḥ |

	ābdike pitṛkārye ca māsaś cāndramasaḥ smṛtaḥ || **[547]**

laghuhārītaḥ |

	cakravat parivarteta sūryaḥ kālavaśād yataḥ |

	ataḥ sāṃvatsaraṃ śrāddhaṃ kartavyaṃ māsacihnitam ||

	māsacihnaṃ tu kartavyaṃ pauṣamādhādyam eva hi |

	ataś cāndravidhānena māsaḥ sa parikīrtitaḥ ||

pauṣādisaṃjñā cāndrasyaiva hi | tathā hi — puṣyeṇa yuktaś candro yasyāṃ sā pauṣī sā yasmin māsi sa pauṣo māsaḥ | evaṃ māghādayo 'pi | yady api dvyahatryahādau paurṇamāsī bhavati tathāpi nāsau pauṣādisaṃjñakaḥ | māsārthamāsasaṃvatsarāṇām eva pauṣādiḥ saṃjñā na dvyahādes tad āha pāṇiniḥ: "sāsmin paurṇamāsīti saṃjñāyām" (Pāṇ 4.2.21) iti | na ca saurasāvanamāsayor uktaprakārapaurṇamāsīniyamo 'sti | tasmāc cāndra eva māso māsika ābdike ca grāhyaḥ | yat punaḥ smṛtyantare 'py uktam,

	yasmin rāśau gate sūrye vipattiṃ yāti mānavaḥ |

	tadrāśāv eva kartavyaṃ pitṛkāryaṃ mṛtāhani ||

adhimāsamaraṇaviṣayam etat | yad āha sa eva,

	adhimāse vipattiś cet sauraṃ māsaṃ samāśrayet |

	sa eva divasas tasya śrāddhapiṇḍodakādiṣu || iti |

adhimāsamṛtasya punas tad adhimāsaprāptau satyām etad veditavyam | tathā ca bhṛguḥ |

	malamāsamṛtānāṃ tu yac chrāddhaṃ prativatsaram |

	malamāse tu tat kāryaṃ nānyeṣāṃ tu kathaṃcana ||

[anyeṣāṃ malamāsamadhye 'mṛtānām | malamāsamadhye sāṃvatsarikaṃ na kāryam | kiṃ tu tadvyapagama ity arthaḥ | ] kaḥ punar adhimāso nāmety apekṣāyām āha gargaḥ |

	yadā cāndreṣu māseṣu meṣādiṃ kramate raviḥ |

	caitrādays tadocyante tadabhāve 'dhimāsakaḥ ||

laghuhārīto 'pi |

	indrāgnī yatra hūyete māsādiḥ sa prakīrtitaḥ |

	agnīṣomau smṛtau madhye samāptau pitṛsomakau ||

	tam atikramya tu yadā ravir gacchet kadācana |

	ādyo malimluco jñeyo dvitīyo prakṛtaḥ smrtaḥ ||

indrāgnī yatre hūyete iti śuklapratipada upalakṣaṇam | agnīṣomāv iti kṛṣṇapratipadaḥ | **[548]** pitṛsomāv iti darśasya | etena cāndro māsa upalakṣitaḥ | taṃ māsaṃ samatikramyānyasmin māse yadā sūryo rāśyantaraṃ gacchet tadā pūrvo malimlucaḥ | uttaraḥ prakṛtaḥ | śātātapaḥ |

	sinīvālīm atikramya yadā saṃkramate raviḥ |

	malamāsas tu sa proktas tat kāryaṃ tūttare bhavet ||

sinīvālīṃ iti sakalasinīvālyantamāsābhiprāyam | kāṭhakagṛhya |

	yasmin māse na saṃkrāntiḥ saṃkrāntidvayam eva vā |

	malamāsaḥ sa vijñeyo māse triṃśattame bhavet ||

tatra malimluce 'pi māsikaṃ śrāddhaṃ kāryam ity āha kuthumiḥ |

	abdam ambughaṭaṃ dadyād annaṃ cāmiṣasaṃyutam |

	saṃvatsare vivṛddhe 'pi pratimāsaṃ ca māsikam ||

hārītaḥ |

	asaṃkrānte 'pi kartavyam ābdikaṃ prathamaṃ dvijaiḥ |

	tathaiva māsikaṃ pūrvaṃ sapiṇḍīkaraṇaṃ tathā ||

pūrvaṃ prathamasaṃvatsaravihitaṃ māsikam | na tu darśaśrāddham, tasya hi tatra niṣedham āha ṛṣyaśṛṅgaḥ |

	saṃvatsarātireko vai māso yaḥ syāt trayodaśaḥ |

	tasmiṃs trayodaśaṃ śrāddhaṃ na kuryād indusaṃkṣaye ||

yat tu śātātapenoktam,

	ekasaṃjñau yadā māsau syātāṃ saṃvatsare kvacit |

	tatrādye pitṛkāryāṇi devakaryāṇi cottare ||

iti, tat sapiṇḍīkaraṇaparyantapitṛkāryaviṣayam | ata eva laghuhārītaḥ |

	sapiṇḍīkaraṇād ūrdhvaṃ yat kiṃcic chrāddikaṃ bhavet |

	iṣṭaṃ vāpy atha vā pūrtaṃ tatra kuryān malimluce ||

yat tu satyavrataḥ,

	varṣe varṣe tu yac chrāddhaṃ mātāpitror mṛtāhani |

	malamāse na kartavyaṃ vyāghrasya vacanaṃ yathā ||

iti, tad adhimāsād anyatra mṛtasya prathamābdikaśrāddhavyatiriktaśrāddhaviṣayam | yatu tu gabhastivākyam,

	na kuryān malamāse tu karmī karma kathaṃcana |

	muktvā naimittikaṃ śrāddhaṃ tad dhi tatraiva kīrtitam ||

	ekoddiṣṭaṃ hi yac chrāddhaṃ tan naimittikam ucyate |

	tat kāryaṃ pūrvamānena kālādhikye 'pi dharmataḥ || **[549]**

iti, tat sapiṇḍīkaraṇāt prāktanaikoddiṣṭaviṣayam | yac ca vṛddhavasiṣṭhenoktam,

	śrāddhīye 'hanit saṃprāpte adhimāso bhaved yadi |

	śrāddhadvayaṃ prakurvīta hy evaṃ kurvan na muhyati ||

iti, tan māsikaviṣayam | vārṣikaviṣaye tu laghuhārītaḥ |

	pratyabdaṃ dvādaśe māsi kāryā piṇḍakriyā budhaiḥ |

	kvacit trayodaśe 'pi syād ādyaṃ muktvā tu vatsaram ||

asyārthaḥ — sarvadā dvādaśe māsi parisamāpte trayodaśe ca prāpte sāṃvatsarikaṃ kāryam adhimādopanipāte tu trayodaśe vyatīte caturdaśe ca pravṛtte piṇḍakriyā kāryā | ādye tu saṃvatsare 'dhimāse trayodaśa evābdikaṃ kāryam iti | prasaṅgād anyad api malamāsaviṣayaṃ kiṃcid ucyate | tatra bṛhaspatiḥ |

	nityanaimittike kuryāt prayataḥ san malimluce |

	tīrthasnānaṃ gajacchāyāṃ pretaśrāddhaṃ tathaiva ca ||

matsyapurāṇe |

	candrasūryagrahe caiva maraṇe putrajanmani |

	malamāse 'pi deyaṃ syād dattam akṣayakārakam ||

vṛddhamanuḥ |

	agnyādheyaṃ pratiṣṭhāṃ ca yajñadānavratāni ca |

	vedavratavṛṣotsargacūḍākaraṇamekhalāḥ ||

	maṅgalyam abhiṣekaṃ ca malamāse vivarjayet ||

vṛṣotsargasya ca naikādaśāhikasya pratiṣedhaḥ | tasya niyatakālatvāt pretopakārakatvāc ca |

	bāle vā yadi vā vṛddhe śukre cāstam upāgate |

	malamāsa ivaitāni varjayed devadarśanam ||

	vāpīkūpataḍāgādipratiṣṭhā yajñakarma ca |

	na kuryān malamāse ca mahādānavratāni ca ||

devadarśanaṃ someśvarādidevadarśanaṃ tac cātra prathamaṃ vivakṣitam | gṛhyapariśiṣṭāt |

	avaṣaṭkārahomāś ca parva cāgrā(gra)yaṇaṃ tathā |

	malamāse 'pi kartavyaṃ kāmyā iṣṭīr vivarjayet ||

parāśaraḥ |

	upākarma tathotsargaprasavāhotsavāṣṭakāḥ |

	māsavṛddhau parāḥ kāryā varjayitvā ca paitṛkam ||

prasavanimittaṃ jātakarmādi kāryam eva | ata evāha satyavrataḥ |

**[550]**	jātakarmaṇi yac chrāddhaṃ navaśrāddhaṃ tathaiva ca |

	pratisaṃvatsaraṃ śrāddhaṃ malamāse 'pi tat smṛtam || iti |

ata eva prasavanimitto 'nya evotsavaḥ śiṣṭācāraprāpto 'tra pratiṣidhyate | paitṛkam iti candrasūryoparāgagajacchāyāśrāddhādi kathyate | yasyāsvśyakasya nāśti kālāntaram | ata eva matsyapurāṇam |

	candrasūryagrahe caiva maraṇe putrajanmani |

	malamāse 'pi deyaṃ syād dattam akṣayakārakam ||

satyaḥ |

	devatārāmavāpyādipratiṣṭhodaṅmukhe ravau |

	dakṣiṇāśāmukhe kurvan na tatphalam avāpnuyāt ||

prāsaṅgikaṃ parisamāpya prakṛtam anusarāmaḥ || 1.255. ||

	**piṇḍāṃs tu go'javiprebhyo dadyād agnau jale 'pi vā |**

**	prakṣipet satsu vipreṣu dvijocchiṣṭaṃ na mārjayet || 1.256 ||**

pārvaṇādiśrāddhasaṃbandhinaḥ piṇḍān gochāgaviprāṇām anyatamāya dadyād anyatamaṃ bhojayed ity arthaḥ | atha vāgnau jale 'pi vā prakṣipet stasu vipreṣu svasmād āsanād anutthiteṣu tad ucchiṣtaṃ na mārjayen na śodhayet | piṇḍān iti bahuvacanam avivakṣitam | tena patnīprāśite madhyamapiṇḍe piṇḍadvayasyāpi pratipattiḥ kāryā | atra matsyapurāṇam |

	piṇḍāṃs tu go'javiprebhyo dadyād agnau jale 'pi vā |

	viprānte vātha vidhivad vayobhir athavāśayet ||

	patnīṃ vā madhyamaṃ piṇḍam āśrayed vinayānvitām |

	ādhatta pitaro garbham antaḥ sāmtānavardhanam ||

vayāṃsi pakṣiṇaḥ | manuḥ |

	pativratā dharmapatnī pitṛpūjanatatparā |

	madhyamaṃ tu tataḥ piṇḍam adyāt samyak sutārthinī ||

	āyuṣmantaṃ sutaṃ sūte yaśomedhāsamanvitam |

	dhanavantaṃ prajāvantaṃ sāttvikaṃ dhārmikaṃ śucim ||

bṛhaspatiḥ |

	anyadeśasthitā patnī rogiṇī garbhiṇī tathā |

	tadā taṃ jīrṇavṛṣabhaś chāgo vā bhoktum arhati ||

śaṅkhalikhitau: "evaṃ varān yācayitvā namaskṛtya piṇḍān apsu vinyased agnau vā nikṣipet | patnī vā madhayaṃ piṇḍam aśnīyād ārtavasnātā | **[551]** agṛhītagarbhātrārtavasnātety ucyate | yamaḥ |

	apsv ekaṃ plāvayet piṇḍam ekaṃ patnyai nivedayet |

	ekaṃ ca juhuyād agnau trayaḥ piṇḍāḥ prakīrtitāḥ ||

vāyupurāṇe |

	piṇḍam agnau sadā dadyād bhogārthī satataṃ naraḥ |

	patnyai prajārthī dadyād vai madyamaṃ mantrapūrvakam ||

	uttamāṃ gatim anvicchan gobhyo nityaṃ prayacchati |

	ājñāṃ prajñāṃ yaśaḥ kīrtim apsu piṇḍaṃ nidhāpayet ||

	prārthayan dīrgham āyuś ca vāyasebhyaḥ prayacchati |

	ākāśaṃ gamayed apsu sthito vā dakṣiṇāmukhaḥ ||

	pitṝṇāṃ sthānam ākāśaṃ dakṣiṇādik tathaiva ca ||

dvijocciṣṭamārjane vasiṣṭho 'nyathāha |

	śrāddhe nodvāsanīyāni ucchiṣṭāny ā dinakṣayāt |

	cyotante vai svadhādhārās tāḥ pibanty akṛtodakāḥ || 1.256 ||

_yena dravyeṇa yāvatī tṛptiḥ pitṝṇāṃ bhavati tad āha_ |

	**haviṣyānnena vai māsaṃ pāyasena tu vatsaram |**

**	mātsyahāriṇakaurabhraśākunacchāgapārṣataiḥ || 1.257 ||**

**	eiṇarauravavārāhaśāśair māṃsair yathākramam |**

**	māsavṛddhyābhitṛpyanti dattair hi pitāmahāḥ || 1.258 ||**

haviṣyānnena pradattena pitṛpitāmahādyā uddeśyā māsaṃ tṛpyanti | haviṣyam āha manuḥ |

	munyannāni payaḥsomau māṃsaṃ yac cānupaskṛtam |

	akṣāralavaṇaṃ caiva prakṛtyā havir ucyate ||

payasi śṛta odanaḥ pāyasaḥ | tena dattena vatsaraṃ yāvat pitrādayas tṛpyanti | tad uktam,

	saṃvatsaraṃ tu gavyena payasā pāyasena ca |

iti manunā | pāyasaś cāpratiṣiddhapayo(yā) grāhyaḥ | tatra payoviśeṣaniṣedham āha mārkaṇḍeyaḥ |

	mārgam āvikam auṣṭraṃ ca sarvam aikaśaphaṃ ca yat |

	māhiṣaṃ cāmaraṃ caiva dhenvā yac cāpy anidaśam ||

**[552]**	pitrarthaṃ me prayacchasvety uktvā yac cāpy upāhṛtam |

	varjanīyaṃ sadā sadbhis tat payaḥ śrāddhakarmaṇi ||

matsyasyedaṃ māṃsaṃ mātsyaṃ tena dattena dvau māsau pitrādayas tṛpyanti | matsyaś cātra bhakṣaṇārtha eva pāṭīnaprabhṛtir jñeyaḥ | hariṇasyedaṃ hāriṇam | evam aurabhrādiṣu māsasaṃkhyāvṛddhir draṣṭavyā | urabhro meṣaḥ | tasyedam aurabhram | evaṃ śāukanādīny api | śakuniḥ pakṣī | so 'py atra śiṣṭabhojanīya eva grāhyaḥ | chāgaḥ prasiddhaḥ | pṛṣataś citramṛgaḥ | eṇaḥ kṛṣṇamṛgaḥ | lohitas tu hariṇaḥ | tad uktam āyurvede |

	eṇaḥ kṛṣṇas tayor jñeyas tāmro hariṇa ucyate |

rurur mṛgaviśeṣaḥ | varāho 'trāraṇyo na grāmyo 'tyantābhakṣyatvāt | śaśasyedaṃ śāśam | atra manuḥ |

	tilair vrīhiyavair māṣair adbhir mūlaphalena vā |

	dattena māsaṃ prīyante pitaro vidhivan nṛṇām ||

tathā |

	vādhrīṇasasya māṃsena tṛptir dvādaśavārṣikī ||

viṣṇuḥ: "tilair vrīhiyavair māṣair adbhir mūlaphalaiḥ śākaiḥ syāmakaiḥ priyaṅgubhir nīvārair mudgair godhūmair māsaṃ prīyante | nava gāvayenaikādaśa tūpareṇājena" | gavayasyedaṃ gāvayam | tena nava māsān prīyante | tūparaḥ śṛṅgahīnaḥ | śaṅkhaḥ |

	lājān madhuyutān dadyāt saktūñ śarkarayā saha |

	dadyāc chrāddhe prayatnena śṛṅgāṭakagavedhukam ||

śṛṅgāṭakaṃ jalajaṃ trikaṇṭakam | gavedhukaṃ śaṅkhākāraṃ tṛṇaviśeṣaphalam || 1.257, 258 ||

	**khaḍgāmiṣaṃ mahāśalkaṃ madhu munyannam eva ca |**

**	lohāmiṣaṃ kālaśākaṃ māṃsaṃ vādhrīṇasasya ca || 1.259 ||**

**	yad dadāti gayāsthaś ca sarvam ānantyam aśnute |**

khaḍgo gaṇḍakākhyo mṛgaviśeṣaḥ | tad āmiṣam | mahāśalko matsyaviśeṣaḥ | tena ca tanmāṃsaṃ lakṣyate | madhu kṣaudram | munyannam āraṇyaṃ nīvārādi sasyam | loho lohitacchāgas tadāmiṣam | kālaśākaḥ prasiddhaḥ | vādhrīṇasa ukto nigame |

	tripibaṃ tv indriyakṣīṇaṃ śvetaṃ vṛddham ajāpatim |

	vādhrīṇasaṃ tu taṃ prāhur yājñikāḥ śrāddhakarmaṇi || **[553]**

yasya pibataḥ karṇau jalaṃ spṛśataḥ sa tripibas tribhir mukhena karṇābhyāṃ ca pibantīti vyutpattyā | kṣīṇendriyaṃ saṃbhogākṣamam ajāpatim ajam ity arthaḥ | tasya māṃsam | tathā |

	kṛṣṇagrīvo raktaśirāḥ śvetapakṣo vihaṃgamaḥ |

	sa vai vādhrīṇasaḥ proktaḥ ity eṣā naigamī śrutiḥ ||

tasya māṃsaṃ vā | tathā gayāstho yad dadāti ca | etat sarvam ānantyam akṣayatvam aśnute prāpnoti | etajjanitā tṛptir anantā bhavatīti tātparyārthaṃ | gayāgrahaṇaṃ pradarśanārtham | ata evoktam |

	gaṅgādvāre prayāge ca naimiṣe puṣkare 'rbude |

	saṃnihityāṃ gayāyāṃ ca śrāddham akṣayatāṃ vrajet ||

atra vāyupurāṇam |

	śyāmākair ikṣubhiś caiva pitṝṇāṃ sārvakālikam |

	kuryād āgrayaṇaṃ yas tu sa śīghraṃ siddhim āpnuyāt ||

	śyāmākā hastināmāno viddhi tān yajñaniḥsṛtān |

	praśāntikāḥ priyaṅguś ca grāhyāḥ syuḥ śrāddhakarmaṇi ||

	etāny api samāni syuḥ śyāmākānāṃ sadā guṇaiḥ |

	kṛṣṇamāṣās tilāś caiva śreṣṭhāḥ syur yavaśālayaḥ ||

	mahāyavā vrīhiyavās tathaiva ca madhūlikāḥ |

	kṛṣṇāḥ śvetā lohitāś ca grāhyāḥ syuḥ śrāddhakarmaṇi ||

	bilvāmalakamṛdvīkāpanasāmrātadāḍimam |

	bhavyapālevatākṣoṭakharjūrāmalakāni ca ||

	kaśeruḥ kovidāraś ca tālakandaṃ tathā bisam |

	tamālaṃ śatakandaṃ ca madhyāluḥ śītakandakam ||

	kalāyaṃ kālaśākaṃ ca suniṣaṇṇaṃ suvarcalā |

	māṃsaṃ śākaṃ dadhikṣīraṃ cañcur vetrāṅkuras tathā ||

	kaṭphalaṃ kaṅkaṇī drākṣā lakucaṃ mocam eva ca |

	karkandhur jīrakaṃ cāraṃ tindukaṃ madhusāhvyam ||

	vaikaṅkataṃ nāgarikaṃ śṛṅgāṭakaparūṣakam |

	pippalī maricaṃ caiva paṭolaṃ bṛhatīphalam ||

	sugandhimatsyamāṃsaṃ ca kalāyāḥ sarva eva ca |

	evamādīni cānyāni svādūni madhurāṇi ca ||

**[554]**	nāgaraṃ cātra vai deyaṃ dīrghamūlakam eva ca ||

ādityapurāṇe |

	madhukaṃ rāmaṭhaṃ caiva karpūraṃ maricaṃ guḍam |

	śrāddhakarmaṇi śastāni saindhavaṃ trapusaṃ tathā ||

mārkaṇḍeyapurāṇe |

	yavavrīhī sagodhūmau tilamudgāḥ sasarṣapāḥ |

	priyaṅgavaḥ kovidāro niṣpāvāś cātra śobhanāḥ ||

vāyupurāṇe |

	bhakṣān pūpaṃ karambhaṃ ca iṣṭakāghṛtapūrakān |

	kṛsarā madhusarpiś ca payaḥ pāyasam eva ca ||

	snigdham uṣṇaṃ ca yo dadyād agniṣṭomaphalaṃ labhet |

	dadhi gavyam asaṃsṛṣṭaṃ bhakṣyān nānāvidhān api ||

	datvā na śocati śrāddhe varṣāsu ca maghāsu ca |

	ghṛtena bhojayed viprān ghṛtaṃ bhūmau samusṛjet ||

	śarkarākṣīrasaṃyuktāḥ pṛthukā nityam akṣayāḥ |

	syuś ca saṃvatsaraṃ prītāḥ kukarair meṣakaiṇakaiḥ ||

	saktūṃl lājāṃs tathā pūpān kulmāṣān vyañjanaiḥ saha |

	sarpiḥsnigdhāni sarvāṇi dadhnā saṃskṛtasya bhojayet ||

	śrāddheṣv etāni yo dadyāt pitaraḥ prīṇayanti tam ||

matsyapurāṇe |

	yat kiṃcin madhunā miśraṃ gokṣīraghṛtapāyasaiḥ |

	dattam akṣayam ity āhuḥ pitaraḥ pañca devatāḥ ||

brahmapurāṇe |

	alābuṃ grīvakaṃ cāṇu karkarīṃ trapusaṃ tathā |

	madhūkaṃ nārikelaṃ ca lakucaṃ ca harītakīm ||

	mārākṣaṃ dadhiśākaṃ ca śākam utpalasaṃjñitam |

	bhṛṅgarājam aduṣṭāni vanyāni ca nivedayet ||

	atha mūlāni deyāni śuṇṭhyārdrakabisāni ca |

	tamālaṃ śatakandaṃ ca bahusūcī ca kaṇṭakī ||

	kūrcālakaṃ ca piṇḍālaṃ dīrghamūlaṃ varūṭakam |

	deyaṃ takraṃ tu sadyaskaṃ navanītād anuddhṛtam ||

	pakvaṃ tu gorasaṃ deyaṃ ghṛtāt pakvād anantaram |

	nirdoṣāyāś ca goḥ kṣīraṃ kvathitaṃ śarkarānugam ||

	āraṇyamahiṣīkṣīraṃ śarkarāśuṇṭhisaṃyutam |

	madhvāktaṃ tuhinaṃ caiva dadyād amṛtam eva tat ||

**[555]**	dadhiśuktaṃ ca dātavyaṃ sarvatra dadhisaṃbhavam |

	dāpayen maricopetaṃ yuktaṃ madhuguḍair api ||

pulastyaḥ |

	munyannaṃ brāhmaṇasyoktaṃ māṃsaṃ kṣatriyavaiśyayoḥ |

	madhupradānaṃ śūdrasya sarveṣāṃ cāvirodhi yat || 1.259 ||

_tathā_ |

	**varṣāsv evaṃ trayodaśyāṃ madhāsu ca na saṃśayaḥ || 1.260 ||**

varṣāsu yā trayodaśī yāś ca madhās tasyāṃ tāsu ca yat pitṛbhyo dadāti tad api tṛptilakṣaṇasya phalasyānantyam aśnute | anantāṃ pitṛtṛptiṃ sādhayatīty arthaḥ | atra ca proṣṭhapady aparapakṣe yā trayodaśī yāś ca maghās tā eva gṛhyante | manuḥ |

	yat kiṃcin madhusaṃyuktaṃ pradadyāt tu trayodaśīm |

	tad apy akṣayam eva syād varṣāsu ca maghāsu ca ||

trayodaśīm iti dvitīyā saptamyarthe | pitṛgāthā |

	api naḥ sa kule bhūyād yo no dadyāt trayodaśīm |

	pāyasaṃ madhusarpirbhyāṃ varṣāsu ca maghāsu ca ||

vasiṣṭhaḥ |

	pitā pitāmahaś caiva tathaiva prapitāmahaḥ |

	upāsate sutaṃ jātaṃ śakuntā iva pippalam ||

	madhumāṃsaiś ca śākaiś ca payasā pāyasena ca |

	eṣa no dāsyati śrāddhaṃ varṣāsu ca madhāsu ca ||

paiṭhīnasiḥ |

	ajena sarvalohena varṣāsu ca maghāsu ca |

	putro vā yadi vā pautro yo no dadyāt trayodaśīm ||

pitṛgāthe |

	api jāyeta so 'smākaṃ kule kaścin narottamaḥ |

	prāvṛṭkāle 'site pakṣe trayodaśyāṃ samāhitaḥ ||

	madhūtkaṭena yaḥ śrāddhaṃ pāyasena samācaret |

	kārtikaṃ sakalaṃ vāpi prākchāye kuñjarasya vā ||

yat tu bṛhaspatinoktam,

	kṛṣṇapakṣe trayodaśyāṃ yaḥ śrāddhaṃ kurute naraḥ |

	pañcatvaṃ tasya jānīyāj jyeṣṭhaputrasya niścitam ||

iti, yac ca ṣaṭtriṃśanmatam,

	gṛhī trayodaśīśrāddhaṃ na prakurvīta putravān |

	upavāsaṃ ca saṃkrāntau candrasūryagrahe tathā ||

**[556]**	trayodaśyāṃ tu vai śrāddhaṃ na kuryāt putravān gṛhī |

	neṣyate copavāsaś ca kaiścid apy ayanadvaye ||

iti, tatredaṃ civāraṇīyam — kiṃ sarvāparapakṣeṣu jñātiśraiṣṭhyādikāmas trayodaśyām evāparapakṣikaṃ śrāddhaṃ kuryād ity anena yad vihitaṃ tasyaiṣa niṣedhaḥ | yadi vā yugādiṣu śrāddhaṃ kuryād iti vidhito bhādrapadāsitatrayodaśyāṃ yat prāptaṃ tasya niṣedhaḥ | yad vā tisro 'ṣṭakās tisro 'nvaṣṭakāḥ proṣṭhapadyūrdhvaṃ trayodaśīvrīhiyavapākau cetu anena | tatra yugāditvaprayuktaṃ proṣṭhapadyūrdhvaṃ trayodaśītvaprayuktaṃ yac chrāddhaṃ tan nityaṃ tasya ced ayaṃ pratiṣedhas tadā vihitatvāt pratiṣiddhatvāc ca vikalpa āpadyetātirātraṣōḍaśigrahaṇāgrahaṇavat | na ca vācyaṃ sāmānyaviṣayād vidheḥ putravadgṛhirūpaviśeṣaviṣayo niṣedho balavān ato na vikalpa iti | yadviṣayo hi niṣedhas tadviṣayāṃ niṣedhyaprāptim apekṣate | prasaktipūrvakatvān niṣedhasya | tataś ca putravadgṛhiviṣayā trayodaśīśrāddhaprāptir astīti niṣedhād eva gamyate | ato hi durnivāro vikalpaḥ | nanu ca nāyaṃ prasajyapratiṣedhaḥ hiṃ tu paryudāsaḥ, tataś ca putravad gṛhivyatiriktaṃ praty eva śrāddavidhir ayam ato na vikalpaḥ | tan na | tathā sati hi na kuryād ity anvayo na syāt | kiṃ tu na gṛhī na putravān iti syāt | na cārthapadakramān yathābhāvaḥ kāryo hetyabhāvāt | na ca karoty arthānvito nañparyudāso bhavati kiṃ tu nāmānvito dhātvantarānvitaś ca | tasmān na naityakatrayodaśīśrāddhaviṣayo 'yaṃ pratiṣedhaḥ, kiṃ tu kāmyaviṣya eva | na hi tadviṣayatve vikalpaḥ prasajyeta | na hi rāgaprāptaṃ kalañjabhakṣaṇaṃ tatpratiṣedhena vikalpyate | nanu ca kalañjabhakṣaṇam aśāstrīyam | śāstrīyaś ca tatpratiṣedhas tasmād avikalpaḥ | taryodaśīśrāddhaṃ tu kāmyam api śāstreṇa vihitam | ato yuktas tasya śāstrīyeṇa pratiṣedhena vikalpaḥ | satyaṃ vihitam, kiṃ tu phalaṃ praty upāyatayā na punar anuṣṭheyatayā | anuṣṭheyatā ca tasya phalarāganibandhanaiva | ato yuktā kalañjabhakṣaṇatulyatā | yeṣām api mate yatra vidhiḥ puruṣaṃ pravartayati tasya phalasādhanatvaṃ śāstrād avabudhyata iti, tanmate 'pi viṣayasya phalasādhanatvāvagamaparam eva vidheḥ pravatrakatvaṃ pratīyate, na puruṣapravṛttisiddhyarthaṃ phalarāgata eva tatsiddheḥ | trikālāyāṃ hy aprāptau vidhir arthavān | ata evāhuḥ: "apravṛttapravartako vidhir ajñātajāpakaś ca" iti | **[557]** tasmād yat kāmyaṃ trayodaśīśrāddhaṃ tadviṣayo 'yaṃ niṣedho na punar yan nityaṃ tadviṣayaḥ | ata eva āpastambaḥ kāmyasyaivāsya nindām āha: "sarveṣv evāparapakṣasyāhaḥsu kriyamāṇaṃ pitṝn prīṇāti kartus tu kālādiniyamāt phalaviśeṣaḥ | prathame 'hani kriyamāṇaṃ strīprāyam apatyaṃ jāyate | dvitīye stenās tṛtīye brahmavarcasvinaḥ | caturthe kṣudrapaśumān | pañcame bahupumāṃso bahvapatyo na cānapatyaḥ pramīyate | ṣaṣṭhe 'dhvaśīlo 'kṣaśīlaś ca | saptame kṛṣer vṛddhiḥ | aṣṭame puṣṭir nama ekaśapho daśame vyavahāre rāddhiḥ | ekādaśe kṛṣṇāyasatrapusīsam | dvādaśe paśumāṃs trayodaśe bahuputro bahumitro darśanīyapatyo yuvamāriṇas tu bhavanti | caturdaś āyudhe rāddhiḥ | pañcadaśe puṣṭiḥ" iti | sarveṣv evāparapakṣasyāhaḥsu kriyamāṇa ity anenāparapakṣikasya śrāddhasya nityatvam āha | kratus tu kālāniyamāt phalaviśeṣa ity anena tu pratipadāditithiniyamena tadaiva kriyamāṇaṃ phalaviśeṣapradaṃ bhavatīty āha | tasmāt kāmyasyaiva trayodaśīśrāddhasya pratiṣedho 'yam | yā tu ṣaṭtriṃśanmate maghāśrāddhasya nindā,

	maghāsu kurvataḥ śrāddhaṃ jyeṣṭhaḥ putro vinaśyati |

	saṃkrātāv upavāsaś ca candrasūryagrahe tathā ||

iti, sā na niṣedhaṃ kalpayati kḷptatvāt tasya | tathā ca kanyāgatāparapakṣādhikāre devīpurāṇam |

	tatrāpi mahatī pūjā kartavyā pitṛdaivate |

	ṛkṣe piṇḍapradānaṃ tu jyeṣṭhaputrī vivarjayet || iti |

pitṛdaivatam ṛkṣaṃ maghā | pūjā śrāddham, tena piṇḍadānasahitam eva bhādrapadāparapakṣamaghāsu śrāddhaṃ ninditam | na śrāddhamātraṃ piṇḍadānasyaiva pratiṣiddhatvāt | na ca niṣedhavākye piṇḍadānaśabdaḥ śrāddhalakṣakaḥ, lakṣaṇākāraṇābhāvāt | evaṃ tāvan maghāśrāddhaṃ piṇḍadānarahitam uktam, śrāddhāntarāṇy api piṇḍadānarahitāny uktāny matsyapurāṇe |

	ayanadvitaye śrāddhaṃ viṣuvaddvitaye tathā |

	saṃkrāntiṣu ca sarvāsu piṇḍanirvapaṇād ṛte ||

**[558]**	vaiśākhasya tṛtīyāyāṃ navamyāṃ kārtikasya ca |

	śrāddhaṃ kāryaṃ ca śuklāyāṃ saṃkrāntividhinā naraiḥ ||

mahābhārate |

	nakṣatreṇa na kurvīta yasmiñ jāto bhaven naraḥ |

	na proṣṭhapadayoḥ kāryaṃ tathāgneye ca bhārata ||

	dāruṇeṣu ca sarveṣu pratyavare ca vivarjayet |

	jyotiṣe yāni coktāni tāni sarvāṇi varjayet ||

āgneyaṃ kṛttikāḥ | dāruṇāni ārdrāśleṣājyeṣṭhāmūlāni | janmanakṣatrāt pañcamaṃ caturdaśaṃ trayoviṃśaṃ ca pratyaram | śrāddhaniṣedho 'yaṃ kṛṣṇapakṣaśrāddhaviṣayaḥ | tad dhy aniyamenaikasyāṃ tithau kartavyam it pratiṣiddhaṃ parityajyāny atrāpi śakyaṃ kartum iti pratiṣedhe 'pi nātyantabādhaḥ| anyaviṣayatve tu śrāddhavidher atyantiko bādha āpadyate | jyotiṣam |

	sādhāraṇadhruvogreṣu maitre 'pi ca na śasyate |

	manuṣyāṇāṃ pretakriyā kathaṃcit tripuṣkare yamaladhiṣṇye ca ||

sādhāraṇe kṛttikāviśākhe | uttarātrayaṃ rohiṇī ca dhruvāṇi | ugrāṇi pūrvātrayaṃ bharaṇī maghāś ca | maitram anurādhā | tripuṣkaraṃ tripāt | yamalaṃ dvipāt | putrādināpi kriyamāṇaṃ śrāddhaṃ tatpitrādīnāṃ tṛptilakṣaṇaṃ phalaṃ sādhayatīti śāstraprāmānyād āśrayaṇīyam | tathā pitrāpi kriyamāṇā vaiśvānarejyā putrasya brahmavarcasādikaṃ niṣpādayatīti | evaṃ ca sati pitṛtṛptyāśrito 'tiśayo havirviśeṣāt kālaviśeṣād deśaviśeṣāc ca bhavatīti śakyaṃ śātrād avagantum || 1.260 ||

_kṛṣṇapakṣe śrāddham ekasyāṃ tithau kāryam ity uktaṃ tad yasyāṃ kriyamāṇaṃ yasmai phalāya saṃpadyate tad idānīm āha_ |

	**kanyāṃ kanyāvedinaś ca paśūn mukhyān sutān api |**

**	dyūtaṃ kṛṣiṃ ca vāṇijyaṃ dviśaphaikaśaphāṃs tathā || 1.261 ||**

**	brahmavarcasvinaḥ putrān svarṇarūpye sakupyake |**

**	jñātiśraiṣṭhyaṃ sarvakāmān āpnoti śrāddhadaḥ sadā || 1.262 ||**

**	pratipatprabhṛtiṣv ekāṃ varjayitvā caturdaśīm |**

**	śastreṇa tu hatā ye vai tebhyas tatra pradīyate || 1.263 ||**

pratikṛṣṇapakṣaṃ sarvadā pratipadi śrāddhapadaḥ kanyāṃ prāpnoti | evaṃ dvitīyāyāṃ **[559]** kanyāvidinā jāmātṝn | tṛtīyāyāṃ paśūn | caturthyāṃ pradhānān sutān | pañcamyāṃ dyūtam | ṣaṣṭhyāṃ kṛṣim | saptamyāṃ vāṇijyam | aṣṭamyāṃ dviśaphaṃ gavādi | navamyām ekaśapham aśvādi | daśamyāṃ brahmavarcasvinaḥ putrān | ekādaśyāṃ svarṇarūpye | dvādaśyāṃ kupyaṃ trapusīsādikam | trayodaśyāṃ jñātīnāṃ madhye śreṣṭhatām | amāvāsyāyāṃ sarvān uktān kāmān | caturdaśī cātra varjanīyā | śastrahastebhya eva tasyāṃ śrāddham pradeyam | śastrahatagrahaṇaṃ śāstrāntaroktadurmaraṇapradarśanārtham | tatra brahmapurāṇam |

	prāyānaśanaśastrāgniviṣodbandhanināṃ tathā |

	caturdaśyāṃ tu kartavyaṃ tṛptyartham iti niścayaḥ ||

vāyupurāṇāt |

	yuvān astu gṛhe yasya mṛtās teṣāṃ pradāpayet |

	śastreṇa nihatā ye vai teṣāṃ dadyāc caturdaśīm ||

marīciḥ |

	viṣaśastraśvāpadāhitiryagbrāhmaṇaghātinām |

	caturdaśyāṃ kriyāḥ kāryā anyeṣāṃ tu vigarhitāḥ ||
