iti vacanāc chastrahatādīnām eva caturdaśyāṃ kriyā ity avadhāryate na tu tasyām eva teṣām iti | tenāmāvāsyādikālāntareṣv api teṣāṃ śrāddhaṃ yuktam | ata eva devīpurāṇam |

	āhaveṣu vipannānāṃ jalāgnibhṛgupātinām |

	caturdaśyāṃ bhavet pūjā hy amāvāsyā tu kāmikī ||

gargaḥ |

	caturdaśyāṃ tu yac chrāddhaṃ sapiṇḍīkaraṇe kṛte |

	tad ekoddiṣṭavidhinā kartavyaṃ śatraghātine ||

tathā |

	sapiṇḍīkaraṇād ūrdhvam ṛte kṛṣṇacaturdaśīm |

	pratisaṃvatsarād anyad ekoddiṣṭaṃ na pārvaṇam ||

atra caikasya śastrahastva ekoddiṣṭavidhānaṃ na tu trayāṇāṃ tathātve, tatra pārvaṇam eva || 1.261, 262, 263 ||

_nakṣatraviśeṣāt phalaviśeṣam āha_ |

	**svargaṃ hy apatyam ojaś ca śauryaṃ kṣetraṃ balaṃ tathā |**

**	jñāti śraiṣṭhyaṃ susaubhāgyaṃ samṛddhiṃ mukhyatāṃ sutān || 1.264 ||**

**	pravṛttacakratāṃ putrāṇ vāṇijyaprabhṛtīṃs tathā |**

**	arogitvaṃ yaśo vītaśokatāṃ paramāṃ gatim || 1.265 ||**

**[560]**	**dhanaṃ vidyāṃ bhiṣaksiddhiṃ kupyaṃ gā apy ajāvikam |**

**	aśvān āyuś ca vidhivad yaḥ śrāddhaṃ saṃprayacchati || 1.266 ||**

**	kṛttikādibharaṇyantaṃ sa kāmān āpnuyād imān |**

**	āstikaḥ śraddadhānaś cāpy apetamadamatsaraḥ || 1.267 ||**

kṛttikādibharaṇyanteṣu nakṣatreṣu śrāddham āstikaḥ śraddhāvān vigatamatsaraś ca san yathāvidhi yaḥ pitṛbhyaḥ saṃprayacchati sa yathānakṣatrakramaṃ svargādīn kāmān āpnuyāt | tataś ca svargakāmaḥ kṛttikāsu śrāddhaṃ kuryāt | apatyakāmo rohiṇyām | tajaskāmo mṛgaśirasi | śauryakāma ārdrāyām | kṣetrakāmaḥ punarvasvoḥ | balakāmaḥ puṣye | putrakāmo 'śleṣāyām | śraiṣṭhyakāmo maghāsu | saubhāgakāmaḥ pūrvāsu phalgunīṣu | samṛddhikāma uttarāsu phalgunīṣu | mukhyatākāmo haste | sutakāmaś citrāsu | cakrapravṛttikāmaḥ svātau | putrakāmo viśākhāyām | vāṇijyakāmo 'nurādhāsu | arogitvakāmo jyeṣṭhāyām | yaśaskāmo mūle | viśokatvakāmaḥ pūrvāṣāḍhāsu | muktikāma uttarāṣāḍhāsu | dhanakāmaḥ śravaṇe | vidyākāmo dhaniṣṭhāsu | bhiṣaksiddhikāmaḥ śatabhiṣaji | kupyakāmaḥ pūrvayor bhadrapadayoḥ | gokāma uttaryor bhadrapadayoḥ | ajāvikakāmo revatyām | aśvakāmo 'śvayuji | āyuṣkāmo bhraṇyām | ā phalaprāpteḥ kṛttikādinakṣatre śrāddhaṃ prayoktavyam | ata eva vāyupurāṇe,

	śrāddhaṃ yaḥ kṛttikāyoge karoti satataṃ naraḥ |

ityādi uktam || 1.264, 265, 266, 267 ||

	**vasurudrāditisutā pitaraḥ śrāddhadevatāḥ |**

**	prīṇayanti manuṣyāṇāṃ pitṝñ śrāddena tarpitāḥ || 1.268 ||**

uktaṃ svasaṃbandhibhyaḥ pretebhyaḥ śrāddhaṃ pradeyam iti tatra pitrādiṣu śrāddhadevatābhūteṣu vasvādibuddhiḥ kāryety anena vidhīyate | ye pitṛpitāmahaprapitāmahāḥ śrāddhadevatātvena niyuktāḥ śrāstreṣu ye yathākramaṃ vasurudrādityā boddhavyā ity anvayaḥ | te vasvādayaḥ śrāddena tarpitāḥ śrāddheṣu devatātvena niviṣṭā manuṣyāṇāṃ pitrādīṃs tarpayanti | vasvādirūpeṇa dhyātāḥ śrāddhāt tṛptim upayāntīty arthaḥ | ata eva manuḥ |

**[561]**	vasūn vadanti hi pitṝn rudrāṃś caiva pitāmahān |

	prapitāmahāṃs tathādityāñ śrutir eṣā purātanī || 1.268 ||

	**āyuḥ prajāṃ dhanaṃ vidyāṃ svargaṃ mokṣaṃ sukhāni ca |**

**	prayacchanti tathā rājyaṃ nṝṇāṃ prītāḥ pitāmahāḥ || 1.269 ||**

āyurādīni phalāni śrāddhakartṛbhyaḥ prayacchanti na punar vasvādayaḥ | yathāśrutagrāhiṇaḥ pūrvaślokād vasvādidai(de)vatyam eva sarvaṃ śrāddhaṃ na punaḥ pitrādidai(de)vatyam iti kasyacid buddhir utpadyate | tannivṛttidvāreṇa śrāddhasyāyurādiphalatvapratipādanaparo 'yaṃ ślokaḥ | atra ca pitāmahagrahaṇaṃ pitrādyupalakṣaṇārtham | tataś ca śrāddhakartṝṇāṃ manuṣyāṇāṃ śrāddhe devatābhāvena saṃbadhyamānāḥ pitrādaya āyurādiphalapradā bhavantīty uktaṃ bhavati | yady apy apūrvaphalapradātṛtvaṃ na devatāyās tathāpi sarvāṅgopetakarmānuṣṭhānāt phaladāpūrvodaya iti yuktāṅgabhūtapitrādidevatāyāḥ phalahetutvoktiḥ | āyurādīnāṃ ca pratyekaṃ phalatvaṃ pratyekaṃ dvitīyāyogāt | evaṃ cāmāvāsyāṣṭakādiśrāddhānāṃ nityatvaṃ kāmyatvaṃ ca jñeyam | yad vā nityasyaiva śrāddhasya prayogāt kartur āyurādisiddhiḥ | nityayor iv darśapūrṇamāsayoḥ sūktavākanirdiṣṭāyurādiphalasiddhiḥ | 

	atra śrāddhakālātikrame yat kāryaṃ tad ucyate | tatra ṛṣyaśṛṅgaḥ |

	deye pitṝṇāṃ śrāddhe tu āśaucaṃ jāyate yadi |

	āśauce tu vyatikrānte tebhyaḥ śrāddham pradīyate ||

	ekoddiṣṭe tu saṃprāpte yadi vighnaḥ prajāyate |

	māse 'nyasmiṃs tithau tasyāṃ śrāddhaṃ kuryāt prayatnataḥ ||

māsikaviṣayam etat | marīciḥ |

	śrāddhavighne samutpanne avijñāte mṛtāhani |

	ekādaśyāṃ tu kartavyaṃ kṛṣṇapakṣe viśeṣataḥ ||

ṣaṭtriṃśanmatāt |

	māsikābde tu saṃprāpte tv antarā mṛtasūtake |

	vadanti śuddhau tat kāryaṃ darśe vāpi vicakṣaṇaḥ ||

yan mṛtāhani pratimāsaṃ kriyate tad atra māsikam || 1.269 ||

**iti śrīvidhyādharavaṃśaprabhavaśrīśilāhāranarendrajīmūtavāhanānvayaprasūta-**

**śrīmadaprādityadevaviracite yājñavalkīyadharmaśāstranibandhe 'parārke**

**śrāddhaprakaraṇaṃ samāptam || 9 ||**

**[562]**

**atha saṭīkayājñavalkyasmṛtau**

**vināyakapūjāvidhiprakaraṇam (10) |**

_abhīṣṭakarmaphalaprāptau vighnaparihārasyāpy upāyam idānīm āha_ |

	**vināyakaḥ karmavighnasiddhyarthaṃ viniyojinaḥ |**

**	gaṇānām ādhipatye ca rudreṇa brahmaṇā tathā || 1.270 ||**

vināyakākhyo devaviśeṣaḥ sarveṣāṃ kartṝṇāṃ karmavighnārthaṃ karmasiddhyarthaṃ ca gaṇānāṃ puṣpadantādīnām īśvaratve ca rudracaturmukhābhyāṃ niyukto 'to 'sau vihitopāyenaiva nivārayituṃ ca śakyata iti tadupāyavidhir ārabhyate || 1.270 ||

_tatra vināyakopadrave sati tacchamanādhikāra iti tadupadravalakṣaṇaṃ tāvad āha_ |

	**tenopasṛṣṭo yas tasya lakṣaṇāni nibodhata |**

**	svapne 'vagāhate 'tyarthaṃ jalaṃ muṇḍāṃś ca paśyati || 1.271 ||**

**	kāṣāyavāsasaś caiva kravyādāṃś cādhirohati |**

**	antyajair gardabhair uṣṭraiḥ sahaikatrāvatiṣṭhate || 1.272 ||**

**	vrajantaṃ ca tathātmānaṃ manyate 'nugataṃ paraiḥ |**

tena vināyakenopasṛṣṭa upadruto yo manuṣyas tasya vakṣyamāṇāni cihnāni he munayaḥ śṛṇuta, svapne 'tiśayena jalam avagāhate jalam agram ātmānaṃ paśyatīty arthaḥ | muṇḍān kṛtavapanān kāṣāyavasanāṃś ca narān paśyati | tathā kravyādān vyāghrādīn adhirohaty antyajātibhiḥ sahaikatra deśe 'vatiṣṭhate ca | tathā gacchantaṃ māṃ pṛṣṭhataḥ pare 'nugacchantīti manyate | kravyam āmamāṃsaṃ tad adanti ye te kravyādā iti svapne || 1.271, 272 ||

_atha jāgaraṇe_ |

	**vimanā viphalārambhaḥ saṃsīdaty animittataḥ || 1.273 ||**

**	tenopasṛṣṭo labhate na rāṣṭraṃ rājanandanaḥ |**

**	kumārī ca na bhartāram apatyaṃ garbham aṅganā || 1.274 ||**

**[563]	ācāryatvaṃ śrotriyaś ca śiṣyo 'dhayanaṃ tathā |**

**	vaṇig lābhaṃ na cāpnoti kṛṣiṃ caiva kṛṣīvalaḥ || 1.275 ||**

vimanā udvignamanā viphalārambo niṣphalodyamaḥ saṃsīdaty avasīdati animittato dṛṣṭanimittābhāvataḥ | rājanandano rājaputro na rājyaṃ kumārī guṇavaty api na bhartāram aṅganā ca garbhaṃ prasūtāv apatyam āyuṣmac chrotriyaś cācāryatvaṃ śiṣyaś cādhyayanaṃ vanijyājīvī ca tannimittaṃ dhanopacayaṃ kṛṣīvalaś ca kṛṣiṃ na labhate | imāni vināyakopasṛṣṭasya lakṣaṇāni | tatra baijavāpagṛhyam: "atha vināyakāḥ | catvāraḥ khalu vināyakā bhavanti | mitaś ca saṃmitaś ca śālakaṭaṅkaś ca kūṣmāṇḍarājaputraś cety etair vināyakair upasṛṣṭalakṣaṇā brāhmaṇāḥ svādhyāyavanto 'py ācāryatvaṃ na labhante | kumārā rājaputrā rājalakṣaṇasaṃpannā api rājyaṃ na labhante | kumāryo 'pi lakṣaṇavatyo 'pi bhartṝn na labhante | strīṇām ācāravatīnām apy apatyāni mriyante | vināyakopasṛṣṭalakṣaṇaṃ khalu bhavati svapne sarvān paśyati | atyantam apo 'vagāhate | antarikṣaṃ krāmati pāṃsukardame cāvasīdati | pṛṣṭhato māṃ kaścid dhāvantīti manyate | uṣṭrān gardabhāñ śuno divākīrtm anyāṃś cāprayatān paśyati | karaṇe gūḍham ātmānaṃ malināntaram anyāṃś ca prayatān paśyati" | bhaviṣyatpurāṇe |

	karaṇe mūḍham ātmānaṃ malināntaragas tathā |

	caturbhiś cāvṛtaṃ yāntaṃ śmaśānāntikagaṃ nṛpa ||

	paśyate nṛpaśārdūla paśyate nātra saṃśayaḥ |

	tailārdragātraṃ ca vibho karavīravibhūṣitam || 1.273, 274, 275 ||

	**snāpanaṃ tasya kartavyaṃ puṇye 'hni vidhipūrvakam |**

tasya vināyakopasṛṣṭasya tadupasargaśāntaye puṇyāhe vakṣyamāṇavidhinā snapanaṃ kāryam | yat tu bhaviṣyatpurāṇe,

	śuklapakṣe caturthyāṃ ca vāreṇa dhiṣaṇasya ca |

	tiṣye ca vīranakṣatre tasyaiva purato nṛpa ||

iti, tat tu śrīkāmavināyakasnapane draṣṭavyam | tad upasṛṣṭasnapanaviṣayāṇāṃ tu **[564]** puṇyāhavidhānam | upasṛṣṭasya cirakālavilambāyogāt | dhiṣaṇo bṛhaspatiḥ | tasyaiva vināyakasyetu arthaḥ ||

_snapanavidhim āha_ |

	**gaurasarṣapakalkena sājyenotsāditasya ca || 1.276 ||**

**	sarvauṣadhaiḥ sarvagandhair viliptaśirasas tathā |**

**	bhadrāsanopaviṣṭasya svasti vācyā dvijāḥ śubhāḥ || 1.277 ||**

śuklasarṣapāṇāṃ cūrṇenājyasahitena sa udvartanīyaḥ | tataḥ sarvaiṣadhaiḥ sagandhaiś cūrṇitaiḥ sodakair vilipamastakaḥ kāryas tato bhadrāsana upaveśyas tatas tasya svasti bhavanto bruvantv iti dvijā viprāḥ śubhāḥ kalyāṇa(ṇaṃ) vācyāḥ | atra kartari ṣaṣṭhī | tataś ca tena vācyā ity arthaḥ | tatsādanādi śai(śi)vādidevapūjāṃ kṛtvā kāryam ity uktaṃ bhaviṣyatpurāṇe |

	vyomakeśaṃ tu saṃpūjya pārvatīṃ bhīmajaṃ tathā |

	kṛṣṇasya pitaraṃ tāta arakam āraṃ sitaṃ tathā ||

	dhiṣaṇaṃ kledaputraṃ ca koṇaṃ lakṣma ca bhārata |

	vidhuṃtudaṃ bāhuleyaṃ nandakasya ca dhāriṇam ||

vyomakeśaḥ śivaḥ | bhīmajo gaṇeśaḥ | kṛṣṇasya pitā vasudevaḥ | āro bhaumaḥ | sitaḥ śukraḥ | kledaputro budhaḥ | koṇaḥ śaneśvaraḥ | lakṣma lakṣmavāṃś candraḥ, pūrṇa ity arthaḥ | vidhuṃtudo rāhuḥ | ketur atrānukto 'pi grāhyaḥ sāhacaryāt | bāhuleyaḥ skandaḥ | nandakasya dhārī viṣṇuḥ | sarvauṣadhāni sahadevyādīni | tathā ca matsyapurāṇam |

	sahadevī vacā vyāghrī balā cātibalā tathā |

	śaṅkhapuṣpī tathā siṃhī aṣṭamī tu suvarcalā ||

	mahauṣadhyaṣṭakaṃ hy etan mahāsnāneṣu yojayet ||

brahma(brāhmī)suvarcalādīni vā | tathā ca bhaviṣatpurāṇam |

	brāhmī suvarcalā mustā viṣṇukrāntā śatāvarī |

	durlabhā śaṅkhapuṣpī ca priyaṅgurajanī vacā ||

surādīni vā | tathā smṛtiḥ |

	surā māṃsī vacā kuṣṭaṃ rajanīdvayam |

	satī caṇyakamustaṃ ca sarvauṣadhigaṇaḥ smṛtaḥ || **[565]**

surā tābhorā iti prasiddhā | rajanīdvayaṃ haridrādāruharidre | satī karpūraviśeṣaḥ | vālukādīni vā | tathā ca vasiṣṭhaḥ |

	vālukā śaṅkhapuṣpī ca kuṣṭhaṃ caiva vacā tathā |

	nāgakesarcūrṇaṃ ca sarvauṣadhigaṇo bhṛgo || 1.276, 277 ||

_api ca_ |

	**aśvatthānād gajasthānād valmīkāt saṃgamād dhradāt |**

**	mṛttikāṃ rocanāṃ gandhān guggulaṃ ca vinikṣipet || 1.278 ||**

**	yā āhṛtā hy ekavarṇaiś caturbhiḥ kalaśair hradāt |**

ekavarṇaiś caturbhiḥ kalaśair apa āhṛtya tāsv aśvasthādibhyaḥ samāhṛtā mṛttikā gorocanām agurukastūrīkarpūracandanakesarātmakān gandhān guggulaṃ ca vinikṣipet | atra baijavāpagṛhyam: "caturbhyaḥ prasravaṇebhyaś caturaḥ kumbhān āhṛtya teṣu sarvauṣadhīḥ sarvagandhān hiraṇyaṃ vrīhiyavau guggulaṃ mṛdam ākhūtkarām" iti | prakṣiped iti śeṣaḥ || 1.278 ||

	**carmaṇy ānaḍuhe rakte sthāpyaṃ bhadrāsanaṃ tataḥ || 1.279 ||**

anaḥ śakaṭaṃ yo vahati tat so 'nadvān balīvardaḥ | taccarmaṇi lohite bhadrāsaṇaṃ pratiṣṭhātantrokam | tato 'psu mṛdādiprakṣepād anantaraṃ sthāpyam || 1.279 ||

	**sahasrākṣaṃ śatadhāram ṛṣibhiḥ pāvanaṃ kṛtam |**

**	tena tvām abhiṣiñcāmi pāvamānyaḥ punantu te || 1.280 ||**

**	bhagaṃ te varuṇo rājā bhagaṃ sūryo bṛhaspatiḥ |**

**	bhagam indraś ca vāyuś ca bhagaṃ saptarṣayo daduḥ || 1.281 ||**

**	yat te keśeṣu daurbhāgyaṃ sīmante yac ca mūrdhani |**

**	lalāṭe karṇayor akṣṇor āpas tad ghnantu te sadā || 1.282 ||**

sahasrākṣam ityādibhir mantrais tribhir ekaikena kalaśena vināyakopasṛṣṭasya guruḥ snapanaṃ karoti | pratikalaśaṃ mantratrayāvṛttiḥ || 1.280, 281, 282 ||

**[566]**

	**snātasya sārṣapaṃ tailaṃ sruveṇaudumbareṇa tu |**

**	juhuyān mūrdhani kuśān savyena parigṛhya ca || 1.283 ||**

**	mitaś ca saṃmitaś caiva tathā śālakaṭaṅkaṭaḥ |**

**	kūṣmāṇḍarājaputraś cety ante svāhāsamanvitaiḥ || 1.284 ||**

**	nāmabhir balimantraiś ca namaskārasamanvitaiḥ |**

**	dadyāc catuṣpathe śūrpe kuśān āstrīya suvrataḥ || 1.285 ||**

**	kṛtākṛtāṃs taṇḍulāṃś ca palalaudanam eva ca |**

**	matsyān pakvāṃs tathā cāmān māṃsam etāvav eva tu || 1.286 ||**

**	puṣpaṃ citraṃ sugandhaṃ ca surāṃ ca vividhām api |**

**	mūlakaṃ pūrikāpūpāṃs tathaivoṇḍerakasrajam || 1.287 ||**

**	dadhy annaṃ pāyasaṃ caiva guḍamiśraṃ samodakam |**

pūrvoktena prakāreṇa snātakasya śirasi savyena pāṇinā kuśān parigṛhyetarapāṇigṛhītenaudumaravṛkṣamayena sruveṇa sarṣpatailaṃ mitāya svāhā saṃmitāya svāha śālakaṭaṅkaṭāya svāhā kūṣmāṇḍarājaputrāya svāheti guru juhuyāt | tair eva mitādibhiś caturbhir nāmabhiś caturthyantair namaskārasamanvitaiś catuṣpathe śūrpaṃ sthāpayitvā tatra ca sarvataḥ sarvadigagrān kuśān āstīrya kṛtākṛtataṇḍulādirūpaṃ baliṃ dadyāt | nāmabhir balimantraiś ceti viśeṣeṇa nirdeśān mitādināmabhiś caturthyantair namaskāramantrair balimantratām āpannair balir deya iti gamyate | avaghātādinā yeṣāṃ vrīhīṇāṃ taṇḍulībhāvaḥ prārabdhāparisamāptaś caite kṛtākṛtās taṇḍulāḥ | tilapiṣṭamiśra odanaḥ palalaudanaḥ | mūlakaṃ śākādiviseṣaḥ | bhṛṣṭā lopikāḥ pūrikāḥ | kṣudrāpūpās tūṇḍerakāḥ | prasiddham anyat | etat sarvam ekasmin pātre kṛtvā sakṛd eva dadyāt || 1.283, 284, 285, 286, 287 ||

	**vināyakasya jananīm upatiṣṭhet tadāmbikām || 1.288 ||**

**[567]**	**dūrvāsarṣapuṣpāṇāṃ datvārghaṃ(ghyaṃ) pūrṇam añjalim |**

**	rūpaṃ dehi yaśo dehi bhagaṃ bhaveti dehi me || 1.289 ||**

**	putrān dehi dhanaṃ dehi sarvakāmāṃś ca dehi me |**

dūrvayā sarṣapaiḥ puṣpair udakena ca pūrṇam añjalim arghyaṃ vidhāya vināyakasya jananyā ambikāyai datvā rūpaṃ dehīty anena tām upatiṣṭheta || 1.288, 189 ||

	**tataḥ śuklāmbaradharaḥ śuklamālyānulepanaḥ || 1.290 ||**

**	brāhmaṇān bhojayed dadyād vastrayugmaṃ guror api |**

ambikām upasthāya śukle vāsasī paridhāya śuklamālyānulepanaiś cātmānam alaṃkṛtya brāhmaṇān bhojayet | gurave ca vastradvayaṃ dadyāt | guruśabdaprayogāt snapanakartā guruvat pūjya iti gamayati || 1.290 ||

	**evaṃ vināyakaṃ pūjya grahāṃś caiva vidhānataḥ || 1.291 ||**

**	karmaṇāṃ phalam āpnoti śriyam āpnoty anuttamām |**

evam uktena prakāreṇa vināyakaṃ pūjayitvā grahāṃś ca vakṣyamāṇavidhinā karmaṇāṃ kṛtānāṃ kariṣyamāṇānāṃ ca phalaṃ vighnaśāntidvāreṇa prāpnoti | śriyaṃ cānuttamāṃ sarvotkṛṣṭām āpnoti | na vidyata uttamā yasyāḥ sānuttamā | āpnotīti punarvacanaṃ śrīkāmaṃ prati vināyakādipūjāyāḥ pṛthagvidhānārtham || 1.291 ||

	**ādityasya sadā pūjāṃ tilakaṃ svāminas tathā || 1.292 ||**

**	mahāgaṇapateś caiva kurvan siddhim avāpnuyāt |**

iti vināyakapūjāvidhiprakaraṇam || 10 ||

ādityasya svāminaḥ skandasya mahāgaṇapateś ca sarvakālaṃ pūjāṃ tilakaṃ suvarṇādimayaṃ kurvan karmaphalasiddhim avāpnuyād iti || 1.292 ||

**iti śrīvidhyādharavaṃśaprabhavaśrīśilāhāranarendrajīmūtavāhanānvayaprasūta-**

**śrīmadaprādityadevaviracite yājñavalkīyadharmaśāstranibandhe 'parārke**

**vināyakapūjāvidhiprakaraṇaṃ samāptam || 9 ||**

**atha saṭīkāyājñavalkyasmṛtau**

**grahayajñavidhiprakaraṇam | (11)**

_atha grahayajñavidhim āha_ |

	śrīśāntyādikāmo 'bhicaran vā grahayajñaṃ vakṣyamāṇasvarūpaṃ samācared anutiṣṭhet | śāntiḥ phaladānonmukhaduritanivāraṇam | puṣṭiḥ śarīrādyupacayaḥ | abhicāra āyuṣpradadharmapratibandhaḥ | prasiddham anyat | vṛṣṭyāyuḥpuṣṭīnāṃ pratyekaṃ kāmasaṃbandho netaretarayuktānām, pramāṇāntarasiddhatve saty uddiśyamānatvāt | evaṃvidhasyoddeśyasya viśeṣaṇam avivakṣitam | pūrvaṃ vināyakasnānasahito grahayajñaḥ śriye vihitaḥ | idānīṃ kevalaḥ phalāntarebhyaś ceti vidhibhedaḥ | abhicarann iti śatṛpratyayo 'bhicārasya grahayajñaṃ prati hetutām ācaṣṭe | abhicārasya cāsiddhatvān na svarūpeṇa hetutā, kiṃ tu tadicchāyās teneṣyamānatayā karmasaṃbandhād abhicārasya phalatvam || 1.293 ||

_grahān āha_ |

	**sūryaḥ somo mahīputraḥ somaputro bṛhaspatiḥ || 1.294 ||**

**	śukraḥ śanaiśvaro rāhuḥ ketuś ceti grahāḥ smṛtāḥ |**

etā grahayajñadevatāḥ | vṛttavaśāc cātra sūryādiśabdanirdeśo yāgaprayoge punar ādityādiśabdair uddeśaḥ kāryaḥ | tathā ca bahvṛcagṛhyapariśiṣṭam: "guḍaudanam ādityāya ghṛtapāyasaṃ somāya haviṣyan annam aṅgārakāya kṣauraudanaṃ budhāya ṣaṣṭikaṃ bṛhaspataye dadhyodanaṃ śukrāya māṣaudanaṃ tilapiṣṭamiśraṃ saghṛtaṃ śanaiśvarāya rāhave māṃsaudanaṃ ketave citraudanam" iti | naivaṃ gadyagranthe 'smiñ śrūyamāṇaśabdasyāvivakṣāyāṃ hetur asti || 1.294 ||

_ādityādigrahapratimāprakṛtidravyāṇy āha_ |

	**tāmrakāt sphaṭikād raktacandanāt svarṇakād ubhau || 1.295 ||**

**[569]	rajatād ayasaḥ sīsāt kāṃsyāt kāryā grahāḥ kramāt |**

**	svavarṇair vā paṭe lekhyā gandhamaṇḍalake 'pi (keṣu) vā || 1.296 ||**

tāmram eva tāmrakaṃ tasmād ādityasya pratimā kāryā | sphaṭikāt somasya | raktacandanād aṅgārakasya | svarṇakād budhabṛhaspatyoḥ | rajatāc chukrasya | kṛṣṇamayaḥ kārṣṇāyasaṃ tasmāc chanaiścarasya | sīsād rāhoḥ | kāṃsyāt ketoḥ | pratimānirmāṇāsamarthas tu grahasamānavarṇair varṇakair grahān paṭe likhet | tatrāpy asamartho grahasamānavarṇeṣu candanādigandhamaṇḍalakeṣu grahān ullikhet | atra matsyapurāṇam |

	padmāsanaṃ padmakaraḥ padmagarbhasamadyutiḥ |

	saptāśvarathasaṃsthaś ca dvibhujaḥ syāt sadā raviḥ ||

	śvetaḥ svetāmbaradharo daśā(raḥ śvetā)śvaḥ śvetabhūṣaṇaḥ |

	gadāpāṇir dvibāhuś ca kartavyo varadaḥ śaśī ||

	raktamāllyāmbaradharaḥ śaktiśūlagadākaraḥ |

	caturbhujo meṣagamo varadaḥ syād dharāsutaḥ ||

	pītamālyāmbaradharaḥ karṇikāradaladyutiḥ |

	khaḍgacarmagadāpāṇiḥ siṃhastho varado budhaḥ ||

	devadaityagurū tadvat pītaśvetau caturbhujau |

	daṇḍinau varadau kāryau sākṣasūtrakamaṇḍalū ||

	indranīladyutiḥ śūlī varado gṛdhravāhanaḥ |

	bāṇabāṇāsanakaraḥ kartavyo 'rkasutaḥ sadā ||

	karālavadanaḥ khaḍgacarmaśūlī varapradaḥ |

	nīlasiṃhāsanayuto rāhus tatra praśasyate ||

	dhūmrā dvibāhavaḥ sarve gadino vikṛtānanāḥ |

	gṛdhrāsanagatā nityaṃ ketavaḥ syur varapradāḥ ||

	sarve kirīṭinaḥ kāryā grahā lokahitapradāḥ |

	svāṅgulenocchritāḥ sarve śatam aṣṭottaraṃ sadā ||

	bhāskarāṅgārakau raktau śvetau śukraniśākarau |

	somaputro guruś caiva tāv ubhau pītakau smṛtau ||

**[570]**	kṛṣṇaṃ śanaiśvaraṃ vidyād rāhuṃ ketuṃ tathaiva ca ||

nigadavyākhyātam etat | [atha rājānakaśitikaṇṭhakaviśeṣaḥ ] | devīpurāṇe |

	prabhākarasya pratimām idānīṃ śṛṇuta dvijāḥ |

	rathasthaṃ kārayed devaṃ padmahastaṃ sulocanam ||

	saptāśvaṃ caikavaktraṃ ca rathaṃ tasya prakalpayet |

	mukuṭena vicitreṇa padmagarbhasamaprabham ||

	nānābharaṇabhūṣābhyāṃ karābhyāṃ ghṛtapuṣkaram |

	skandhasthe puṣkare caiva līlayaiva ghṛte sadā ||

	colakacchannavapuṣaṃ kvacic citreṣu darśayet |

	vastrayugmasamopetaṃ caraṇau tejasāvṛtau ||

	pratīhārau ca kartavyau pārśvayor daṇḍapiṅgalau |

	kartavyau daṇḍahastau ca pārśvayoḥ puruṣāv ubhau ||

	lekhanīkṛtahastaṃ ca pārśve dhātāram avyayam |

	nānādevagaṇair yuktam evaṃ kuryād divākaram ||

	anūruṃ sārathiṃ cāsya padminīpatrasaṃnibham |

	aśvau ca valitagrīvau gandhasthau tasya pārśvayoḥ ||

	bhujaṅgarajjubhir baddhāḥ saptāśvarathasaṃyutāḥ |

	saptāśvasthaṃ padmahastaṃ tasmiṃś caiva prakalpayet ||

padmapurāṇe |

	ata eva raveḥ pādau na kaścit kārayet kvacit |

	yaḥ karoti sa pāpiṣṭhāṃ gatim āpnoti ninditām ||

	kuṣṭharūpam avāpnoti loke 'smin duḥkhasaṃjñitam ||

prasaṅgād vahnyādīnāṃ lakṣaṇam ucyate |

	vahnes tu lakṣaṇaṃ vakṣye sarvalakṣaṇalakṣitam |

	dīptaṃ suvarṇavapuṣam ardhacandrāsanaṃ vibhum ||

	bālārkasadṛśaṃ tasya vasanaṃ cātra kārayet |

	yajñopavītinaṃ kuryāl lambakūrcabhruvaṃ tathā ||

	kamaṇḍaluṃ vāmakare dakṣiṇe 'syākṣasūtrakam |

	jyālāvitānasaṃyuktam ajavāhanam ujjvalam ||

**[571]**	kuṇḍasthaṃ vāpi kurvīta mūrdhni saptaśikhānvitam |

	kātyāyanyāḥ pravakṣyāmi rūpaṃ daśabhujaṃ tathā ||

	trayāṇām api devānām anukārānukāriṇīm |

	jaṭājūṭasamāyuktām ardhendukṛtalakṣaṇām ||

	locanatrayasaṃyuktāṃ pūrṇedusadṛśānanām |

	atasīpuṣpasaṃkāśāṃ supratiṣṭhāṃ sulocanām ||

	navayauvanasaṃpannāṃ sarvāvayavabhūṣitām |

	sucārudaśanāṃ tadvat pīnonnatapayodharām ||

	tribhaṅgasthānsaṃsthānāṃ mahiṣāsuramardinīm |

	triśūlaṃ dakṣiṇe dadyāt khaḍgacakre tathaiva ca ||

	tīkṣṇadhārāṃ tathā śaktiṃ vāmato 'pi nibodhata |

	kheṭakaṃ pūrṇacāpaṃ ca pāśam aṅkuśam eva ca ||

	ghaṇṭāṃ ca paraśuṃ vāpi vāmataḥ saṃniveśayet |

	adhastān māhiṣaṃ tadvad dviśiraskaṃ pradarśayet ||

	śiraśchede nyaset tadvad dānavaṃ khaḍgapāṇikam |

	hṛdi śūlena nirbhinnaṃ tiryag ūrdhvaṃ ca bhūṣitam ||

	raktaraktīkṛtāṅgaṃ ca raktavisphuritekṣaṇam (?) |

	veṣṭitaṃ nāgapāśena bhrukuṭībhīṣaṇānanam ||

	vamadrudhiravaktraṃ ca devyāḥ siṃhaṃ pradarśayet |

	devyās tu dakṣiṇaṃ pādaṃ samaṃ siṃhopari sthitam ||

	kiṃcid ūrdhvaṃ tathā vāmam aṅguṣṭhaṃ mahiṣopari |

	stūyamānaṃ ca tadrūpam amaraiḥ saṃniveśayet ||

	vināyakaṃ pravakṣyāmi gajavaktraṃ trilocanam |

	sambodaraṃ caturbāhuṃ vyālayajñopavītinam ||

	stabdhakarṇaṃ bṛhattuṇḍam ekadaṃṣṭraṃ pṛthūdaram |

	svadantaṃ dakṣiṇakare utpalaṃ capare tathā ||

	modakaṃ paraśuṃ caiva vāmataḥ parikalpayet |

	bṛhatsaṃkṣiptagahanaṃ pīnaskandhāṅghripāṇikam |

	yuktaṃ buddhikubuddhibhyām adhastān mūṣakānvitam ||

	brahmā kamaṇḍaludharaḥ kartavyaḥ sa caturmukhaḥ ||

**[572]**	haṃsārūḍhaḥ kvacit kāryaḥ kvacic ca kamalāsanaḥ |

	varṇena kamalābhaś ca caturbāhuḥ śubhekṣaṇaḥ ||

	kamaṇḍaluṃ vāmakare sūtraṃ haste ca dakṣiṇe |

	vāme daṇḍadharas tadvat sruksruvau cāpi kalpayet ||

	munibhir devagandharvaiḥ stūyamānaṃ samantataḥ |

	kurvāṇam iva lokāṃs trīñ śuklāmbaradharaṃ vibhum ||

	mṛgacarmadharaṃ cāpi divyayajñopavītinam |

	ājyasthālī tathā pārśve tenaiva ca caruḥ puraḥ ||

	vāme pārśve ca sāvitrī dakṣiṇena sarasvatī |

	agre ca ṛṣayas tadvat kāryāḥ paitāmahe pade ||

iti rājānakaśitikaṇṭhapustake viśeṣaḥ | prāsaṅgikam uktvā prakṛtam ucyate | ete grahā agniṃ praṇīyāgnyāyatanasyottarapūrvadeśe pūjyāḥ | tathā ca matsyapurāṇam |

	gartasyottarapūrveṇa vitastidvayavistṛtām |

	vapratrayānvitāṃ vediṃ vitastyucchrāyasaṃyutām ||

	saṃsthāpanāya devānāṃ caturaśrām udakplavām ||

kuryād iti śeṣaḥ | gartaḥ khātam agnyāyatanam | vapro mekhalā |

	agnipraṇayanaṃ kṛtvā tasyām āvāhayet surān |

tasyāṃ tisraḥ koṣṭhakapaṅktayaḥ kāryā ekaikasyāṃ trayas trayaḥ koṣṭhakā bhavanti |

	bu.		śu.		caṃ.

	bṛ.		ā.		bhau.

	ke.		śa.		rā.

tatra |

	madhye tu bhāskaraṃ vidyāl lohitaṃ dakṣiṇena tu |

	uttareṇa guruṃ vidyād budhaṃ pūrvottareṇa tu ||

	pūrveṇa bhārgavaṃ vidyāt somaṃ dakṣiṇapūrvake |

	paścimena śaniṃ vidyād rāhuṃ dakṣiṇapaścime ||

	paścimottarataḥ ketuṃ sthāpec chuklataṇḍulaiḥ ||

ete cādityābhimukhāḥ sthāpyāḥ || 1.296 ||

_grahapūjām āha |_

**[573]**

	**yathāvarṇaṃ pradeyāni vāsāṃsi kusumāni ca |**

**	gandhāś ca balayaś caiva dhūpo deyaś ca gugguluḥ || 1.297 ||**

yo graho yad varṇas tasmai tad varṇāny eva vastrādīni deyāni | dhūpārthaṃ ca guggulur deyaḥ | atra vṛttavaśāt kramo na vivakṣitaḥ so 'nyato 'vagantavya iti gandhapuṣpadhūpavastrabalayaḥ krameṇa deyāḥ | atra sarvebhyo grahebhyo gandhapuṣpāṇi deyāni tathā dhūpādi na punar ekasmai gandhādibaliparyantaṃ dattvānyasmai deyam || 1.297 ||

_homavidhim āha_ |

	**kartavyā mantravantaś ca caravaḥ pratidaivatam |**

na kevalam ādityādīnāṃ pūjaiva kāryā | kiṃ tu pratyekaṃ caravaś ca | te ca mantravantaḥ kāryāḥ | anavasrāvito viśado 'ntarūṣmapakva odanaś caruḥ | tantravanta iti pāṭhe pākayajñetikartavyatā tantram | atra ca navānām api grahayāgānāṃ(ṇāṃ) tulyakālatvād idhmādyabhedaḥ | tad āha śaunakaḥ: "ekabarhiridhmājyasviṣṭakṛtaḥ syus tulyakālāḥ" | tad eṣābhiyajñabhāgā gathābhigīyate |

	pākayajñān samāsādya ekājyān ekabarhiṣaḥ |

	ekasviṣṭakṛtaḥ kuryān nānāpi sati daivate || iti |

_homamantrān āha_ |

	**ākṛṣṇena imaṃ devā agnir mūrdhā divaḥ kakut || 1.298 ||**

**	udbudhyasveti ca ṛco yathāsaṃkhyaṃ prakīrtitāḥ |**

**	bṛhaspate atiyadaryas tathaivānnāt parisrutaḥ || 1.299 ||**

**	śaṃ no devīs tathā kāṇḍāt ketuṃ kṛṇvan nimā api |**

bhagavato yogīśvarasya vājasaneya(yi)tvād vājasaneyake samāmnātā evātra mantrā grāhyāḥ | tatratyāny evārṣādīni veditavyāni | ākṛṣṇenetyādyā navasaṃkhyākā mantrā navasaṃkhyākeṣv evādityādidai(de)vatyeṣu homeṣu yathāsaṃkhyaṃ prakīrtitā vihitāḥ | tatraikaikasya caror ekaivāhutiḥ pākayajñātideśena prāptā saty ekaikena mantreṇa kāryā, āhutīnāṃ saṃkhyāntarāvidhānāt | ākṛṣṇeneti hiraṇyastūpa **[574]** āṅgirasa ṛṣir ādityo devatā triṣṭup chandaḥ | imaṃ devā iti devāḥ somo yajuḥ | agnir mūrdheti viśvarūpa āṅgiraso 'ṅgārako gāyatrī | udbudhyasveti parameṣṭhī budhas triṣṭup | annāt parisruta iti aśvisarasvatīndrāḥ śukro 'tijagatī | saṃ no devīr iti sindhudvīpaḥ śanaiścaro gāyatrī | kāṇḍāt kāṇḍād ity agnī rahur anuṣṭup | ketuṃ kṛṇvann iti madhucchandāḥ ketur gāyatrī || 1.298, 299 ||

_caruhomānantaraṃ samidhāṃ svarūpapratipādanapūrvakaṃ tad dhomam āha_ |

	**arkaḥ palāśaḥ khadiras tv apāmārgo 'tha pippalaḥ || 1.300 ||**

**	udumbaraḥ śamī dūrvā kuśāś ca samidhaḥ kramāt |**

**	ekaikasyāṣṭaśatakam aṣṭāviṃśatir eva vā || 1.301 ||**

**	hotavyā madhusarpirbhyāṃ dadhnā kṣīreṇa saṃyutāḥ |**

arkādyāḥ samidho yathā grahasyā(ma)ṣṭottaraśatam aṣṭāviṃśatir vā madhughṛtābhyāṃ dadhipayobhyāṃ vābhyaktāḥ pūrvoktair mantrair hotavyāḥ | ekaikasyeti ṣaṣṭī caturthyarthe | eṣā ca saṃkhyā samidhām eva tadekavākyatvāt | na ca sakṛn mantram uccāryaikadevatātvena saha samidhaḥ prakṣeptavyāḥ kiṃ tv ekaikāḥ, pratyekaṃ ca mantrāvṛttiḥ | tad uktaṃ matsyapurāṇe |

	svena svenaiva mantreṇa hotavyāḥ samidhaḥ pṛthak |

tathā |

	prādeśamātrāḥ saśikhāḥ śākhāparṇavipāṭitāḥ |

	samidhaḥ kalpayet prājñaḥ sarvakarmasu sarvadā || 1.300, 301 ||

_brāhmaṇabhojanadrayam āha_ |

	**guḍaudanaṃ pāyasaṃ ca haviṣyaṃ kṣīraṣa(ṣā)ṣṭikam || 1.302 ||**

**	dadhyodanaṃ ghṛtānnaṃ ca kṛsarāmiṣacitrakam |**

**	dadyād grahakramād etad dvijebhyo bhojanaṃ budhaḥ || 1.303 ||**

**	śaktito vā yathālābhaṃ satkṛtya vidhipūrvakam |**

guḍaudanādikaṃ yathāgrahakramaṃ dvijebhyo bhojanaṃ dadyāt | bhujyata iti **[575]** vyutpattyā bhojyam eva bhojanam | yadi guḍaudanaṃ na śaknuyād dātuṃ tato yathāśakti yathālābhaṃ sādhāraṇaṃ yathāvidhi dadyāt | guḍamiśra odano guḍaudanaḥ | kṣīramiśraṃ ṣaṣṭikānnaṃ kṣīraṣāṣṭikam | ṣaṣṭiko vrīhiviśeṣaḥ | guḍaudanaṃ sarvam evātra citrakam || 1.302, 303 ||

_dakṣinā āha_ |

	**dhenuḥ śaṅkhas tathānaḍvān hema vāso hayaḥ kramāt || 1.304 ||**

**	kṛṣṇā gaur āyasaṃ chaga etā vai dakṣiṇā smṛtāḥ |**

grahakrameṇa dakṣiṇā dātavyāḥ | dhenur navaprasūtā gauḥ | anaso voḍhā gaur anaḍvān | āyasaṃ lohamayam | prasiddham anyat | etāś ca dakṣiṇā ṛtvigbhya eva deyāḥ | tathā matsyapurāṇam |

	yajamānaḥ sapatnīka ṛtvijas tu samāhitaḥ |

	dakṣiṇābhiḥ prayatnena pūjayed gatavismayaḥ ||

	sūryāya kapilāṃ dhenuṃ dadyāc chaṅkhaṃ tathendave |

	raktaṃ dhuraṃdharaṃ dadyād bhaumāya kakudānvitam ||

	budhāya jātarūpaṃ tu gurave pītavāsasī |

	śvetāśvaṃ daityagurave kṛṣṇāṃ gām arkasūnave ||

	āyasaṃ rāhave dadyāt ketave chāgam uttamam |

	suvarṇena samāḥ kāryāḥ yajamānena dakṣiṇāḥ ||

	sarveṣām atha vā gāvo dātavyā hemabhūṣitāḥ |

	suvarṇam atha vā dadyād gurur vā yena tuṣyati || 1.304 ||

	**yaś ca yasya yadā duḥsthaḥ sa taṃ yatnena pūjayet || 1.305 ||**

**	brahmaṇaiṣāṃ varo dattaḥ pūjitāḥ pūjayiṣyatha |**

yasya puruṣasya yo graho duḥstho duḥkhapradarāśisthito yathā janmarāśito 'ṣṭamarāśisthaḥ sa taṃ graham itaragrahapūjāyām asamartha ekam eva yatnenādareṇoktavidhinā pūjayet | pūjito hi na duḥkhakaro bhavati | yata eṣāṃ grahāṇāṃ yūyaṃ pūjayitāraṃ pūjayiṣyathābhilaṣitena phalena yojayiṣyatheti brahmaṇā prajāpatinā varo dattaḥ || 1.305 ||

_atraiva hetvantaram āha_ |

**[576]**	**grahādhīnā narendrāṇām ucchrāyāḥ patanāni ca || 1.306 ||**

**	bhāvābhāvau ca jagatas tasmāt pūjyatamā grahāḥ |**

anekajanmārjitapuṇyopacayavatām api narendrāṇāṃ yato grahādhīnā ucchrāyāḥ saṃpadatiśayāḥ patanāni ca vipadatiśayarūpāṇi | tathā jagato bhāvābhāvāv udayapralayau grahādhīnāv eva | tasmād anyebhyaḥ pūjyatarebhyo 'tiśayena grahā uktaprakāreṇa pūjyāḥ | yady api dharmādharmau sukhaduḥkhānubhavahetū tathāpi kālaviśeṣam anapekṣya na tad dhetū bhavataḥ | na ca grahāṇāṃ gativiśeṣam antareṇ kālaniśeṣaḥ śakyo nirūpayitum iti bhavati grahādhīnatvaṃ narendrocchrāyāder ato viruddhaṃ grahasthānaṃ dṛṣṭvā tatsūcitāgāmiduḥkhasaṃghātavighātāya grahayajñaḥ kāryaḥ | sa hi śāntikāmasya vihita iti tātparyārthaḥ || 1.306 ||

**iti śrīvidhyādharavaṃśaprabhavaśrīśilāhāranarendrajīmūtavāhanānvayaprasūta-**

**śrīmadaprādityadevaviracite yājñavalkīyadharmaśāstranibandhe 'parārke**

**grahayajñavidhiprakaraṇaṃ samāptam || 11 ||**

**atha saṭīkāyājñavalkyasmṛtau**

**rājadharmaprakaraṇam | (12)**

_uktā varṇadharmā brahmacārigṛhasthadharmāś ca | idānīṃ rājño gṛhasthasyāpi guṇavato janapadaparipālanādīn dharmān vaktuṃ yair guṇair yuktaḥ prajpālanayogyo bhavati tāṃs tāvad āha_ |

	**mahotsāhaḥ sthūlalakṣaḥ kṛtajño vṛddhasevakaḥ || 1.307 ||**

**	vinītaḥ sattvasaṃpannaḥ kulīnaḥ satyavāk śuciḥ |**

**	adīrghasūtrī smṛtimān akṣudro 'paruṣas tathā || 1.308 ||**

**	dhārmiko 'vyasanaś caiva prājñaḥ śūro rahasyavit |**

**	svarandhragoptānvīkṣikyāṃ daṇḍanītyāṃ tathaiva ca || 1.309 ||**

**	vinītas tv atha vārtāyāṃ trayyāṃ caiva narādhipaḥ |**

**[577]**

mahotsāhatvādiguṇavān nṛpo bhavati | brāhmaṇādīnāṃ svakarmasthāpanayogyo bhavatīty arthaḥ | mahotsāho mahodyamaḥ | mahāviṣayatvam avihanyamānatvaṃ cotsāhasya mahattvam | sthūlalakṣo bahupradaḥ | yaḥ pratyupakārāyopakāriṇaṃ smarati sa kṛtajñaḥ | vṛddhasevako jñānādiguṇavṛddhapuruṣopāsakaḥ | vinīto gurvādiṣu namraḥ | durdaśām āpanno 'pi na nyāyaḍ apaiti yaḥ sa sāttvikaḥ | kulīnaḥ śuddhavaṃśajaḥ | satyavāk satyapratijñaḥ | śucir bāhyābhyantaraśaucavān | adīrghasūtrī pramite 'rthe nirāśaṅkaḥ | smṛtimān praśastasmṛtiḥ | akṣudro 'nalpahṛdayaḥ | yo 'lpāpakāropakārābhyāṃ kopaprasādavān so 'lpahṛdayaḥ | aparuṣo 'kaṭhoravāk | dhārmikaḥ prasiddhaḥ | puruṣārthavikṣepakaṃ dyūtādikaṃ vyasanaṃ tadrahito 'vyasanaḥ | prājñaśūrau prasiddhau | rahasyavid atmajño mantrajñaḥ pararandhrajño vā | svarandhragoptā yatra rājyāṅgavaikalye paraḥ praviśati tad randhraṃ tasya goptā rakṣakaḥ | ānvīkṣikyāṃ daṇḍanītyāṃ vārtāyāṃ trayyāṃ ca vinītaḥ śikṣitaḥ | ānvīkṣikī vedādyaviruddhanyāyavidyā | daṇḍanītir arthaśāstram | vārtā kṛṣyādividyā | ṛgyajuḥsāmāni trayī | trayīgrahaṇāt tatparikarabhūtāni vyākaraṇādyaṅgāni mīmāṃsāpurāṇadharmaśāstrāṇi gṛhyante || 1.307, 308, 309 ||

	**sa mantriṇaḥ prakurvīta prājñān maulān sthirāñ śucīn || 1.310 ||**

**	taiḥ sārdhaṃ cintayed rājyaṃ vipreṇātha tataḥ svayam |**

sa uktaguṇo rājā mantriṇaḥ kāryākāryavidaḥ | prājñān ūhāpohasamarthān | maulān pitṛpāramparyāgatān | sthirān svāmihiteṣv acañcalān | śucīñ śuddhopadhān | prakurvīta prayatnād upādadīta | atha taiḥ saha rājyaṃ rājakarma ṣāḍguṇyaṃ tadaṅgāni ca svāmyādīni cintayet | heyopādeyatayā vicārayed ity arthaḥ | atha ṣāḍguṇyavidā punar vipreṇa saha vicārayet | punaś ca svayaṃ tam evārthaṃ sādhakabādhakapramāṇavattayā niścinuyāt || 1.310 ||

	**purohitaṃ ca kurvīta daivajñam uditoditam || 1.3111 ||**

**	daṇḍanītyāṃ ca kuśalam atharvāṅgirase tathā |**

daivajñatvādiguṇopetaṃ brāhmaṇaṃ purohitaṃ kurvīta | daivajño jyotiḥśāstravit | tena hi śāstreṇa prāṇināṃ daivaṃ karmavipāko jñāyate | ye mantriṇām uditā uktāḥ **[578]** prājñādayo guṇās te yasyoditā udbhūtāḥ sa uditoditaḥ | purohitaṃprakurvīta vṛṇvīta, vareṇa hi purohitatvam utpadyate yathādhvaryutvādikam || 1.311 ||

	**śrautasmārtakriyāhetor vṛṇuyād eva cartvijaḥ || 312 ||**

**	yajñāṃś caiva prakurvīta vidhivad bhūridakṣiṇān |**

śrutismṛtivihitāgihotrādikarmaṇāṃ kriyānuṣṭhānaṃ tasmāt prayojanībhūtād dhetor brahmādīn ṛtvijo vṛṇuyāt, varaṇena kuryāt | yathādhānenāvahanīyādīn | tathā haviḥsaṃsthāsomasaṃsthādīn yajñān bhūridakṣiṇān prāthamakalpitakadakṣiṇādānayuktān kuryāt || 312 ||

	**bhogāṃś ca dadyād viprebhyo vasūni vividhāni ca || 1.313 ||**

**	akṣayo 'yaṃ nidhī rājñāṃ yad vipreṣūpapāditam |**

**	askannam avyathaṃ caiva prāyaścittair aduṣitam || 1.314 ||**

**	agneḥ sakāśād viprāgnau hutaṃ śreṣṭham ihocyate |**

bhogān bhoktavyān annaviśeṣān vasūni draviṇāni ca gobhūhiraṇyādīni viprebhyo rājā dadyāt | atra praśaṃsā — ātmopakārakatvena nidhitulyatvān nidhir ayaṃ rājñāṃ yad vipreṣūpapāditaṃ viprebhyo dattam | laukiko nidhir upabhogāt prāk caurādivaśāt kadācit kṣīyate dattaṃ na tu tatheti viśeṣo 'yam iti vaktum uktam akṣaya iti | bhūmau nihitaṃ suvarṇādikaṃ nidhiḥ | na kevalaṃ nidher utkṛṣṭaṃ dānam api tv agnihotrāder api | na hi dāne kascyacid dhaviṣaḥ skannaṃ vyathanaṃ vā vidyate yena viguṇaṃ sad agnhotrādivad aphalaṃ syāt | prāyaścittaiś ca prāyaścittanimittaiś cānyair doṣair adūṣitam | ata āhavanīyādyagnisaṃbandhino hutād dhomād viprātmany agnau hutaṃ dattaṃ śreṣṭhaṃ praśastataraṃ bhavati || 1.313, 314 ||

_evaṃ dīyamānaṃ dhanaṃ yato 'tyantopakārakaṃ bhavaty atas tadarjanādikaṃ yathā kāryaṃ tad āha_ |

	**alabdham īhed dharmeṇa labdhaṃ yatnena pālayet || 1.315 ||**

**	pālitaṃ vardhayen nītyā vṛddhaṃ pātreṣu nikṣipet |**

alabdham aprāptaṃ dharmeṇeheta lipseta | ātmasātkṛtaṃ yatnena tat praṇidhānena pālayed rakṣet | pālitaṃ ca nītyā śāstroktena prakāreṇa vardhayed upacayaṃ gamayet | vivṛddhaṃ ca pātreṣu vidyātapvṛttasaṃpanneṣu nikṣiped dadyāt || 1.315 ||

**[579]**

	**datvā bhūmiṃ nibandhaṃ vā kṛtvā lekhyaṃ ca kārayet || 1.316 ||**

**	āgāmibhadranṛpatiparijñānāya pārthivaḥ |**

bhūmiṃ kṣetrārāmagrāmādikāṃ viprāya datvā nibandhanaṃ vā kṛtvā bhadrāṇāṃ śāstrārthakāriṇām āgāmināṃ nṛpatīnāṃ parijñānāya pariniścayāya pārthivaḥ pṛthivīpatir likhitaṃ lekhyaṃ vakṣyamāṇaprakāraṃ kārayet | asmin grāme pratikṣetraṃ kṣetrasvāminaitad dhanam asmai pratyabdaṃ pratimāsaṃ vā deyam ity evamādiniyamo nibandhaḥ || 1.316 ||

_lekhyavidhim āha_ |

	**paṭe vā tāmrapaṭṭe vā svamudroparicihnitam || 1.317 ||**

**	abhilekhyātmano vaṃśyān ātmānaṃ ca mahīpatiḥ |**

**	pratigrahaparīmāṇaṃ dānacchedopavarṇanam || 1.318 ||**

**	svahastakālasaṃpannaṃ śāsanaṃ kārayet sthiram |**

paṭe vā kārpāsādimaye tāmrapaṭṭe vātmanaḥ pitṛpitāmahādīn vidyāvikramadharmādiguṇopetān abhilekhyāsyāyaṃ putro 'syāyaṃ pautra ity evaṃ lekhayitvātmānaṃ ca mahīpatir lekhayitvā pratigṛhyata iti pratigraho bhūmir nibandhaś ca tasya chedo 'pahāraḥ sa upavarṇyate pratyavāyajanakatayā yena śāstreṇa tad dānacchedopavarṇanaṃ tac ca lekhayitvā svahastena mataṃ me 'mukaputrasya mahīpater iti svahastalikhitena dānakālena ca vatsarādinā saṃpannaṃ śāsanaṃ śiṣyante dānāpahārān nivartyante bhāvino bhūpatiprabhṛtayo yena tacchāsanaṃ svamudrayā svakulacihnena garuḍādinā cihnitam aṅkitaṃ cirakālasthāpi kārayet | na hi tena vinā pratigrahītā tadvaṃśyo vā bhūminibandhau śaknuyād upabhoktum | atra bṛhaspatiḥ |

	datvā bhūmyādikaṃ rājā tāmrapaṭṭe 'tha vā paṭe |

	śāsanaṃ kārayed dharmyaṃ sthānavaṃśyādisaṃyutam ||

	anācchedyam anāhāryaṃ sarvabhāvyavivarjitam |

	candrārkasamakālīnaṃ putrapautrānvayāgatam ||

**[580]**	dātuḥ pālayituḥ svargaṃ hartur narakam eva ca |

	ṣaṣṭiṃ varṣasahasrāṇi dānacchedaphalaṃ likhet ||

	svamudrāvarṣamāsārdhadinādhyakṣākṣarānvitam |

	evaṃvidhaṃ rājakṛtaṃ śāsanaṃ samudāhṛtam ||

vyāsaḥ |

	rājñā tu svayam ādiṣṭaḥ saṃdhivigrahalekhakaḥ |

	tāmrapaṭṭe paṭe vāpi pralikhed rājaśāsanam ||

	sthānaṃ vaṃśānupūrvī ca deśaṃ grāmam upāgatam |

	brāhmaṇāṃs tu tathaivānyān mānyān adhikṛtāṃl likhet ||

	kuṭumbino 'tha kāyasthadūtavaidyamahattarān |

	medacaṇḍālaparyatān sarvān saṃbodhaynn iti ||

	mātāpitror ātmanaś ca puṇyāyāmukasūnave |

	dattaṃ mayāmukāyādya dānaṃ sabrahmacāriṇe ||

	candrārkasamakālīnaṃ putrapautrānvayānugam |

	anācchedyam anāhāryaṃ sarvabhāvyavivarjitam ||

	dātuḥ pālayituḥ svargaṃ hartur narakam eva ca |

	ṣaṣṭiṃ varṣasahasrāṇi dānacchedaphalaṃ likhet ||

	jñātaṃ mayeti likhitaṃ dātradhyakākṣarair yutam |

	abdamāsatadardhāhārājamudrāṅkitaṃ tathā ||

	anena vidhinā lekhyaṃ rājaśāsanakaṃ likhet || 1.317, 318 ||

_kaṃ deśaviśeṣam adhivasitvaitat kāryam ity apekṣyate 'ta āha |_

	**ramyaṃ paśavyam ājīvyaṃ jāṅgalaṃ deśam āvaset || 1.319 ||**

**	tatra durgāṇi kurvīta janakośātmaguptaye |**

ramyo manoharaḥ | paśavyaḥ paśubhyo hitaḥ | ājīvyaḥ samantād upajīvyauṣadhivanaspatitṛṇakāṣṭhādimān | jāṅgalaḥ svalpavṛkṣodakaparvato bahupakṣimṛgaḥ pracuravarṣātapaś ca | evaṃvidhaṃ deśaṃ nṛpatir āvaset | tatra ca durgāṇi giridurgaprabhṛtīni prajādhanayor ātmanaś ca rakṣārthaṃ kurvīta || 1.319 ||

	**tatra tatra ca niṣṇātān adhyakṣān kuśalāñ śucīn || 1.320 ||**

**	prakuryād āyakarmāntavyayakarmasu codyatān |**

**[581]**

tatra tatra dharmārthakāmaprayojaneṣu karmasu niṣṇātān pravīṇān dharmaśāstrābhijñān karmakuśalāñ śucīn artheṣu codyatān udyamino dhanāgamāntaḥpuravyayakarmasv adhyakṣān adhikṛtapuruṣaniyantṝn prayatnena kuryāt | yogyān adhyakṣān kuryād iti tātparyārthaḥ | yogyatā coktā |

	prājñatvam upadhāśuddhir apramādo 'bhiyuktatā |

	kāryeṣu vyasanābhāvaḥ svāmibhaktiś ca yogyatā ||

manuḥ |

	teṣām artha niyuñjīta śūrān dakṣān kulodgatān |

	śucīn ākarakarmānte bhīrūn antarveśmani ||

viṣṇuḥ: "ākaralakṣaṇaśulkataranāgavaneṣv āptān niyuñjīta | dharmiṣṭhān dharmakāryeṣu nipuṇān arthakāryeṣu śūrān saṅgrāmakarmasu | ugrān ugreṣu ṣaṇḍān strīṣu" | manuḥ |

	adhyakṣān vividhān kuryāt tatra tatra vipaścitaḥ |

	te 'sya sarvāṇy avekṣeran nṝṇāṃ kāryāṇi kurvatām ||

kāryāṇi sukṛtaduṣkṛtakarmāṇi || 1.320 ||

	**nātaḥ parataro dharmo nṛpāṇāṃ yad raṇārjitam || 1.321 ||**

**	viprebhyo dīyate dravyaṃ prajābhyaś cābhayaṃ sadā |**

yad raṇāptadhanapradānaṃ viprebhyaḥ prajābhyaś ca yad abhayapradānaṃ nāsmād adhiko 'nyo nṛpāṇāṃ dharmo 'sti | etad upāyaś ca śatruvijaya iti tatsiddhaye ca raṇaṃ kuryād iti tātparyārthaḥ || 1.321 ||

_<span style="text-decoration:underline;">nanu</span> pākṣikānarthaśaṅkayā prekṣāvatāṃ raṇe pravṛttir anupapanneti vidhir ayaṃ na ghaṭata ity atrāha |_

	**ya āhaveṣu yudhyante bhūmyartham aparāṅmukhā || 1.322 ||**

**	akūṭair āyudhair yānti te svargaṃ yogino yathā |**

ye kṣatriyāḥ svakīyāṃ bhūmiṃ rakṣituṃ parakīyāṃ ca jetum akūṭair āyudhair yudhyante na ca śatrūn prati parāṅmukhā bhavanti te śatrubhir hatā yogivat svargaṃ yānti svargaṃ bhuktvā mucyanta ity arthaḥ | āhavāḥ saṅgrāmāḥ | kūṭāni viṣadighānīti tadanyāny akūṭāni | akūṭair viṣarahitair ity arthaḥ | evaṃ ca sati niyamenāyam asau vā loko jito bhavatīti nāsty anarthaśaṅkā nivartikā || 1.322 ||

**[582]**

	**padāni kratutulyāni bhagneṣv avinivartinām || 1.323 ||**

**	rājā sukṛtam ādatte hatānāṃ vipalāyinām |**

nijarājasainikeṣu śatrubhayāt palāyanapareṣu bhagneṣu ye na nivartante kiṃ tu śatruṃ pratyabhimukhā yānti teṣāṃ padāni kratubhir yajñais tulyāni pade pade yajñaphalaṃ labhanta ity arthaḥ | palāyanaparāṇāṃ tu śatruhatānāṃ dharmaṃ svāmī gṛhṇāti || 1.323 ||

	**tavāhaṃvādinaṃ klībaṃ nirhetiṃ parasaṃgatam || 1.324 ||**

**	na hanyād vinivṛttaṃ ca yuddhaprekṣaṇakādikam |**

tavāham asmīti vadantaṃ klībaṃ bhītaṃ nirhetiṃ nirāyudhaṃ parasaṃgatam anyena yudhyamānaṃ nivṛttaṃ palāyamānaṃ yuddhaprekṣaṇakādīṃś ca hanyāt || 1.324 ||

_kiṃ ca_ |

	**kṛtarakṣaḥ samutthāya paśyed āyavyayau svayam || 1.325 ||**

**	vyavahārāṃs tato dṛṣṭvā snātvā bhuñjīta kāmataḥ |**

ātmanaḥ prajānāṃ ca rakṣāṃ vidhāyodyamam avalambyādhikṛtaiḥ kriyamāṇāv āyavyayau svayaṃ paśyet | svayaṃ grahaṇam ādarārtham | tadanantaram anyeṣām ṛṇādānādīn vyavahārān dṛṣṭvā snātvā kāmato bhuñjīta | snānagrahaṇaṃ sakalamādhyāhnikopalakṣaṇam | kāmata iti satyāṃ bubhukṣāyām ity arthaḥ || 1.325 ||

	**hiraṇyaṃ vyāpṛtānītaṃ bhāṇḍāgāre nyaset tataḥ || 1.326 ||**

**	paśyec cārāṃs tato dūtān preṣayen mantrisaṃgataḥ |**

vyāpṛtaiḥ karādidānādhikṛtair ānītaṃ hiraṇyādidhanaṃ bhāṇḍāgāre dhananidhānaśālāyāṃ kṣipet | tataś cārāñ śatruprabhṛticeṣṭitajñānāya gūḍhaprahitān āgatāṃs tadvākyaśravaṇāya paśyet | tato mantribhiḥ saṃgataḥ kāryajātaṃ niścitya tatsiddhaye dūtān preṣayet || 1.326 ||

	**tataḥ svairavihārī syān mantribhir vā samāgataḥ || 1.327 ||**

**	balānāṃ darśanaṃ kṛtvā senānyā saha cintayet |**

**[583]**

bhuktvā yatheccham aṅganābhiḥ saha krīḍet | kāryavaśān mantrisamāgato vā bhavet | tato hastyaśvādibalāni dṛṣṭvā senānyā camūpatinā saha balaviṣayam arthaṃ cintayet || 1.327 ||

	**saṃdhyām upāsya śṛṇuyāc cārāṇāṃ gūḍhabhāṣitam || 1.328 ||**

**	gītanṛttaiś ca bhuñjīta paṭhet svādhyāyam eva ca |**

sāyaṃsaṃdhyām upāsya rahasyaṃ cāravākyaṃ śrutvā gītanṛttaiḥ kiyantam api kālaṃ nītvā vedaṃ paṭhet || 1.328 ||

	**saṃviśet tūryaghoṣeṇa pratibudhyet tathaiva ca || 1.329 ||**

**	śāstrāṇi cintayed buddhvā sarvakartavyatās tathā |**

tūryaghoṣeṇa vīṇāveṇumṛdaṅgādinādena svāpārthaṃ viśet | tūryaghoṣeṇaiva pratibudhyeta | brāhme muhūrte buddhvā śāstrāṇi śrutismṛtivacāṃsi tadarthāvagamopāyāṃś ca nigamaniruktādīn sarvāṇi kāryāṇi cintayet || 1.329 ||

	**preṣayec ca tataś cārān sveṣv anyeṣu ca sādaram || 1.330 ||**

**	ṛtvikpurohitācāryair āśīrbhir abhinanditaḥ |**

**	dṛṣṭvā jyotirvido vaidyān dadyād gāḥ kāñcanaṃ mahīm || 1.331 ||**

**	naiveśikāni ca tathā śrotriyāṇāṃ gṛhāṇi ca |**

saṃdhyām upāsya rahasi sthitvā vaṇigvaidyaparivrājakabauddhadigambarādiveśadhāriṇo nigūḍhān paraceṣṭāvedinaś cārān sveṣu svakīyeṣu sāmantādiṣu cānyeṣu cāmitrādiṣu rājasu sādaraṃ yathā bhavati tathā preṣayet | tata ṛtvigādibhir āyurārogyavijayaiśvaryādiviṣayābhir āśīrbhir abhinandito jyotirvido vaidyāṃś cāgatān dṛṣṭvā tadadhīnaṃ ca kāryaṃ taiḥ saha vicārya gāḥ kāñcanaṃ mahīṃ naiveśikāni ca śrotriyebhyo dadyāt | vivāhopakaraṇaṃ gṛhopakaraṇaṃ vā naiveśikam | śrotriyāṇām iti ṣaṣṭhī caturthyarthe || 1.330, 331 ||

	**brāhmaṇeṣu kṣamī snigdheṣv ajihmaḥ krodhano 'riṣu || 1.332 ||**

**	syād rājā bhṛtyavarge ca prajāsu ca yathā pitā |**

brāhmaṇān snigdhāñ śatrūn prati yathāsaṃkhyaṃ kṣamām ārjavaṃ krodhaṃ ca kuryāt | bhṛtyān prajāś ca pitṛvat pālayet || 1.332 ||

**[584]**

_prajāpālanaphalam āha_ |

	**puṇyaṣaḍbhāgam ādatte nyāyena paripālayan || 1.333 ||**

**	sarvadānādhikaṃ yasmāt prajānāṃ paripālanam |**

rājñā nyāyena śāstroktaprakāreṇa pālyamānāḥ prajā yat puṇyaṃ kurvanti tat ṣaṣṭhāṃśasaṃmitaṃ rājā puṇyaṃ labhate sarvebhyo 'pi dānebhyaḥ prajānāṃ paripālanam abhayadānātmakam adhikaṃ yasmāt tasmād upapannaḥ puṇyaṣaḍbhāgalābhaḥ | evaṃ prajāpālanaṃ ca dhanaprāptau hetur yathā brāhmaṇasya pratigrahādiḥ || 1.333 ||

_kiṃ ca_ |

	**cāṭataskaradurvṛttamahāsāhasikādibhiḥ || 334 ||**

**	pīḍyamānāḥ prajā rakṣet kāyasthaiś ca viśeṣataḥ |**

cāṭādibhyo duḥkhakāribhyaḥ prajā rakṣet | pūrvaślokaiḥ svayaṃ na pīḍayed ity arthād uktam | atra tu yathā paro na pīḍayet tathā kuryād ity ucyate | cāṭaḥ piśunaḥ | taskaraḥ prasiddhaḥ | durvṛttaḥ paradārahārakādiḥ | mahāsāhasiko manuṣyamāraṇabandigrahādikārī | ādiśabdena kūṭamānakūṭasuvarṇādikāriṇo lakṣyante | kāyasthāḥ karādhikṛtāḥ || 1.334 ||

_prajānām rakṣaṇe doṣagauravam āha |_

	**arakṣyamāṇāḥ kurvanti yat kiṃcit kilbiṣaṃ prajāḥ || 1.335 ||**

**	tasmāt tu nṛpater ardhaṃ yasmād gṛhṇāty asau karān |**

arakṣyamāṇā nṛpeṇāpālyamānā adharmād anivāryamāṇāḥ prajāś cauryapāradāryādikaṃ yat pāpaṃ kurvanti tasmāt pāpān nṛpater ardhaṃ bhavati | nṛpatir ardhaṃ gṛhṇātīty arthaḥ | yasmād asau tāsāṃ pālanārthaṃ karān ādatte | atrāpi pāpārdhasaṃmitaṃ pāpaṃ rājño bhavatīti mantavyam | na hy anyakṛtam adṛṣṭam anyasya bhavati || 1.335 ||

	**ye rāṣṭrādhikṛtās teṣāṃ cārair jñātvā viceṣṭitam || 1.336 ||**

**	sādhūn saṃmānayed rājā viparītāṃs tu ghātayet |**

**	utkocajīvino dravyahīnān kṛtvā vivāsayet || 1.337 ||**

**	sadānamānasatkārāñ śrotriyān vāsayet sadā |**

**[585]**

ye rāṣṭre karādānāya prajāpālanāya cādhikṛtā niyuktās teṣāṃ viceṣṭitaṃ vividhaṃ vyāpārajātaṃ cāravacanebhyo 'vadhārya sādhūn yathoktakāriṇo dānādinā saṃmānayet | viparītān asādhūn ghātayed yathādoṣaṃ daṇḍayet | utkocajīvanaśīlān dravyahīnān kṛtvā deśān nirvāsayet | kāryārthaṃ kāryino dhanādānam utkocaḥ | śrotriyān dānamānasatkārayuktān kṛtvā sarvadā vāsayet | mānaḥ pūjāsatkāraḥ sādhutvakhyāpako vyāpāraḥ || 1.336, 337 ||

	**anyāyena nṛpo rāṣṭrāt svakośaṃ yo 'bhirakṣati || 1.338 ||**

**	so 'cirād vigataśrīko nāśam eti sabāndhavaḥ |**

anyāyena pratiṣiddhamārgeṇa svarāṣṭrād dhanam ādāya yo rājā kośaṃ dhanasaṃcayair vardhayati so 'cirād vyapetalakṣmīkaḥ sabāndhavo vinaśyati || 1.338 ||

	**prajāpīḍanasaṃtāpāt samudbhūto hutāśanaḥ || 1.339 ||**

**	rājñaḥ śriyaṃ kulaṃ prāṇān nādagdhvā vinivartate |**

prajānāṃ pīḍanād anyāyena dhanādānād yaḥ saṃtāpo duḥkhātiśayas tasmād dhutāśana iva duḥkhahetur adharmarāśiḥ samudbhūto rājñaḥ śrīprabhṛtīny adagdhvā pradhvaṃsam anītvā na nivartate na viramati || 1.339 ||

	**ya eva nṛpater dharmaḥ svarāṣṭraparipālane || 1.340 ||**

**	tam eva kṛcchram āpnoti pararāṣṭraṃ vaśaṃ nayan |**

nigadavyākhyātam etat || 1.340 ||

_pararāṣṭraviṣaye viśeṣam āha |_

	**kiṃ tu yasmin ya ācāro vyavahāraḥ kulasthitiḥ || 1.341 ||**

**	tathaiva paripālyo 'sau yadā vaśam upāgataḥ |**

yasmin pararāṣṭre ya ācāro holākādir yaś ca vyavahāro nāṇakādinibandhano yā ca kulasthitir etāvad dhanaṃ rājñe 'nena kulena deyam ity evamāirūpā sa rāṣṭro vaśam upāgatas tenaivācārādinā yuktaḥ paripālanīyaḥ || 1.341 ||

	**mantramūlaṃ yato rājyam ato mantraṃ surakṣitam || 1.342 ||**

**	kuryād yathāsya na viduḥ karmaṇām ā phalodayāt |**

**[586]**

karmaṇāṃ mantrato 'nuṣṭheyatayā niścitānām ā mantraphalodayāt prāktanakarmānuṣṭhānāt pare yathā mantraṃ na vidus tathā taṃ surakṣitaṃ kuryāt | surakṣitamantramūlatvād rājyasya || 1.342 ||

	**arir mitram udāsīno 'nantaras tatparaḥ paraḥ || 1.343 ||**

**	kramaśo maṇḍalaṃ cintyaṃ sāmādibhir upakramaiḥ |**

anantaraikāntaradvyantarā rājāno yathākramam arir mitram udāsīnaś catasṛṣu dikṣu vijñeyāḥ | etad dvādaśarājakaṃ maṇḍalaṃ vakṣyamāṇasvarūpaiḥ sāmādibhir upāyaiḥ sādhayituṃ cintanīyam | tatra hīno daṇḍena samaḥ sāmneṣadadhiko dānena tato 'py adhiko bhedena sādhyāḥ | atha vā śatruṃ daṇḍena | mitraṃ sāmnā | udāsīnaṃ dānena | sarve 'pi bhedena sādhyāḥ || 1.343 ||

	**upāyāḥ sāma dānaṃ ca bhedo daṇḍas tathaiva ca || 1.344 ||**

**	samyak prayuktāḥ sidhyeyur daṇḍas tv agatikā gatiḥ |**

uktānām ariprabhṛtīnāṃ vaśīkāropāyāḥ sāmādayaś catvāro veditavyāḥ | te samyag yathāvat prayuktāḥ sidhyeyuḥ kāryasiddhisamarthāḥ syur ity arthaḥ | eṣāṃ daṇḍo gatyantarābhāve gatiḥ | upāyāntarābhāve daṇḍo 'bhyupāya ity arthaḥ | dānaṃ prasiddham | bhedaḥ svāmibhṛtyānāṃ vimatīkaraṇam | daṇḍo vittasya śarīrasya vā pīḍanam || 1.344 ||

	**saṃdhiṃ ca vigrahaṃ yānam āsanaṃ saṃśrayaṃ tathā || 1.345 ||**

**	dvaidhībhāvaṃ guṇān etān yathāvat parikalpayet |**

saṃdhiprabhṛtīn yathānyāyaṃ yathāviṣayaṃ ṣaḍguṇān parikalpayet prayuñjīta | saṃdhir nāvābhyām anyonyam apakartavyam iti vyavasthāparigrahaḥ, vigraho vairam, yānaṃ yātrā, āsanam upekṣaṇam, saṃśrayaḥ parapīḍitasya prabalarājāntarāśrayaṇam, dvaidhībhāvaḥ svabalasya dvidhākaraṇam || 1.345 ||

_yātrākālam āha_ |

	**yadā sasyaguṇopetaṃ pararāṣṭraṃ tadā vrajet || 1.346 ||**

**	paraś ca hīna ātmā ca hṛṣṭavāhanapūruṣaḥ |**

**[587]**

yadā parasya śatro rāṣṭraṃ sasyair anyaiś ca hiraṇyādiguṇair upetaṃ syāc chatruś ca vāhanādihīnaḥ svayaṃ ca hṛṣṭagajāśvādir hṛṣṭapuruṣaś ca tadā pararāṣṭraṃ vrajet || 1.346 ||

_na ca yātrāyā aniyataphalatvena puruṣeṇa pravartitavyam ity atra hetum āha |_

	**daive puruṣakāre ca karmasiddhir vyavasthitā || 1.347 ||**

**	tatra daivam abhivyaktaṃ pauruṣaṃ paurvadaihikam |**

daive puruṣakāre ca sati karmaṇaḥ karmaphalasya siddhir vyavasthitā niyatā saty api puruṣakāre daivābhāve na phalaṃ sidhyati | na ca prāk pravṛtter daivābhāvaḥ śakyaḥ paricchettum | ato 'rthasaṃśayād yātrādau pravṛttir upapadyata ity abhiprāyaḥ | tatra daivaṃ nāma pūrvadehaprabhavaṃ pauruṣaṃ puruṣasya vyāpāraḥ prayatnākhyo 'pūrvaparyantaḥ | tatra paurvadaihikam iti bāhulyābhiprāyam | kārīryādīnām anuṣṭhāne phalopabhoge ca dehaikyāt || 1.347 ||

_evaṃ tarhi puruṣakārāpekṣaṇīyaṃ daivam evāstu phalasādhakaṃ kiṃ puruṣakāreṇety ata āha |_

	**kecid daivād dhaṭhāt kecit kecit puruṣakārataḥ || 1.348 ||**

**	sidhyanty arthā manuṣyāṇāṃ teṣāṃ yonis tu pauruṣam |**

vṛṣṭimahāpātavidyutpātādayo manuṣyādīnāṃ prāṇinām upakārakā apakārakā vā daivād bhavanti | haṭhāt parakīyapuruṣakārāt kecit | yathānicchantam api sutaṃ mātā payaḥ pāyayati pitādhyāpayati vyāghraḥ sarpo vā dehino vyāpādayati | kecit punar arthāḥ svakīyād eva yatnāt sidhyanti | yathāgnihotrādayo hiṃsāsteyādayaś ca | teṣāṃ sarveṣāṃ pauruṣaṃ prayatno yoniḥ kāraṇam | keṣucid anvayavyatirekābhyām eva prayatnasya kāraṇatvam avagamyate | yeṣāṃ tu vidyutpātādikāraṇatayā prayatno na pramāṇāntarād avagamyate teṣāṃ vedād eva tadavagatiḥ | kārīryādiprayatno vṛṣṭihetutayā vacanasiddha eva | vidyutpātādayas tu duḥkhahetutvenādharmaprayatnajanyatayā sāmānyataḥ śāstrād evāvagamyante | tasmād yātrādau yatitavyam eva || 1.348 ||

**[588]**

_idānīṃ daivapuruṣakārayor anyonyasāpekṣatām āha |_

	**yathā hy ekena cakreṇa rathasya na gatir bhavet || 1.349 ||**

**	evaṃ puruṣakāreṇa vinā daivaṃ na sidhyati |**

yathā rathagatikāraṇatvena pramitam api rathādicakram ekam ekāki cakrāntaravidhuraṃ rathaṃ na gamayati evaṃ sukhaduḥkhānubhāvātmakakāryajananatayā pramitam api daivaṃ na puruṣakāreṇa sahakāriṇā vinā kāryaparyantena rūpeṇa sidhyati | vidyunnipātādy api sādhayato daivasya deśaviśeṣe puruṣasyāvasthānāpādakaṃ pauruṣaṃ bhavaty eva sahakāri | tasmāt phalārthinā na kevalaṃ daivapareṇa bhavitavyam || 1.349 ||

_sāmādīnām upāyānāṃ parasparaviruddhānekaphalodayaprasaṅge yad grāhyaṃ tad āha |_

	**hiraṇyabhūmilābheṣu mitralabdhir varā yataḥ || 1.350 ||**

**	ato yateta tatprāptau rakṣet satyaṃ samāhitaḥ |**

sāmādīn upāyān praty upeyatayāvasthitānāṃ hiraṇyabhūmimitralābhānāṃ madhye mitralabdhir varā śreṣṭhā, ato mitraprāptiviṣayo yatnaḥ kāryaḥ | maitrīkaraṇakāle kṛtasya satyasyārakṣaṇe mitram apy amitraṃ bhavet | ataḥ satyarakṣaṇe samādhir vidheyaḥ | etac ca sāmādisādhyād dhiraṇyabhūmilābhād adhikalābhahetor mitrasya prāptau veditavyam | anyadā tu hiraṇyalābha eva balavān || 1.350 ||

_rājyāṅgāny āha_ |

	**svāmyamātyau jano(nā) durgaḥ kośo daṇḍas tathaiva ca || 1.351 ||**

**	mitrāṇy etāḥ prakṛtayo rājyaṃ saptāṅgam ucyate |**

rājñaḥ karma janapadapālanaṃ rājyaṃ tat saptāṅgam | saptāsyāṅgāni bhavanti | kāni tānīty apekṣite svāmītyādinā mitrāṇītyantena tadviśeṣo nirdiṣṭaḥ | kutas teṣām aṅgatvam ity ākāṅkṣita uktam etāḥ prakṛtaya iti | yataḥ kāryam utpadyate 'vatiṣṭhate niyamena bhavati sā prakṛtiḥ | yathā hiraṇyaṃ kuṇḍalasya | rājyaṃ ca vinā svāmyādibhir notpadyata utpannam api na tair vinā cirakālam anuvartate | tato bhavanti svāmyādayo rājyāṅgāni | svāmī mahotsāhatvādiguṇayuktaḥ puruṣaviśeṣaḥ | **[589]** amātyāmantriprabhṛtayaḥ, janāḥ pālanīyāḥ prajāḥ, durgaṃ prasiddham, saṃcitaṃ vasu, daṇḍaś camūḥ, mitrāṇy upakārakā rājānaḥ || 1.351 ||

_prāptarājyena yat kāryaṃ tad āha |_

	**tad avāpya nṛpo daṇḍaṃ durvṛtteṣu nipātayet || 1.352 ||**

**	dharmo hi daṇḍarūpeṇa brahmaṇā nirmitaḥ purā |**

tad rājyaṃ kāryatayāvāpya rājyādhikāraṃ labdhveti yāvat | rājā daṇḍaṃ dhanaśarīrapīḍanaviṣayaṃ durvṛtteṣu śāstrātikramakāriṣu nipātayet prayuñjīta | na ca daṇḍaṃ prayuñjānasya rājñaḥ pratyavāyaḥ śaṅkanīyaḥ | yato bhagavatā brahmaṇā vidhinā dharma eva daṇḍātmanā nirmito vihitaḥ | rājānaṃ prati vihitatvād daṇḍo nādharmāyety arthaḥ || 1.352 ||

	**sa netuṃ nyāyataḥ śakyo 'lubdhena kṛtabuddhinā || 1.353 ||**

**	satyasaṃdhena śucinā susahāyena dhīmatā |**

alubdhena nyāyadhanavyayakāriṇā kṛtabuddhinā vṛddhasevāvidyāgamābhyāṃ labdhaprajñena satyasaṃdhena satyasaṃkalpena śucinā śuddhopadhena bāhyābhyantraśaucavatā ca susahāyena śāstroktaguṇagaṇayuktamantriprabhṛtisahāyavatā dhīmatādhigatārthānucintanavatā sa daṇḍo nyāyato yathāśāstraṃ netuṃ praṇetuṃ śakyo bhavati na punar anyena || 1.353 ||

_samyag daṇḍaṃ praṇayato 'bhyudayo 'nyathā pratyavāya ity āha |_

	**yathāśāstraṃ prayuktaḥ san sadevāsuramānavam || 1.358 ||**

**	jagad ānandayet sarvam anyathā tu prakopayet |**

śāstrānatikrameṇa prayukto daṇḍo devādisahitaṃ jagad ānandayet | tataś ca svasya sukhayogaḥ | asamyakpraṇayane tu tad eva prakopayet | tataś cātmano duḥkhayogaḥ || 1.354 ||

_aparam api phalam āha |_

	**adharmadaṇḍanaṃ svargakīrtilokavināśanam || 1.355 ||**

**	samyak tu daṇḍanaṃ rājñaḥ svargakīrtijayāvaham |**

**[590]**

daṇḍasyāsamyakpraṇayanaṃ prāganuṣṭhitadharmavaśād upārjitasya svargasya kīrter asya ca lokasya vināśakaṃ bhavati | samyakpraṇyanaṃ tu dharmāntarārjitaṃ svargaṃ kīrtiṃ jayaṃ ca vighnanivāraṇadvāreṇāvahati | tasmāt samyag eva daṇḍaḥ praṇeyaḥ || 1.355 ||

_daṇḍyam āha_ |

	**api bhrātā suto 'rghyo vā śvaśuro mātulo 'pi vā || 1.356 ||**

**	nādaṇḍyo nāma rājño 'sti dharmād vicalitaḥ svakāt |**

svakīyavarṇāśramādidharmam akurvan daṇḍyaḥ | na tasya saṃbandhiviśeṣād gurutvād vā daṇḍanīyatvanivṛttiḥ | arghyaḥ pūjyaḥ | prasiddham anyat | yat tu smṛtyantaram: "adaṇḍyau mātāpitarau | snātakapurohitaparivrājakavānaprasthaśrutaśīlaśaucācāravantas te hi dharmādhikāriṇaḥ" iti, tat svalpāparādhaviṣayam | na sarvātmanā daṇḍābhāvābhiprāyam | ata eva dakṣaḥ |

	pārivrājyaṃ gṛhītvā tu yaḥ svadharme na tiṣṭhati |

	śvapādenāṅkayitvā taṃ rājā śīghraṃ vivāsayet || 1.356 ||

_na kevalaṃ daṇḍanīyān daṇḍayato rājñaḥ pratyavāyābhāvaḥ kiṃ tv abhyudayaviśeṣo 'pi bhavatīty āha_ |

	**yo daṇḍyān daṇḍayed rājā samyag vadhyāṃś ca ghātayet || 1.357 ||**

**	iṣṭaṃ syāt kratubhis tena samāptavaradakṣiṇaiḥ |**

dhigdaṇḍādibhir daṇḍanīyān daṇḍayatā vadhārhaṃś ca ghātayatā samyag āptā labdhā varā dakṣiṇā yais taiḥ krutubhir iṣṭaṃ syāt | na caitāvatā daṇḍasya kāmyatvam āśaṅkanīyam | yataś ca tadapraṇayane prāyaścittam āha vasiṣṭhaḥ: "daṇḍyotsarge rājaikarātram uapavaset trirātraṃ purohitaḥ kṛcchram adaṇḍyadaṇḍane purohitas trirātraṃ rājā" iti | tathā |

	eno rājānam ṛcchaty utsṛjantaṃ vai sakilbiṣam |

	taṃ ced ghātayate rājā ghnan dharmeṇa na duṣyati || 1.357 ||

	**iti saṃcintya nṛpatiḥ kratutulyaphalaṃ pṛthak || 1.358 ||**

**	vyavahārān svayaṃ paśyet sabhyaiḥ parivṛto 'nvaham |**

**[591]**

evaṃ daṇḍyadaṇḍanasya kratusamānaphalatvaṃ saṃcintya samyak paribhāvya daṇḍyādaṇḍyavivekāya vakṣyamāṇalakṣaṇaiḥ sabhyaiḥ parivṛto nṛpatir vyavahārān vivādān pṛthakkāryāntarāsaṃkareṇa pratyahaṃ paśyet parīkṣeta || 1.358 ||

	**kulāni jātīḥ śreṇīś ca gaṇāñ janapadān api || 1.359 ||**

**	svadharmāc calitān rājā vinīya sthāpayet pathi |**

kulāni kuṭumbādīni, jātīr brāhmaṇādyāḥ, śreṇīḥ suvarṇakārādyāḥ, gaṇān maṭhabrāhmaṇādīñ janapadān rāṣṭrāṇi, svadharmād apetāni vinīya daṇḍayitvā pathi svadharme sthāpayet | pūrvatraikaikasya daṇḍo vihito 'tra tu bahūnām ity apunar uktā || 1.359 ||

_daṇḍopayogi kṛṣṇalādinirūpaṇam āha_ |

	**jālasūryamarīcisthaṃ trasareṇū rajaḥ smṛtam || 1.360 ||**

**	te 'ṣṭau likṣā tu tās tisro rājasarṣapa ucyate |**

gavākṣapraviṣṭādityakiraṇeṣu yat susūkṣmaṃ vaiśeṣikoktanītyā dvyaṇukatrayārabdhaṃ dṛśyate rajas tat trasareṇur iti manvādibhiḥ smṛtam | te 'ṣṭau trasareṇavo likṣaikā, tās tisro rājasarṣapa ucyate || 1.360 ||

	**gauras tu te trayaḥ ṣaṭ te yavo madhyas trayas tu te || 1.361 ||**

**	kṛṣṇalaḥ pañca te māṣas te suvarṇas tu ṣoḍaśa ||**

te rājasarṣapās traya eko gaurasarṣapaḥ | te ca ṣaṭsaṃkhyākā eko madhyamo yavaḥ, trayo yavā ekaḥ kṛṣṇalaḥ, evaṃ kṛṣṇalāḥ pañca māṣaḥ, ṣoḍaśa māṣā ekaḥ suvarṇaḥ || 1.361 ||

	**palaṃ suvarṇāś catvāraḥ pañca vāpi prakīrtitam || 1.362 ||**

uktāḥ suvarāś catvāraḥ pañca vāpi palaṃ prakīrtitam | deśānusāreṇa palavyavasthā kartavyā || 1.362 ||

_kanakaparimāṇam uktam adhunā rajataparimāṇam āha_ |

	**dve kṛṣṇale raupyamāṣo dharaṇaṃ ṣoḍaśaiva te |**

**	śatamānaṃ tu daśabhir dharaṇaiḥ palam eva tu || 1.363 ||**

**[592]**

	**niṣkaḥ suvarṇāś catvāraḥ**

kṛṣṇaladvayaparimito raupyasya māṣo bhavati | te ṣoḍaśa māṣā raupyasya dharaṇam | daśabhir dharaṇaiḥ śatamānasaṃjñakaṃ raupyasya parimāṇam, tad eva ca palam | catvāraḥ suvarṇā raupyasya niṣkaḥ || 1.363 ||

_tāmrasya parimāṇam āha_ |

	**kārṣikas tāmrikaḥ paṇaḥ |**

suvarṇasya palasya caturthāṃśaḥ karṣas tena saṃmitaḥ kārṣikaḥ sa tāmrikaḥ paṇo bhavati | tāmrasyāyaṃ tāmrikaḥ ||

	**sāśītiḥ paṇasāhasro daṇḍa uttamasāhasaḥ || 1.364 ||**

**	tadardhaṃ madhyamaḥ proktas tadardham adhamaḥ smṛtaḥ |**

aśītyadhikasahasrasaṃkhyākāḥ paṇā uttamasāhasākhyo daṇḍaḥ | catvāriṃśadadhikāḥ pañcaśatasaṃkhyākapāṇātmako madhyamasāhasākhyo daṇḍaḥ | saptatyadhikaśatadvayasaṃkhyākapaṇātmako 'dhamasāhasākhyo daṇḍaḥ, sa eva śāstrāntare prathamasāhasākhya ity ucyate | yat tu manunoktam,

	paṇānāṃ dve śate sārdhe prathamaḥ sāhasaḥ smṛtaḥ |

	madhyamaḥ pañca vijñeyaḥ sahasraṃ tv eva cottamaḥ ||

iti, tad alpāparādhaviṣayam || 1.364 ||

	**digdaṇḍas tv atha vāgdaṇḍo dhanadaṇḍo vadhas tathā || 1.365 ||**

**	yojyā vyastāḥ samastā vāpy aparādhavaśād ime |**

dhigdaṇḍo dhik tvāṃ kāpuruṣam ityādi | vāgdaṇḍaḥ sarvasvaṃ te harāmi tvāṃ deśān nirvāsayāmītyādi paruṣabhāṣaṇam | dhanadaṇḍaḥ kṛṣṇalāpaharaṇādisarvaharaṇāntaḥ | vadhadaṇḍaḥ śarīratāḍanam, prāṇacchedo vā | ete daṇḍā aparādhānusāreṇa vyastā ekaśaḥ samastā dvau trayaś catvāro vā prayojyāḥ || 1.365 ||

	**jñātvāparādhaṃ deśaṃ ca kālaṃ balam athāpi vā |**

**	vayaḥ karma ca vittaṃ ca daṇḍaṃ daṇḍyeṣu pātayet || 1.366 ||**

iti rājadharmaprakaraṇam || 12 ||

**[593]**

aparādhādi jñātvā daṇḍaṃ daṇḍyeṣu pātayet prayuñjīta | atra ca pūrvavākyaprāptatvād aparādhajñānam anūdyate | deśādijñānaṃ tu vidhīyate | kvacid videśe svalpenaiva śītenātapena vā svalpakālīnena bhojananivāraṇenādhikā pīḍā bhavati | kvacit tu mahatāpi na tāvatī | tathā kāle śaradādau | tathā daṇḍanīyabalaṃ viditvā tāḍanādidaṇḍo vidheyaḥ | tathā vayaḥkarmavittāni | anyathā tatsvarūpanāśo 'gnihotrādikarmalopo vittāprāptiś ca syāt | deśādi viditvā tu daṇḍapraṇayane yogakṣemāv upapadyete iti | etat sarvaṃ kṣatriyasya rājyaṃ kurvataḥ pravihitam | yadā punar akṣatriyaḥ kṣatriyakāryaṃ kuryāt tadānenāpy etat sarvam anuṣṭheyam, "tatkāryāpattyā taddharmalābhaḥ" iti nyāyāt, karādānaprayuktatvāc ca prajāpālanasya | sarvo hi dhanaṃ prayacchann ātmasamavāyi prayojanam uddiśati | na ca karadānasya svagupter anyat prayojanam asti | tasmāt karam ādadānena prajāpālanaṃ vidheyam iti siddham || 1.366 ||

**iti śrīvidhyādharavaṃśaprabhavaśrīśilāhāranarendrajīmūtavāhanānvayaprasūta-**

**śrīmadaprādityadevaviracite yājñavalkīyadharmaśāstranibandhe 'parārke**

**rājanītiprakaraṇaṃ samāptam || 12 ||**

**samāptaś cāyam ācārādhyāyaḥ prathamaḥ ||**
